+++
dvādaśaḥ skandhaḥ

<details><summary>English</summary>

(First published Oct. 24, 2007)

1.04 (Nov. 7, 2009)

Version 1.05 (Sept. 27, 2011)

This version contains the full Madhva commentary (_Bhāgavata-tātparya-nirṇaya_) with footnotes by Bannanje Govindacharya, _Bhāgavata-bhāvārtha-dīpikā_ by Śrīdhara Svāmī (entered by Gauranga for the BBT), _Caitanya-mata-mañjuṣa _by Śrīnātha Cakravartī, Sanātana Gosvāmī’s comments on verses quoted from this canto in the _Hari-bhakti-vilāsa, Krama-sandarbha _by Jīva Gosvāmī, first entered by Gauranga for the BBT supplemented by additional notes from the _Ṣaṭ-sandarbhas _and corrected against the Puridas edition, and Viśvanātha Cakravartī’s _Sārārtha-darśinī. _Where not otherwise attributed, all text entered and edited by Jagadananda Das.

</details>



## atha prathamo’dhyāyaḥ


### rāja-vaṁśānukīrtanaṁ

_oṁ namo bhagavate vāsudevāya_

**|| 12.1.1 ||**[^1]

**rājovāca—**

**svadhāmānugate kṛṣṇe yadu-vaṁśa-vibhūṣaṇe |**

**kasya vaṁśo’bhavat pṛthvyām etad ācakṣva me mune ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :**

śrī-guruṁ paramānandaṁ vanda ānanda-vigraham |

yasya sannati-mātreṇa cid ānandāyate bapuḥ ||

jayanti śrī-parānanda-kṛṣāpāṅga-lasad-dṛśaḥ |

yā nityam anuvartante saṁpado vigatādṛśaḥ ||

uktas trayodaśādhyāyair dvādaśe tv āśrayaḥ sataḥ |

adhiṣṭhānāvadhitvābhyām āśrayaś ceśvaraḥ sataḥ ||

ukto layāvadhitvena prākṛtātyantike laye |

adhiṣṭhānatayā cokto mahā-puruṣa-varṇane ||

tatrādau ṣaḍbhir adhyāyaiḥ śukaḥ prāha parīkṣite |

śeṣais tatrākhilāny āha sūtaḥ pṛṣṭo’tha satribhiḥ ||

svāśraya-śravaṇe kāryo na vilambo manīṣiṇā |

ity etat kāla-vaiṣamyaṁ caturbhis tāvad ucyate ||

tatra tu prathame bhāvi- māgadhānvaya-bhūmi-pān |

kali-prabhāvataḥ prāha saṅkarādim alīmasān ||

tad evaṁ vaivasvata-manu-vaṁśe soma-vaṁśa-prastāvena śrī-kṛṣṇāvatāra-caritāni sa-prapañcamanuvarṇitāni, athedānīṁ bhāvī soma-vaṁśaḥ kalau vijātīya-saṅkarādim alīmaso vairaṅya-dvārā śrī-kṛṣṇaika-bhakti-nigamanāyānuvarṇyate, tatra tu soma-vaṁśa-śākhāsu cira-kālānuvartitayā māgadha-vaṁśo’nukramyate, tatra pūror vaṁśe uparicaro vasus tasya bṛhad-rathas tasya jārasandhas tasya sahadevaḥ putro’bhūd ity uktaṁ navama-skandhe | tatraiva sahadevān mārjāris tataḥ śrutaśravā ity-ādayo ripuñjayāntā viṁśatir bhāvino rājāno nirūpitāḥ | (tatra rājā pṛcchati, svadhāmeti | idānīṁ) ||1||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **oṁ svasti śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ |  


    vande'haṁ gopikānāthaṁ yaśodānandanandanam |


    vṛndārakagaṇādhīśaṁ vṛndāvananikuñjagam ||


    namaskṛtya gurūnsarvānakhilābhīpsitapradān |


    dvādaśa-skandhavivṛtiṁ prārabhe viduṣāṁ mude ||


    śrīguruṁ paramānandaṁ vanda ānandavigraham |


    yasya saṁnatimātreṇa cidānandāyate vapuḥ ||

śloko'yamadhikaḥ keṣucitpustakeṣu dṛśyate maṅgalarūpatvānmayāpyatrālekhīti | jayanti śrīparānandetyādipadyam ekādaśe vyākhyātam api punar api kiñcidvyākhyāsyāmaḥ—śrīḥ rādhā tayā sahitaḥ parānandaḥ śrī-kṛṣṇaḥ | yad vā, śriyāṁ parastatparaḥ śrīparaḥ śrīḥ kaiṭabhārīhṛdayaikakṛtādhivāsā iti mārkaṇḍeyoktaḥ | sa cāsāvānandaścati śrīparānandaḥ | yad vā,  śrīḥ parotkṛṣṭā yāsu tāḥ śrīparā gopyastā ānandayatīti śrīparānandaḥ | kṛpayā yuktā apāṅagagā kaṭākṣāḥ kṛpāpāṅgāstair lasantyo dedīpyamānā yā dṛśaḥ dṛkpātāstāḥ kṛpāpāṅgalasadṛśaḥ, śrīparānaṅdasya kṛpāpāṅgalasadṛśaḥ śrīparānanda kṛpāpāṅgalasadṛśo jayanti sarvotkarṣeṇa vartate | yā anu nityaṁ sampado vartate | kiṁbhūtā dṛśaḥ—vigatāścakṣuragocarā ity arthaḥ | yad vā, vigatādṛgajñānaṁ yābhistā ity arthaḥ| bhaktyādirūpā ity arthaḥ| yad vā, yādṛśo'nusampado'vigatāḥ sadā vartanta ity arthaḥ (1) | sataḥ sadūpatayā pratīyamānasya prapañcasyāśrayastrayodaśādhyāyair ukta ityanvayaḥ | tam evāha—sata īśvara āśrayaḥ | kābhyāmityata āha adhiṣṭhāneti (2) prākṛtaḥ sarvaprakṛtilayātmakaḥ ātyantiko mokṣaḥ, etallayadvaye'vadhitvena sarvāvasānabhūmitveneśvaraḥ uktaḥ | mahāpuruṣo virāṭ tadvarṇane cādhiṣṭhānatayā sarvādhāratayoktaś ca sarvalokānāṁ tadavayavakalpanayā tadādhāro'vayavī virāḍrūpīśa ukta ity arthaḥ (3) | tatra trayodaśādhyāyeṣu | śeṣaiḥ saptabhiḥ | khilānyākāṅkṣitārthapūrakāṇyākhyānāni | satribhiḥ śaunakādibhiḥ (4) | ityetad iti kālavilambaparityāgārtham | kālavaiṣamyaṁ kālakṛtabuddhivaiṣamyam | tāvadādau (5) | tatra caturṣv api | saṅkaro varṇasaṅkaratvam tadādibhirasatyasambhāṣaṇādidoṣair malīmasānmalinān (6) | evaṁbhūte pūrvoktapāvanatvādiviśeṣaṇaviśiṣṭe | vaṁśaḥ somasya pāvanaḥ ity-ādinavanavamokteḥ| buddhau sannihitatvādevaṁbhūta ity uktam | mukundasya hareḥ| svairakrīḍā svena vedarūpeṇātmanā varṇitā pūtanādivadharāsādirūpā krīḍā | pūtanāvadhādirūpā krīḍāpi vedenoktā, tatra pramāṇībhūtāḥ kāścichrutayo'pi tatratatra sabhāṣyā uktā eva | svairakrīḍā vedāvihitā krīḍeti vyākhyānamatra na śobhanam yadāyadā hi dharmasya ity-ādiśrīgītāvirodhāt | sa eva candravaṁśa eva | muktvā tyaktvā | muktyai mokṣāya | anyadvartmānyo mārgo nāstīti kathayitum | kalau nityanaimittikādikarmākaraṇādantaḥkaraṇaśuddheranudayājjñānayogādyasambhavādbhaktir eva mukhyo muktimārgaḥ kalau bhaktiḥ kalau bhaktirbhaktyā kṛṣṇaḥ puraḥsthitaḥ ity-ādipāyokteḥ 87) | svadhāmetyādipraśnaślokaś ca na svāmisaṁmata iti bhāti | taiś ca tad evamityārabhya ripuñjayāntā viṁśatirbhāvino rājāno nirūpitā ityantena pūrvasambandhamanūdya taduparitanaṁ vaṁśaṁ saṅkarādidauṣaiḥ prapañcayati—yontya iti ślokāvataraṇaṁ dattavadbhiḥ praśnasya kvāpyanullekhāt , vaṁśakathanaprastāvasya navamaskandhataḥ pravṛttatvādbhagavanniryāṇānantaraṁ svavaṁśasya māgadhavaṁśasya ca vidyamānatvena tādṛśapraśnāsambhavāc ca | ata evāyaṁ praśnaśloko vijayadhvajaviśvanāthābhyāṁ parityaktaḥ ||1||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **śrī-rādhā-kṛṣṇābhyāṁ namaḥ |[^2] atha dvādaśa-skandhasya krama-sandarbhaḥ |

dvādaśa-krama-sandarbhe sandarbhāṇāṁ samāhṛtiḥ |

kriyate yan-nideśena sa me’nanya-gater gatiḥ ||

tad evam ekādaśa-skandha-paryanta-granthena nijābhīṣṭaṁ śrī-kṛṣṇa-lakṣaṇam āśrayaṁ yathāvan nirūpya purāṇopasaṁhārāya dvādaśa-skandha ārabhyate ||1|| 

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **śrī-gurave namaḥ |

praṇamya śrī-guruṁ bhūyaḥ śrī-kṛṣṇaṁ karuṇārṇavam |

lokanāthaṁ jagac-cakṣuḥ śrī-śukaṁ tam upāśraye ||

gopa-rāmā-jana-prāṇa-preyase’tiprabhuṣṇave |

tadīya-priya-dāsyāya māṁ madīyam ahaṁ dade ||

trayodaśabhir adhyāyair dvādaśe tu caturvidhaḥ |

nirodha uktaḥ śrī-kṛṣṇa-kathāpy atropasaṁhṛtau ||

tribhir ādau kaler dharma-drohiṇaḥ kathyate kathā |

ekena pralayāsyātha dvābhyāṁ śuka-parīkṣitoḥ ||

purāṇasya tathaikena mārkaṇḍeyasya ca tribhiḥ |

sūryasyākhyāna-vṛndasya bhāvi-bhūmipānāṁ kathocyate |

māgadhānvaya-jātānāṁ kali-kalmaṣa-śālinām ||

 **...**

**|| 12.1.2-3 ||**

**śrī-śuka uvāca—**

**yo’ntyaḥ purañjayo nāma bhaviṣyo bārahadrathaḥ |**

**tasyāmātyas tu śunako hatvā svāminam ātma-jam ||**

**pradyota-saṁjñaṁ rājānaṁ kartā yat-pālakaḥ sutaḥ |**

**viśākhayūpas tat-putro bhavitā rājakas tataḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tad-uparitanaṁ vaṁśaṁ saṅkarādi-doṣaiḥ prapañcayati—yo’ntya iti | ripuñjaya eva purañjayaḥ | svāminaṁ purañjayaṁ hatvā sva-putraṁ pradyota-saṁjñaṁ rājānaṁ kariṣyati | yasya pālako nāma suto bhaviṣyati ||2||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **antyo vaṁśāvasānabhavaḥ | bhāvyo bārhadratho nṛpaḥ iti pracuraḥ pāṭhaḥ | bārahadratha iha rephe'kārāgamastvārṣa eva dhyeyaḥ | tasya purañjayasya | amātyo mantrī amātyaḥ sacivo mantrī ityabhidhānāt || tatputraḥ pālakaputraḥ | tato viśākhayūpāt ||2-3||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **yatra tad-antardhāne lokānāṁ duḥkham eva syād iti darśayitva, kathañcit taṁ bhajatāṁ tu nistāraḥ syād iti darśayiṣyate—śrī-śuka uvāca | yo’ntyo purañjaya ity-ādinā ||2||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **tad evaṁ candra-vaṁśāvataṁsasya śrī-kṛṣṇa-candrasya caritāmṛta-kathā-sindhuḥ, skandha-dvayena varṇitaḥ | tatraiva lokān nimajya ānandayitum idānīṁ teṣāṁ tato’nyatra vairāgyam utpādayituṁ tasyaiva candra-vaṁśyāntimo bhāgo varṇyate | tatra candra-vaṁśa-śākhāyāṁ puror vaṁśe uparicaro vasuḥ | tasya putro bṛhadrathaḥ, tasya jarāsandhaḥ | tasya sahadevaḥ | putro’bhūd ity uktaṁ navama-skandhe | punaś ca tatraiva sahadevasya mārjāris tasya śrutaśravā ity evaṁ ripuñjayāntā viṁśati-bhāvino rājāno nirūpitāḥ | atra skandhe tad-uparitanaṁ vaṁśaṁ saṅkarādi-doṣair malinībhūtaṁ varṇayati—yo’ntya iti | ripuñjaya eva purañjayaḥ, bārahadrathaḥ bṛhadratha-vaṁśyaḥ | svāminaṁ ripuñjayaṁ hatvā sva-putraṁ pradyotaṁ rājānaṁ kariṣyati | yat yasya pradyotasya sutaḥ pālakaḥ pālaka-saṁjñaḥ ||2||

 **...**

**|| 12.1.4 ||**

**nandivardhanas tat-putraḥ pañca pradyotanā ime |**

**aṣṭa-triṁśottara-śataṁ bhokṣyanti pṛthivīṁ nṛpāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **pradyotanāḥ pradyota-saṁjñāḥ ||4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tatputro rājakaputraḥ | ime pradyotanena saha pañcasaṅkhyākā aṣṭātriṁśaduttaravarṣaśatakaṁ 138 pṛthvīṁ bhokṣyanti pālayiṣyanti bhujo'vane ityataḥ parasmaipadam ||4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** pradyota-vaṁśatvāt pradyotanāḥ ||4||

 **...**

**|| 12.1.5-8 ||**

**śiśunāgas tato bhāvyaḥ kākavarṇas tu tat-sutaḥ |**

**kṣemadharmā tasya sutaḥ kṣetrajñaḥ kṣemadharma-jaḥ ||**

**vidhisāraḥ sutas tasyā- jātaśatrur bhaviṣyati |**

**darbhakas tat-suto bhāvī darbhakasyājayaḥ smṛtaḥ ||**

**nandivardhana ājeyo mahānandiḥ sutas tataḥ |**

**śiśunāgā daśaivaite ṣaṣṭy-uttara-śata-trayam ||**

**samā bhokṣyanti pṛthivīṁ kuru-śreṣṭha kalau nṛpāḥ |**

**mahānandi-suto rājan śūdrā-garbhodbhavo balī ||**

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tataḥ pradyotanebhyaḥ paścāt | bhāvyo bhaviṣyati | tatsutaḥ śiśunāgaḥ sutaḥ | tasya kākavarṇasya || tasya kṣetrajñasya, tasya ajātaśatruḥ, tasyetyubhayānvayi | tatsuto'jātaśatrusutaḥ || ājeyo'jayaputraḥ | atraikāramadhyatvamārṣam | tato nandivarddhanasya | ṣaṣṭyuttaraśatatrayaṁ 360 rājyabhogavarṣasaṅkhyeyam ||5-8||

 **...**

**|| 12.1.9 ||**

**mahāpadma-patiḥ kaścin nandaḥ kṣatra-vināśa-kṛt |**

**tato nṛpā bhaviṣyanti śūdra-prāyās tv adhārmikāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **nando nāma kaścin mahā-padma-saṅkhyāyā senāyāḥ dhanasya vā patir bhaviṣyati | ata eva mahā-padma ity api tasya nāma ||9||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** ājeyaḥ ajayasya sutaḥ | sa nando mahā-padma-patitvān mahā-padmaḥ ||9||

 **...**

**|| 12.1.10 ||**

**sa eka-cchatraṁ pṛthivīm anullaṅghita-śāsanaḥ |**

**śāsiṣyati mahāpadmo dvitīya iva bhārgavaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ekam eva chatraṁ yasyāṁ tāṁ pṛthivīṁ śāsiṣyati pālayiṣyati | kṣatrotsādane dṛṣṭāntaḥ, bhārgavaḥ paraśurāma iva ||10||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **samā varṣāṇi hāyano'strī śaratsamāḥ ity amaraḥ | he kuruśreṣṭheti—tvaṁ tvatīya pavitre'pi kuruvaṁśe śreṣṭho'si yena śrī-kṛṣṇalīlāmṛtamante pītam iti bhāvaḥ | he rājann iti—tvaṁ tu dharmeṇaiva rājase na tu gaṇitanṛpasadṛśo'sīti bhāvaḥ ata eva mahāpadmasenādipatitvādeva | matvarthīyājantāśrayaṇe tasyāpi tannāma sambhavati, mahāpadmāḥ santyasyeti nirukteḥ | svena saha bhojanasambandhādikamakurvatāṁ kṣatriyāṇāṁ vināśakaḥ, tantrasabhayācchuddhāḥ kṣatriyāstataḥ palāyitvā yavanādideśa gatā vaiśyavṛttyādijīvino bhaviṣyanti, tataḥ prabhṛti nṛpāḥ śūdraprāyā bhaviṣyanti | prāyaḥśabdena śūdrarājyabāhulye kvacitkṣatriyāvaśeṣo bodhyate, kṣatravaṁśavirodhe ca dvitīyabhārgava iva | tathā ca bhārgaveṇaikaviṁśativāraṁ pṛthivyāṁ kṣatrahanane yatkārtavīryadveṣeṇa hananaṁ tasyaiva pañcaputrāvaśeṣaśravaṇāt, kimu vācyaṁ kṣatriyāntaravaṁśyānām, tathāpi bahavo hatā bahavo deśāntaraṁ gatā iti jñeyam ||9-10||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **kṣatra-vināśakatve dṛṣṭāntaḥ, bhārgavaḥ paraśurāma iva ||10||

 **...**

**|| 12.1.11-12 ||**

**tasya cāṣṭau bhaviṣyanti sumālya-pramukhāḥ sutāḥ |**

**ya imāṁ bhokṣyanti mahīṁ rājānaś ca śataṁ samāḥ ||**

**nava nandān dvijaḥ kaścit prapannān uddhariṣyati |**

**teṣām abhāve jagatīṁ mauryā bhokṣyanti vai kalau ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **samāḥ saṁvatsarān ||11|| nava nandān nandaṁ ca tat-putrāṁś cety evaṁ nava | prapannān viśvas tān vikhyātān vā | dvijaḥ kauṭilya-vātsyāyanādi-paryāyaś cāṇakya uddhariṣyaty unmūlayiṣyati | mauryā maurya-saṁjñāḥ |

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tasya mahāpadmākhyanandasya || viśvastahananasya mahāpāpatvādāha—vikhyātānveti | viśvastaghātasya mahāpāpatve bhojiyakapisiṁhakathānusandheyā dṛṣṭāntatvena | tathā hi—kadācidbhojanṛpataye tadājñayā tadbhāyaryāyā bhānumatyā mūrtiṁ likhitvā kālidāso darśayāmāsa | sa ca tāṁ jaghanadeśe tilakālakāṅkitāṁ dṛṣṭvā'nena madbhāryā ramiteti śaṅkito bhūtvā taṁ deśānniṣkāsayāmāsa | tadanu kadācinmṛgayāṁ gato nṛpo viṣamavane bhayārtaḥ kvacidārūḍhavānaravṛkṣamāruroha, vānaro'pi tena maitrīṁ kṛtavān, sa ca tatraiva viśvasya śiśye | tadā ca kaścitkapivirodhisiṁhastatrāgatyemaṁ me dehīti vairaniryātanārthamuvāca | sa ca śaraṇāpannatyāge doṣaṁ dṛṣṭvā na dadau | tataś ca kapir api siṁhāyāhaṁ na prakṣepyastvayetyuktvā śiśye | sa eva siṁhaḥ punarāgatya rājānamuvāca dehi ma imaṁ kapinno cettvāṁ bhakṣiyiṣyāmīto'vatīm iti, tacchrutvā kapi rājā prakṣiptavān, sa ca patankācittadvṛkṣaśākhāmālambya tatraivāgatya rājānaṁ kuṣṭhī bhaveti śaśāpa | punā rājñā prasāditaḥ vi-se-me-rā iti varṇacatuṣkārthaśravaṇenollāgho bhaviṣyasītyuvāca | tato nṛpo gṛhamāgatya vanyavṛttaṁ mantribhya uktvā vidvatsamājamakṣaracatuṣkārthaśravaṇārthaṁ cakāra | tatra ca rājaniṣkāsitaḥ kālidāsaḥ strīveṣeṇa kasyacidviduṣo gṛhe dhārānagaryāmevāsīt | sa tatas tadrājavṛttamākarṇya | pitrīkṛtaṁ paṇḍitamitthamuvāca—madīyā putrī tvadabhilaṣitavarṇacatuṣkārthaṁ jānāti tāmihāhūya pṛccheta nṛpāya kathayeti | sa ca tathā kṛtvā strīveṣiṇaṁ taṁ nṛpasadasi nināyāsa | sa ca strīveṣī kālidāsaḥ pṛthagarthaṁ pratyekavarṇasyoktavān | tathā hi—


    viśvāsapratipanneṣu ye ca viśvāsaghātakāḥ | 


    te yānti narakaṁ ghoraṁ tāḍitā yamakiṅkaraḥ (1) setubandhe samudre ca gaṅgāsāgarasaṅgame | snātvā pāpavimuktaḥ syānmitradrohakaraṁ vinā (2) merutulyānmahāpāpānkṛtvā saṅgaṁ satāṁ naraḥ | mucyate na hi sandeho mitradrohī na mucyate (3) rājanbhoḥ śṛṇu madvākyaṁ yadi kalyāṇamicchasi | dehi dānaṁ suviprebhyastataḥ śreyo bhaviṣyati (4) ityākarṇya bhojaḥ svastho bhūtvā tāmuvāca—gṛhe vasasi bho devi vanaṁ kvāpi na gacchasi | pañcāsyakapimadvṛttaṁ kathaṁ jānāsi sundara (5) || 

sa covāca—


    devadvijaprasādena kaṇṭhe vasati śāradā | sarvaṁ jānāmi bho rājanbhānumatyāstilaṁ yathā (6) || 

tato nṛpastaṁ kālidāsaṁ jñātvā prasādyānayāmāseti bṛhadbhojaprabandhe ||11-12||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **nava nandān nandaṁ ca tat-putrān aṣṭau cety evaṁ nava prapannān viśvastān dvijaś cāṇakyaḥ uddhariṣyati unmūlayiṣyati | mauryā maurya-saṁjñāḥ ||11||

 **...**

**|| 12.1.13 ||**

**sa eva candraguptaṁ vai dvijo rājye’bhiṣekṣyati |**

**tat-suto vārisāras tu tataś cāśokavardhanaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kathaṁ bhokṣyanti tad āha—sa eveti | candraguptaṁ maurya-prathamam ||13||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **sa eva kuṭilo dvija eva | tatputraścandraguptaputraḥ | tato vārisārāt ||13||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.1.14 ||**

**suyaśā bhavitā tasya saṅgataḥ suyaśaḥ-sutaḥ |**

**śāliśūkas tatas tasya somaśarmā bhaviṣyati |**

**śatadhanvā tatas tasya bhavitā tad bṛhadrathaḥ ||**

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tasyāśokavarddhanasya | tataḥ suyaśasaḥ| tasya śāliśūkasya ||14||

 **...**

**|| 12.1.15 ||**

**mauryā hy ete daśa nṛpāḥ sapta-triṁśac-chatottaram |**

**samā bhokṣyanti pṛthivīṁ kalau kuru-kulodvaha ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **teṣāṁ pañcamo daśarathaḥ pāraśarādibhir ukto’trāpy anusandheyaḥ | tena saha mauryā daśa | sapta-triṁśac-chatottaraṁ sapta-triṁśad-uttaraṁ śataṁ samāḥ ||15||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tatas tadanantarama | tasya somaśarmaṇaḥ | tattasmāta śatadhanvanaḥ| mauryā maravaṁśajāḥ hīnajātayaḥ kaivartāḥ muro daityaviśeṣe ca kaivarte cauṣadhe striyām iti kośāt | saptatriṁśacchatottaram 137 rājyābdāḥ ||15||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** rājā sapta-triṁśad-uttaraṁ śataṁ samāḥ ||15||

 **...**

**|| 12.1.16 ||**[^3]

**hatvā bṛhad-rathaṁ mauryaṁ tasya senāpatiḥ kalau |**

**puṣyamitras tu śuṅgāhvaḥ svayaṁ rājyaṁ kariṣyati ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **bṛhad-rathasya senāpatiḥ puṣyamitro nāma svāminaṁ bṛhad-rathaṁ hatvā rājyaṁ kariṣyati | sa ca śuṅgānāṁ prathamaḥ ||16|| 

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **he kurukulamūrddhvavamādhikyaṁ prāpayatīti tathā, bhavatā tu kurukulakīrtirādhikyaṁ nīto'tastvādṛśām eva rājñāṁ bhavanamucitam iti bhāvaḥ | atra ṭīkānusāreṇa—


    hatvā bṛhadrathaṁ mauryaṁ tasya senāpatiḥ kalau | 


    puṣpamitras tu śuṅgāhvaḥ svayaṁ rājyaṁ kariṣyati ||

iti ślokopi kacitpustakeṣu dṛśyate | tasmādagnimitrāt | atha sujyeṣṭhāt ||16||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **bṛhad-rathasya senāpatiḥ svāminaṁ rājyaṁ kariṣyati | sa puṣyamitro nāma śuṅgānāṁ prathamaḥ ||16||

**...**

**||** **12.1.17-19 ||**

**agnimitras tatas tasmāt sujyeṣṭho bhavitā tataḥ |**

**vasumitro bhadrakaś ca pulindo bhavitā sutaḥ ||**

**tato ghoṣaḥ sutas tasmād vajramitro bhaviṣyati |**

**tato bhāgavatas tasmād devabhūtiḥ kurūdvaha ||**

**śuṅgā daśaite bhokṣyanti bhūmiṁ varṣa-śatādhikam |**

**tataḥ kāṇvān iyaṁ bhūmir yāsyaty alpa-guṇān nṛpa ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tato’gni-mitrādayo navety evaṁ śuṅgā daśa-varṣa-śatādhikaṁ dvādaśādhikaṁ varṣa-śatam ||17-19||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **vasumitrastato bhadrakastataḥ pulindaḥ| tataḥ pulindāt | tasmādvoṣāt || tataḥ puṣpamitrāt | tato vajramitrāt | ete śuṅgā daśavarṣaśatāni dvādaśādhikāni 1012 bhokṣyatīttham api kecidvyākhyānti ||17-19||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **tato’gni-mitrādayo navety evaṁ śuṅgā daśa-varṣa-śatādhikaṁ dvādaśādhikaṁ varṣa-śatam ||17-19||

 **...**

**|| 12.1.20 ||**

**śuṅgaṁ hatvā devabhūtiṁ kāṇvo’mātyas tu kāminam |**

**svayaṁ kariṣyate rājyaṁ vasudevo mahā-matiḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kathaṁ kaṇvān yāsyati ? tad āha—śuṅgam iti | para-strī-kāminaṁ devabhūti-nāmānaṁ śuṅgaṁ hatvā tad-amātyo vasudeva-nāmā kaṇvo rājyaṁ kariṣyati ||20||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tasya vasudevasya | tasya bhūmitrasya | atha tato nārāyaṇādanantaram ||20||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **kathaṁ kaṇvān yāsyati ? tad āha—śuṅgam iti | para-strī-kāminaṁ devabhūti-nāmānaṁ śuṅgaṁ hatvā ||20||

 **...**

**|| 12.1.21 ||**

**tasya putras tu bhūmitras tasya nārāyaṇaḥ sutaḥ |**

**nārāyaṇasya bhavitā suśarmā nāma viśrutaḥ ||**[^4]

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kāṇvānāṁ caturthaḥ suśarmā jñeyaḥ ||21||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** _na vyākhyātam._

 **...**

**|| 12.1.22 ||**

**kāṇvāyanā ime bhūmiṁ catvāriṁśac ca pañca ca |**

**śatāni trīṇi bhokṣyanti varṣāṇāṁ ca kalau yuge ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ime vasudevādayaḥ kāṇvāyanā varṣāṇāṁ trīṇi śatāni pañca-catvāriṁśad-varṣāṇi ca bhūmiṁ bhokṣyanti ||22||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **paścacatvāriṁśaduttaraśatatrayaṁ 345 rājyābdāḥ ||21-22||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **vasudevādayaḥ kāṇvāyanāḥ ||22||

 **...**

**|| 12.1.23 ||**

**hatvā kāṇvaṁ suśarmāṇaṁ tad-bhṛtyo vṛṣalo balī |**

**gāṁ bhokṣyaty andhra-jātīyaḥ kañcit kālam asattamaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kāṇvānām antimaṁ suśarmāṇaṁ hatvā balī-nāmā tad bhṛtyo gāṁ bhokṣyati ||23||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tadbhratā balibhrātā | tatputraḥ kṛṣṇaputraḥ | tatsutaḥ śrīśāntakarṇasutaḥ ||23||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **suśarmāṇam iti kāṇvānām antimaḥ suśarmā jñeyaḥ | balī bali-saṁjñaḥ ||23||

 **...**

**|| 12.1.24-26 ||**

**kṛṣṇa-nāmātha tad-bhrātā bhavitā pṛthivī-patiḥ |**

**śrī-śāntakarṇas tat-putraḥ paurṇamāsas tu tat-sutaḥ ||**

**lambodaras tu tat-putras tasmāc cibilako nṛpaḥ |**

**meghasvātiś cibilakād aṭamānas tu tasya ca ||**

**aniṣṭakarmā hāleyas talakas tasya cātma-jaḥ |**

**purīṣabhīrus tat-putras tato rājā sunandanaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** _na vyākhyātam._

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tatputraḥ paurṇamāsaputraḥ | tasmāllambodarāt | tasya meghasvāteḥ || tasya ceti cakārāt tasyāṭamānasyāniṣṭakarmā, tasya ca hāleyaḥ, tasya hāleyasya | tatputrastalakaputraḥ | tataḥ purīṣabhīroḥ || bahavo bahusaṁjñāḥ | aṣṭasu caramo'ṣṭama eva | tasya śivasvāteḥ | tato gomatinaḥ ||24-26||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **aniṣṭa-karmeti hāleyasya[^5] viśeṣaṇam ||26||

 **...**

**|| 12.1.27 ||**

**cakoro bahavo yatra śivasvātir arin-damaḥ |**

**tasyāpi gomatī putraḥ purīmān bhavitā tataḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **yatra yeṣu bahu-saṁjñeṣv aṣṭasu caramaḥ śivasvāti-nāmā bhavitā ||27||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tataḥ purīmato medaśirāḥ, tataḥ śivaskandhasutaḥ tato yajñaśriyaḥ | tatsuto vijayasutaḥ | bhāvyo bhaviṣyati | tataścandravijñātsa prasiddho lomadhiḥ, sakārasahito vā nāma ||27||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **yatra yeṣu aṣṭasu anukteṣu navamaḥ śiva-svātir ity arthaḥ | iti dvāviṁśatiḥ | gaumatī-putra-purīmantau dvau ||27||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** āvabhṛtyā avabhṛtir nagarī tatra bhavāḥ ||27||

 **...**

**|| 12.1.28-29 ||**

**medaśirāḥ śivaskando yajñaśrīs tat-sutas tataḥ |**

**vijayas tat-suto bhāvyaś candravijñaḥ sa-lomadhiḥ ||**

**ete triṁśan nṛpatayaś catvāry abda-śatāni ca |**

**ṣaṭ-pañcāśac ca pṛthivīṁ bhokṣyanti kuru-nandana ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **he kurunandaneti—tvaṁ tu bhagavad-bhaktatvātkurukulam eva nandayasi gaṇitanṛpās tu svātmanandakā api neti bhāvaḥ | ṣaṭpañcāśaduttaracatuśśataṁ 456 rājyābdāḥ || gardabhino gardabhisaṁjñakāḥ | kaṅkāḥ kaṅkasaṁjñāḥ | lolupā lampaṭāḥ ||28-29||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **anye bālyādival lomadhi-paryantāḥ pṛthak pṛthag anyā[^6] iti triṁśat ||27||

 **...**

**|| 12.1.30 ||**

**saptābhīrā āvabhṛtyā daśa gardabhino nṛpāḥ |**

**kaṅkāḥ ṣoḍaśa bhū-pālā bhaviṣyanty ati-lolupāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **āvabhṛtyāḥ avabhṛtir nagarī tad rājānaḥ ||30||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tataḥ kaṅkebhyaḥ paścāt | yavanā mlecchāḥ | puṣkasā niṣādācchūdryudbhūtāḥ guruṇḍā guruṇḍasaṁjñāḥ, gurugururityevaṁ ḍuvanti bhāṣanta iti guruṇḍāḥ—


    ḍū—bhāṣaṇe tudādirvyākaraṇāntarajñeya, tata auṇādikā ḍakhpratyayaḥ auṇādiko aparibhitāḥ prayogamanusṛtya prayoktavyāḥ | ity-ukteḥ |

dhātūnāmapyanantatvānnānārthatvāc ca sarvathā ityanubhūtyuktarḍūr apy ūdanto dhātuḥ kalpanīyaḥ ||30||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **āvabhṛtyāḥ avabhṛtir nagarī tatra bhavāḥ ||30||

 **...**

**|| 12.1.31 ||**

**tato’ṣṭau yavanā bhāvyāś caturdaśa turuṣkakāḥ |**

**bhūyo daśa guruṇḍāś ca maulā ekādaśaiva tu ||**

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **kiṁ ca—duryodhanajanmanyeva kalerārambhaḥ, tadvarṣottaraṁ kṛṣṇāvirbhāvaḥ, tato navativarṣottaraṁ parīkṣijjanma, tato nandābhiṣekāvadhi pañcadaśaśataṁ daśa ca, tanmilitvaikādhikaṣoḍaśaśatam | tato navanandānāṁ śatam, mauryāṇāṁ saptatriṁśaduttaraśataṁ ca, śuṅgānāṁ dvādaśādhikaṁ daśavarṣaśatam, kāṇvāyanānāṁ trīṇi śatāni pañcacatvāriṁśacca, balyāditriṁśadrājñāṁ catvāri śatāni, saptābhīrādīnāṁ ṣaṭpañcāśattriṇi śatāni ca tato yavanādiguruṇḍāntānāṁ sahasraṁ navanavatyadhikaṁ ca, evaṁ pañcādaśādhikapañcasahasra 5050 varṣāṇi jātāni | tatra taṭṭīkāpraṇayanakālikavikramārkaśaranigamanadendu 1945 mitābdaparyantaṁ kaleścatuḥ— sahasranavaśataikonanavatisaṅkhyāni varṣāṇyatītānīti ṭīkāntarānurodhādanusandheyam ||31||

 **...**

**|| 12.1.32-33 ||**

**ete bhokṣyanti pṛthivīṁ daśa varṣa-śatāni ca |**

**navādhikāṁ ca navatiṁ maulā ekādaśa kṣitim ||**

**bhokṣyanty abda-śatāny aṅga trīṇi taiḥ saṁsthite tataḥ |**

**kilakilāyāṁ nṛpatayo bhūtanando’tha vaṅgiriḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ete ābhīrādayo maula-vyatiriktāḥ pañca-ṣaṣṭi-nṛpā ekona-śatādhikaṁ varṣa-sahasraṁ pṛthivīṁ bhokṣyanti | tataḥ pūrvoktā evaikādaśa maulās trīṇy abda-śatāni kṣitiṁ bhokṣyanti ||32|| 

taiḥ saṁsthite teṣu mṛteṣu kilikilāyāṁ puryāṁ nṛpatayo bhaviṣyantīty uttareṇānvayaḥ ||33||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tata etad-uktarājyottaram | tair iti saptamyarthe tṛtīyā, teṣvity arthaḥ | saṁsthite ityekatvam api bahutve, saṁsthiteṣvity arthaḥ || tadbhrātā yaśonandibhrātā ||32-33||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **ete maula-vyatiriktāḥ | maulās tv ekādaśa | trīṇy abda-śatāni | tair maulaiḥ saṁsthite mṛte sati | kilakilāyāṁ puryām ||32-33||

 **...**

**|| 12.1.34 ||**

**śiśunandiś ca tad-bhrātā yaśonandiḥ pravīrakaḥ |**

**ity ete vai varṣa-śataṁ bhaviṣyanty adhikāni ṣaṭ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **adhikāni ṣaḍ-varṣāṇi ca ||34||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **ṣaṭ-varṣāṇy adhikāni bhaviṣyanti bhāvīni vyāpya bhokṣyanti pālayiṣyanti ||34||

 **...**

**|| 12.1.35-36 ||**

**teṣāṁ trayodaśa sutā bhavitāraś ca bāhlikaḥ |**

**puṣpamitro’tha rājanyo durmitro’sya tathaiva ca ||**

**eka-kālā ime bhū-pāḥ saptāndhrāḥ sapta kauśalāḥ |**

**vidūra-patayo bhāvyā niṣadhās tata eva hi ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **teṣāṁ bhūtanandādīnāṁ yathā-yathaṁ bāhlika-nāmānas trayodaśa sutā bhaviṣyanti | atha puṣpamitro nāmānyo rājanyaḥ | asya ca durmitro nāma putraḥ ||35||

tathā āndhrāḥ kośalā vidūra-patayo niṣadhāś ca ete ca tat tad deśa-nāmabhiḥ prakhyātās tulya-kālāḥ khaṇḍa-maṇḍaleṣu bhūpās tata eva tebhyo bāhlikebhya eva bhāvyā bhaviṣyanti ||36||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **atha vāhlikarājyānantaram || ity artha iti—pulindādīnhīnajātīneva | brāhmaṇādisthāne sthāpayiṣyati, brāhmaṇādikarma taiḥ kārayiṣyatīti bhāvaḥ ||34-36||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **teṣāṁ bhūta-nandādīnāṁ trayodaśa bāhlika-nāmāno bhaviṣyanti | athety anya eva puṣyamitraḥ kṣatriyo’sya durmitro nāma putraḥ ||35|| eka-kālāḥ khaṇḍa-maṇḍala-patayaḥ ||36||

**...**

**|| 12.1.37 ||**

**māgadhānāṁ tu bhavitā viśvasphūrjiḥ purañjayaḥ |**

**kariṣyaty aparo varṇān pulinda-yadu-madrakān ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tataś ca māgadhānāṁ tu rājā viśvasphūrjir nāma bhavitā | sa cāpūrvoktāt purañjayād aparaḥ purañjaya iti prasiddhaḥ san varṇān brāhmaṇādīn pulinda-yadu-madraka-saṁjñān mleccha-prāyān kariṣyati | aparān iti pāṭhe anyān pulindādi-saṁjñān varṇān kariṣyatīty arthaḥ ||37||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **sa purañjayaḥ | kṣatraṁ kṣatriyajātimutsādya nāśayitvā yatra kutra sthitaṁ guptam api kṣatraṁ yathākathañcinnāśayiṣyatīty arthaḥ ||37||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **tataś ca māgadhānāṁ madhye kaścid viśvasphūrji-nāma purāṇāṁ jetā paraḥ pracīnaḥ purañjayo dvitīya ivety arthaḥ | varṇān brāhmaṇādīn pulinda-yadu-madraka-saṁjñān mleccha-prāyān kariṣyati ||37||

 **...**

**|| 12.1.38 ||**

**prajāś cābrahma-bhūyiṣṭhāḥ sthāpayiṣyati durmatiḥ |**

**vīryavān kṣatram utsādya padmavatyāṁ sa vai purī ||**

**anu-gaṅgam ā-prayāgaṁ guptāṁ bhokṣyati medinīm**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kiṁ caivaṁ kṛtvābrahma-bhūyiṣṭhā atraivarṇyāpracurāḥ satīḥ prajāḥ sthāpayiṣyati pālayiṣyati | sa ca padmavatyāṁ puri vasan anugaṅgāṁ gaṅgā-dvāram ārabhya prayāga-paryantaṁ guptāṁ pālitāṁ medinīṁ bhokṣyati ||38||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **vrātyaḥ saṁskārahīnaḥ syāt ity amaraḥ | prāyapadena kvacitkṣatraparā api bhaviṣyantītyasūci ||38||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **abrahma-bhūyiṣṭhā veda-rahitā bahutarāḥ | kṣetraṁ puṇya-kṣetram utsādya utsannaṁ kṛtvā ||38||

 **...**

**|| 12.1.39 ||**

**saurāṣṭrāvanty-ābhīrāś ca śūrā arbuda-mālavāḥ |**

**vrātyā dvijā bhaviṣyanti śūdra-prāyā janādhipāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tad-anantaraṁ ca saurāṣṭrādi-deśa-vartino dvijā vrātyā upanayana-rahitā bhaviṣyanti ||39||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **sindhunāmnī nadī, samudraś ca | kauntīpuram | abrahmavarcasaḥ brāhmaṇabhaktihīnāḥ varcastejasi sevane iti niruktiḥ ||39||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **tataś ca saurāṣṭrādi-deśa-vartino dvijā vrātyāḥ saṁskāra-hīnā bhaviṣyanti ||39||

 **...**

**|| 12.1.40 ||**

**sindhos taṭaṁ candrabhāgāṁ kauntīṁ kāśmīra-maṇḍalam |**

**bhokṣyanti śūdrā vrātyādyā mlecchāś cābrahma-varcasaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **abrahma-varcaso vedācāra-śūnyāḥ ||40||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ime āṅghrādyāḥ | mlecchaprāyāḥ śāstrāsvīkārāt ||40||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.1.41 ||**

**tulya-kālā ime rājan mleccha-prāyāś ca bhūbhṛtaḥ |**

**ete’dharmānṛta-parāḥ phalgu-dās tīvra-manyavaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ime ca mleccha-prāyā bhūbhṛtas tulya-kālā bhaviṣyanti | kiṁ ca, ete sarve’dharmānṛta-parā adharme’nṛte ca pariniṣṭhitāḥ phalgu-dā alpa-dātāraḥ ||41||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **uditāstamitaprāyā alpakālasthitimantaḥ ||41||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.1.42 ||**

**strī-bāla-go-dvija-ghnāś ca para-dāra-dhanādṛtāḥ |**

**uditāsta-mita-prāyā alpa-sattvālpakāyuṣaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **uditāsta-mita-prāyā harṣa-śokādi-bahulāḥ ||42||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **śāstrāvihitakartṛtve sati gohisādiparatvaṁ mlecchatvam, tadvanto mlecchāḥ ||42||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.1.43 ||**

**asaṁskṛtāḥ kriyā-hīnā rajasā tamasāvṛtāḥ |**

**prajās te bhakṣayiṣyanti mlecchā rājanya-rūpiṇaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **asaṁskṛtā garbhādhānādi-saṁskāra-rahitāḥ | prajā bhakṣayiṣyanti dhanādy-apahārādinā pīḍayiṣyanti ||43||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **anyattatsaṅgakṛtānartham āha—tannāthā iti 43 kiñcidbailakṣaṇyenaidadhyāyārtho bhaviṣye'pi brahmaṇā kārttikeyaṁ prati varṇitaḥ | tathā hi—


    kalau ke cai bhaviṣyanti nṛpacihnayutā narāḥ | 


    jñātumicchāmi teṣāṁ tu nāmānīha jagadguro ||1||


    te vai rājyaṁ kariṣyati kati varṣāṇi tatra hi | 


    brahmannetatsamācakṣva paraṁ kautūhalaṁ hi me ||2|| 


    brahmovāca | satyādikeṣu bahuśaḥ śrutā bhūpāstvayā guha | 


    śṛṇu vakṣye kaliyuge saṅkṣepaṁ puruṣottama ||3|| 


    pāṇḍavānāṁ kulotpannā viṣṇurātādikā nṛpāḥ | 


    ikṣvākuvaṁśajā bhūpāste māgaghavaṁśajāḥ ||4|| 


    kalau rājyaṁ kariṣyanti varṣāṇāṁ vai sahasrakam | 


    kalisandhyā samārabhya rājyametattrayaṁ smṛtam ||5|| 


    tato nṛpā bhaviṣyanti pañca pradyotasaṁjñakāḥ | 


    aṣṭatriṁśottaraśataṁ kalau te rājyakārakāḥ ||6|| 


    śiśunāgā daśa nṛpāḥ ṣaṣṭyuttaraśatatrayam | 


    kalau bhokṣyanti pṛthivīṁ rājāno dharmatatparāḥ ||7|| 


    ataḥ paraṁ nṛpā loke śūdraprāyāstvadhārmikāḥ | 


    śiśunāgatpare rājye śūdrīgarbhodbhavo balī ||8|| 


    mahāpadmadharaḥ kaścinnando rājyaṁ kariṣyati | 


    nandasya cāṣṭaṁ putrāś ca bhaviṣyanti ca bhūmipāḥ | 


    teṣāṁ tu vaśagā bhūmirbhaviṣyati śataṁ samāḥ ||9|| 


    abrahmaṇyāndvijaḥ kacidduṣṭānnaṁdasutānatha | 


    ayogyā iti matvā tu rājyāttānuddhariṣyati ||10|| 


    arājake tu jagatīṁ vipradattaṁ kalau yuge | 


    bhokṣyati daśa mauryāś ca saptatriṁśottaraṁ śatam ||11|| 


    tataḥ śuṅgā daśa nṛpā daśavarṣaśatādhikama | 


    kalau rājyaṁ kariṣyanti vikhyātāḥ sarvato diśi ||12|| 


    kaṇvo hatvā nṛpaṁ śuṅgaṁ rājyalobhena svāminam | 


    svayaṁ kariṣyate rājyaṁ vasudeveti viśrutaḥ ||13|| 


    tatputrapautrāḥ pṛthivīṁ catvāriṁśacca pañca ca | 


    śatāni trīṇi varṣāṇāṁ bhokṣyanti ca kalau yuge ||14|| 


    tadbhṛtyastvandhrajātīyaḥ kañcitkālamuśattama | 


    cakāra rājyaṁ hatvā vai kāṇvaṁ tu vṛkalo balī ||15|| 


    tasya vaṁśodbhavāstriśadbhaviṣyanti kalau nṛpāḥ | 


    bhokṣyantyāndhrās tu pṛthivī catvāryadvaśatāni ca ||16|| 


    ṣaṭpañcāśottaraṁ kālaṁ paraṁ tasmānnibodha me | 


    saptābhīrāś ca pṛthivīṁ bhokṣyāntyadvaśata kalau ||17|| 


    tato nṛpā bhaviṣyanti daśa gardabhisaṁjñakāḥ | 


    aṣṭādhikāṁ ca navatiṁ teṣāṁ rājyaṁ bhaviṣyati ||18|| 


    kaṅkā ṣoḍaśa bhūpālā bhavaṣyanti kalau guha | 


    pālayiṣyanti gāṁ te vai varṣāṇāṁ ca śatadvayam ||19|| 


    tato va vikramo nāma bhavitojjayinīpatiḥ | 


    yo vai mlechānsusampannānkoṭiśo nihaniṣyati ||20|| 


    tasya rājyaṁ kalau skandha pañcaviṁśottaraṁ śatam | 


    bhaviṣyati pare kāle śālivāhastato nṛpaḥ ||21|| 


    śataṁ varṣāṇi pṛthivīṁ bhokṣyatyavitathodyamaḥ | 


    tato'ṣṭau yavanā bhāvyāsturuṣkā vai caturdaśa | 


    varṣāṇi caiva pṛthivīṁ bhākṣyānta śivanandana ||22|| 


    bhūyaḥ kalau bhaviṣyanti maunā ekādaśaiva tu | 


    te vai bhokṣyanti pṛthivīṁ varṣāṇāṁ ca śatatrayam ||23|| 


    kilakilāyāṁ tato jātā bhūrānandādayo nṛpāḥ | 


    kalau rājyaṁ kariṣyanti pañcādhikaśataṁ samāḥ ||24|| 


    ete kalau sārvabhaumāḥ khaṇḍarājyamataḥ param | 


    teṣāṁ trayodaśa sutā bhaviṣyanti ca vāhlikāḥ ||25|| 


    tataḥ paraṁ saptasapta kauśalāndhrāś ca kīrtitāḥ | 


    vaidūrapatayo bhāvyā naiṣadhāstadanantaram ||26|| 


    viśvasphūrtiś ca bhavitā kariṣyatyanyathā janān | 


    tīvramanyuḥ sarvavarṇānmlecchaprāyānkariṣyati ||27|| 


    tasminkāle sindhutīraṁ kauntīṁ kāśmīramaṇadaḍalam | 


    bhokṣyanti brāhmaṇāḥ śūdrā mlecchāścābrahmavarcasaḥ ||28|| 


    mlecchaprāyā ime bhūpāḥ phalgudāstībramanyavaḥ | 


    alpāyuṣo'lpasattvāś ca bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge ||29|| 


    prajāste bhakṣayiṣyanti mlecchā rājanyarūpiṇaḥ | 


    anyonyato rājabhiś ca kṣayaṁ yāsyanti vai prajāḥ ||30|| 


    ete bhokṣyanti pṛthivīṁ dvādaśorddhacatuṣṭayam | 


    evaṁ vai dharmaprādharṣyaṁ bhaviṣyati kalau yadā ||31|| 


    bhaviṣyati tadā skanda brahmajñānaikamānasaḥ | 


    tasyopadiṣṭaṁ mārgaṁ vai grahīṣyanti ca ye janāḥ ||32|| 


    te vai rājya kariṣyanti tasya śikṣānusārataḥ | 


    dharmeṇa rājyavṛddhiś ca kalau teṣāṁ bhaviṣyati ||33|| 


    yadā vede ca vipre ca vaiṣṇave ca parāṅmukhāḥ | 


    tadā teṣāṁ kṣayaḥ skanda bhaviṣyatyacireṇa hi ||34|| 


    teṣāṁ rājyātpare kāle mlecchā gauramukhā nṛpāḥ | 


    prabalāḥ sambhaviṣyanti prajāpālanatatparāḥ ||35|| 


    alpakālena teṣāṁ vai rājyavṛddhirbhaviṣyati | 


    nṛpā baliṁ hariṣyanti gauravarṇānugākhilāḥ ||36|| 


    aśītiśatavarṣaṁ te rājyaṁ nītyanusārataḥ| kṛtvā paścimadeśīyair nṛṣair yasyantyadarśanam ||37|| 


    yadā vedeṣu vipreṣu vaiṣṇaveṣu ca śudvadhīḥ | 


    tadā nṛpā vijeṣyanti mlecchāndharmaparāṅmukhān ||38|| 


    tasminkāle khaṇḍanārthe śataśaś ca sahasraśaḥ | 


    bhaviṣyanti kalau skanda rājyapālanatatparāḥ ||39|| 


    dharmaścaiva kalau skanda tataḥ saṁsthā gamiṣyati | 


    kiñcitkālāntare bhūyo bhavitā vijayo nṛpaḥ ||40|| 


    teṣāṁ kule samutpanno dharmajñānakatatparaḥ | 


    tasya vaṁśodbhavā bhūpāḥ kalau pañcaśatāni te | 


    varṣāṇi vai kariṣyanti rājyaṁ pañcāśaduttaram ||41|| 


    ataḥ paraṁ rohitake pattane sambhaviṣyati | 


    kalau nāgārjuno nāma nṛpacihnayutaratadā ||42|| 


    tadvaṁśe rājyabhogas tu varṣāṇāṁ vai sahasrakam | 


    tasmātparaṁ balirnāma nṛpo ve sbhaviṣyati ||43|| 


    tasya vaṁśodbhavā bhūpāḥ sahasrāṇi śatādhikam | 


    varṣāṇi te kalau skanda nṛpā rājyakarāḥ smṛtāḥ ||44|| 


    ataḥ paraṁ kaliyuge nṛpāḥ śūdrādayaḥ smṛtāḥ | 


    mlecchaprāyā janapadā bhaviṣyanti kalau guha ||45|| 


    ekībhūtaṁ jagatsarvaṁ mlecchajñānaikasaṁsthitam | 


    dṛṣṭvā cādharmabāhulyaṁ viṣṇuḥ kalkirbhaviṣyati ||46|| 


    āśugaṁ hayamāruhya mlecchānvai sa vadhiṣyati | 


    tataḥ kṛtayugaṁ bhūyo bhaviṣyati śivātmaja ||47|| 


    evaṁ kalau mayā proktā nṛpacihnayutā narāḥ | 


    samāsenava te skanda kiṁ bhūyaḥ śrotumicchasi ||48|| 

iti bhaviṣye caturthakalpe ||43||

iti śrīmad-bhāgavata-bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśe dvādaśa-skandhe prathamo'dhyāyaḥ ||1||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.1.44 ||**

**tan-nāthās te janapadās tac-chīlācāra-vādinaḥ |**

**anyonyato rājabhiś ca kṣayaṁ yāsyanti pīḍitāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kiṁ ca, tan-nāthāḥ te nāthā yeṣāṁ te janapadā deśa-vartino manuṣyās tac-chīlācāra-vādinas teṣām iva śīlam ācāro vādaś ca tadvantaḥ ||44||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

iti sārārtha-darśinyāṁ harṣiṇyāṁ bhakta-cetasām |

dvādaśe prathamo’dhyāyaḥ saṅgataḥ saṅgataḥ satām ||*||

 **...**


    iti śrīmad-bhāgavate mahā-purāṇe brahma-sūtra-bhāṣye pāramahaṁsyaṁ saṁhitāyāṁ vaiyāsikyāṁ dvādaśa-skandhe 


    rāja-vaṁśānukīrtanaṁ nāma 


    prathamo’dhyāyaḥ |

|| 12.1 ||

**...**

**(12.2)**

**atha dvitīyo’dhyāyaḥ**


## kali-dharmaḥ

**|| 12.2.1 ||**

**śrī-śuka uvāca—**

**tataś cānudinaṁ dharmaḥ satyaṁ śaucaṁ kṣamā dayā |**

**kālena balinā rājan naṅkṣaty āyur balaṁ smṛtiḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :**

dvitīye tu kaler doṣa-vṛddhau kalky-avatārataḥ |

adharmiṣṭhe jane naṣṭe punaḥ kṛta-yugāgamaḥ ||

kali-dharmān prapañcayati—tataś cety-ādinā ||1||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **satyayugāgamaḥ| kṛtayugāgamaḥ | tataḥ kalikṛtaprajākṣayaprāpteḥ | anudinaṁ pratyaham | he rājann iti—yathā rājā tathā prajā iti nyāyena yathā tvadīyarājye dharmādīnāṁ vṛddhis tathā kalirājye dharmādihrāsaśceti bhāvaḥ ||1||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :**

dvitīye tu kalau nṝṇāṁ janmācāra-guṇodayaḥ |

kaler vṛddhi-parijñānaṁ tad-ante satyam ucyate ||

kali-doṣān āha—tata iti ||1||

 **...**

**|| 12.2.2 ||**

**vittam eva kalau nṝṇāṁ janmācāra-guṇodayaḥ |**

**dharma-nyāya-vyavasthāyāṁ kāraṇaṁ balam eva hi ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **dharma-nyāyayor vyavasthāyāṁ balam eva ||2||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **janmādyutkarṣaheturna tu brāhmaṇatvādir iti bhāvaḥ | 


    yasyāsti vittaṁ sa naraḥ kulīnaḥ sa paṇḍitaḥ sa śrutavān guṇajñaḥ | 


    sa eva vaktā sa ca darśanīyaḥ sarve guṇāḥ kāñcanamāśrayanti | 

iti bhartṛharyukteḥ | dharmanyāyayorvyavasthāyāmayaṁ dharmo'yaṁ nyāya iti nirṇaye kartavye yo dhanādinā balī tasyaiva vākyaṁ dharmo nyāyaśceti lokā maṁsyantīty arthaḥ ||2||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** vittam eveti | yasya vittaṁ vartate, sa eva sat-kula-janmā, sa eva sad-ācāraḥ, sa eva sad-guṇa ity evāgre vyākhyeyam ||2||

 **...**

**|| 12.2.3 ||**

**dāmpatye’bhirucir hetur māyaiva vyāvahārike |**

**strītve puṁstve ca hi ratir vipratve sūtram eva hi ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **dāmpatye bhāryā-pati-bhāve’bhirucir eva hetur na kula-gotrādiḥ | vyāvahārike kraya-vikrayādau | strītve puṁstve ca tayoḥ śraiṣṭhye rati-kauśalam eva hetur na kulam ācāro vā ||3||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **dampatibhāve vivāhe—


    kuśaviprāmbupitragnivedabhūkāladiksurāḥ | 


    sākṣye yatra vivāhe tu taddāmpatyamudīritam | iti nāradīyoktam | 

kuśaviprādīnvinaiva vivāhā bhaviṣntīty arthaḥ | māyaiva kapaṭam eva | sūtraṁ tantumātram eva na tu nityanaimittikānuṣṭhānasvādhyāyādi, brāhmaṇo'haṁ dṛśyatāṁ matkaṇṭhe sūtramityevaṁ svīyavipratvaṁ sūcayiṣyanti na tu vedoccāraṇādineti bhāvaḥ | yajñasūtram iti vaktavye sūtramity uktyā tasya mantranirmitatvādyabhāvena kevalaṁ kartanayantrādigatasūtratulyataiva dhvanitā | tad uktam—


    anadhyāyakṛtaṁ yacca tathā mantravivarjitam | aviprapatnīsūtrotthamavīrāsūtranirmitam | 


    grāmamadhye kṛtaṁ yacca bhuktvā caiva kṛtaṁ tu yat | 


    abrāhmaṇakṛtaṁ yaccāśucinā nirmitaṁ tu yat | 

tatsūtraṁ vibudhair jñeyaṁ paśubandhanarajjuvat || iti nirṇayasudhākare ||3||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.2.4 ||**

**liṅgam evāśrama-khyātāv anyonyāpatti-kāraṇam |**

**avṛttyā nyāya-daurbalyaṁ pāṇḍitye cāpalaṁ vacaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **āśramāṇāṁ khyātau jñāne liṅgam eva daṇḍājinādikaṁ hetur na tv ācāra-viśeṣaḥ | anyonyāpatti-kāraṇaṁ cāśramād āśramāntara-prāptau ca kāraṇam | yad vā,  bahūdaka-haṁsādīnām anyonyāpattau namaskārādi-vyavahāre kāraṇam | avṛttyā mudrārpaṇādi-dānāsāmarthyena nyāye daurbalyaṁ parājayaḥ | cāpalaṁ vaco bahu-bhāṣaṇam ||4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **anyonyaṁ viprā namante ity-ādy-uktyā sajātīyeṣvevānyonyādiprayogadarśanādvijātīyabrahmacaryasannyāsādau tatkathaṁ prayuktaṁ tatrāha—tadveti ||4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **anyonyāpattau .parasparam utkarṣāpakarṣa-prāptau liṅgam eva daṇḍājina-śikhā-tyāgādikam eva kāraṇaṁ, na tu jñāna-sad-ācārādikam | avṛttyā mūdrādy-arpaṇā-sāmarthyenaiva hetunā nyāya-daurbalyaṁ nyāye parājayaḥ | cāpalaṁ vacaḥ cāpalya-yuktaṁ bhāṣaṇam ||4||

 **...**

**|| 12.2.5 ||**

**anāḍhyataivāsādhutve sādhutve dambha eva tu |**

**svī-kāra eva codvāhe snānam eva prasādhanam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **asādhutve cauryādy-abhiyoge | prasādhanam alaṅkāraḥ ||5||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **abhiyogaḥ prāpaṇam, duṣṭatva ity arthaḥ | tvaṁ me bhāryeti svīkārahetuḥ | prasādhanaṁ śarīraśuddhiralaṅkāro veti tīrthaḥ | udvāhe vivāhasthāne svīkārastvaṁ me bhāryetyaṅgīkaraṇam eva na tu pitrādikartṛkārpaṇam | alaṅkārasthāne kevalaṁ snānam eva na tu svarṇādi, ghore kalau svarṇādyaprāptagranthāntarokteḥ ||5||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.2.6 ||**

**dūre vāry-ayanaṁ tīrthaṁ lāvaṇyaṁ keśa-dhāraṇam |**

**udaram-bharatā svārthaḥ satyatve dhārṣṭyam eva hi ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **dūre vartamānaṁ vāryayanaṁ jalāśayas tīrthaṁ, na tu gurv-ādi | svārthaḥ puruṣārthaḥ ||6||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **

tīrtha mukhyaṁ pitā mātā guruḥ śāstraṁ tathā hariḥ | 


    gauṇaṁ tīrthaṁ tvammayaṁ syād ity uktaṁ tīrthavedibhiḥ || iti | 

lāvaṇye śarīrasaundaryadyotanāya keśānāmitastataḥ prasādhanamātram eva bhaviṣyati vastrabhūṣādyanāpteḥ | udarabharaṇam eva puruṣārthaṁ maṁsyante na tu harismaraṇādikamity arthaḥ | dhārṣṭyaṁ vṛthā haṭhaḥ yo vṛthā haṭhaṁ kariṣyati taṁ satyavādinaṁ maṁsyanta ity arthaḥ ||6||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **lāvaṇye nimitte keśa-dhāraṇam eva kariṣyantīti saptamy-antānām anvayaḥ ||6||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** vāryayanaṁ jalāśayaḥ ||6||

 **...**

**|| 12.2.7-8 ||**

**dākṣyaṁ kuṭumba-bharaṇaṁ yaśo’rthe dharma-sevanam |**

**evaṁ prajābhir duṣṭābhir ākīrṇe kṣiti-maṇḍale ||**

**brahma-viṭ-kṣatra-śūdrāṇāṁ yo balī bhavitā nṛpaḥ |**

**prajā hi labdhai rājanyair nirghṛṇair dasyu-dharmabhiḥ ||**

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **dākṣyaṁ naipuṇyam | yaśortha iti—kalyāṇabuddhyā na kopi dharmaṁ kariṣyatīty arthaḥ || nirdhṛṇair nirdayaiḥ ||7-8||

 **...**

**|| 12.2.9-11 ||**

**ācchinna-dāra-draviṇā yāsyanti giri-kānanam |**

**śāka-mūlāmiṣa-kṣaudra-phala-puṣpāṣṭi-bhojanāḥ ||**

**anāvṛṣṭyā vinaṅkṣyanti durbhikṣa-kara-pīḍitāḥ |**

**śīta-vātātapa-prāvṛḍ-himair anyonyataḥ prajāḥ ||**

**kṣut-tṛḍbhyāṁ vyādhibhiś caiva santapsyante ca cintayā |**

**triṁśad viṁśati varṣāṇi paramāyuḥ kalau nṛṇām ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ācchinnā apahṛtā dārā draviṇāni ca yāsāṁ tāḥ | aṣṭir bījam ||9||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **āmiṣaṁ māṁsam, kṣaudraṁ madhu || kṣudhādibhiś ca naṅkṣyati | yad vā, triṁśatā sahitā viśatistriṁśadviśatiḥ, pañcāśad ity arthaḥ | paramāyuḥ ahopuṇyavānayamanena bahu jīvanaṁ prāptamity arthaḥ ||9-11||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ),** **viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.2.12 ||**

**kṣīyamāṇeṣu deheṣu dehināṁ kali-doṣataḥ |**

**varṇāśrama-vatāṁ dharme naṣṭe veda-pathe nṛṇām ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kṣīyamāṇeṣv ity-ādīnām itthaṁ kalau gata-prāya iti pañcamenānvayaḥ | kṣīyamāṇeṣv alpa-prāyeṣu ||12||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **kalerdoṣā asatyasambhāṣaṇādayastebhya ity arthaḥ ||12||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.2.13 ||**

**pāṣaṇḍa-pracure dharme dasyu-prāyeṣu rājasu |**

**caryānṛta-vṛthā-hiṁsā- nānā-vṛttiṣu vai nṛṣu ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **dasyu-prāyeṣu caura-tulyeṣu | cauryānṛta-vṛthāhiṁsādyā nānā-vṛttayo yeṣāṁ teṣu |

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **prāyaśabdārthastvatra tulyataiva | vṛthā hiṁsā pitrādyanuddiśya paśuhananam ||13||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.2.14 ||**

**śūdra-prāyeṣu varṇeṣu cchāga-prāyāsu dhenuṣu |**

**gṛha-prāyeṣv āśrameṣu yauna-prāyeṣu bandhuṣu ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **chāga-prāyāsu pramāṇataḥ kṣirataś cājātulyāsu |

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **āśrameṣu sannyāsādipu parigrahādinā gṛhasthatulyeṣu | yonisambandhena sambandhino yaunāḥ śvaśuraśyālādayastatprāyeṣu, prāyaśabdo'tra pradhāne śvasurādipradhāneṣu kartavyāthānusaṅghānātha śyālaśyālīpatyādīnāśrayiṣyantīti bhāvaḥ ||14||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.2.15 ||**

**aṇu-prāyāsv oṣadhīṣu śamī-prāyeṣu sthāsnuṣu |**

**vidyut-prāyeṣu megheṣu śūnya-prāyeṣu sadmasu ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **aṇu-prāyāsu śyāmāka-tulyāsu | sthāsnuṣu vṛkṣeṣu | vidyut-prāyeṣu taḍid-bahuleṣu | śūnya-prāyeṣu dharmādi-rahiteṣu sadmasu gṛheṣu ||15||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **oṣadhyo yavagodhūmavrīhyādyāḥ | aṇuprāyāsu śyāmākatulyāsu | yad vā, oṣadhīṣa harītakyādiṣu, aṇuprāyāsu niṣphalāsu tṛṇaprāyāsu—


    oṣadhyo yavavrīhyādyāḥ śivādyā api kīrtitāḥ | 


    aṇuvrīhiviśeṣe nā tṛṇasūkṣmāphaleṣu ca tucche mānaviśeṣe ca | iti kośāt | 

śamīsaktuphalā, sā cālpavṛkṣajātiḥ, yatkāṣṭhe yajñe'gnimathana kriyate yājñikeḥ vṛkṣeṣu vaṭā—śvatthādiṣu chāyādyabhāvena śamītulyeṣvity arthaḥ ||15||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **sthāsnuṣu vṛkṣeṣu ||15||

 **...**

**|| 12.2.16 ||**

**itthaṁ kalau gata-prāye janeṣu khara-dharmiṣu |**

**dharma-trāṇāya sattvena bhagavān avatariṣyati ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **jane tu khara-dharmiṇi duḥsaha-ceṣṭite kalau gata-prāye samāpta-prāye ||16||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **kvacit jane tu iti pāṭhastatra kharadharmiṇīti tadviśeṣaṇam | kharo rāsabhastaddharmo nirjalamaithunakaśmalāśanādilakṣaṇastadvati satīty arthaḥ | kvacit teṣu kharadharmiṣu iti pāṭhaḥ ||16||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.2.17 ||**

**carācara-guror viṣṇor īśvarasyākhilātmanaḥ |**

**dharma-trāṇāya sādhūnāṁ janma karmāpanuttaye ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **etat prapañcayati caturbhiḥ—carācara-guror īśvarasyeti ca | dharma-trāṇe hetuḥ, gurutveśvaratvayor upapādanam akhilasya viśvasyātmanaḥ kāraṇasyeti | evaṁ-bhūtasya viṣṇor janma sādhūnāṁ dharma-trāṇāya | dharma-trāṇa-prayojanam āha—karmāpanuttaye mokṣāya ||17||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **sādhūnāṁ vedānugāminām | dharmo yajñādirūpastasya rakṣaṇāya | dharma evānuṣṭhitontaḥkaraṇaśuddhidvārā mokṣaheturityata uktaṁ mokṣāyeti ||17||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** viṣṇor janma bhaviṣyati sādhūnāṁ karmāpanuttaye mokṣāya ||17||

 **...**

**|| 12.2.18 ||**

**śambhala-grāma-mukhyasya brāhmaṇasya mahātmanaḥ |**

**bhavane viṣṇuyaśasaḥ kalkiḥ prādurbhaviṣyati ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **śambhala-grāme mukhyasya pradhānasya nāmnā viṣṇuyaśaso brāhmaṇasya | bhavane gṛhe ||18||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **kaliṁ kṛpati vilikhati bhinattīti kalkiḥ | pṛṣodarādirayam | kṛṣaterḍipratyaye ṭilope kalerikāralope ca rūpasiddheḥ | yad vā, kaṁ sukhaṁ lāti dadātīti kalo dharmaḥ, taṁ kāyatyupadiśatīti kalkiḥ vāsudevānuśikṣāyā ity-ukteḥ ||18||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.2.19-20 ||**

**aśvam āśu-gam āruhya devadattaṁ jagat-patiḥ |**

**asināsādhu-damanam aṣṭaiśvarya-guṇānvitaḥ ||**

**vicarann āśunā kṣauṇyāṁ hayenāpratima-dyutiḥ |**

**nṛpa-liṅga-cchado dasyūn koṭiśo nihaniṣyati ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **dharma-trāṇa-prakāram āha, aśvam iti | asādhavo damyante yena tam aśvam āruhyāsinā dasyūn koṭiśo nihaniṣyatīty uttareṇānvayaḥ | asādhu-damana iti pāṭhe kalki-viśeṣaṇam | aṇimādy-aṣṭaiśvaryāṇi guṇāś ca satya-saṅkalpatvādayas tair anvitaḥ ||19||

tat-prapañcaḥ, āśunā śīghra-gāminā tena hayenāśvena kṣoṇyāṁ pṛthivyāṁ vicaran | nṛpa-liṅga-cchado rāja-veṣa-cchannān ||20||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **devair indrādibhirdattamānītam || apratimadyutiḥ sarvotkṛṣṭadīptiyutaḥ ||19-20||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** devaiḥ prasthāpitatvāt devadattatvaṁ, āśunā śīghra-gāminā, asādhavo damyante yena, tam asādhu-damanaṁ, nṛpa-liṅga-cchadaḥ rāja-veśa-cchannān ||19-20||

 **...**

**|| 12.2.21 ||**

**atha teṣāṁ bhaviṣyanti manāṁsi viśadāni vai |**

**vāsudevāṅga-rāgāti- puṇya-gandhānila-spṛśām ||**

**paura-jānapadānāṁ vai hateṣv akhila-dasyuṣu ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tataś ca punaḥ kṛta-yuga-pravṛttiṁ vaktum āha, atheti sārdhābhyām | teṣāṁ paura-jānapadānāṁ manāṁsi viśadāni bhaviṣyanti | tatra hetuḥ, vāsudevasyāṅga-rāgeṇa candanādināti-puṇya-gandho yo’nilas taṁ spṛśantīti tathā teṣām |

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tato dasyuhananottaram | ayam eva mūloktārthaśabdārthaḥ | teṣāṁ kaliyugasamāptyuttarakālikānāṁ paurajānapadānāṁ tattatpuradeśavāsināṁ janānām | tatra maneviśadatve ||21||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.2.22 ||**

**teṣāṁ prajā-visargaś ca sthaviṣṭhaḥ sambhaviṣyati |**

**vāsudeve bhagavati sattva-mūrtau hṛdi sthite ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **sthaviṣṭhiḥ sthūlaḥ ||22||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **sthaviṣṭhir dharma-niṣṭhatayā sthūlataraḥ ||22||

 **...**

**|| 12.2.23 ||**

**yadāvatīrṇo**[^7]** bhagavān kalkir dharma-patir hariḥ |**

**kṛtaṁ bhaviṣyati tadā prajā-sūtiś ca sāttvikī ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kṛta-yuga-pravṛttim āha—yadāvatīrṇa iti | prajānāṁ sūtiḥ prasūtiḥ ||23||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **teṣām eva sthūlo'dhikaḥ ||22-23||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **sūtiḥ prasūtiḥ ||23||

 **...**

**|| 12.2.24 ||**

**yadā candraś ca sūryaś ca tathā tiṣya-bṛhaspatī |**

**eka-rāśau sameṣyanti bhaviṣyati tadā kṛtam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tad-avatāra-kālopalakṣaṇam āha—yadā candraś ceti | tiṣyaḥ puṣyaḥ | ayam arthaḥ, candra-sūrya-bṛhaspatīnāṁ yadā puṣya-nakṣatre yogas tadā tat kṛta-yugaṁ bhaviṣyati | yady api ca prati-dvādaśābdaṁ karka-rāśau bṛhaspatau vartamāne dvi-trāsv amāvāsyāsu teṣāṁ trayāṇām api puṣya-yogaḥ saṁbhavati, tathāpi teṣāṁ saha praveśo’tra vivakṣitaḥ | sameṣyantīti vacanāt | ato nātiprasaṅgaḥ ||24||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **atrāśayam āha—ayamartha iti | atassamakālikatattrayapuṣyapraveśavivakṣaṇāt ||24||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **satya-yugārambha-kālaṁ darśayati—yadeti | tiṣyaḥ puṣyaḥ | ayam arthaḥ—candra-sūrya-bṛhaspatīnāṁ yadā puṣya-nakṣatre yogas tadā kṛta-yugaṁ bhaviṣyatīti | yadyapi prati-dvādaśābdaṁ karkaṭa-rāśau bṛhaspatau vartamāne dvi-trāsv amāvāsyāsu teṣāṁ trayāṇām api puṣya-yogaḥ saṁbhavati, tathāpi teṣāṁ saha praveśo’tra vivakṣitaḥ | sameṣyantīti vacanāt | ato nātiprasaṅgaḥ ||24||

 **...**

**|| 12.2.25 ||**

**ye’tītā vartamānā ye bhaviṣyanti ca pārthivāḥ |**

**te ta uddeśataḥ proktā vaṁśīyāḥ soma-sūryayoḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **evaṁ navama-skandham ārabhyānukrāntaṁ vaivasvata-manor vaṁśa-dvayaṁ nigamayati—ye’tītā iti | uddeśataḥ saṅkṣepataḥ ||25||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **samāsodde śasaṅkṣepāstraya ekārthavācakāḥ iti śabdaratnasaṁgrahokteḥ ||25||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** navamam ārabhyopakrāntāṁ kathām upasaṁharati—ye’tītā iti ||25||

 **...**

**|| 12.2.26 ||**

**ārabhya bhavato janma yāvan nandābhiṣecanam |**

**etad varṣa-sahasraṁ tu śataṁ pañcadaśottaram ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kali-yugāvāntara-viśeṣaṁ vaktum āha—ārabhyety-ādinā | varṣa-sahasraṁ pañcadaśottaraṁ śataṁ ceti kayāpi vivakṣayāvāntara-saṅkhyeyam | vastutas tu parīkṣin-nandayor antaraṁ dvābhyāṁ nyūnaṁ varṣāṇāṁ sārdha-sahasraṁ bhavati | yataḥ parīkṣit-sama-kālaṁ māgadhaṁ mārjārim ārabhya ripuñjayāntā viṁśati-rājānaḥ sahasra-saṁvatsaraṁ bhokṣyantīty uktaṁ navama-skandhe, ye bārhadratha-bhū-pālā bhāvyāḥ sāhasra-vatsaraṁ [bhā.pu. 9.22.49] iti | tataḥ paraṁ pañca pradyotanā aṣṭa-triṁśottaraṁ śatam | śiśunāgāś ca ṣaṣṭy-uttara-śata-trayaṁ bhokṣyanti pṛthivīm ity atraivoktatvāt ||26||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **atra svāmicaraṇair eva suvyākhyātatvādasmābhirupanyasyate ||26||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **etad-varṣa-sahasram ity eṣaiva saṅkhyā pramāṇī kartavyā | parīkṣitaḥ sama-kāla-varti-mārjāri-prabhṛtīnām ānandād bhoga-kāla-saṅkhyayā tu kiñcin nyūnaṁ sārdha-sāhasraṁ yad varṣāṇi, tat teṣāṁ khaṇḍa-maṇḍala-patīnāṁ vilāpyānantaryeṇa saṅkhyātānīti jñeyam ||26||

 **...**

**|| 12.2.27-28 ||**

**saptarṣīṇāṁ tu yau pūrvau dṛśyete uditau divi |**

**tayos tu madhye nakṣatraṁ dṛśyate yat samaṁ niśi ||**

**tenaiva ṛṣayo yuktās tiṣṭhanty abda-śataṁ nṛṇām |**

**te tvadīye dvijāḥ kāla adhunā cāśritā maghāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kaleḥ pravṛttiṁ vṛddhiṁ ca nirūpayituṁ kāla-jñānopalakṣaṇam āha—saptarṣīṇāṁ tv iti | ayam arthaḥ—prāg agra-śakaṭākāraṁ tārā-saptakaṁ saptarṣi-maṇḍalam | tatra kiñcid unnateṣāgra-sthānīyo marīciḥ | tataḥ paścād ānamra-yuga-kandharākāro vasiṣṭhaḥ sa-bhāryaḥ | tataḥ paścād īṣad-unnateṣāmūla-sthānīyo’ṅgirāḥ | tataḥ paścāc caturasra-tārā-catuṣke īśānyām atriḥ | tato dakṣiṇataḥ pulastyaḥ | pulastyāt paścimataḥ pulahaḥ | tata uttarataḥ kratuḥ | evaṁ sthite, teṣāṁ madhye yau pūrvau udaya-samaye prathamam uditau dṛśyete pulaha-kratu-saṁjñau, tayos tu madhye tayoḥ pūrvayos tu madhye yat samaṁ dakṣiṇottara-rekhāyāṁ sama-deśāvasthitam aśviny-ādiṣu yad anyatamaṁ nakṣatraṁ dṛśyate, tena tathaiva yuktā ṛṣayaḥ nṛṇām abda-śataṁ tiṣṭhanti, te ca dvijās tvadīye kāle’dhunā maghā āśritā vartante ||27-28||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **atrāśayam āha—ayamartha iti | tatra śakaṭākāre | īṣā rekhā sīradaṇḍaḥ śakaṭāṅgaviśeṣaś ca tadagrasthānīyastatsthānāpannaḥ| yugaḥ śakaṭāgrabaddhaḥ vṛṣayojanārthakaḥ śakaṭāṅgabheda eva, tadgrīvā ca tanmadhyabhāga uccākāra eva bodhyaḥ ||27||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** atha kaler utpatti-kālaṁ vṛddha-kālaṁ ca nirūpayituṁ kāla-jñāna-viśeṣam āha— saptarṣīṇām iti | prāg agraṁ śakaṭākāraṁ tārā-saptakaṁ saptarṣi-maṇḍalam | tatrodaya-samaye pūrvau prathamam uditau pulaha-kratu-saṁjñau yau niśi dṛśyete, tayor madhye gatam aśviny-ādy-anyatamam ekaikaṁ nakṣatraṁ tiṣṭhati, ekaika-śata-varṣaṁ vyāpya tena tenaiva yuktā ṛṣayas tiṣṭhantīti niyamaḥ | adhunā tu te maghāśritā vartanta iti, tenāśleṣāśriteṣu kṛṣṇa-prādurbhāvaḥ | maghāśriteṣu teṣu tad-antardhānaṁ kali-praveśaś ca, pūrvāṣāḍhaṁ prāpteṣu kaler vṛddhir ity uttara-graha-dṛṣṭyā jñeyam ||27-28||

 **...**

**|| 12.2.29 ||**

**viṣṇor bhagavato bhānuḥ kṛṣṇākhyo’sau divaṁ gataḥ |**

**tadāviśat kalir lokaṁ pāpe yad ramate janaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **teṣu maghasu vartamāneṣu satsu yadā **viṣṇor bhānur** bhātīti bhānuḥ śuddha-sattvātmako deho **divaṁ** vaikuṇṭhaṁ **gataḥ**, **tadā kali-**yugam **aviśat** | **yad** yasmin yuge **janaḥ pāpe ramate** iti kali-yugasya lakṣaṇam ||29||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tena pulahakratumadhyagatanakṣatreṇa ||28-29||

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) : viṣṇor bhagavato bhānuḥ kṛṣṇākhyo’sau divaṁ gata** iti bhagavato viṣṇor api bhānuḥ prakāśakaḥ, sarveśvareśvaratvāt kṛṣṇa ity ākhyā yasya, divaṁ sva-dhāma ||29||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **śrī-kṛṣṇa-lokaṁ eva dyu-śabdenāpy āha[^8]—viṣṇor iti | yadā guṇāvatārasya bhagavato viṣṇos tad-aṁśatvād raśmi-sthānīyasya kṛṣṇākhyo bhānuḥ sūrya-maṇḍala-sthānīyaḥ divaṁ prāpañcika-lokāgocaraṁ mathurādīnām eva prakāśa-viśeṣa-rūpaṁ vaikuṇṭha-lokaṁ gataḥ, tadā kalir lokam aviśat | eṣāṁ ca prakāśaḥ pṛthivī-stho’py[^9] antardhāna-śaktyā tām aspṛśann eva virājate | atas tayā na spṛśyate, pṛthivy-ādi-bhūta-mayair asmābhir vārāhokta-mahā-kadambādir iva[^10] | yas tu prāpañcika-loka-gocaro mathurādi-prakāśaḥ, so’yaṁ kṛpayā pṛthivīṁ spṛśann evāvatīrṇaḥ | atas tayā spṛśyate tādṛśair asmābhir dṛśyamāna-kadambādir iva | asmiṁś ca prakāśe yadāvatīrṇo bhagavān, tadā tat-sparśenāpi tat-sparśāt tāṁ spṛśann evāste sma | samprati tad-aspṛṣṭa-prakāśe viharamāṇaḥ punar aspṛśann eva bhavati | yadyapy evaṁ tathāpi kvacid dvayor bhedena kvacid abhedena vivakṣā tatra tatrāvagantavyā ||29|| [śrī-kṛṣṇa-sandarbha 107]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** tatrāpi maghāsv eva yadā bhagavato bhānuḥ śrī-kṛṣṇasya kiraṇa-rūpo vaikuṇṭha-nāthaḥ divaṁ vaikuṇṭhaṁ gataḥ, kṛṣṇākhyaḥ kṛṣṇatvena ā samyak khyātir yasya saḥ | bhātīti bhānuḥ śuddha-sattvātmako deha iti svāmi-caraṇāḥ ||29||

 **...**

**|| 12.2.30 ||**

**yāvat sa pāda-padmābhyāṁ spṛśan āste ramā-patiḥ |**

**tāvat kalir vai pṛthivīṁ parākrantuṁ na cāśakat ||**[^11]

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **nanu śrī-kṛṣṇe pṛthivyāṁ vartamāne’pi sandhyā-rūpeṇa kaliḥ praviṣṭa evāsīt, satyam, tathāpi tāvat tasya parākramo nābhavad ity āha—yāvad iti | parākrāntum abhibhavitum ||30||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **atrākṣipati—nanv iti | abhibhavituṁ svasāmarthyaṁ darśayitum ||30||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tad etad abhipretyāha—yāvad iti | parākrāntum ity anena tat-pūrvam api kañcit kālaṁ vyāpya praviṣṭo’sāv iti jñāpitam ||30|| [śrī-kṛṣṇa-sandarbha 107]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** nanu dvāparasya sandhyāṁśa-śeṣe bhagavad-avatāra-madhye eva yadā duryodhano dyūtaṁ pravartayāmāsa, tato draupadī-vastrākarṣaṇa-samayam eva bhagavad-āviṣṭaḥ | kaliḥ pṛthivyām adhikartuṁ prathamaṁ śubha-muhūrtaṁ cakāreti śrutam | satyaṁ, tad api sa tadākiñcitkara evāsī ity āh—yāvad iti | kṛṣṇāvatāra-madhye kila caturbhir vartase yena pādair loka-sukhāvahair iti pṛthivy-uktes tretā-yugato’pi dharmasya prābalyāt kutaḥ kales tadā parākrama iti bhāvaḥ ||30||

 **...**

**|| 12.2.31 ||**

**yadā devarṣayaḥ sapta maghāsu vicaranti hi |**

**tadā pravṛttas tu kalir dvādaśābda-śatātmakaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ato yathokta eva kali-praveśa-kāla ity āha—yadā devarṣaya iti | dvādaśābda-śatātmaka iti | divyena mānena sandhyā-sandhyāṁśābhyāṁ saha yo dvādaśābda-śatātmakaḥ, sa kalis tadā sandhyām atikramya praviṣṭa ity arthaḥ ||31||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ataḥ parākramābhāvāt | ity artha iti—śrī-kṛṣṇakāle svasandhyā vihāya svena rūpeṇaiva praviṣṭa iti bhāvaḥ ||31||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** ato maghāstheṣu ṛṣiṣu kṛṣṇāntardhāna-kṣaṇa-samanantara-kṣaṇa eva kaliḥ praviṣṭa ity āha—yadeti | dvādaśābda-śatātmaka iti divyena mānena sandhyā-sandhyāṁśābhyāṁ sahety arthaḥ ||31||

 **...**

**|| 12.2.32 ||**

**yadā maghābhyo yāsyanti pūrvāṣāṭhāṁ maharṣayaḥ |**

**tadā nandāt prabhṛty eṣa kalir vṛddhiṁ gamiṣyati ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kaleḥ praveśa-kālam uktvā tasya vṛddhi-kālam āha—yadeti | tadā pradyotanāt prabhṛti vṛddhiṁ gacchan nandāt prabhṛty ativṛddhiṁ gamiṣyatīty arthaḥ ||32|| 

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ity artha iti—parīkṣitkālikasaptarṣimaṇḍalagatamaghānakṣatrataḥ pūrvāṣāḍharkṣaṁ daśamamasti, tatrakaikarkṣasya śatavarṣaṁ tatra sthāyitvānnadakāle kalevarṣasahasramuktirāyāti | ata evoktam—ārabhya bhavato janma yāvannandābhiṣecanam | etadvarṣasahasram iti tac ca pūrvaṁ parākrāntam eveti bhāvaḥ ||32||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **kaler vṛddhi-kālam āha—yadeti ||32||

 **...**

**|| 12.2.33 ||**

**yasmin kṛṣṇo divaṁ yātas tasminn eva tadāhani |**

**pratipannaṁ kali-yugam iti prāhuḥ purā-vidaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **nanu yadā kaler liṅgam upalabdhaṁ, tadaiva praviṣṭa iti yuktam | tataḥ pūrvam eva praveśas tataḥ paraṁ vṛddhir ity atra kiṁ pramāṇam ? tatrāha—yasminn iti | pratipannaṁ praviṣṭam iti jñātam | purā-vidaḥ pūrva-jñātāraḥ ||33||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **punarākṣipati—nanv iti | tasminnevāhani | tadā tasminnaiva kṣaṇe ||33||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** nanu kaleḥ prathama-sandhyāyāṁ kṛṣṇo’vatīrṇa iti navīnā vadanti tan nety āha—yasminn iti | ato yugānāṁ pūrva-sandhyāṁśa-śeṣe eva ārambha-samaya iti yo niyamaḥ, so’pi kaler bhagavat-prabhāvād vyartha evābhūd iti bhāvaḥ ||33||

 **...**

**|| 12.2.34 ||**

**divyābdānāṁ sahasrānte caturthe tu punaḥ kṛtam |**

**bhaviṣyati tadā nṝṇāṁ mana ātma-prakāśakam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kaler anantaraṁ kṛta-yuga-praveśam āha—divyābdānām iti | caturthe kalau praveśanābda-parimitenāṁśenāpi sahātīte satīty arthaḥ | kṛta-yuga-praveśa-cihnam āha—yadā nṝṇāṁ mana ātma-prakāśakaṁ bhaviṣyati tadeti ||34||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ity artha iti—divyābdānāṁ sahasrasyāntaḥ sthitiryasminsandhyāṁśe sa sahasrāntastasmiṁs tathā tadguṇasaṁvijñānabahubrīhitvādvādaśaśatābdātmake sandhyāṁśasahite kṛtayugāpekṣayā caturthe kalāv iti śeṣeṇāyaṁ bhāvaḥ | divyābdānāṁ sahasrānta ityaluksamāsaḥ anto nāśe sthitāvapi ityabhidhānāt | yahā—divyābdānāṁ sahasreṇānto nāśo yasya tasmiṁścaturthe'tīte sati sahasrapadaṁ sandhyāṁśarūpaśatadvayasyāpyupalakṣaṇam ||34||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **kṛta-yuga-praveśa-kālam āha—divyeti | caturthe kalau tadīya-sandhyāṁśa-śeṣa-samaye ity arthaḥ ||34||

 **...**

**|| 12.2.35 ||**

**ity eṣa mānavo vaṁśo yathā saṅkhyāyate bhuvi |**

**tathā viṭ-śūdra-viprāṇāṁ tās tā jñeyā yuge yuge ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **rāja-vaṁśoktāṁ sthitiṁ brāhmaṇādi-vaṁśeṣv apy atidiśati—ity eṣa iti | yathā yābhir ucca-nīcāvasthābhiḥ | tās tā avasthāḥ | vaṁśā iti vā pāṭhaḥ ||35||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** mānavo vaṁśo yathā saṅkhyāyate manu-vaṁśyānāṁ yāvatyaḥ saṅkhyā yathoktā ity arthaḥ | tathaiva tatra tatratyānāṁ vaiśyādi-vaṁśyānām api tāvatyaḥ saṅkhyā anuktā api jñeyāḥ ||35||

 **...**

**|| 12.2.36 ||**

**eteṣāṁ nāma-liṅgānāṁ puruṣāṇāṁ mahātmanām |**

**kathā-mātrāvaśiṣṭānāṁ kīrtir eva sthitā bhuvi ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **etat-kīrtanasya vairāgyopayogitām āha—eteṣām iti | nāmaiva liṅgaṁ jñāpakaṁ yeṣāṁ, teṣāṁ kathā-mātreṇaivāvaśiṣṭānāṁ kīrtir eva sthitā, na tu rājyaṁ putrādayo vā ||36||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tāstā ityasya sthāne vaṁśā iti vā pāṭhaḥ ||35-36||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** nāmaiva liṅgaṁ jñāpakaṁ yeṣām ||36||

 **...**

**|| 12.2.37 ||**

**devāpiḥ śāntanor bhrātā maruś cekṣvāku-vaṁśa-jaḥ |**

**kalāpa-grāma āsāte mahā-yoga-balānvitau ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kalāv utsannānāṁ rāja-vaṁśānāṁ punaḥ pravṛtti-prakāram āha—devāpiḥ soma-vaṁśa-jaḥ | marus tu sūrya-vaṁśa-jaḥ | kalāpa-grāmo nāma yoginām āvāsaḥ prasiddhaḥ ||37||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **badarikāśrame kalāpagrāmo'sti | mahāyogabalānvitāvaṇimādyaiśvaryayuktau ||37||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **kalāv utsannānāṁ rāja-vaṁśānāṁ punaḥ pravṛtti-prakāram āha—devāpiḥ soma-vaṁśa-jaḥ ||37||

 **...**

**|| 12.2.38 ||**

**tāv ihaitya kaler ante vāsudevānuśikṣitau |**

**varṇāśrama-yutaṁ dharmaṁ pūrva-vat prathayiṣyataḥ ||**

_na katamenāpi vyākhyātam._

 **...**

**|| 12.2.39 ||**

**kṛtaṁ tretā dvāparaṁ ca kaliś ceti catur-yugam |**

**anena krama-yogena bhuvi prāṇiṣu vartate ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā),** **viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **imam eva prakāraṁ prati catur-yugaṁ darśayati—kṛtam iti ||39||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tau marudevāpisaṁjñau | ihāryāvarte | etya prāpya | vasudevena kalkirūpeṇa hariṇā anuśikṣitau bodhitau | pūrvavadgatakṛtayugavat ||38-39||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

**...**

**|| 12.2.40 ||**

**rājann ete mayā proktā nara-devās tathāpare |**

**bhūmau mamatvaṁ kṛtvānte hitvemāṁ nidhanaṁ gatāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **eteṣāṁ nāma-liṅgānāṁ [bhā.pu. 12.2.36] ity-ādi yad uktaṁ tat prapañcayati—rājann iti pañcabhiḥ ||40||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **he rājann iti—rājamātrāṇāmiyam eva daśeti bhāvaḥ | ate dehānte | imāṁ bhuvam ||40||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** nāmaiva liṅgaṁ jñāpakaṁ yeṣām ||40||

 **...**

**|| 12.2.41 ||**

**kṛmi-viḍ-bhasma-saṁjñānte rāja-nāmno’pi yasya ca |**

**bhūta-dhruk tat-kṛte svārthaṁ kiṁ veda nirayo yataḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **mamatvaṁ kṛtvety anena sūcitāṁ bhūta-droha-pravṛttiṁ nindati—kṛmīti | rāja-nāmno rājeti nāma yasya tasyāpi dehasyānte kṛmayo viṣṭhā bhasmeti vā saṁjñā bhaviṣyati | tat-kṛte tad-arthaṁ yo bhūta-dhruk bhūtebhyo druhyati, sa kiṁ svārthaṁ veda ? kiṁ tu na vedaiva | kutaḥ ? ity apekṣāyāṁ hetutvena bhūta-drohaṁ viśinaṣṭi, yato bhūta-drohān nirayo bhavati ||41||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** rāja-nāmno’pi dehasya ante maraṇe sati kṛmy-ādikam eva nāma bhavet | tasya dehasya kṛte ||41||

 **...**

**|| 12.2.42 ||**

**kathaṁ seyam akhaṇḍā bhūḥ pūrvair me puruṣair dhṛtā |**

**mat-putrasya ca pautrasya mat-pūrvā vaṁśa-jasya vā ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **mamatva-prakāraṁ prapañcayati—katham iti | seyam akhaṇḍā bhūr me pūrva-jair dhṛtā satī idānīṁ mat-pūrvā ca satī mat-putrādeḥ kathaṁ syād ity evam ||42||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **svārthaṁ svakartavyaṁ kiṁ veda kintu na vedetyarthaḥ ||41-42||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** mamatva-prakāram abhinayena darśayati—katham iti | mat-pūrvā ca satī mat-putrādeḥ kathaṁ syād ity evam ||42||

 **...**

**|| 12.2.43 ||**

**tejo-'b-anna-mayaṁ kāyaṁ gṛhītvātmatayābudhāḥ |**

**mahīṁ mamatayā cobhau hitvānte’darśanaṁ gatāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ubhau mahīṁ kāyaṁ ca | adarśanaṁ mṛtyum ||43||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tejobannamayam iti trivṛtkaraṇaśrutyabhiprāyeṇoktam ||43||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** kāyam ātmatayā, mahīṁ ca mamatayā, gṛhītvā ubhayau mahī-kāyau, adarśanaṁ mṛtyum ||43||

 **...**

**|| 12.2.44 ||**

**ye ye bhū-patayo rājan bhuñjate bhuvam ojasā |**

**kālena te kṛtāḥ sarve kathā-mātrāḥ kathāsu ca ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **upasaṁharati—ye ye iti | te sarve ca kathāsu kriyamāṇāsu | kathā-mātrāḥ kālena kṛtāḥ ||44||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **kathāmātrā iti—kathaiva teṣāmavaśiṣṭā na svarūpam iti bhāvaḥ |44| yadi kalkyavatārāntarājakathāviśeṣajijñāsā cettarhi bhaviṣyasaṁhitādigranthā matsaṁgṛhītacaturyugīyarājacaritagranthaścāvalokanīyaḥ ||44||

iti śrīmad-bhāgavata-bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśe dvādaśa-skandhe dvitīyo'dhyāyaḥ ||2||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

iti sārārtha-darśinyāṁ harṣiṇyāṁ bhakta-cetasām |

ekaviṁśo’tra daśame saṅgataḥ saṅgataḥ satām ||*||

 **...**


    iti śrīmad-bhāgavate mahā-purāṇe brahma-sūtra-bhāṣye pāramahaṁsyaṁ saṁhitāyāṁ vaiyāsikyāṁ dvādaśa-skandhe 


    kali-dharmo nāma 


    dvitīyo’dhyāyaḥ |

|| 12.2 ||

**...**

**(12.3)**

**atha tṛtīyo’dhyāyaḥ**


## yugānuvarṇanaṁ

**|| 12.3.1 ||**

**śrī-śuka uvāca—**

**dṛṣṭvātmani jaye vyagrān nṛpān hasati bhūr iyam |**

**aho mā vijigīṣanti mṛtyoḥ krīḍanakā nṛpāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :**

tṛtīye bhūmi-gītaiś ca rājya-doṣādi varṇyate |

kalau ca doṣa-bhūyiṣṭhe doṣa-hantrī harer natiḥ ||

dehe’hantāṁ bhūmau ca mamatāṁ kurvanty ato’buddhā ity uktaṁ tad eva bhūmi-gītaiḥ prapañcayati—dṛṣṭvety-ādi | ātmani pṛthivyā jaye vyagrān udyuktān | hāsa-prakāram evāha—aho iti | mā mām ||1||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **natirnamaskāraḥ| kṛṣṇapraṇāmī na punarbhavāya ity-ukteḥ ātmani svasyāṁ pṛthivyāmity arthaḥ ||1||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :**

tṛtīye tu bhuvo hāsyaṁ dharma-pāda-vyavasthitiḥ |

kaler doṣo doṣa-hāri hari-smaraṇam ucyate ||

kathaṁ seyam akhaṇḍā bhūr ity abudhānāṁ manoratha uktas tam eva pṛthivyā varṇanena prapañcayati—dṛṣṭveti | mā mām ||1||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.2 ||**

**kāma eṣa narendrāṇāṁ moghaḥ syād viduṣām api |**

**yena phenopame piṇḍe ye’tiviśrambhitā nṛpāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **yena kāmena | phenopame piṇḍe dehe’tiviśrambhitā viśvāsaṁ nītā ye teṣāṁ narendrāṇām eṣa kāmo mogha eva syāt ||2||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **viduṣāṁ nītividām | phenopame ḍiṇḍīrapiṇḍatulye naśvare ||2||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** yena kāmena piṇḍe dehe ||2||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.3-4 ||**

**pūrvaṁ nirjitya ṣaḍ-vargaṁ jeṣyāmo rāja-mantrinaḥ |**

**tataḥ saciva-paurāpta- karīndrān asya kaṇṭakān ||**

**evaṁ krameṇa jeṣyāmaḥ pṛthvīṁ sāgara-mekhalām |**

**ity āśā-baddha-hṛdayā na paśyanty antike’ntakam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kāmam eva darśayati dvābhyām—pūrvam iti | indriyārtha-lampaṭasya na rājya-prāptiḥ syād iti prathamam indriya-ṣaḍ-vargaṁ nirjitya, rāja-mantriṇo jiṣyāmo vaśī-kariṣyāmaḥ | sacivā amātyāḥ karīndrā hastipāḥ, tāṁś ca jeṣyāmaḥ | kaṇṭakān pratipakṣān | asya apāsya | “atha kaṇṭakān” iti vā pāṭhaḥ ||3-4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **karīndrānityupalakṣaṇaṁ senāmātrasya | amātyāḥ karmasacivāḥ | mantrī buddhisahāyaḥ syāt ity amaraḥ | āptā viśvastāḥ| kaṇṭakāḥ kṣudraśatravaḥ || evaṁkrameṇa pūrvoktakrameṇa ||3-4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **kāmam eva darśayati—pūrvam iti dvābhyām | tatrendriyārtha-lampaṭasya rājya-prāptir na syāt, ataḥ prathamam indriya-ṣaḍ-vargaṁ jitvā, asya mat-pratipakṣa-nṛpsya ||3-4||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.5 ||**

**samudrāvaraṇāṁ jitvā māṁ viśanty abdhim ojasā |**

**kiyad ātma-jayasyaitan muktir ātma-jaye phalam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **evaṁ kecid āśā-baddhā eva kecin māṁ punar jitvāpy atitṛṣṇayābdhiṁ viśanti | tad evam indriya-jayena ye rājyaṁ sādhayitum icchanti te ’timandā ity āha—kiyad iti ||5||

———————————————————————————————————————
