**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **abdhiṁ viśantītyuktyā dvīpajayo dhvanitaḥ bhūjayādinā kim api na prayojanam apitvanartha evāvaśiṣyate manojayāpekṣayetyabhiprāyeṇāha—kiyad iti | manojaye kiṁ syāttatrāha—muktir iti bandha indriyavikṣepo mokṣa epāṁ ca saṁyyamaḥ ityekādaśonaviṁśādhyāye bhagavad-ukter nyāyanaye manasopyantarindriyatve siddhepīha tu ṣaḍvargapadokter eva tadgṛhyata iti dhyeyaṁ sujñaiḥ ||5||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** māṁ pṛthivīṁ jitvā atitṛṣṇayā abdhiṁ viśanti tadīya-ratnāny āhartum iti bhāvaḥ | evam indriya-jayena ye rājyaṁ sādhayitum icchanti, te madnā ity āha—kiyad iti ||5||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.6 ||**

**yāṁ visṛjyaiva manavas tat-sutāś ca kurūdvaha |**

**gatā yathāgataṁ yuddhe tāṁ māṁ jeṣyanty abuddhayaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **antakaṁ na paśyanti ity uktaṁ, tad evāha—yām iti | kurūdvaheti bhūmi-gītaṁ kathayan śukaḥ saṁbodhayati, “kulodvahāḥ” iti tu pāṭhaḥ sugamaḥ ||6||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **he kurūdvaheti—tvam api yatkuruvaṁśaṁ vahasi sa vaṁśo'pyadhunā bhavaccheṣa eveti bhāvaḥ | yathāgatam iti āgatamanatikramya yathā tetrāgatā nirupaskarās tathaiva gatā ity arthaḥ ||6||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** yathāgataṁ yathā-jñānaṁ sva-sva-jñānam antikramya viraktā bhūtvā vanaṁ gatā ity arthaḥ | tāṁ mām ete mandā yuddhe jeṣyanti ||6||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.7-8 ||**

**mat-kṛte pitṛ-putrāṇāṁ bhrātṝṇāṁ cāpi vigrahaḥ |**

**jāyate hy asatāṁ rājye mamatā-baddha-cetasām ||**

**mamaiveyaṁ mahī kṛtsnā na te mūḍheti vādinaḥ |**

**spardhamānā mitho ghnanti mriyante mat-kṛte nṛpāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **“abuddhayaḥ” ity uktaṁ tat prapañcayati—mat-kṛta iti ||7||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **na kevalamitareṣām eva madarthe virodho bhavaty api tu pitrādidehasambandhināmapīty āha—matkṛta iti | matkṛte madarthe vigrahaḥ saṁyugaḥ vigrahas tu samāsārthavākye bhāge raṇeṅgake ityabhidhānāt 

ayam api prāyika ityāha—asatāmapraśastakarmaṇām || kiṁprakāro vigrahastatrāha mamaiveti ||7-8||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.3.9 ||**

**pṛthuḥ purūravā gādhir nahuṣo bharato’rjunaḥ**[^12]** |**

**māndhātā sagaro rāmaḥ khaṭvāṅgo dhundhuhā raghuḥ ||**

**madhvācāryaḥ (bhāgavata-tātparyam) :** 


    jīva-viṣṇvor abhedaś ca deha-yoga-viyojane |


    viṣṇor duḥkhaṁ vraṇitvādi parābhāvas tathaiva ca |


    asvātantryaṁ ca vedādāv uktavad bhāsate vibhoḥ |


    kvacit kvacid vimohāya daityādīnāṁ durātmanām || iti brahmāṇḍe ||[^13]

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **rāmo nāma kaścid rājā | yad vā, loka-dṛṣṭyā dāśarathir eva nirdiṣṭaḥ ||9||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **kācinnāmato'pyāha—pṛthur iti | śrīrāmacandrasyāpi māyayā tathātvāṅgīkāre na doṣa ityāha—yadveti ||9||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **pṛthur iti pañcakam ||9||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** rāmo nāma kaścid anyo rājā, na tu dāśarathir iti svāmi-caraṇāḥ ||9||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.10 ||**

**tṛṇabindur yayātiś ca śaryātiḥ śantanur gayaḥ |**

**bhagīrathaḥ kuvalayāśvaḥ kakutstho naiṣadho nṛgaḥ ||**

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **akṣarādhikyaṁ tṛtīyapāda ārṣam | naiṣadho nalaḥ ||10||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.11 ||**

**hiraṇyakaśipur vṛtro rāvaṇo loka-rāvaṇaḥ |**

**namuciḥ śambaro bhaumo hiraṇyākṣo’tha tārakaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **lokaṁ rāvayati rodayatīti loka-rāvaṇaḥ ||11||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **manuṣyoktanyāyaṁ daity-ādiṣvapyatidiśati—hiraṇyakaśipur iti ||11||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **+++

 **...**

**|| 12.3.12 ||**

**anye ca bahavo daityā rājāno ye maheśvarāḥ |**

**sarve sarva-vidaḥ śūrāḥ sarve sarva-jito’jitāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** _na vyākhyātam._

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ajitā anyaiḥ svayamajitā ity arthaḥ ||12||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **anye ca bahava iti | ca-kārāt te ca mayi mamatāṁ kṛtvā mayy avartanta | tatra ye mameśvarā bhagavad-avatārā bhāgavatā vā, te sarve sarva-vidaḥ śūrāś ca jñāna-kriyā-śaktibhyāṁ parama-paryāptā ity arthaḥ | ata eva sarva-jitaḥ svayam ajitāś ca sarva-śabdāvṛttir atiharṣeṇātidārḍhya-vivakṣayā ca ||12||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** _na vyākhyātam._

 **...**

**|| 12.3.13 ||**

**mamatāṁ mayy avartanta kṛtvoccair martya-dharmiṇaḥ |**

**kathāvaśeṣāḥ kālena hy akṛtārthāḥ kṛtā vibho ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **mayi uccair mamatāṁ kṛtvā ye ’vartanta te kālena kathāvaśeṣāḥ kṛtāḥ | vibho iti saṁbodhanaṁ kurūdvahetivat ||13||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **vibho iti śrīśukasyaiva rājānaṁ prati sambuddhirityāha—kurūdvaheti | yaditi—viśeṣeṇa buddhirvabhavena bhātīti tathā, tvaṁ tu buddhibalena sarvaṁ jānāsyeveti bhāvaḥ| atra cakravartikāraḥ—kiṁtu tena akṛtārthā api tu kṛtārthā eva prāptasvābhīṣṭā eva kṛtāḥ paryāptāḥ pūrṇā eva guṇarūpādibhistadaṣi kathāvaśeṣā evābhūvan, arvārcānāstu—akṛtārtha dhanādibhir apy apūrṇā iti bhāvaḥ ||13||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **ye tu tatra martya-dharmiṇo martya-svabhāvāsaktāḥ, te kālenākṛtārthāḥ kathā-mātrāvaśeṣitāś[^14] ca kṛtā ity arthaḥ ||13||	

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **mayi uccair mamatāṁ kṛtvā ye’vartanta, te kāle kathāvaśeṣā abhūvan, kintu te na hy akṛtārthāḥ, api tu kṛtārthā eva, prāpta-sva-svābhīṣṭā eva, kṛtāḥ paryāptāḥ, pūrṇā eva rasa-śāstra-guṇādibhis tad api te yathāvaśeṣā abhūvan, arvācīnās tu akṛtārthā dhanādibhir apy apūrṇāḥ kim uteti bhāvaḥ | yuga-paryāptayoḥ kṛtaṁ, paryāptiḥ paripūrṇatā ity amaraḥ ||12||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.14-15 ||**

**kathā imās te kathitā mahīyasāṁ**

**vitāya lokeṣu yaśaḥ pareyuṣām |**

**vijñāna-vairāgya-vivakṣayā vibho**

**vaco-vibhūtīr na tu pāramārthyam ||**

**yat**[^15]** tūttamaḥ-śloka-guṇānuvādaḥ**

**saṅgīyate’bhīkṣṇam amaṅgala-ghnaḥ |**

**tam eva nityaṁ śṛṇuyād abhīkṣṇaṁ**

**kṛṣṇe’malāṁ bhaktim abhīpsamānaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **rāja-vaṁśānukathanasya tātparyam āha--**kathā imā** iti | **vijñānaṁ** viṣayāsāratā-jñānaṁ tato **vairāgyaṁ,** tayor vivakṣayā **pareyuṣāṁ** mṛtānāṁ **vaco-vibhūtīr** vāg-vilāsa-mātra-rūpā **na tu pāramārthyaṁ** paramārthaṁ yuktaṁ kathanaṁ na bhavatīty arthah | kas tarhi puruṣāṇām upādeyaḥ paramārthas tam āha—**yas tv** iti | **nityaṁ** pratyaham | tatrāpy **abhīkṣṇam** ||14-15||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : _ity artha_** iti—teṣāṁ naṣṭatvād adhunā kathā-mātratvam evāvaśiṣṭaṁ, na tu te'pīti bhāvaḥ | mahatāṁ priyavratādīnām | paraṁ śrīharimīyuṣāṁ prāptānām | kim-artham ?  **vijñānaṁ** bhagavad-anubhavaḥ | śrotṛ-janān praty api tādṛśāḥ syur iti bhāvaḥ | tad uktam—


    pūrvaṁ gṛhītaṁ guṇa-karma-citram ajñānam ātmany aviviktam aṅga | 


    nivartante tat punar īkṣayaiva na gṛhyate nāpi visṛjya ātmā || 


    yathā hi bhānor udayo nṛ-cakṣuṣāṁ tamo nihanyān na tu sad vidhate | 


    evaṁ samīkṣā nipuṇā satī me hanyāt tamisraṁ puruṣasya buddheḥ || [bhā.pu. 11.28.33-34]]

ity uddhavaṁ prati śrī-kṛṣṇena | vitāyety ārṣaḥ | yad vā, kim-arthaṁ kathitāḥ ? iti tatrāha—**vijñāna**- iti | **vaco-vibhūtir** vacasā vibhūtayo vividha-bhavana-viṣayāḥ **vijñāna-vairāgya-vivakṣayā **yogyasya puṁso vijñāna-vairāgye syātām ity abhipretya vivṛtā, na tu **pāramārthye** paramārtha uttamārtho veda-mukhyārtho bhagavāṁs tam uddiśya tasya svarūpa-bhūtatvena vidhi-niṣedhāviṣayatvāt | yad vā, kiṁ-bhūtāḥ kathāḥ ? vacasāṁ bhakti-jñāna-kriyātmakānāṁ vibhūtir viśeṣeṇa pratipādanaṁ yāsu, tāḥ | **pāramārthyam** uddiśyopadeśe tu kevalaṁ bhakti-mātram evāpadeṣṭavyā syāt tasyā evāntakāla ucitatvāt janma-lābhaḥ paraḥ puṁsām ante nārāyaṇa-smṛtiḥ [bhā.pu. 2.1.6] ity-ukteḥ | yad vā, te kathitā imāḥ kathāḥ pāramārthyam eva paramārtha-phalakā eva, na tu vaco-vibhūtayaḥ puruṣārthāyoginya iti mantavyam | dvitīyā prathamārthe | śrutayaḥ pramāṇam itivat sambandhaḥ | yad vā, imāḥ buddhi-sannihitatvād devāsura-saṁgrāmādi-rūpāḥ kathā vaco-vibhūtayaḥ | pāramārthyaṁ paramātma-līlā-varṇanaṁ, na tu vaco-vibhūtayas tasya tat-prāpakatvāt | 


    pibanti ye bhagavata ātmanaḥ satāṁ 


    kathāmṛtaṁ śravaṇa-puṭeṣu saṁbhṛtam | 


    punanti te viṣaya-vidūṣitāśayaṁ 


    vrajanti tac-caraṇa-saroruhāntikam || [bhā.pu. 2.1.6] ity-ukteḥ | 

yad vā, imāḥ kathā vacovibhūtayo na tu kiṁtu pārāmārthyam eva sarvāsāṁ paramārthe bhagavati tātparyakatvād ity arthaḥ || pāramārtham eva pṛcchati—_kas tarhi_ ? iti | tatrāpi _pratyaham_ api | tam eva **uttama-śloka-guṇānuvādam** eva hari-bhakty-utpādakatvāt, anyā vāco vimuñcatha iti śruteḥ ||14-15||

———————————————————————————————————————

**kaivalya-dīpikā : antareṇa** vinā | **davo** vana-vahniḥ | atra ūrjitaikā **līlā-kathā** iti padāni jñāna-miśratve bījam ||15|| [mu.pha. 8.15]

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** kathā imās te kathitā ity-ādi | etā vaṁśa-kathā vijñāna-vairāgya-vivakṣayaiva kathitā, na tv atra paramārtha-bhāvaḥ ko’pīty arthaḥ ||14|| anyac ca, eṣāṁ rājñāṁ madhye yo bhāgavatas tat-kathā-caraṇāravindenāntaḥ-śodhanam apy astīti vastu ity āha—yas tūttama-śloka ity-ādi ||15||

———————————————————————————————————————

**sanātana-gosvāmī : **[ha.bha.vi. 10.445] tam eva, na tu tad-vyatiriktaṁ śṛṇuyāt | nityaṁ pratyaham | tatrāpy abhīkṣṇaṁ kṛṣṇaṁ yā amalā bhaktiḥ prema-lakṣaṇā tām abhīpsamānaḥ, guṇānuvāda-śravaṇenaiva sā sampadyetety arthaḥ ||15||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (bhakti-sandarbha 129) **: atha **guṇa-śravaṇam**—kathā ity-ādi dvābhyām | ṭīkā ca—


    rāja-vaṁśānukīrtanasya tātparyam āha kathā imā iti | vijñānaṁ viṣayāsāratā-jñānam | tato vairāgyam | tayor vivakṣayā | pareyuṣāṁ mṛtānāṁ vaco-vibhūtīr vāg-vilāsa-mātra-rūpāḥ | pāramārthyaṁ paramārtha-yuktaṁ kathanaṁ na bhavatīty arthaḥ | kas tarhi puruṣāṇām upādeyaḥ paramārthas tam āha yas tv iti | nityaṁ pratyaham | tatrāpy abhīkṣṇam ity eṣā |

atra yat kvacic chrī-rāma-lakṣmaṇādayo’pi teṣāṁ rājñāṁ madhye vairāgyārthaṁ chatri-nyāyena paṭhyante tan nirasyate | ato yadyapi nigama-kalpa-taror [bhā.pu. 1.1.3] ity ādy-anusāreṇa sarvasyaiva prasaṅgasya rasa-rūpatvaṁ tathāpi kvacit sākṣād-bhakti-maya-śāntādi-rasa-rūpatvaṁ kvacit tad-upakaraṇa-śāntādi-rasa-rūpatvaṁ ca samarthanīyam | asti hi tatra tatra bhakti-raseṣv api tāratamyam iti | guṇāḥ kāruṇyādayaḥ | tad-guṇa-kīrtiḥ svabhāva evāsāv iti śrī-gītāsv api dṛṣṭam—sthāne hṛṣīkeśa tava prakīrtyā jagat prahṛṣyaty anurajyate ca [gītā 11.36] ity ādau | 

atra mahā-bhāgavatānām api bhagavata iva guṇa-śravaṇaṁ matam—


    tat kathyatāṁ mahā-bhāga yadi kṛṣṇa-kathāśrayam |


    athavāsya padāmbhoja- makaranda-lihāṁ satām || [bhā.pu. 1.16.6]

iti śaunakokteḥ | yadyapy atra guṇa-śabdena rūpa-līlayor api sauṣṭhavaṁ gṛhyate tathāpi tat-prādhānya-nirdeśāt pṛthag-grahaṇam | evam uttaratrāpi jñeyam | bhaktiṁ premāṇam | amalāṁ kaivalyādīcchā-rahitām ||14-15||[^16]

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tad eva vyanakti—kathā imā iti dvābhyām | mahīyasāṁ bhagavad-avatāra-bhāgavatebhya itareṣāṁ mahārājānām | atra yat kvacic chrī-rāma-lakṣmaṇādayo’pi teṣāṁ rājñāṁ madhye vairāgyārthaṁ chatri-nyāyena paṭhyante, tan nirasyate | ato yadyapi nigama-kalpa-taror [bhā.pu. 1.1.3] ity-ādy-anusāreṇa sarvasyaiva prasaṅgasya rasa-rūpatvam, tathāpi kvacit sākṣād-bhakti-maya-śāntādi-rasa-rūpatvam, kvacit tad-upakaraṇa-śāntādi-rasa-rūpatvaṁ ca samarthanīyam | asti hi tatra tatra prasaṅgeṣu bhakti-raseṣv api tāratamyam ||14|| 

śrī-bhagavad-guṇa-śravaṇasyāvaśyakatvam āha—yas tv iti | guṇāḥ kāruṇyādayaḥ | tad-guṇānuvādasya svabhāva evāsau [sa-mūlāmaṅgala-nāśa-pūrvaka-śrī-kṛṣṇe’mala-bhakti-pradarśinī śaktir ity arthaḥ] iti śrī-gītāsv api dṛṣṭam—sthāne hṛṣīkeśa tava prakīrtyā jagat prahṛṣyaty anurajyate ca [gītā 11.36] ity ādau | uttama-ślokānāṁ bhagavad-avatārāṇāṁ bhāgavatānāṁ ca guṇānuvādo yas tam eva nityaṁ śṛṇuyāt, tatra tv atiśayenānugrahaṁ kuryād ity arthaḥ | sarvasya tasyāpi paramaṁ phalam āha—kṛṣṇa iti | kṛṣṇe kṛṣṇas tu bhagavān svayaṁ [bhā.pu. 1.3.28] ity-ādinātiprasiddhe śrī-gopāla iti ||15|| 

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** rājavaṁśa-kathanasya tātparyam āha—kathā iti mahīyasāṁ priyavratādīnāṁ, pareyuṣāṁ paraṁ śrī-bhagavantam īyuṣāṁ prāptānāṁ, kim-arthaṁ kathitāḥ ? tatrāha—vijñānaṁ teṣāṁ bhagavad-anubhavaḥ, vairāgyaṁ ca tayor vivakṣayā, teṣāṁ tathācaraṇaṁ śrotṛ-janā api śikṣatv iti bhāvaḥ | he vibho ! iti tvam api tādṛśa eko bhavasīiti bhāvaḥ | kiṁ ca, imāḥ kathā vaco-vibhūtīr vacasāṁ vibhūtayo na bhavanti, kintu pāramārthyaṁ kathānāṁ paramārthatayaiva jñeyety arthaḥ ||14||

tasmān mahīyasāṁ teṣāṁ kathā nityaṁ śṛṇuyād eva, kṛṣṇa-guṇānuvāde tu tebhyo mahiṣṭhebhyo’py adhikatamānāṁ kṛṣṇa-līlā-parikarāṇāṁ mahatāṁ kathābhir vicitre viśeṣaṁ śṛṇv ity āha—ya iti | uttamaḥ-ślokasya bhagavato guṇānuvādas teṣu teṣu skandheṣu kvacit kvacid daśame tu sarvatraiva taṁ, nityam eva abhīkṣṇam eva bhaktim abhīpsamāna eva śṛṇuyād evety avadhāraṇa-catuṣṭayam ||14||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.16 ||**

**śrī-rājovāca—**

**kenopāyena bhagavan kaler doṣān kalau janāḥ |**

**vidhamiṣyanty upacitāṁs tan me brūhi yathā mune ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kali-doṣopacaye sati bhakter asaṁbhavaṁ manyamānaḥ pṛcchati—kenopāyeneti | vidham iṣyanti nāśayiṣyanti | yathā yathāvat ||16||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **jñātakalidoṣaparihāro'pi lokahitāya pṛcchati—keneti vāvataraṇikā | bhagavanmune iti saṁbuddhiryena sarvakathanasāmarthyaṁ dyotayatīti bhāvaḥ ||16||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **vidham iṣyanti nāśayiṣyanti | yathā yathāvat ||16||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.17 ||**

**yugāni yuga-dharmāṁś ca mānaṁ pralaya-kalpayoḥ |**

**kālasyeśvara-rūpasya gatiṁ viṣṇor mahātmanaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kali-yuge kaḥ paro dharma iti bubhutsayā pṛcchati—yugānīti | bruhīty anuṣaṅgaḥ | ātyantika-pralaya-jijñāsayā punaḥ pṛcchati, pralaya-kalpayoḥ saṁhāra-sthiti-kālayoḥ | na cāyaṁ bahir-mukhaḥ praśna ity āha—kālasyeti ||17||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **gatiṁ gamanaprakāram ||17||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **yugānīti | bruhīty anuṣaṅgaḥ | pralaya-kalpayoḥ saṁhāra-sthiti-kālayoḥ | na cāyaṁ bahir-mukhaḥ praśna ity āha—kālasyeti ||17||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.18 ||**

**śrī-śuka uvāca—**

**kṛte pravartate dharmaś catuṣ-pāt taj-janair dhṛtaḥ |**

**satyaṁ dayā tapo dānam iti pādā vibhor nṛpa ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tatra yuga-dharmāṁs tāvad āha—kṛta iti | taj-janais tat-kālīnair janaiḥ | dānam arāga-dveṣatayā’bhaya-dānam | tad eva prathama-skandhe śauca-śabdenoktam | vibhoḥ saṁpūrṇasya dharmasya ||18||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** prathamaṁ yuga-dharmān āha—kṛta iti | taj-janais tat-kāla-bhavair lokair bhṛto dhṛtaḥ | dānam iti | daipa śodhane ity asmāt śaucam ity arthaḥ | tathaiva prathama-skandhokteḥ ||18||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.19 ||**

**santuṣṭāḥ karuṇā maitrāḥ śāntā dāntās titikṣavaḥ |**

**ātmārāmāḥ sama-dṛśaḥ prāyaśaḥ śramaṇā janāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tadānīntana-janān āha—santuṣṭā iti | maitrā bhūta-maitrī-yuktāḥ | śramaṇā ātmābhyāsavantaḥ ||19||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tatra pṛṣṭārtheṣu madhye | tāvadādau | nṛpeti—dharmajñānaṁ vinā nṛpālanaṁ durghaṭam iti bhāvaḥ  ||18-19||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** śramaṇā ātmābhyāsavantaḥ ||19||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.20 ||**

**tretāyāṁ dharma-pādānāṁ turyāṁśo hīyate śanaiḥ |**

**adharma-pādair anṛta- hiṁsāsantoṣa-vigrahaiḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **anṛtena satyam, hiṁsayā dayā, asantoṣeṇa tapaḥ, vigraheṇa dānam iti yathā-saṅkhyaṁ yojyam ||20||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **turyāṁśo dānalakṣaṇaḥ pādo hīyate hrasati | pādahānau pratipakṣam āha—adharmeti ||20||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tretāyām ity-ādikaṁ prathama-skandha-sandarbhā’nusāreṇa samyak jñeyam ||20||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **anṛtena satyaṁ, hiṁsayā dayā, asantoṣeṇa tapaḥ, vigraheṇa śaucam ||20||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.21 ||**

**tadā kriyā-tapo-niṣṭhā nāti-hiṁsrā na lampaṭāḥ |**

**trai-vargikās trayī-vṛddhā varṇā brahmottarā nṛpa ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā),** **viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **brahmottarā brāhmaṇādhikāḥ ||21||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.3.22 ||**

**tapaḥ-satya-dayā-dāneṣv ardhaṁ hrasati dvāpare |**

**hiṁsātuṣṭy-anṛta-dveṣair dharmasyādharma-lakṣaṇaiḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **hiṁsātuṣṭy-anṛta-dveṣair ity ayaṁ kramo na vivakṣitaḥ | dharmasyārdhaṁ hrasati kṣīyate | adharmasya lakṣaṇaiś cihnaiḥ, pādair ity arthaḥ ||22||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tadā tretāyām | kriyā yajñādirūpā | lampaṭā viṣayarāgiṇaḥ | traivargikāstrivargapradhānāḥ | trivargo dharmakāmārthaiḥ ity amaraḥ | trayīvṛddhā vedavidyāviśāradāḥ ||21-22||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** hiṁsety atra kramo na vivakṣitaḥ ||22||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.23 ||**

**yaśasvino mahā-śīlāḥ svādhyāyādhyayane ratāḥ |**

**āṭhyāḥ kuṭumbino hṛṣṭā varṇāḥ kṣatra-dvijottarāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **yaśasvinaḥ kīrti-priyāḥ | kṣatra-dvijottarāḥ kṣatriya-brāhmaṇa-pradhānāḥ |

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **mahāśālā yajñādikartāraḥ | āḍhyā dhaninaḥ ||23||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.3.24 ||**

**kalau tu dharma-pādānāṁ turyāṁśo’dharma-hetubhiḥ |**

**edhamānaiḥ kṣīyamāṇo hy ante so’pi vinaṅkṣyati ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kalau dharma-pādānāṁ turyāṁśaś caturthāṁśo ’vaśiṣyate |

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **turyāṁśaḥ satyalakṣaṇaḥ ||24||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** dharma-hetūnāṁ satyādīnām adharma-hetubhir anṛtādibhiḥ ||24||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.25 ||**

**tasmin lubdhā durācārā nirdayā śuṣka-vairiṇaḥ |**

**durbhagā bhūri-tarṣāś ca śūdra-dāsottarāḥ prajāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **śūdra-dāśottarāḥ śūdra-kaivartādi-pradhānāḥ ||25||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tasminkalau | śuṣkavairiṇo nirnimittavairiṇaḥ | durācārā māṁsāśanādyācāraparāyaṇāḥ ||25||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.3.26 ||**

**sattvaṁ rajas tama iti dṛśyante puruṣe guṇāḥ |**

**kāla-sañcoditās te vai parivartanta ātmani ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **yugānām evaṁ-bhūta-vaiṣamye kāraṇam āha—sattvam iti pañcabhiḥ ||26||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** yathā ekasyāpi grahasya sūryāder daśāyāṁ grahāṇām antardaśā bhavanti, tathaikaikasyāpi yugasya madhye catvāri yugāni tiṣṭhanty ataḥ kali-madhye’pi kadācit kadācin na dharma-hrāsas tatrāpy ekaikasmin puṁsy evaṁ draṣṭavyam ity āha—sattvam iti | ātmany antaḥkaraṇe parivartante, yātāyātaṁ kurvanti ||26||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.27 ||**

**prabhavanti yadā sattve mano-buddhīndriyāṇi ca |**

**tadā kṛta-yugaṁ vidyāj jñāne tapasi yad ruciḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **manaś ca buddhiś cendriyāṇi ca sattve yadā prabhavanty atiśayena vartante ||27||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **evaṁbhūtavaiṣamye | parivartate yarthakasyāpi grahamahādaśāyāmantardaśā vartate tathā kalāvapi catvāro yugā iti bhāvaḥ | ātmani manasi ||26-27||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** etad vivṛṇoti—prabhavantīti | sattve niṣkāma-dharme ||27||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.28 ||**

**yadā karmasu kāmyeṣu bhaktir yaśasi dehinām |**

**tadā tretā rajo-vṛttir iti jānīhi buddhi-man ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **yadā dharmādiṣu bhaktiḥ prītiḥ, tadā rajo-vṛtti-pradhānaṁ tretā-yugam iti jānīhi ||28||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** kāmyeṣu sa-kāma-dharmeṣu bhaktiḥ prītiḥ ||28||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.29_ _||**

**yadā lobhas tv asantoṣo māno dambho’tha matsaraḥ |**

**karmaṇāṁ cāpi kāmyānāṁ dvāparaṁ tad rajas-tamaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kāmyānāṁ karmaṇāṁ viṣaye yadā prītiḥ, tat tadā rajas-tamaḥ-pradhānaṁ dvāparaṁ jānīhīti pūrveṇānuṣaṅgaḥ ||29||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **paryāyeṇa vartate he buddhimann iti—buddhyairvaitanniśceyam iti bhāvaḥ ||28-29||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** yadā kāmyānāṁ karmaṇāṁ kāmyeṣu karmasv ity arthaḥ | ca-kārād adharmeṣv api prītis tadā rajas-tamaḥ-pradhāna-dvāparaṁ jānīhi, tatra lobhādayo bhavantīty anvayaḥ ||29||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.30 ||**

**yadā māyānṛtaṁ tandrā nidrā hiṁsā viṣādanam |**

**śoka-mohau bhayaṁ dainyaṁ sa kalis tāmasaḥ smṛtaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **viṣādanaṁ duḥkham ||30||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** yadā kevaleṣv adharmeṣv eva prītis tadā tāmasa-prasiddhaḥ kalir eva tadā māyānṛtādayaḥ viṣādanaṁ viṣādaḥ ||30||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.31 ||**

**tasmāt kṣudra-dṛśo martyāḥ kṣudra-bhāgyā mahāśanāḥ |**

**kāmino vitta-hīnāś ca svairiṇyaś ca striyo’satīḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kali-doṣān prapañcayati—yasmād ity-ādinā | yasmāt kaler hetoḥ | kṣudra-dṛśo manda-matayaḥ | kṣudra-bhāgyā alpa-bhāgyaḥ | mahā-śanā bahv-āhārāḥ | vitta-hīnā api kāminaś ca | svairiṇyaḥ puṁś-calyaḥ | asatīr asatyaḥ ||31||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **atha kaler doṣān prapañcayati—tasmād iti | tasmāt kaler hetoḥ ||31||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.32 ||**

**dasyūtkṛṣṭā janapadā vedāḥ pāṣaṇḍa-dūṣitāḥ |**

**rājānaś ca prajā-bhakṣāḥ śiśnodara-parā dvijāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **dasyava utkṛṣṭāḥ pracurā yeṣu te ||32||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **dasyūtkṛṣṭā dasyava eva utkṛṣṭāḥ pradhānā yeṣu te ||32||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** _na vyākhyātam._

 **...**

**|| 12.3.33 ||**

**avratā baṭavo’śaucā bhikṣavaś ca kuṭumbinaḥ |**

**tapasvino grāma-vāsā nyāsino’tyartha-lolupāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **avratā vihitācāra-śūnyāḥ | aśaucāḥ śauca-śūnyāś ca baṭavo brahmacāriṇo bhaviṣyanti | kuṭumbinaś ca gṛhasthāḥ svayaṁ bhikṣāṭana-parā bhaviṣyanti, na tu bhikṣāṁ dāsyanti | tapasvino vana-sthā vanaṁ hitvā grāma-vāsā bhaviṣyanti | nyāsino yatayo ’tīvārtha-lolupā bhaviṣyanti ||33||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** baṭavo brahmacāriṇaḥ avratā vratāhīnāḥ śauca-hīnāś ca bhaviṣyanti | kuṭumbino gṛhasthā bhikṣavaḥ bhikṣāṭana-parā eva, na tu bhikṣāṁ dāsyanti | tapasvino bāṇa-prasthāḥ vanaṁ hitvā grāma-vāsāḥ grāme gṛhasthān eva svatapo darśayiṣyantīty arthaḥ | nyāsino yatayaḥ atyartha-lolupāḥ vitta-saṅgrahe payatiṣyante ||33||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.34 ||**

**hrasva-kāyā mahāhārā bhūry-apatyā gata-hriyaḥ |**

**śaśvat kaṭuka-bhāṣiṇyaś caurya-māyoru-sāhasāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **punar api strīṇāṁ svabhāvam āha, hrasva-kāyā iti | kaṭuka-bhāṣiṇyo ’priya-vādinyaḥ | cauryaṁ ca māyā kapaṭam uru ca sāhasaṁ yāsāṁ tāḥ ||34||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tāmasaḥ kevalatamoguṇapradhānaḥ ||30-34||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** punar api striyo varṇayati—hrasveti ||34||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.35 ||**

**paṇayiṣyanti vai kṣudrāḥ kirāṭāḥ kūṭa-kāriṇaḥ |**

**anāpady api maṁsyante vārtāṁ sādhu jugupsitām ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** kiṁ ca, kirāṭā vaṇijaḥ | paṇayiṣyanti kraya-vikrayādi-vyavahāraṁ pravartayiṣyanti | kiṁ ca, sarve janā anāpady api jugupsitāṁ ninditāṁ vārtāṁ vṛttiṁ sādhu maṁsyante ||35||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **kirāṭā vaṇijaḥ | kuṭa-kāriṇaḥ adharmeṇa kapaṭaṁ kṛtvā paṇayiṣyanti vyavahāraṁ pravartayiṣyante | kiṁ ca, sarve eva varṇā anāpady api jugupsitāṁ vārtāṁ sādhu maṁsyante ||35||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.36 ||**

**patiṁ tyakṣyanti nirdravyaṁ bhṛtyā apy akhilottamam |**

**bhṛtyaṁ vipannaṁ patayaḥ kaulaṁ gāś cāpayasvinīḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **sarvottamam api patiṁ dravya-hīnaṁ bhṛtyās tyakṣyanti | patayaś ca vipannaṁ rogādibhir vyāpārākṣamaṁ kaulaṁ kula-paramparāyātaṁ tyakṣyanti | apayasvinīrdugdha-dohāḥ ||36||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **anyadāha—kiñceti | kirāṭo hiṁsake vaiśye iti niruktiḥ | kūṭaṁ mānakūṭaṁ tulākūṭaṁ lipikūṭaṁ ca kartuṁ śīlaṁ yeṣāṁ te tathā kūṭaṁ pūrdvārayantrayoḥ | māyādambhādriśṛṅgeṣu sīrāṅge'nṛtatucchayoḥ | iti hemacandrakośāt ||35-36||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** akhilottamam api patiṁ nirdravyaṁ bhāryās tathā bhṛtyā api tyakṣyanti | patayaś ca vipannaṁ rogādi-grastaṁ kaulaṁ kula-paramparā-gatam api tyakṣyanti | gāś ca vṛddhatvād apayasvinīs tyakṣyanti ||36||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.37 ||**

**pitṛ-bhrātṛ-suhṛj-jñātīn hitvā saurata-sauhṛdāḥ |**

**nanāndṛ-śyāla-saṁvādā dīnāḥ straiṇāḥ kalau narāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : saurataṁ** surata-nimittaṁ **sauhṛdaṁ** yeṣāṁ te | ata eva **nanāndaro**’tra bhāryā-bhaginyaḥ, **śyālā** bhāryā-bhrātaraḥ, taiḥ **saṁvādo** mantrālocanaṁ yeṣāṁ te | nanandṛ iti vā pāṭhaḥ ||37||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ata eva **saurata-sauhṛdatvād** eva | straiṇāḥ strīvaśāḥ ||37||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** **nanāndaro**’tra bhāryā-bhaginyaḥ ||37||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.38 ||**

**śūdrāḥ pratigrahīṣyanti tapo-veṣopajīvinaḥ |**

**dharmaṁ vakṣyanty adharma-jñā adhiruhyottamāsanam ||**

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **śūdralakṣaṇaṁ tu—


    dvijetaro'mantrayāgī mlecchabhinno vivāhavān | 


    dvijabhakto bhavecchūdrastadanyastvantyajādikaḥ || iti saṁhitāyām | 

tena trivarṇetare sarve śūdrā eva | yattukaiścit—


    na śūdrā bhagavad-bhaktā viprā bhāgavatā matāḥ | 


    caturvarṇeṣu te śūdrā ye na bhaktā janārdane || 

iti sarva-purāṇādṛṣṭaṁ purāṇīyatvenoktaṁ tasya cāyam arthaḥ—hari-bhakteṣu śūdreṣv api jāti-buddhyā tad-avamāno na kāryaḥ, kintu brāhmaṇavat sat-kāraḥ kārya iti, teṣāṁ vastuto vipratve vidur adharma-vyādhādīnāṁ bhāratādau śūdratvena vyapadeśo'narthakaḥ syād iti vastutas tu śloko'yaṁ vaiṣṇavābhāsa-kalpita eva | tapoveṣeṇa brahmacārivanasthayativeṣeṇopajīvanaṁ vṛttiryeṣāṁ te tathā | tapaḥ-śabdo'tra tapasviparatayā neyaḥ, kvacittiviṣaye taddhitapratyayānāṁ lopasvīkārāt | kalau śūdrā eva brahmacāriṇaḥ sannyāsinaś ca bhaviṣyanti te cānyādhikārapravṛttatvānnarake patiṣyanti—


    hīno bhūtvottamād varṇāt kṛtvā yeṣaṁ tapasvinām | 


    ātmānaṁ pūjayed yas tu sa paten narake dhruvam | iti saṁhitokteḥ | 

uttamāsanaṁ vyāsāsanam | vakṣyanty upadekṣyanti | ardham ajñāḥ santaḥ te'pi śāstrānugāmino rājñāṁ daṇḍyā eva—


    ye śūdra-mukhataḥ śāstraṁ śṛṇvantīha narādhamāḥ | 


    teṣāṁ karṇe trapu siktvā varjihvāṁ prakartayet | 


    anyathā kṣmāpāntaryāti narakān bhṛśa-dāruṇān || ity-ādy-ukteḥ | 

pratigrahīṣyanti dānaṁ svīkariṣyanti te'pi nārakā bhaviṣyanti—


    dānaṁ gṛhṇāti yaḥ śūdro mahatyām api cāpadi | 


    yaś ca tasmai sampradadyāt tāv ubhau nārakau dhruvam | iti saṁhitokteḥ ||38||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.39 ||**

**nityam udvigna-manaso durbhikṣa-kara-karśitāḥ |**

**niranne bhū-tale rājan anāvṛṣṭi-bhayāturāḥ ||**

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **udvignamanasastrastamanasaḥ | durbhikṣamannālpatvam, karo rājabhāgastābhyāṁ karśitāṁ durbalāḥ ||39||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.40 ||**

**vāso-'nna-pāna-śayana- vyavāya-snāna-bhūṣaṇaiḥ |**

**hīnāḥ piśāca-sandarśā bhaviṣyanti kalau prajāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **piśāca-sandarśāḥ piśāca-sadṛśāḥ |

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **piśāco vikṛto bhūtaviśeṣaḥ ||40||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.3.41 ||**

**kalau kākiṇike’py arthe vigṛhya tyakta-sauhṛdāḥ |**

**tyakṣyanti ca priyān prāṇān haniṣyanti svakān api ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kākiṇike viṁśati-varāṭakā-mātre’py arthe viṣaya-bhūte | vigṛhya vairaṁ kṛtvā ||41||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **svakān svīyānbhrātṛputrādīn | apinā kiṁ parakīyānityasūci ||41||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **kākiṇike viṁśati-varāṭikā-mātre’py arthe viṣaye vigṛhya kalahaṁ kṛtvā ||41||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.42 ||**

**na rakṣisyanti manujāḥ sthavirau pitarāv api |**

**putrān bhāryāṁ ca kula-jāṁ kṣudrāḥ śiśnodaram-bharāḥ ||**

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **kvacit putrānbhāryāṁ ca kulajām iti vā pāṭhaḥ | kṣudrāḥ krūrāḥ kṣudraḥ syādadhame krūrakṛpaṇālpeṣu vācyavat iti medinī ||42||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.43 ||**

**kalau na rājan jagatāṁ paraṁ guruṁ**

**tri-loka-nāthānata-pāda-paṅkajam |**

**prāyeṇa martyā bhagavantam acyutaṁ**

**yakṣyanti pāṣaṇḍa-vibhinna-cetasaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **mahāntam anartham āha dvābhyām—kalāv iti | tri-loka-nāthair ānataṁ namas-kṛtaṁ pāda-paṅkajaṁ yasya tam | na yakṣyanti na pūjayiṣyanti | pākhaṇḍair vibhinnam anyathā kṛtaṁ ceto yeṣāṁ te ||43||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **he rājann iti—tvaṁ tu dharmeṇaiva rājasi tvadrājyataḥ paramevedaṁ bhaviṣyatīti bhāvaḥ | prāyeṇeti pāṭhāt—


    kvacitkacinmahārāja drāviḍeṣu ca bhūriśaḥ | 


    kalau khalu bhaviṣyanti nārāyaṇaparāyaṇāḥ || ity-ādi jñeyam ||43||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tad evaṁ ekādaśe pañcamādhyāyokta-diśā kalau bhagavan-nāma-kīrtana-pracāra-prabhāveṇaiva parama-bhagavat-parāyaṇatva-siddhir darśitā | tatra pāṣaṇḍa-praveśena nāmāparādhino ye, teṣāṁ tu tad-bahirmukhatvam eva syād iti vyatirekeṇa tad draḍhayati—kalāv iti ||43|| 

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** kiṁ ca, kaleḥ sandhyānantaraṁ tu mahāntam anartham āha—kalāv iti dvābhyām ||43||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.44 ||**

**yan-nāmadheyaṁ mriyamāṇa āturaḥ**

**patan skhalan vā vivaśo gṛṇan pumān |**

**vimukta-karmārgala uttamāṁ gatiṁ**

**prāpnoti yakṣyanti na taṁ kalau janāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : vivaśo gṛṇan** san | **vimuktāḥ karma**-rūpā **argalāḥ** pratibandhā yasya saḥ ||44||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **kapāṭam araraṁ tulye tad-viṣkambhe'rgalaṁ na nā ity amaraḥ | **yan-nāmadheyaṁ mriyamāṇaḥ** iti, 


    yasāvatāra-guṇa-karma-viḍambanāni


    nāmāni ye'su vigame vivaśā gṛṇanti | 


    te'neka-janma-śamalaṁ sahasaiva hitvā 


    saṁyānty apāvṛtamṛtaṁ tam ajaṁ prapadya || [bhā.pu. 3.9.15] 

iti tṛtīye brahma-stuty-ukteḥ ||44||

———————————————————————————————————————

**kaivalya-dīpikā : yad** iti | **āturaḥ** sa-rogaḥ | **karma** pāpam | **uttamā gatir** mokṣaḥ | **no yakṣyanti** na pūjayanti ||44|| [mu.pha. 8.38]

———————————————————————————————————————

**sanātana-gosvāmī : **[hari-bhakti-vilāsaḥ 11.372] tatra ca yat phalonmukhaṁ karma, tad eva prārabdham ucyate | tac ca dvividhaṁ—vartamāna-dehopabhogyam ekam, anyac ca śarīrāntaropabhogyam | yathā—bharatasya mṛga-śarīra-kāraṇaṁ, tac ca śrī-bhāgavate śrī-bādarāyaṇenaiva siddhāntitam asti | mṛga-dārakābhāsena svārabdha-karmaṇā yogārambhaṇato vibhraṁśita ity-ādibhiḥ | tatra nātaḥ paraṁ [bhā.pu. 6.2.46] iti pūrva-ślokena vartamāna-śarīra-bhogya-prārabdha-nāśanaṁ likhitvā, idānīṁ śarīrāntare’vaśya-bhogyasyāpi prārabdhasya kṣapaṇaṁ likhati | yad vā, dvābhyām eva ślokābhyām aśeṣa-prārabdha-vināśitvam eva darśayati—yan-nāmeti | vivaśo’pi gṛṇan uccārayan san | vimuktāḥ karma-rūpā argalā avaśya-bhogyatvena durvārā api pratibandhā yasya saḥ | uttamāṁ śrī-vaikuṇṭha-prāpti-lakṣaṇāṁ gatiṁ phalaṁ, taṁ na yakṣyanti, nāma-saṅkīrtanādinā na seviṣyanta iti kali-doṣa uktaḥ ||44|| 

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tadānīṁ pāṣaṇḍair vibhinna-cetastvena tad-yājana[^17]-vaimukhyaṁ tu tan-nāma-vimukhānām eva syād ity abhipretya prāyeṇety eva vyanakti—yan-nāmeti | nāmāny evopasaṁhariṣyate—kaleḥ [bhā.pu. 12.3.43-44] ity ādi-dvābhyām[^18] ||44||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** _na vyākhyātam._

 **...**

**|| 12.3.45 ||**

**puṁsāṁ kali-kṛtāṁ doṣān dravya-deśātma-sambhavān |**

**sarvān harati citta-stho bhagavān puruṣottamaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tad evaṁ kali-doṣān prapañcya prastutaṁ tan nistāroṣāyam āha—puṁsām iti ṣaḍbhiḥ | dravya-deśātmabhiḥ saṁbhavo yeṣāṁ tān | citta-sthaś citte sphuritaḥ ||45||

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** kaler doṣam uktvā tad-doṣa-śamanārtham anāyāsa-siddham auṣadhaṁ darśayati—puṁsāṁ kali-kṛtān doṣān ity-ādi | kalau na rājan jagatāṁ paraṁ gurum [bhā.pu. 12.3.43] ity-ādinā, yan nāma-dheyaṁ mriyamāṇa āturaḥ [bhā.pu. 12.3.44] ity-ādinā ca śloka-dvayena kalau bhagavad-bhajana eva nāsti, kathaṁ sarvān harati cittastho bhagavān puruṣottamaḥ ? śrutaḥ saṅkīrtitaḥ [bhā.pu. 12.3.46] ity-ādinā kalau bhagavati citta-sthirī-karaṇam ? tatrāha—kaler doṣa-nidhe rājan [bhā.pu. 12.3.51] ity-ādi, kalau tad dhari-kīrtanāt [bhā.pu. 12.3.52] iti cet tathāpi pūrva-pakṣas tad-avastha eva sthitaḥ | hari-kīrtanaṁ yadi bhavati, tadaivam | hari-saṅkīrtanam eva kathaṁ bhavatu ? evaṁ cet bhagavata eva kṛpāvatāro gūḍhaṁ kaścid atra boddhavyaḥ | uktaṁ ca navama-skandhānte—


    yadā yadā hi dharmasya kṣayo vṛddhiś ca pāpmanaḥ | 


    tadā tu bhagavān īśa ātmānaṁ sṛjate hariḥ ||** **[bhā.pu. 9.24.56] iti |

atra bhagavad-avatāre kāla-viṣayo nāsti, na cāvatārasya kathita-krama-rūpeṇaiva niyama iti sthitam ||45||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **yad eva nāma bhagavad-rūpeṇa sphurat tad vidadhātīty āha—puṁsām iti ||45||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** yad uktaṁ kenopāyena kali-doṣān nāśayiṣyanti tatrottaram āha—puṁsām iti | dravya-deśa-manaḥsu śuddhy-abhāvena sambhavo yeṣāṁ tān ||45||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.46 ||**

**śrutaḥ saṅkīrtito dhyātaḥ pūjitaś cādṛto’pi vā |**

**nṛṇāṁ dhunoti bhagavān hṛt-stho janmāyatāśubham ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** _na vyākhyātam._

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **dravyamannādi, deśaḥ kīkaṭādiḥ, ātmāna indriyāṇi taiḥ ||45-46||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **bhagavataḥ svabhāva eva tādṛśa ity āha—śruta iti tribhiḥ ||46||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **citta-sthaḥ smṛtaḥ san, na kevalam etān eva doṣān harati, api tu prācīnārvācīnaṁ sarvam api pāpam ity āha—śrutaḥ iti ||46||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.47 ||**

**yathā hemni sthito vahnir durvarṇaṁ hanti dhātu-jam |**

**evam ātma-gato viṣṇur yoginām aśubhāśayam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ayam evoṣāyo nānya iti sa-dṛṣṭāntam āha—yatheti | dhātu-jaṁ tāmrādi-saṁśleṣa-jātaṁ hemno durvarṇaṁ mālinyaṁ tatra sthito vahnir eva hanti harati, na tu toyādi | evaṁ yoginām api viṣṇur eva, na tu yogādikam ity arthaḥ ||47||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tat-svabhāvas tv ayaṁ nānyatra sambhavatīty āha—yatheti dvābhyām ||47||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** kiṁ cāntaḥ-karaṇa-śuddhau bhagavat-smaraṇādir evopāyo nānya iti sa-dṛṣṭāntam āha—yatheti | dhātujaṁ tāmrādi-saṁśleṣa-jātaṁ hemno durvarṇaṁ mālinyaṁ, tatra sthito vahnir eva harati, na tu toyādi evaṁ yoginām api viṣṇur eva, na tu yama-niyamādikam ||47||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.48 ||**

**vidyā-tapaḥ-prāṇa-nirodha-maitrī**

**tīrthābhiṣeka-vrata-dāna-japyaiḥ |**

**nātyanta-śuddhiṁ labhate’ntar-ātmā**

**yathā hṛdi-sthe bhagavaty anante ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **etad eva vivṛṇoti—**vidyā** iti | **vidyā** deva-toṣāsanā ||48||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **mandādhikāriṇāṁ kṣipra-pravṛtty-arthaṁ sa-dṛṣṭāntam āha | durvarṇam ity anena ratna-śāstroktā aṣṭādaśa doṣā uktās te ca dhātv-antara-saṅga-kṛtāḥ santi tān hantīty arthaḥ | yad vā, dhātujaṁ gaurika-samudbhūtam ity arthaḥ | viśeṣād gaurike'sthina ca iti medinyāṁ dhātur gairikam uktam | **ātmā** manaḥ ||47-48||

———————————————————————————————————————

**kaivalya-dīpikā : vidyā** vairājopāsanā[^19] | **prāṇa-nirodhaḥ** prāṇāyāmaḥ | **japyaṁ** praṇavādi nānyat ||48|| [mu.pha. 9.5]

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **etad vivṛṇoti—vidyeti ||48||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.49 ||**

**tasmāt sarvātmanā rājan hṛdi-sthaṁ kuru keśavam |**

**mriyamāṇo hy avahitas tato yāsi parāṁ gatim ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā),** **viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** _na vyākhyātam._

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **yato vidyādibhyo harerhṛdi karaṇaṁ śreṣṭhaṁ tasmād ity arthaḥ| avahitaḥ sāvadhānaḥ| tato hṛdi keśavakaraṇāt | parāṁ tadrūpāvāptirūpām ||49||

———————————————————————————————————————

**kaivalya-dīpikā : tasmāt** yasmāt | tato hari-smaraṇāt | puruṣaḥ parāṁ gatim yāti ||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tad evaṁ tat-pṛṣṭārthān sarvān samāpayiṣyaṁs tat kartavyam upadiśati—tasmād iti | sarvātmanā sarveṇaiva prayatnena | tatraiva kaimutyena hetum āha—mriyeti | hi yasmād anyo’pi yaḥ kaścit mriyamāṇo’py avahitaḥ, tasmin kṛtāvadhānaś cet, tan-mātrād eva parāṁ sarvotkṛṣṭāṁ gatiṁ[^20] yāti | tvaṁ punas tasya paramāntaraṅgaḥ kim utety arthaḥ ||49||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.50 ||**

**mriyamāṇair abhidhyeyo bhagavān puruṣottamaḥ |**

**ātma-bhāvaṁ nayaty aṅga sarvātmā sarva-saṁśrayaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ātma-bhāvaṁ sva-svarūpam ||50||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tāmevāha—ātmabhāvam iti | tatra hetuḥ—sarvamādatta iti sarvātmā | tatrāpi hetuḥ—sarvasaṁśrayaḥ sarvādhāraḥ ||50||

———————————————————————————————————————

**kaivalya-dīpikā : mriyamāṇair** iti | **ātma-bhāvaṁ** svarūpa-prāptim | **sarvātmanā** sulabhatvam | sarvātmatvāt sarva-sambhavatvāt | bhaktasya viṣṇu-vivartatvāt sad-bhāvāpattiḥ ||50|| [mu.pha. 9.7]

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **ata evānyair api **mriyamāṇair abhidhyeyaḥ** | **ātma-bhāvaṁ** ātmano bhaktiṁ | yad vā, parama-premṇātma-tulyatām ity arthaḥ ||50||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** yato mriyamāṇo hy ajāmilādi-sadṛśo’pi janaḥ, avahitaḥ na vidyate vahitam avahitam avadhānaṁ yasya tathā-bhūto’pi, tataḥ keśavāt yathā-kṛtatracid api smṛtāt abhidhyeyaḥ dhyātuṁ śakyaś cet tadā ātma-bhāvam ātmani premāṇaṁ nayati tān prāpayati | nanu tat-samaye bhagavad-dhyānaṁ teṣāṁ kathaṁ jñeyaṁ syāt, tatrāha—sarvātmā lokā na jānantu nāma, sa tu jānāty evety arthaḥ | nanu kathaṁ sakṛd dhyāna-mātrād eva premāṇaṁ dadāti ? tatrāha—sarveṣāṁ sādhyānāṁ sādhanānāṁ ca sambhavo yasmāt saḥ | mahodārasya tasya kim etac citram iti bhāvaḥ ||50||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.51 ||**

**kaler doṣa-nidhe rājann asti hy eko mahān guṇaḥ |**

**kīrtanād eva kṛṣṇasya mukta-saṅgaḥ paraṁ vrajet ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **idānīṁ kaliṁ stauti dvābhyām—kaler doṣa-nidhe rājann iti ||51||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **kaliḥ kevalaṁ doṣākara eva na kintu guṇāpādakopyauṣadhopacitadravyavadityāha—kaler iti | doṣanidherdoṣasamudrasya guṇam āha—kīrtanādeveti, yathaiko nṛpo'saṅkhyāna daṇḍyānhanti tathaiko guṇaḥ sarvān doṣāniti bhāvaḥ ||51||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **kalim ity-ādinaiva kaler ity-ādi vyākhyātam eva | kali-doṣa-praśamanatvena nāma-kīrtana-smaraṇa-māhātmyam uktvopasaṁharati—kaler iti | astu tāvad āyāsa-sādhyaṁ dhyānam[^21] | hi yasmāt | anāyāsa-sādhyāt kīrtanād evety arthaḥ |[^22] sa ca kaliḥ śreyo’tikrama-hetūnāṁ doṣāṇāṁ nidhir api | kaler eko guṇaḥ kīrtanādara-rūpo mahān evāsti, kaṁsādeḥ śrī-nāradādara iva | atas tasya vighnodyamābhāvāt siddhyaty eva nāma-kīrtayitety āha—kīrtanād eveti ||51|| [bhakti-sandarbha 87-anucchedo draṣṭavyaḥ]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** idānīṁ kaleḥ sarvebhyo’pi yugebhyaḥ śraiṣṭhyam āha—kaler iti dvābhyām | doṣāṇāṁ nidher api kaler eko guṇo rājann asti virājamāno vāsti | yathā eka eva rājā asaṅkhyān api dasyūn hanti, tathaivaika eva guṇaḥ sarvān apy ukta-lakṣaṇa-doṣān hantīti bhāvaḥ | sa eva kaḥ ? tatrāha—kīrtanād eveti | nātra dhyānāder apy apekṣety arthaḥ | yad vā, kīrtanād eva, kim uta kīrtana-sahita-dhyānādibhyaḥ, paraṁ sarvotkṛṣṭaṁ puruṣārthaṁ premāṇam ||51||

 **...**

**|| 12.3.52 ||**

**kṛte yad dhyāyato viṣṇuṁ tretāyāṁ yajato makhaiḥ |**

**dvāpare paricaryāyāṁ kalau tad dhari-kīrtanāt ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tat sarvaṁ hari-kīrtanād eva kalau bhavati nānyasmin yuge | uktaṁ ca—


    dhyāyan kṛte yajan yajñais-tretāyāṁ dvāpare’rcayan |


    yad āpnoti tad āpnoti kalau saṅkīrtya keśavam || iti ||52||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tatsarvaṁ kṛtādiyugaprāpyam | kalāveva nānyasminyuge | tad uktam—dhyāyankṛte iti purāṇāntare ||52||

iti śrīmadbhāgavate ma0 dvādaśa-skandhe bhāvārthadīpikāyāṁ ṭīkāyāṁ tṛtīyo'dhyāyaḥ ||3||

———————————————————————————————————————

**sanātana-gosvāmī : **[ha.bha.vi. 11.457] param utkṛṣṭaṁ bhagavad-bhakti-māhātmyādi-viṣayakaṁ jñānam ||52||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **iyaṁ ca kīrtanākhyā bhaktir bhagavato jīveṣu dravya-jāti-guṇa-kriyābhir dīna-janaika-viṣayāpāra-karuṇā-mayīti śruti-smṛti-purāṇādi-viśrutiḥ | kalau ca dīnatvaṁ, yathā brahma-vaivarte—


    ataḥ kalau tapo-yoga-vidyā-yājñādikāḥ kriyāḥ |


    sāṅgāḥ bhavanti na kṛtāḥ kuśalair api dehibhiḥ || iti |

ata eva kalau svabhāvata evātidīneṣu lokeṣv āvirbhūya tān anāyāsenaiva tat-tad-yuga-gata-mahā-sādhanānāṁ sarvam eva phalaṁ dadānā sā kṛtārthayati | yata eva tayaiva kalau bhagavato viśeṣataś ca santoṣo bhavati | 


    tathā caivottamaṁ loke tapaḥ śrī-hari-kīrtanam |


    kalau yuge viśeṣeṇa viṣṇu-prītyai samācaret ||

iti skānda-cāturmāsya-māhātmya-vacanānusāreṇa | tad evam vadan kīrtanaṁ hi kalāv api sarva-guṇa-vāridhir ity āha—kṛta iti | yad yat kṛtādiṣu tena tena sādhanena syāt, tac ca tac ca, tad ity eka-śeṣāt, tat sarvaṁ kalau hari-kīrtanād eva bhavati, prāpnotīty arthaḥ | ata evoktam anyatra,


    dhyāyan kṛte yajan yajñais-tretāyāṁ dvāpare’rcayan |


    yad āpnoti tad āpnoti kalau saṅkīrtya keśavam || iti ||52|| [bhakti-sandarbhaḥ 270]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** sarva-yuga-gatāni bhagavat-prāpti-sādhanāni kalir eka eva dadāti, tatrāpi sva-sambhavād ekasmāt sarva-sugamāt kīrtanād eva dadātīty āha—kṛte iti | tat sarvaṁ hari-kīrtanād eva bhavati ||52||

iti sārārtha-darśinyāṁ harṣiṇyāṁ bhakta-cetasām |

dvādaśe tṛtīyo’dhyāyaḥ saṅgataḥ saṅgataḥ satām ||*||

 **...**


    iti śrīmad-bhāgavate mahā-purāṇe brahma-sūtra-bhāṣye pāramahaṁsyaṁ saṁhitāyāṁ vaiyāsikyāṁ dvādaśa-skandhe 


    yugānuvarṇanaṁ nāma 


    tṛtīyo’dhyāyaḥ |

|| 12.3 ||

**…**

**(12.4)**


### atha caturtho’dhyāyaḥ


## pralaya-varṇanaṁ nāma

**|| 12.4.1 ||**

**śrī-śuka uvāca—**

**kālas te paramāṇv-ādir dvi-parārdhāvadhir nṛpa |**

**kathito yuga-mānaṁ ca śṛṇu kalpa-layāv api ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :**

caturthe tu caturdhoktā layā naimittikādayaḥ |

tatra saṁsāra-nistāro hari-kīrtyaiva varṇyate ||

kali-doṣa-nivartakaṁ hari-nāma-saṅkīrtanādikaṁ sa eva ca kalau paramo dharma iti praśna-dvayasyottaram uktam | yac cānyat pṛṣṭaṁ pralaya-kalpayor mānaṁ brūhīti [bhā.pu. 3.1.11] tad idānīṁ tṛtīya-skandhokta-kāla-mānānuvāda-pūrvakaṁ nirūpayati—kāla iti | sa kālaḥ paramāṇur vai yo bhuṅkte paramāṇutāṁ [bhā.pu. 3.11.4] ity-ādinā kālaḥ kathitaḥ | 


    catvāri trīṇi dve caikaṁ kṛtādiṣu yathā-kramam | 


    saṅkhyātāni sahasrāṇi dvi-guṇāni śatāni ca || [bhā.pu. 3.11.19] iti yuga-mānaṁ kathitam ||1||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **evakāreṇa kalau nāmaiva nāmaiva kalau nāmaiva kevalam iti smṛtirākṛṣyate | tatra naimittikādimadhye nṛpeti—kālajñānaṁ vinā nṛpālanaṁ na sambhavatīti bhāvaḥ ||1||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :**

naimittikādyān pralayāṁś caturthe caturaḥ kramāt |

uktvopasañjahāra śrī-śukaḥ kṛṣṇa-kathāmṛtam ||

yac ca pṛṣṭaṁ pralayāklapayor mānaṁ brūhi [bhā.pu. 3.1.11] iti, tatra tṛtīya-skandhokta-kālānuvāda-pūrvakam āha—kāla iti ||1||

 **...**

**|| 12.4.2 ||**

**catur-yuga-sahasraṁ tu brahmaṇo dinam ucyate |**

**sa kalpo yatra manavaś caturdaśa viśām-pate ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tatra kalpa-mānam āha—catur-yugeti | yatra caturdaśa manavaḥ krameṇa bhavanti ||2||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **yatra dine | viśāmpate iti—prajāpālanāsaktatvāttvaṁ kālaṁ nākalayasīti bhāvaḥ ||2||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.4.3 ||**

**tad-ante pralayas tāvān brāhmī rātrir udāhṛtā |**

**trayo lokā ime tatra kalpante pralayāya hi ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **pralayas tu catur-vidhaḥ—naimittikaḥ, prākṛtikaḥ, ātyantikaḥ, nityaś ceti | tatra naimittikaṁ pralayaṁ māna-sahitam āha—tad anta iti dvābhyām | tāvān catur-yuga-sahasra-pramāṇaḥ | saiva brāhmī rātriḥ ||3||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tadante dinānte | yatra rātrau ||3||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** tāvān caturyuga-sahasra-pramāṇaḥ ||3||

 **...**

**|| 12.4.4 ||**

**eṣa naimittikaḥ proktaḥ pralayo yatra viśva-sṛk |**

**śete’nantāsano viśvam ātmasāt-kṛtya cātma-bhūḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **naimittikatvaṁ darśayati | yatra yadā viśva-sṛk śrī-nārāyaṇo viśvam ātma-sāt-kṛtya svasminn upasaṁhṛtya śete, ātma-bhūr brahmā ca tasmin śete | tayor abheda-vivakṣayā vā brahmaṇa evānantāsanatvam uktam | brahmaṇo nidrāṁ nimittī-kṛtya pravartamāno loka-traya-pralayo naimittika ity ārthaḥ ||4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **eṣa naimittaka ity upalakṣaṇam |_|_4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **pralayāś catvāras tatraiṣa pralayo naimittikaḥ prathamaḥ, viśva-sṛk nārāyaṇa ātma-sātkṛtya svasminn upasaṁhṛtya śete | ātma-bhūr brahmā ca tasmin praviśya śete | ata eva brahmaṇo nidrāṁ nimittīkṛtya pravartamāno loka-traya-pralayo naimittikaḥ, eṣa eva dainandina-śabda-vācyaś ca ||4||

 **...**

**|| 12.4.5 ||**

**dvi-parārdhe tv atikrānte brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ |**

**tadā prakṛtayaḥ sapta kalpante pralayāya vai ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **prākṛtikaṁ pralayam āha dvābhyām, dvi-parārdhe tu brahmaṇa āyuṣi | sapta-prakṛtayo mahad-ahaṅkāra-pañca-tan-mātrāṇi ||5||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ity artha iti—atra pravartamānerthe ṭhak pratyayaḥ ||4-5||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **manvantara-nimittatvam api tad-antar-bhūtaṁ jñeyam |_|_5||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **prākṛtikaṁ pralayam āha—dvi-parārdhe tv iti dvābhyām | ādyaḥ parārdhopakrānta eva, dvitīye’pi parārdhe atikrānte sati brahmaṇa āyuḥ-samāptau satyāṁ sapta-prakṛtayo mahad-ahaṅkāra-tan-mātra-pañcakāni ||5||

 **...**

**|| 12.4.6 ||**

**eṣa prākṛtiko rājan pralayo yatra līyate |**

**aṇḍa-koṣas tu saṅghāto vighāta upasādite ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **saṅghāto mahad-ādi-kārya-bhūtaḥ, prakṛtīnāṁ tat-kārya-brahmāṇḍasya ca pralayāt prākṛtika ity arthaḥ | vighāte vighāta-kāraṇe upasādite sati ||6||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **he rājann iti—dhairyeṇa mṛtyukāle'pi tava dīptirna naṣṭeti bhāvaḥ | vighātakāraṇe'kāle upasādite prāpte sati ||6||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **prakṛteḥ sakāśād udbhūta-vastūnāṁ prākṛtāv eva praveśāt prākṛtikaḥ saṅghātaḥ | mahad-ādi-tattva-samūha evāṇḍa-koṣaḥ | vighāte vighāta-kāle upasanne sati ||6||

 **...**

**|| 12.4.7 ||**

**parjanyaḥ śata-varṣāṇi bhūmau rājan na varṣati |**

**tadā niranne hy anyonyaṁ bhakṣyamāṇāḥ kṣudhārditāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tad evāha—parjanya ity-ādinā buddhīndriyārtha-rūpeṇety ataḥ prāktanena granthena ||7||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tad eva vighātakāraṇamevāha | tadā varṣaṇābhāvena niranne'nnābhāve sati ||7||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** tatra prakāram āha—parjanya iti ||7||

 **...**

**|| 12.4.8 ||**

**kṣayaṁ yāsyanti śanakaiḥ kālenopadrutāḥ prajāḥ |**

**sāmudraṁ daihikaṁ bhaumaṁ rasaṁ sāṁvartako raviḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **sāmudrādikaṁ sarvaṁ rasaṁ raviḥ ||8||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **sāṁvartakaḥ pralayakālikaḥ | rasaṁ rasanīyamārdratvam iti yāvat, rasaṁ jalamity arthaḥ | yadyapi meghapuṣpaṁ ghanarasaḥ ity amarokterna kevalarasaśabdo jalavācī tathāpyekadeśanyāyena tathāstyeveti jñeyam ||8||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.4.9 ||**

**raśmibhiḥ pibate ghoraiḥ sarvaṁ naiva vimuñcati |**

**tataḥ saṁvartako vahniḥ saṅkarṣaṇa-mukhotthitaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** pibate ākarṣati ||8||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tato rasaśoṣānantaram ||9||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.4.10 ||**

**dahaty anila-vegotthaḥ śūnyān bhū-vivarān atha |**

**upary adhaḥ samantāc ca śikhābhir vahni-sūryayoḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **anila-vegottho vāyu-vegodbhūtaḥ | “anila-vego vā” iti pāṭhe anilena vego yasya saḥ, vāḥ raviṇā raśmibhiḥ pītam udakaṁ ca dahatīty arthaḥ | “anila-vego vai” iti tu pāṭhaḥ su-gamaḥ | bhū-vivarān pātālādīn śūnyān raviṇā daihika-rasākarṣaṇāt prāṇi-rahitān | śikhābhir jvālābhiḥ ||10||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ity artha iti—meghāntargatam api jalaṁ śoṣayatīti bhāvaḥ | sūryapakṣe śikhābhī raśmibhiḥ ||10||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** _na vyākhyātam._

 **...**

**|| 12.4.11 ||**

**dahyamānaṁ vibhāty aṇḍaṁ dagdha-gomaya-piṇḍa-vat |**

**tataḥ pracaṇḍa-pavano varṣāṇām adhikaṁ śatam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kiñcid adhikaṁ varṣāṇāṁ śatam | sāṁvartakaḥ pralaya-hetuḥ paro vāyur vāti tadā rajasāvṛtaṁ khaṁ dhūmraṁ bhavati ||11||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tato brahmāṇḍadāhottaram | pracaṇḍapavanaḥ saśabdo vāyuḥ | adhikaṁ kiñcidadhikam ||11||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **kiñcid adhikaṁ varṣāṇāṁ śataṁ vyāpya vāti, tadā rajasāvṛtaṁ khaṁ dhūmraṁ bhavati ||11||

 **...**

**|| 12.4.12 ||**

**paraḥ sāṁvartako vāti dhūmraṁ khaṁ rajasāvṛtam |**

**tato megha-kulāny aṅga citra-varṇāny anekaśaḥ ||**

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **paro balavattaraḥ | tato rajaḥkṛtākāśadhūmratvānantaram ||12||

 **...**

**|| 12.4.13 ||**

**śataṁ varṣāṇi varṣanti nadanti rabhasa-svanaiḥ |**

**tata ekodakaṁ viśvaṁ brahmāṇḍa-vivarāntaram ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **rabhasa-svanais tīvra-garjitaiḥ | brahmāṇḍa-vivaram adhyagataṁ viśvam ekodakam akārṇavodaka-vyāptaṁ bhavati ||13||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **antare tiṣṭhatītyāntaraṁ brahmāṇḍavivarasyāntaraṁ brahmāṇḍavivarāntaram | ekamudakam eva yatra pratīyate nānyattadekodakam ||13||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** _na vyākhyātam._

 **...**

**|| 12.4.14 ||**

**tadā bhūmer gandha-guṇaṁ grasanty āpa uda-plave |**

**grasta-gandhā tu pṛthivī pralayatvāya kalpate ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **uda-plave udakenāplave sati | pralayatvāyābhāvāya ||14||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **bhūmergandhaguṇamāpo prasanti bhūlayāya tasyāmabhibhāvayanti | evamagre'pyūhyam | anyaguṇasyānyatra layāsambhavāt tanmātrāṇāṁ kāraṇatvakalpane pūrvaṁ layāsambhavāttanmātrakāryatve bhūtānāṁ bhūtāntare layāsambhavāc ca grastadhedakaguṇāpralayatvāya kalpate yogyo bhavati ||14||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **pralayatvāya prakṛṣṭo layo yasyā sā pralayā, tasyā bhāvaḥ pralayatvaṁ tasmai, nāśāyety arthaḥ ||14||

 **...**

**|| 12.4.15 ||**

**apāṁ rasam atho tejas tā līyante’tha nīrasāḥ |**

**grasate tejaso rūpaṁ vāyus tad-rahitaṁ tadā ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā), jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tā āpaḥ | anīrasā rasahīnāḥ santaḥ | tadrahitaṁ rūparahitam ||15||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** apāṁ rasaṁ tejo grasati ||15||

 **...**

**|| 12.4.16 ||**

**līyate cānile tejo vāyoḥ khaṁ grasate guṇam |**

**sa vai viśati khaṁ rājaṁs tataś ca nabhaso guṇam ||**

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **vāyorguṇaṁ sparśam | khamākāśaḥ | sa vāyuḥ ||16||

 **...**

**|| 12.4.17 ||**

**śabdaṁ grasati bhūtādir nabhas tam anu līyate |**

**taijasaś cendriyāṇy aṅga devān vaikāriko guṇaiḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **bhūtādis tāmaso ’haṅkāraḥ | guṇair vṛttibhiḥ saha ||17||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **he aṅga rājan ||17||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **bhūtādis tāmaso ’haṅkāraḥ | taijaso’haṅkāra indriyāṇi grasati | mahān ahaṅkāraṁ guṇais tad-vṛttibhiḥ saha grasati taṁ mahāntam ||17||

 **...**

**|| 12.4.18 ||**

**mahān grasaty ahaṅkāraṁ guṇāḥ sattvādayaś ca tam |**

**grasate’vyākṛtaṁ rājan guṇān kālena coditam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **avyākṛtaṁ pradhānam ||18||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **mahān īkṣaṇam | ahaṅkāraṁ bahubhavanasaṅkalpam | mahadahaṅkārayorbhagavad-īkṣaṇasaṅkalparūpayostajjanyatve sati tajjanyajanako vyāpāra iti lakṣaṇasadbhāvena māyopahiteśvaravyāpāratvena nimittatvepyupādānatvāsambhavākālena svopahiteneśvareṇa noditamavyaktaṁ tadupādhimāyātmakājñānam | guṇānsvakāryabhūtān ||18||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.4.19 ||**

**na tasya kālāvayavaiḥ pariṇāmādayo guṇāḥ |**

**anādy anantam avyaktaṁ nityaṁ kāraṇam avyayam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tasya tu layo nāstīty āha—tasyeti | kāla-vayavair aho-rātrādibhiḥ | guṇā bhāva-vikārāḥ | pariṇāmo vipariṇāmaḥ | avyaktam astitva-vikāra-śūnyam | nityaṁ sarvadaika-rūpam, hrāsa-vṛddhi-rahitam ity arthaḥ | avyayam apakṣaya-śūnyam | sarvatra hetuḥ—kāraṇam iti |

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tasyāvyākṛtasya tadavayavavibhāgasya paścādbhāvitayā taddhetutvānupapatteḥ | guṇā dharmāḥ bodhātpūrvamabādhīnnityatvāvyayatve tasyeti kecit ||19||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **tasya pradhānasya kālāvayavair aho-rātraiḥ pariṇāmo vipariṇāmaś caturtho vikāraḥ | anādīti prathamo vikāro janma na, anantam ity anto na, avyaktam ity astitva-lakṣaṇa-vikāro na, nityaṁ sadaika-rūpam iti vṛddhir na, avyayam ity apakṣayo neti | vikāra-ṣaṭkaṁ niṣiddham ||18||

 **...**

**|| 12.4.20 ||**

**na yatra vāco na mano na sattvaṁ**

**tamo rajo vā mahad-ādayo’mī |**

**na prāṇa-buddhīndriya-devatā vā**

**na sanniveśaḥ khalu loka-kalpaḥ ||**[^23]

**madhvācāryaḥ (bhāgavata-tātparyam) :** na yatra vāca ity-ādi kālākhyasya brahmaṇaḥ svarūpam ||20||[^24]

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kiṁ ca, vāg-ādi-gocarasya sa-viśeṣasya vikārā bhavanti, idaṁ tu na tathety āha—na yatreti dvābhyām | loka-kalpo loka-rūpaḥ sanniveśo racanā-viśeṣo nāsti ||20||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **anyadāha—kiñceti | idamavyaktaṁ tu na tathā vāgādigocaro netyarthaḥ | guṇānāṁ tadrūpeṇa sattve'pi sāmye vibhāgābhāvenābhāvoktiḥ ||20||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** kiṁ ca, vāg-ādi-gocarasya sa-vikārasya vikārā bhavanti, idaṁ tu na tathety āha—na yatreti dvābhyām | loka-kalpo loka-rūpaḥ sanniveśo racanā-viśeṣaḥ ||20||

 **...**

**|| 12.4.21 ||**

**na svapna-jāgran na ca tat suṣuptaṁ**

**na khaṁ jalaṁ bhūr anilo’gnir arkaḥ |**

**saṁsupta**[^25]**-vac chūnya-vad apratarkyaṁ**

**tan mūla-bhūtaṁ padam āmananti ||**[^26]

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **svapna-jāgrat svapna-jāgarāvasthā-yuktam | saṁsupta-vad indriyābhāvāt | śūnya-sādṛśye hetuḥ—apratarkyam | na punaḥ śūnyam evety āha—tad iti ||21||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **suṣuptaṁ vyaṣṭisuṣuptirneti jñeyam | suṣuptavat kāryādarśanāt ||21||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.4.22 ||**

**layaḥ prākṛtiko hy eṣa puruṣāvyaktayor yadā |**

**śaktayaḥ sampralīyante vivaśāḥ kāla-vidrutāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **upasaṁharati—laya iti | śaktayaḥ sattvādayaḥ ||22||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **saṁpralīyante sāmyenākṣubdhāstiṣṭhanti | śaktayaḥ pṛthivyādaya iti tīrthaḥ | layaḥ | kathita iti śeṣaḥ | kālena vidrutā abhibhūtā ata eva vivaśāḥ ||22||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **upasaṁharati—laya iti | śaktayaḥ sattvādaya eva līyante, na tu tayoḥ kadāpi kāpi kṣatir iti bhāvaḥ ||22||

 **...**

**|| 12.4.23 ||**

**buddhīndriyārtha-rūpeṇa jñānaṁ bhāti tad-āśrayam |**

**dṛśyatvāvyatirekābhyām ādy-antavad avastu yat ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ātyantikaṁ layam āha—buddhīndriyeti dvadaśabhiḥ | ātyantika-layo mokṣaḥ sa ca brahma-jñānena sarva-prapañca-layātmakaḥ | na ca prapañcasyātmavat satyatve layaḥ sambhavatīti jñāna-rūpād brahmaṇaḥ pṛthag-bhūtasya tasyāsattvam upapādayati | **buddhiś cendriyāṇi cārthāś** cety evaṁ grāhaka-karaṇa-grāhya-rūpeṇa **teṣām āśraya**-bhūtaṁ **jñānam** eva **bhāti,** na pṛthak | tatra hetum āha—**dṛśyatvāvyatirekābhyām** iti | ato **yad ādy-antavat tad avastu** | atraivaṁ prayogaḥ—vimataṁ san na bhavati | dṛśyatvāt kāraṇāvyatirekād ādy-antavattvāc ca, rajju-sarpādivad iti ||23||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **buddhirūpeṇendriyarūpeṇa viṣayarūpeṇa ca teṣāṁ buddhyādīnāmāśrayamātmasvarūpaṁ jñānam eva | tatrātmasvarūpajñānatve | ato dṛśyatvāvyatirekābhyām, atra buddhyādīnāmātmasvarūpajñānatve niścetavye | evaṁ vakṣyamāṇarītyā | prayogo'numānam | vimataṁ vivādāspadībhūtaṁ buddhyādi | kāraṇāvyatirekāt kāraṇābhinnatvāt | ādinā svapnadṛśyavadghaṭādivad iti gṛhyate ||23||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tatra tad-āśrayatva-tat-prakāśyatva-tad-vyatiriktatvebhyo hetubhyo buddhīndriyādīnāṁ paramātma-svabhāva-śaktimayatvam āha—buddhīti | antaḥkaraṇa-bahiḥ-karaṇa-viṣaya-**rūpeṇa** paramātma-lakṣaṇaṁ **jñānam** eva **bhāti** | tasmād anyad eva buddhy-ādi-vastv ity arthaḥ, yatas **tad-āśrayaṁ** teṣām āśraya-rūpaṁ taj jñānam | klībatvam ārṣam | tathāpi rāja-bhṛtyayor ivātyanta eva bhedaḥ syāt | tatra hetv-antare’py āha—**dṛśyatvaṁ** tat-prakāśyatvam, **avyatirekas** tad-vyatireke vyatirekaḥ, tābhyām | tasmāt eka-deśa-sthitasyāgner jyotsnā vistāriṇī yathā [vi.pu. 1.22.56] ity-ādivad buddhy-ādīnāṁ tat-svābhāvika-śaktimayatvam eva setsyatīti bhāvaḥ | 

yat khalv **ādy-antavad** vaṇig-vīthy-ādau siddhaṁ śukty-ādau kadācid evāropitaṁ rajatam, tat punar **avastu,** tad-āśrayakatva-tat-prakāśakatva[^27]-tad-vyatirekābhāvāt[^28] śukty-ādi-vastu na bhavati, śukty-ādibhyo’nanyan[^29] na bhavatīty arthaḥ | tataś caika-vijñānena sarva-vijñāna-pratijñā virudhyeteti bhāvaḥ | evam asat-kārya-vādāntare’pi jñeyam ||23|| [paramātma-sandarbha 72]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** atha nirvāṇa-mokṣārthinā brahmaikya-bhāvanā-maya ātyantikaḥ pralaya ucyate | tac ca siṣādhayiṣitaṁ brahmaikyaṁ brahma-kāryasya dvaita-prapañcasyāsatyatve sādhita eva syād iti prauḍhiś cet tadāsatyam evedaṁ kārya-jātam ity āha—buddhīndriyeti navabhiḥ | **jñānaṁ** brahmaiva **buddhīndriyārtha-rūpeṇa bhāti** buddhy-ādīnāṁ brahma-śakti-pariṇāmatvād iti bhāvaḥ | jñānaṁ kīdṛśam ? **tad-āśrayaṁ** tasya buddhy-ādi-prapañcasya kāraṇatvād āśrayaḥ | klībatvam ārṣam | 

kiṁ ca, yad buddhy-ādi-prapañca-jātaṁ tat **ādy-antavat** utpatti-laya-viśiṣṭaṁ, ato vastutvenābhijñātam api asārvakālikatvāt paramārthato’**vastv** evety arthaḥ | aparāv api hetū āha—**dṛśyatvaṁ** ca, **avyatirekaḥ** kāraṇād vyatirekābhāvaś ca, tābhyām api avastu | 

atraivaṁ prayogaḥ | buddhy-ādi-prapañca-jātam adṛśyatvāt kāraṇāvyatirekādy-antavattvāc ca kanaka-kuṇḍalādivat paramārthato’vastu | atra vastu mithyaiveti mate’pi, syāc cec cit-sama ātmavat [bhā.pu. 12.4.29] ity agrima-stham anusṛtya dṛśyatvād ity atra cid-bhinnatve satīti viśeṣaṇam avaśya-deyam anyathāsya hetor vyabhicāraḥ syāt | tāsāṁ madhye sākṣād brahma-gopāla-purī hi [go.tā.u. 2.26] ity-ādi-śrutyā | man-niketaṁ tu nirguṇaṁ [bhā.pu. 11.25.25], nirguṇo mad-apāśrayaḥ [bhā.pu. 11.25.26] ity-ādi-bhagavad-uktyā ca dṛśyānām api bhagavad-dhāmādīnāṁ nirguṇatva-pratipādanena nityatvāt ||23||

 **...**

**|| 12.4.24 ||**

**dīpaś cakṣuś ca rūpaṁ ca jyotiṣo na pṛthag bhavet |**

**evaṁ dhīḥ khāni mātrāś ca na syur anyatamād ṛtāt ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tatrāvyatirekaṁ dṛṣṭāntena prapañcayati—dīpa iti | **dīpa-cakṣū-rūpāṇāṁ** tejo-viśeṣāṇāṁ tejaso yathā na vyatirekaḥ, tathā **dhīḥ** kartrī, **khāni** karaṇāni, **mātrā** viṣayāḥ, **ṛtād** brahmaṇaḥ **pṛthak na** **syuḥ**, brahma-kāryatvāt | nanv evaṁ kārya-kāraṇayor abhede kāryāsattve kāraṇasyāpy asattvaṁ prasajjeta ? tatrāha—**anyatamād** iti kāryād atyanta-vyatiriktād brahmaṇaḥ | prapañcād brahmaṇo’sti vyatirekaḥ, prapañcasya tu tato nāsti vyatireka ity arthaḥ ||24||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tatra dvayorhetvoḥ | atrākṣipati—nanv iti | ity artha iti—kāraṇasattātaḥ kāryasattā na pṛthak, kāryasattātaḥ kāraṇasattā tu pṛthagasti, tac ca mṛdghaṭādau sphuṭataram iti bhāvaḥ | yad vā, anyatamātsuṣuptisamādhyādau buddhyādibādhe'pi pariśiṣyamāṇatvāvyatiriktatvam ||24||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **ekasyāpi vastuno’ṁśa-bhedenāśrayāśrayitvaṁ svayam eva dṛṣṭāntena spaṣṭayati—dīpa iti | **dīpaś** **cakṣū-rūpāṇāṁ** mahā-bhūta-**jyotir**-aṁśa-rūpatvāt dīpādikaṁ **na** tataḥ **pṛthak** | evaṁ **dhī**-prabhṛtīni **ṛtāt** paramātmano **na** pṛthak **syuḥ** | tathāpi, yathā mahā-bhūta-jyotir-dīpādi-doṣeṇa na lipyate, tathā buddhy-ādi-doṣeṇa paramātmāpi | tadvad asyāpy anyatamatvād ity āha—**anyatamād** iti ||24|| [paramātma-sandarbha 73]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** atra dṛṣṭāntaḥ—**dīpa-cakṣū-rūpāṇāṁ** tejo-viśeṣāṇāṁ te yathā tejasaḥ kāraṇāvyatirekaḥ, tathā **dhīḥ** kartā, **khāni** indriyāṇi karaṇāni, **mātrā** viṣayāḥ, **ṛtād** brahmaṇaḥ **pṛthak na syuḥ** | yathā tejaḥ-kāryāṇi dīpa-cakṣū-rūpāṇi tejāṁsy evocyante, evaṁ brahma-kāryaṁ buddhīndriya-viṣayādikaṁ brahmaivocyate ity arthaḥ | 

nanv evaṁ kārya-kāraṇayor abhede kāryasyāsatyatve kāraṇasyāpy asatyatvaṁ prasajjeta, kāraṇasyaiva kārya-rūpeṇa pariṇatatvāt, tatrāha—**anyatamāt**, kāryebhyaḥ svarūpato’tyanta-vyatiriktāt, tasya kāraṇa-rūpāyāḥ prakṛter api paratvād iti bhāvaḥ ||24||

 **...**

**|| 12.4.25 ||**

**buddher jāgaraṇaṁ svapnaḥ suṣuptir iti cocyate |**

**māyā-mātram idaṁ rājan nānātvaṁ pratyag-ātmani ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **yadā tu buddher asattvaṁ, tadā tad-avasthanāṁ sutarām asattvam ity āśayenāha—buddher iti | nanu viśva-taijasa-prājñānām etā avasthā na buddher ity āśaṇkhyāha—**māyā-mātram** iti | **idaṁ** viśva-taijasa-prājña-rūpam ||25||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **atrākṣipati—nanv iti | yad vā, jāgaraṇaṁ svapnaḥ suṣuptiś ca pratyagātmanyadhiṣṭhāne buddher eva pariṇāmastasyāś ca māyākāryatvādidaṁ nānātvaṁ māyāmātraṁ nānātvātsvapnanānātvavat ||25||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tad evaṁ dhī-prabhṛtīnāṁ paramātma-svābhāvika-śaktimayatvam uktvā, tathāpi tebhyo bahiraṅga-śaktimayebhyo’ntaraṅga-śakti-taṭastha-śakti-viśiṣṭa-paramātmano ’nyatamatvena teṣām aśuddhatva-vyañjanayā sa-doṣatvam uktvā, teṣu dhī-prabhṛtiṣu adhyāsaṁ parityājayituṁ tisṛṣu dhī-vṛttiṣu tāvac chuddhasyaiva jīvasya sa-kāraṇam adhyāsam āha—buddher iti | buddhi-vṛtti-rūpaṁ **jāgaraṇaṁ** **svapnaḥ suṣuptir** **iti idaṁ pratyag-ātmani** śuddha-jīve viśva-taijasa-prājñatvākhyaṁ **nānātvaṁ** **māyā-mātraṁ** māyā-kṛtādhyāsa-mātreṇa jātam ity arthaḥ ||25|| [paramātma-sandarbha 74]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** yat tu viśva-taijasa-prājña iti jīvasya nānātvaṁ, tat tu buddhi-vṛttīnāṁ tritayatvāt, tasyāpi tritayatvaṁ mithyaivety āha—buddher iti | **jāgara-svapna-suṣuptayas** tisro vṛttayo **buddher** evety **ucyante** | atas tad-adhyāsāt **pratyag-ātmani** jīve’pi viśva-taijasa-prājña-saṁjñābhir **nānātvaṁ māyā-mātraṁ** mithyaivety arthaḥ ||25||

 **...**

**|| 12.4.26 ||**

**yathā jala-dharā vyomni bhavanti na bhavanti ca |**

**brahmaṇīdaṁ tathā viśvam avayavy udayāpyayāt ||**

**madhvācāryaḥ (bhāgavata-tātparyam) :** 

pratyekaṁ viṣṇu-rūpāṇāṁ bhrānti-mātrā bhidā matā |


    jagataś caiva viṣṇoś ca satyo bhedaḥ sadaiva tu ||


    yathākāśa-ghanau nityaṁ bhinnāv eva parasparam |


    evam īśo jagac caiva bhinnāv eva parasparam || iti ||25-26||

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ādy-antavattvād ity asya hetor asiddhim āśaṅkya sāvayavatvena sādhayati, yatheti | avayavīti | yat sāvayavaṁ tad ādy-anta-vad dhaṭādi-vad ity arthaḥ | ata udayāpyayād ādy-anta-vattvād viśvaṁ sanna bhavatīty arthaḥ | yad vā, pṛthag evāgamāpāyitvād viśvaṁ mithyā | brahma tu tad avadhitvāt satyam ity anena sādyate | dṛṣṭāntas tu pūrvokta eva | yathā jala-dharā vyomnīti dṛṣṭāntas tvāgamāpāyi-tad-avadhitva-mātre, na tu mithyātve ||26||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **na kadācidanīdṛśaṁ jagad iti mīmāṁsakamatena viśvasyādyantavattvaṁ nāstītyabhipretyāha—ādyantavattvād iti | asiddhiṁ svarūpāsiddhim | ity artha iti—yathā ghaṭādayaḥ sāvayavatvādādyantavantas tathedamapīti bhāvaḥ | ataḥ sāvayavatvāt | ity artha iti—ādyantavadrajjusarpāderyathā sattvaṁ nāsti tathāsyāpīti bhāvaḥ | nanu viśvasya brahmānanyatve brahmaṇo nityatvena tasyāpi nityatvaṁ syād iti cettatrāha—yadveti | brahmaṇaḥ pṛthagidaṁ viśvaṁ mithyaiva, āgamāpāyitvāt | tadavadhitvāt tadāśrayatvāt | pūrvokta eva rajjusarpavadityeva | nanu yathā jaladharā iti dṛṣṭāntasattve pūrvokta dṛṣṭāntāśrayaṇaṁ kimarthaṁ kṛtaṁ tatrāha—yathā jaladharo vyomnītyādi ||26||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tataḥ paramātmani buddhy-ādi-mayasya jagataḥ sato’pi samparkaḥ sutarāṁ nāstīty arthaṁ cāha—yatheti | **yathā vyomni** vyoma-kārya-vāyu-jyotiḥ-salila-pārthivāṁśa-dhūma-pariṇatā **jaladharāḥ** sveṣām evāvayavinām udayād **bhavanti** dṛśyante, **apyayān** **na bhavanti** na dṛśyante ca, te ca tan na spṛśantīti jñeyam | **tathā brahmaṇīdaṁ viśvam** iti yojyam |[^30] tataḥ sūkṣma-rūpeṇa tasya sthitir asty eva jagac-chakti-viśiṣṭa-kāraṇāstitvāt ittham evoktaṁ sato’bhivyañjakaḥ kāla [bhā.pu. 11.24.19] iti ||26|| [paramātma-sandarbha 75]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** pariṇāma-vāde kārya-kāraṇāvyatireko darśitaḥ | athārambha-vāde viśvasyādy-antaratvaṁ tat-kāraṇasya parameśvarasya satyatvaṁ ca krameṇa darśayati—yatheti dvābhyām | na bhavanti naśyanti, tathaiva brahmaṇīdaṁ viśvaṁ bhavati, na bhavati ca | atra vyomnīti dṛṣṭāntena paramātmano nirlepatā darśitā | avayavīti yat sāvayavaṁ tad-ādy-antavat ghaṭādivad ity arthaḥ | ata udayāpyayāt ādy-antavad viśvaṁ na sarvadā satya	m ity arthaḥ ||26||

 **...**

**|| 12.4.27 ||**

**satyaṁ**[^31]** hy avayavaḥ proktaḥ sarvāvayavinām iha |**

**vinārthena pratīyeran paṭasyevāṅga tantavaḥ ||**[^32]

**madhvācāryaḥ (bhāgavata-tātparyam) :** 

avayavy-avayavābhedāt koṭy-aṁśo bheda īritaḥ |


    so’pi bhedo na cābhedāt pṛthag eva pravartate ||


    avayavy-avayavānāṁ ca kārya-kāraṇa-vastūnām |


    eka eva niyantāsau harir nārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ || iti ca ||27||[^33]

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **“anyatamād ṛtāt” iti pratijñāta-kāraṇasya satyatvam upapādayati—satyam iti | avayavaḥ kāraṇaṁ proktaḥ, vācāraṁbhaṇaṁ vikāro nāmadheyaṁ mṛttikety eva satyaṁ [chā.u. 6.1.4] ity-ādi-śrutibhiḥ | atra yuktim api darśayati—vineti | aṅga he rājan ! hi yasmād arthenāvayavinā pṛthag evāvayavāḥ pratīyeran | yathā paṭasyāvayavās tantavaḥ paṭāt pṛthak pratīyante tadvad iti ||27||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **atrāvayavasatyatve | uktārthagrahaṇa utsāhavṛddhaye sambodhayati—he aṅgeti | guruprītivākyaśruteḥ svayamevārthaḥ sphuratīti bhāvaḥ | paṭaṁ vinā pṛthakpratīteḥ sattvam eva tantūnāṁ, tantūnvinā paṭasya pṛthagapratīterasattvāmeti bhāvaḥ ||27||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tad evaṁ vaktuṁ kāraṇāstitvaṁ dṛṣṭāntena pratipādayati—satyam iti | **sarveṣām avayavināṁ** sthūla-vastūnām **avayavaḥ** kāraṇaṁ **satyaṁ,** satyo vyabhicāra-rahitaḥ **proktaḥ** | loke yathā darśanād ity āha—**vinā** iti | **arthena** sthūla-rūpeṇa **paṭenāpi** vinā ||27||_ _[paramātma-sandarbha 76]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **kiṁ ca, sarveṣām avayavinām avayavaḥ kāraṇaṁ satyaṁ, loke tathā darśanād ity āha—vineti | aṅga, he rājan, hi yasmāt, arthenāvayavinā vināpi pṛthag evāvayavāḥ pratīyante, yathā paṭasyāvayavās tantavaḥ paṭāt pṛthak pratīyante tadvat | atra kārya-kāraṇa-vastv-aikyam adarśanaṁ paṭa-tantuvad iti saptamokteḥ | siṣādhayiṣitaṁ brahmaikyaṁ tu labhyata eva ||27|| 

 **...**

**|| 12.4.28 ||**

**yat sāmānya-viśeṣābhyām upalabhyeta sa bhramaḥ |**

**anyo'nyāpāśrayāt sarvam ādy-antavad avastu yat ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **nanu kāryābhāve kāraṇatvaṁ brahmaṇaḥ kuto ghaṭeta ? satyam, tad api nātīva satyam ity āha—yad iti | sāmānyaṁ kāraṇam, viśeṣaḥ kāryam, tad-rūpeṇānyo'nyāpāśrayāt parasparāpekṣatvena nirūpaṇāsahatvād ity arthaḥ | ataḥ kāraṇatvam avadhitvaṁ vyāpakatvam ity-ādikam api yat parāpekṣatvād ādy-antavat, tat sarvam avastv ity arthaḥ | 

yad vā, tatraiva hetv-antaram etat | **yad upalabhyeta sa bhramaḥ**, sāmānya-viśeṣa-rūpatvāt svapnavat | **anyonyāpāśrayāt** itīdam api hetv-antaraṁ guṇa-guṇi-viśeṣaṇa-viśeṣya-vyāpya-vyāpakatvādi-rūpeṇa parasparādhīna-siddhitvāt | tathā-bhūta-svapnavad iti nigamanam | ato yad ādy-antavat tat sarvam avastv iti ||28||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **atrākṣipati—nanv iti | ity artha iti—anyonyasiddhāvanyonyāpekṣaṇamanyonyāśrayaḥ, sa ca doṣa eva | tathāpi—kāraṇatvaṁ hi kāryatvanirūpyaṁ, kasya kāraṇamityanuyogaviṣayatvāt, evaṁ kāryatvam api kāraṇatvamanirūpyaṁ kasya kāryamityanuyogagocaratvādato'nayoḥ paurvāparyanirṇayābhāvāddoṣatvameveti bhāvaḥ | uktamarthamanyatrāpyatidiśati—ataḥ kāraṇatvamity-ādi | ity artha iti—parasya kāryāvadheyavyāpyasyāpekṣāvattvātkāraṇatvādīnām api pūrvoktadoṣavattvam iti bhāvaḥ | ādinā prakāśakatvādigrahaḥ | astu kāryatvādibhāvopi mithyākāraṇatvādibhāvasya mithyātve brahmaṇo'pi mithyātvaṁ prasajyeta tatrāha—yadveti | tatraiva viśvamithyātva eva | tathābhūtasvapnavat | nidrānirūpitasvāpnavat yathā svapnanirūpyā nidrā, nidrānirūpyaḥ svapnaḥ, ubhāvetāvasatyau tathedamapīti nigamanaṁ dṛṣṭāntaḥ | upasaṁharati—atha iti,— uktahetusamūhāt ||28||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tasmin kāryāstitvam api vyatirekeṇa pratipādayati—yad iti | ayam arthaḥ—yady evam ucyate, pūrvaṁ sūkṣmākāreṇāpi jagan nāsīt, kintu sāmānyaṁ kevalaṁ śuddhaṁ brahmaivāsīt, tad eva śaktyā nimitta-bhūtayā viśeṣākāreṇa jagad-rūpeṇa pariṇatam iti tad asat | yataḥ **yad** eva **sāmānya-viśeṣābhyām upalabhyeta sa bhramo** vivarta-vāda eva | tatra hi śuddhaṁ brahmaivājñāna-rūpayā śaktyā jagattayā vivṛtam iti mataṁ na cāsmākaṁ tad-abhyupapattiḥ, pariṇāma-vādasya sat-kāryatā-pūrvakatvād ity arthaḥ | 

nanv apūrvam eva kāryam ārambha-vivarta-vādinām iva yuṣmākam api jñāyatāṁ ? tatrāha— **yad ādy-antavad** apūrvaṁ kāryaṁ, tat punar **avastu** nirūpaṇāsaham ity arthaḥ | tatra hetuḥ—**anyonyāpaśrayāt** | yāvat kāryaṁ na jāyate, tāvat kāraṇatvaṁ mṛc-chukty-āder na sidhyati, kāraṇatvāsiddhau ca kāryaṁ na jāyata eveti paraspara-sāpekṣatva-doṣāt | tataḥ kāraṇatva-siddhaye kārya-śaktis tatrāvaśyam abhyupagantavyā | sā ca kārya-sūkṣmāvasthaiveti kāryāstitvaṁ sidhyati | tathāpi sthūla-rūpatāpādakatvān mṛd-ādeḥ kāraṇatvam api sidhyatīti bhāvaḥ ||28||_ _[paramātma-sandarbha 77-78]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **vivarta-vāde tu brahma-kāryaṁ jagad asatyaṁ, yathā tathā brahmaṇaḥ kāraṇatvādikam apy asatyam ity āha—yad iti | sāmānyaṁ kāraṇaṁ, viśeṣaḥ kāryaṁ, tābhyāmtābhyāṁ yad upalabhyate sa bhramaḥ kṛtaḥ | anyonyāpāśrayāt +pūrvāpekṣatvena nirūpaṇāsahatvād ity arthaḥ | 

+athavāyathāāthavāyathā rajjūr evājñānena sarpatvena vivartate, tatra rajjū-kāraṇaṁ, sarpaḥ kāryaḥ, sa tu mithyaiva | tathaiva sāmānyaṁ brahmaiva ajñānena jagad-rūpatattvrūpatayā vivṛttaṁ, tatra jagataḥ kāryasyābhāve tad-apekṣatattvapekṣatayā siddhaṁ brahmaṇaḥ kutaḥ kāraṇatvam iti ||28||

 **...**

**|| 12.4.29 ||**

**vikāraḥ khyāyamāno’pi pratyag-ātmānam antarā |**

**na nirūpyo’sty aṇur api syāc cec cit-sama ātma-vat ||**
