**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tad evam anekair hetubhiḥ prapañcasyāsattvaṁ sādhitam | tatra śaṅkā, nanu prapañcasyāpi prakāśamānatvād ātma-vat sattvaṁ kiṁ na syāt ? iti tatrāha—vikāra iti khyāyamānaḥ prakāśamāno’pi vikāraḥ prapañcaḥ pratyag-ātma-prakāśaṁ vinā’ṇu-mātro’pi na nirūpyo’sti | taṁ vinā nirūpyaḥ syāc cet tarhi so’pi cit-samaḥ syat, cid-rūpeṇātmanā samaḥ sva-prakāśo bhavet | tathā ca sati so’py ātmavat syāt | eka-rūpaḥ syād ity arthaḥ ||29||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tatra prapañcāsatyatve | śaṅkākṣepaḥ | tām āha—nanv iti | khyāyata iti khyāyamānaḥ, khyāteḥ karmaṇi śānac | ity artha iti—na hyacitaḥ prakāśaścitaṁ vihāya kadāpi bhavatyataścideva tattadākāreṇa prakāśate'citaḥ pṛthaksattānaṅgīkārāt sarvaṁ khalvidaṁ brahma - neha nānāsti kiñcana ity-ādiśruter iti bhāvaḥ ||29||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tad evaṁ svābhāvika-śakti-mayam eva paramātmano jagad ity upasaṁharati—vikāra iti | yadyapi **khyāyamāmanaḥ** prakāśamāna eva, tathāpi svalpo’**pi vikāraḥ pratyag-ātmānaṁ** paramātmānaṁ vinā tad-vyatirekeṇa svatantratayā **na nirūpyo’sti** | tad uktaṁ tad-ananyatva-vivaraṇa eva | yadi ca taṁ vināpi syāt, tadā **cit-samaḥ** **syāc** cid-rūpeṇa samaḥ sva-prakāśa evābhaviṣyat | **ātmavat** paramātmavan nityaikāvasthaś cābhaviṣyat ||_ _[29|| (paramātma-sandarbha 79]) 

** **

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **kiṁ ca, vikāraḥ khyāyamānaḥ vikāratvena prasiddhim ānayaṁ prapañcam | pratyag-ātmānaṁ vinā aṇur api na nirūpaṇīyaḥ | kintu sarvaḥ paramātmaiva, paramātmany eva prapañca āropitaḥ | yathā marīcikāyāḥ jalatvena prasiddhaṁ vastu tejo vinā aṇu-mātram api na nirūpyam | kintu sarvaṁ teja eva tejasy eva jalatvam āropyata ity arthaḥ | 

nanu ca kvacid vikāratvena prasiddhimān api padārthaś cid eva satya evekṣyate, yathā bhaktis tat-karaṇādhikaraṇa-kartādir bhagavat-purī ca | tathā hi—lakṣaṇaṁ bhakti-yogasya nirguṇasyety udāhṛtam [bhā.pu. 3.29.12] iti, mat-sevāyāṁ tu nirguṇam [bhā.pu. 11.25.27] iti, man-niketaṁ tu nirguṇaṁ [bhā.pu. 11.25.25] iti, nirguṇo mad-apāśrayaḥ [bhā.pu. 11.25.26] iti, man-niṣṭhaṁ nirguṇaṁ smṛtam [bhā.pu. 11.25.24] ity- ādi-bhagavad-ukter bhakty-upakaraṇī-bhūtaḥ padārtha-mātra eva nirguṇaḥ, tathā, tāsāṁ madhye sākṣād brahma gopāla-purī [go.tā.u. 2.26] iti, sarvātmaika-rase bhakti-yoge tiṣṭhati [go.tā.u. 2.78] iti ca gopāla-tāpinī-śruteḥ | bhagaval-loko bhakti-yogaś ca nirguṇa evātaḥ param asatya eveti tatrāha—syāc cid iti | yadi nirguṇatvena nirūpyo bhavati, tarhi so’piso'pi cit-samaḥ | sītā sā sītayā sametivad abhede upamā cid evety arthaḥ | ātmavat paramātmaiva nirguṇaḥ paramātma-vilāsatvāt paramātmaiva sa eka evety arthaḥ ||29||

 **...**

**|| 12.4.30 ||**

**na hi satyasya nānātvam avidvān yadi manyate |**

**nānātvaṁ chidrayor yadvaj jyotiṣor vātayor iva ||**

**madhvācāryaḥ (bhāgavata-tātparyam) :** 

mahākāśo bahiḥsthaś ca ghaṭādy-anta-stha eva ca |


    dvedhā samudito’nyau ca dvāv ākāśau prakīrtitau ||


    ghaṭa-rūpas tad anyaś ca mahākāśāt paro laghuḥ |


    mahākāśavad evātra paramātmā sanātanaḥ ||


    ghaṭāntastha-mahākāśa-pratimo’ntargato hariḥ |


    ghaṭasthāntargatākāśo mahākāśāt paro mataḥ ||


    tadvad devādayaḥ sarve jīvā muktvy-upayoginaḥ |


    tamogāś caiva ye sarve ghaṭa-rūpa-khavan narāḥ || iti tattva-saṁhitāyām ||30||

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kutaḥ ? ity ata āha—nahīti | nanu satyasyāpy ātmano jīva-brahma-rūpaṁ nānātvam asty eva tatrāha—yady evaṁ nānātvaṁ manyate, tarhy avidvān | kathaṁ tarhi tayor bheda-vyavahāra upādhi-kṛtaḥ ? ity āha—nānātvam iti | tatra chidrayor ghaṭākāśa-mahākāśayor iveti paricchedāparicchede dṛṣṭāntaḥ | jyotiṣor ākāśa-jalasyayoḥ sūryayor ivety upādhi-kṛta-vikāra-sad-asad-bhāve | vātayor bāhya-śarīra-stha-vāyvor iveti kriyā-bhede ||30||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **atra hetumāśaṅkyāha—kuta iti | atrākṣipati—nanv iti | tayorjīvabrahmaṇoḥ | tatra chidrādidṛṣṭānteṣu | paricchedāparicchede'lpānalpatve ||30||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **nanu yadi paramātmānaṁ vinā vikāro nāsti, tarhi paramātmanaḥ sopādhitve nirupādhitvaṁ na sidhyati | tasmāt sopādher nirupādhir anya eva kim ? ity atrāha—nahīti | **satyasya** paramātmano **nānātvaṁ na hi** vidyate | **yadi** tasya nānātvaṁ **manyate** tarhy **avidvān,** yatas tasya nirupādhitva-sopādhitva-lakṣaṇaṁ **nānātvaṁ** mahākāśa-ghaṭākāśayor **yadvat**, tadvad gṛhāṅgana-gata-sarva-vyāpi-tejasor **iva**, bāhya-śarīra-vāyvor **iva** ceti ||30|| [paramātma-sandarbha 80]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** nanu kena prakāreṇaikyaṁ mantavyam ? tatrāha—nahīti | satyasya parama-parama-satyasya cid-vastuno nānātvaṁ naivāsti, tad api yadi nānātvaṁ manyate, tarhy avidvān, yathā chidrayor ghaṭa-dvaye idam ekam ākāśam idam aparam ākāśam iti, evaṁ jyotiṣor dīpa-dvaya-gatayor vā tayor deha-dvaya-gatayoḥ prāṇayor iti ||30|| 

 **...**

**|| 12.4.31 ||**

**yathā hiraṇyaṁ bahudhā samīyate**

**nṛbhiḥ kriyābhir vyavahāra-vartmasu |**

**evaṁ vacobhir bhagavān adhokṣajo**

**vyākhyāyate laukika-vaidikair janaiḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **brahmaṇa eva prapañca-vyavahārālambanatvaṁ dṛṣṭāntena spaṣṭayati—yatheti | **kriyābhis** tat-tad-racanā-bhedair **bahudhā** kaṭaka-kūṇḍalādi-rūpeṇa | **laukika-vaidikair** vacobhiḥ | **janair** ahaṅkāropahitaih ||31||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **kriyābhistattadracanābhedaiḥ | bhagavān bahudhākāśādirūpeṇa brahmādirūpeṇa ca vyākhyāyate prakāśyate—eṣa brahmā eṣa śiva ity-ādinā vaidikaiśva śāstradhiyā laukikaiś ca śāstrajñānābhāvāt ghaṭo'yaṁ paṭoyamity-ādinā sa eva prakāśyata iti bhāvaḥ ||31||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **yasmād vikāraḥ khyāyamāno’pi pratyag-ātmānam antarā | na nirūpyo’sty aṇur api_ _[bhā.pu. 12.4.29, §79] tasmāt sarva-śabda-vācyo’pi sa eveti sa-dṛṣṭāntam āha—yathā hiraṇyam iti | **kriyābhis** tat-tad-racanā-bhedair **bahudhā** kaṭaka-kuṇḍādi-rūpeṇa **yathā** suvarṇam eva **vacobhis** tat-tan-nāmabhiḥ **pratīyate**, tathā **laukika-vaidikaiḥ** sarvair eva **vacobhir bhagavān** eva **vyākhyāyate** | tad uktam—sarva-nāmābhidheyaś ca sarva-vedeḍitaś ca saḥ iti skānde |_|_31||_ _[paramātma-sandarbha 81]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** tad evaṁ sṛṣṭi-samaye’pi prapañcasya nānā-vyavahārālambanatvena dṛṣṭe’py ekaṁ brahmaiva jñānī jānīyād ity āha—yathaiveti | **kriyābhis** tat-tad-racanā-bhedaiḥ **bahudhā** kaṭaka-kuṇḍalādi-rūpeṇa, **evaṁ** **laukika-vedikair vacobhiḥ** ||31||

 **...**

**|| 12.4.32 ||**

**yathā ghano’rka-prabhavo’rka-darśito**

**hy arkāṁśa-bhūtasya ca cakṣuṣas tamaḥ |**

**evaṁ tv ahaṁ brahma-guṇas tad-īkṣito**

**brahmāṁśakasyātmana ātma-bandhanaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **nanv ahaṅkārasya kathaṁ brahma-svarūpāvaraṇena bheda-vyavahāra-hetutvam, tasya sva-kāraṇa-bhūta-brahmāvarakatvāsaṁbhavād āvaraṇe vā, svasyāpi prakāśāsaṁbhavāt ? ity āśaṅkya sa-dṛṣṭāntam āha—**yathā** iti | **arka**-raśmaya eva megha-rūpeṇa pariṇatā varṣanti | 


    agnau prāstāhutiḥ samyag ādityam upatiṣṭhate | 


    ādityāj jāyate vṛṣṭir vṛṣṭer annaṁ tataḥ prajāḥ ||** **[manu 3.76]

ity-ādi-vacanāt | tasmād **arka-prabhavaḥ**, **arkeṇaiva darśitaḥ** prakāśitaś ca, **tamaḥ** svarūpa-bhūtārka-darśana-pratibandhako bhavati | **aham** ahaṅkāro **brahma-guṇo** brahma-kārya-bhūta ity arthaḥ, **tad-īkṣitas** tenaiva prakāśitaś ca, **ātmano** jīvasya **ātma-bandhano** brahma-svarūpa-darśana-pratibandhako bhavati ||32||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **atrākṣipati—_nanv_ iti | brahma-svarūpa-darśana-pratibandhakaḥ svādhyāsena bandha-bhramāpādako bhavati ||32||

**yathā ghano’rka-prabhavo’rka-darśito**

**hy arkāṁśa-bhūtasya ca cakṣuṣas tamaḥ |**

**evaṁ tv ahaṁ brahma-guṇas tad-īkṣito**

**brahmāṁśakasyātmana ātma-bandhanaḥ ||**

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tad evaṁ jagataḥ paramātma-svābhāvika-śakti-mayatvam uktvā, tena ca jīva-kartṛkena jñānena tan-nāśanāsāmarthyaṁ vyajya, mokṣārthaṁ tad-adhyāsa-parityāgam upadeṣṭuṁ paramātma-śakti-mayasyāpi tasyopādhy-adhyāsātmakasyāhaṅkārasya jīva-svarūpa-prakāśāvarakatva-rūpaṁ doṣā sa-dṛṣṭāntam upapādayati—**yathā ghana** iti | 

**arka**-raśmaya eva megha-rūpeṇa pariṇatā varṣanti,


    agnau prāstāhutiḥ samyag-ādityam upatiṣṭhate |


    ādityāj jāyate vṛṣṭir vṛṣṭer annaṁ tataḥ prajāḥ || [manu 3.76]

ity-ādi-vacanāt | ayam arthaḥ—**yathārka-prabhavo**’**rkeṇaiva darśitaḥ** prakāśitaś ca **ghano** niviḍo megho'**rkāṁśa-bhūtasya** **cakṣuṣas tamo** divi bhūmau ca mahāndhakāra-rūpo bhavati, **evam ahaṁ** prākṛtāhaṅkāro **brahma-guṇaḥ** paramātma-śakti-kārya-bhūtas **tad-īkṣitas** tenaiva paramātmanā prakāśitaś ca **brahmāṁśakasya** taṭastha-śakti-rūpatvāt paramātmano yo hīnāṁśas tasyātmano jīvasya **ātma-bandhanaḥ** svarūpa-prakāśāvarako bhavati |_|_32||_ _[paramātma-sandarbha 82]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** nanu yady evaṁ sarvam eva brahma-kāryatvād ekaṁ brahmaiva, brahma-kāryeṇāhaṅkāreṇāsatyena brahmāṁśa-bhūtāś citkaṇāḥ satyāḥ jīvāḥ kṛt? āvriyante | te vā tad-āvṛtāḥ kṛt? muhyantīti tatra sa-dṛṣṭāntam āha—**yathā** iti | arka-raśmaya eva megha-rūpeṇa pariṇatā varṣanti—


    agnau prāstāhutiḥ samyag-ādityam upatiṣṭhate |


    ādityāj jāyate vṛṣṭir vṛṣṭer annaṁ tataḥ prajāḥ || [manu 3.76] ity-ādi-vacanāt |

tasmād arka-prabhava eva ghanaḥ arkeṇaiva darśitaḥ prakāśitaś ca | atha arkāṁśu-bhūtasya cakṣuṣas tama-āvarakaḥ | evam evāhaṅkāra ātmano jīvasya ātma-bandhanaḥ ātmanā svenaiva jīvaṁ badhnātīty arthaḥ ||32||

 **...**

**|| 12.4.33 ||**

**ghano yadārka-prabhavo vidīryate**

**cakṣuḥ svarūpaṁ ravim īkṣate tadā |**

**yadā hy ahaṅkāra upādhir ātmano**

**jijñāsayā naśyati tarhy anusmaret ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ata evāhaṅkāra-nāśe svarūpa-darśanaṁ bhavatīti, tenaiva dṛṣṭāntenāha—ghana iti **ātmana upādhiḥ** | **jijñāsayā** vicāreṇa | **tarhi** tadā **anusmaret**, brahmāham iti paśyatīty arthaḥ ||33||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **yato'haṅkāra eva pratibandhakosti ato hetor eva | ity artha iti—pratibandhakanāśe svata eva svarūpajñānaṁ bhavatīti bhāvaḥ ||33||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **sa cādhyāsa-parityāgaḥ svato na bhavati, kintu paramātma-jijñāsayā tat-prabhāvenaiveti vaktuṁ pūrvavad eva dṛṣṭānta-paripāṭīm āha—ghana iti | 

**ghano** **yadārka-prabhavo vidīryate** iti dṛṣṭāntāṁśe tad-vidāraṇasya na cakṣuḥ-śakti-sādhyatvam, kintu sūrya-prabhāva-sādhyatvam iti vyaktam | anena dārṣṭāntike’pi **ātmanaḥ **paramātmano **jijñāsayā** jātena tat-prasādena **ahaṅkāro naśyati** palāyate ity atrāṁśe puruṣa-jñāna-sādhyatvam ahaṅkāra-nāśasya khaṇḍitam | ato vivarta-vādo nābhyupagataḥ | atra ca **upādhir** iti viśeṣaṇena svarūpa-bhūtāhaṅkāras tv anya eveti spaṣṭībhūtam | 

evaṁ yathā dṛṣṭānte ghana-maya-mahāndhakārāvaraṇābhāvāt tat-prabhāveṇa yogyatā-lābhāc ca **cakṣuḥ** kartṛ-bhūtaṁ svarūpaṁ karma-bhūtam **īkṣate,** sva-svarūpa-prakāśam astitvena jānāti, sva-śakti-prākaṭyaṁ labhata ity arthaḥ | kadācit tad-īkṣaṇonmukhaḥ san **raviṁ** cekṣate, tathā dārṣṭāntike’py **anusmaret,** smartum[^34] anusandhātuṁ yogyo bhavati |, ātmānaṁ ceti śeṣaḥ |_|_33_|| _[paramātma-sandarbha 83]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** tasyaivāhaṅkārasya nāśe satyāvaraṇa-bhaṅgo brahma-svarūpa-darśanaṁ bhavatīti tenaiva dṛṣṭāntenāha—ghana iti | vidīryate vinaśyati, tadā cakṣuḥ kartṛtvaṁ rūpaṁ ravim īkṣate iti manuṣyāder eve cakṣur, na tu ulūkādeś cakṣū ravim īkṣate | yathā bhaktimatām eva jñānināṁ, na tu bhaktim akurvatām iti, bhaktyāham ekayā grāhya [bhā.pu. 11.14.21] ity-ādy-ukteḥ | anusmaret brahmānubhavati ||33||

 **...**

**|| 12.4.34 ||**

**yadaivam etena viveka-hetinā**

**māyā-mayāhaṅkaraṇātma-bandhanam |**

**chittvācyutātmānubhavo’vatiṣṭhate**

**tam āhur ātyantikam aṅga samplavam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** so’yam ātyantikaḥ pralaya ity upasaṁharati—yadaivam iti | **viveka-hetinā** jñāna-śastreṇa | **ahaṅkaraṇam evātma-bandhanam** | **acyutaṁ** paripūrṇam **ātmānam** anubhavatīti tathā ||34||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **jijñāsayāhaṅkārabādhaprakāram āha—yadaivaṁ gurormahāvākyaśravaṇottaraṁ śrūyamāṇeśajīvābhedasya virodhādanupapatteretena māyāvidyādhupādhivivekarūpahetinā bhāgatyāgalakṣaṇatadbādhakarūpakhaḍgena tayormāyāhaṅkaraṇopādhirūpamātmabandhanaṁ chittvācyuto harirevātmā matsvarūpamityanubhavo'parokṣabodho yasya tathābhūtaḥ śuddhanirupahitasvarūpeṇāvatiṣṭhate, tamātyantikamaṅgasamplavaṁ sthūlasūkṣmakāraṇāṅgatrayapralayamāhuḥ | aṅgeti sambodhanam asaṅkaraṇamātmāvarakamahaṅkāram | aṅgeti saṁyuddhiḥ pūrvavad iti viśvaṁ ||34||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (prīti-sandarbha 1**): **acyut**ākhye** ātmani** paramātmani **anubhavo** yasya, tathābhūtaḥ san **avatiṣṭhate** yat, tam **ātyantikaṁ samplavaṁ** muktim āhur ity arthaḥ ||34||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **nigamayati—yadaiveti | **etena** pūrvokta-viveka-śastreṇa **māyāmaya-** iti viśeṣaṇaṁ svarūpa-bhūtāhaṅkārasya vyavacchedārtham | **avatiṣṭhate** sva-svarūpeṇāvasthito bhavati | na kevalam etāvad eva, **acyutātmānubhavaḥ,** acyute’cyuta-nāmny ātmani paramātmany anubhavo yasya tathābhūta eva sann avatiṣṭhate ||34|| [paramātma-sandarbha 84]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** ahaṅkāra-vidāraṇe bhakti-miśraṁ jñānaṁ khalu sādhanam ity āha—yadeti | **viveka-hetinā** jñāna-śastreṇa **acyute** bhagavati **ātmano** manaso’**nubhavaḥ** sudṛḍha-dhyānaṁ yasya tathābhūtaḥ sann **avatiṣṭhate** | 

yad vā, evam ahaṅkāraṁ chittvā sthitasya yoginaḥ **actyutātmānubhavaḥ** pūrṇa-brahmānubhavaḥ avatiṣṭhate sthirībhavati, yas tam **ātyantikaṁ samplavaṁ** pralayam āhuḥ ||34||

 **...**

**|| 12.4.35 ||**

**nityadā sarva-bhūtānāṁ brahmādīnāṁ paran-tapa |**

**utpatti-pralayāv eke sūkṣma-jñāḥ sampracakṣate ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **nitya-pralayam āha—nityadeti ||35||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.4.36 ||**

**kāla-sroto-javenāśu hriyamāṇasya nityadā |**

**pariṇāminām avasthās tā janma-pralaya-hetavaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kutaḥ ? ity ata āha—kāleti | pariṇāminā nadī-pravāha-pradīpa-jvālādīnāṁ yā ucca-nīcāvasthās tāḥ kāla-rūpa-srotaso vegenāśu hriyamāṇasya dehāder dṛśyamānās tā eva nityadā janma-pralaya-hetavo bhavanti | dehaḥ pratikṣaṇaṁ pradhvaṁsī, pratikṣaṇam avasthābhedāspadatvāt, pradīpādi-vad ity anumānam ||36||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **he parantapeti—śatrutāpakasya tavājñānatāpakatāpyastyeveti bhāvaḥ ||35-36||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** kutaḥ ? ity ata āha—kāleti | kāla-rūpa-srotaso vegenāśu hriyamāṇasya eka-vacanam ārṣaṁ hriyamāṇānām ity arthaḥ | pariṇāmināṁ dehādīnām avasthā bālya-paugaṇḍādyā janma-pralaya-hetavaḥ janma-pralayayor anumāpakāḥ dehādyāḥ pratikṣaṇaṁ janma-pralayavantaḥ āsthā-bhedānāṁ vidyamānatvāt pradīpādivad ity anumānam ||36||

 **...**

**|| 12.4.37 ||**

**anādy-antavatānena kāleneśvara-mūrtinā |**

**avasthā naiva dṛśyante viyati jyotiṣām iva ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **nanu yadi pratikṣaṇam avasthā bhavanti tarhi kiṁ na dṛṣyante, ato hetur asiddha ity āśaṅkyāha, anādy-antavatā kālena jāyamānā avasthā naiva lakṣyante, ākāśe gacchatāṁ jyotiṣāṁ candrādīnāṁ gamanāvasthāviśeṣā yathā naiva lakṣyante tadvat | ato yathā teṣāṁ pradeśāntara-prāptyā pratikṣaṇaṁ gaty-avasthāḥ kalpyante tadvad atrāpi bālya-tāruṇyādi-darśanena madhya-vartinyo’vasthāḥ kalpyanta iti na hetur asiddha ity arthaḥ ||37||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **atrākṣipati—nanv iti | ato darśanābhāvāt | hetuḥ pratikṣaṇamavasthābhedāspadatvād iti hetuḥ | ato darśanābhāvāta | teṣāṁ jyotiṣām | ity artha iti—hetuḥ pakṣe'styeveti bhāvaḥ ||37||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **yadi pratikṣaṇam avasthā bhavanti, tarhi kiṁ na dṛṣyante ? ato hetur asiddha ity āśaṅkyāha—anādy-antavatā kālena pratikṣaṇaṁ janyā nāśyāś cāvasthā naiva lakṣyante, yathā viyaty ākāśe gacchatāṁ jyotiṣāṁ candrādīnāṁ gamanāvasthā-viśeṣā naiva lakṣyante, tadvat | ato yathā teṣāṁ deśāntara-prāptyā pratikṣaṇaṁ gaty-avasthāḥ kalpyante, tadvad atrāpi bālya-tāruṇyādi-darśanena tan-madhya-vartinyaḥ sūkṣmā apy avasthāḥ kalpyanta iti na hetur asiddha ity arthaḥ ||37||

 **...**

**|| 12.4.38 ||**

**nityo naimittikaś caiva tathā prākṛtiko layaḥ |**

**ātyantikaś ca kathitaḥ kālasya gatir īdṛśī ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **upasaṁharati—nitya iti ||38||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **kālasya ca gati brūhīti praśnasyottaramupasaṁharanāha—kālasyeti ||38||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

**...**

**|| 12.4.39 ||**

**etāḥ kuru-śreṣṭha jagad-vidhātur**

**nārāyaṇasyākhila-sattva-dhāmnaḥ |**

**līlā-kathās te kathitāḥ samāsataḥ**

**kārtsnyena nājo’py abhidhātum īśaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **purāṇārtham upasaṁharati—etā iti | **līlā**-viṣayāḥ **kathā** **ajo** brahmāpi **kārtsnyenābhidhātuṁ neśaḥ** ||39||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **he kuruśreṣṭheti—antāvasthāyāṁ śrī-bhāgavataśravaṇattvaṁ sarvebhyaḥ svakulamukhyebhyaḥ śreṣṭhosīti bhāvaḥ| kiṁ ca—bhagavallīlā asmadādilīlāvadrāgapūrvikā na kintu yogamāyaiva | tathā ca śrutiḥ—


    yadacarastanvā vāvṛdhāno balānīndra prabrūvāṇo janeṣu māyetsā te yā niyuddhānyāhurnādyaśatruṁ nanu purā vivitse | iti | 

asyā arthaḥ—he indra parameśvara yat tanvā matsyakūrmādiśarīreṇācaraḥ caraṇaṁ kṛtavānasi vāvṛdhānaḥ vavṛdhe daityādīnhatvā mahattvaṁ ca prāptavānasi loke balāni bhūmeruddharaṇādīni janeṣu prabruvāṇaḥ khyāpitavānabhūḥ sā sarvā te tava māyet māyaiva sā kā yā niyuddhānyāhuḥ devāsurasaṁgrāmāḥ sarve māyaiva | kuta etat—yastvaṁ nanu niścitam adya vartamānakāle purā vā śatruṁ nāśanīyaṁ na vivitse labhase, sarvasyāntarātmakatvātkālatraye'pi tatra śatrurnāstoti tasmātsvānānuvādavadetatpurāṇaṁ bhagavallīlāmanubadatīti mantrārthaḥ ||39||

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** etāḥ kuru-śreṣṭhety-ādi | akhila-sattva-dhāmnaḥ sarva-prāṇi-nilayasya jagad-vidhātur līlās te tubhyaṁ kathitāḥ, ajo’pi brahmāpi kārtsnyena yāḥ kathayitum na śaknoti | ataḥ śrī-kṛṣṇasya gokulādiṣv anyā anyā api yā līlā ūhanīyāḥ ||39||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** bhagavat-kathā upasaṁharati—etā iti ||39||

 **...**

**|| 12.4.40 ||**

**saṁsāra-sindhum atidustaram uttitīrṣor**

**nānyaḥ plavo bhagavataḥ puruṣottamasya |**

**līlā-kathā-rasa-niṣevanam antareṇa**

**puṁso bhaved vividha-duḥkha-davārditasya ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **nanu yadi sākalyenābhidhātuṁ na śakyante, tarhi kiṁ tad-abhidhānena ? tatrāha—saṁsāreti | vividhaṁ duḥkham eva davo dāvānalaḥ, tenārditasya pīḍitasya, ata **uttitīrṣoḥ** puṁso bhagavato yā **līlāh,** tāsāṁ **kathāḥ,** tāsāṁ **rasah,** tan-**niṣevaṇam** **antareṇānyaḥ plavas** taraṇa-sādhanaṁ na bhavet, upāyāntarāsaṁbhavāt | tat-kathā-śravaṇam eva yathā-śakti niṣevyam ity arthaḥ ||40||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **punar ākṣipati—_nanv_ iti | _ity artha_ iti | yathā mahad-anekānna-rāśito yat kiñcit tad-annaika-deśāśanenān nivṛttir bhavati tathā līla-kathaika-deśo'pi saṁsāra-duḥkha-nivartako'taḥ so'vaśyaṁ sevya iti bhāvaḥ | 

viśvanāthas tu—yat prathama-skandha-pṛṣṭaṁ mriyamāṇasya kiṁ kṛtyaṁ [bhā.pu. 1.19.37] tad-uttaram āha—**saṁsāra-** iti | duḥsaha-kṣudhāyāṁ bhojanam **antareṇa** nopaśama itivan **nānyo** jñānādikaḥ **plava** uttaraṇa-sādhanaṁ duḥsaha-kṣudhāyāḥ srak-candanādir iva, tenaitad-uttarādhyāye mayāpy upadeṣṭavyaḥ | mahā-rahasya-bhakti-ratna-cchādanārthaṁ yaj-jñānaṁ tattvayāpyatvena na pratyetavyam iti bhāvaḥ | **rasa**-śabdena **līlā-kathānām** amṛtatvam āropitam | ata eva vividha-duḥkha-mahā-rogāṇāṁ dava-mahā-jvālās tat-pīḍitasya sadya evaikam amṛtaṁ vinā nānyad auṣadhaṁ prayoktavyam iti bhāvaḥ ||40||

———————————————————————————————————————

**kaivalya-dīpikā : antareṇa** vinā | **davo** vana-vahniḥ | atra ūrjitaikā **līlā-kathā** iti padāni jñāna-miśratve bījam ||40|| [mu.pha. 6.34]

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** kintu līlās tāvad dvividhāḥ—sṛṣṭy-ādi-līlāḥ, śrī-vṛndāvana-līlāś ceti | tāsāṁ madhye vṛndāvanādi-līlāyāḥ caraṇāravindaṁ yathā saṁsāra-sindhu-taraṇopayuktaṁ bhavati, nānyathānya-līlayeti darśayati—**saṁsāra-sindhum** ity-ādi | aho aticitram etat ! **saṁsāra-sindhu-taraṇe** **līlā-kathā**-rūpā ye **rasāḥ**, teṣāṁ **niṣevaṇam** eva **plavaḥ** | jale jala-rūpa-plava iti citram etat ||40||

———————————————————————————————————————

**sanātana-gosvāmī : **[ha.bha.vi. 10.436] **vividhaṁ duḥkham** eva **dāvānalaḥ** | tena **arditasya** pīḍitasya | ata **uttitīrṣoḥ** puṁsaḥ bhagavato yā **līlā-kathāḥ**, tāsāṁ **rasaḥ**, tan-**niṣevaṇam antareṇa anyaḥ plavaḥ** uttaraṇa-sādhanaṁ na bhavet ||40||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **evaṁ śrī-śukaḥ sva-kṛtopadeśopasaṁhāre ca śravaṇam upalakṣya śrī-bhagaval-līla-kathā-māhātmyam āha |[^35] eṣā ca līlā-kathā tad-bhakty-eka-puruṣārthibhir yathāyathaṁ śrotavyaiva, mokṣārthibhir apy avaśyaṁ śrotavyety āha—**saṁsāra-** iti | anyāsām api bhaktīnāṁ tat-pūrvakatvenaiva pravṛtter upāyāntarāsambhavatvaṁ yuktam |_|_40|| [bhakti-sandarbhaḥ 86][^36]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** etā vividhāḥ kathāḥ khalu vividha-bhaktānāṁ jīvātava eva | mokṣārthinām apy etāḥ kathā vinā jñānādibhir na mokṣa ity āha—kiṁ kṛtyaṁ ? tad-uttara-niṣkarṣo’yam ity āha—saṁsāra- iti | duḥsahāyāḥ kṣudhāyā bhojanam **antareṇa** nopaśama itivat, **nānyo** jñānādikaḥ **plava** uttaraṇa-sādhanam, duḥsahāyāṁ kṣudhāyāṁ srak-candanādir iva | tenaitad uttarādhyāye mayāpy upadeṣṭavyaṁ mahā-rahasya-bhakti-ratna-cchādanārthaṁ yaj jñānaṁ, tat tvayā sopādeyatvena na pratyetavyam iti bhāvaḥ | **rasa**-śabdena **līlā-kathānām** amṛtatvam āropitam, ata eva **vividha-duḥkha**-mahā-rogāṇāṁ **davā** mahā-jvālās teṣāṁ sadya evaikam amṛtaṁ vinā nānyad auṣadhaṁ prayoktavyam iti bhāvaḥ ||40||

 **...**

**|| 12.4.41 ||**

**purāṇa-saṁhitām etām ṛṣir nārāyaṇo’vyayaḥ |**

**nāradāya purā prāha kṛṣṇa-dvaipāyanāya saḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **śrotur ādara-dārdhyāya saṁpradāya-pravṛttim āha, purāṇa-saṁhitām iti tribhiḥ |

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **avyayaḥ sarvadaikarasaḥ nārāyaṇa ṛṣiḥ sarvajñaḥ brahmadvārā purā nāradāya prāha | sa nāradaḥ ||41||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **śrī-śuka-sampradāyaṁ śuddham avicchinnam anusṛtyaivaitat paṭhana-pāṭhana-śravaṇa-śrāvaṇādikaṁ kāryam ity abhiprāyeṇāha—purāṇeti | ṛṣir nārāyaṇo brahmaṇe ity adhyāhāryam | sa ca brahmā avyayaḥ aparādhābhāvād bhakti-vyaya-rahito nāradāya purāṇa-saṁhitām etām iti ||41||

 **...**

**|| 12.4.42 ||**

**sa vai mahyaṁ mahā-rāja bhagavān bādarāyaṇaḥ |**

**imāṁ bhāgavatīṁ prītaḥ saṁhitāṁ veda-sammitām ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **sa vai bādarāyaṇaḥ prītaḥ san mahyam imāṁ saṁhitāṁ prāheti pūrveṇānvayaḥ |

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **sa kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ | he mahārājeti—mahena bhagavatprāptyutsadhenādhunā samantāttvaṁ rājasīti bhāvaḥ| tattvajñāpakatvena sarvavedatulyām ||42||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** imaṁ bhāgavatīm iti vākya-bhedān na paunaruktyam ||42||

 **...**

**|| 12.4.43 ||**

**imāṁ vakṣyaty asau sūta ṛṣibhyo naimiṣālaye |**

**dīrgha-satre kuru-śreṣṭha sampṛṣṭaḥ śaunakādibhiḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **asau sūta iti purataḥ sthitam aṅgulyā nirdiśyāha | naimiṣālaye naimiṣāraṇya-sthāne ||43||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **he kuruśreṣṭheti saṁbuddhirvyākhyātacarī ||43||

iti śrīmad-bhāgavata-bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśe dvādaśa-skandhe caturtho'dhyāyaḥ ||4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** asau sūta iti pura-sthitam aṅgulyān nirdiśati ||43||

iti sārārtha-darśinyāṁ harṣiṇyāṁ bhakta-cetasām |

dvādaśasya caturthe’pi saṅgataḥ saṅgataḥ satām ||*||

 **...**


    iti śrīmad-bhāgavate mahā-purāṇe brahma-sūtra-bhāṣye pāramahaṁsyaṁ saṁhitāyāṁ vaiyāsikyāṁ dvādaśa-skandhe 


    pralaya-varṇanaṁ nāma caturtho’dhyāyaḥ |

|| 12.4 ||

**...**

**(12.5)**


### atha pañcamo’dhyāyaḥ


## brahmopadeśaḥ

**|| 12.5.1 ||**

**śrī-śuka uvāca—**

**atrānuvarṇyate’bhīkṣṇaṁ viśvātmā bhagavān hariḥ |**

**yasya prasāda-jo brahmā rudraḥ krodha-samudbhavaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :**

pañcame tu samāsena para-brahmopadeśataḥ |

rājñas takṣaka-sandaṁśān mṛtyu-bhīti-nivāraṇam ||

etat purāṇaṁ śṛṇvann abhayaṁ prāpnotīty abhipretya purāṇārtham anusmārayati—atreti | ayaṁ bhāvaḥ—jagataḥ kartā **brahmāpi** **yasya prasāda-jaḥ** | prasādo’tra rajo-vṛttir harṣaḥ | tato jātatvāt para-tantraḥ | sarva-saṁhartā **rudraś** ca yasya **krodha-saṁbhavaḥ**, na tu svatantraḥ | sa viśvasyātmā niyantā **bhagavān atrānuvarṇyate** | ata evaṁ-bhūtaṁ bhagavantaṁ śṛṇvataḥ kuto’nyasmād bhaya-śaṅketi ||1||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **samāsena saṅkṣepeṇa | atra granthe | atra tātparyaṁ svāmicaraṇā āhuḥ—ayaṁ bhāva ity-ādinā | śāstrārthamupasaṁhṛtya śrīśukaḥ kiñcidātmanaiva parāmamarśa—aho asādhvanuṣṭitaṁ yanmahārahasyamasamādhikaṁ svahṛdaya sampuṭātsamudghāṭya sarvalokadṛggocarīkṛtam | yaḥ khalu matprabhuṇā rājavidyā rājaguhyam ityanena vidyānāṁ rājeti, guhyānāṁ rājetyuktaḥ, punaś ca sarvaguhyatamaṁ bhūyaḥ śṛṇu me ityanena guhyatamaśabdenoktaḥ, sa khalu bhaktiyogo mayā parīkṣiti kṛṣāvaśatayā prāyaḥ prakaṭīkṛtyaivoktaḥ | tathā hi—


    akāmaḥ sarvakāmo vā mokṣakāma udāradhīḥ | 


    trīvreṇa bhaktiyogena yajeta puruṣaṁ param || 

ity-ādinā mukhabāhūrupādebhyaḥ puruṣasyāśramaiḥ saha ityatra—


    ya eṣāṁ puruṣaṁ sākṣādātmaprabhavamīśvaram | 


    na bhajantyavajānanti sthānādbhraṣṭāḥ patantyadhaḥ || 

ity-ādinā cānvayavyatirekābhyāṁ bhaktir eva sarva phalasādhanatvenopapāditā | svargādisādhanāni karmāṇi dūre tāvadāsatām, mokṣasādhanasyātiprasiddhasyāpi jñānasya mokṣakāraṇatvaṁ parāstīkṛtam eva | naiṣkarmyamapyacyutabhāvavarjitaṁ na śobhate jñānamalaṁ nirañjanam iti, caturthāśramiṇo jñānino'pi sthānādbhraṣṭāḥ patantyadhaḥ iti āruhya kṛcchreṇa paraṁ padaṁ tataḥ patantyadho nādṛtayuṣmadaṅghrayaḥ ity-ādy-uktejñānāsattve'pi bhaktyā vinā mokṣāsiddheḥ | 


    yatkarmabhiryattapasā jñānavairāgyataś ca yat | 


    sarvaṁ madbhaktiyogena puruṣo labhartejasā || 

iti jñānavyatireke'pi bhaktyaiva mokṣasiddheruktatvāt | mokṣaṁ prati jñānaṁ naivānvayavyatirekīti tadapi jñānānmokṣa iti yā prasiddhistatra jñānagatā guṇībhūtā bhaktir eva mokṣaṁ janayati, jñānasya tu nāmamātreṇa kāraṇatā bhaktyāham ekayā grāhyaḥ iti, na tapo nātmamīmāṁsā iti—


    kiṁ vā yogena sāṅkhyena nyāsasvādhyāyayor api | 


    śreyobhiritaraścaiva na yatrātmaprado hariḥ || 

ity-ādivākyairbrahmānubhavaṁ prati jñānasya sahakārītāpi vastuto na pratipāditā, bhaktarevopakramovasaṁhārābhyāseṣu prapañcitam, tadapi yadantarāntarā yogajñānādikamupanyastaṁ tatkhalu bhakterutkarṣaṁ tattanmatāni ca bhaktānprati jñāpayitumeveti | kiṁ ca—yannāmadheyaśravaṇānukīrtanādyatprahvaṇādyatsmaraṇād api kvacit iti, aho vataśvapaco'to garīyān yajjihvāgre vartate nāma tubhyam iti yannāma sakṛcchravaṇātpulkasopi vimucyate ity-ādibhyaḥ | kiṁ ca—na mātrayāpi bhaktyā mokṣaḥ iti, tathā—


    tāpatrayeṇābhihatasya ghore santapyamānasya bhavādhvanīha | 


    paśyāmi nānyaccharaṇaṁ tavāṅghridvandvātapatrādamṛtābhivarṣāt || 

ityuddhavavākyena, saṁsārasindhumatidustaramuttitīrṣornānyaḥ plavaḥ ityupasaṁhāre madvākyena ca tāṁ vinā tu nānyenopāyena saṁsārānmokṣa ity api nirdhāritam | kiṁ ca—bhaktyā tayaiva parayā nirvṛtyā hyapavargamātyantikaṁ paramapuruṣārtham api svayamāsādita no evādriyante bhavadīyatvenaiva parisamāptasarvārthā iti, mayi sañjāyate bhaktiḥ ko'nyo'rtho'syāvaśiṣyate iti, na parilaṣanti kecidapavargam api iti, sā brahmaṇi svamahimanyapi nātha mā bhūt iti, svargāpavarganarakeṣv api tulyārthadarśinaḥ ity-ādi vākyebhyaścaturthaṁ puruṣārtham api tiraskṛtya bhakter eva puruṣārthaśiromaṇitvaṁ mayā sthāpitam | kiṁ ca—munyantaravākyasya prāmāṇyamāpekṣikameva, madvākyasya tu prāmāṇyamātyantikameveti sarvatra vaikuṇṭhe'pi prasiddhirbhūyasī | parokṣavādā ṛṣayaḥ parokṣaṁ ca mama priyam iti bhagavad-ukter mahārahasyodghāṭanapaṭiṣṭho bhūtvā bhagavad-apriyaṁ karo'pyabhūvam | tadadhunā kiṁ kariṣye purāṇārthaś ca samāptīkṛta eva, bhavatvadhanāpi bhaktermahāmahimānaṁ saṁvarītuṁ yatiṣye, yathā kaścinmahāratnamatigopyam api rabhasavaśena sarvalokānpradāpi punaḥ kiścitparāmṛśya tadalakṣitaṁ sampuṭitaṁ kṛtvā mahākośābhyantare saṁsthāpya ratnāntaraṁ bahiḥ prakāśyānenaivāsmākaṁ sarvārthasiddhir iti brūte, tathaiva rājānamahaṁ jñānamupadiśāmi yathā gamanasamaye tu śukaḥ parīkṣite jñānamevopadiṣṭavāniti bhagavanmāyāprabhāvājjñānamevotkṛṣṭaṁ, bhaktis tu tatsādhanam iti maṁsyante | kiṁ ca—bhaktisiddhāñjanānprati prādurbhūya bhagavāṁstānparīkṣamāṇo mokṣaṁ gṛhāṇa yathā brūte, tathaivānena jñānopadeśenāsya macchiṣyasya parīkṣito bhaktimadvyutpattiṁ ca parīkṣiṣye | parīkṣā ceyaṁ sarvajñenāpi jagatyasminparīkṣito bhaktiniṣṭājñāpanārthā jñeyā | kiṁ ca—bhaktijñānayoḥ phalamantato muktir eva kevalamityanabhijñavyākhyānaṁ naiva madabhiprāyasambaddhaṁ jñeyam, yataḥ—


    rājan patirgururalaṁ bhavatāṁ yadūnāṁ daivaṁ priyaḥ kulapatiḥ kva ca kiṅkaro vaḥ | 


    astyevamaṅga bhagavānbhajatāṁ mukundo muktiṁ dadāti karhicitsma na bhaktiyogam || 

ity uktavatā mayā mukteḥ sakāśād api bhakterutkṛṣṭaphalasya pratipāditvāt | na copadeṣṭavyenānena jñānena parīkṣito nirvāṇamuktiprāptireveti jñeyam—


    sa vai mahābhāgavataḥ parīkṣidyenāpavargākhyamadabhrabuddhiḥ | 


    jñānena vaiyāsakiśabditena bheje khagendradhvajapādamūlam | 


    iti madabhiprāyābhijñenānena macchiṣyeṇa sūtenāgre vakṣyamāṇatvāt | 

rājanpatirgururalam ityatra bhajadbhyas tu bhaktiyogaṁ dadāti iti parīkṣitaḥ premabhaktiprāptir eva vyañjitā, na copadiśyamānenānenaiva dehādivyatiriktātmajñānena brahmānubhavaḥ sidhyet, kintvasyāpi jñānasya bhaktyā nirjayenaiva yaduktaṁ bhagavatā—


    dravyaṁ deśaḥ phalaṁ kālo jñānaṁ karma ca kārakaḥ | 


    śraddhāvasthākṛtirniṣṭhā traiguṇye sarva eva hi | 


    sarve guṇamayā bhāvāḥ puruṣā vyaktyadhiṣṭhitāḥ | 


    dṛṣṭaṁ śrutamanudhyātaṁ buddhyā vā puruṣarṣabha | 


    etāḥ saṁsṛtayaḥ puṁso guṇakarma nibandhanāḥ | 


    yenemā nirjitāḥ saumya guṇā jīvena cittajāḥ | 


    bhaktiyogena manniṣṭho madbhāvāya prapadyate | iti | 

kiṁ ca—bhagavad-bhaktasya mokṣakāmatve'pi nāsti jñānena prayojanam | yaduktaṁ svayaṁ bhagavatā—


    jñāne karmaṇi yoge ca vārtāyāṁ daṇḍadhāraṇe | 


    yāvānartho nṛṇāṁ tāta tāvāṁste'haṁ caturvidhaḥ || iti | 

tasmādanena sarvānte jñānopadeśenāsya śāstrasyaspaṣṭatayaiva mohinīsādharmyaṁ pratipādayiṣye | yathā hyasurāḥ premasudhayā vañcitā eva bhaveyur iti | api ca—jñānopadeśātprāgekaṁ vākyaṁ vyañjanayā vṛttyā bhaktān prīṇayituṁ bhaktirasamrakṣitam eva kariṣye, tadanantaraṁ jñānopadeśavākyānyapi yāni bhaktipratikūlāni vakṣye tānyapyantarbhūtabhaktyanukūlārthāneva kariṣya ity-ādikaṁ vicāryāha—atreti | atra samāptīkṛte'sminpurāṇaśāstra ity arthaḥ | yasya hareḥ prasādajo brahmeti—prasādasya sattvaguṇatvādbrahmaṇas tu rajaḥsambhavatvādetanna saṁgacchate, tathā rudraḥ krodhasamudbhava iti bhagavato nirguṇa tvātsvarūpeṇa tāmasaḥ krodho'pi na sambhavedyadudbhavo rudraḥ syāt tasmādvākyamidamatiśayoktyārthāntaratātparyakaṁ jñeyam | tac caivam—nirguṇasya bhagavataḥ svabhaktasevini jane prasādaḥ svabhaktadrohiṇi krodhaś ca dṛṣṭastau ca bhaktavatsalasya śuddhasattvasvarūpādevetyata evaṁ vyākhyeyam—yasya prasādajo yasya prasādākhyo bhāgyaviśeṣo brahmaivoktasamastasādhyasādhanotpattiheturatas tadartham eva bhaktairyatanīyaṁ, tathaivoktasādhyasādhanavināśaheturbhagavatkopa evetyatas tadanudbhava eva yatanīyamityetāvatpurāṇatātparyamavadheyam iti bhāvaḥ | nanu yadi śrīśukadevena bhāgavatapurāṇamidamatraiva samāptīkṛtaṁ kathaṁ tarhi prathamaskandhasyāvaśiṣṭadvādaśasya ca śrī-bhāgavatatvamucyate, yajñasya prāguttarakriyayor api yāgatvameva, nāṭakaśāstrasya yathā prākpaścādgatayoḥ prastāvanāśīrvādayor api nāṭakatvam eva tathaiva prathamadvādaśārddhayor api bhāgavatatvam, yathā ca—


    gītā sugītā kartavyā kimanyaiḥ śāstravistaraiḥ | 


    yā svayaṁ padmanābhasya mukhapadmādviniḥsṛtā || 

ityaṣṭādaśādhyāyāḥ śrīgītāyāḥ sarvasyā bhagavatproktatvābhāve'pi bhagavatproktatvamucyate, tathaiva saprathamadvādaśasya śrī-bhāgavatatvaṁ śrīśukadevaproktatvābhāve'pi śrīśukaproktatvañceti samādhiḥ ||1||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (paramātma-sandarbhaḥ 16) : **atra śrī-viṣṇur na kathita iti tena sākṣād abheda evety āyātam | tad uktam—sa u eva viṣṇur [bhā.pu. 3.8.15] iti | śrutiś ca—puruṣo vai nārāyaṇo’kāmayata | atha nārāyaṇād ajo’jāyata, yataḥ prajāḥ sarvāṇi bhūtāni [nā.u. 1] iti | 


    nārāyaṇaḥ paraṁ brahma 


    tattvaṁ nārāyaṇaḥ param |


    ṛtaṁ satyaṁ paraṁ brahma 


    puruṣaṁ kṛṣṇa-piṅgalam || [ma.nā.u. 13.4, 23.1] iti |


    eko ha nārāyaṇa āsīn, na brahmā, na ca śaṅkaraḥ | sa munir bhūtvā samacintayat |


    tata eva vyajāyanta viśvo hiraṇyagarbho’gnir varuṇa-rudrendrā[^37] iti ca |

tasmāt tasyaiva varṇanīyatvam api yuktam ||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **atrānuvarṇyata ity-ādi | prāk-kalpa-līna-sādhaka-bhaktān utpadya mad-bhaktiṁ kariṣyantīti bhāvanā-mayād yasya **prasādāj jātāḥ**, teṣu mukhyo **brahmā** | tathā kālena tad-vimukha-prāye loke tad-vaimukhya-hetuṁ bhāvaṁ prati jātād yasya **krodhāj jātaḥ** svābhakta-śāstā rudra[^38] ity arthaḥ ||1||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** 

etac-chāstrārtha-tātparyācchādanāyātra pañcame |

brahma-jñānopadeśaḥ śrī-munīndreṇa nṛpe kṛtaḥ ||

śāstrārtham upasaṁhṛtya śrīman-munīndraḥ kiñcid ātmanaiva parāmamarśa | aho asādhv-anuṣṭhitaṁ, yan-mahā-rahasya-ratnam asamādhikaṁ sva-hṛdaya-saṁpuṭād udghaṭayya sarva-loka-dṛṣṭi-gocarīkṛtaṁ, yaḥ khalu mat-prabhuṇā, rāja-vidyā rāja-guhyaṁ [gītā 9.1] ity anena vidyānāṁ rājeti guhyānāṁ rājety uktaḥ | punaś ca sarva-guhyatamaṁ bhūyaḥ śṛṇu me [gītā 18.64] ity anena sarva-guhyatama-śabdenoktaḥ, sa khalu bhakti-yogo’tra śāstre mayā parīkṣiti kṛpā-paravaśatayā prāyaḥ prakaṭī-kṛtyaivoktaḥ | tathā hi—


    akāmaḥ sarva-kāmo vā mokṣa-kāma udāra-dhīḥ |


    tīvreṇa bhakti-yogena yajeta puruṣaṁ param || [bhā.pu. 2.3.10] ity-ādinā,


    mukha-bāhūru-pādebhyaḥ puruṣasyāśramaiḥ saha ity atra,


    ya eṣāṁ puruṣaṁ sākṣād ātma-prabhavam īśvaram |


    na bhajanty avajānanti sthānād bhraṣṭāḥ patanty adhaḥ || [bhā.pu. 11.5.2-3]

ity-ādinā cānvaya-vyatirekābhyāṁ bhaktir eva sarva-phala-sādhanatvena pratipāditā | svargādi-sādhanāni karmādīni dūre tāvad āsatāṁ, mokṣa-sādhanatvenātiprasiddhasyāpi jñānasya mokṣa-kāraṇatvaṁ parāstī-kṛtam eva | naiṣkarmyam apy acyuta-bhāva-varjitaṁ na śobhate jñānam alaṁ nirañjanaṁ [bhā.pu. 12.12. 53] iti | caturthāśramiṇo jñānino’pi, sthānād bhraṣṭāḥ patanty adaḥ [bhā.pu. 11.5.3] iti, āruhya kṛcchreṇa paraṁ padaṁ tataḥ patanty adho’nādṛtya yuṣmad-aṅghrayaḥ [bhā.pu. 10.2.32] ity-ādy-ukter jñānānvaye’pi bhaktyā vinā mokṣāsiddheḥ | 


    yat karmabhir yat tapasā jñāna-vairāgyataś ca yat |


    yogena dāma-dharmeṇa śreyobhir itarair api || [bhā.pu. 11.20.32]

iti jñāna-vyatireke’pi bhaktyaiva mokṣa-siddher uktatvāt | mokṣaṁ pratijñānaṁ naivānvaya-vyatirekīti | tad api jñānān mokṣa iti yā prasiddhis tatra jñāna-gatā guṇībhūtā bhaktir eva mokṣaṁ janayet | jñānasya tu nāma-mātreṇaiva kāraṇatā, bhaktyāham ekayā grāhyaḥ [bhā.pu. 11.14.21] iti, na tapo nātma-mīmāṁsā [bhā.pu. 10.23.42] iti, 


    kiṁ vā yogena sāṅkhyena nyāsa-svādhyāyayor api |


    kiṁ vā śreyobhir anyaiś ca na yatrātma-prado hariḥ || [bhā.pu. 4.31.12] 

ity-ādi-vākyair brahmānubhavaṁ prati jñānasya sahakāritāpi, vastuto na pratipāditeti | bhakter eva sādhanatvam upakramopasaṁhārābhyāseṣu prapañcitam | tad api yad antarāntarā jñāna-yogādikam apy upanyastaṁ, tat khalu bhakter utkarṣaṁ tat-tan-matāni ca bhaktān jñāpayitum eveti | 

kiṁ ca, 


    yan-nāmadheya-śravaṇānukīrtanād


    yat-prahvaṇād yat-smaraṇād api kvacit |


    śvādo’pi sadyaḥ savanāya kalpate


    kutaḥ punas te bhagavan nu darśanāt ||


    aho bata śva-paco’to garīyān


    yaj-jihvāgre vartate nāma tubhyam |


    tepus tapas te juhuvuḥ sasnur āryā


    brahmānūcur nāma gṛṇanti ye te || [bhā.pu. 3.33.6-7] iti |


    yan-nāma sakṛc chravaṇāt


    pukkaśo’pi vimucyate saṁsārāt [bhā.pu. 6.16.44] 

ity-ādibhyaḥ kiñcin-mātryāpi bhaktyā mokṣa iti | tathā, 


    tāpa-trayeṇābhihatasya ghore


    santapyamānasya bhavādhvanīśa |


    paśyāmi nānyac charaṇaṁ tavāṅghri-


    dvandvātapatrād amṛtābhivarṣāt || [bhā.pu. 11.19.9] ity uddhava-vākyena,

saṁsāra-sindhum ati-dustaram uttitīrṣor nānyaḥ plavaḥ [bhā.pu. 12.4.40] ity upasaṁhāre mad-vākyena ca tāṁ vinā tu nānyenopāyena saṁsārād api mokṣa ity api nirdhāritam | 

kiṁ ca, bhaktyā tayaiva parayā nirvṛtyā hy apavargam ātyantikaṁ parama-puruṣārtham api svayam āsāditaṁ no evādriyante bhagavadīyatvenaiva parisamāpta-sarvārthāḥ [bhā.pu. 5.6.17] iti | mayi sañjāyate bhaktiḥ ko’nyo’rtho’syāvaśiṣyate [bhā.pu. 11.19.24] iti, na parilaṣanti kecid apavargam api [bhā.pu. 10.87.21] iti, sā brahmaṇi sva-mahimany api nātha mā bhūt [bhā.pu. 4.9.10] iti, svargāpavarga-narakeṣv api tulyārtha-darśinaḥ [bhā.pu. 6.17.28] ity-ādi-vākyebhyaś caturtha-puruṣārtham api tiraskṛtya bhakter eva puruṣārtha-śiromaṇitvaṁ ca mayā sthāpitam |

kiṁ ca, muny-antara-vākyasya prāmāṇyam āpekṣikam eva mad-vākyasya tu prāmāṇyam ātyantikam eveti sarvatra vaikuṇṭhe’pi prasiddhir bhūyasī, parokṣa-vādā ṛṣayaḥ parokṣaṁ mama ca priyaṁ [bhā.pu. 11.21.36] iti bhagavad-ukter mahā-rahasyodghāṭana-paṭiṣṭho bhūtvā bhagavad-apriyaṅkaro’py anubhavam | tad adhunā kiṁ kariṣye ? purāṇārthaś ca samāpti-kṛta eva, bhavatv adhunāpi bhakter mahā-mahimānaṁ saṁvarītuṁ yatiṣye | yathā kaścin mahā-ratnam atigopyaṁ rabhasa-vaśena sarva-lokān sandarśyāpi punaḥ kiñcit parāmṛśya tad alakṣitaṁ sampuṭa-gataṁ kṛtvā mahā-koṣābhyantare saṁsthāpya ratnāntaraṁ bahiḥ-prakāśyānenaivāsmākaṁ sarvārtha-siddhir iti brūte, tathaivādhunā rājānam ahaṁ jñānam upādiśāmi, yathā gamana-samaye tu śukaḥ, parīkṣite jñānam evopadiṣṭavān iti bhagavan-māyā prabhāvāj jñānam evotkṛṣṭaṁ, bhaktis tu tat-sādhanam eveti maṁsyante | 

kiṁ ca, bhakti-siddhān janān prati prādurbhūya bhagavāṁs tān parīkṣamāṇo mokṣaṁ gṛhāṇeti yathā brūte, tathaivānena jñānopadeśenāsya mac-chiṣyasya parīkṣito bhaktimad-vyutpattiṁ ca parīkṣiṣye, parīkṣā ceyaṁ sarvajñenāpi jagaty asmin parīkṣid-bhakti-niṣṭhā jñāpanārthā jñeyā | 

kiṁ ca, bhakti-jñānayoḥ phalam antato muktir eva kevalam ity anabhijña-vyākhyānaṁ naiva mad-abhiprāya-sambandhaṁ jñeyam | yato, 


    rājan patir gurur alaṁ bhavatāṁ yadūnāṁ


    daivaṁ priyaḥ kula-patiḥ kva ca kiṅkaro vaḥ |


    astv evam aṅga bhagavān bhajatāṁ mukundo


    muktiṁ dadāti karhicit sma na bhakti-yogam || [bhā.pu. 5.6.18]

ity uktavatā mayā mukteḥ sakāśād api bhakter utkṛṣṭa-phalatvasya pratipāditatvāt, na copadeṣṭavyenānena jñānena parīkṣito nirvāṇa-mukti-prāptir evety āśaṅkanīyam | 


    sa vai mahā-bhāgavataḥ parīkṣid


    yenāpavargākhyam adabhra-buddhiḥ |


    jñānena vaiyāsaki-śabditena


    bheje khagendra-dhvaja-pāda-mūlam || [bhā.pu. 1.18.16]

iti mad-abhiprāyābhijñenānena mac-chiṣyeṇa sūtenāgre vakṣyamāṇatvāt | mayi rājan patir gurur alam ity atra bhavadbhyas tu sva-bhakti-yogaṁ dadāti | iti parīkṣitaḥ prema-bhakti-prāptir abhivyañjitaiva na copadiṣyamānenānenaiva dehādi-vyatiriktātma-jñānena brahmānubhavaḥ siddhyet | kiṁ tv asyāpi jñānasya bhaktyā nirjayenaiva yad uktaṁ bhagavatā—


    dravyaṁ deśaḥ phalaṁ kālo jñānaṁ karma ca kārakaḥ |


    śraddhāvasthākṛtir niṣṭhā traiguṇyaḥ sarva eva hi ||


    sarve guṇa-mayā bhāvāḥ puruṣāvyakta-dhiṣṭhitāḥ |


    dṛṣṭaṁ śrutam anudhyātaṁ buddhyā vā puruṣarṣabha ||


    etāḥ saṁsṛtayaḥ puṁso guṇa-karma-nibandhanāḥ |


    yeneme nirjitāḥ saumya guṇā jīvena citta-jāḥ |


    bhakti-yogena man-niṣṭho mad-bhāvāya prapadyate || [bhā.pu. 11.25.30-32] iti |

kiṁ ca, bhagavad-bhaktasya mokṣa-kāmatve’pi nāsti jñānena prayojanaṁ, yad uktaṁ svayaṁ bhagavatā—


    jñāne karmaṇi yoge ca vārtāyāṁ daṇḍa-dhāraṇe |


    yāvān artho nṛṇāṁ tāta tāvāṁs te’haṁ catur-vidhaḥ || [bhā.pu. 11.29.33] iti |

tasmād anena sarvās te jñānopadeśenāsya śāstrasya spaṣṭatayaiva mohinī-sādharmyaṁ pratipādayiṣye | yathā hy asurāḥ prema-sudhayā vañcitā eva bhaveyur iti | api ca jñānopadeśāt prāg ekaṁ vākyaṁ punar vyañjanayā vṛttyā bhaktān prīṇayituṁ bhaktir asamrakṣitam eva kariṣye | tad-anantaraṁ jñānopadeśa-vākyāny api yāni bhakti-pratikūlāni vakṣye, tāny apy antar-bhūta-bhakty-anukūlārthāny eva kariṣye ity-ādikaṁ vicāryāha—atreti | atra samāptīkṛte’smin purāṇa-śāstra ity arthaḥ | yasya hareḥ prasādajo brahmeti prasādasya sattva-guṇatvāt, brahmaṇas tu rajaḥ-sambhavatvād etan na saṅgacchate | tathā rudraḥ krodha-samudbhava iti bhagavato nirguṇatvāt svarūpeṇa tāmasaḥ krodho’pina sambhavet | yad-udbhavo rudraḥ syāt tasmād vākyam atiśayoktyā arthāntara-tātparyakaṁ jñeyam |

tac caivaṁ—nirguṇasya bhagavataḥ sva-bhakta-sevini jane prasādaḥ, sva-bhakta-drohiṇi krodhaś ca dṛṣṭaḥ | tau ca bhakta-vatsalasya śuddha-sattva-svarūpāv eveti | ata evaṁ vyākhyeyaṁ—yasya prasādajaḥ yasya prasādottho bhāgya-viśeṣo brahmaivokta-samasta-sādhya-sādhanotpatti-hetur atas tad-artham eva bhaktair yatanīyam | tathaivokta-sādhya-sādhana-vināśa-hetur bhagavat-kopa evety atas tad-udbhava eva yatanīyam ity etat purāṇa-tātparyam avadheyam iti bhāvaḥ | 

nanu yadi śrī-śukadevena śrī-bhāgavata-purāṇam idam atra samāptī-kṛtaṁ kathaṁ tarhi prathama-skandhasyāvaśiṣṭa-dvādaśasya ca śrī-bhāgavatatvam ? ucyate—yajñasya yathā prāg uttara-kriyā-kalāpayor api yogyatvam eva, nāṭaka-śāstrasya yathā prāk-paścād-gatayoḥ prastāvanāśīrvādayor api nāṭakatvam eva, tathaiva prathama-dvādaśārdhayor api śrī-bhāgavatatvam | yathā ca—


    gītā sugītā kartavyā kim anyaiḥ śāstra-vistaraiḥ |


    yā svayaṁ padmanābhasya mukha-padmād viniḥsṛtā || 

ity aṣṭādaśādhyāyyāḥ gītāyāḥ sarvasyā bhagavat-proktatvābhāve’pi bhagavat-proktatvam ucyate | tathaivāsya dvādaśa-skandhasya śrī-bhāgavatasya sarvasya śuka-proktatvābhāve’pi śuka-proktatvam iti samādhiḥ ||1|| 

 **...**

**|| 12.5.2 ||**

**tvaṁ tu rājan mariṣyeti paśu-buddhim imāṁ jahi |**

**na jātaḥ prāg abhūto’dya deha-vat tvaṁ na naṅkṣyasi ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tvaṁ punaḥ kṛtārtha evety anusmārayati—tvaṁ tv iti | **paśu-buddhim** avivekam | yasmān **na naṅkṣyasi** | kutaḥ ? ity ata āha—na jāta iti | yathā dehaḥ prāg abhūta evādya jāto naṅkṣyati | na caivaṁ tvaṁ pūrvaṁ nābhūḥ, na cādya jāto’sy ato na naṅkṣyasi ||2||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **mariṣya iti chedaḥ, sandhirārṣaḥ | he rājann iti—maddattajñānena rājasveti bhāvaḥ | atha jñānopadeśaḥ—tvaṁ tv iti | turbhinnopakrame | mariṣyetīti sandhirārṣaḥ| paśūnāmiva buddhiṁ jahi vivekena nāśayeti | 


    tamopayātaṁ pratiyantu viprā gaṅgā ca devī dhṛtacittamīśe | 


    dvijopasṛṣṭaḥ kuhakastakṣako vā daśatvalaṁ gāyata viṣṇugāthāḥ || 

iti bhāgavataśravaṇātprāgeva pratijñātavatas tasya paśubuddheḥ prasaktir eva nāstītyatas tannivartako jñānopadeśaṁ na rājānaṁ prati sambhavetkituṁ ye paśubuddhayastāneva prati, tadapi rājann iti sambodhanaṁ tu tam eva lakṣyīkṛtyānyaviṣayakasyāpyupadeśasya vaktumaucityāttasyaiva tacchiṣyatvāt yathā sarvaviṣayakopyupadeśaḥ śrīgītāyāmarjunaṁ lakṣyīkṛtyaivoktaḥ | vivekamevāha—na jāta iti | yathā dehaḥ prāgabhūta evedānīṁ jāto naṅkṣyati, na tathā tvaṁ jātaḥ nāpi prāgabhūto nāpyadya ṅkṣyasi, tvaṁ jīvātmā jaḍādyupādheḥ pṛthagevāsīti nāyaṁ bhaktipratikūlorthaḥ ||2||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **prathama-skandhānte tatra mriyamāṇasya kṛtyaṁ yat pṛṣṭaṁ, tat tu svārthaṁ tavāyuktam ity abhipretya pratyācaṣṭe—tvaṁ tv iti | **paśu-buddhim** iti yataḥ paśor eva sā buddhir yuktā, na tu taveti bhāvaḥ | **na jāta** ity antar-bhūtānaśvara-bhagavat-pārṣada-dehatvād iti bhāvaḥ | vyatireke dṛṣṭāntaḥ **dehavat** dṛśyamāna-deha eva ||2||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** atha jñānopadeśaḥ—tvaṁ tv iti | **tur** bhinnopakrame | **mariṣyetīty** ārṣaṁ mariṣyāmīti | **paśūnām **iva** buddhiṁ** **jahi** vivekena nāśayeti, 


    taṁ mopayātaṁ pratiyantu viprā


    gaṅgā ca devī dhṛta-cittam īśe |


    dvijopasṛṣṭaḥ kuhakas takṣako vā


    daśatv alaṁ gāyata viṣṇu-gāthāḥ || [bhā.pu. 1.19.15] 

iti śrī-bhāgavata-śravaṇāt pūrvam eva pratijñātavatas tasya paśu-buddheḥ prasaktir eva tasya nāstīty atas tan-nivartako jñānopadeśo na rājānaṁ prati sambhavet, kintu ye paśu-buddhayo’nye tān eva prati tad api rājann iti sambodhanaṁ tu tam eva lakṣyī-kṛtyānya-viṣayakasyāpy upadeśasya vaktum aucityāt tasyaiva tac-chiṣyatvāt | yathā sarva-viṣayako’py upadeśo gītāyām arjunaṁ lakṣīkṛtyaivoktaḥ vivekam evāha—**na jāta** iti | yathā dehaḥ **prāg abhūta** eva idānīṁ jāto’dya naṅkṣyati, na tathā tvaṁ jātaḥ, nāpi prāg abhūta, nāpy adya naṅkṣyati, tvaṁ jīvātmā jaḍādy-upādheḥ pṛthag evāsīti nāyaṁ bhakti-pratikulo’rthaḥ ||2||

 **...**

**|| 12.5.3 ||**

**na bhaviṣyasi bhūtvā tvaṁ putra-pautrādi-rūpavān |**

**bījāṅkuravad dehāder vyatirikto yathānalaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **nanu bījād aṅkura-vat svasmāt putra-rūpeṇāpi svayam eva bhavati, yathāha śrutiḥ—


    aṅgād aṅgāt saṁbhavasi hṛdayād abhijāyase | 


    ātmā vai putra-nāmāsi sa jīva śaradaḥ śatam || iti | 

tataḥ punar aṅkurād bījam iva pautrādi-rūpeṇāpi svayam eva bhavati | pitā putreṇa pitṛmān yoni-yonau iti śruteḥ | atas teṣu naśyatsu kathaṁ na naṅkṣyāmīti cet tatrāha—na bhaviṣyasīti | bhūtvā putra-pautrādi-rūpavān bījāṅkuravan na bhaviṣyasi | yasmād dehāder vyatiriktas tvaṁ yathānalaḥ kāṣṭhāt | dehād deho jāyate nātmeti bhāvaḥ ||3||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **atrākṣipati—nanv iti | aṅgādaṅgātpratyekaṁ bhinnādbhinnādaṅgādbhinnabhinnamaṅgaṁ bhavatītyabhiprāyaḥ | sa tvaṁ śaradaḥ varṣāṇāṁ śataṁ jīvetyarthaḥ | tatā putrāt | yoniyonau pautraprapautrādijanmani pitā tattatputreṇa pitṛmān pitṛpaṅktibhāgbhavatīty arthaḥ | yataḥ putrādayo'pi tadrūpā evāto hetoḥ | teṣu putrādiṣu | iti bhāva iti—ajo nityaḥ śāśvato'yaṁ purāṇaḥ ity-ādiśruterityāśayaḥ ||3||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **dṛśyamānaṁ cāsminn āveśābhāvān na bhaviṣyatīti ||3||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** yathā deho bhūtvā bhūtvā punar bhavati, na tathā tvam ātmā, ity āha—neti | putra-pautrādi-rūpavān iti, yathāha śrutiḥ—


    aṅgād aṅgāt saṁbhavasi hṛdayād abhijāyase | 


    ātmā vai putra-nāmāsi sa jīva śaradaḥ śatam || iti | 

bījāṅkuravat svayam eva putro bhavati | tataḥ punar aṅkurāt bījam iva pautro’pi svayam eva bhavati, tathā tvaṁ bhaviṣyasi | yasmād dehāder upādher jaḍatvam ātmā vyatirikto bhinnaḥ | yathānalaḥ kāṣṭhāt | dehād deho jāyate nātmeti bhāvaḥ ||3||

 **...**

**|| 12.5.4 ||**

**svapne yathā śiraś-chedaṁ pañcatvādy ātmanaḥ svayam |**

**yasmāt paśyati dehasya tata ātmā hy ajo’maraḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **janmādīnāṁ deha-dharmatvaṁ dṛṣṭāntena prapañcayati—svapne yathātmanaḥ śiraś chedaṁ svayaṁ paśyati, evaṁ jāgaraṇe’pi | yasmād dehasya pañcatvādikaṁ paśyati, tatas tadvad evātmana idaṁ bhrama-mātram | vastutaś cātmājo’maraś cety arthaḥ | tad uktam—


    ātmanaḥ pitṛ-putrābhyām anumeyau bhavāpyayau | 


    na bhavāpyaya-vastūnām abhijño’dvaya-lakṣaṇaḥ || ity-ādi ||4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tadvadeva svapnavadeva | ātmana idaṁ pañcatvādi | ity artha iti—yajjanyaṁ tadvināśīti vyāpterdehasyaiva janyatvānmṛtyujanmādi, ātmanastvajanyatvāttanneti bhāvaḥ | taddehasya maraṇādi | uktam ekādaśaskandhe | ātmana iti ślokas tu vyākhyātacara eva | janmādyavasthāvato dehātmanaḥ pārthakyaṁ dṛṣṭāntenāha—svapna iti | na hi svaśiraśchedaṁ svayaṁ paśyati, ata ātmā tataḥ pṛthageva taddraṣṭā, tathaiva jāgare'pi tasmātpṛthagbhūta evātmano dehasya pañcatvādi paśyati, ato hetorātmājo'maro janmamṛtyuhīna iti ||4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **sādhāraṇānām api tad-āveśo’bhūma evety āha—svapna iti pañcabhiḥ ||4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** janma-maraṇādy-avasthāvato dehād ātmanaḥ pārthakyaṁ dṛṣṭāntena spaṣṭayati—svapne iti | nahi sva-śiraś-chedaṁ svayaṁ paśyet, ata ātmā tataḥ pṛthag eva | tad-draṣṭā, tathaiva jāgare’pi tasmāt pṛthag-bhūta eva ātmano dehasya pañcatvādi paśyati | tato hetor ātmā ajo janma-rahitaḥ, amaro mṛtyu-rahitaś ca ||4||

 **...**

**|| 12.5.5 ||**[^39]

**ghaṭe bhinne ghaṭākāśa ākāśaḥ syād yathā purā |**

**evaṁ dehe mṛte jīvo brahma sampadyate punaḥ ||**[^40]

**madhvācāryaḥ (bhāgavata-tātparyam) :** 


    mahākāśo bahiḥ-sthaś ca ghaṭādy antaḥ-stha eva ca |


    dvedhā samudito’nyau ca dvāv ākāśau[^41] prakīrtitau ||


    ghaṭa-rūpas tad-anyaś ca mahākāśāt paro laghuḥ |


    mahākāśavad evātra paramātmā sanātanaḥ ||


    ghaṭānta-stha-mahākāśa-pratimo’ntargato hariḥ |


    ghaṭasyāntargatākāśo mahākāśāt paro mataḥ ||[^42]


    tad vada devādayaḥ sarve jīvā mukty-upabhoginaḥ |


    tamogāś caiva ye sarve ghaṭa-rūpa khavan narāḥ || iti tattva-saṁhitāyām |


    pratyekaṁ viṣṇu-rūpāṇāṁ bhrānti-mātrā bhidā matā |


    jagataś caiva viṣṇoś ca satyo bhedaḥ sadaiva tu ||


    yathākāśa-ghaṭau nityaṁ bhinnāv eva parasparam |


    evam īśo jagac caiva bhinnāv eva parasparam ||[^43] iti ca ||5||

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **yasmād dehopādhiko’yam ātmano janmādi-saṁsāra-bhramaḥ, tasmād upādhi-nivṛttau mucyata iti sa-dṛṣṭāntam āha—ghaṭa iti | yathā purā ghaṭopādheḥ pūrvam iva punar ghaṭe bhinne tad-antar-varty-avakāśa ākāśa eva syāt, tathā | evaṁ dehe mṛte tattva-jñānena līne sati ||5||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **yathā purā tannāśātpūrvamapyākāśa eva, evaṁ jīvo dehe mṛte nirupādhiryathā punarbrahma sampadyate, tathā purāpi brahmaiva sanbrahmāpyeti iti śruteḥ | tadapyātmano liṅgaśarīrādhyāso durjaro yaḥ so'yaṁ jñāne sati nivartate, ihaikyātmavādināṁ dṛṣṭāntam āha ghaṭa iti | bhinne vidīrṇe | yathā pureti—ghaṭotpatteḥ pūrvaṁ yathā mahānākāśas tathā ghaṭe bhagnapīty arthaḥ | evaṁ dehe mṛte tattvajñānena līne sati | aprakaṭārtham āha—yatheti | nanu dehātpṛthagbhūto yathā jīvātmā tathā paramātmāpi, tāvubhāvapi dehāvṛtau dṛśyete, liṅge bhagne satyubhāvapi muktau syātām iti kathaṁ nocyate | atra paramātmana āvaraṇaṁ kālatraye'pi nāstīti sadṛṣṭāntam āha—ghaṭa iti, yathā pureti | ghaṭe vartamāne'pi ākāśaḥ | ākāśa evānāvṛtas tathā ghaṭe bhagnapīty arthaḥ | ākāśasya ghaṭāntar-bahir-madhye'pi vartamānatvād ākāśaṁ ghaṭaḥ katham āvṛṇotv iti bhāvaḥ | evaṁ dehe'mṛte vartamāne'pi ajīvo jīva-bhinnaḥ paramātmā brahma sarva-vyāpakaḥ sann eva sampadyate virājate ||5||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **deha iti deha-dvayam ity arthaḥ | brahma-tattvaṁ[^44] sampadyate yathā-yathaṁ prāpnoti | atropādheḥ saṁyoga eva parityajyate, na tu tasya mithyātvaṁ pratipādyate[^45] ||5||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **tad apy ātmano liṅga-śarīrādhyāso durjaro yaḥ, so’yaṁ jñāne sati nivartata ity atraikātma-vādināṁ dṛṣṭāntam āha—ghaṭa iti | **bhinne** vidīrṇe | **yathā purā** iti ghaṭotpatteḥ pūrvaṁ, yathā mahān **evākāśas** tathaiva ghaṭe bhagne’pīty arthaḥ, evaṁ **dehe mṛte** tattva-jñānena līne sati aprakaṭo’rtho, yathā |

nanu dehāt pṛthag-bhūto yathā jīvātmā, tathā paramātmāpi, tāv ubhāv api dehāvṛtau dṛśyete | liṅge bhaṅge saty ubhāv api muktau syātām iti kathaṁ nocyate ? atra paramātmana āvaraṇaṁ kāla-traye’pi nāstīti sa-dṛṣṭāntam āha—ghaṭa iti | yathā pureti ghaṭe vartamāne’pi **ākāśa ākāśa eva** yathā anāvṛtaṁ tathaiva ghaṭe bhagne’pīty arthaḥ | ākāśasya ghaṭāntar-bahir-madhye’pi vartamānatvād ākāśaṁ ghaṭaḥ katham āvṛṇotv iti bhāvaḥ | evaṁ dehe amṛte vartamāne’pi ajīvo jīva-bhinna-paramātma brahma sarva-vyāpakaḥ sann eva sampadyate virājate ||5||

 **...**

**|| 12.5.6 ||**

**manaḥ sṛjati vai dehān guṇān karmāṇi cātmanaḥ |**

**tan manaḥ sṛjate māyā tato jīvasya saṁsṛtiḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **jñānena layaṁ bhāvayituṁ māyā-kṛtam ātmano dehādy-upādhi-saṁbandha-prakāram āha—mana iti | mana ātmano dehādīn sṛjati | tac ca mano māyā sṛjati | tato māyādy-upādhi-samudāyāj jīvasya saṁsṛtiḥ, na svataḥ ||6||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **svāpna-dehavaj jāgare'py ātmano nānā-dehān guṇān karmāṇi ca mana eva saṅkalpātmakaṁ sṛjati kalpayati | tan manaḥ svāpna-saṅkalpādivan māyā sṛjati, tato jīvasya saṁsṛtir māyaivety arthaḥ | yad vā, manaḥ pūrva-karma-preritaṁ sad-guṇān sattvādīn sṛjati paryāyeṇa vibhāvayati, tato guṇa-mayāni vividhāni karmāṇi sṛjati, tataḥ karmānurūpān dehān sṛjatīti bhāvaḥ | jñānena layaṁ sambhāvayituṁ māyā-kṛtam ātmano dehādy-upādhi-sambandha-prakāram āha—mana ātmano dehādīn sṛjati | tad uktam—yato yato dhāvati daiva-coditaṁ mano vikārātmakam [bhā.pu. 9.4.51] ity-ādi | tato mano māyā sṛjati | tato māyādyupādhisamudāyāt ||6||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **māyādīnāṁ sraṣṭṛtvaṁ yat kiñcit tad-dhetutvāt ||6||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **jñānena layaṁ sambhāvayituṁ māyā-kṛtam ātmano dehādy-upādhi-sambandha-prakāram āha—mana ātmano dehādīn sṛjati | yad uktaṁ—yato yato dhāvati daiva-coditaṁ mano-vikārātmakaṁ [bhā.pu. 10.1.42] ity-ādi | tac ca mano māyā sṛjati, tato māyādy-upādhi-samudāyāt ||6||

 **...**

**|| 12.5.7 ||**

**snehādhiṣṭhāna-varty-agni-saṁyogo yāvad īyate |**

**tāvad dīpasya dīpatvam evaṁ deha-kṛto bhavaḥ ||**

**rajaḥ-sattva-tamo-vṛttyā jāyate’tha vinaśyati |**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **yasmād upādhi-nibandhano jīvasya saṁsāro’tas tan-nāśe jīvatvaṁ gacchatīty etad eva sa-dṛṣṭāntam āha sārdhena—sneheti | **dīpasya** jyotiṣo **dīpatvaṁ** jvālā-rūpaḥ pariṇāmaḥ | tatra taila-sthānīyaṁ karma, tad-**adhiṣṭhāna**-sthānīyaṁ manaḥ, **varti**-sthānīyo dehaḥ, **agni-saṁyoga**-sthānīyaś caitanyādhyāsaḥ | dīpa-sthānīyaṁ saṁsāra iti yojyam | **deha-kṛto** deha-nibandhanaḥ | yad vā, deha-kṛto manaso na tv ātmanaḥ ||7||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **yasmādupādhinibandhano jīvasya saṁsāro'tastannāśo naśyatīti sadṛṣṭāntam āha—tataratāvad ity arthaḥ | tatra dārṣṭāntike | tadadhiṣṭānasthānīyaṁ tailādhiṣṭānaśarāvasthānīyam | dehanibandhano dehādhyāsahetukaḥ | dehādhyāso'pi manastādātmyaivetyāha—yadveti | dehakṛto dehasambandhakṛtaḥ | bhavaḥ saṁsāraḥ ||7||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : dīpasya** jyotiṣo **dīpatvaṁ** snehādy-adhiṣṭhātṛtvena vikāritvam ity arthaḥ | tatas tasmāt svayaṁ-jyotir-ādi-rūpatvād anantopamaḥ paramātma-sadṛśaḥ, dvā suparṇā sayujā sakhāyā [mu.u. 1.1.3, śve.u. 4.6] iti śrutau, suparṇāv etau sadṛśau sakhāyau [bhā.pu. 11.11.6] ity ekādaśe ||7-8||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** etad eva sa-dṛṣṭāntam āha—sārdhena sneheti | **dīpasya** jyotiṣaḥ **dīpatvaṁ** jvālā-rūpaḥ pariṇāmaḥ, tatra taila-sthānīyaṁ karma, tad-adhiṣṭhāna-sthānīyaṁ manaḥ, varti-sthānīyo dehaḥ, agni-saṁyoga-sthānīyaś caitanyādhyāsaḥ, dīpa-sthānīyaḥ saṁsāra iti yojyam | **deha-kṛto** deha-saṁyoga-nibandhano’yaṁ bhavaḥ saṁsāraḥ ||7||

 **...**

**|| 12.5.8 ||**

**na tatrātmā svayaṁ-jyotir yo vyaktāvyaktayoḥ paraḥ |**

**ākāśa iva cādhāro dhruvo’nantopamas tataḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ato dīpavat saṁsāra eva naśyati, na tv ātma jyotirvad ity āha—neti | **na** tu **tatra** pratīyamāna ātmā | kutaḥ ? ity ata āha—ya iti | **vyaktāvyaktayoḥ** sthūla-sūkṣma-dehayoḥ **paro**’nyaḥ, yataḥ **svayaṁ-jyotiḥ** | paratvaṁ prapañcayati—**ākāśa iveti** | **ādhāro** dehādeḥ prapañcasya | **dhruvo** nirvikāraḥ | nāsty anta upamā ca yasya so’**nantopamaḥ **| tato vibhuḥ ||8||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **yato dīpasthānīyaḥ saṁsāro'to hetaḥ | tatra dehe | ato dehadvayabhinnatvāt | ātmānāśe hetuḥ—ya iti | ya ātmā | yad vā, anantenākāśenopamayita ityanantopamaḥ, ākāśo yathāsaṅgas tathetyarthaḥ | anantaṁ suravartma kham ity amaraḥ | tato vyāpakaḥ, tanoteḥ ktaḥ ||8||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** _na vyākhyātam._

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** ato dīpavat saṁsāra eva naśyati, na tv ātmā jyotirvad ity āha—neti | na tu tatra pratīyamāna ātmā | kutaḥ ? ity ata āha—ya iti | **vyaktāvyaktayoḥ paraḥ** sthūla-sūkṣma-dehābhyām anyaḥ, yataḥ **svayaṁ-jyotiḥ** | ata eva hetoḥ **ādhāro** dehādi-prapañcasya **dhruvo** nirvikāraḥ | nāsty anta upamā ca yasya so’**nantopamaḥ** | pakṣe, yaḥ khalu vyaktāvyaktayoḥ kārya-kāraṇayoḥ paraḥ kāraṇa-rūpaḥ paramātmā, sa tu ākāśa iva sarvādhāra ity-ādi ||8||

 **...**

**|| 12.5.9 ||**

**evam ātmānam ātma-stham ātmanaivāmṛśa prabho |**

**buddhyānumāna-garbhiṇyā vāsudevānucintayā ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **atas tvam evaṁ cintayety āha—evam iti | **ātma-sthaṁ** dehādy-upādhi-sthitam | **āmṛśa** vicāraya | **anumāna-garbhiṇyā** draṣṭṛ-dṛśyānvaya-vyatireka-yuktayā ||9||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **yata ātmā dehādeḥ pṛthagato hetoḥ | dṛṣṭa-dṛśyayor ātma-dehayor anvaya-vyatirekābhyāṁ yuktayā | tathā hi—jīvaś cetano draṣṭṛtvāt, paramātmavat, yaś cetano na bhavati sa draṣṭāpi na bhavati, yathā ghaṭaḥ | evaṁ deho jaḍo dṛśyatvāt, ghaṭavat, yo dṛśyo na bhavati sa jaḍo'pi na bhavati, yathātmeti | 

kiṁ ca, ātmā sthāyī, avasthā-traya-sākṣitvāt, paramātmavat deho vināśī ādy-antayor avidyamānatvāt, śukti-rajatavat, ity-ādy-anvaya-vyatirekānumāna-sahakṛtayā buddhyā | evaṁ vakṣyamāṇa-rītyā | vāsudevasyānucintā tātparyeṇāvagatir yasyāṁ buddhyāntayā | yad vā, buddhyā śravaṇaja-bodhenānumāna-garbhiṇyā manana-sahakṛtena vasanty asminn iti vāsu adhiṣṭhānaṁ paraṁ brahma, devayatīti devaḥ sarvāvabhāsakaḥ sākṣi-cid-ātmā eva tad-anucintayā nididhyāsanenāvagata-svarūpaṁ tvāṁ vipra-vākyena coditas takṣako na dhakṣyati na bhasmīkariṣyati | na kevalaṁ takṣaka eva tvāṁ na dhakṣyaty api tu mṛtyu-hetavo'nye'pi siṁha-vyāghra-rogādayo nopadhakṣyanti | tatra hetuḥ—mṛtyūnām api teṣām api mṛtyum mārayan mṛtyunāntakam ity ukteḥ | tatrāpi hetuḥ—īśvaraṁ jñāna-balenāvāpteśvara-bhāvam | atra hetu-garbhita-viśeṣaṇa-dvayaṁ pratīyate | svāmi-caraṇair atra hetava iti bahutvaṁ tu mṛtyavas tvāṁ yato nopadhakṣyanti ity api hetutvenaivābhipretaṁ deha-bhinnatvāt | buddhy-ādi-pravartakatvena yadātmano'numānaṁ tad eva garbhe yasya tad-yuktayā tad-vyavasāyavatyā, yathā buddhy-ādīni karaṇāni kartṛ-prayojyāni karaṇatvād vāsyādivad iti kartā cātmaiva sa ca vāsudeva eva, sarvatra lakṣyaḥ | sakalam idam ahaṁ ca vāsudeva ity evānucintā yasyāṁ tādṛśayā ||9||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **pūrvoktātideśenopadiśati—evam iti | **ātmānam** antar-bhūta-bhagavat-pārṣada-bhāvātmakam **ātmanā** jīva-svarūpeṇa saha **ātma-sthaṁ buddhyāmṛśa** | kīdṛśyā ? pūrvokt**ānumāna-garbhiṇyā**, tathā **vāsudeva**-sthānugata-**cintā** yasyāṁ tayā ||9||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** _na vyākhyātam._

 **...**

**|| 12.5.10 ||**

**codito vipra-vākyena na tvāṁ dhakṣyati takṣakaḥ |**

**mṛtyavo nopadhakṣyanti mṛtyūnāṁ mṛtyum īśvaram ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **evaṁ ca sati tvāṁ takṣako na dahed ity āha—codita iti | tatra hetavaḥ—mṛtyava iti | mṛtyu-hetavaḥ ||10||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tvām ātmānaṁ dehāt pṛthag-bhūtam | takṣakasya kā vārtā svayaṁ mṛtyavo'pi mūrtimantaḥ nahi vāsudeva-rūpaṁ tvāṁ dehaṁ takṣakaṁ ca dhakṣyanti svasya svayaṁ hananāyogāt, brahma-śāpādīnāṁ vyartha-prāyatvād iti bhāvaḥ ||10||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tvāṁ pūrvokta-rūpaṁ, yato mṛtyava iti ||10||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** **ātma-sthaṁ** dehādy-upādhi-sthitam **ātmanā** manasā **āmṛśa** vicāraya, buddhy-ādi-pravartakatvena yadātmano’**numānaṁ** tad eva **garbhaḥ**, tad-yuktayā **buddhyā** sad-vyavasāyavatyā saha **vāsudevasyānucintā** yasyāṁ tayā | tvām ātmānaṁ dehāt pṛthag-bhūtaṁ takṣakasya kā vārtā, svayaṁ mṛtyavo’pi mūrtimantaḥ | pakṣe, īśvaram upādhi-muktatvād dehādy-apara-tantraṁ, mṛtyūnāṁ bhakty-antarāyāṇāṁ mṛtyuṁ nāśa-hetuṁ, tvāṁ prāpya bhakty-antarā yā brahma-śāpādyā eva, vaiyarthyān naṣṭā eva babhūvur ity arthaḥ ||9-10||

 **...**

**|| 12.5.11-12 ||**

**ahaṁ brahma paraṁ dhāma brahmāhaṁ paramaṁ padam |**

**evaṁ samīkṣya cātmānam ātmany ādhāya niṣkale ||**

**daśantaṁ takṣakaṁ pāde lelihānaṁ viṣānanaiḥ |**

**na drakṣyasi śarīraṁ ca viśvaṁ ca pṛthag ātmanaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **vimarśa-prakāraṁ darśayaṁs takṣakādarśanaṁ darśayati dvābhyām, yo’**haṁ** sa **brahmaiva**, yad **brahma** tad **aham** eveti **samīkṣan** | tatrāhaṁ brahmeti bhāvanayā jīvasya śokādi-nivṛttiḥ | brahmāham iti bhāvanayā ca brahmaṇaḥ pārokṣya-nivṛttir bhavatīti vyatihāro darśitaḥ | **niṣkale** nirupādhau | **ātmani** brahmaṇi ||11||

**viṣa**-yuktair **ānanair** **daśantaṁ** grasantaṁ **takṣakam** | **lelihānaṁ** sarpam | yad vā, lelihānaṁ jihvābhir oṣṭha-prāntān saniṣpeṣam āsvādayantam | **ātmanaḥ** pṛthak ||12||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **paraṁ dhāma sarvāvabhāsakatvena dehendriyādi-dharmair aspaṣṭañjyotiḥ svarūpam | paramaṁ sarva-bādhāvadhitvena paramārthaṁ padaṁ padanīyam | tatra vimarśa | ādinā bhayādi-grahaḥ | pārokṣya-nivṛttiḥ sākṣātkāraḥ | parasparīkaraṇaṁ vyatihāraḥ || oṣṭha-prāntāsvādane ca lelihāno bhujaṅgame ity abhidhānād arthāntaram āha—yad veti | niṣpeṣaḥ peṣaṇābhāvābhīkṣṇyāpeṣaṇakeṣu ca ity abhidhānāt sa-niṣpeṣaṁ paunaḥpunyena sahitam ||11-12||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **kuto’ham īśvaraḥ ? tad-eka-pālyaitvābhimānena tac-chaktyaiva sva-śakty-abhimānena vā tad-abhedābhimānād ity āha—ahaṁ brahmeti yugmakena | **niṣkale** māyātīte | **ātmani** brahmaṇi **ādhāya** nivedya | **ātmanaḥ pṛthak** **yac charīraṁ viśvaṁ ca**, tat tan **na drakṣasy** eveti, kim uta tad-upakāreṇa svāpakāraṁ manyasa iti ||11||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **vimarṣa-prakāraṁ darśayan takṣaka-daṁśanaṁ darśayati dvābhyām | yo’haṁ sa brahmaivāhaṁ, na saṁsārīti bhāvanayā śokādi-nivṛttiḥ, brahmāham iti aham eva brahmeti bhāvanayā ca brahmaṇaḥ parokṣa-nivṛttir bhavatīti vyatīhāro darśitaḥ | niṣkale nirupādhau ātmani brahmaṇi | 

pakṣe, ahaṁ dhāma sūryopamasya paśyasya tviṭ-kaṇaś cit-kaṇa evety arthaḥ | gṛha-deha-tviṭ-prabhāvā dhāmāni ity amaraḥ | kīdṛśam ? brahma-param, nārāyaṇa-paro vipraḥ itivad brahmopāsakam ity arthaḥ | ata eva brahmāhaṁ brahmaṇaḥ paśyasyaivāham iti ṣaṣṭhī-tatpuruṣaḥ | evaṁ paramaṁ padaṁ brahma-svarūpaṁ caraṇāravindaṁ vā samīkṣya ātmānaṁ svam ātmani paramātmani kṛṣṇe niṣkale niṣko vakṣo’laṅkāras tadvati | viṣānanair viṣa-yuktair ānanair daśantaṁ lelihānaṁ jihvābhir oṣṭha-prāntaṁ sa-niṣpeṣam āsvādayantaṁ takṣakaṁ na drakṣyasi, nāpi tena daṣṭaṁ śarīraṁ ca, ātmanaḥ pṛthag-bhūtaṁ viśvaṁ ca pakṣe śrī-kṛṣṇa-caraṇāravinda-sākṣātkārānanda-mūrcchāṁ prāptas tvaṁ na drakṣyasīti ||11-12||

 **...**

**|| 12.5.13 ||**

**etat te kathitaṁ tāta yad ātmā pṛṣṭavān nṛpa |**

**harer viśvātmanaś ceṣṭāṁ kiṁ bhūyaḥ śrotum icchasi ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **hareś ceṣṭām ātmā tvaṁ yat pṛṣṭavāṁs tad etat te kathitam | śiṣyasya kṛtārthatā-parīkṣaṇāya pṛcchati—kim iti ||13||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **he nṛpeti—nṛbhyo bhaya-janakatvena vikṣepakebhyaḥ kāla-janma-jarādibhyaḥ pāyate rakṣyata iti nṛpaḥ, tathā ca mayā tattvopadeśenānvartha-nāmā kṛto'sīti bhāvaḥ | ataḥ paraṁ śrotavyaṁ nāstīty āha—kiṁ bhūya iti | 

atra sandarbhaḥ—līlā-kathā-rasikasya tasya pūrvoktenātirucim ālakṣyopasaṁharati—etat ta iti | te tubhyam | tvaṁ tu rājan mariṣyeti ity-ādinā kathitam | nanu mamānabhīṣṭam anupakrāntaṁ ca tat kathaṁ kathitaṁ ? tatrāha—ātmā kasyacid ātma-niṣṭhasya mano yat pṛṣṭavān parīkṣito' syātma-jñānaṁ jātaṁ na veti sandihya svagatam evam api yaj jñātum iṣṭavān ity arthaḥ | aham tatrānuvarṇyate ity-ādinopakrāntaṁ bhagavan-mahimānam eva punar api varṇayiṣyāmīty āha—harer iti | 

**viśvātmana** iti—kiṁ vyaṣṭyātmanaḥ svarūpa-varṇaneneti bhāvaḥ | nanv asmin prakaraṇe śrī-śukadevasyopadeśe bhaktāv eva tātparyaṁ jñāne veti sandihānaṁ prati punar vicāryate | tatra atrānuvarṇyate'bhīkṣṇam ity-ādy-upakrame etat te kathitaṁ tāta ity-ādy-upasaṁhāre'pi tādṛśa-mahimatvena punar līlā-kathā-śravaṇasyaiva prādhānyāt, tata upakramopasaṁhāra-nirdiṣṭatvāc chravaṇopalakṣita-bhakter evātrāpi prādhānyam | yas tu tan-madhye tvaṁ tu rājan mariṣyeti ity-ādinā jñānopadeśaḥ, sa ca tasya prāg eva gatā yā bhakti-niṣṭhā tasyāḥ sampraty api sthairya-prakaṭanārtha eva, ekānta-bhakteṣu bhagavatā mokṣa-vara-cchandanavat pūrvam api bhakti-niṣṭhā maraṇa-bhaya-tyāgāt | anantaraṁ ca śrutvāpi taj-jñānopadeśaṁ svasya bhakti-niṣṭhāyā eva darśayiṣyamāṇatvāt | tatra prācīnā tan-niṣṭhā yathā prathame—kṛṣṇāṅghri-sevām adhimanyamānaḥ iti, dadhyau mukundāṅghrimananyabhāva iti ca | tanniṣṭhayaiva tadbhayaparityāgo yathā tad-vākye—dvijopasṛṣṭaḥ kuhakara-takṣako vā daśatvalaṁ, gāyata viṣṇu-gāthāḥ iti tajjñāna-śravaṇānantaram api tādṛśa-niṣṭhāyāḥ sthairya-darśanaṁ yathā tatra tāvat padya-trayeṇa taj-jñānopadeśaṁ bahu matvā śravaṇa-lakṣaṇayā bhaktyaiva sva-kṛtārthatvam uktaṁ ṣaṣṭādhyāyārambhe—siddho'smy anugṛhīto'smi ity-ādinā | atyadbhutam idaṁ ity-ādi, purāṇa-saṁhitām ity-ādinā ca | punaś caikena padyena tad-vākya-gaurava-mātreṇāṅgīkṛtasya brahma-jñānasya takṣakādi-bhaya-nivṛtta-hetutva muktvāpy anyena tad-ūrdhva-vāk-cetasos tan-nāma-kīrtana-dhyānāveśānujñā prārthitā bhagavaṁs takṣakādibhyaḥ ity-ādinā, anujānīhi māṁ brahman ity-ādinā ca | atha punar anyena padyenājñāna-nirāso jñāna-vṛddhiś ca bhagavat-padāravinda-darśana-sukhāntarbhūtaiva mama sphuratīti jñāpitam | 


    ajñānaṁ ca nirastaṁ me jñāna-vijñāna-niṣṭhayā | 


    bhavatā darśitaṁ kṣemaṁ paraṁ bhagavataḥ padam || iti | 

atra pada-śabdasya caraṇāravindābhidhāyakatve jñānena vaiyāsaki-śabditena bheje khagendra-dhvaja-pāda-mūlam ity evāsti prathame sādhakam | etat-prakaraṇārthas tu śrīsūtenaiva spaṣṭīkṛtaḥ—


    brahmakopotthitādyas tu takṣakātprāṇaviplavāt | 


    na saṁmumohorubhayādbhagavatyarpitāśayaḥ || 


    nottamaślokavārtānāṁ juṣatāṁ tatkathāmṛtam | 


    syātsaṁbhramo'ntakāle'pi smaratāṁ tatpadāmbujam || iti | 

tathā pūrvaṁ dvādaśasya tṛtīye prathamaskandhāṁ tasthasya—


    ataḥ pṛcchāmi saṁsiddhiṁ yogināṁ paramaṁ gurum | 


    puruṣasyeha yatkāryaṁ mriyamāṇasya sarvathā || 

ityasya rājapraśnasyottaratvena bhagavad-dhyānakīrtane eva svayaṁ śrīśukadevenāpyupadiṣṭe—


    tasmātsarvātmanā rājan hṛdisthaṁ kuru keśavam | 


    mriyamāṇo hyavahitatas to yāsi parāṁ gatim | 


    mriyamāṇairabhidhyeyo bhagavānparameśvaraḥ | 


    ātmabhāvaṁ nayatyāṅga  sarvathā sarvasambhavaḥ | 


    kalerdoṣanidhe rājan | ity-ādinā | 

tatas tatra keśave hyavahitaḥ kṛtāvadhānaḥ | ātmabhāvamātmano bhaktim | astu tāvadāyāsasādhyaṁ dhyānaṁ hi yasmādanāyāsasādhyātkīrtanādevetyarthaḥ | dvitīyaskandhepi—na hyato'nyaḥ śivaḥ panthāḥ ity-ādinā evametannigaditam ityantena granthena nānāṅgavāñchuddhabhaktiyoga evātrottaratvena paryavasitaḥ | tatra pibanti ye bhagavataḥ ity-ādinā līlākathāśravaṇa eva paryavasānaṁ dṛśyate tasmātsādhūktam—tvantu rājanmarivyeti ity-ādikaṁ bhagavad-bhaktiniṣṭāprakaṭanārthameveti | ato bhaktāveva tadupadeśasya tātparyamata eva dvitīyāṣṭame rājaprārthanānvarthā syāt—kṛṣṇe niveśya nissaṅgaṁ manastyakṣye kalevaram iti ||13||

iti śrīmad-bhāgavata-bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśe dvādaśa-skandhe pañcamo'dhyāyaḥ ||5||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **līlā-kathaika-rasikasya tasya pūrvokte tu nātirucim ālakṣya tathopasaṁharati—etat ta iti | te tubhyam etat, tvaṁ tu rājan mariṣyeti [bhā.pu. 12.5.2] ity-ādinā kathitam | 

nanu, mamānabhīṣṭam anupakrāntaṁ ca tat kathaṁ kathitam ? tatrāha—ātmā kasyacid ātma-niṣṭhasya mano yat pṛṣṭavān | parīkṣito’syātma-jñānaṁ jātam asti na veti sandihya, svagatam evam api yaj jñātum iṣṭavān ity arthaḥ | ahaṁ tv atrānuvarṇyate [bhā.pu. 12.5.1] ity-ādinopakrāntaṁ śrī-bhagavan-mahimānam eva punar api varṇayiṣyāmīty āha—harer iti | viśvātmana iti kiṁ vyaṣṭy-ātmanaḥ svarūpādi-varṇaneneti bhāvaḥ | 

nanv asmin prakaraṇe śrī-śukadevasyopadeśe bhaktāv eva tātparyaṁ jñāne veti sandihānaṁ prati punar vicāryate atrānuvarṇyate’bhīkṣṇaṁ [bhā.pu. 12.5.1] ity-ādy-upakrame, “etat te kathitaṁ tāta” ity-ādy-upasaṁhāre’pi tādṛśa-mahimatvena pūrvokta-līlā-kathā-śravaṇasyaiva prādhānyāt | ata upakramopasaṁhāra-nirdiṣṭatvāt śravaṇopalakṣita-bhakter evātrāpi prādhānyam | yas tu tan-madhye tvaṁ tu rājan mariṣyati [bhā.pu. 12.5.2] ity-ādinā jñānopadeśaḥ sa ca tasya yā prāg avagatā bhakti-niṣṭhāyā eva svayaṁ darśayiṣyamāṇatvāt | tatra prācīnā tan-niṣṭhā yathā prathame kṛṣṇāṅghri-sevām adhimanyamānaḥ [bhā.pu. 1.19.5] iti | dadhyau mukundāṅghrim ananya-bhāvaḥ [bhā.pu. 1.19.7] ity-ādi tan-niṣṭhataiva | tad-bhaya-parityāgo yathā tad-vākye—


    dvijopasṛṣṭaḥ kuhakas takṣako vā


    daśatv alaṁ gāyata viṣṇu-gāthāḥ || [bhā.pu. 1.19.15] iti |

tad etat prakaraṇārthas tatra śrī-sūtenaiva spaṣṭīkṛtaḥ—


    brahma-kopotthitād yas tu takṣakāt prāṇa-viplavāt |


    na sammumohoru-bhayād bhagavaty arpitāśayaḥ || [bhā.pu. 1.18.2] 


    nottamaśloka-vārtānāṁ juṣatāṁ tat-kathāmṛtam |


    syāt sambhramo’nta-kāle’pi smaratāṁ tat-padāmbujam || [bhā.pu. 1.18.4] iti |

dvitīya-skandhe’pi na hy ato’nyaḥ śivaḥ panthā [bhā.pu. 2.2.33] ity ādinā evam etan nigaditaṁ [bhā.pu. 2.3.1] ity antena granthena nānāṅgavān śuddha-bhakti-yoga eva tatrottaratvena paryavasitaḥ | tatrāpi pibanti ye bhagavataḥ [bhā.pu. 2.2.37] ity ādinā līlā-kathā-śravaṇa eva parama-paryavasānaṁ dṛśyate | tasmāt sādhūktaṁ tvaṁ tu rājan mariṣyetīty ādikaṁ tad-bhakti-niṣṭhā-prakaṭanārtham eveti | yato bhaktāv eva tad-upadeśasya tātparyam | 

ata eva dvitīyasyāṣṭame rāja-prārthanā ca nānyathā syāt | kṛṣṇe niveśya niḥsaṅgaṁ manas tyakṣye kalevaraṁ [bhā.pu. 2.8.2] ity ādi ||13|| [bhakti-sandarbha 86][^46]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** etad brahma-jñānaṁ tvayā sampraty apṛṣṭam api te kathitaṁ yad dhareś ceṣṭāṁ līlām ātmā tvaṁ pṛṣṭavān māṁ pūrvam apṛcchaḥ, tāṁ tu pūrvam evāvocam iti śeṣaḥ | śiṣyasya tasya pūrṇatva-jñāpanāya pṛcchati—kim iti ||13||

 **...**

iti sārārtha-darśinyāṁ harṣiṇyāṁ bhakta-cetasām |

dvādaśasya pañcamo’pi saṅgataḥ saṅgataḥ satām ||*||

 **...**


    iti śrīmad-bhāgavate mahā-purāṇe brahma-sūtra-bhāṣye pāramahaṁsyaṁ saṁhitāyāṁ vaiyāsikyāṁ dvādaśa-skandhe 


    brahmopadeśo nāma 


    pañcamo’dhyāyaḥ |

|| 12.5 ||

**…**

**(12.6)**


### ṣaṣṭho’dhyāyaḥ


## veda-śākhā-praṇayanam

**|| 12.6.1 ||**

**sūta uvāca—**

**etan niśamya muninābhihitaṁ parīkṣid**

**vyāsātmajena nikhilātma-dṛśā samena |**

**tat-pāda-mūlam upasṛtya natena mūrdhnā**

**baddhāñjalis tam idam āha sa viṣṇurātaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :**

ṣaṣṭhe parīkṣito mokṣaḥ sarpa-homādi tat-sutāt |

veda-śāstra-vibhāgoktau tri-vedi-vyāsa-varṇanam ||

etat purāṇaṁ niśamya nikhilātmā haris taṁ paśyati nikhilaṁ vātmani paśyatīti tathā tena | ataḥ samena | na tenāvanatena mūrdhnā tat-pāda-talam upasṛtya | tat-pādau śirasi nidhāyety arthaḥ ||1||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tatsutātparīkṣitputrājjanamejayātaf | ādinā takṣakarakṣaṇādigrahaḥ | trayāṇāṁ vedānāṁ samāhārastrivedī tasya vyāso vistarastasya varṇanam atoḥ nikhilātmadarśitvāt | ity artha iti—śirasi pādasthāpanaṁ vinā pādatalasparśo na bhavatīti bhāvaḥ | yad vā, nikhilānāmātmānaṁ manaḥ paśyatīti tena tātkālikajñānopadeśe tatratyānāṁ keṣāñcijjñāninām api mana ānanditam iti bhāvaḥ ||1||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :**

ṣaṣṭhe kṛṣṇa-pada-prāptī rājño’tha janam ejayāt |

sarpa-homas tato veda-traya-śākhopavarṇanam ||

nikhilātmā śrī-kṛṣṇas taṁ paśyatīti tena | yad vā, nikhilānām apy ātmānaṁ manaḥ paśyatīti tena tātkālikena brahma-jñānopadeśena tatratyānāṁ keṣāṁcit jñāninām api mana ānanditam iti bhāvaḥ, yataḥ samena ||1||

**...**

** || 12.6.2 ||**

**rājovāca—**

**siddho’smy anugṛhīto’smi bhavatā karuṇātmanā |**

**śrāvito yac ca me sākṣād anādi-nidhano hariḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : siddhaḥ** kṛtārtho’**smi** | yato’**nugṛhīto’smi** | anugraham evāha—**yad** yasmāc **chrāvitaḥ** | **ca**-śabdāt prāpti-sādhanaṁ ca śrāvitam ||2||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **sākṣādgarbhe bālye ca | yaḥ sākṣādṛṣṭaḥ sa eva śrāvita iti sākṣātpadārthaḥ ||2||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** siddho’smīty-ādi | taj-jñānopadeśa-śravaṇānantaram api tādṛśa-sva-niṣṭhāyāḥ sthairya-darśanaṁ yathā tatra tāvat padya-trayeṇa taj-jñānopadeśam abahu matvā śravaṇa-lakṣaṇayā bhaktyaiva sva-kṛtārthatvam uktaṁ ṣaṣṭhādhyāyārambhe—siddho’smy anugṛhīto’smi ity-ādi | nātyadbhutam ahaṁ manye [bhā.pu. 12.6.3] ity-ādi, purāṇa-saṁhitām [bhā.pu. 12.6.4] ity-ādi | punaś caikena padyena tad-vākya-gaurava-mātreṇāṅgīkṛtasya brahma-jñānasya takṣakādi-bhaya-nivṛtti-hetutvam uktvāpy anyena tad-ūrdhvam adhokṣaja eva vāk-cetasos tan-nāma-kīrtana-dhyānāveśānujñā prārthitā—bhagavaṁs takṣakādibhyaḥ [bhā.pu. 12.6.5] ity-ādinā, anujānīhi māṁ brahman [bhā.pu. 12.6.6] ity-ādinā | atha punar anyena padyenājñāna-nirāsaka-jñāna-vijñāna-siddhiś ca bhagavat-padāravinda-darśanānandāntar-bhūtaiva mama sphuratīti vijñāpitam | yathā—


    ajñānaṁ ca nirastaṁ me jñāna-vijñāna-niṣṭhayā |


    bhavatā darśitaṁ kṣemaṁ paraṁ bhagavataḥ padam || [12.6.7] iti ||2|| [bhakti-sandarbha 86] 

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** siddho’smi kṛtārtho’smi | me sākṣād iti garbhe bālye ca sākṣāt-kṛto yo hariḥ śrī-kṛṣṇaḥ, sa eva śrāvitas tvayā sa eva mayā śrutaḥ ||2||

**...**

** || 12.6.3 ||**

**nātyadbhutam ahaṁ manye mahatām acyutātmanām |**

**ajñeṣu tāpa-tapteṣu bhūteṣu yad anugrahaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **karuṇātmatām abhinandati dvābhyam—nātyadbhutam iti ||3||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **mahatāṁ bhavādṛśānām | ajñeṣu mādṛśeṣu ||3||

———————————————————————————————————————

**sanātana-gosvāmī : **[ha.bha.vi. 10.216] ajñeṣu bhagavad-bhajanādi-mahimānabhijñeṣu, ata eva tāpais tapteṣu bhūteṣu prāṇi-mātreṣu anugraha iti yat, idam adbhuta-ghaṭamānaṁ na manye, yataḥ acyutasyaiva ātmā svabhāvaḥ dīnānām eva śaraṇatvādi-rūpo yeṣām iti ||3||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** kiṁ ca, acyutātmanām acyutasyevātmā svabhāvo yeṣāṁ, teṣāṁ mahatām ātmārāmāṇām apīti | tad-bhāva-bhāvitatvād anugrahādayo guṇā yuktā eva | tasmān nātyadbhutam ity arthaḥ ||3||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **acyuta eva ātmā mano yeṣāṁ teṣām ||3||

**...**

**|| 12.6.4 ||**

**purāṇa-saṁhitām etām aśrauṣma bhavato vayam |**

**yasyāṁ khalūttama-śloko bhagavān anuvarṇyate ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **aśrauṣma śrutavantaḥ | bhavataḥ sakāśāt ||4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **saṁhitāmity uktyā vedatulyatvamasya purāṇasya sūcayati | anuvarṇyate abhīkṣṇaśastattatkathāprasaṅgena pratipādyate ||4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **yasmād aśrauṣma tasmādeva bhagavann iti ||4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** nanu mattaḥ śrutasya asya śāstrasya kaḥ khalv arthas tvayāvadhārita ity apekṣāyām āha—purāṇeti | bhagavān anuvarṇyate ity anya-varṇanasyāpi tat-poṣaṇārthatvena tad-aṅgatvāt bhagavad-anuvarṇanatvam eveti bhāvaḥ ||4||

**...**

**|| 12.6.5 ||**

**bhagavaṁs takṣakādibhyo mṛtyubhyo na bibhemy aham |**

**praviṣṭo brahma nirvāṇam abhayaṁ darśitaṁ tvayā ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **“siddho’smi” ity uktaṁ tad evāviṣkaroti—bhagavann iti | yatas **tvayā darśitaṁ brahma praviṣṭaḥ** | kathaṁ bhūtam ? **abhayam**, yato **nirvaṇaṁ** kaivalya-rūpam ||5||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **he bhagavann iti śrīśukaṁ sākṣādbhagavāñśrī-kṛṣṇastadrūpeṇāmantrayatīti bhāvaḥ | yathā śrī-kṛṣṇena jagato'bhayaṁ duṣṭadaityahananādi darśitaṁ tathā mama tvayāpi taddarśitam iti tatsābhyamuktam | yad vā, nānyattvadabhayaṁ paśye iti śrīkuntyukteḥ abhayaḥ śrī-kṛṣṇa eva | klībattvamārṣam | śrī-bhāgavataśrāvaṇenāpi sākṣācchrīkṛṣṇa eva darśito bhavatīti bhāvaḥ | yad vā, brahmanirvāṇarūpamabhayaṁ darśitam | 


    adhokṣajālambamihāśubhātmanaḥ śarīriṇaḥ saṁsṛticakraśātanam | tadbrahmanirvāṇasukhaṁ vidurbudhāstato majadhvaṁ hṛdaye hṛdīśvaram || 

iti sarvabhaktaśiromaṇinā śrīkāyādhavena manasā śrī-kṛṣṇacintanasyaiva saṁsānirāsakatvamuktam iti ||5||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **adhunā tu yad upadiṣṭaṁ, tac ca mama jātam evety āha—praviṣṭa iti | **nirvāṇaṁ** paramānanda-svarūpaṁ **brahma** sarvato`pi bṛhad-bhagavat-tattvaṁ **praviṣṭas** tasminn āviṣṭa ity arthaḥ ||5||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** kiṁ tv ekam eva vākyaṁ man-mano’bhijñena tvayā māṁ prati noktam | yadyapi tad apy āśaṅkāvato mamaiva tāvad evāsahyam abhūd ity āha—he **bhagavan** ! sarvajña ! mac-cit tasya bhaktyaika-niṣṭhatvaṁ jānann api kim evam upadiśasīti bhāvaḥ | **takṣakādibhyas** tathā vividha-janmāntara-prāptebhyo **mṛtyubhyaḥ** sakāśād **ahaṁ na bibhemi** | kiṁ tu **tvayā darśitam abhayaṁ brahma nirvāṇaṁ praviṣṭaḥ** sann eva bibhemīty arthaḥ | atra gṛha-sthito nānupadravebhyo na bibhemi, kiṁ tu vanaṁ praviṣṭaḥ sann eveti | tasmāt vanaṁ na praviśāmīti tatrābhiprāyaḥ | tathaivātrāpi takṣakādibhyaḥ punaḥ punar mṛtyubhyaś ca sakāśād api, tvayā darśitād brahma-nirvānān mama mahā-bhayam iti vākyārthaḥ |
