tena pañcama-skandha-vākyād bhagavadīyatvenaiva samāpta-sarvārthānāṁ—


    nārāyaṇa-parāḥ sarve na kutaścana bibhyati |


    svargāpavarga-narakeṣv api tulyārtha-darśinaḥ || [bhā.pu. 6.17.28]

ity uktavatā bhagavatā śrīman-mahā-rudreṇaiva prakaṭitābhiprāyāṇām asmākaṁ bhaktānāṁ nirvāṇa-mokṣaḥ khalv asahya eva | atrāpi—


    punaś ca bhūyād bhagavaty anante


    ratiḥ prasaṅgaś ca tad-āśrayeṣu |


    mahatsu yāṁ yām upayāmi sṛṣṭiṁ


    maitry astu sarvatra namo dvijebhyaḥ || [bhā.pu. 1.19.16]

iti prāyopaveśārambhata eva pratijñātavantaṁ mām api brahma-nirvāṇam upadiśāmīti śrī-munīndre īrṣaiva dhvanitā | tayāpi śrī-śukasya tasya tad-bhakti-niṣṭhāṁ parīkṣamāṇasya sukham evābhūt | yathā rāsārambhe ājñā-laṅghayantīnāṁ vraja-sundarīṇām īrṣyayā kṛṣṇasya atra kintv ity ākṣepa-labdham eva—


    tvām asmi vacmi viduṣāṁ samavāyo’tra tiṣṭhati |


    ātmīyāṁ matim ādāya sthitim atra vidhehi tat || [kā.pra. 23]

ity asya pūrvārdhānte yathā kintv ity ākṣepa-labdhaṁ kāvya-prakāśa-ṭīkā-kṛdbhis tathā vyākhyānāt | vyākhyāntaraṁ tu śāstrasya mohinītva-pratipādakaṁ bhaktair agrāhyam ||5||

**...**

**|| 12.6.6 ||**

**anujānīhi māṁ brahman vācaṁ yacchāmy adhokṣaje |**

**mukta-kāmāśayaṁ cetaḥ praveśya visṛjāmy asūn ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **“kiṁ bhūyaḥ śrotum icchasi” iti yad uktam, tatra siddho’haṁ na kiñcic chrotum icchāmi | kevalam anujñāṁ dehīty āha—anujānīhīti | vācam ity upalakṣaṇaṁ sarvendriyāṇām | vācaṁ niyamya kiṁ kariṣyasi ?tad āha—muktāḥ kāmāśayās tad vāsanā yena tac ceto’dhokṣaje praveśyāsūn visṛjāmi ||6||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **he brahmann iti—sākṣātparabrahmamūrtistvamato māmājñāpayeti bhāvaḥ | adhokṣaje parabrahmaṇi śrī-kṛṣṇa eva kṛṣṇe manaḥ saṁmāveśya santyakṣye'haṁ kalevaram iti dvitīyokteḥ | asūnprāṇān ||6||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **adhokṣaje śrī-kṛṣṇe, adho’nena śayānena [ha.vaṁ. 2.100.30] ity-ādi śrī-hari-vaṁśokteḥ ||6_|_|

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **tasmāt kṛpayā ma etad evājñāpaya, na tv etat pratikūlam ity āha—anujānīhi anujñāṁ dehīty arthaḥ | adhokṣaje śrī-kṛṣṇe muktam āśayaṁ tyakta-kāma-vāsanām ||6||

**...**

**|| 12.6.7 ||**

**ajñānaṁ na nirastaṁ me jñāna-vijñāna-niṣṭhayā |**

**bhavatā darśitaṁ kṣemaṁ paraṁ bhagavato padam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **nanu kiṁ prāṇa-tyāgena ? kiñcit kālaṁ jñāna-niṣṭho bhava, iti cet tatrāha—ajñānaṁ ceti | ca-kārāt tat-saṁskāraś ca tac ca tvat-kṛpayaivety āha—bhavateti ||7||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **atrākṣipati—nanv iti | jñānaṁ śrī-kṛṣṇānubhavo vijñānaṁ tadaiśvaryānubhavaratatra niṣṭhā sthitistayā ||7||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **bhagavataḥ padam iti | atra pada-śabdasya caraṇāravinda-vācakatvam[^47], jñānena vaiyāsaki-śabditena bheje khagendra-dhvaja-pāda-mūlaṁ [bhā.pu. 1.18.16] ity evāsti prathamaṁ sādhakam ||7||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **jñānaṁ bhagavad-viṣayakaṁ vijñānaṁ tad-aiśvarya-mādhuryānubhavaḥ, jñāna-vijñāna-niṣṭhā tava kuto jātety ata āha—bhavateti | padaṁ svarūpaṁ caraṇa-kamalaṁ dhāma vā ||7||

**...**

**|| 12.6.8 ||**

**sūta uvāca—**

**ity uktas tam anujñāpya bhagavān bādarāyaṇiḥ |**

**jagāma bhikṣubhiḥ sākaṁ nara-devena pūjitaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā), jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** bhikṣubhih sarva-munīndraiḥ ||8||

**...**

** || 12.6.9 ||**

**parīkṣid api rājarṣir ātmany ātmānam ātmanā |**

**samādhāya paraṁ dadhyāv aspandāsur yathā taruḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ātmanā buddhyā | ātmānaṁ mana ātmani pratyak prakāśe samādhāya paramātmānaṁ dadhyau | aspandāsuḥ līna-prāṇaḥ | yathā taruḥ sthāṇuḥ ||9|| 

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **param adhokṣajaṁ tad-ākhyaṁ śrī-kṛṣṇam eva dadhyau ||9||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** ātmanā buddhyā | ātmānaṁ śrī-kṛṣṇam ātmani manasi param atiśayena aspandāsuḥ antar eva līna-prāṇaḥ ||9||

**...**

**|| 12.6.10 ||**

**prāk-kūle barhiṣy āsīno gaṅgā-kūla udaṅ-mukhaḥ |**

**brahma-bhūto mahā-yogī niḥsaṅgaś chinna-saṁśayaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tam eva viśinaṣṭi—prāk-kūle prāg agre | barhiṣi darbhe ||10||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **bhikṣubhistatratyaiḥ kathāśravaṇārthamāgatairdurvāsaḥ—prabhṛtibhiḥ sannyāsibhiḥ | naradevena parīkṣitā | pūjito'bhyutthānapuṣpādyairarcitaḥ ||8-10||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **gūḍhaṁ paraṁ brahma manuṣya-liṅgam [bhā.pu. 7.10.48, 7.15.75] ity-ādi-rītyā para-brahma-śrī-kṛṣṇe premāveśāt tan-mayaḥ[^48] ||10||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **prāk-kule barhiṣi prāg agre | darbhe triguṇātītatvād brahma-bhūtaḥ | hi tāsāṁ madhye sākṣād brahma gopāla-purī itivat ||10||

**...**

** || 12.6.11 ||**

**takṣakaḥ prahito viprāḥ kruddhena dvija-sūnunā |**

**hantu-kāmo nṛpaṁ gacchan dadarśa pathi kaśyapam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tad evaṁ brahma-bhūte tasmiṁs takṣakāgamanādikaṁ piṣṭa-peṣaṇam ivābhavad iti darśayati—takṣaka iti tribhiḥ | he viprāḥ ||11||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **aho brāhmaṇānāṁ tapobalaṁ mahadityabhipretyāha—he viprā iti ||11||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** tad evaṁ brahma-bhūte tasmin takṣakāgamanādikaṁ piṣṭa-peṣaṇam ivābhavad iti darśayati—takṣaka iti tribhiḥ ||11||

**...**

**|| 12.6.12 ||**

**taṁ tarpayitvā draviṇair nivartya viṣa-hāriṇam |**

**dvija-rūpa-praticchannaḥ kāma-rūpo’daśan nṛpam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **taṁ viṣa-cikitsayā parīkṣid-rakṣaṇena dravyārjanāyāgacchantam | tatra svālīḍha-vaṭa-vṛkṣasya bhasmī-bhūtasya punar aṅkurādi-krameṇotthāpanād viṣa-hāriṇaṁ tad-apekṣita-draviṇaiḥ santarpya tato nivartya dvija-rūpeṇa tirohitaḥ sann adaśat |

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tatra mārge | svālīḍhaḥ svadaṣṭo yo vaṭavṛkṣastasya | kāmarūpo devatvāt ||12||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **taṁ viṣa-cikitsayā parīkṣid-rakṣaṇena dravyārjanāyāgacchantam, tatra svālīḍha-vaṭa-vṛkṣasya bhasmī-bhūtasya punar aṅkurādi-krameṇotthāpanād viṣa-hāriṇaṁ tad-apekṣita-draviṇaiḥ santarpya tato nivartya dvija-rūpeṇa tirohitaḥ sann adaśat ||12||

**...**

** || 12.6.13 ||**

**brahma-bhūtasya rājarṣer deho’hi-garalāgninā |**

**babhūva bhasma-sāt sadyaḥ paśyatāṁ sarva-dehinām ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tac ca putra-kṛtyam iva jātam ity āha—brahma-bhūtasyeti ||13||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tac ca daṁśanam | putreṇa yathā piturdeho dahyate tadvajjātam | ahigaralamevāgnistena | brahmabhūtasya vicāreṇa tādrūpyaṁ prāptasya ||13||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** tac ca putra-kṛtyam iva jātam ity āha—brahma-bhūtasyeti ||15||

**...**

** || 12.6.14-15 ||**

**hāhā-kāro mahān āsīd bhuvi khe dikṣu sarvataḥ |**

**vismitā hy abhavan sarve devāsura-narādayaḥ ||**

**deva-dundubhayo nedur gandharvāpsaraso jaguḥ |**

**vavṛṣuḥ puṣpa-varṣāṇi vibudhāḥ sādhu-vādinaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tatra kṣaṇaṁ sarveṣāṁ duḥkhaṁ ca tataḥ param utsavaṁ cāha dvābhyām, hāhākāra iti ||14-15||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tatra tadā | kṣaṇa kṣaṇamātram | tataḥ kṣaṇottaram | aho brāhmaṇarūpeṇa phalāni dātumāgatena kiṁ kṛtamityevaṁ vismitā abhavan || devaloke'pi tadgamana utsavo'bhūdityāha—devadundubhaya iti ||14-15||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

**...**

** || 12.6.16 ||**

**janmejayaḥ sva-pitaraṁ śrutvā takṣaka-bhakṣitam |**

**yathājuhāva saṅkruddho nāgān satre saha dvijaiḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **prāsaṅgikam āha—janmejaya ity-ādi | sarpābhicāra-satre dvijaiḥ saha vartamāno yathāvad ājuhāva juhāveti vā | sarva-sarpāvāhane kāraṇam āha—saṅkruddha iti ||16||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **prāsaṅgikaṁ prakṛtam | takṣakeṇa bhakṣitaṁ daṣṭam, bhakṣaṇavaddaṁṣṭrāvyāpārasāmyāddaśo'pi bhakṣaṇaśabdenocyate | āhvāne prayojanābhāvādākārapraśleṣaṁ tyaktvāha—juhāveti veti ||16||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** yathā yathāvat niḥsarpam idaṁ jagat kariṣya iti vadan kruddho dvijaiḥ saha sthitaḥ san ||16||

**...**

** || 12.6.17-18 ||**

**sarpa-satre samiddhāgnau dahyamānān mahoragān |**

**dṛṣṭvendraṁ bhaya-saṁvignas takṣakaḥ śaraṇaṁ yayau ||**

**apaśyaṁs takṣakaṁ tatra rājā pārīkṣito dvijān |**

**uvāca takṣakaḥ kasmān na dahyetoragādhamaḥ ||**

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **bhayena saṁvignastrastaḥ ||17||

**...**

** || 12.6.19 ||**

**taṁ gopāyati rājendra śakraḥ śaraṇam āgatam |**

**tena saṁstambhitaḥ sarpas tasmān nāgnau pataty asau ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** kasmāt takṣako na dahyetety uktāḥ santo dvijā ūcuḥ, tam iti | tenendreṇa | asau sarpaḥ ||19||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tatra yajñakuṇḍāgnau ||18-19||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

**...**

** || 12.6.20 ||**

**pārīkṣita iti śrutvā prāha rtvija udāra-dhīḥ |**

**sahendras takṣako viprā nāgnau kim iti pātyate**[^49]** ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ṛtvijaḥ pratyāha—sahendraḥ indra-sahitaḥ indra-sahitaḥ kim iti na pātyate ||20||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

**...**

**|| 12.6.21 ||**

**tac chrutvājuhuvur viprāḥ sahendraṁ takṣakaṁ makhe |**

**takṣakāśu patasveha sahendreṇa marutvatā ||**

**madhvācāryaḥ (bhāgavata-tātparyam) :** 

sva-santānodbhavaṁ kīrtyā yogayan janam ejayan |


    śakto’py aśaktavad viṣṇur indra āsīd upekṣakaḥ ||


    evam eva ṛṣīṇāṁ ca kīrtiṁ yojayatāmunā |


    kṛto’pekṣā mahendreṇa kim u viṣṇuḥ parātparaḥ ||


    tasmād viṣṇor aśakyaṁ na bhūta-bhavya-bhavatsv api |


    na cāniṣṭaṁ guṇair eṣa pūrṇo nārāyaṇaḥ sadā ||[^50] iti vāmane ||20-22||

nityādoṣa-svarūpāya guṇa-pūrṇāya sarvadā |

nārāyaṇāya haraye namaḥ preṣṭhatamāya me ||

iti śrmad-ānanda-tīrtha-bhagavat-pāda-viracite śrī-bhāgavata-tātparya-nirṇaye dvādaśa sakndhaḥ samāptaḥ | samāpto’yaṁ granthaḥ ||

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** tad-rājño vacaḥ śrutvā ājuhuvuḥ | sākṣepam āhvānaṁ darśayati, takṣaketīhāgnāv āśu patasva maruttvatā marud-gaṇa-vatendreṇa saha ||21||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **he viprā iti—yūyamarthimanorathamavaśyaṁ pūrayanti viśeṣeṇa prānti pūrayantyarthijanābhilaṣitam iti viprā ityanvarthasaṁjñāvannirukter iti bhāvaḥ | kim iti na kuto na ||20-21||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** marutvateti | are indra, tava devendro’ham iti garvo’sti tasmāt tvāṁ devair api samaṁ pātayāma iti bhāvaḥ | marutau pavanā’marau ity arthaḥ ||21||

**...**

** || 12.6.22 ||**

**iti brahmoditākṣepaiḥ sthānād indraḥ pracālitaḥ |**

**babhūva sambhrānta-matiḥ sa-vimānaḥ sa-takṣakaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **brāhmaṇair uktair ākṣepaiḥ paruṣa-vākyaiḥ ||22||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** adya prāṇāḥ khalu gatā eva iti sambhrāntā vyākulā matir yasya saḥ ||21||

**...**

** || 12.6.23-24 ||**

**taṁ patantaṁ vimānena saha-takṣakam ambarāt |**

**vilokyāṅgirasaḥ prāha rājānaṁ taṁ bṛhaspatiḥ ||**

**naiṣa tvayā manuṣyendra vadham arhati sarpa-rāṭ |**

**anena pītam amṛtam atha vā ajarāmaraḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **taṁ takṣakam | aṅgirasaḥ putro bṛhaspatiḥ prāha |

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **itīttham || he manuṣyendreti manuṣyeṣveva tava prabhāvo na tu deveṣvapīti bhāvaḥ | anena takṣakeṇa | athātaḥ | vai niścitam | ajarāmaro jāta ity arthaḥ | yad vā, sarpeṇa takṣakeṇa saha rājata iti sarparāḍidraviśeṣaṇam | athavā—ata eva ajarāmara iti viśvanāthaḥ ||22-24||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** āṅgirasaḥ aṅgirasaḥ putra iti gaurava-vyañjanā eṣa indro manuṣyendreṇa tvayā devendrasya vadhānaucityāt sarpeṇa takṣakeṇa saha rājate iti saḥ | atha ata eva | vai niścitam ajarāmaraḥ ||24||

**...**

** || 12.6.25 ||**

**jīvitaṁ maraṇaṁ jantor gatiḥ svenaiva karmaṇā |**

**rājaṁs tato’nyo nāsty asya pradātā sukha-duḥkhayoḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **bhavatu nāmājarāmaras tathāpi pitṛ-mārakaṁ dhakṣyāmīti cet tatrāha—jīvitam iti | gatiḥ para-lokaḥ | ato durmaraṇa-nimittā pitur durgatir anena kṛtety api na śaṅkanīyam ity arthaḥ ||25||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ity artha iti—nimittamātraṁ sarveṣāṁ kṛtakarmānusārataḥ ity ukter nāsyāparādha iti bhāvaḥ | he rājan pitṛśokādevaṁ yadyavasyasi tatra tattvaṁ śṛṇvityāha—jovitam iti | gatiḥ svargādiḥ | jantoriti—nikṛṣṭajīvasyaveyaṁ vyavasthā tava pitus tu jīvitamaraṇabhagavad-dhāmaprāptayo bhagavatkṛtā eva | tathā hi—svahastenaiva drauṇyastrato rakṣaṇaṁ, muniśāpadvārā nidhanaprāpaṇaṁ, svapraṣṭheśukopadeśadvārā nijapadaprāpaṇam iti tasyaiva karmāṇi takṣakas tu nimittamātram iti viśvanāthaḥ ||25||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** he rājan ! sva-pitṛ-śokād evaṁ yad vyavasyasi, tatra tattvaṁ śṛṇv ity āha—jīvitam iti | gatiḥ svargādi jantor iti nikṛṣṭa-jīvasyaiveyaṁ vyavasthā, tava pitus tu jīvita-maraṇa-bhagavad-dhāma-prāptaye bhagavat-kṛtā eva, tathā hi sva-hastenaiva drauṇy-astrato rakṣaṇaṁ muni-śāpa-dvārā nidhana-prāpaṇaṁ, sva-preṣṭha-śukopadeśa-dvārā sva-pada-prāpaṇam iti tasyaivaitāni karmāṇi | takṣakas tu nāma-mātreṇaiva nimittam iti bhāvaḥ ||25|| 

**...**

** || 12.6.26 ||**

**sarpa-caurāgni-vidyudbhyaḥ kṣut-tṛḍ-vyādhy-ādibhir nṛpa |**

**pañcatvam ṛcchate jantur bhuṅkta ārabdha-karma tat ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **katham anyaḥ sukha-duḥkha-pradātā nāsti sarpādīnām upalabhyamānatvād iti cet tatrāha—**sarpādinā** **jantuḥ pañcatvaṁ** mṛtyum **ṛcchati** prāpnotīti yat, **tad ārabdhaṁ karmaiva bhūṅkte**, sva-karma-prayuktā eva sarpādayo na sva-tantrā iti bhāvaḥ ||26||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **iti bhāva iti—sukhasya duḥkhasya na ko'pi dātā paro dadātīti kubuddhireṣā ity-ādipurāṇāntarāt ātmaiva hyātmano bandhurātmaiva ripurātmanaḥ iti śrīmukhavākyāc ca svakarmānusāreṇa svasyaiva svaduḥkhādihetutvamityāśayaḥ prākṛta eva lokassvakarmavaśātsarpādibhirmṛtiṁ yāti na tu tvatpitāmaho bhaktarāja ityāha—sarpeti | janturantinikṛṣṭajīva iti viśvanāthaḥ ||26||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **prākṛta eva lokaḥ sarpādibhiḥ karma-vaśān maraṇaṁ prāpnoti, na tu tvat-pitā mahā-bhakta-rāja ity āha—sarpeti | **jantur** iti nikṛṣṭa-jīvaḥ ||26||

**...**

** || 12.6.27 ||**

**tasmāt satram idaṁ rājan saṁsthīyetābhicārikam |**

**sarpā anāgaso dagdhā janair diṣṭaṁ hi bhujyate ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : saṁsthīyeta** samāpyatām | **ābhicārikaṁ** hiṁsā-phalam | **diṣṭaṁ** prācīnaṁ karma | ataḥ sarpādṛṣṭa-prayuktasya tavāpy ayaṁ nāparādha iti bhāvaḥ ||27||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **yantaḥ prārabdhakarmata eva sarvaṁ bhavati tasmāddhetoḥ | idaṁ sarpasatram | nanu tajjātitvāttakṣakāparādha evaiṣāmaparādhaḥ ekaḥ pāpāni kurute phalaṁ bhuṅkta mahājanaḥ ity uktes tatrāha—takṣakasyāpyaparādho nāsti daivena taddaṁśanena svakṛtapūrvakarmaṇā parīkṣito maraṇasya klṛptatvādityāśayenāha—janairdiṣṭam iti | yato diṣṭam eva phaladamato hetoḥ | iti bhāva iti—tava cetasyapi mātṛkṛtasarpadāharūpaśāpādṛṣṭavaśenaiva sarpasatrakṛtisphūrtirjāteti tātparyam | atra mahābhāratīyakathānusaṁveyā—kadāciduccaiḥśravaso'śvasya varṇanirṇayārthaṁ kadrūvinatayorvivādaḥ pravṛttaḥ | vinatayoktaṁ śvetavarṇo'yaṁ, kadravā coktaṁ kṛṣṇavarṇa iti | tataḥ śvo nirṇayārthaṁ gamiṣyāvo yaduktirmṛṣā sā dāsī bhavatu, tadā ca nāgamātrā svaputrānpratyuktaṁ yūyaṁ kṛṣṇaromākārā bhūtvāśvapucche lagnā bhavata, ye na kariṣyanti madvākyaṁ te sarve janamejayayajñe dagdhā bhaviṣyantīti | ābhicārika nindyam | abhicārasya śatrumaraṇakāmaḥ śyenenābhicaret iti vihitatve'pi prāyaścittaśravaṇānnindyatvam iti tatrāpi tava nāparādha ityāha—janair iti viśvanāthaḥ ||27||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._ **

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : saṁsthīyate** samāpyatāṁ, yata **ābhicārikaṁ** nindyaṁ, vṛthaiva etāvantaḥ **sarpā dagdhāḥ**, tatrāpi tava nāparādha ity āha—janair iti | **diṣṭaṁ** prācīnaṁ karma, sarper api sva-prārabdha-phalaṁ bhuktam idam iti bhāvaḥ ||27||

**...**

** || 12.6.28 ||**

**ity uktaḥ sa tathety āha maharṣer mānayan vacaḥ |**

**sarpa-satrād uparataḥ pūjayām āsa vāk-patim ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **vāk-patiṁ bṛhaspatim ||28||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **maharṣerbṛhaspateḥ | vāgvai bṛhatī iti śrutim eva bṛhacchabdasya vāgarthe mānaṁ matvāha—bṛhaspatim ||28||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

**...**

** || 12.6.29 ||**

**saiṣā viṣṇor mahā-māyā- bādhyayālakṣaṇā yayā |**

**muhyanty asyaivātma-bhūtā bhūteṣu guṇa-vṛttibhiḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **nanu kathaṁ viduṣām apy evaṁ sammoho yato brahma-kopāt parīkṣito mṛtyur janamejaya-kopāt sarpāṇām ity-ādi ? tatrāha—saiṣeti | tasyā mahattvaṁ darśayati—**alakṣaṇā** na lakṣyata ity alakṣaṇā, apratarkyety arthaḥ | kāsau ? ity ata āha—**yayā asya viṣṇor evātma-bhūtā** ātmāṁśa-bhūtāḥ prāṇino **guṇa-vṛttibhiḥ** krodhādibhiḥ saha **bhūteṣu** deheṣu **muhyanti** | bādhya-bādhakataṁ vrajantīty arthaḥ | nanu śravaṇādinā bādhitayā tayā kuto mohaḥ syāt ? tatrāha—**abādhyayā** bādhitum aśakyayā ||29||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **atrākṣipati—nanv iti | ity artha iti—lakṣita eva vastuni tarko bhavatīti bhāvaḥ | ity artha iti—anyathābhāvasyaiva mohatvād iti bhāvaḥ | punarākṣipati—nanv iti | abādhyayā brahmātmabodhaṁ vinā bādhitumaśakyayā ||29||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **nanu kathaṁ viduṣām apy evaṁ sammohaḥ ? yato janamejayasya kopāt sarpāṇāṁ vadhas tat-sabhāsadāṁ viduṣām api viprāṇām ābhicārike satre pravartanam iti | tatrāha—saiṣeti | tasyā mahattvaṁ darśayati—**alakṣaṇā** na lakṣyata ity alakṣaṇā apratarkyety arthaḥ | **yayā abādhyayā** vidvadbhir api bādhitum aśakyayā **muhyanti** | ke te ? ity ata āha—**asyaiva viṣṇor ātma-bhūtā** ātmāṁśa-bhūtāḥ prāṇino **bhūteṣu** prāṇiṣu viṣayeṣu yā **guṇa-vṛttayaḥ** krodha-dveṣādyās tābhir muhyanti ||29||

**...**

** || 12.6.30 ||**

**na yatra dambhīty abhayā virājitā**

**māyātma-vāde’sakṛd ātma-vādibhiḥ |**

**na yad vivādo vividhas tad-āśrayo**

**manaś ca saṅkalpa-vikalpa-vṛtti yat ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kathaṁ tarhi māyā-tat-kārya-nivṛttiḥ ? ity āśaṅkya śrī-viṣṇu-svarūpa-nirūpaṇa-pūrvakaṁ tad-bhajanāt sarvānartha-nivṛttir iti śāstrārtham upasaṁharati—na yatreti pañcabhiḥ | dambhīti | māyā, kapaṭavān ayaṁ pumān ity evaṁ-bhūtāyāṁ buddhāvasa-kṛd ullikhyamānā yā māyety arthāh | sātma-vāde kriyamāṇe ātma-vādibhir yatrābhayā na virājitā na prakāśitā, kintu bhīteva sva-karyaṁ mohādikam akurvatī kathañcid vartata iti pratipāditety arthaḥ | tad uktam—


    tasmai namo bhagavate vāsudevāya dhīmahi | 


    yan māyayā durjayayā māṁ bruvanti jagad-gurum ||


    vilajjamānaya yasya sthātum īkṣā-pathe’muyā | 


    vimohitā vikatthante mamāham iti durdhiyaḥ || [bhā.pu. 2.5.12-13] iti | 

kiṁ ca, yad yasmiṁs tad-āśrayo māyāśrayo vividho vivādo’pi nāsti | viśeṣa-viṣayatvād vivādānāṁ tasya viśeṣātītatvād iti bhāvaḥ | saṅkalpa-vikalpā vṛttayo yasya tan mano’pi yatra nāsti | saṅkalpa-vikalpānām api viśeṣa-viṣayatvāt ||30||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **viṣṇustarhi dambhī yena tasya māyetyucyate tatrāha—na yatreti | yatra viṣṇau yasya viṣṇossannidhāne nimitte ā īṣat virājitā yatkicillabdhasāmarthyāpi dambhī dambhavānayamityabhayā na bhavati kintu tasmindambhādarśanātsabhayaiva bhavatīty arthaḥ | māyā hi sadambha eva nirbhayā bhavatīti | tad uktam—


    vilajjamānayā yasya sthātumīkṣāpathe'muyā | 


    vimohitā vikatthante mamāham iti durdhiyaḥ || 

iti viṣṇo mahābhāgavate ca māyādhikāro nāstīty arthaḥ | kīdṛśī—dambhini dambhavati puruṣe itau gamane ākrame ity arthaḥ | abhayā nirbhayaiva virājitā | iṇ—gatau ktyantaḥ | viṣṇutadbhaktayos tu śūnyeva bhavatīti bhāvaḥ | tathātmavādibhirati bahudhātmavāde pravartite viṣṇusvarūpe sphurite sati vividho vādo nāsti yatas tadāśrayo māyāśraya eva saḥ yacchaktayo vadatāṁ vādināṁ vai vivādasaṁvādabhuvo bhavanti ity-ukteḥ | tathā saṅkalpādirūpā māyāvṛttayo yatra tanmanopi nāstītyartha iti viśvanāthaḥ | ity artha iti—atra māyāśabdaḥ kapaṭapara eva na tu bhāgavacchaktirūpayogamāyāpara iti bhāvaḥ | ity artha iti—itthaṁ pratipāditā yā māyā sā yatrātmasvarūpe nāstīti bhāvaḥ | atra pramāṇam āha—tad uktam iti | ślokau tu vyākhyātacarāveva | anyadā—kiñceti | yadyasminnātmasvarūpe | iti bhāva iti—neha nānāsti kiñcana ity-ādiśrutes tasyātmasvarūpasya sarvaviśeṣarahitatvasya niścayād iti tātparyam | viśeṣaviṣayatvādbhedaviṣayatvāt ||30||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **kathaṁ tarhi viṣṇur dambhī, yena tasya mahāmāyety ucyate ? tatrāha—na yatreti | **yatra **viṣṇau yasya viṣṇoḥ sannidhāne nimitte **ā** iṣat **virājitā** yat kiñcit labdha-sāmarthyāpi **dambhī** dambhavān ayam ity **abhayā** na bhavati, kintu tasmin dambhā-darśanāt sa-bhayaiva[^51] bhavatīty arthaḥ | māyā hi sa-dambha eva nirargalā bhavatīti | tad uktaṁ vilajjamānayā yasya sthātum īkṣā-pathe’muyā [bhā.pu. 2.5.13] iti | 

kiṁ ca, ātma-vādibhir ātma-vāde kartavye yat yatra tad-āśrayo vividho vivādo na vidyate, ātmanaḥ paratvād iti bhāvaḥ | ato manaś ceti | tatas tu sutarāṁ vivādābhāva iti bhāvaḥ | tad evaṁ tat-sānnidhya-mātreṇa sthitā, na tu tat sammatā, tasyām anāsaktatvāt tasyeti sthitam ||30||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **nanu yadi krodha-dveṣādimatsu sarva-jīveṣv evāsyā māyāyā mohanād dhetor adhikāraḥ, tarhi kutra nādhikāraḥ ? iti cet—


    vilajjamānaya yasya sthātum īkṣā-pathe’muyā | 


    vimohitā vikatthante mamāham iti durdhiyaḥ || [bhā.pu. 2.5.13] 

iti brahmokter bhagavati, viṣṇau mahā-bhāgavate ca loke’syā naivādhikāraḥ, satyam | kīdṛśaṁ tarhi viṣṇoḥ svarūpam ? ity apekṣāyām āha—na yatreti tribhiḥ | **yatra** viṣṇu-svarūpe **māyā** na prabhavati | kīdṛśī ? **dambhini** dambhavati puruṣe itau gamane ākrama ity arthaḥ | **abhayā** nirbhayaiva **virājitā**, in gatau kty-antaḥ | viṣṇau tad-bhakte ca dambhābhāvāt tatra sabhayā virājana-śūnyeva bhavatīti bhāvaḥ | tathā **ātma-vādibhir** api **asakṛt** punaḥ punaḥ **ātma-vāde** pravartite sati, yat yatra viṣṇu-svarūpe sphurite sati vividho vivādo nāsti | kīdṛśas tad-āśrayaḥ ? tāṁ māyām evāśrayata iti saḥ | yad uktaṁ—


    yac-chaktayo vadatāṁ vādināṁ vai


    vivāda-saṁvāda-bhuvo bhavanti [bhā.pu. 6.4.31] iti ||30|| 

 **...**

**|| 12.6.31 ||**

**na yatra sṛjyaṁ sṛjatobhayoḥ paraṁ**

**śreyaś ca jīvas tribhir anvitas tv aham |**

**tad etad utsādita-bādhya-bādhakaṁ**

**niṣidhya cormīn virameta tan muniḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kiṁ ca, **sṛjyaṁ** karma **sṛjatā** kāraka-vargeṇa **sahobhayoḥ** sṛjya-sraṣṭroḥ **paraṁ** sādhyaṁ **śreyaḥ** phalam api | atas **tribhiḥ** sṛjya-sraṣṭṛ-phalair **anvito** jīvaś cāhaṅkārātmako **yatra nāsti** | ata eva **utsāditau** nirastau **bādhya-bādhakau** yasmiṁs **tad etat** svayam ātma-svarūpam ity arthaḥ | tat tasminn **ūrmīn** ahaṅkārādīn **niṣidhya** **virameta**, viśeṣeṇa krīḍed ity arthah ||31||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **anyadapyādhikyam āha—kiñceti | kārakavargeṇendriyasamūhena | ataḥ sṛjyāditrayābhāvāt | ata evāhaṅkārābhavādeva | bādhya dvaitaṁ, bādhakaṁ vṛttirūpaṁ jñānaṁ ca | ity artha iti—sarvabādhāvidhitvena jñeyam iti bhāvaḥ| kecittvātmasvarūpamihāvagatyeti śeṣaṁ kṛtvā yojayaṁstadaśobhanamiva bhātīti | ūrmiśabdenātrahaṅkārādayo lakṣyante jale taraṅgavatteṣām api citta utthānadarśanāt | ity artha iti—kaścittamanuvartate iti verupasargasya dhātvarthānugatatvādayaṁ bhāvaḥ | yatra sphurīte sati sṛjyādirna yat ubhayoḥ sraṣṭṭasṛjyayoḥ paraṁ pṛthagbhūtaṁ tatsvayaṁ tathā śreyaḥ svargādiphalam api yatra na sphurati tathā tribhirguṇarjāgarādibhirvā yukto'haṅkārātmako jīvo'pi na sphurati tasmādetadviṣṇusvarūpam | utsāditā nirastā bādhyā jīvā bādhakā guṇāś ca tasmāttathābhūtam | nanu tarhyaitatkaḥ prakāśayettatrāha—niṣidhyeti | svabhaktahṛdgatānamūnkāmakrodhādīnsvayam eva | tatra viśeṣato ramate tatprasiddham iti viśvanāthaḥ ||31||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **māyāśraya-vyavadhānam asattvaṁ vivṛṇoti—na yatra sṛjyam iti | **jīvas** **tv aham** ity anvayaḥ nigamayati | tat-pūrva-nirdiṣṭam etat-prakāram **utsādita-bādhya-bādhakaṁ** viṣṇu-tattvam iti | tad etan-mananena **ūrmīn** māyādīn **niṣidhya munir virameta** | tasmād anyatra svayam eva virato bhavati, na tu yatnāntareṇety arthaḥ ||31||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **tathā saṅkalpa-vikalpa-rūpā māyikyo vṛttayo yasya tathā-bhūtaṁ mano’pi yatra nāsti | yathā yatra sphurite sati sṛjyaṁ vastu sṛjatā kāraṇa-vargeṇa saha na sphuratīty arthaḥ | yata ubhayoḥ paraṁ sṛjya-sraṣṭṛtyāṁ pṛthag bhūtaṁ tat svayaṁ tathā yatra sphurite sati śreyaś ca svargādi-phalam api na sphurati | tathā tribhir guṇair jāgarādibhir vā anvito’haṅkārātmako jīvo’pi na | **tat** tasmād **etat** viṣṇu-rūpam **utsāditā** nirastā **bādhyā** jīvā **bādhakā** guṇāś ca yasmiṁs tathā-bhūtam | nanu tarhy etat kaḥ praśrayet ? tatrāha—niṣiddheti | sva-bhakta-hṛd-gatān **ūrmīn** kāma-krodhādīn svayam eva tatra **vi**śeṣato **rameta,** tat prasiddham ||31|| 

**...**

**|| 12.6.32 ||**

**paraṁ padaṁ vaiṣṇavam āmananti tad**

**yan neti netīty atad-utsisṛkṣavaḥ |**

**visṛjya daurātmyam ananya-sauhṛdā**

**hṛdopaguhyāvasitaṁ samāhitaiḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **yatas tad-vaiṣṇavaṁ padam āmanantīty āha—param iti | yad etat tad eva paraṁ vaiṣṇavaṁ padaṁ svarūpam āmananti | ke ? atat ātma-vyatiriktam utsisṛkṣavas tyaktum icchavaḥ | yato’nanya-sauhṛdāḥ nāsty anyasmin sauhṛdaṁ yeṣāṁ te | kutaḥ | daurātmyaṁ dehādy-ahaṁ-bhāvaṁ visṛjya | dehe’haṅkārābhāvād anyatra sauhṛdaṁ nāsty atas tyaktum icchava ity arthaḥ | katham | neti netīty evam | atra vidvad anubhavam api pramāṇayati, hṛdopaguhya dhyānādinā | tataḥ samāhitair avasitaṁ niścitam | yad vā, , avasitam avabaddham ātmatayā gṛhītam ity arthaḥ ||32||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **kimarthaṁ tatra krīḍed iti tatrāha—yatas tadvaiṣṇavam iti | tad iti brahmaṇo nāma iti śrutes tadvyatiriktaṁ prapañcam | tatra hetuḥ—yata iti | ananyasauhṛdatve hetumāśaṅkate—kuta iti | ity arthaḥ iti pūrvoktaṁ yata iti padamatra yojyam iti bhāvaḥ| kena prakāreṇa tyaktumicchavastatrāha—netīti| deho'pyātmā na, jaḍatvāt, ghaṭavat | indriyāṇyapyātmā na, taijasatvāt, dīpādivadityevaṁ prakāreṇetyarthaḥ | atrātmasvarūpasya vaiṣṇavapadatve | ādinā dhāraṇāgrahaḥ | tato dhyānānantaram | samāhitaiḥ kṛtasamādhibhiḥ | dhātvarthaprasiddhimādāyāha—yadveti | ity artha iti—ātmarūpatayā grahaṇasyaivārthakaratvād iti bhāvaḥ | yad vā, nānyasminsauhṛdaṁ mamatvaṁ yeṣāṁ te, anyatra tyaktamamatvādviraktā vivekino'nvayavyatirekādiyuktyā ca daurāmyaṁ dehādikośapañcake ātmatvādhyāsaṁ visṛjya brahmaṇi yat atat ātmasvarūpātiriktaṁ māyopādhiṁ tatprayuktassṛṣṭikartṛtvādi ca tadutsisṛkṣavaḥ, evaṁ bhāgatyāgalakṣaṇayā tattvaṁpadārthayoviruddhabhāgatyāgena lakṣitaṁ hṛdaupaniṣadabodhena samāhitaiḥ pratyayairupaguhya nididhyāsya yadavasitaṁ sākṣātkṛtaṁ pratyagabhinnaṁ brahma tad eva viṣṇoḥ paraṁ padaṁ svarūpamāmananti vedapratipādyamadhyavasyantītyarthaḥ| tadvaiṣṇavaṁ padaṁ viṣṇoḥ svarūpamāmananti punaḥ punaḥ smaraṇenābhyasyanti kīdṛśāḥ—daurātmyamahaṁmameti daurjanyaṁ visṛjya neti neti naitadanukūlaṁ naitadanukūlam iti kṛtvā tat tadvyatiriktadehagehaputrādikam ahaṁmamatāspadaṁ yadvastu tatkrameṇa tyaktamicchavaḥ yato'nanyeṣvaikāntikamakteṣveva sauhṛdaṁ prītiryeṣāṁ te'taḥ samāhitaikāgracittaistair eva bhaktṛrhṛdā manasā upaguhya jñātvāvasitaṁ tadvaiṣṇavaṁ padaṁ niścitaṁ nānyair iti viśvanāthaḥ ||32||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **punas tad eva viśadayati—paraṁ padam iti | atat viṣṇu-tattva-vyatiriktaṁ daurātmyaṁ tasmin sauhṛdābhāvaṁ samāhitais tasmin samāhitāntaḥ-karaṇaiḥ ātmārāmair api vā avasitam anubhūtam ||32||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **yatas tad-vaiṣṇavaṁ padam āmanantīty āha—param iti | yad etat tad eva paraṁ vaiṣṇavaṁ padaṁ svarūpam āmananti | ke ? atat ātma-vyatiriktam utsisṛkṣavas tyaktum icchavaḥ | yato’nanya-sauhṛdāḥ nāsty anyasmin sauhṛdaṁ yeṣāṁ te | kutaḥ | daurātmyaṁ dehādy-ahaṁ-bhāvaṁ visṛjya | dehe’haṅkārābhāvād anyatra sauhṛdaṁ nāsty atas tyaktum icchava ity arthaḥ | katham | neti netīty evam | atra vidvad anubhavam api pramāṇayati, hṛdopaguhya dhyānādinā | tataḥ samāhitair avasitaṁ niścitam | yad vā, , avasitam avabaddham ātmatayā gṛhītam ity arthaḥ ||32||

**...**

** || 12.6.33 ||**

**ta etad adhigacchanti viṣṇor yat paramaṁ padam |**

**ahaṁ mameti daurjanyaṁ na yeṣāṁ deha-geha-jam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **etat prāptāv adhikāriṇo darśayati, ta etad iti | deha-jam aham iti | geha-jaṁ mameti ||33||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **etat pratyuktayā nityāparokṣaṁ paramaṁ padamupādhivimuktaṁ śuddhasvarūpam | daurjanyaṁ durjanatālakṣakam ||33||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tatra pūrvāṅgam āha—ta etad iti dvābhyām ||33||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** uktam arthaṁ spaṣṭīkṛtya vyācaṣṭe—ta iti | adhigacchantīti avasitam ity asyārthaḥ | daurjanyam iti daurātmya-padasyārthaḥ ||33||

**...**

** || 12.6.34 ||**

**ativādāṁs titikṣeta nāvamanyeta kañcana |**

**na cemaṁ deham āśritya vairaṁ kurvīta kenacit ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tat-prāpty-upāyam āha—ativādān iti ||34||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **etadvaiṣṇavapadamaparādhe sati tirohitaṁ bhavedato'parādhānudbhavavidhim āha—ativādān kaṭūktīḥ sahetaiva na tu tādṛśamuttaraṁ dadyāt ||34||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** kiṁ caitad viṣṇu-svarūpaṁ kvāpy aparādhe sati tirohitaṁ bhaved etaḥ aparādhānudbhave prakāraṁ śikṣayati—**ativādān** kaṭūktīḥ **titikṣetaiva**, na tu tathaiva kaṭu-pratyuttaraṁ dadyād ity arthaḥ | **imaṁ** sādhaka-**deham āśrityeti** sādhaka-daśāyām api smaryamāṇaṁ svasya siddha-deham āśritya tu smaryamāṇena sva-vipakṣeṇa saha **vairaṁ** **na kuryād** iti rāgānugīya-rasika-bhaktā abhiprāyam āhuḥ—**kañcana** avamantāram api ||34||

**...**

**|| 12.6.35 ||**

**namo bhagavate tasmai kṛṣṇāyākuṇṭha-medhase |**

**yat-pādāmburuha-dhyānāt saṁhitām adhyagām imām ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **śāstra-samāptau guruṁ praṇamati—nama iti | **kṛṣṇāya** vyāsāya | **adhyagām** adhigatavān asmi ||35||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **guruṁ śrīvyāsam | yadyapi śrīśuka eva tadupadeṣṭā tathāpi śrī-kṛṣṇadvaipāyananatisadupadeśasyāpi tatprasādamananādeveti dhyeyam | yad vā, śāstraṁ samāpya sveṣṭadevaṁ bhagavantaṁ namati—nama iti | adhyagāṁ śrīśukādadhigatavānasmīti ||35||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tad etac ca śrīmad-bhāgavatād eva jñāyata ity abhipretya svasmiṁs tad-upadeṣṭāraṁ praṇamati—nama iti | yadyapy asya śrī-śukadevopadeṣṭā, tathāpi śrī-kṛṣṇa-dvaipāyana-namaskāras tat-kṛtopadeśasyāpi tat-prasāda-prāptatvena mananāt | tad etad āha—yad iti ||35||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** śāstraṁ samāpya sveṣṭa-devaṁ bhagavantaṁ praṇamati—nama iti | **adhyagāṁ** śrī-śuka-mukhād adhigatavān asmi ||35||

**...**

**|| 12.6.36 ||**

**śrī-śaunaka uvāca—**

**pailādibhir vyāsa-śiṣyair vedācāryair mahātmabhiḥ |**

**vedāś ca kathitā vyastā etat saumyābhidhehi naḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **“imāṁ saṁhitām adhyagām” ity uktaṁ tatra purāṇa-saṁhitā-vibhāgaṁ viśeṣato bubhutsur veda-vibhāgam api prasaṅgāt pṛthak pṛcchati—pailādibhir iti | he saumya ||36||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **he saumyeti—somavaccittasantāpaharatvena prakāśasa iti bhāvaḥ | tatra vedavibhāgapurāṇasaṁhitāvibhāgayormadhye ||36||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** saṁhitā-madhyagām iti śrutvā saṁhitā-vibhāgaṁ bubhūtsate—pailādibhir iti ||36||

**...**

** || 12.6.37 ||**

**sūta uvāca—**

**samāhitātmano brahman brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ |**

**hṛdy ākāśād abhūn nādo vṛtti-rodhād vibhāvyate ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tatra prathamaṁ vedāvirbhāva-prakāram āha—samāhitātmana ity aṣṭabhiḥ | brahmaṇo hṛdi ya ākāśas tasmān nādo’bhūt | yaḥ karṇa-puṭa-pidhānena śrotra-vṛtti-nirodhād asmad ādiṣv api vibhāvyate vitarkyate ||37||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tatretyuktārtham eva | he brahmann iti—tvaṁ tu jānāsyeva lokahitārthamevāyaṁ praśna iti bhāvaḥ | vedakalpataroḥ phalaṁ nirūpya śākhā api saṅkṣepata āha—sameti | parameṣṭhino brahmaṇo hṛdi ya ākāśastasmānnādo'bhūt yatra nāde vṛttirodhādekāgrayā buddhyā brahma vibhāvyate cintyate yogibhirityapyarthaḥ ||37||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **vṛtti-rodhād iti | gurūpadeśa-balena samāhite’ntaḥ-karaṇe satīty arthaḥ ||37||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** veda-kalpa-taroḥ phalaṁ sādhutayā nirūpya śākhā api saṅkṣepato nirdiśaṁs tasya prathamam āvirbhāva-prakāram āha—samāhitety aṣṭabhiḥ | brahmaṇo hṛdi ya ākāśas tasmān nādo’bhūt, yaḥ karṇa-puṭāpidhānena śrotra-vṛtti-nirodhād asmad-ādiṣv api vibhāvyate vitarkyate ||37||

**...**

** || 12.6.38 ||**

**yad-upāsanayā brahman yogino malam ātmanaḥ |**

**dravya-kriyā-kārakābhyāṁ dhūtvā yānty apunar-bhavam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **prasaṅgān nādopāsakānāṁ mokṣa-phalam āha—yasya nādasyopāsanayātmano malaṁ dhūtvāpohya | kathaṁ-bhūtaṁ malam ? tam āha—dravyam adhibhūtam, kriyā adhyātmam, kārakam adhidaivam, evaṁ tridhā-bhūtā ākhyā yasyeti tathā tam ||38||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **yadbrahmopāsanayā svātmatattvānusandhānenātmano malaṁ māyā vidyādīśajīvopādhitatkāryaṁ ca dravyaṁ samaṣṭivyaṣṭidehaṁ kriyā indriyāṇi kārakaṁ kartṛ antaḥkaraṇākhyaṁ dhūtvā tadviviktaṁ pratyagabhinna brahmāvagatyāpunarbhavaṁ mokṣaṁ yāntīti vārthaḥ ||38||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tad-āśrayamāṇasya[^52] tasyopāsanā-phalam āha—yad-upāsanayeti ||38||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** yasya nādasyopāsanayā dravya-kriyā-kārakāni adhibhūtādīni ākhyā yasya taṁ malaṁ dhūtvā nāśayitvā ||38||

**...**

** || 12.6.39 ||**

**tato’bhūt trivṛd oṁkāro yo’vyakta-prabhavaḥ svarāṭ |**

**yat tal liṅgaṁ bhagavato brahmaṇaḥ paramātmanaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tri-vṛt tri-mātraḥ kaṇṭhoṣṭhādibhir uccārya-māṇasy oṁkārasyākṣara-samāmnāyāntarbhāvāt sūkṣmatayā taṁ viśinaṣṭi, avyaktaḥ prabhavo yasya saḥ | tad evāha—svarāṭ svata eva hṛdi prakāśamānaḥ | tam eva kāryeṇa lakṣayati—yat tad iti | napuṁsakatvaṁ liṅga-śabda-viśeṣaṇatvāt | liṅgaṁ gamakam ||39||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **avyakto'sphuṭaḥ, prabhava udbhavaḥ | tad evāvyaktotpattikatvam eva | tam eva praṇavam eva | gamaka jñāpakam | tato nādāt ghaṇṭānādatulyanādāt | tribhirakārādyairvartate trīnakārādīn vṛṇotyādatteveti trivṛt | trivṛdakārokāramakārātmaka oṁkāro yovyaktasya pramāṇāntarāgamyasya brahmaṇaḥ prabhavo'parokṣo yasmātsa svarāṭ svataḥ pramāṇabhūtaḥ bhagavato brahmaṇaḥ pratyagātmanaś ca paraliṅgam | akārokāramakāravācyaviśvataijasaprājñavilāpanenānuccāryārddhamātrāvabodhyavāgagocarabrahma jñāpakam ||39||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **liṅgaṁ bodha-dvāram avayava-rūpaṁ vā ||39||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** tato nādāt trivṛt a-kārokāra-makārātmakaḥ avyakto’spaṣṭaḥ prabhavo janma yasya saḥ | svarāṭ sākṣāt parameśvara eva yat yo bhagavad-ādi-trayasya liṅgaṁ gamakaṁ bhakta-jñāni-yogibhir upāsyatvāt, liṅga-śabda-viśeṣaṇatvāt tad ity asya napuṁsakatvam ||39||

**...**

**|| 12.6.40-41 ||**

**śṛṇoti ya imaṁ sphoṭaṁ supta-śrotre ca śūnya-dṛk |**

**yena vāg vyajyate yasya vyaktir ākāśa ātmanaḥ ||**

**sva-dhāmno brahmaṇaḥ sākṣād vācakaḥ paramātmanaḥ |**

**sa sarva-mantropaniṣad veda-bījaṁ sanātanam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ko’sau paramātmā ? tam āha—śṛṇotītīmaṁ sphoṭam avyaktam oṁkāram | nanu jīva eva taṁ śṛṇotu ? nety āha—supta-śrotre karṇa-pidhānādinā, vṛttike’pi śrotre sati | jīvas tu karaṇādhīna-jñānatvān na tadā śrotā | tad-upalabdhis tu tasya paramātma-dvārikaiveti bhāvaḥ | īśvaras tu naivam, yataḥ śūnya-dṛk | śūnye’pīndriya-varge dṛk jñānaṁ yasya | tathā hi—supto yadā śabdaṁ śrutvā prabudhyate na tadā jīvaḥ śrotā, līnendriyatvāt | ato yas tadā śabdaṁ śrutvā jīvaṁ prabodhayati, sa yathā paramātmaiva tadvat | ko’sāv oṁkāraḥ ? taṁ viśinaṣṭi sārdhena—yena vāg bṛhatī vyajyate | yasya ca hṛdayākāśe ātmanaḥ sakāśād vyaktir abhivyaktiḥ ||40||

kiṁ ca, sva-dhāmnaḥ svasyāśrayaḥ kāraṇaṁ yad brahma tasya | kiṁ ca, paramātmāṁśa-bhūta-samasta-devatā-vācako’pīty āśayenāha—sa iti | sarva-mantrāṇām upaniṣad-rahasya-sūkṣma-rūpam ity arthaḥ | tatra hetuḥ, vedānāṁ bījaṁ kāraṇam | bījatve’py avikāritām āha—sanātanaṁ sadaika-rūpam, tasya brahma-rūpatvāt ||41||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **atrākṣipati—nanv iti | iti bhāva iti—na hi jīva indriyaṁ vinaindriyikamadhigacchatyanyathāndhāde rūpādijñānaṁ syād iti tātparyam | naivaṁ jīvasadṛśo netyarthaḥ | yad vā, yaḥ puruṣa imaṁ sphuṭyate'neneti sphoṭaṁ suptaśrotre mudritakarṇe śṛṇoti sa śūnyadṛk sūkṣmadarśī syāt | tam eva viśeṣayati—yataḥ sphoṭātsarvā vāgvyajyate prakaṭībhavati yannimittikā hṛdayākāśe ātmano vyaktiḥ | praṇavarūpasphoṭopāsanayaiva hṛdyātmāvirbhāvo bhavatīty arthaḥ || anyadādhikyam āha—kiñceti | na kevalaṁ brahmavācaka evāpi tvanyeṣāmapīty āha—kiñceti | ity artha iti—tattaddevabodhakākhilamantrasūkṣmarūpamidamevākṣaram iti bhāvaḥ | tatra sūkṣmarūpatve | yad vā, svadhāmnaḥ svaprakāśasyāpi brahmaṇaḥ paramātmano'pi sākṣādāvaraṇabādhena vācako bodhakaḥ | sa eva sarvadharmāgamantrāṇāṁ brahmavyañjakopaniṣadāṁ ca sanātanaṁ bījam, svasya dhāmāśrayo yadbrahma tasya paramātmano'pi bhagavataś ca vācakaḥ oṁmityetadbrahmaṇo diṣṭaṁ nāma iti śruteḥ ||40-41||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **nanu, tasya śabdasya sadāstitve kiṁ pramāṇam ? karṇe pihite śravaṇam eveti cet huṅkārādikam api śrūyate | tathā supto jāgrad eva vāhūti-sahasreṇāpy avadhārayituṁ yo na śakyate tena tu janma-vadhireṇendriyābhāvāt na śrūyate eva, sa tatrāha—śṛṇotīti | yaḥ varamātmā supte śrotre ca-kārāt asupte'pi śṛṇoti tasya jīvavad indriyāpekṣā) vasthā nāstīty āha—śūnya-dṛg iti | apāṇi-pādaḥ [śve.u. 3.19] ity ādi, svābhāvikī jñāna-bala-kriyā ca [śve.u. 6.8] iti śruteḥ | tatra hetum āha—yena vāg-ādīndriyam api vyajyate yasya cātmano vyaktiḥ kārya-rūpeṇāvirbhāvaḥ śabdāśrayaḥ ākāśaḥ kim uta spaśādy-āśrayo vāyv-ādir ity arthaḥ | tasmāj jīvas tu tad-upādhy-upāsanayā tad-anugraheṇaiva śṛṇotīti bhāvaḥ ||40||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **bhagavad-ādi-śabda-vācyaḥ sa parameśvara eva kas tatrāha—śṛṇotīti | ya imaṁ sphoṭam avyaktaṁ nādātmakam oṅkāraṁ śṛṇoti saḥ | nanu jīva eva śṛṇoti ? nety āha—supta-śrotre karṇa-pidhānādinā śrotre śravaṇendriye supte sati avṛttike sati yaḥ sṛṇotīty arthaḥ | jīvas tu karaṇādhīna-jñānatvān na tadā śrotā kintu paramātmaiva tasya śrotā | tad api jīvasya yā tad-upalabdhiḥ sā paramātma-dvārikaiveti jñeyam | yataḥ parameśvaraḥ śūnya-dṛk śūnye’pīndriye varge dṛk jñānam asya saḥ | tathāpi supto yadā śabdaṁ śrutvā prabuddhyate na tadā jīvaḥ śrotā līnendriyatvāt, ato yas tadā śabdaṁ śrutvā jīvaṁ prabodhayati sa paramātmaiva | ko’sāv oṁkāras taṁ viśinaṣṭi sārdhena | yena vāk veda-lakṣaṇā bṛhatī vyajyate yasya hṛdayākāśe ātmanaḥ sakāśād abhivyaktiḥ | kiṁ ca, svasya dhāma āśrayo yad brahma tasya paramātmano bhagavataś ca vācakaḥ | om ity etad brahmaṇo nediṣṭhaṁ nāmeti nediṣṭhaṁ nāma iti śruteḥ | sa-praṇavaḥ sarve mantrā upaniṣadaś ca yatra, tasya vedasya bījaṁ kāraṇaṁ bījatve’py avikāritvam āha—sanātanaṁ sadaika-rūpaṁ tasya brahma-rūpatvāt ||41||

**...**

**|| 12.6.42 ||**

**tasya hy āsaṁs trayo varṇā a-kārādyā bhṛgūdvaha |**

**dhāryante yais trayo bhāvā guṇa-nāmārtha-vṛttayaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **idānīṁ tataḥ sarva-prapañcotpatti-prakāram āha—tasya hīti | trayas tri-saṅkhyā-yuktā bhāvā yair a-kāro-kāra-ma-kārair dhāryante tat-kāraṇatvāt | tān evāha—**guṇāḥ** sattvādayaḥ | **nāmāni** ṛg-yajuḥ-sāmāni | **arthā** bhūr-bhuvaḥ-svar-lokāḥ | **vṛttayo** jāgrad-ādyāḥ ||42||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tataḥ praṇavāt | tasya praṇavasya | tatkāraṇatvāt teṣāṁ bhāvānāṁ kāraṇatvāt| dhāryate svebhya utpādyate | tāneva bhāvānpadārthān | etaccopapāditamadhastāt | yaistribhirvaṇaistrayo bhāvā vedā dhāryate, yaiś ca tribhirvedairguṇāḥ ojaḥprasādādayo nāmāni śabdā arthā vācyaliṅgā vṛttayo'bhidhālakṣaṇā vyañjanāḥ yathā vaṭabījenaiva vaṭavṛkṣo dhāryate tena ca skandhaśākhāpatrapuṣpaphalādayaś ca ||42||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **sākṣād-vācaka iti māyāvādinām iva lakṣaṇā nādṛtā—om ity etad brahmaṇo nediṣṭhaṁ nāma [atharva-śirā] iti śruteḥ ||42||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** tasya veda-bījatvam eva darśayati—tasya praṇavasya **trayaḥ** a-kāro-kāra-ma-kārā **yair** eva tribhir varṇais **trayo bhāvā** vedā dhāryante, yaiś ca tribhir vedair **guṇa-nāmārtha-vṛttayo dhāryante** | tatra guṇā ojaḥ prasādādyā nāmāni śabdāḥ | arthā vācya-liṅga-vyaṅgyāḥ, vṛttayo’bhidhā-lakṣaṇā-vyañjanāḥ | yathā baṭa-bījenaiva baṭa-vṛkṣo dhāryate, tena ca skandha-śākhā-puṣpa-phalādayaḥ ||42||

**...**

** || 12.6.43-44 ||**

**tato’kṣara-samāmnāyam asṛjad bhagavān ajaḥ |**

**antasthoṣma-svara-sparśa-hrasva-dīrghādi-lakṣaṇam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tatas tebhyo varṇebhyaḥ | akṣarāṇāṁ samāmnāyaṁ samāhāram | tam evāha—anta-sthā ya-ra-la-vāḥ | ūṣmāṇaḥ śa-ṣa-sa-hāḥ | svarā a-kārādyāḥ | sparśāḥ kādayaḥ | hrasva-dīrghāś ca | ādi-śabdāj jihvā-mūlīyādayaḥ | ta eva lakṣaṇaṁ svarūpaṁ yasya tam ||43||

vibhuś catur-mukha-svarūpe bhagavān | asṛjad iti pūrvasyaivānuṣaṅgaḥ | cātur-hotra-vivakṣayā catvāro hotropalakṣitā ṛtvijaś caturhotāras tair anuṣṭheyaṁ hautrādhvarya-vādikaṁ karma cātur-hotraṁ tad-vivakṣayā ||44||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tebhyo'kārādibhyaḥ | akṣarāṇāṁ samāmnāyam a i u ṇ ity-ādisūtracaturdaśarūpam | yenākṣarasamāmnāyamadhigamya maheśvarāt ityatra caturdaśasūtryāmevākṣarasamāmnāyapadasya prayuktatvāt | yad vā, mātṛkārūpam | tatprakāraścāsmatpraṇītamātṛkāvilāse draṣṭavyaḥ || tenākṣarasamāmnāyena | asau brahmā | vyāhṛtayo bhūrbhuvaḥsvar iti vyastāssamastāś ca | tatsahitān vyaktoṁkārasahitān | soṁkārānity ukter oṁkārasahitānām eva sarveṣāṁ yajñādau prayogaṁ sūcayati ||43-44||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tata iti | svarā udāttādayo hrasva-dīrghādayas tu sa-plutā acaḥ, visargādayaś catvāraś ca so’ṁkārān ity oṁkārasya kāraṇasyāpi kāryeṣu punar uktir vaikhary-avasthā-bhedena ||43||[^53]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** praṇavād vedotpattau kramaṁ darśayati—tata oṁkārāt akṣarāṇāṁ samāmnāyaṁ samāhāraṁ tam evāha—antasthā ya-ra-la-vāḥ | uṣmāṇaḥ śa-ṣa-sa-hāḥ | svarā a-kārādyāḥ | sparśāḥ kādayo māvasānāḥ | hrasva-dīrghāḥ svara-bhedāḥ | ādi-śabdāj jihvā-mūlīyādayaḥ, ta eva lakṣaṇaṁ svarūpaṁ yasya tam | tenākṣara-samāmnāyena vibhur viṣṇu-rūpo brahmā asṛjad iti pūrvasyaivānuṣaṅgaḥ ||43-44||

**...**

**|| 12.6.45 ||**

**putrān adhyāpayat tāṁs tu brahmarṣīn brahma-kovidān |**

**te tu dharmopadeṣṭāraḥ sva-putrebhyaḥ samādiśan ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **putrān marīcy-ādīn | tān vedān | brahma-kovidān vedoccāraṇādi-nipuṇān ||45||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **te tu marīcyādayas tu | svaputrebhyaḥ kaśyapādibhyaḥ ||45||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **putrān marīcy-ādīn ||45||

**...**

** || 12.6.46 ||**

**te paramparayā prāptās tat-tac-chiṣyair dhṛta-vrataiḥ |**

**catur-yugeṣv atha vyastā dvāparādau maharṣibhiḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **evaṁ catur-yugeṣu prāptāḥ | dvāparādau dvāparam ādir yasya tad antyāṁśa-lakṣaṇasya kālasya tasmin, dvāparānte veda-vibhāga-prasiddheḥ, śantanu-sama-kālaṁ vyāsāvatāra-prasiddheś ca | vyastā vibhaktāḥ ||46||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **te vedāḥ ||46||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** te vedāḥ ||46||

**...**

** || 12.6.47 ||**

**kṣīṇāyuṣaḥ kṣīṇa-sattvān durmedhān vīkṣya kālataḥ |**

**vedān brahmarṣayo vyasyan hṛdi-sthācyuta-coditāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tatra hetuḥ—kṣīṇāyuṣo janān | tarhi puruṣa-buddhi-prabhavatvād anādaraṇīyatvaṁ syād ity aśaṅkyāha—hṛdi-stheti ||47||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tatra vedavibhāge | atrākṣipati—tarhīti | na teṣāṁ svātantryam iti dhvanitaṁ—hṛdisthetyādinā ||47||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

**...**

**|| 12.6.48 ||**

**asminn apy antare brahman bhagavān loka-bhāvanaḥ |**

**brahmeśādyair loka-pālair yācito dharma-guptaye ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **evaṁ sāmānyate veda-vibhāga-kramam uktvā vaivasvata-manvantare viśeṣato nirūpayitum āha—asminn apīti ||48||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **asminn api śrāddhadeva-manvantare'pi ||48||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** antare vaivasvata-manvantare ||48||

**...**

**|| 12.6.49 ||**

**parāśarāt satyavatyām aṁśāṁśa-kalayā vibhuḥ |**

**avatīrṇo mahā-bhāga vedaṁ cakre catur-vidham ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **aṁśo māyā tasyā aṁśaḥ sattvaṁ tasya kalayāṁśenāvatīrṇaḥ san ||49||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **aṁśeṣu svāṁśeṣu jīveṣu svāṁśena bodhena yatkaṁ sukhaṁ tatsvarūpāvirbhāvena lāti tayā kṛpayāvatīrṇa iti vārthaḥ ||49||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **aṁśāṁśa-kalayeti | aṁśo mahā-puruṣaḥ, tasyāṁśo viṣṇuḥ, tasya kalayā aṁśena vibhur bhagavān ||49||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** _na vyākhyātam._

**...**

**|| 12.6.50 ||**

**ṛg-atharva-yajuḥ-sāmnāṁ rāśīr uddhṛtya vargaśaḥ |**

**catasraḥ saṁhitāś cakre mantrair maṇi-gaṇā iva ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **cātur-vidhyam evāha—ṛg iti | ṛg-ādi-mantrāṇāṁ rāśīn vargaśas tat-tat-prakaraṇa-bhedair uddhṛtya yathāneka-vidha-maṇi-rāśer maṇi-gaṇāḥ padma-rāgādayo vivicyoddhriyante, tadvad uddhṛtya tair mantraiś catasra ṛg-ādi-saṁhitāś cakre ||50||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **nanu brahmaṇaiva catubhirmukhaiścatvāro vedā ādāveva kṛtāstatkathamucyate vedaṁ cakraṁ caturvidham iti tatrāha—ṛgiti | rāśīn kṛtvā tattatprakaraṇabhedairmaṇigaṇā iva, yathā maṇikṣetre'pi padmarāgahīrakādayaḥ pṛthakpṛthagudhṛtya kūṭaṁ kriyante tadvad iti bhāvaḥ ||50||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** nanu brahmaṇaiva caturbhir mukhaiś catvāro vedāḥ prathamam eva kṛtās tat katham ucyate vedaṁ cakre caturvidham [12.6.49] iti, tatrāha—ṛg-atharveti | rāśīn kṛtvā vargaśas tat-tat-prakaraṇa-bhedair maṇi-gaṇā iveti | yathā maṇi-kṣetre’pi padmarāga-hīrakādaya uddhṛtya vivicya pṛthak pṛthak kuṭaṁ kriyata iti | catasraḥ ṛg-ādi-saṁhitāḥ ||50||

**...**

**|| 12.6.51 ||**

**tāsāṁ sa caturaḥ śiṣyān upāhūya mahā-matiḥ |**

**ekaikāṁ saṁhitāṁ brahman ekaikasmai dadau vibhuḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tāsāṁ saṁhitānāṁ madhye ekaikām ||51||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

**...**

** || 12.6.52 ||**

**pailāya saṁhitām ādyāṁ bahv-ṛcākhyām uvāca ha |**

**vaiśampāyana-saṁjñāya nigadākhyaṁ yajur-gaṇam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ṛk-samudāya-rūpatvād bahv-ṛcākhyām | nitarāṁ praśleṣeṇa gadyamānatvān nigadākhyam ||51||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **viśeṣeṇa bhātīti vibhuḥ sarvajñaḥ ||52||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **bahv-ṛcākhyām ṛk-saṁhitāṁ, nitarāṁ gadyamānatvān nigadākhyam ||51||

**...**

**|| 12.6.53 ||**

**sāmnāṁ jaiminaye prāha tathā chandoga-saṁhitām |**

**atharvāṅgirasīṁ nāma sva-śiṣyāya sumantave ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **saṁhitām | chandaḥsu gīyamānatvāc chandogākhyām ||52||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **sāmnāṁ sambrandhinīm ||53||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

**...**

**|| 12.6.54-57 ||**

**pailaḥ sva-saṁhitām ūce indrapramitaye muniḥ |**

**bāṣkalāya ca so’py āha śiṣyebhyaḥ saṁhitāṁ svakām ||**

**caturdhā vyasya bodhyāya yājñavalkyāya bhārgava |**

**parāśarāyāgnimitra indrapram itir ātma-vān ||**

**adhyāpayat saṁhitāṁ svāṁ māṇḍūkeyam ṛṣiṁ kavim |**

**tasya śiṣyo devamitraḥ saubhary-ādibhya ūcivān ||**

**śākalyas tat-sutaḥ svāṁ tu pañcadhā vyasya saṁhitām |**

**vātsya-mudgala-śālīya-gokhalya-śiśireṣv adhāt ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tatra ṛg-veda-śākhā-vibhāgam āha—paila iti | sva-saṁhitāṁ dvidhā vibhajya indra-pramitaye bāṣkalāya ca ūce | sa bāṣkalo’pi svakāṁ saṁhitāṁ caturdhā vyasya bodhyādibhyaḥ śiṣyebhya āha—he bhārgava, indra-pram itir api svāṁ saṁhitāṁ sva-sutaṁ māṇḍūkeyam adhyāpayām āsa | tasya māṇḍūkeyasya śiṣyo devamitraḥ ||53-56|| tat-suto māṇḍūkeya-sutaḥ śākalyo vātsyādiṣu pañcasv adhāt | tān adhyāpayāmāsety arthaḥ ||57||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tatra caturṣu || he bhārgaveti—bhṛguvaṁśajatvāttvamapyetaṁ vibhāgaṁ jānāsyeveti bhāvaḥ agnimitra iti caturthyarthe saptamī | yad vā, agniṁ mimīte prāmāṇyena sthāpayatītyagnimitaḥ tasmai ||54-57||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** tatra ṛg-veda-śākhā-vibhāgam āha—paila iti | sva-saṁhitāṁ dvidhā vibhajya indra-pramitaye bāṣkalāya ca ūce | sa bāṣkalo’pi caturdhā sva-saṁhitāṁ vyasya bodhyādibhyaś caturbhyaḥ sva-śiṣyebhya āha—he bhārgava, he śaunaka ! indra-pram itir api sva-saṁhitāṁ sva-sutaṁ māṇḍūkeyam adhyāpayāmāsa | tasya māṇḍūkeyasya śiṣyo devamitraḥ ||53-56|| tat-suto māṇḍūkeya-sutaḥ śākalyo vātsyādiṣu pañcasv adhāt | tān adhyāpayām āsety arthaḥ ||57||

**...**

** || 12.6.58 ||**

**jātūkarṇyaś ca tac-chiṣyaḥ sa-niruktaṁ sva-saṁhitām |**

**balāka-paila-jābāla- virajebhyo dadau muniḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **tac-chiṣyaḥ śākalya-śiṣyaḥ sva-saṁhitāṁ tredhā vibhajya caturthaṁ vaidika-padārtha-vyākhyānurūpaṁ niruktaṁ ca kṛtvā balākādibhyaś caturbhyo dadau ||58||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

**...**

** || 12.6.59 ||**

**bāṣkaliḥ prati-śākhābhyo vālakhilākhya-saṁhitām |**

**cakre vālāyanir bhajyaḥ kāśāraś caiva tāṁ dadhuḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **bāṣkaliḥ pūrvoktasya bāṣkalasya putraḥ | pratiśākhābhya ukta-sarva-śākhābhyaḥ | bālāyanyādayas tām ādadhur adhītavantaḥ ||59||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **bāṣkalir bāṣkala-putraḥ | pratiśākhābhyaḥ śākhabhyaḥ śākhābhya saṅgṛhya ||59||

**...**

**|| 12.6.60 ||**

**bahv-ṛcāḥ saṁhitā hy etā ebhir brahmarṣibhir dhṛtāḥ |**

**śrutvaitac-chandasāṁ vyāsaṁ sarva-pāpaiḥ pramucyate ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ṛk-śāsvopasaṁhāra-pūrvakaṁ tac-chravaṇa-phalam āha—bahv-ṛcā iti | etac-chandasām eteṣāṁ chandasām ||60||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **vyāsaṁ vibhāgam ||60||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

**...**

**|| 12.6.61 ||**

**vaiśampāyana-śiṣyā vai carakādhvaryavo’bhavan |**

**yac cerur brahma-hatyāṁhaḥ-kṣapaṇaṁ sva-guror vratam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **yajur-vede taittirīya-śākhotpatti-prastāvam āha—vaiśaṁpāyana-śiṣyā ity-ādinā | caraka-nāma-niruktim āha—**yac cerur** iti | **yad** yasmād **brahma-hatyā**-rūpam **aṁhaḥ** **kṣapayatīti** tathā tat **sva-guror** anuṣṭheyaṁ **vrataṁ,** tac caraṇāc **carakā** ity arthaḥ ||61||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **yajur-vede taittirīyaka-śākhotpatti-prakāram āha—vaiśaṁpāyaneti | **caraka**-nāma-niruktam āha—**yac cerur** iti | **brahma-hatyā**-rūpam **aṁhaḥ kṣapayatīti**, tathā | tat **sva-guror** anuṣṭheyaṁ **vrataṁ,** tac-caraṇāc **carakāś** ca te **adhvaryavaś** ceti te tathā ||61||

**...**

**|| 12.6.62 ||**

**yājñavalkyaś ca tac-chiṣya āhāho bhagavan kiyat |**

**caritenālpa-sārāṇāṁ cariṣye’haṁ suduścaram ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tac-chiṣyo vaiśaṁpāyana-śiṣyaḥ | **alpa-sārāṇām** eteṣāṁ caritena kiyat ? **suduścaram ahaṁ cariṣyāmīti** ||62||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** **yājñavalkyo**’pi **tac-chiṣyaḥ** vaiśampāyana-śiṣyaḥ **alpasārāṇām** eṣāṁ caritena prāyaścittācaraṇena kiyat ? ete sukhaṁ tiṣṭhantu, **aham** eka eva tapaḥ samarthaś **cariṣyāmi** ||62||

**...**

**|| 12.6.63 ||**

**ity ukto gurur apy āha kupito yāhy alaṁ tvayā |**

**viprāvamantrā śiṣyeṇa mad-adhītaṁ tyajāśv iti ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **viprāṇām avamantrāvajñā-kartrā | matto’dhītam āśu tyajeti ||63||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **brahmahatyākāraṇamukta viṣṇupurāṇe—


    ṛṣiyo'dya mahāmerau samāje nāgamiṣyati | 


    tasya vai saptarātrāttu brahmahatyā bhaviṣyati | 


    pūrvamevaṁ munigaṇaḥ samayābhūtkṛtā dvija | 


    vaiśampāyana ekas tu taṁ vyatikrāntavāṁstadā | 


    svasvīyaṁ bālakaṁ so'tha padā spṛṣṭamadhātayat | 


    śiṣyānāha ca bhī śiṣyā brahmahatyāpahaṁ vratam | 


    caradhvaṁ matkṛte sarve na vicāryam idaṁ tathā || iti ||61-63||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** kupita iti | vato garva-vaśāt | etān vinītān api alpasārān uktvā ākṣipasi tasmāt yāhīty apasara | **tvayā** śiṣyeṇa **mamālam** | tataś ca bhavatv ahaṁ yāmīty uktvā jigamiṣantaṁ taṁ punar āha—mad-adhītam iti ||63||

**...**

**|| 12.6.64-65 ||**

**devarāta-sutaḥ so’pi charditvā yajuṣāṁ gaṇam |**

**tato gato’tha munayo dadṛśus tān yajur-gaṇān ||**

**yajūṁṣi tittirā bhūtvā tal-lolupatayādaduḥ |**

**taittirīyā iti yajuḥ- śākhā āsan supeśalāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **devarāta-suto yājñavalkyaḥ ||64|| charditasyādānaṁ vipra-rūpeṇānucitam iti **tittirāḥ** pakṣi-viśeṣā **bhūtvā** **ādaduḥ** | tataś ca **taittirīyā** iti prasiddhāḥ | **supeśalā** atiramyāḥ | bahu-vacanam avāntara-bheda-vivakṣayā ||65||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tato gurukulāt || teṣu yajuṣṣu lolupatayā lālasayā munayo'nye vaiśampāyanaśiṣyā ādadurjagṛhuḥ | na hi cetaḥ sukṛtināmakāyeṁ gacchati kvacit iti nyāyena charditā api mantrā aśucitāṁ na gatā iti tadgrahaṇe munigaṇecchotpatterjñāyate | ata evoktam—supeśalā iti śākhāviśeṣaṇam | surabhye peśalaḥ proktaḥ śuddhe mṛdutare tathā ityabhidhānacintāmaṇokteḥ suṣṭhu peśalā atīvaśodhakajñānopayogipañcakośādinirṇāyakatvenātiśuddhāḥ | na hi kadācidbhakṣitahemagulikā purīṣamārgatodgīrṇā vāśucitāmeti kintu yāvanmalayogaṁ tataḥ kṣālanādyathā śuddhā tathaiva tittirirūpeṇa tadupādānasamaye evānnarūpeṇa charditatvātteṣvaśucitvabhrāntyaiva munirbhirna brāhmaṇa-rūpeṇa te svīkṛtās tad-rūpatyāgottaraṁ sarve munayas tān jagṛhus te ca mantrāḥ kṛṣṇa-yajuṣṭvena prasiddhā yajñādiśūpayujyante, na hyaśucimantrairyajñaḥ pratāyata iti vedasya sākṣānnārāyaṇarūpatvāduccāvacatā na bhavati noccāvacatvaṁ bhajate nirguṇatvāddhiyo guṇaiḥ ityaṣṭame matsyacaritokteḥ vānte yātayāmaḥ iti nighaṇṭūktes tadbhinno'yātayāmastakāmanayā śrīyājñavalkyoktaṁ sarvaṁ devapūjyam brahmendra-nārāyaṇa-rudra-vanditaḥ sā naḥ sadā yacchatu maṅgalaṁ raviḥ ity uktes tuṣṭāveti vaiṣṇavādau ||64-65||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **devarāta-suto yājñavalkyaḥ | charditasyādānaṁ vipra-rūpeṇāyuktam iti tittirāḥ pakṣi-viśeṣā bhūtvā ādaduḥ | tataś ca taittirīyā iti khyātāḥ ||64-65||

**...**

**|| 12.6.66 ||**

**yājñavalkyas tato brahmaṁś chandāṁsy adhi gaveṣayan |**

**guror avidyamānāni sūpatasthe’rkam īśvaram ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kāṇvamādhyandinādi-śākhā-prasaṅgam āha—yājñavalkya ity-ādinā | guror vaiśaṁpāyanasya vyāsena vibhajyānuktatvād avidyamānāny adhikāni gaveṣayan mṛgayan sūpatasthe samyak tuṣṭāva | īśvaram ṛg-ādi-vedānām | tathā ca śrutiḥ—


    ṛgbhiḥ pūrvāhṇe divi deva īyate 


    yajur-vede tiṣṭhati madhye ahnaḥ | 


    sāma-vedenāsta-maye mahīyate 


    vedair aśūnyas tribhir eti sūryaḥ || iti ||66||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **sūryo devaḥ īyate pratīyate mahīyate pūjyate | tato vaiśampāyanāt ||66||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **īśvaram iti | tad-antaryāmy-abhedena bhāvyamānam ity arthaḥ ||66||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** adhigaveṣayan anviṣyan guror vaiśampāyanasyāpi avidyamānāni tenāpy anadhigatānīty arthaḥ ||66||

**...**

**|| 12.6.67 ||**

**śrī-yājñavalkya uvāca—**

**oṁ namo bhagavate ādityāyākhila-jagatām ātma-svarūpeṇa kāla-svarūpeṇa catur-vidha-bhūta-nikāyānāṁ brahmādi-stamba-paryantānām antar-hṛdayeṣu bahir api cākāśa ivopādhināvyavadhīyamāno bhavān eka eva kṣaṇa-lava-nimeṣāvayavopacita-saṁvatsara-gaṇenāpām ādāna-visargābhyām imāṁ loka-yātrām anuvahati ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **namo bhagavate tubhyam ādityāya | yo bhagavān eka evemāṁ loka-yātrām anuvahatīty anvayaḥ | tad eva darśayati—akhila-jagatām ātma-svarūpeṇāntar-hṛdayeṣu kāla svarūpeṇa ca bahir api vartamāna iti | akhila-jagatām ity asya prapañcaḥ, catur-vidheti | hṛdayāntar-vartitve’pi jīva-vat tenopādhināvyavadhīyamāno’nācchādyamānaḥ | kāla-svarūpeṇa cety asya prapañcaḥ—kṣaṇeti | kṣaṇa-lavādayo ye’vayavās tair upacitāḥ saṁvatsarās teṣāṁ gaṇena praty abdam apām ādānaṁ śoṣaṇaṁ visargo vṛṣṭis tābhyām | anena gāyatrī-prathama-pādokta-vareṇyatā nirṇitā ||67||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **caturvidheti—jarāyujāṇḍajasvedajodbhidbhedājjīvāścaturvidhāḥ | yathā ghaṭādyupādhinākāśa iva paricchinna iva pratīyate iti vā ||67||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **yat tu oṁ namas te ity-ādi-gadyeṣu tad-arthatvena sūryaḥ stutaḥ, tat paramātma-dṛṣṭyaiva, na tu svātantryeṇety adoṣaḥ ||67||[^54]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **yo bhagavān eka imāṁ loka-yātrām anuvahati, tasmai ādityāya akhila-jagatāṁ bhagavate śrīmate nama ity anvayaḥ | bhagaṁ śrī-kāma-māhātmya- ity amaraḥ | caturvidha-bhūta-nikāyānām antar bahir api krameṇātma-svarūpeṇa kāla-svarūpeṇa vartamāna ity arthaḥ | hṛdayāntar-vartitve’pi jīvavat tena upādhinā avyavadhīyamāno’nācchādyamānaḥ, ākāśavat | kṣaṇa-lavādayo ye’vayavās tair upacitāḥ saṁvatsarās teṣāṁ gaṇena praty abdam apām ādānaṁ śoṣaṇaṁ visargo vṛṣṭis tābhyām ||67||

**...**

** || 12.6.68 ||**

**yad u ha vāva vibudharṣabha savitar adas tapaty anusavanam ahar ahar āmnāya-vidhinopatiṣṭhamānānām akhila-durita-vṛjina-bījāvabharjana bhagavataḥ samabhidhīmahi tapana maṇḍalam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **dvitīya-pādārthānuvarṇanena stauti—yad u heti | he **vibudharṣabha** ! he **savitaḥ** ! yad apy **ado** **bhagavatas** tava **maṇḍalaṁ tapati**, tat **samabhidhīmahīti** samyag ābhimukhyena dhyāyema | punas tasyaiva saṁbodhanam | pratyahaṁ **tri-savaṇaṁ** vaidika-karma-mārgeṇa stuvatāṁ bhaktānāṁ yāny **akhilāni duritāni**, tat-phalāni ca **vṛjināni** duḥkhāni, teṣāṁ **bījam** ajñānaṁ ca, teṣām **avabharjana** vināśaka ! he **tapana** ! iti ||68||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** he vibudharṣabha ! savitaḥ ! yan maṇḍalaṁ tapati, adaḥ samabhidhīmahi | anusavanaṁ pratisamayam ahar ahaḥ pratyahaṁ ca | āmnāya-vidhinā vaidika-mārgeṇa upatiṣṭhatām atvhetuām | yāny akhilāni duritāni, tat-phalāni ca vṛjināni duḥkhāni ca, teṣāṁ bījam ajñānaṁ ca, teṣām avabharjana vināśaka ! he tapana ! ||68||

**...**

**|| 12.6.69 ||**

**ya iha vāva sthira-cara-nikarāṇāṁ nija-niketanānāṁ mana-indriyāsu-gaṇān anātmanaḥ svayam ātmāntaryāmī pracodayati ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tṛtīya-pādena stauti—ya iheti | bhavān sthāvara-jaṅgama-samūhānāṁ svāśrayāṇāṁ jīvānāṁ mana-indriya-prāṇa-gaṇān anātmano jaḍān svayam ātmaivāntaryāmī san pracodayati pravartayati ||69||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ādareṇa prītyutpādanārthamāmantrayati—he vibudharṣabheti | sarva-devaśreṣṭhatvāttvāmahaṁ staumīti bhāvaḥ | savitariti—sarvaviśvotpādakasya tava mama sarvavedajñānotpādanaṁ na durghaṭam iti bhāvaḥ | jñānotpādanaṁ hyajñānanāśaṁ vinā na sambhavatīti cettatrāha—anusavanamity-ādi | ata ārabhyāvabharjanāntāṁ saṁbuddhim āha—sevakājñānanāśadyotikām | ajñānasya tamorūpatvāttaddhananaṁ prakāśena bhavatīti cettaddyotikā saṁbuddhiṁ punarāha—tapaneti | tapa—aiśvarye dhātuḥ | aiśvaryaṁ cātra prakāśalakṣaṇam eva sarvavilakṣaṇaṁ tavaivātaḥ sarva-devādhikastvamevāsīti bhāvaḥ ||68-69||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **anātmano jaḍān pracodayati pravartayati ||69||

**...**

**|| 12.6.70 ||**

**ya evemaṁ lokam ati-karāla-vadanāndhakāra-saṁjñā-jagara-graha-gilitaṁ mṛtakam iva vicetanam avalokyānukampayā parama-kāruṇika īkṣayaivotthāpyāhar ahar anusavanaṁ śreyasi sva-dharmākhyātmāvasthāne pravartayati ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tṛtīya-pādam eva maṇḍala-stha-paratayā vyācakṣāṇaḥ stauti—ya eveti | ya eka eva bhagavān atikarāla-vadano yo’ndha-kāra-saṁjño’jagara-grahas tena gilitam ata eva mṛtakam iva vicetanaṁ sva-dharmākhyaṁ yad ātmāvasthānaṁ pratyak pravaṇatvaṁ tad eva śreyas tasmin pravartayati | kiṁ ca, yo bhavānavani-patir ivāṭati gacchati ||70||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** īkṣayaivotthāpya pūrvādrāv uditya īkṣaṇa-pradānenaivety arthaḥ | sva-dharmākhyaṁ yat ātmāvasthānam ātmopāsanaṁ, tatra ||70||

**...**

**|| 12.6.71 ||**

**avani-patir ivāsādhūnāṁ bhayam udīrayann aṭati parita āśā-pālais tatra tatra kamala-kośāñjalibhir upahṛtārhaṇaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **āśā-pālair indrādibhiḥ | kamala-kośa-yuktais tat tulyair vāñjalibhir upahṛtārhaṇo dattārghyaḥ ||71||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ata evāṁdhakārājagaragilitatvādeva | pratyakpravaṇatvaṁ tadekaparatvam | anyadādhikyam āha—kiñceti ||70-71||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **āśā-pālair dik-pālair indrādibhiḥ | kamala-kośa-yuktais tat tulyair vāñjalibhir upahṛtārhaṇo dattārghyaḥ ||71||

**...**

**|| 12.6.72 ||**

**atha ha bhagavaṁs tava caraṇa-nalina-yugalaṁ tri-bhuvana-gurubhir abhivanditam aham ayāta-yāma-yajuṣ-kāma upasarāmīti ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **yata evaṁ-bhūtas tvam athātaḥ ha sphuṭam ayāta-yāmāny anyair yathāvad avijñātāni yajūṁṣi tat-kāmo’ham upasarāmi bhajāmi ||72||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **he bhagavann iti—tvam eva sākṣādbhagavāniti bhāvaḥ | tatra hetuḥ—tribhuvanagurubhir iti | brahmedranārāyaṇarudravanditaḥ sa nassadā yacchatu maṅgalaṁ raviḥ iti bhaviṣyokteḥ ||72||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** ayāta-yāmāni ūrjasvanti anyair jñātum aśakyānīty arthaḥ | yāni yajūṁṣi tat-kāmo’ham upasarāmi bhajāmi ||72||

**...**

**|| 12.6.73 ||**

**sūta uvāca—**

**evaṁ stutaḥ sa bhagavān vāji-rūpa-dharo raviḥ |**

**yajūṁṣy ayāta-yāmāni munaye’dāt prasāditaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **evaṁ stutaḥ prasāditaś ca ||73||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **vājī turaṅgas tadrūpadharo hariḥ sūryaḥ haririndro harirbhānurhariviṣṇurharirmarut ityabhidhānāt ||73||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

**...**

**|| 12.6.74 ||**

**yajurbhir akaroc chākhā daśa pañca śatair vibhuḥ |**

**jagṛhur vājasanyas tāḥ kāṇva-mādhyandinādayaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **pañcadaśa śākhāḥ yāḥ śatair aparimitair yajurbhir akarot | sa tair iti pāṭhe sa eṣa yājñavalkyas tair yajurbhir akarod iti | jagṛhur adhītavantaḥ | raviṇāśva-rūpeṇa vājebhyaḥ kesarebhyo vājena vegena vā sannyastās tyaktāḥ śākhā vājasanī-saṁjñās tāḥ śākhā iti vā ||74||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **vājasanyas tā ity atra prathame vyākhyāne, vā padāntasya [pā. 8.4.59] svarasya na-kāraḥ, vyākhyāntare anaci ca [pā. 8.4.47] iti dvitvam |_|_74||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** pañcadaśa śākhāḥ śatair aparimitair yajurbhir akarot | sa tair iti dantya-pāṭhe sa vibhur yājñavalkyas tair yajurbhir akarod iti | vājebhyaḥ sūryāśva-keśarebhyaḥ | samyag nayantīti vāja-saṁnyaḥ śākhās tāḥ, kaṇvādayo munayo jagṛhur adhītavantaḥ ||74||

**...**

**|| 12.6.75 ||**

**jaimineḥ sama-gasyāsīt sumantus tanayo muniḥ |**

**sutvāṁs tu tat-sutas tābhyām ekaikāṁ prāha saṁhitām ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **sāma-śākhā-vibhāgam āha—jaiminer iti | tat-sutaḥ sumantu-sutaḥ | tābhyāṁ putra-pautrābhyāṁ krameṇaikaikāṁ prāha ||75||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **sāma-veda-śākhā-vibhāgam āha—jaiminer iti | tat-sutaḥ sumantu-sutaḥ | jaiminis tābhyāṁ putra-pautrābhyāṁ krameṇaikaikāṁ prāha ||75||

**...**

** || 12.6.76-77 ||**

**sukarmā cāpi tac-chiṣyaḥ sāma-veda-taror mahān |**

**sahasra-saṁhitā-bhedaṁ cakre sāmnāṁ tato dvija ||**

**hiraṇyanābhaḥ kauśalyaḥ pauṣyañjiś ca sukarmaṇaḥ |**

**śiṣyau jagṛhatuś cānya āvantyo brahma-vittamaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tac-chiṣyo jaimineḥ śiṣyaḥ | mahān atimedhāvī | sahasra-saṁhitā-rūpaṁ bhedaṁ cakre | sāmnāṁ taṁ saṁhitā-bhedam | tatas tad anantaram | sukarmaṇaḥ śiṣya ekaḥ kauśalyo hiraṇyanābhaḥ pauṣyañjir nāmaikas tau jagṛhatuḥ | āvantyaś cānyas tasyaiva śiṣyaḥ so’pi jagrāha ||76-77||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ananusvārasakāre tu prathamā dvitīyārthe || kauśalyaḥ kośalāvāsī | āvantyo'vantībhavaḥ ||74-77||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **tac-chiṣyo jaimineḥ śiṣyaḥ sāma-veda-taroḥ sāma-veda-taru-sambandhī tac-chiṣyo mahān abhūd ity arthaḥ | ata eva sāmnām eṣa saṁhitā-bhedaṁ cakre hiraṇyanābhaḥ kauśalyaḥ kośala-deśodbhavaḥ pauṣyañjiś ca, sukarmaṇaḥ śiṣyo’nya āvantyaś ca, tac-chiṣyaḥ so’pi jagrāha ||76-77||

**...**

**|| 12.6.78 ||**

**udīcyāḥ sāma-gāḥ śiṣyā āsan pañca-śatāni vai |**

**pauṣyañjy-āvantyayoś cāpi tāṁś ca prācyān pracakṣate ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **pauṣyañjy-āvantyayor api ca-kārād dhiraṇyanābhasyāpi pañca-śatāni śiṣyā āsan | te tāvatīḥ śākhā yathāyathaṁ jagṛhuḥ | tān udīcyān sataḥ kālataḥ kāṁścit prācyāṁś ca pracakṣata ity arthaḥ | yathaivoktaṁ vaiṣṇave—


    udīcya-sāmagāḥ śiṣyās tasya pañca-śataṁ smṛtāḥ | 


    hiraṇyanābhāt tāvatyaḥ saṁhitā yair dvijottamaiḥ | 


    gṛhītās te’pi cocyante paṇḍitaiḥ prācya-sāmagāḥ || iti ||78||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ity artha iti—vakṣyamāṇavaiṣṇavavākyaprāmāṇyād iti bhāvaḥ | tad evāha—yathaivoktam iti | tasya hiraṇyanābhasya | tāvantyaḥ pañcaśatasaṅkhyākāḥ ||78||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** tatra hiraṇyanābhasya pañca-śatāni śiṣyā udīcyā āsan | pauṣyāñjāvantyayor api tāvanta eva śiṣyāḥ, tāṁs tu prācyān prācya-sāmagān, te ca te ca tāvatīḥ śākhā jagṛhuḥ ||78||

**...**

** || 12.6.79 ||**

**laugākṣir māṅgaliḥ kulyaḥ kuśīdaḥ kukṣir eva ca |**

**pauṣyañji-śiṣyā jagṛhuḥ saṁhitās te śataṁ śatam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **punar apy eteṣāṁ trayāṇāṁ sukarmaṇaḥ śiṣyāṇāṁ śiṣyāntaraiḥ śākhā-bāhulyaṁ darśayati—laugākṣir iti dvābhyām ||79||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **śatamṛtam iti pāṭhe ṛtaṁ satyam, svataḥ pramāṇamity arthaḥ ||79||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** punar api pauṣyañji-śiṣyā laugākṣyādayaḥ pañca ||79||

**...**

** || 12.6.80 ||**

**kṛto hiraṇyanābhasya catur-viṁśati saṁhitāḥ |**

**śiṣya ūce sva-śiṣyebhyaḥ śeṣā āvantya ātmavān ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kṛto nāma hiraṇyanābhasya śiṣyaḥ sva-śiṣyebhya ūce | śeṣā anyā api yāḥ prasiddhāḥ śākhās tā āvantyaḥ sva-śiṣyebhya ūca iti ||80||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ātmavān jñānī ||80||

iti śrīmad-bhāgavata-bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśe dvādaśa-skandhe ṣaṣṭho'dhyāyaḥ ||6||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** punar api hiraṇyanābhasya śiṣyaḥ kṛtaḥ | śeṣā anyā api yāḥ śākhāḥ prasiddhās tā āvantyaḥ sva-śiṣyebhya ūce ||80||

iti sārārtha-darśinyāṁ harṣiṇyāṁ bhakta-cetasām |

ṣaṣṭho’dhyāyo dvādaśasya saṅgataḥ saṅgataḥ satām ||*||

**...**


    iti śrīmad-bhāgavate mahā-purāṇe brahma-sūtra-bhāṣye pāramahaṁsyaṁ saṁhitāyāṁ vaiyāsikyāṁ dvādaśa-skandhe 


    veda-śākhā-praṇayanaṁ nāma 


    ṣaṣṭho’dhyāyaḥ |

|| 12.6 ||



**...**

**(12.7)**


### atha saptamo’dhyāyaḥ 


## purāṇa-lakṣaṇa-varṇanaṁ nāma

**|| 12.7.1 ||**

**sūta uvāca—**

**atharva-vit sumantuś ca śiṣyam adhyāpayat svakām |**

**saṁhitāṁ so’pi pathyāya veda-darśāya coktavān ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :**

saptame’tharva-vistāraḥ purāṇa-vyasanaṁ tataḥ |

purāṇa-lakṣaṇādīni phalaṁ bhāgavata-śruteḥ ||

krama-prāptam atharva-veda-vibhāgam āha, atharva-vid iti | śiṣyaṁ kabandha-nāmānam | svakāṁ svakīyāṁ saṁhitām | so’pi śiṣyo’pi tāṁ dvidhā vibhajya | tad uktaṁ vaiṣṇave—


    atharva-vedaṁ sa muniḥ sumantur amita-dyutiḥ | 


    śiṣyam adhyāpayām āsa kabandhaṁ so’pi ca dvidhā | 


    kṛtvā tu veda-darśāya tathā pathyāya dattavān || iti ||1||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **purāṇānāṁ vyasanaṁ vibhāgaḥ | bhāgavataśruter iti bhagavānvyāsas tasyeme śiṣyā bhāgavatāḥ pailādyāsteṣāṁ śrutiḥ śravaṇaṁ tasyāḥ phalam | yad vā, vedo nārāyaṇaḥ sākṣāt ity ukter bhagavato vedasyāyaṁ vibhāgo bhāgavatas tasya śruteḥ phalaṁ, taccādhyāyāntimaślokena brahmatejovivarddhanam iti vakṣyatyeva | vaiṣṇave viṣṇupurāṇe | tadetacchlokoktaṁ vṛttamuktam ||1||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **

saptamo’tharvāṇo vyāsaṁ purāṇasya ca tasya ca |

lakṣaṇāni daśa procya tasya saṅkhyā ca kathyate ||

śiṣyaṁ viṣṇu-purāṇoktaṁ kabandha-saṁjñam ||1||

 **...**

**|| 12.7.2 ||**

**śauklāyanir brahmabalir modoṣaḥ pippalāyaniḥ |**

**vedadarśasya śiṣyās te pathya-śiṣyān atho śṛṇu |**

**kumudaḥ śunako brahman jājaliś cāpy atharva-vit ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tatra veda-darśaḥ sva-saṁhitāṁ caturdhā vibhajya caturaḥ śiṣyān adhyapayām āsa | pathyaś ca tridhā vibhajya trīn ity āha sārdhena, śauklāyanir iti |

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.7.3 ||**

**babhruḥ śiṣyo’thāṅgirasaḥ saindhavāyana eva ca |**

**adhīyetāṁ saṁhite dve sāvarṇādyās tathāpare ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **aṅgirasaḥ śunakasya śiṣyo babhruḥ saindhavāyanaś ca | tad uktam—


    śunakas tu dvidhā kṛtvā dadāv ekāṁ tu babhrave | 


    dvitīyāṁ saṁhitāṁ prādāt saindhavāyana-saṁjñine || iti | 

sāvarṇyādyāḥ saindhavāyanādīnāṁ śiṣyāḥ ||3||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tatra dvayormadhye | he brahmann iti saṁbuddhiraktābhiprāyā ||2-3||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** aṅgirasaḥ śunakasya śiṣyo babhurḥ | sāvarṇādyāḥ saindhavāyanādīnāṁ śiṣyāḥ ||3||

 **...**

**|| 12.7.4 ||**

**nakṣatra-kalpaḥ śāntiś ca kaśyapāṅgirasādayaḥ |**

**ete ātharvaṇācāryāḥ śṛṇu paurāṇikān mune ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **nakṣatra-kalpaḥ śānti-kalpaś ceti dvau | tad uktam—


    nakṣatra-kalpo vedānāṁ saṁhitānāṁ tathaiva ca | 


    caturthaḥ syād āṅgirasaḥ śānti-kalpaś ca pañcamaḥ || iti | 

nakṣatra-kalpādīnāṁ kartāras tat tan nāmabhir ucyante ||4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tad uktamity-ādi vākyaṁ viṣṇupurāṇīyam eva | kalpaśabdasya pratyekaṁ sambandhaḥ | vedakalpaḥ, saṁhitākalpaḥ, āṅgirasakalpa iti | nakṣatrakalpo nakṣatrādipūjāvidhiḥ, vedakalpo vaitānikabrahmatvādividhiḥ, saṁhitākalpaḥ saṁhitāvidhiḥ, āṅgirasakalpo'bhicārādividhiḥ, śāntikalpo'śvagajādyaṣṭādaśamahāśāntyādividhir iti taṭṭīkā ca ||4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **pañcama-vedasya vibhāga-jñāpanārtham āha—śṛṇu paurāṇikān iti ||4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.7.5 ||**

**trayyāruṇiḥ kaśyapaś ca sāvarṇir akṛtavraṇaḥ |**

**vaiśampāyana-hārītau ṣaḍ vai paurāṇikā ime ||**

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ime iti buddhisannihitatvāt ||5||

 **...**

**|| 12.7.6 ||**

**adhīyanta vyāsa-śiṣyāt saṁhitāṁ mat-pitur mukhāt |**

**ekaikām aham eteṣāṁ śiṣyaḥ sarvāḥ samadhyagām ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **mat-pitur mukhād iti | prathamaṁ vyāsaḥ ṣaṭ-saṁhitāḥ kṛtvā mat-pitre romaharṣaṇāya prādāt | tasya ca mukhād ete trayyāruṇyādaya ekaikāṁ saṁhitām adhīyanta | eteṣāṁ ṣaṇṇāṁ śiṣyo’haṁ tāḥ sarvāḥ samadhītavān |
