———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ekaikām iti—tribhistribhirmilitvaikatvam | triṣaṭ iti vakṣyamāṇāt | tac ca—brāhma pādmaṁ vaiṣṇavam iti militvaikādirūpām | avāntarasaṁhitā tu kvacidekā, yathā śrī-bhāgavatasya paramahaṁsasaṁhitātvam, kvacidekaikasyaiva vibhāgaśaḥ| yathā—skāndasya sanatkumāraproktasaṁhitānāmādikā, śrī-bhāgavatasya śrīśukāttu paścādvyaktiḥ sūryādeva yajurbhāgasya vājasaneyasyādau vyaktatvāt ||6||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **ekaikām iti tribhis tribhir militvaikatvaṁ triṣaḍ iti vakṣyamāṇāt | tac ca brāhmaṁ pādmaṁ vaiṣṇavam [bhā.pu. 12.7.23] iti militvaikety-ādi-kramāt | avāntara-saṁhitā tu kvacid ekā, yathā śrī-bhāgavatasya paramahaṁsa-saṁhitātvam | kvacid ekaikasyaiva vibhāgaśaḥ, yathā skāndasya sanatkumāra-prokta-saṁhitā-nāmādikā | ekaikām aham ity atra śrī-śukāt tu śrī-bhāgavatasya camatkāra-vaiśiṣṭyatayā[^55] paścād-vyaktiḥ sūryād eva yajur-bhāgasya vājasaneyasya jñeyam ||6||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** mat-pitū romaharṣaṇasya | eteṣāṁ ṣaṇṇām apy ahaṁ śiṣyāḥ ||6||

 **...**

**|| 12.7.7 ||**

**kaśyapo’haṁ ca sāvarṇī rāma-śiṣyo’kṛtavraṇaḥ |**

**adhīmahi vyāsa-śiṣyāc catvāro mūla-saṁhitāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **rāma-śiṣyo’kṛtavraṇaḥ | evaṁ catvāro vayam | mūla-saṁhitā ity anena tataḥ saṁhitā-bāhulyaṁ sūcitam |

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **kaśyapo'hamugraśravāḥ sāvarṇirakṛtavraṇaścaturtha ete catvāro vayamity arthaḥ | mūlatvameṣām itihāsāpekṣayā jñeyam aṣṭādaśa purāṇāni kṛtvāsatyavatīsutaḥ | bhārataṁ kṛtavānpaścāt iti mātsyāt | 


    brāhmī bhāgavatī śaivī vaiṣṇavī ca prakīrtitāḥ | 


    catasraḥ saṁhitāḥ puṇyā dharmakāmārthamokṣadāḥ || iti | 

kvacitpañcoktāḥ | 


    brahmaṇaḥ syuḥ śivasyāpi prahlādasyāpi saṁhitāḥ | 


    gautamasya kumārasya saṁhitāḥ pañca varṇitāḥ || 

kvacit ṣaḍuktāḥ—


    ādyā sanatkumāroktā dvitīyā sūtasaṁhitā | 


    tṛtīyā śāṅkarī viprāścaturthī vaiṣṇavī tathā | 


    tatparā saṁhitā brāhmī saurāntyā parikīrtitā | 


    anyā api saṁhitās tu vijñeyā muninirmitāḥ | 


    kauśikī saṁhitā mukhyā vāsiṣṭhī mānavī tathā | 


    gargādimā ca sā pārāśarī vaiyāsakī tathā | 


    hanumatsaṁhitā jñeyā tathā saudarśanī matā | 

iti sarvārthacintāmaṇyuktaḥ | vyāsaśiṣyānmatpitū romaharṣaṇāt ||7||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **mūlasaṁhitā iti tv itihāsaviśeṣāpekṣayā jñeyaṁ bahūnāmanyeṣām itihāsānāṁ mūlatvāt mūlam idaṁ ca pariśeṣeṇa lakṣyate “itihāsapurāṇānāṁ pitā me romaharṣaṇaḥ” ity-ukteḥ te ca mahābhāratādyāḥ śṛṇu paurāṇikāniti tūpalakṣaṇatayoktam |

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** vyāsa-śiṣyāt lomaharṣaṇāt ||7||

 **...**

**|| 12.7.8 ||**

**purāṇa-lakṣaṇaṁ brahman brahmarṣibhir nirūpitam |**

**śṛṇuṣva buddhim āśritya veda-śāstrānusārataḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **śuka-parīkṣit-saṁvāde nirūpitam api purāṇa-lakṣaṇaṁ tad-bheda-kathanāya darśayati, purāṇeti ||8||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **veda eva śāstraṁ tadanusārato yathā vede purāṇalakṣaṇamuktaṁ tadanatilandhyaiveha varṇayāmīty arthaḥ ||8||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** brahmarṣibhiḥ śrī-śuka-vacanair upakrame yad uktaṁ prāyeṇa tad evopasaṁhāre’py ucyate ||8||

 **...**

**|| 12.7.9-10 ||**

**sargo’syātha visargaś ca vṛtti-rakṣāntarāṇi ca |**

**vaṁśo vaṁśānucaritaṁ saṁsthā hetur apāśrayaḥ ||**

**daśabhir lakṣaṇair yuktaṁ purāṇaṁ tad-vido viduḥ |**

**kecit pañca-vidhaṁ brahma mahad-alpa-vyavasthayā ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **asya viśvasya “atra sargo visargaś ca sthānaṁ poṣaṇam ūtayaḥ | manvantareśānukathā nirodho muktir āśrayaḥ |” ity atrokte sthāna-poṣaṇe vṛtti-rakṣā-śabdābhyām ucyete | antarāṇi manvantarāṇi vaṁśo vaṁśyānucaritam itīśānukathāḥ | saṁsthā nirodhaḥ | anenaivātyantika-laya-rūpā muktir apy uktā | hetu-śabdena jīvāśraya-vāsanā-śabda-vācyā ūtayo gṛhītāḥ |

daśabhir etair lakṣaṇair arthair yuktaṁ mahā-purāṇaṁ viduḥ | kecit pañca-vidham, “sargaś ca pratisargaś ca vaṁśo manvantarāṇi ca | vaṁśānucaritaṁ ceti purāṇaṁ pañca-lakṣaṇam |” iti | mahat-purāṇam alpaṁ ceti vyavasthayā yatra daśāpi lakṣaṇāni pṛthak pṛthaṅ nirūpyante tan mahā-purāṇam | yatra tv anyeṣāṁ pañcasv evāntarbhāvasya vivakṣā tad alpam iti vyavasthayety arthaḥ |

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **poṣaṇaṁ tadanugrahaḥ iti pūrvalakṣitaṁ poṣaṇamevātra rakṣāśabdenocyate, tāṁ vyācaṣṭe || ity arthaḥ iti—antarbhāvas tu svabuddhyaiva sarge rakṣāyāḥ, pratisarge saṁsthāyā ityevaṁ rītyā yathāyathamanusandheyam iti vaṁśavaṁśānucaritayorīśakathāyāmantarbhāvam iti bhāvaḥ ||9-10||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **sargo’syety ādikaṁ dvitīya-skandha [bhā.pu. 2.10.1-7] eva vyākhyātam | asya śrī-bhāgavatasya mahā-purāṇatva-vyañjaka-lakṣaṇaṁ prakārāntareṇa ca vadann api tasyaivāśrayatvam āha dvayena—sarga iti | antarāṇi manvantarāṇi | pañca-vidham—


    sargaś ca pratisargaś ca vaṁśo manvantarāṇi ca |


    vaṁśānucaritaṁ ceti purāṇaṁ pañca-lakṣaṇam || iti kecid vadanti ||[^56]

sa ca mata-bhedo mahad-alpa-vyavasthayā mahā-purāṇam alpa-purāṇam iti bhinnādhikaraṇatvena | yadyapi viṣṇu-purāṇādāv api daśāpi tāni lakṣyante, tathāpi pañcānām eva prādhānyenoktatvād alpatvam | atra daśānām arthānāṁ skandheṣu yathā-kramaṁ praveśo na vivakṣitaḥ, teṣāṁ dvādaśa-saṅkhyatvāt | dvitīya-skandhoktānāṁ teṣāṁ tṛtīyādiṣu yathā-saṅkhyaṁ na samāveśaḥ | nirodhādīnāṁ daśamādiṣv aṣṭama-varjam | anyeṣām apy anyeṣu yathokta-lakṣaṇatayā samāveśanāśakyatvād eva | tad uktaṁ śrī-svāmibhir eva—


    daśame kṛṣṇa-sat-kīrti-vitānāyopavarṇyate |


    dharma-glāni-nimittas tu nirodho duṣṭa-bhūbhujām |


    prākṛtādi-caturdhā yo nirodhaḥ sa tu varṇitaḥ || iti |

ato’tra skandhe śrī-kṛṣṇa-rūpasyāśrayasyaiva varṇana-prādhānyaṁ tair vivakṣitam | uktaṁ ca svayam eva—daśame daśamaṁ lakṣyam āśritāśraya-vigraham iti | evam anyatrāpy unneyam | ataḥ prāyaśaḥ sarve’rthāḥ sarveṣv eva skandheṣu guṇatvena vā mukhyatvena vā nirūpyanta ity eva teṣām abhimatam | śrutenārthena cāñjasā [bhā.pu. 2.10.2] ity atra ca tathaiva pratipannaṁ sarvatra tat-tat-sambhavāt | tataś ca prathama-dvitīyayor api mahā-purāṇatāyāṁ praveśaḥ syāt | tasmāt kramo na gṛhītaḥ ||9-10|| [tattva-sandarbhaḥ 61]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** kecit pañca-vidham iti | 


    sargaś ca pratisargaś ca vaṁśo manvantarāṇi ca |


    vaṁśānucaritaṁ ceti purāṇaṁ pañca-lakṣaṇam || iti |

mahat alpaṁ ceti vyavasthayā yatra daśāpi lakṣaṇāni pṛthaṅ nirūpyante tan mahā-purāṇaṁ, yatra tv anyeṣāṁ pañcasv antarbhāvo vivakṣitas tad alpam iti vyavasthayety arthaḥ ||9-10||

 **...**

**|| 12.7.11 ||**

**avyākṛta-guṇa-kṣobhān mahatas tri-vṛto’hamaḥ |**

**bhūta-sūkṣmendriyārthānāṁ sambhavaḥ sarga ucyate ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **sargādi-lakṣaṇāni vyācaṣṭe, avyākṛtety-ādinā | avyākṛtasya pradhānasya guṇānāṁ kṣobhādyo mahāṁs tasmād yas tri-vṛd-ahaṅkāras tasmād bhūta-mātrāṇāṁ sukṣmāṇām indriyāṇāṁ ca tad-arthānāṁ ca sthūlānāṁ devatānāṁ ca saṁbhavaḥ sargaḥ kāraṇa-sṛṣṭi-sarga ity arthaḥ | ucyata iti yathā’pekṣam uttaratrāpy anuṣaṅgaḥ |

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ity artha iti—visargasya pṛthagupādānātsargapadena kāraṇasṛṣṭirevātra jñeyeti bhāvaḥ ||11||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **atha sargādīnāṁ lakṣaṇam āha—avyākṛteti | pradhāna-guṇa-kṣobhān mahān, tasmāt triguṇo’haṅkāraḥ | tasmād bhūta-mātrāṇāṁ bhūta-sūkṣmāṇām indriyāṇāṁ ca, sthūla-bhūtānāṁ ca, tad-upalakṣita-tad-devatānāṁ ca sambhavaḥ sargaḥ | kāraṇa-sṛṣṭiḥ sarga ity arthaḥ ||11|| [tattva-sandarbhaḥ 62]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** atra sargaṁ vyācaṣṭe | avyākṛtasya pradhānasya guṇānāṁ kṣobhāt yo mahān tasmāt | yas tri-bṛhad-ahaṅkārs tasmāt bhūta-mātrādīnāṁ sambhavaḥ sargaḥ | atrārtha-śabdena devatā jñeyāḥ | kāraṇa-sṛṣṭiḥ sarga ity arthaḥ | ucyata iti yathāpekṣam uttaratrāpy ānuṣaṅgaḥ ||11||

 **...**

**|| 12.7.12 ||**

**puruṣānugṛhītānām eteṣāṁ vāsanā-mayaḥ |**

**visargo’yaṁ samāhāro bījād bījaṁ carācaram ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** visargaṁ vyācaṣṭe | puruṣeṇeśvareṇānugṛhītānām eteṣāṁ mahad-ādīnām | pūrva-karma-vāsanā-pradhāno’yaṁ samāhāraḥ kārya-bhūtaś carācara-prāṇi-rūpo bījād bījam iva pravāhāpanno visarga ucyate ity arthaḥ ||12||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ity artha iti—viśiṣṭaḥ sargo visarga iti bhāvaḥ ||12||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **puruṣeti | puruṣaḥ paramātmā | eteṣāṁ mahad-ādīnāṁ, jīvasya pūrva-karma-vāsanā-pradhāno’yaṁ samāhāraḥ | kārya-bhūtaś carācara-prāṇi-rūpo bījād bījam iva pravāhāpanno visarga ucyate | vyaṣṭi-sṛṣṭi-visarga ity arthaḥ | anenotir apy uktā ||12|| [tattva-sandarbhaḥ 62]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** visargaṁ vyācaṣṭe | puruṣeṇeśvareṇānugṛhītānām eteṣāṁ yaḥ samāhāraḥ kārya-bhūtaḥ samaṣṭi-vyaṣṭi-jīvopādhirūpaḥ | kīdṛśaḥ ? vāsanā-mayaḥ sadasad-vāsanā-pradhānaḥ sa visargaḥ | tatra carācaraṁ jaṅgama-sthāvarātmakaṁ jagad idaṁ bījād bījam iva pravāhāpannaṁ bhavati | ūtayaḥ karma-vāsanā iti pūrva-lakṣitā yā ūtiḥ sātra visarga evāntarbhāvitā ||12||

 **...**

**|| 12.7.13 ||**

**vṛttir bhūtāni bhūtānāṁ carāṇām acarāṇi ca |**

**kṛtā svena nṛṇāṁ tatra kāmāc codanayāpi vā ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **carāṇāṁ bhūtānāṁ sāmānyato’carāṇi, ca-kārāc carāṇi ca vṛttiḥ | tatra nṝṇāṁ svena svabhāvena kāmāc codanayāpi vā yā niyatā vṛttir jīvikā kṛtā, sā vṛttir ucyata ity arthaḥ ||13||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tatra sarvajīveṣu | svabhāvena brīhyādīni kāmanayā, phalādīni codanayā, vidhinā puroḍāśādīni | ity artha iti—na tu sāmānyato'bhakṣyabhakṣaṇamapīti bhāvaḥ | tatra kāmyā vṛttirgārhyā, māṁsāśanalaśunapalāḍvādiṣv api tadguṇaśravaṇena kāmanotpatteḥ ||13||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **vṛttir iti | carāṇāṁ bhūtānāṁ sāmānyato’carāṇi, ca-kārāc carāṇi ca, kāmād vṛttiḥ | tatra tu nṝṇāṁ svena svabhāvena kāmāc codanayāpi vā yā niyatā vṛttir jīvikā kṛtā, sā vṛttir ucyata ity arthaḥ ||13|| [tattva-sandarbhaḥ 62]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** pūrvoktaṁ sthānaṁ pālanam evātra vṛtti-śabdenocyate | tāṁ vyācaṣṭe vṛttir iti | carāṇāṁ bhūtānāṁ sāmānyato’carāṇi ca kāmād vṛttiḥ | tatra nṝṇāṁ svena svabhāvena kāmāc codanayāpi vā yā niyatā vṛttir jīvikā kṛtā, sā vṛttir ucyata ity arthaḥ | teṣāṁ carācarāṇās tv āśrayaḥ sarvaiva pṛthvīti vṛtti-prasaṅga eva bhūgoaca-cakraṁ pañcama-skandhe nirūpitam ||13||

 **...**

**|| 12.7.14 ||**

**rakṣācyutāvatārehā viśvasyānu yuge yuge |**

**tiryaṅ-martyarṣi-deveṣu hanyante yais trayī-dviṣaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** tiryaṅ-martyarṣi-deveṣu ye’cyutāvatārās teṣām īhā līlā sā viśvasya rakṣo’cyuta ity arthaḥ | yair avatārair iti samāsān niṣkṛṣya kathañcit sambandhaḥ | trayī-dviṣo daityāḥ ||14||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ity artha iti—na tu gavāśvādirakṣaṇamātram eva rakṣāpadārtha iti bhāvaḥ | avatārehā'vatārakāraṇaṁ saiva rakṣā | kuta ityata āha—yair iti | samāsānniṣkṛtya kathañcidagatyā | yathā—bhīṣmadroṇapramukhataḥ sarveṣāṁ ca mahīkṣitām ityatra pramukhata ityasya vivakṣāvaśānmahīkṣitāmityanena sambandhas tadvadatrāpi | yad vā, yasyaite rājamātaṅgās tasyaivaite turaṅgamāḥ iti buddhisthagrāhakatvam api tyadādīnām iti jñeyam | hanyata iti—duṣṭanigrahātsvabhaktarakṣaṇam eva rakṣetyāgatam | upalakṣaṇametadanyadāpi mahābhayātsvabhaktarakṣaṇaṁ rakṣocyate'ta eva ṣaṣṭhe'jāmilādibhaktānāṁ rakṣoktā ||14||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **rakṣeti | yair avatāraiḥ | aneneśa-kathā | sthānaṁ poṣaṇaṁ ceti trayam uktam ||14|| [tattva-sandarbhaḥ 62]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **poṣaṇaṁ tad-anugraha iti pūrva-lakṣitaṁ poṣaṇam evātra rakṣā-śabdenocyate | tāṁ vyācaṣṭe rakṣeti | tiryag-ādiṣu yācyutasyāvatārehā avatāra-kāraṇaṁ saiva rakṣā, kuta ity ata āha yair avatārais trayī-dviṣo hanyante ity ato duṣṭa-nigrahāt svabhakta-rakṣaṇam eva rakṣety artha āyātaḥ | upalakṣaṇam etad anyadāpi mahā-bhayāt svabhakta-rakṣaṇaṁ rakṣocyate | ata eva ṣaṣṭhe’jāmilādi-bhaktānāṁ rakṣoktā ||14||

 **...**

**|| 12.7.15 ||**

**manvantaraṁ manur devā manu-putrāḥ sureśvarāḥ |**

**ṛṣayo’ṁśāvatārāś ca hareḥ ṣaḍ-vidham ucyate ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** ṣaḍ-vidhaṁ manvantaram ucyate | ṣaḍvidhatvam evāha—manur iti |manvādayaḥ ṣaḍ ete vargāḥ sva-svādhikāreṇa, yadā pravartante tan manvantaram ity arthaḥ ||15||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ity artha iti—eṣāṁ pravṛttikāla eva manvantaram iti bhāvaḥ ||15||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **manvantaram iti | manv-ādy-ācaraṇa-kathanena sad-dharma evātra vivakṣita ity arthaḥ | tataś ca prāktana-granthenaikārthyam ||15|| [tattva-sandarbhaḥ 62]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **manvantarāṇi sad-dharma iti pūrva-lakṣitam | manvantaraṁ vyācaṣṭe manvantaram iti | vidadhati sva-sva-kṛtyaṁ kurvantīti vidhā manvādayas te ṣaṭ, yatra tat ṣaḍ-vidham ity arthaḥ | manvādayaḥ ṣaḍ sva-svādhikāreṇa, yatra pravartante tan manvantaram ity arthaḥ ||15||

 **...**

**|| 12.7.16 ||**

**rājñāṁ brahma-prasūtānāṁ vaṁśas trai-kāliko’nvayaḥ |**

**vaṁśānucaritaṁ teṣāṁ vṛttaṁ vaṁśa-dharāś ca ye ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** vaṁśam āha—rājñām iti | brahmaṇaḥ sakāśāt prasūtir yeṣāṁ śuddhānām ity arthaḥ | tesām anvayo vaṁśaḥ | teṣāṁ vṛttam | ye ca tad-vaṁśadharās teṣāṁ ca vṛttaṁ vaṁśānucaritam ucyate ||16||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : _ity artha_** iti—idaṁ cakāreṇa jñeyam iti bhāvaḥ | vṛttaṁ śīlam | tadvaṁśadharāḥ priyavratadhruvapṛthvādayaḥ ||16||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **brahma-prasūtānāṁ brahmata ārabdhānām ity arthaḥ | teṣāṁ rājñāṁ ye ca vaṁśa-dharās teṣāṁ vṛttaṁ vaṁśyānucaritam ||16|| [tattva-sandarbhaḥ 62]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **vaṁśaṁ vyācaṣṭe—rājñām iti | brahmaṇaḥ sakāśāt prasūtir yeṣāṁ teṣām anvayo vaṁśaḥ | vaṁśānucaritaṁ vyācaṣṭe—teṣāṁ madhye ye vaṁśa-dharāḥ prasiddhāḥ priyavrata-dhruva-pṛthv-ādayas teṣāṁ vṛttaṁ caritraṁ vaṁśānucaritam ucyate | etad-dvayaṁ pūrvam īśānukathāyām evāntarbhāvitam ||16||

 **...**

**|| 12.7.17 ||**

**naimittikaḥ prākṛtiko nitya ātyantiko layaḥ |**

**saṁstheti kavibhiḥ proktaś caturdhāsya svabhāvataḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **asya viśvasya | svabhāvato māyāto niṣpannasya | yad vā, māyāto yaś catur-vidho laya iti ||17||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **svasyaiva śaktirūpeṇa bhavanaṁ svabhāvo māyā na kevalaṁ māyāto laya eva kintu pralayo'pīty āha—yadveti | avyaktādīni bhūtāni vyaktamadhyāni bhārata | avyaktānidhanānyeva iti śrīmukhokteḥ ||17||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **asya parameśvarasya | svabhāvato māyākhya-svābhāvika-śaktitaḥ | ātyantika ity anena muktir apy atra praveśitā ||17|| [tattva-sandarbhaḥ 63]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** pūrvokta-nirodha-śabda-vācyāṁ saṁsthāṁ vyācaṣṭe | naimittika iti | asya viśvasya svabhāvataḥ svasya bhāveṣu kāraṇeṣu pṛthivy-ādi-tattveṣu krameṇa layaḥ saṁsthocyate ||17||

 **...**

**|| 12.7.18 ||**

**hetur jīvo’sya sargāder avidyā-karma-kārakaḥ |**

**yaṁ cānuśāyinaṁ prāhur avyākṛtam utāpare ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : asya** jagataḥ **sargāder hetur** nimittaṁ jīvaḥ, so’tra hetur ucyata ity arthaḥ | tasya nimittatām āha—**avidyayā karma-kārakaḥ** karma-kartā | jīvādṛṣṭa-prayuktatvād viśva-sargādeḥ, sa tu tatra hetur ity arthaḥ | nanv **anuśayī** nimittam iti kecit, **avyākṛtam** ity **apare**, tatrāha—**yam** iti | caitanya-prādhānyenānuśayinam, upādhi-prādhānya-vivakṣayāvyākṛtam ||18||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ity artha iti—jīva eva svakarmadvārā sṛṣṭikāraṇam iti bhāvaḥ | tasya jīvasya | ity artha iti— jīvasamudāyasukhaduḥkhaprāptaye taṁ hetuṁ kṛtvā jagataḥ sṛṣṭyādikamastīti bhāvaḥ | atrāśaṅkate—nanv iti | yaṁ jīvam | upādhiḥ prakṛtiḥ | cakravartikārastu—asya sargādejīvaḥ kāraṇaṁ sa cāvidyayā karma kartā jīvārtham eva bhagavatā viśvasya kṛtatvājjīvo nimittam iti bhāvaḥ | ata eva yamanuśayinaṁ māyikopādhimanuśayānaṁ māyikaśarīravaramevaike prāhuḥ | aparabhaktāstu—āvidyakakarmakartāraṁ jīvaṁ sādhusaṅgavaśādbhaktimārgasthatve sati avyākṛtaṁ cinmayapārṣadaśarīravantamapyāhuḥ | apyarthe ut śabdaḥ | tad-uktaṁ nāradena—śuddhāṁ bhāgavatī tanum | ārabdhakarmanirvāṇo nyapatatpāñcabhautikaḥ iti | vedastavārambhepi—


    buddhīndriyamanaḥprāṇāñjanānāmasṛjatprabhuḥ | 


    mātrārthaṁ ca bhavārthaś ca ātmane kalpanāya ca || iti | 

ātmane'kalpanāya buddhīndriyamanaḥprāṇānsaṁprāpayitum iti tatrārthaḥ | etanmata eva navamaṁ lakṣaṇaṁ pūrvatroktam | muktirhitvānyathā rūpaṁ svarūpeṇa vyavasthitiḥ iti viśeṣeṇa ciddhanaśarīratvenāvasthitir iti tatra vyākhyeti viśvanāthaḥ ||18||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : hetur** nimittam | **asya** viśvasya | yato’yam **avidyayā karma-kārakaḥ** | **yam** eva hetuṁ kecic caitanya-prādhānen**ānuśayinaṁ** karma-vāsanā-yuktaṁ jīvaṁ **prāhuḥ** | **apare** upādhi-prādhānyen**āvyākṛtaṁ** pradhānam ||18|| [tattva-sandarbha 63]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** hetuṁ vyācaṣṭe—**asya** jagataḥ **sargāder hetur** nimittaṁ **jīvaḥ** | sa **cāvidyā-karma-kārakaḥ** avidyayā karma-kartā | jīvārtham eva bhagavatā viśvasya sargādeḥ kṛtatvāj jīvo nimittam iti bhāvaḥ | ata eva **yam anuśayinaṁ** māyikopādhim anuśayānaṁ māyika-śarīravantam evaike prāhuḥ | **apare** bhaktās tu āvidyaka-karma-kartāraṁ jīvaṁ sādhu-saṅga-vaśāt bhakti-mārga-sthatve sati **avyākṛtam** aprākṛtaṁ cinmaya-pārṣada-śarīravantam **api prāhuḥ** | apy-arthe **uta**-śabdaḥ | 

yad uktaṁ nāradena—


    prayujyamāne mayi tāṁ śuddhāṁ bhāgavatīṁ tanum |


    ārabdha-karma-nirvāṇo nyapatat pāñca-bhautikaḥ || [bhā.pu. 1.6.29] iti |

ata evoktaṁ veda-stavārambhe—


    buddhīndriya-manaḥ-prāṇān janānām asṛjat prabhuḥ |


    mātrārthaṁ ca bhavārthaṁ ca ātmane’kalpanāya ca || [bhā.pu. 10.87.2] iti |

ātmane kalpanāya buddhīndriya-manaḥ-prāṇān samprāpayitum iti tatrārthaḥ | etan-mata eva navamaṁ lakṣaṇaṁ pūrvatroktam—muktir hitvānyathā-rūpaṁ [bhā.pu. 2.10.6] iti viśeṣeṇa cid-ghana-śarīratvenāvasthitir iti tatra vyākhyā ||18||

 **...**

**|| 12.7.19 ||**

**vyatirekānvayo yasya jāgrat-svapna-suṣuptiṣu |**

**māyā-mayeṣu tad brahma jīva-vṛttiṣv apāśrayaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** apāśrayam āha—vyatireketi | jāgrad-ādiṣv avasthāsu jīvatayā vartanta iti jīva-vṛttayo viśva-taijasa-prājñās teṣu māyā-mayeṣu sākṣitayānvayaḥ samādhy-ādau ca vyatireko yasya tad brahma saṁsāra-pratīti-bādhayor adhiṣṭhānāvadhi-bhūtam apāśraya ucyata ity arthaḥ ||19||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **samādhyāhāvidādinā mūrchāgrahaḥ | samādhau svarūpāvasthānena mūrchāyāṁ pratītyabhāvena ca vyatirekaḥ ||19||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **śrī-bādarāyaṇa-samādhi-labdhārtha-virodhād atra ca jīva-śuddha-svarūpam evāśrayatvena na vyākhyāyate, kintv ayam evārthaḥ—jāgrad-ādiṣv avasthāsu, māyā-mayeṣu māyā-śakti-kalpiteṣu mahad-ādi-dravyeṣu ca jīva-vṛttiṣu śuddha-jīva-svarūpāsu sva-śakti-vṛttiṣu ca kevala-svarūpeṇa vyatirekaḥ parama-sākṣitayānvayaś ca yasya, tad brahma cāpāśraya ucyate | tasmād apakṛṣṭānām anyeṣāṁ samastānām āśraya ity arthaḥ | jīvānāṁ vṛttiṣu—śuddha-svarūpatayā sopādhitayā ca vartaneṣu sthitiṣv apāśrayaḥ sarvam atikramyāśraya ity arthaḥ | apa ity etat khalu varjane, varjanaṁ cātikrame paryavasyatīti |_|_19|| [tattva-sandarbha 63]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **apāśrayaṁ vyācaṣṭe—vyatireketi | jāgrat-svapna-suṣuptiṣv avasthāsu | tathā māyā-mayeṣu sarveṣv eva padārtheṣu yasya hetutayā anvayaḥ | tebhyo vyatirekaś ca | tad brahma apāśraya ucyate ||19||

 **...**

**|| 12.7.20-21 ||**

**padārtheṣu yathā dravyaṁ san-mātraṁ rūpa-nāmasu |**

**bījādi-pañcatāntāsu hy avasthāsu yutāyutam ||**

**virameta yadā cittaṁ hitvā vṛtti-trayaṁ svayam |**

**yogena vā tadātmānaṁ vedehāya nivartate ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** etad eva sadṛṣṭāntaṁ prapañcayati—padārtheṣu ghaṭādiṣu dravyaṁ mṛd-ādi yathā yutam anvitam ayutaṁ ca bahir apy avasthānāt | rūpa-nāmasu ca san-mātraṁ sattā-mātraṁ yathā | evaṁ bījaṁ garbhādhānam ādir yāsāṁ pañcatānto yāsāṁ tāsu dehāvasthāsu navasv apy adhiṣṭhānatvena sākṣitvena ca yutam ayutaṁ ca yat tad apāśraya iti ||20||

evaṁ daśāpi lakṣaṇāni vyākhyāya—daśamasya viṣuddhy-arthaṁ navānām iha lakṣaṇam | varṇayanti mahātmanaḥ [bhā.pu. 2.10.2] iti yad uktaṁ, tad āha—virameteti | yadā sargādīnāṁ māyāmayatvānusandhānena vāmadevāder iva svayam eva cittaṁ virameta | ihaivānuṣṭhitena yogena vā devahūty-ādivat | tadā vikṣepābhāvād ātmānaṁ veda | tadā cāvidyā-nivṛtter īhāyāḥ saṁsāra-rūpāyā nivartata ity arthaḥ ||21||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **etad evānvayavyatirekatvam eva | rūpanāmasv iti—samīpasthe merurayamity ukte merurūpe sattānvayaḥ, dūrasthena merurity ukte tu merudarśanābhāvānmerunāmnyeva sattānvayaḥ | yad vā, rūpanāmayukteṣu padārtheṣv iti yojyam | navāvasthāstu—


    niṣekagarbhajanmāni bālyakaiśorayauvanam | 


    vayomadhyaṁ jarā mṛtyurityavasthāstanornava || 

ityekādaśaskandhe svayaṁ bhagavataivoktāḥ | 

adhiṣṭhānatvena yutaṁ sākṣitvenāyutam || vṛttitrayaṁ jāgradāditrayam | vāmadeva ṛṣiviśeṣaḥ | ādinā dattātreyādigrahaḥ | dvitīyādināsuryādigrahaḥ | ity artha iti—īhānivṛtter eva mokṣatvāt—


    yadā sarve pramucyante kāmā ye'sya hṛdi śritāḥ | 


    atha martyo'mṛto'bhavatyatra brahma samaśnute || 

iti śruterayaṁ bhāvaḥ ||20-21||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tad evam apāśrayābhivyakti-dvāra-bhūtaṁ hetu-śabda-vyapadiṣṭasya jīvasya śuddha-svarūpa-jñānam āha dvābhyām—padārtheṣu iti | rūpa-nāmātmakeṣu padārtheṣu ghaṭādiṣu yathā dravyaṁ pṛthivyādi yutam ayutaṁ ca bhavati | kārya-dṛṣṭiṁ vināpy upalambhāt | tathā tan-mātraṁ śuddhaṁ jīva-caitanya-mātraṁ vastu garbhādhānādi-pañcatāntāsu navasv apy avasthāsv avidyayā yutaṁ svatas tv ayutam iti śuddham ātmānam itthaṁ jñātvā nirviṇṇaḥ sann apāśrayānusandhāna-yogyo bhavatīty āha virameteti | vṛtti-trayaṁ jāgrat-svapna-suṣupti-rūpam | ātmānaṁ paramātmānam | svayaṁ vāsudevāder iva māyāmayatvānusandhānena deva tyāder ivāniṣṭhitena yogena vā | tataś cehāyās tad-anuśīlana-vyatirikta-ceṣṭāyāḥ || [tattva-sandarbha 63]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** etad eva sa-dṛṣṭāntaṁ prapañcayati | padārtheṣu ghaṭādiṣu dravyaṁ mṛdādi yathā yutam anvitaṁ, ayuktaṁ ca bahir-avasthānāt | rūpa-nāmasu vācya-vācaka-vastuṣu yathā tan-mātraṁ gandhādikaṁ ca | tathaiva bījādi-pañcatās tāsu bījaṁ garbhādhānam ādir yāsāṁ pañcatā anto yāsāṁ tāsu dehāvasthāsu adhiṣṭhitatvena sākṣitvena ca yutam ayutaṁ ca yat tad apāśrayaḥ ||20||

evaṁ daśa-lakṣaṇāni vyākhyāyedānīṁ—daśamasya viṣuddhy-arthaṁ navānām iha lakṣaṇam | varṇayanti mahātmanaḥ [bhā.pu. 2.10.2] iti yad uktaṁ tad āha—virameteti | jarayaty āśu yā koṣaṁ nigīrṇam analo yathā [bhā.pu. 3.25.33] iti nyāyena kevalayā śravaṇa-kīrtanādi-bhaktyaiva svayam eva vṛtti-trayaṁ hitvā cittaṁ svayam eva virameta guṇebhyo virataṁ syāt | bhagavac-caraṇāravinde viśeṣeṇa rameta vā | yogenāṣṭāṅga-yogena vā virameta cittaṁ nirvāṇaṁ syāt, tadā ātmānaṁ veda | paramātmānam anubhavanti, tadaiva īhāyā vaiṣayikāt kāmāt nivartate ||21||

 **...**

**|| 12.7.22 ||**

**evaṁ-lakṣaṇa-lakṣyāṇi purāṇāni purā-vidaḥ |**

**munayo’ṣṭādaśa prāhuḥ kṣullakāni mahānti ca ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **purāṇa-vibhāga-prastāvena tal-lakṣaṇādi-prāsaṅgikam uktvā prastutam āha, evaṁ-vidhair lakṣaṇair lakṣyāṇi ||22||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** _na vyākhyātam._

 **...**

**|| 12.7.23-24 ||**

**brāhmaṁ pādmaṁ vaiṣṇavaṁ ca śaivaṁ laiṅgaṁ sa-gāruḍam |**

**nāradīyaṁ bhāgavatam āgneyaṁ skānda-saṁjñitam ||**

**bhaviṣyaṁ brahma-vaivartaṁ mārkaṇḍeyaṁ sa-vāmanam |**

**vārāhaṁ mātsyaṁ kaurmaṁ ca brahmāṇḍākhyam iti tri-ṣaṭ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **purāvidaḥ atītānāgatavido vyāsādayo munayaḥ | kṣullakāni ślokasaṅkhyā parimitāni na tvarthataḥ, kānicidarthataḥ śabdataḥ phalataś ca mahānti || trirāvṛttāḥ ṣaṭ triṣaṭ | śaive tu—


    brāhmaṁ purāṇaṁ tatrādyaṁ saṁhitāyāṁ vibhūṣitam | 


    ślokānāṁ daśasāhasraṁ nānā puṇyakathāyutam | 


    pādmaṁ dvitīyaṁ kathitaṁ tṛtīyaṁ vaiṣṇavaṁ smṛtam | 


    caturthaṁ vāyunā proktaṁ vāyavīyam iti smṛtam | 


    tato bhāgavataṁ proktaṁ bhāgadvayavibhūṣitama | 


    caturbhiḥ parvabhiḥ proktaṁ bhaviṣyaṁ tadanantarama | mārkaṇḍeyamathāgneyaṁ nāradīya tataḥ param | 


    daśamaṁ brahmavaivartaṁ liṅgam ekādaśaṁ smṛtama | 


    bhāgadvayena liṅgaṁ ca tato vārāhamattamama | 


    saṁyuktamaṣṭabhiḥ khaṇḍaḥ skāndaṁ caivātivistaram | 


    tatas tu vāmanaṁ kaurmaṁ bhāgadvayavirājitam | 


    mātsyaṁ ca gāruḍaṁ proktaṁ brahmāṇḍaṁ ca tataḥ param | 


    bhāgadvayena kathitaṁ brahmāṇḍam api śabditam | 


    idaṁ brahmapurāṇasya khilaṁ sauramanuttamam | 


    saṁhitādvayasaṁyuktaṁ puṇyaṁ śivakathāśrayam | 


    ādyā sanatkumāroktā dvitīyā sūryabhāṣitā | iti | 

kaurme tu—anyānyupapurāṇāni munibhiḥ kathitānyapi mātsye tu— 


    aṣṭādaśabhyas tu pṛthak purāṇaṁ yat pradṛśyate | 


    vijānīdhvaṁ dvijaśreṣṭhāstadetebhyo vinirgatam | 


    pañcāṅgavatpurāṇaṁ syādākhyānamitaratsmṛtam | 


    pādme purāṇe yā proktā nārasiṁhopavarṇanā | 


    tadaṣṭādaśasāhasraṁ nārasiṁhamihocyate | 


    yacca sāmbaṁ puraskṛtya bhaviṣye'pi kathānakam | 


    procyate tatpunarloke sāmbam eva munīśvaraḥ | 


    evamādityasaṁjñaṁ ca tatraiva paribhāṣitam | iti sandarbhaḥ ||22-24||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tathā ca vārāhe—


    brāhmaṁ pādmaṁ vaiṣṇavaṁ ca śaivaṁ bhāgavataṁ tathā |


    tathānyaṁ nāradīyaṁ ca mārkaṇḍeyaṁ ca saptamam ||


    āgneyam aṣṭamaṁ proktaṁ bhaviṣyaṁ navamaṁ tathā |


    daśamaṁ brahma-vaivartaṁ liṅgam ekādaśaṁ tathā ||


    vārāhaṁ dvādaśaṁ proktaṁ skāndaṁ cātra trayodaśam |


    caturdaśaṁ vāmanaṁ ca kaurmaṁ pañcadaśaṁ tathā |


    mātsyaṁ ca gāruḍaṁ caiva brahmāṇḍāṣṭādaśaṁ tathā ||

śaiva-purāṇe—


    brāhmaṁ purāṇaṁ tatrādyaṁ saṁhitāyāṁ vibhūṣitam |


    ślokānāṁ daśa-sāhasraṁ nana-puṇya-kathā-yutam ||


    pādmaṁ dvitīyaṁ kathitaṁ tṛtīyaṁ vaiṣṇavaṁ smṛtam |


    caturthaṁ vāyunā proktaṁ vāyavīyam iti smṛtam ||


    tato bhāgavataṁ proktaṁ bhāga-dvaya-vibhūṣitam |


    caturbhiḥ pañcabhiḥ proktaṁ bhaviṣyaṁ tad-anantaram ||


    mārkaṇḍeyam atho jñeyaṁ nāradīyam ataḥ param |


    daśamaṁ brahma-vaivartaṁ liṅgam ekādaśaṁ smṛtam ||


    bhāga-dvayena liṅgaṁ ca tato vārāham uttamam |


    saṁyuktam aṣṭabhiḥ khaṇḍaiḥ skāndaṁ caivātra vistaram ||


    tatas tu vāmanaṁ kaurmaṁ bhāga-dvaya-virājitam |


    mātsyaṁ ca gāruḍaṁ proktaṁ brahmāṇḍaṁ ca tataḥ param ||


    bhāga-dvayena kathitaṁ brahmāṇḍam api saṁjñitam |


    idaṁ brahma-purāṇasya khilaṁ sauram anuttamam ||


    saṁhitā-dvaya-saṁyuktaṁ puṇyaṁ śiva-kathāśrayam |


    ādyā sanat-kumāroktā dvitīyā sūrya-bhāṣitā ||

kūrma-purāṇe—


    anyāny upapurāṇāni munibhiḥ kathitāny api ||

mātsye—


    aṣṭādaśabhyas tu pṛthak ṣurāṇaṁ yat pradṛśyate |


    vijānīdhvaṁ dvija-śreṣṭhās tad etebhyo vinirgataḥ ||


    pañcāṅgavat purāṇaṁ syād ākhyānam itaraṁ smṛtam |


    pādmaṁ purāṇe yā proktā narasiṁhopavarṇanā ||


    tad aṣṭādaśa-sāhasraṁ nārasiṁham ihocyate |


    yac ca sāmbaṁ puraskṛtya bhaviṣye’pi kathā-navam ||


    procyate tat punar loke sāmbam eva muni-vrataiḥ |


    evam āditya-saṁjñaṁ ca tatraiva paripaṭhyate ||24||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** triṣaṭ aṣṭādaśa ||23-24||

 **...**

**|| 12.7.25 ||**

**brahmann idaṁ samākhyātaṁ śākhā-praṇayanaṁ muneḥ |**

**śiṣya-śiṣya-praśiṣyāṇāṁ brahma-tejo-vivardhanam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **upasaṁharati—brahmann iti | **muner** vyāsasya | **śiṣyādīnāṁ** ca | **brahma-tejo** **brahma**-varcasaṁ tad-**vivardhanam** | śrotṝṇām iti śeṣaḥ ||25||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **brahmann iti | vyākhyāta-carī saṁbuddhiḥ | brahma-varcasaṁ yadyapi brāhmaṇa evāsti, tathāpītareṣām api vedokta-karma-kāritvena yathā kathañcit tad asty eva, tat-tat-karma-phalādhikyaṁ bhavatīti bhāvaḥ ||25||

iti śrīmad-bhāgavata-bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśe dvādaśa-skandhe saptamo'dhyāyaḥ ||7||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : śākhā-praṇayanam** iti purāṇetihāsānāṁ śākhā-sthānīyatvād ity abhiprāyaḥ **śiṣyāḥ** sākṣād-upadeśyāḥ **śiṣya-praśiṣyāḥ** śiṣyāṇāṁ śiṣya-paramparāḥ ||25||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** **muner** vyāsasya, **śiṣyāṇāṁ śiṣyāḥ,** teṣām api **praśiṣyāḥ,** teṣāṁ **śākhā-praṇayanaṁ**, **brahma-tejo-vivardhanam** iti śrotṝṇām iti śeṣaḥ ||25||

 **...**

iti sārārtha-darśinyāṁ harṣiṇyāṁ bhakta-cetasām |

dvādaśe saptamo’dhyāyaḥ saṅgataḥ saṅgataḥ satām ||*||

 **...**


    iti śrīmad-bhāgavate mahā-purāṇe brahma-sūtra-bhāṣye pāramahaṁsyaṁ saṁhitāyāṁ vaiyāsikyāṁ dvādaśa-skandhe 


    purāṇa-lakṣaṇa-varṇanaṁ nāma 


    saptamo’dhyāyaḥ |

|| 12.7 ||

**…**

**(12.8)**


### athāṣṭamo’dhyāyaḥ


## nārāyaṇa-stavaḥ

**|| 12.8.1 ||**

**śrī-śaunaka uvāca—**

**sūta jīva ciraṁ sādho vada no vadatāṁ vara |**

**tamasy apāre bhramatāṁ nṝṇāṁ tvaṁ pāra-darśanaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :**

aṣṭame tu tapaś-caryā mārkaṇḍeyasya mohakaiḥ |

kāmādibhir asammoho nara-nārāyaṇa-stutiḥ ||

purāṇa-vibhāga-prasaṅgena purāṇa-kartur mārkaṇḍeyasya carita-praśnam āha--sūteti | tvam eva vaktuṁ yogya ity āha--**tamasi** saṁsāre **bhramatāṁ pāra-darśanas** tan-nivartakaḥ ||1||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **jagato mohakair api | mārkaṇḍeyaṁ savāmanam iti śrutatvenādbhutanāmatvena smṛtipathamārūḍhasya mārkaṇḍeyasya caritaṁ pṛcchati | vaktuḥ kathanotsāhavarddhanārthaṁ saṁbuddhitrayam | sūteti sāmānyata uktaṁ prātilomyabhrāntivāraṇāya—sādho iti, tatsamarthanāyavadatāṁ vareti ||1||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tad evaṁ nānā-prabhāvānāṁ kathā-mayaṁ purāṇam idaṁ samāpyamānaṁ vitaktyaṁ tatra nija-kulāvataṁsa-tādṛśa-mārkaṇḍeya-kathām aprastutāṁ prastāvayati—sūta jīvety-ādinā ||1||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :**

aṣṭame’tra tapo-bhaṅgā śaktiḥ svar-yoṣitocyate |

mārkaṇḍeyasya tenātha nara-nārāyaṇa-stutiḥ ||

mārkaṇḍeyaṁ sa-vāmanam iti mārkaṇḍeya-purāṇa-śrutyaiva smṛti-patham ārūḍhasya mārkaṇḍeyasya caritaṁ praṣṭum āha—sūteti tamasi saṁsāre ||1||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.2 ||**

**āhuś cirāyuṣam ṛṣiṁ mṛkaṇḍu-tanayaṁ janāḥ |**

**yaḥ kalpānte hy urvarito yena grastam idaṁ jagat ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **vaktavyam āha—āhur iti | **urvarito**’vaśiṣṭaḥ | **yena** kalpāntena | etat kathaṁ ghaṭate ? ity ekaḥ praśnaḥ ||2||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **āhuḥ paurāṇikāḥ| kalpāntatvaṁ durghaṭam eva ||2||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : kalpasyānte** **urvaritaḥ**, avaśiṣṭatvena dṛṣṭaḥ ||2||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : urvarito**’vaśiṣṭaḥ | **yena** kalpāntena ||2||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.3 ||**

**sa vā asmat-kulotpannaḥ kalpe’smin bhārgava-rṣabhaḥ |**

**naivādhunāpi bhūtānāṁ samplavaḥ ko’pi jāyate ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **pralayābhāvād apy etan na ghaṭata ity āha—sa vā iti | yato **bhārgava-rṣabhaḥ** | **ko’pi** prākṛtiko naimittiko vā ||3||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **kalpāntatvaṁ na ghaṭata ity āha—sa vā iti | katham asminn eva kalpa iti jñāyate ? tatrāha—naiveti | kalpānte samplavasyāvaśyaṁ bhāvitvād bhūta-paramparāyāś cāvicchedena samprati prāptatvād iti bhāvaḥ ||3||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **sa kalpānte urvarita iti prasiddhiḥ, kintu **adhunāpi samplavaḥ** pralayo nāstīti saṁśayaḥ ||3||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.4 ||**

**eka evārṇave bhrāmyan dadarśa puruṣaṁ kila |**

**vaṭa-patra-puṭe tokaṁ śayānaṁ tv ekam adbhutam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **anyad apy aghaṭitam evety āha—eka eveti | **tokaṁ** bālakam ||4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **nanu kāśyaḥ kuśo gṛtsamadaḥ iti suhotranṛpasyātmajādgṛtsamadācchunakas tasmācchaunakotpattiśruteḥ kathamuktaṁ śrīśaunakena—sa vā asmatkulotpanna iti, tatredaṁ bodhyam—gṛtsamado'rinṛpabhīto bhārgavāśramamitvā taṁ natvā ca bhagavanmāṁ pāhi ripor iti provāca, sa ca taṁ mā bhairityāśvāsyāśramādbahirāgatya tadvairiṇamiha sarve brāhmaṇāḥ santi na kopi kṣatriya ityuvāca | tadākarṇya jitaṁ mayetyuktvā sa gatas tadā bhārgavo'bhūd iti mahābhārate | sati pralaye'smatkulaṁ kathamavaśiṣṭam iti praśnāntaram ||3-4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **kalpānte urvaritatve kiṁ pramāṇam ? tad āha—**eka evārṇava** iti | **kila** prasiddhau ||4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **anyad apy aghaṭitam evety āha—eka eveti ||4||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.5 ||**

**eṣa naḥ saṁśayo bhūyān sūta kautūhalaṁ yataḥ |**

**taṁ naś chindhi mahā-yogin purāṇeṣv api sammataḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : kautūhalam** autsukyam | **taṁ** saṁśayam | na kevalaṁ tvaṁ **mahā-yogī**, kintu **purāṇeṣv** api jñātṛtvena **sammataḥ** ||5||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **purāṇeṣu prācīnavṛttapratipādikeṣu śrīvyāsarṣipraṇītaśāstreṣu | 


    anāgatamatītaṁ ca vartamānamatīndriyam | 


    sannikṛṣṭaṁ vyavahitaṁ samyakpaśyanti yoginaḥ ||

ity ukter yogināmetatkathanasāmarthyamasti kiṁ punarmahāyoginaḥ taveti | saṁbuddhyabhiprāyaḥ ||5||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** _na vyākhyātam._

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : yataḥ** saṁśayād eva **kautūhalaṁ** **taṁ** saṁśayaṁ **chindhi** | na kevalaṁ tvaṁ **mahā-yogī**, kintu **purāṇeṣv** api jñātṛtvena **sammataḥ** ||5||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.6 ||**

**sūta uvāca—**

**praśnas tvayā maharṣe’yaṁ kṛto loka-bhramāpahaḥ |**

**nārāyaṇa-kathā yatra gītā kali-malāpahā ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **praśnam abhinandati—he maharṣe | ayaṁ praśnaḥ | tatra hetuḥ—nārāyaṇeti | yatra praśna-viṣaye ||6||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **he maharṣe iti saṁbuddhyā tattādṛśajñānavattvaṁ sūcayati | ṛṣaya eva trikālajñā bhavanti kiṁ punarmaharṣiḥ bhavāniti bhāvaḥ | ṛṣistraikālikajñānī vipro vedas tathā ṛṣiḥ iti saṁhitokteḥ | tatra lokabhramāvahatve | lokabhramaḥ saṁsāre bhramaṇaṁ tamapahantīti tathā ||6||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **iha khalu kalpe manvantarāṇy evocyante samplavaś ca tad-ante prakṣālanam eva, yat tu eka evārṇave bhrāmyan [bhā.pu. 12.8.4] ity-ādi bhavatā pṛṣṭaṁ, tat khalu māyikam eva saptānām api kalpānāṁ māyikatve tu kṣaṇa-mātratvena sambhavāc cira-jīvitva-vighātaḥ syād ity uttarayitum āha—praśna iti ||6||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** _na vyākhyātam._

 **...**

**|| 12.8.7 ||**

**prāpta-dvi-jāti-saṁskāro mārkaṇḍeyaḥ pituḥ kramāt |**

**chandāṁsy adhītya dharmeṇa tapaḥ-svādhyāya-saṁyutaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tatra mārkaṇḍeyas tapasā bhagavantam ārādhya māyā-pradarśanaṁ vavre | tataś ca tenaiva bhagavan-māyayā sapta-kalpā dṛṣṭā nānyair ity uttaraṁ vaktum ādita ārabhya tasya caritam āha—prāpta ity-ādinā | mārkaṇḍeyo mṛtyuṁ jigye iti pañcama-ślokenānvayaḥ | madhyama-granthena tasya dharmaḥ kathyate | prāpto dvi-jāti-saṁskāra upanayanākhyo yena saḥ | pituḥ sakāśād garbhādhānādi-kramāt | chandāṁsi vedān ||7||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tatrāpasthitaprakṛte | atha prasaṅgāgatam āha—viduṣāṁ mude | piturity ukter nātra pitaivopanayetputram iti niyamaḥ, kintu pitetyupalakṣaṇaṁ pitāmahādeḥ tad-uktaṁ gargeṇa—


    pitā pitāmaho bhrātā jñātayo gotrajāgrajāḥ | 


    upanāye'dhīkārī syātpūrvābhāve paraḥ || 

uktādhikāryabhāve vyāsaḥ—


    vedaikaniṣṭhaṁ dharmajñaṁ kulīnaṁ śrotriyaṁ śucim | 


    svaśākhīyamanālasyaṁ vipramācāryamāśrayet || iti | 


    ācāryaṁ hi kṣatravaiśyau vṛṇuyātāṁ purohitam | 


    tadabhāve'nyavipraṁ hi gṛhasthaṁ vedapāragam || 


    tyaktagotrābhimānaṁ tu yo vipram api dhārayet | 


    vadakarmapyathācāryaṁ patitaḥ so'bhidhīyate || 


    tatkāritaṁ tatkṛtaṁ ca śubhaṁ karmākhilaṁ vṛthā | 


    prāyaścittaṁ tataḥ kṛtvā tatkarma punarācaret || 

prāyaścittaṁ tūktaṁ vāratāntavinā—


    viprebhyo daśa gā dadyādvā kṛcchrāṇi daśācaret | 


    kārayetsaṁhitāpāṭhaṁ gāyatryā vā daśāyutam | 


    tatas tūpanayedvipro viprakṣatraviśaḥ sudhīḥ || iti | 

kramāditi—garbhādhānādyāḥ ṣoḍaśasaṁskārāḥ pūrvamuktāḥ ||7||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **prāpteti pañcakam ||7||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** _na vyākhyātam._

 **...**

**|| 12.8.8 ||**

**bṛhad-vrata-dharaḥ śānto jaṭilo valkalāmbaraḥ |**

**bibhrat kamaṇḍaluṁ daṇḍam upavītaṁ sa-mekhalam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **bṛhad-vrata-dharo naiṣṭhiko brahmacārī san ||8||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **mekhalā mauñjī ta sahitam ||8||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.8.9 ||**

**kṛṣṇājinaṁ sākṣa-sūtraṁ kuśāṁś ca niyamarddhaye |**

**agny-arka-guru-viprātmasv arcayan sandhyayor harim ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **niyama-rddhaye dharma-vṛddhaye agny-ādiṣu pañcasu harim arcayan ||9||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **akṣasūtramakṣamālā ādikṣāntagatairvaṇairjapamālākṣamālikā iti tantrokteḥ | gautamīye ca—


    pañcāśanmaṇibhirmālā vihitā sarvakarmasu | 


    akārādikṣākārāntā hyakṣamālā prakīrtitā || iti |


    rudrākṣaśaṅkhapadmākṣaputrajīvakamauktikaiḥ | 


    sphāṭikaurmāṇiratnaiś ca sauvarṇairvidrumais tathā | 


    rājataiḥ kuśamūlaiś ca gṛhasthasyākṣamālikā | 


    aṅgulīgaṇanādekaṁ parvaṇyaṣṭaguṇaṁ bhavet | 


    putrajīvairda śaguṇaṁ śataṁ śaṅkhaiḥ sahasrakram | 


    pravālairmaṇiratnaiś ca daśasāhasrika phalam | 


    tad eva sphāṭikaiḥ proktaṁ mauktikairlakṣamucyate | 


    padmākṣairdaśalakṣaṁ syātsauvarṇaiḥ koṭirucyate | 


    kuśagranthyā koṭiśataṁ rudrākṣaiḥ syādanantakam || iti | 

kuśāṁścetyukteḥ kuśatrayapavitrādi jñeyam | vipro'tra gurubhinno jñeyaḥ | atra viprapadasya pṛthagukter vipratarasya gurutvaṁ na śaṅkanīyam, janmanā brāhmaṇo guruḥ iti śrīgargaṁ prati nandokteḥ varṇānāmāśramāṇāṁ ca mukhyo'bhūdbrāhmaṇo guruḥ iti maitreyokteś ca ||9||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.8.10 ||**

**sāyaṁ prātaḥ sa gurave bhaikṣyam āhṛtya vāg-yataḥ |**

**bubhuje gurv-anujñātaḥ sakṛn no ced upoṣitaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **bhaikṣyaṁ gurv-artham āhṛtya tenānujñātaś cet tarhi bubhuje no cet sakṛt kadācid upoṣito bhavati ||10||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **no cet kadācidgurvanujñābhāve upoṣitaḥ kṛtopavāsa eva bhavatīty arthaḥ ||10||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **sāyaṁ prātaritiṁ samāvartanāt pūrvāvasthāyām eva geyaṁ varṣāṇām ayutāyutam iti kalpābhiprāyeṇa kalpa-jīvitvāt, yāvaj-jīvam evārādhayatas tasya mṛtyur na chidraṁ prāpety arthaḥ | tasyaivaṁ yuñjata [bhā.pu. 12.8.14-15] iti vakṣyamāṇa-padya-dvayāt ||10||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** _na vyākhyātam._

 **...**

**|| 12.8.11 ||**

**evaṁ tapaḥ-svādhyāya-paro varṣāṇām ayutāyutam |**

**ārādhayan hṛṣīkeśaṁ jigye mṛtyuṁ su-durjayam ||**

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **svādhyāyo vedābhyāsaḥ | ayutāyutaṁ koṭiḥ, asaṅkhyātānyeva varṣāṇi jagmurity arthaḥ ||11||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.12 ||**

**brahmā bhṛgur bhavo dakṣo brahma-putrāś ca ye’pare |**

**nṛ-deva-pitṛ-bhūtāni tenāsann ati-vismitāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tena mṛtyu-jayena ||12||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tena mṛtyuñjayarūpakarmaṇā ||12||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.8.13 ||**

**itthaṁ bṛhad-vrata-dharas tapaḥ-svādhyāya-saṁyamaiḥ |**

**dadhyāv adhokṣajaṁ yogī dhvasta-kleśāntarātmanā ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **dhvastāḥ kleśā rāgādayo yasya tenāntar-ātmanā pratyāhṛta-manasā ||13||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ādinā dveṣādigrahaḥ | avidyāsmitārāgadveṣābhiniveśāḥ pañca kleśāḥ iti patañjalisūtrāt ||13||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **dhvastāḥ kleśā rāgādayo yasya tenāntar-ātmanā manasā ||13||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.14 ||**

**tasyaivaṁ yuñjataś cittaṁ mahā-yogena yoginaḥ |**

**vyatīyāya mahān kālo manvantara-ṣaḍ-ātmakaḥ ||**

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ṣaḍityasya parvanipātābhāvo viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvavyatyāsāt ||14||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.15 ||**

**etat purandaro jñātvā saptame’smin kilāntare |**

**tapo-viśaṅkito brahmann ārebhe tad-vighātanam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tasya tapo-niṣṭhām itihāsena varṇayati—etad ity-ādinā | asmin saptame manvantare | tapasā mat-padaṁ grahīṣyatīti viśaṅkitaḥ ||15||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **tapasā mat-padaṁ grahīṣyatīti viśaṅkitaḥ ||15||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.16 ||**

**gandharvāpsarasaḥ kāmaṁ vasanta-malayānilau |**

**munaye preṣayām āsa rajas-toka-madau tathā ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **munaye muniṁ bhraṁśayitum | rajasas tokam atipriyam apatyaṁ lobho madaś ca tau ||16||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **asminvaivasvatākhye | etanmārkaṇḍeyatapasa ādhikyam | tadvighātanaṁ taponāśanam | he brahmann iti varṇitābhiprāyam ||15-16||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** _na vyākhyātam._

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **rajasas tokam apatyaṁ lobhaś ca madaś ca, tau ||16||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.17 ||**

**te vai tad-āśramaṁ jagmur himādreḥ pārśva uttare |**

**puṣpabhadrā nadī yatra citrākhyā ca śilā vibho ||**

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **te gandharvādyāḥ | tadāśramaṁ mārkaṇḍeyāśramam ||17||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.18 ||**

**tad-āśrama-padaṁ puṇyaṁ puṇya-druma-latāñcitam |**

**puṇya-dvija-kulākīrṇaṁ puṇyāmala-jalāśayam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tad-āśrama-padaṁ praviṣṭo vāyur vavāv iti tṛtīyenānvayaḥ | puṇyair drumair latābhiś cāñcitaṁ pūjitam | puṇya-dvijānām ṛṣīṇāṁ kulair ākīrṇam | puṇyā amalā jalāśayā yasmin ||18||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **puṇyadrumā aśvatthādayaḥ, puṇyalatā viṣṇukrāntādyāḥ, puṇyadvijāḥ śukasārasādayaḥ | jalāśayāḥ sarovarāḥ ||18||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.8.19 ||**

**matta-bhramara-saṅgītaṁ matta-kokila-kūjitam |**

**matta-barhi-naṭāṭopaṁ matta-dvija-kulākulam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **matta-bhramarāṇāṁ saṅgītaṁ yasmin | matta-kokilānāṁ kūjitaṁ yasmin | mattā barhiṇa eva naṭās teṣām āṭopo nṛtya-saṁbhrāmo yasmin | mattānāṁ pakṣiṇā kulair ākulaṁ vyāptam ||19||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **āṭopo nṛtyasaṁbhramaḥ ||19||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.8.20 ||**

**vāyuḥ praviṣṭa ādāya hima-nirjhara-śīkarān |**

**sumanobhiḥ pariṣvakto vavāv uttambhayan smaram ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **evaṁ-bhūtaṁ tad āśrama-padaṁ praviṣṭaḥ san vāyur malayānilo vavau prasasāra | uttambhayann uhīpayan | tatra vṛkṣeṣu praveśān māndyaṁ hima-nirjhara-kaṇānām ādānāc chaityaṁ puṣpa-pariṣvaṅgāt saugandhyaṁ coktam ||20||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tatra vāyau ||20||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.8.21 ||**

**udyac-candra-niśā-vaktraḥ pravāla-stabakālibhiḥ |**

**gopa-druma-latā-jālais tatrāsīt kusumākaraḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kiṁ ca, udyaṁś candro yasmiṁs tan-niśā-vaktraṁ rajanī-mukhaṁ yasmin saḥ | pravāla-stavakānām ālayaḥ śreṇayo yeṣu taiḥ | gupyanti viṭapaiḥ saṁśliṣyantīti gopā drumā latāś ca teṣāṁ jālaiḥ samūhair upalakṣita āvir babhūva ||21||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **anyadāha—kiñceti | kusumākaro vasantaḥ | gāṁ pṛthvīṁ phalapuṣpādyaiḥ pānti tarpayantīti gopā āmrādayaḥ | yad vā, gāḥ kiraṇāni pānti rakṣanti patrādiṣu prakaṭayantīti gopā aśvatthādayaste ca te drumāśceti gopadrumāḥ ||21||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **udyad iti | gāṁ pṛthvīṁ phala-puṣpādibhiḥ pāntīti go-pāḥ sarva-santarpakā ye drumā ity arthaḥ ||21||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **udyaṁś candro yasmiṁs tādṛśaṁ niśā-vaktraṁ niśā-mukhaṁ yasmin saḥ | pravālānāṁ stavakānām ālayo yatra taiḥ | gāḥ kiraṇān pānti rakṣanti ye drumā latāś ca, teṣāṁ jālaiḥ | saha kusumākaro vasantaḥ ||21||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.22 ||**

**anvīyamāno gandharvair gīta-vāditra-yūthakaiḥ |**

**adṛśyatātta-cāpeṣuḥ svaḥ-strī-yūtha-patiḥ smaraḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kiṁ ca, tadā gīta-vāditra-yūthakair gāyakādi-samudāyibhir gandharvair anvīyamānaḥ | tathā svaḥ-striyo’psarasas tāsāṁ yūthasya patiḥ | āttaṁ cāpam iṣuś ca yena, sa smaraś ca tatrādṛśyata ||22||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **anyadāha—kiñceti | smaraḥ kāmaḥ | tatrāśrame ||22||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** _na vyākhyātam._

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **gīta-vāditra-yūthakair gīta-vāditra-yūthavadbhiḥ | adṛśyata muni-manasi svayam eva kiñcid anvabhūyateti vyakampayann iti prabodhyāhiṁ [bhā.pu. 12.8.29] iti dharṣito’pīty agrima-vākyād avagamyate | matv-arthīyaṣṭan ||22||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.23 ||**

**hutvāgniṁ samupāsīnaṁ dadṛśuḥ śakra-kiṅkarāḥ |**

**mīlitākṣaṁ durādharṣaṁ mūrtimantam ivānalam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **durādharṣam abhibhavitum aśakyam ||23||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **analamagnim ||23||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** _na vyākhyātam._

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** samupāsīnaṁ munim ||23||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.24 ||**

**nanṛtus tasya purataḥ striyo’tho gāyakā jaguḥ |**

**mṛdaṅga-vīṇā-paṇavair vādyaṁ cakrur mano-ramam ||**

_na katamenāpi vyākhyātam._

 **...**

**|| 12.8.25 ||**

**sandadhe’straṁ sva-dhanuṣi kāmaḥ pañca-mukhaṁ tadā |**

**madhur mano rajas-toka indra-bhṛtyā vyakampayan ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **śoṣaṇa-dīpana-sammohana-tāpanonmādanākhyāni pañca mukhāni yasya tad-astraṁ sandadhe | tadaiva madhur vasantaḥ | rajas-tokaś ca puṁstvam ārṣam | anye cendra-bhṛtyās tasya mano vyakampayan ||25||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tasya muneḥ ||24-25||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **vyakampayan vikampayitum ārabdhā ity arthaḥ ||25||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** śoṣaṇa-mohana-sandīpana-tāpana-mādanākhyāni pañca-mukhāni yasya tat | madhur vasantaḥ | rajas-tokaś ca puṁstvam ārṣam | vyakampayan manaś cālayāmāsuḥ ||25||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.26 ||**

**krīḍantyāḥ puñjikasthalyāḥ kandukaiḥ stana-gauravāt |**

**bhṛśam udvigna-madhyāyāḥ keśa-visraṁsita-srajaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **puñjikasthalyās tan-nāmnyāḥ ||26||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.27 ||**

**itas tato bhramad-dṛṣṭeś calantyā anu kandukam |**

**vāyur jahāra tad-vāsaḥ sūkṣmaṁ truṭita-mekhalam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kiṁ ca, vāyur malayānilaḥ puñjika-sthalyās tat sūkṣmaṁ vāso jahāra ||27||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **keśebhyo visraṁsitā adhaḥ patitā srak puṣpamālā yasyāstasyāḥ ||26-27||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** _na vyākhyātam._

 **...**

**|| 12.8.28 ||**

**visasarja tadā bāṇaṁ matvā taṁ sva-jitaṁ smaraḥ |**

**sarvaṁ tatrābhavan mogham anīśasya yathodyamaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **sarvaṁ teṣāṁ karma | tatra tasmin | moghaṁ vyartham | anīśasya nirdaivasya ||28||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tatra munau | anīśo bhāgyarahitaḥ ||28||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **anīśasya anīśvara-vādinaḥ | udyamaḥ pāralaukika-prayatnaḥ ||28||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** anīśasya bhāgya-rahitasya ||28||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.29 ||**

**ta ittham apakurvanto munes tat-tejasā mune |**

**dahyamānā nivavṛtuḥ prabodhyāhim ivārbhakāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **muner apakurvantaḥ pratikūlam ācarantaḥ | he mune ||29||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **he mune iti—mananaśīlā hi komalasvabhāvatvātpratīkāraṁ na kurvantīti—bhāvaḥ | prabodhyāhim iti na jānīmahe'dya kiṁ bhāvīti bhītāḥ | atrāhidṛṣṭāntena prathamaṁ kāmaṁ prati kiñcitkrodho'pi jātaḥ paścādvivekena kāmakrodhayordvayorevoparāmaḥ kṛta ityavasīyate ||29||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **prabodhyāhim iti na jānīmahe | adya kiṁ bhaviṣyatīti bhītāḥ | atrāhi-dṛṣṭāntena prathamaṁ kiñcid adbhutaṁ kāmaṁ prati krodho’bhūt paścād vivekena kāma-krodhayor ubhayor apy upaśamaḥ kṛta ity avasīyate ||29||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.30 ||**

**itīndrānucarair brahman dharṣito’pi mahā-muniḥ |**

**yan nāgād ahamo bhāvaṁ na tac citraṁ mahatsu hi ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ahamo’haṅkārasya | bhāvaṁ vikāram ||30||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **dharṣito’pi dharṣitum ārabdho’pi ||30||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** ahamo’haṅkārasya ||30||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.31 ||**

**dṛṣṭvā nistejasaṁ kāmaṁ sa-gaṇaṁ bhagavān svarāṭ |**

**śrutvānubhāvaṁ brahmarṣer vismayaṁ samagāt param ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **nistejasaṁ mlāna-vadanam | sva-rāḍ indraḥ ||31||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** _na vyākhyātam._

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **sva-rāḍ indraḥ ||31||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.32 ||**

**tasyaivaṁ yuñjataś cittaṁ tapaḥ-svādhyāya-saṁyamaiḥ |**

**anugrahāyāvirāsīn nara-nārāyaṇo hariḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **nara-nārāyaṇa-rūpo hariḥ ||32||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **dharṣito viprakṛtaḥ ||30-32||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** _na vyākhyātam._

 **...**

**|| 12.8.33 ||**

**tau śukla-kṛṣṇau nava-kañja-locanau**

**catur-bhujau raurava-valkalāmbarau |**

**pavitra-pāṇī upavītakaṁ tri-vṛt**

**kamaṇḍaluṁ daṇḍam ṛjuṁ ca vaiṇavam ||**

**padmākṣa-mālām uta jantu-mārjanaṁ**

**vedaṁ ca sākṣāt tapa eva rūpiṇau |**

**tapat-taḍid-varṇa-piśaṅga-rociṣā**

**prāṁśū dadhānau vibudharṣabhārcitau ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tāv anuvarṇayati dvābhyām—tāv iti | rauravaṁ kṛṣṇājinaṁ valkalaṁ cāmbaraṁ yayos tau | pavitre pāṇyor yayos tau | tri-vṛt tri-guṇaṁ nava-tantukam iti vā tri-vṛd bahiḥ pavamānam ity-ādau navake prayogāt | upavītakādīn dadhānau | vedaṁ darbha-muṣṭim | kiṁ ca, sākṣāt tapa eva tau | tatra hetuḥ, tapat-tāḍid-varṇaṁ dedīpyamāna-vidyut-saṅkāśaṁ yat piśaṅgaṁ rocis tena rūpiṇau mūrtim antau | tādṛk-tejo-yukta-mūrtibhyāṁ tapo-mayatvena prakāśamānāv ity arthaḥ | prāṁśū unnatau ||33-34||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **triguṇam iti—


    yajñopavīte dve dhārye śraute smārte ca karmaṇi | 


    tṛtīyamuttarīyārthaṁ vastrābhāve tadiṣyate || 

iti hemādryuktaṁ stryupavītamity arthaḥ | yad vā, trivṛd iti yajñopavīta svarūpakathananevetyāha—navatantukam iti | atra pramāṇam āha—trivṛddhahir iti | pavitre dvitrikuśanirmite pāṇyordakṣavāmakarānāmikayoryayostau | yad vā, sauvarṇe pavitre grāhye | tad uktamatharvaṣaṣṭhānuvāke—


    nainaṁ rakṣāṁsi na piśācāḥ sahante devānāmojaḥ prathamaṁ hye tat | 


    yo bibharti dākṣāyaṇaṁ hiraṇyaṁ sa jīveṣu kṛṇute dīrghamāyuḥ || iti | 

kṛṇute prāpnoti | kṛvi—gatau taṅārṣaḥ || 

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **padmānāmakṣamāleti vaiṣṇavamālātvabodhanāyaiva | jantumārjanaṁ sūkṣmakīṭapipīlikādimārjanam, tac ca nānātantukhaṇḍanirmitaścāmaraviśeṣa iti kecit | apare tu vastrakhaṇḍam iti | anye tu jantūnāṁ mārjanaṁ yena tathāvidhaṁ vedaṁ ceti vedaviśeṣaṇatayā vyācakhyuḥ | piśaṅgaṁ pītam | ity artha iti—tejoviśeṣeṇa mūrtidhāri tapa evemāv iti pratīyamānāv iti bhāvaḥ ||33-34||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **upavītādikaṁ dadhānau ||33||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **rauravaṁ kṛṣṇājinaṁ valkalam ambaraṁ yayos tau | tri-vṛt tri-guṇaṁ nava-tantukam upavītaṁ dadhānau kamaṇḍalv-ādikaṁ hasteṣu dadhānau | vedaṁ veda-śāstraṁ jantūnāṁ mārjanaṁ śuddhir yatas taṁ vedaṁ darbha-muṣṭim iti kecit | tapa eva rūpiṇau tapo-mūrtir ity arthaḥ | tapas taḍid-varṇaṁ dīpyamāna-vidyut-saṅkāśaṁ yat piśaṅga-rocis tena | prāṁśū atyunnatau ||33-34||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.35 ||**

**te vai bhagavato rūpe nara-nārāyaṇāv ṛṣī |**

**dṛṣṭvotthāyādareṇoccair nanāmāṅgena daṇḍavat ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **uccair mahatādareṇa ||35||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** _na vyākhyātam._

 **...**

**|| 12.8.36 ||**

**sa tat-sandarśanānanda- nirvṛtātmendriyāśayaḥ |**

**hṛṣṭa-romāśru-pūrṇākṣo na sehe tāv udīkṣitum ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tayoḥ sandarśanena ya ānandas tena nirvṛtā upaśāntā ātmendriyāśayā dehendriya-manāṁsi yasya saḥ | na sehe nāśaknot ||36||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** _na vyākhyātam._

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** na sehe na śaśāka ||36||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.37 ||**

**utthāya prāñjaliḥ prahva autsukyād āśliṣann iva |**

**namo nama itīśānau babhāṣe gadgadākṣaram ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **āśliṣann āliṅgann iva ||37||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** prahvo namraḥ ||37||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.38 ||**

**tayor āsanam ādāya pādayor avanijya ca |**

**arhaṇenānulepena dhūpa-mālyair apūjayat ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **pādayor avanijya pādau prakṣālya | arhaṇenārdhyeṇa ||38||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** _na vyākhyātam._

 **...**

**|| 12.8.39 ||**

**sukham āsanam āsīnau prasādābhimukhau munī |**

**punar ānamya pādābhyāṁ gariṣṭhāv idam abravīt ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **pādābhyāṁ pādāv ānamya | gariṣṭhau pūjyatamau tau prati ||39||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **daṇḍavat sāṣṭāṅgam ||35-39||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** _na vyākhyātam._

 **...**

**|| 12.8.40 ||**

**śrī-mārkaṇḍeya uvāca—**

**kiṁ varṇaye tava vibho yad-udīrito’suḥ **

**saṁspandate tam anu vāṅ-mana-indriyāṇi |**

**spandanti vai tanu-bhṛtām aja-śarvayoś ca**

**svasyāpy athāpi bhajatām asi bhāva-bandhuḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **antaryāmiṇas tasyaiva prāṇādi-pravartakatvād ātmanaḥ stutāv asvātantryaṁ paśyann āha—kim iti | **tava** tvāṁ **kim** ahaṁ **varṇaye,** kathaṁ staumi ? **yad** yena tvayaiva **udīritaḥ** prerito’**suḥ** prāṇaḥ **saṁspandate** pravartate, **tam anu** ca **vāg-ādayaḥ spandanti** | atra hetuḥ—**vai** anvaya-vyatirekābhyāṁ, śrotrasya śrotraṁ [bṛ.ā.u. 4.4.18] ity-ādi-śrutibhiś caitat prasiddham ity arthaḥ | na kevalaṁ prākṛtānāṁ **tanu-bhṛtāṁ** kintv **aja-śarvayoś** **ca**, ataḥ **svasya** mamāpi tathaiva | evaṁ yadyapi na kasyāpi svātantryam, **athāpi** dāru-yantravat tvat-pravartitair api vāg-ādibhir **bhajatāṁ** puṁsāṁ **bhāva-bandhur** ātma-bandhur asi, na tu pitrādivad deha-mātra-bandhuḥ | aho kṛpālutā tavety arthaḥ ||40||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **he vibho iti—varṇanaṁ hi paricchinna-vastuno bhavati vibhos tu taddhāsyāyaveti bhāvaḥ | atra vāg-ādi-spandakatve | anvaya-vyatirekau ca yatra śrotrādimattvaṁ tatra tat-pravartakatvaṁ yathāsmad-ādiṣu, yatra tan na tatra na tat-pravartakatvaṁ yathā ghaṭādāv iti jñayau | _ity artha_ iti—śrutibhir ayam arthaḥ sphuṭatayā pratipādita iti bhāvaḥ | _ity artha_ iti—aho nirnimitta-kṛpālutā tavaivāsti na deha-bandhūnām iti bhāvaḥ | 

viśvanāthas tu—yadyapy evaṁ bandhur asi tathāpi bhajatāṁ janānāṁ bhāvena premṇā bandhur bandhur iva vaśyo'si prāṇendriyādibhis tvam eva sva-bhajanaṁ kārayasi punas tādṛśa-bhajanasya pratyupakārāsamartha ṛṇīva bhūtvā prema-vaśyo bhavasīty adbhutaṁ tava kṛpā-vaibhavam iti bhāvaḥ ||40||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **bhakti-rūpāyās tac-chakter jīve’bhivyaktau bhagavān eva kāraṇam | tat-tad-indriyādi-pravṛttau ca sa eveti tasmiṁs tayā jīvasyopakārakābhāsatvam eva | tathāpi bhaktānurajyad ātmatve bhagavataḥ sva-kṛpā-prābalyam eva kāraṇam iti vadan pūrvārtham eva sādhayati—**kiṁ varṇaya** iti |

he **vibho** ! **tava kim** ahaṁ **varṇaye** ? tvat-kṛpālutāyāḥ kiyantam aṁśaṁ varṇayeyam ? ity arthaḥ | yato **yena** tvayaiva **udīritaḥ** prerito’**suḥ** prāṇaḥ **saṁspandate** pravartate, **tam** asum **anu** ca **vāg**-ādayaḥ **spandanti** | tatra hetuḥ—**vai** anvaya-vyatirekābhyāṁ śrotrasya śrotram [bṛ.ā.u. 4.4.18] ity-ādi-śrutibhyaś ca tat prasiddham ity arthaḥ | na kevalaṁ prākṛtānāṁ **tanu-bhṛtāṁ** kintu **aja-śarvayoś ca** | ataḥ **svasya** mamāpi tathaiva | evaṁ yadyapi na kvacid api kasyāpi svātantryam, tathāpi dāru-yantravat pravartitair api vāg-ādibhir bhajatāṁ puṁsāṁ **bhāvena** sva-dattayaiva bhaktyā **bandhur **snigdho’**si** iti ||40|| [bhakti-sandarbhaḥ 144]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** yena tvayaiva **udīritaḥ** prerito’**suḥ** prāṇaḥ **spandate** pravartate, **tam anu ca vāg-ādīni spandante** | śrotrasya śrotraṁ [bṛ.ā.u. 4.4.18] ity-ādi-śrutibhir **vai** niścitam evety arthaḥ | na kevalaṁ prākṛtānāṁ **tanu-bhṛtām** api **aja-śarvayoś ca** | ataḥ **svasya** mama **api** | yadyapy evaṁ, tathāpi **bhajatāṁ** janānāṁ **bhāvena** premnā **bandhur** bandhur iva vaśyo’si | prāṇa-buddhīndriyādibhis tvam eva sva-bhajanaṁ kārayasi, punas tādṛśa-bhajanasya pratyupakāre ’samartho ṛṇīva bhūtvā, tat-prema-vaśyo bhavasīty adbhutaṁ tava kṛpā-vaibhavam iti bhāvaḥ ||40||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.41 ||**

**mūrtī ime bhagavato bhagavaṁs tri-lokyāḥ**

**kṣemāya tāpa-viramāya ca mṛtyu-jityai |**

**nānā bibharṣy avitum anya-tanūr yathedaṁ**

**sṛṣṭvā punar grasasi sarvam ivorṇanābhiḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **nanu katham āvāṁ prāṇādi-pravartakau dharma-putratvād āvayoḥ ? iti cet, tatrāha—mūrtī iti | he bhagavan ! bhagavatas tava ime mūrtī tri-lokyāḥ kṣemāya pālanāya tāpa-viramāya ca duḥkha-nivṛttyai mṛtyu-jityai mokṣāya, na tu tvaṁ kasyāpi putra ity arthaḥ | atra dṛṣṭāntaḥ, yathedaṁ viśvam avitum anyās tanūr matsya-kūrmādi-lakṣaṇā nānā aneka-prakārā bibharṣi, tadvat | na kevalaṁ pālana-mātraṁ tava karma, kintu sṛṣṭi-layāv apīty āha—sṛṣṭveti | tatrāpy anya-nirapekṣatve dṛṣṭāntaḥ—ūrṇanābhir iveti ||41||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **na kevalaṁ svabhajanaṁ kārayituṁ bhaktiparipāke ca tadvaśyo bhavituṁ tavāvatāraḥ kintu jagatpālanārthamapīty āha—mūrtīṁ iti | atrākṣipati—nanv iti | he bhagavann iti—tvaṁ tu sākṣādbhagavāneva lokahitāya prāduṣkṛtamatir iti bhāvaḥ | ity artha iti—bhaktābhīṣṭasampādanāyaiva putrādibhāvena pratīyase na tvaṁ sākṣātputrādiranti bhāvaḥ| na na mātā na pitā tasya ity-ādiśrīdaśamokteḥ | atra jagaddhitāya dhṛtamūrtitve | tatrāpi sṛṣṭyādāvapi | ūrṇanābhirlūtātanturyathānyamanapekṣyaiva svenaiva tantuvitānaṁ kṛtvā tatra vihṛtya ca punaḥ saṁharati tathā tvamapīty arthaḥ ||41||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** _na vyākhyātam._

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **tasmāt sva-bhajanaṁ kārayituṁ bhajana-paripāke ca tvad-bhakta-prema-vaśyo bhavituṁ ca tavāvatāraḥ | na kevalam etad eva nimittaṁ jagat-pālanārtham apīty āha—mūrtī ime iti | mṛtyu-jityai mokṣāya ca | yathā nānānyatanūr matsya-kūrmādyā bibharṣi tathemāmn api tanūṁ bibharṣi | kiṁ ca, sṛṣṭvā yasya pālanārthaṁ tanūr bibharṣi tat sarvaṁ punar grasasi ca ūrṇanābhir ivety adbhutaṁ tava līlā-vaibhavam apīti bhāvaḥ ||41||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.42 ||**

**tasyāvituḥ sthira-careśitur aṅghri-mūlaṁ**

**yat-sthaṁ na karma-guṇa-kāla-rajaḥ spṛśanti |**

**yad vai stuvanti ninamanti yajanty abhīkṣṇaṁ**

**dhyāyanti veda-hṛdayā munayas tad-āptyai ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **yasmād evaṁ-bhūtas tvaṁ tasmāt tavāṅghri-mūlaṁ bhajāmīty āha—tasyeti | tasyāvituḥ pālakasya sthāvara-jaṅgamānām īśvarasyāṅgri-mūlaṁ bhajāmīti tṛtīya-śloka-sthasyānuṣaṅgaḥ | kathaṁ bhūtam aṅghri-mūlam | yat-sthaṁ yatra sthitam | karma-guṇa-kālānāṁ rajo-malam | anye ca pūrvoktās tapādayo na spṛśanti | “rujaḥ” iti va pāṭhaḥ | yato vedo hṛdaye yeṣāṁ te veda-tātparya-vido munayo yad eva stuvanti nitarāṁ namanti tad-āptyai tat-prāptaye eva stavanādi kurvanti ||42||

———————————————————————————————————————

**kaivalya-dīpikā : tasyeti** | **avituḥ** rakṣakasya **īśituḥ** sraṣṭuḥ | saṁhartuś ca **aṅghri-mūlam** | tad uttara-śloka-sthena **bhajāmi** ity anenānvayaḥ | **yat-sthaṁ** yatra sthitaṁ **karma** | puṇya-pāpe guṇā rajaḥ-prabhṛtayaḥ | **kālo** mṛtyuḥ | ta eva vikārāpādakatvāt **rujo** rogāḥ | ete **spṛśanty** apino dūre bādhakārtāḥ | stutir vācā guṇa-kīrtanam | japo manasā | japakṛd uccāra iti dhātu-sūtrāt | **ninamanti** śṛṇvanti, upasarga-yogād ayam arthaḥ | dhātv-arthaṁ bādhate kaścit kaścit tam anuvartate ity upasarga-vṛttī | **vedo hṛdaye** yeṣāṁ te tathā | **tad-āptyai** viṣṇu-prāptaye ||42|| [mu.pha. 10.12]

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **anye ceti bahuvacanopapattaye pūritam iti | rujaḥ iti pāṭhas tu sugamaḥ | evaṁ karmādayo rujaḥ kleśāḥ yatsthaṁ yadaṅghritalasthaṁ bhaktajanaṁ rajaḥ durācārādibhavaṁ mālinyaṁ ca na spṛśantītyadbhutaṁ tava bhaktivaibhavam iti | karmeti—duṣkṛtaṁ sukṛtaṁ prācīnamaprācīnaṁ vā kṛtaṁ na spṛśati puṣkarapalāśaṁ jalamiveti bhāvaḥ | bahutvamārṣam iti viśvanāthaḥ ||42||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** _na vyākhyātam._

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **tasya tavāṅghri-mūlaṁ bhajāmīti tṛtīya-sthasyānuṣaṅgaḥ | yat-sthaṁ yad-aṅghri-tala-sthaṁ bhakta-janaṁ karma-guṇa-kāla-rajo durācāratvādi-bhāvaṁ mālinyañcana spṛśantīti adbhutaṁ tava bhakti-vaibhavam iti karmeti duṣkṛtaṁ sukṛtaṁ prācīnam arvācīnaṁ vā kṛtam api na spṛśatīti puṣkara-palāśe jalam iveti bhāvaḥ | bahutvam ārṣam | yad bhaktā abhīkṣṇaṁ munayo mauna-śīlā veda-hṛdaye vedārtha-tātparya-jñā tat-prāpty-arthaṁ dhyāyanti ||42||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.43 ||**

**nānyaṁ tavāṅghry-upanayād apavarga-mūrteḥ**

**kṣemaṁ janasya parito-bhiya īśa vidmaḥ |**

**brahmā bibhety alam ato dvi-parārdha-dhiṣṇyaḥ**

**kālasya te kim uta tat-kṛta-bhautikānām ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **yato’nyaḥ puruṣārtho nāstīty āha—nānyam iti | aṅghry-upanayāc chrīmac-caraṇa-prāpter anyaṁ kṣemaṁ na vidmaḥ | paritaḥ sarveṣv api lokeṣu bhīr yasya tasya janasya | tad evāha—dvi-parārdhaṁ dhiṣṇyaṁ sthānaṁ yasya, sa brahmāpi te kālasya tvad-bhrū-vijṛmbha-rūpāt kālād alaṁ bibheti | ataḥ kim uta vaktavyam ? tena brahmaṇā kṛtānāṁ bhautikānāṁ prāṇināṁ bhayam iti ||43||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **yatoṅghribhajanāt | tad eva sarvalokabhayatvam eva | yato brahmāpi bibhetyato hetoḥ ||43||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** _na vyākhyātam._

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **aṅghry-upanayāc caraṇa-prāpter anyaṁ kṣemaṁ kuśalaṁ parito-bhiyaḥ saṁsārād bibhyato janasya na vidmaḥ yato brahmety-ādi, te kālasya kāla-svarūpāt, itaḥ asmāt | kim uta vaktavyam ? tat-kṛtānāṁ brahma-kṛtānāṁ bhautikānāṁ prāṇināṁ bhayam iti ||43||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.44 ||**

**tad vai bhajāmy ṛta-dhiyas tava pāda-mūlaṁ**

**hitvedam ātma-cchadi cātma-guroḥ parasya |**

**dehādy apārtham asad antyam abhijña-mātraṁ**

**vindeta te tarhi sarva-manīṣitārtham ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **yasmād evaṁ tat tasmāt tava pāda-mūlaṁ bhajāmi | kathaṁ-bhūtasya ? ṛta-dhiyaḥ satya-jñāna-svarūpasya | yad vā, satyā dhīr yasya yasmin vā tasyātma-guror jīva-niyantur ataḥ kāraṇāt parasya | kiṁ kṛtvā ? ātma-cchadi svātmāvarakam apārthaṁ ca niṣphalam asac ca tuccham antyaṁ ca naś caram idaṁ dehādi hitvā dehādi-bhajanaṁ tyaktvā | asac cet kathaṁ pratīyeta ? tatrāha—abhijña-mātram | na hy atyantam asat, kintv ātma-mātram | na tataḥ pṛthag astīty arthaḥ | 

nanv apavargāya bhavatu mad-bhajanam, phalāntarārthaṁ tv anya-bhajanaṁ kāryam eva tatrāha—tarhīti | yadi tvāṁ bhajati puruṣas tarhi te tvatta eva sarvaṁ manīṣitam arthaṁ vindeteti ||44||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **jñānarūpasya pādakalpanamayuktaṁ matvāha—yadveti | ity artha iti—na hi cetanādhiṣṭhānaṁ vinācitaḥ pratītirupapadyata iti bhāvaḥ| atrākṣipati—nanv iti | akāmaḥ sarvakāmo vā mokṣakāma udāradhīḥ ity uktes tvatta eva sarvābhīṣṭāptirbhavatīti bhāvaḥ ||44||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tad vā iti | tair abhijña-mātram ity asya ṭīkāyām ātma-mātram iti ātmany adhiṣṭhāne bhramād eva pratītir yasya tad ity arthaḥ ||44||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **ṛta-dhiyaḥ satya-jñānasya | ātma-cchadi hitvā ātma-cchādakaṁ dehādi deha-gehādi-mamatvaṁ tyaktvā apārthaṁ niṣphalam asat tuccham antyaṁ naśvaram | evam anyo’pi yo bhajati sa te tvām abhijña-mātraṁ bhakta-sevābhijñam eva prāpnoti | nanu tarhi niṣkāma eva māṁ bhajatu, sakāmas tv anyaṁ, tatrāha—tarhīti | yadi tvāṁ vindeta, tarhi sarva-manīṣitārthaṁ vindetaiva ||44||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.45 ||**

**sattvaṁ rajas tama itīśa tavātma-bandho**

**māyā-mayāḥ sthiti-layodaya-hetavo’sya |**

**līlā dhṛtā yad api sattva-mayī praśāntyai**

**nānye nṛṇāṁ vyasana-moha-bhiyaś ca yābhyām ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **nanu brahma-rudrāv api mamaiva mūrtī, ato mām eva kim atyantam ādriyase ? tatrāha—sattvam iti | yad api yady api tavaiva māyayā kṛṭa etā līlās tvayaiva dhṛtāḥ, tathāpi yā sattva-mayī, saiva praśāntyai mokṣāya, na kevalam asya praśānty-abhāva-mātram anya-bhajane kintv aniṣṭaṁ ca bhaved ity āha—vyasaneti ||45||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **punarākṣipati—nanv iti | he īśeti—he ātmabandho iti sambuddhidvyena harer eva bhajanīyatvam āha | yadyapyubhayavidhatvaṁ brahmarudrayor apy asti tathāpi śuddhasattvapradhānasya tavaiva kalyāṇahetutvaṁ saṅgacchate śreyāṁsi tatra khalu sattvatanornṛṇāṁ syuḥ ity-ādy-ukter iti saṁbuddhyabhiprāyaḥ| etā brahmarudrādilakṣaṇāḥ | anye rajastamomayyau līle praśāntya netyarthaḥ | asya rajastamomayyau lole bhajataḥ puṁsaḥ kintvanyasya śuddhasattvetarasya bhajane'niṣṭaṁ ca syāt, kiṁ tadaniṣṭaṁ bhavettatrāha—vyasaneti | vyasanaṁ vipat, moho'jñānam, bhīḥ saṁsārabhayaṁ ca yābhyāṁ rajastamomayīlīlābhyāṁ syurity arthaḥ | yad vā, anye sattvādanye rajastamasī praśāntyai na syātāṁ, yābhyāṁ rajastamobhyāṁ vyasanādayaḥ syuḥ | ca evārtho | viśvanāthastu—sakāmatve sati devāntaram api bhajantu tadbhajanam eva yato devā manmūrtaya evetyata āha—sattvam iti | he ātmabandho prāṇanātha asyendracandradeva-manuṣyādimayasya jagataḥ sthity-ādihetavaḥ sattvādayo ye guṇāste'pi māyāmayā eva kiṁ punastatkāryā indrādyā naśvarāḥ| teṣāṁ bhajane māyātītaṁ tvāṁ kathaṁ videteti bhāvaḥ | yadyapyāsu līlāsu madhye sattvamayī līlā praśāntyai dhṛtā na tvanye rajastamomayyau yābhyāṁ vyasanādayaḥ santi tadapyetāstisro'pi līlā māyāmayya eveti ||45||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tasya śrī-bhagavataḥ sattvasya prākṛtaād anyatmatvam āha—sattvaṁ raja iti dvayam | anayor arthaḥ—he īśa ! yady api sattvaṁ rajas tama iti tavaiva māyā-kṛtā līlāḥ, katham-bhūtāḥ ? asya viśvasya sthity-ādi-hetavaḥ, tathāpi yā sattva-mayī saiva praśāntyai prakṛṣṭa-sukhāya bhavati, nānye rajas-tamo-mayyau | na kevalaṁ praśānty-abhāva-mātram anayoḥ, kintv aniṣṭaṁ cety āha—vyasaneti ||45|| [bhagavat-sandarbhaḥ 7]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **nanu sa-kāmatve sati devāntaram api bhajatu, tat-tad-bhajanam api mad-bhajanam eva, yato devā man-mūrtaya eva te, iti tatrāha—sattvam iti | ātma-bandho ! he prāṇa-nātha ! asya indra-candrādi-deva-manuṣyādi-mayasya jagataḥ sthity-ādi-hetavaḥ sattvādayo guṇāḥ | te’pi māyā-mayā eva, kiṁ punas tat-kāryā indrādyā naśvarāḥ | teṣāṁ bhajane māyātītaṁ tvāṁ kathaṁ vinde ? iti bhāvaḥ | yadyapy āsu līlāsu madhye sattva-mayī līlā praśāntyai dhṛtā, na tv anye rajas-tamo-mayyau yābhyāṁ vyasana-moha-bhiyā bhavanti | tad apy etās tisro’pi līlā māyā-mayya evety anvayaḥ ||45||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.46 ||**

**tasmāt taveha bhagavann atha tāvakānāṁ **

**śuklāṁ tanuṁ sva-dayitāṁ kuśalā bhajanti |**

**yat sātvatāḥ puruṣa-rūpam uśanti sattvaṁ**

**loko yato’bhayam utātma-sukhaṁ na cānyat ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tad eva sad-ācāreṇa draḍhayati—tasmād iti | he bhagavan ! tava śuklāṁ tanuṁ śrī-nārāyaṇākhyām | atha tāvakānāṁ ca śuklāṁ tanuṁ narākhyām | yad yasmāt sātvatāḥ sattvam eva puruṣasyeśvarasya rūpam uśanti manyante, na tv anyad rajas tamaś ceti | atra hetuḥ, yataḥ sattvāl loko vaikuṇṭḥākhyo lokatve saty apy abhayaṁ ca bhoge saty apy ātma-sukhaṁ ca ||46||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tad eva sattvamayabhajanam eva | yata sattvam eva praśāntihetustasmāddhetoḥ he bhagavann iti | bhajanārhatām āha | atra sattvasya puruṣarūpatve | atas tava māyāmayīmindrādimūrtimaśuddhāṁ vihāya śuddhasattvarūpā eva tava tvadbhaktānāṁ ca mūrtirabhījñā upāsata ityāha—tasmād iti | yadyataḥ sātvatā nāradādyāḥ puruṣarūpaṁ satvamuśanti | nanu kīdṛśaṁ sattvaṁ tatrāha—yato lokaḥ svargādikaḥ na yatrābhayaṁ pātahatukabhayābhāvaḥ, ātmasukhamātmabhūtaṁ sukhaṁ ca na tu karmaphalaṁ sa loko vaikuṇṭhaḥ | yatas tat śuddhasattvaṁ na cānyatprākṛtaṁ sattvam ||46||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** he bhagavan ! tasmāt tava śuklāṁ sattva-maya-līlādhiṣṭhātrīṁ tanuṁ śrī-viṣṇu-rūpāṁ kuśalā nipuṇā bhajanti sevante, na tv anyāṁ brahma-rudra-rūpāṁ te bhajanti anusaranti | na tu dakṣa-bhairavādi-rūpām | katham-bhūtām ? svasya tavāpi dayitāṁ loka-śānti-karatvāt |

nanu mama rūpam api sattvātmakam iti prasiddham | tarhi kathaṁ tasyāpi māyāmayatvam eva ? nahi nahīty āha—sātvatāḥ śrī-bhāgavatā yat sattvaṁ puruṣasya tava rūpaṁ prakāśam uśanti manyante, yataś ca sattvāt loko vaikuṇṭhākhyaḥ prakāśate, tad abhayam ātma-sukhaṁ para-brahmānanda-svarūpam evalakṣaṇa-svarūpa-śakti-vṛtti-viśeṣa ucyate |


    sattvaṁ viśuddhaṁ vasudeva-śabditaṁ


    yad īyate tatra pumān apāvṛtaḥ | [bhā.pu. 4.3.23]

ity-ādy-udāhariṣyamāṇānusārāt | 

agocarasya gocare hetuḥ—PTāpratyakṣa-vastuunaḥ pratyakṣatve kāraṇaṁ PTa-Gaḥ sattvam ity aśuddha-sattva-La-prasiddhy-anusāreṇa, tathāPTāpratyakṣa-vastunaḥ pratyakṣatve KAf SVa-BTa-cic-chakti-vṛtti-viśeṣo’PTa-Go viśuddha-sattvam iti saṅgati-lābhāc ca | tataś ca tasya svarūpa-śakti-vṛttitvena svarūpātmataivety uktam, tad abhayam ātma-sukham iti | 

kitvāprādhānya-vivakṣayoktaṁ—loko yata iti | arthāntare bhagavad-vigrahaṁ prati rūpaṁ yad etad [bhā.pu. 2.8.2] ity ādau śuddha-sattva-svarūpa-mātratva-pratijñā-bhaṅgaḥ | abhayam ity ādau prāñjalatā-hāniś ca bhavati | anyat padasyaikasyaiva rajas tamaś ceti dvir-āvṛttau pratipatti-gauravaṁ cotpadyate | pūrvam api nānye iti dvi-vacanenaiva parāmṛṣṭe ||46|| [bhagavat-sandarbhaḥ 7[^57]]

yad evaikādaśe yat kāya eṣa bhuvana-traya-sanniveśa [bhā.pu. 11.4.4] ity ādau, jñānaṁ svata ity atra ṭīkā-kṛn-mataṁ yasya svarūpa-bhūtāt sattvāt tanu-bhṛtāṁ jñānam ity anena | tathā paro-rajaḥ savitur jāta-vedā devasya bharga [bhā.pu. 5.7.14] ity ādau śrī-bharata-jāpye tan-mataṁ paro-rajaḥ rajasaḥ prakṛteḥ paraṁ śuddha-sattvātmakam ity ādinā | ata eva prākṛtāḥ sattvādayo guṇā jīvasyaiva, na tv īśasyeti śrūyate | athaikādaśe sattvaṁ rajas tama iti guṇā jīvasya naiva me [bhā.pu. 11.25.12] iti |

śrī-bhagavad-upaniṣatsu ca—


    ye caiva sāttvikā bhāvā rājasās tāmasāś ca ye |


    matta eveti tān viddhi na tv ahaṁ teṣu te mayi ||


    tribhir guṇa-mayair bhāvair ebhiḥ sarvam idaṁ jagat |


    mohitaṁ nābhijānāti mām ebhyaḥ param avyayam ||


    daivī hy eṣā guṇa-mayī mama māyā duratyayā |


    mām eva ye prapadyante māyām etāṁ taranti te || [gītā 7.12-4] iti |

yathā daśame—


    harir hi nirguṇaḥ sākṣāt puruṣaḥ prakṛteḥ paraḥ |


    sa sarva-dṛg upadraṣṭā taṁ bhajan nirguṇo bhavet || [bhā.pu. 10.88.5] iti |

śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe ca—


    sattvādayo na santīśe yatra ca prākṛtā guṇāḥ |


    sa śuddhaḥ sarva-śuddhebhyaḥ pumān ādyaḥ prasīdatu || [vi.pu. 1.9.44] iti |

atra prākṛtā iti viśiṣya aprākṛtās tv anye guṇās tasmin santy eveti vyañjitaṁ tatraiva | 


    hlādinī sandhinī saṁvit tvayy ekā sarva-saṁśraye |


    hlāda-tāpa-karī miśrā tvayi no guṇa-varjite || [vi.pu. 1.12.69] iti |

tathā ca daśame devendreṇoktam—


    viśuddha-sattvaṁ tava dhāma śāntaṁ


    tapomayaṁ dhvasta-rajas-tamaskam |


    māyāmayo’yaṁ guṇa-saṁpravāho


    na vidyate te’graṇānubandha || [bhā.pu. 10.27.4] iti |

ayam arthaḥ—dhāma svarūpa-bhūta-prakāśa-śaktiḥ | viśuddhatvam āha viśeṣaṇa-dvayena | dhvasta-rajas-tamaskaṁ tapo-mayam iti ca | tapo’tra jñānaṁ sa tapo’tapyateti śruteḥ | tapomayaṁ pracura-jñāna-svarūpam | jāḍyāṁśenāpi rahitam ity arthaḥ | ātmā jñāna-mayaḥ śuddha itivat | ataḥ prākṛta-sattvam api vyāvṛttam | ata eva māyāmayo’yaṁ sattvādi-guṇa-pravāhas te tava na vidyate | yato’sāv ajñānenaivānubandha iti |

ata eva śrī-bhagavantaṁ prati brahmādīnāṁ sa-yuktikam—sattvaṁ viśuddhaṁ śrayate bhavān sthitau [bhā.pu. 10.2.34-35]ity-ādi-dvābhyām uktam ||46||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** atas tava māyā-mayīm indrādi-mūrtim aśuddhāṁ vihāya śuddha-sattva-svarūpā eva tava tvad-bhaktānāṁ ca mūrtīr abhijñā upāsate ity āha—tasmād iti | yataḥ sātvatā nāradādyāḥ puruṣa-rūpaṁ viṣṇu-svarūpaṁ sattvam uśanti | nanu kīdṛśaṁ sattvam ? tatrāha—yato lokaḥ, kiṁ svargādikaḥ, na yatra abhayaṁ pāta-hetuka-bhayābhāvaḥ, ātma-sukham ātma-bhūtaṁ sukhaṁ ca, na tu karma-phalaṁ, sa-loko vaikuṇṭho yatas tat śuddha-sattvaṁ, na cānyat prākṛtaṁ sattvam ||46||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.47 ||**

**tasmai namo bhagavate puruṣāya bhūmne **

**viśvāya viśva-gurave para-devatāya |**

**nārāyaṇāya ṛṣaye ca narottamāya **

**haṁsāya saṁyata-gire nigameśvarāya ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **atataṁ praṇamati, tasmai nama iti | haṁsāya śuddhāya | saṁyata-gire niyata-vāce | atha ca nigameśvarāya veda-mārga-pravartakāya ||47||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ataḥ sātvatopāsyatvāt | viśvāya viśvanāmne viśvaṁ viṣṇurvaṣaṭkāraḥ iti sahasranāmasūkteḥ | sarvanāmasaṁjñā tvatrābhidhātvādeva | na niyatā vedalakṣaṇā vāgyasya tasmai, tad evāha—atha ceti | ata eva viśvagurave sarvahitopadeṣṭre | parā sarvotkṛṣṭā cāsau devatā ca paramātmaiva tadrūpāya | nārāyaṇāya sarvaprerakāya | ṛṣaye sarvajñāya| narājjīvājīvādarthātkṣarākṣarādattamāya puruṣottamāyetyarthaḥ | 


    yasmāt kṣaram atīto'ham akṣarād api cottamaḥ | 


    ato'smi loke vede ca prathitaḥ puruṣottamaḥ || iti gītāsūkteḥ | 

naro jīve śarīre ca ghoṭake ca kapidhvaje | dharmātmaje ityabhidhānāt puruṣāya puruṣākāratve'pi bhūmne sarva-vyāpakāya, tadapi viśvāya deva-manuṣya-tiryag-ādi-sarva-rūpāya | āvibhova-prayojanam āha—viśvagurave bhaktijñānavairāgyāṇāmupadeṣṭre | na kevalamupadeṣṭaivāpi tu bhajanīyaścetyāha—paradevatāyai iṣṭadevāya | dvābhyām ekākāratvam āha—ṛṣaye ṛṣirūpanārāyaṇāya ṛṣirūpanarottamāya ca | tyaktaparigrahatvam āha—haṁsāya | maunaśālitvam āha saṁyatagire, tadapi nigamāya vedapravartakāya ||47||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**
