———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** puruṣāya puruṣākāratve’pi bhūmne sarva-vyāpakāya, tad api viśvāya daiva-manuṣya-tiryag-ādi-sarva-rūpāya | āvirbhāva-prayojanam āha—viśva-gurave bhakti-jñāna-.viśeṣāṇām upadeṣṭre | na kevalam upadeṣṭaiva tvam api tu bhajanīyaś cety āha—para-devatāyai abhīṣṭa-devāya dvābhyām ekāvatāratvam āha—ṛṣaye ṛṣi-rūpa-nārāyaṇāya ṛṣi-rūpa-narottamāya ca | tyakta-parigrahatvam āha—haṁsāya | mauna-śālitvam āha—saṁyata-gire | tad api nigameśvarāya veda-pravartakāya ||47||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.48 ||**

**yaṁ vai na veda vitathākṣa-pathair bhramad-dhīḥ**

**santaṁ svakeṣv asuṣu hṛdy api dṛk-patheṣu |**

**tan-māyayāvṛta-matiḥ sa u eva sākṣād**

**ādyas tavākhila-guror upasādya vedam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **vedārtha-saṁpradāya-pravartane hetutvaṁ vadan stauti—yam iti | vitathākṣa-pathaiḥ kapaṭendriya-mārgair bhramad-dhīr vikṣipta-buddhiḥ pumān svendriyādiṣu niyantṛtvena santam api yaṁ tvāṁ na veda | dṛk-patheṣu viṣayeṣu | buddhi-vikṣepe hetuḥ, tan-māyayā tasya tavaiva māyayā āvṛtā ātma-niṣṭhā matir yasya sa u so’pi ādya eva pūrvam avidvān evākhila-guros tava tvat-pravartitaṁ vedam upasādya prāpya taṁ tvāṁ sākṣād veda ||48||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **jagadapekṣayādibhavatvādādyo brahmā tvattaḥ sarvagurorvedaṁ prāpyāpi na veda, anyeṣāṁ kā varteti bhāvaḥ | sa u so'pi, ur apy arthe |  pūrvaṁ vedaprāpteḥ pūrvāvasthāyāmavidvān tava sakāśādvedamavasādyaiva yamindriyavikṣiptadhīrna veda taṁ vedetyanvayaḥ | svāmicaraṇairādya eva, avidvāneveti yortho gṛhītastatra brahmākṣepalabdha iti dhyeyam ||48||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **svendriyeṣu santam api eṣām eva vivaraṇam asuṣu karmendriyeṣu dṛk-patheṣu jñānendriyeṣu hṛdy ubhayātmake, nāhaṁ prakāśaḥ sarvasya yoga-māyā-samāvṛtaḥ [gītā 7.25] iti śrī-gītopaniṣadbhyaḥ ||48||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **sarva-durjñeyatvam āha—yaṁ vaīti vitathāṅga-pathaiḥ kapaṭendriya-mārgair bhramad-dhīr vikṣipta-buddhiḥ pumān svendriyeṣu asuṣu prāṇeṣu hṛdy api niyantṛtvena santam api yaṁ tvāṁ na veda | sampraty avatāra-samaye dṛk-patheṣu santam api tvāṁ tan-māyayā tayā prasiddhayā māyayā āvṛta-matir na veda | anyeṣāṁ kā vārtā sa u prasiddhaḥ ādyo brahmāpi te’khila-guroḥ sākṣād vedam upasādya prāpyāpi yaṁ tvāṁ naiva veda ||48||

 **...**

**|| 12.8.49 ||**

**yad-darśanaṁ nigama ātma-rahaḥ-prakāśaṁ**

**muhyanti yatra kavayo’ja-parā yatantaḥ |**

**taṁ sarva-vāda-viṣaya-pratirūpa-śīlaṁ**

**vande mahā-puruṣam ātma-nigūḍha-bodham ||**[^58]

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **vedenaiva tvaj-jñānam ity upapādayan praṇamati—yasya tava darśanaṁ nigame bhavati | kathaṁ-bhūtam ? ātmanas tava raho rahasyaṁ tasya prakāśakam | anyathā durjñeyatām adha, aja-parā brahma-mukhyāḥ kavayo’pi sāñkhya-yogādibhir yatamānā yatra tvayi muhyanti | kutaḥ ? ity ata āha—sarveṣāṁ sāṅkhyādi-vādināṁ ye vādās teṣāṁ viṣayā bhedādayas teṣāṁ pratirūpaṁ tat-tad-anusāri śīlaṁ svabhāvo yasya tam | kutaḥ ? ātmanā dehādi-saṅghātena nigūḍho bodho yasya tam | evaṁ-bhūtaṁ mahā-puruṣaṁ tvāṁ vande ||49||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **nigamo vedaḥ | nigamo vāṇije puryāṁ kaṭe vede vaṇikpathe iti medinī | ajo brahmā para utkṛṣṭo yeṣu te tathā | kuto muhyanti—vādāḥ siddhātāḥ siddhānte ca vivāde ca vādastome ca vādinām iti niruktiḥ | sarvavādānusāriśīlatve hetuṁ pṛcchati—kuta iti | dehādyātmavādanirāsena yajjñānaṁ jāyate taṁ vande | bodho'tra pratyaksvarūpam eva dehādyātmavādanirāsaścādyapadyavyākhyāśatake nirūpita eva | vedaśāstrajñeyatve'pi durjñeyatvam āha—yasya tava darśanaṁ jñānaṁ nigamaṁ vedaśāstra eva | kīdṛśam—ātmanastava rahasyasya prakāśakam | tarhi vedajñā eva māṁ jānantu tatra netyāha—muhyantīti | yatra vede brahmamukhyā api munayo yatanto'pi bhavattattvājñānānmuhyanti vedasya parokṣavāditvādbhavanmātrajñeyatvam iti bhāvaḥ | ata eva hetugarbhaṁ viśinaṣṭi—sarve vādāvivartādayo nigamoktāsteṣāṁ viṣayāś ca ye teṣāṁ pratirūpam eva na tvanurūpaṁ śīlaṁ caritraṁ yasya tamata eva gūḍho guptīkṛto bodhastasvatattvaṁ yena tam ||49||

iti śrīmad-bhāgavata-bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśe dvādaśa-skandhe'ṣṭamo'dhyāyaḥ ||8||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **veda-śāstra-jñeyatve’pi durjñeyatvam āha—yasya tava darśanaṁ jñānaṁ nigame veda-śāstra eva | kīdṛśam ? ātmanas tava rahasyasya prakāśakam | nanu tarhi veda-darśina eva māṁ jānantu, tatra nety āha—muhyantīti yatra vede aja-parāḥ ajo brahmā paraḥ śreṣṭho yeṣām | te munayo’pi yajanto’pi bhavat-tattvājñānān muhyanti | nigamasya parokṣa-vāditvād bhavan-mātra-jñeyatvam iti bhāvaḥ | ata eva hetu-garbhaṁ viśinaṣṭi—sarve vādā vivartādayo nigamoktās teṣāṁ viṣayāś ca ye teṣāṁ pratirūpam eva, na tv anurūpaṁ śīlaṁ caritraṁ yasya tam | ata evātmany eva gūḍho guptīkṛto bodhaḥ sva-tattvaṁ yena tam ||49||

iti sārārtha-darśinyāṁ harṣiṇyāṁ bhakta-cetasām |

dvādaśe’trāṣṭamo’dhyāyaḥ saṅgataḥ saṅgataḥ satām ||*||

 **...**


    iti śrīmad-bhāgavate mahā-purāṇe brahma-sūtra-bhāṣye pāramahaṁsyaṁ saṁhitāyāṁ vaiyāsikyāṁ daśama-skandhe 


    nārāyaṇa-stavo nāma 


    aṣṭamo’dhyāyaḥ |

|| 12.8 ||

**…**

**(12.9)**


### navamo’dhyāyaḥ


## mārkaṇḍeyasya māyā-darśanaṁ

**|| 12.9.1 ||**

**sūta uvāca—**

**saṁstuto bhagavān itthaṁ mārkaṇḍeyena dhīmatā |**

**nārāyaṇo nara-sakhaḥ prīta āha bhṛgūdvaham ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **

navame bhagavan-māyādi- dṛkṣor darśanaṁ muhuḥ |

māyā-śiśor layābdhau ca muner nirveśa-nirgamaiḥ ||

bhagavataḥ paritoṣa-pūrvakaṁ tad apekṣita-vara-dānaṁ kathayitum āha, saṁstuta ity-ādinā ||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **munerlayābdhau pralayakālikasamudre, māyayā kṛpayā, śiśoḥ śiśurūpasya | nirveśaḥ praveśaḥ, nirgamo bahirāgamanam | bhṛgūdvahaṁ mārkaṇḍeyam ||1||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :**

māyā-darśanajaṁ duḥkhaṁ navame tu muneḥ śiśau |

praveśo niṣkramaḥ pāto layābdhau varṇyate muhuḥ ||1||

 **...**

**|| 12.9.2 ||**

**śrī-bhagavān uvāca—**

**bho bho brahmarṣi-varyo’si siddha ātma-samādhinā |**

**mayi bhaktyānapāyinyā tapaḥ-svādhyāya-saṁyamaiḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ātma-samādhinā cittaikāgryeṇa ||2||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tapaḥ-svādhyāya-saṁyamair ya ātma-samādhiś cittaikāgryaṁ, tena yā anapāyinī bhaktiḥ, tayā siddho’sīty anvayaḥ ||2||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** _na vyākhyātam._

 **...**

**|| 12.9.3 ||**

**vayaṁ te parituṣṭāḥ sma tvad-bṛhad-vrata-caryayā |**

**varaṁ pratīccha bhadraṁ te varado’smi tvad-īpsitam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **vayaṁ te parituṣṭāḥ smeti bahu-vacanaṁ sarva-devābhiprāyeṇa | vara-deśād ity eka-vacanaṁ dvayor aikyābhiprāyeṇa | pratīccha gṛhāṇa ||3||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **bho bho iti vīpsādare | he brahmarṣivaryeti—brahmarṣayo madarśanārthaṁ yatantyeva na tu prāpnuvanti tvayā tatprāptamatas teṣu tvam eva śreṣṭho'sīti bhāvaḥ ||2-3||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** vayam iti bahu-vacanam agre prastoṣyamāṇa-śivomādy-abhiprāyeṇa ||3|| 

 **...**

**|| 12.9.4 ||**

**śrī-ṛṣir uvāca—**

**jitaṁ te deva-deveśa prapannārti-harācyuta |**

**vareṇaitāvatālaṁ no yad bhavān samadṛśyata ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **vareṇa cchandayatā tvayā jitam utkarṣo darśitaḥ | mama tu varākāṅkṣā nāstīty āha—vareṇeti ||4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **te jitaṁ tavotkarṣo'styeva svotkarṣeṇaiva mamājñānamapahṛtam | devā indrādyāsteṣāṁ devo brahmā tasyāpi tvameveśosīti bhāvaḥ | prapannānāṁ mādṛśānāmārti saṁsṛtiduḥkhaṁ haratīti tādṛśo'pi tvam eva | cyutirnāśastadrahito'pi tvameva, aho etādṛśasya tava darśane kimahaṁ tucchaṁ varaṁ yāca iti bhāvaḥ | etāvatā etatpramāṇakena | etāvatā kiyateti cettatrāha—yad iti ||4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **etāvatā vareṇaivālaṁ paryāptir jātā | kiṁ tat ? yad bhavān iti ||4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** jitaṁ te tava sarvotkarṣo’sty eva ||4||

 **...**

**|| 12.9.5 ||**

**gṛhītvājādayo yasya śrīmat-pādābja-darśanam |**

**manasā yoga-pakvena sa bhavān me’kṣi-gocaraḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : yasya** tava **śrīmat-pādābja-darśanaṁ manasāpi gṛhītvā** prāpya kṛtārthā **ajādayo** bhavanti, **sa bhavān me’kṣi-gocaro** jāto’sti | kim ataḥ paraṁ vareṇety arthaḥ ||5||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ity artha iti—tava darśanātparo na kopi varo'dhiko'stīti bhāvaḥ ||5||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **yato gṛhītveti | ajādayo’pi kṛtārthā bhavantīti śeṣaḥ ||5||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **gṛhītvā kṛtārthino bhavantīti śeṣaḥ ||5||

 **...**

**|| 12.9.6 ||**

**athāpy ambuja-patrākṣa puṇya-śloka-śikhāmaṇe |**

**drakṣye māyāṁ yayā lokaḥ sa-pālo veda sad-bhidām ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **drakṣye draṣṭum icchāmi | loka-pālair brahmādibhiḥ sahito’yaṁ loko jano yayā sad-bhidāṁ sati vastuni bhedam ||6||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **he abujapatrākṣeti—tava svābhāvikatāpaharadṛṣṭerna kiñcidvaktavyamastīti bhāvaḥ | puṇyaślokā api svayaśorakṣaṇāya vinaivānyapreraṇāṁ parakāryaṁ kurvānti tvaṁ tu teṣāṁ śikhāmaṇiḥ paramamukhya iti bhāvaḥ ||6||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **athāpi prārabdha-maya-kautuka-vaśatayeti bhāvaḥ | nanu jagat paśyan mama māyāṁ paśyann evāsi ? tatrāha—yayeti | antaḥ sato bahir bhidāṁ vidāraṇaṁ pralayaṁ yayā mad-viditayā satyā mad-dvārā anyo’pi sapālo loko veda jānīyāt ||6||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** drakṣye didṛkṣe | sataḥ kāraṇasya bhidāṁ kāryākāreṇa nāmābhedam | yad vā, sato dvaita-prapañcasya bhidāṁ pralaye sati vidāraṇam ||6||

 **...**

**|| 12.9.7 ||**

**sūta uvāca—**

**itīḍito’rcitaḥ kāmam ṛṣiṇā bhagavān mune |**

**tatheti sa smayan prāgād badary-āśramam īśvaraḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tatheti drakṣyasīti | sa īśvaraḥ smayan prāgāt | ṣāṭhāntare kriya-viśeṣaṇam ||7||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** smayann iti | māyā-darśanaṁ duḥkhānubhava-hetur eva kevalam | sa eva varo vriyate ced datta eva, varsyāvaśya-deyatvāt | kintu māyā-darśana-kautukaṁ mayānāsvāditam ity anyathāsya tad-anububhūṣā naiva nivartiṣyate, tasmād duḥkham anubhūyaiva tato nivartatām | yathā sva-duḥkha-hetāv api karmaṇi kvacit pravartamāne haṭhini sva-sute nivartayitum asamarthasya pitur apy anujñā-pradānam eveti | kintu bhaktasyāsya nirvṛty-arthaṁ śiśu-rūpeṇa tan-madhye’pi sva-darśanānando’dāsyata evety abhiprāya-vyañjakaṁ smitam ||7||

 **...**

**|| 12.9.8 ||**

**tam eva cintayann artham ṛṣiḥ svāśrama eva saḥ |**

**vasann agny-arka-somāmbu- bhū-vāyu-viyad-ātmasu ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tam evārthaṁ māyā-darśana-rūpam | agnyādi-mūrtiṣu ||8||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tam eva śrī-harim eva arthaṁ paramārtha-rūpaṁ cintayan, na tu māyā-darśanam ity arthaḥ | sva-karma-phala-nirdiṣṭam iti nyāyena ||8||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** tam evārthaṁ māyā-darśana-rūpam ||8|| 

 **...**

**|| 12.9.9 ||**

**dhyāyan sarvatra ca hariṁ bhāva-dravyair apūjayat |**

**kvacit pūjāṁ visasmāra prema-prasara-samplutaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : bhāva-dravyair** mano-mayair dravyaiḥ | **kvacit** kadācit **prema-prasara-samplutaḥ** premodrekaṁ prāptaḥ ||9||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** **bhāva-dravyair** mano-mayaiḥ ||9||

 **...**

**|| 12.9.10 ||**

**tasyaikadā bhṛgu-śreṣṭha puṣpabhadrā-taṭe muneḥ |**

**upāsīnasya sandhyāyāṁ brahman vāyur abhūn mahān ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **māyā-darśanam āha—tasyety-ādinā ||10||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **pāṭhāntare sasmayam iti pāṭhe ||7-10||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.9.11 ||**

**taṁ caṇḍa-śabdaṁ samudīrayantaṁ**

**balāhakā anv abhavan karālāḥ |**

**akṣa-sthaviṣṭhā mumucus taḍidbhiḥ**

**svananta uccair abhi varṣa-dhārāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **taṁ vāyum anu balāhakā meghā abhavann āvir babhūvuḥ | te ca taḍidbhiḥ sahitā uccaiḥ svananto garjantaḥ | akṣo rathāṅgaṁ tadvat sthaviṣṭhā abhito varṣa-dhārā mumucuḥ ||11||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **akṣā sthāṅgaṁ  cakram | sthaviṣṭhāḥ sthūlāḥ ||11||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** akṣo rathāṅgaṁ tadvad atisthūlāḥ ||11||

 **...**

**|| 12.9.12 ||**

**tato vyadṛśyanta catuḥ samudrāḥ**

**samantataḥ kṣmā-talam āgrasantaḥ |**

**samīra-vegormibhir ugra-nakra-**

**mahā-bhayāvarta-gabhīra-ghoṣāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **catur dikṣu vartamānāḥ samudrāḥ samīra-vegenormayas tair bhūtalaṁ grasantaḥ | ugrā nakrā yeṣu, mahā-bhayā āvartā yeṣu, gabhīro ghoṣo yeṣu, te ca te ca te ca ||12||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tato mahāvṛṣṭyanantaram ||12||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.9.13 ||**

**antar bahiś cādbhir ati-dyubhiḥ kharaiḥ**

**śatahradābhir upatāpitaṁ jagat |**

**catur-vidhaṁ vīkṣya sahātmanā munir**

**jalāplutāṁ kṣmāṁ vimanāḥ samatrasat ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ātmanā saha jarā-yujādi-catur-vidhaṁ jagad antar bahiś copatāpitaṁ vīkṣya | kṣmāṁ jalāplutāṁ vīkṣya | muniḥ samatrasad bhayaṁ prāpa | kenopatāpitam ? adbhiḥ | kathaṁ-bhūtābhiḥ ? atidyubhir atikrāntā dyaur yābhiḥ | svaraiś ca sūrya-raśmibhir vāyubhir veti śeṣaḥ | śata-hradābhiś ca vidyudbhiḥ | dīrghatvam ārṣaṁ chando’nusāreṇa ||13||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **śampāśatahradāhrādinyairāvatyaḥ kṣaṇaprabhā | taḍitsaudāmanī vidyut ity amaraḥ ||13||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** atikrāntā dyaur yābhis tābhir adbhiḥ | kharaiḥ sūrya-raśmibhiḥ śata-hradābhir vidyudbhiḥ | dīrghatvam ārṣam ||13||

 **...**

**|| 12.9.14 ||**

**tasyaivam udvīkṣata ūrmi-bhīṣaṇaḥ**

**prabhañjanāghūrṇita-vār mahārṇavaḥ |**

**āpūryamāṇo varaṣadbhir ambudaiḥ**

**kṣmām apyadhād dvīpa-varṣādribhiḥ samam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **prabhañjanenāghūrṇitaṁ prakampitaṁ vāḥ udakaṁ yasmin saḥ | apy adhācchādayām āsa | samaṁ saha ||14||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **prabhañjano vāyuḥ | varaṣadbhir iti varṇavibhāgaśchāndasaḥ ||14||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.9.15 ||**

**sa-kṣmāntarikṣaṁ sa-divaṁ sa-bhā-gaṇaṁ**

**trai-lokyam āsīt saha digbhir āplutam |**

**sa eka evorvarito mahā-munir**

**babhrāma vikṣipya jaṭā jaḍāndha-vat ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **sa-kṣmāntarikṣaṁ bhūmy-antarikṣa-stha-prāṇi-sahitam | sa-divaṁ svarga-stha-deva-sahitam | bhāgaṇā jyotir gaṇās taiḥ sahitam | jaṭā vikṣipya vikīrya ||15||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **urvaritaḥ avaśiṣṭaḥ ||15||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** sabhāgaṇaṁ jyotir-gaṇa-sahitam ||15||

 **...**

**|| 12.9.16 ||**

**kṣut-tṛṭ-parīto makarais timiṅgilair**

**upadruto vīci-nabhasvatāhataḥ |**

**tamasy apāre patito bhraman diśo**

**na veda khaṁ gāṁ ca pariśrameṣitaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **pariśrameṇa iṣito gataḥ prāpta ity arthaḥ | iṣu sarpaṇe ity asmāt ||16||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **kṣuttṛśḍbhyāṁ parīto vyāptaḥ | makaratimiṅgilau pādo bhedau timiśśatayojano matsyaḥ iti kośāt | ity artha iti—dhātoḥ sarpaṇārthatvātsarpaṇaṁ prasaraṇam iti vyākhyeyam ||16||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** vīci-yuktena nabhasvatā āhataḥ prāptāghātaḥ | pariśrameṇa iṣitaḥ prāptaḥ iṣa-gatāv ity asmāt ||16||

 **...**

**|| 12.9.17 ||**

**kvacin magno mahāvarte taralais tāḍitaḥ kvacit |**

**yādobhir bhakṣyate kvāpi svayam anyonya-ghātibhiḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **anyonya-ghātibhis tad-bhakṣaṇāya parasparaṁ yudhyadbhiḥ ||17||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **yādāṁsi jalajantavaḥ ity amaraḥ ||17||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.9.18 ||**

**kvacic chokaṁ kvacin mohaṁ kvacid duḥkhaṁ sukhaṁ bhayam |**

**kvacin mṛtyum avāpnoti vyādhy-ādibhir utārditaḥ ||**

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ādinādhigrahaḥ | ardita upadrutaḥ ||18||

 **...**

**|| 12.9.19 ||**

**ayutāyuta-varṣāṇāṁ sahasrāṇi śatāni ca |**

**vyatīyur bhramatas tasmin viṣṇu-māyāvṛtātmanaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **viṣṇu-māyāvṛtātmana iti sa tathā dṛṣṭavān ity arthaḥ ||19||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ity artha iti—kṣaṇike'pi kāle'ghaṭanaghaṭanāpaṭīyasyā viṣṇumāyayā tasyānantāvdapratītirabhūd iti bhāvaḥ | etac ca jyotiḥśāstre pratidinaṁ candrādigatau meṣādilagnabhoge cāvagamyate | tathā hi—khakhābhrāṣṭavedā 48000 bhabhogena bhaktāḥ ihoktaghaṭyātmikā ṣaṣṭiguṇitā 2880000 candragatirhi pratyekaṁ vibhinnabhabhogabhaktā 796|35 pañcatriṁśatpalādhikaṣaṇṇavatyuttarasaptaśataghaṭyātmikāyāti | sā ca ṣaṣṭighaṭyātmake'horātre kathaṁ māyāṁ vinā saṅgaccheta | evaṁ pratyekaṁ meṣādilagnaṁ kiñcitpalādhikatryādighaṭyātmakaṁ bhavati tatra pratyekaṁ ṣaṭighaṭyātmakatriṁśāṅkhāḥ kathaṁ saṅgaccheran, triṁśāṁśānāṁ hyaṣṭādaśaśata 1800 ghaṭyaḥ santi vināghaṭanaghaṭanāpaṭīyasīṁ māyāmetatkadācidapi na saṅgataṁ syādityalamaprakṛtacintayā ||19||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **ayutāyuta-varṣāṇām iti tasya bhānaṁ jātam ity arthaḥ ||19||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** _na vyākhyātam._

 **...**

**|| 12.9.20 ||**

**sa kadācid bhramaṁs tasmin pṛthivyāḥ kakudi dvijaḥ |**

**nyāgrodha-potaṁ dadṛśe phala-pallava-śobhitam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kakudy unnata-pradeśe nyagrodha-potaṁ komala-vaṭam ||20||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **kakudastrī kakudo'pi vṛṣāṅge rājalakṣmaṇi | ucce vare pradhāne ca iti kośāt | potaḥ śiśau vāhitre ca gṛhe vāsasi komale ityabhidhānāt ||20||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **kakudi unnata-pradeśe ||20||

 **...**

**|| 12.9.21 ||**

**prāg-uttarasyāṁ śākhāyāṁ tasyāpi dadṛśe śiśum |**

**śayānaṁ parṇa-puṭake grasantaṁ prabhayā tamaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tasyeśāna-dikśākhāyāṁ śiśum api ||21||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **prāguttarayārmadhye yā dik sā prāguttarā tasyām | tasya nyagrodhapotasya | puṭaḥ sampuṭite patrapātre ca karanirmite iti niruktiḥ ||21||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.9.22 ||**

**mahā-marakata-śyāmaṁ śrīmad-vadana-paṅkajam |**

**kambu-grīvaṁ mahoraskaṁ sunāsaṁ sundara-bhruvam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **śrīmad-ramyaṁ vadana-paṅkajaṁ yasya tam | kambuvat tri-rekhāvṛtā grīvā yasya tam | mahoraskaṁ viśāla-vakṣasam | sunāsaṁ śobhanā nāsā yasya tam | sundare bhruvau yasya tam ||22||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **bhruvau netrordhvabhāgau ||22||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

**...**

**|| 12.9.23 ||**

**śvāsaijad-alakābhātaṁ kambu-śrī-karṇa-dāḍimam |**

**vidrumādhara-bhāseṣac- choṇāyita-sudhā-smitam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **śvāsair ejantaḥ kampamānā alakās tair ābhātaṁ śobhitam | kambu-vad-antar-valayena śrīr yayos tau kambu-śriyau tayoḥ karṇayor dāḍima-puṣpe yasya tam | vidruma-tulyādhara-bhāsā īṣac-choṇāyitaṁ sudhā-tulyaṁ smitaṁ yasya tam |

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** śvāsair ejantaḥ kampamānā alakās tair ābhatam | kambuvad antar-valayena śrīr yayos tau kambu-śriyau tayoḥ karṇayor dāḍimba-puṣpe yasya tam ||23||

 **...**

**|| 12.9.24 ||**

**padma-garbhāruṇāpāṅgaṁ hṛdya-hāsāvalokanam |**

**śvāsaijad-vali-saṁvigna- nimna-nābhi-dalodaram ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **padma-garbhavat ā īṣad aruṇāv apāṅgau netra-prāntau yasya tat | hṛdyo hāso yasmiṁs tad-avalokanaṁ yasya tam | śvāsair ejantyaś calantyo valayas tiryaṅ-namna-rekhās tābhiḥ saṁvignā cañcalā nimnā gambhīrā nābhir yasmiṁs tad-dala-vad-aśvattha-patra-saṅkāśam udaraṁ yasya tam ||24||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **karṇayordāḍimapuṣpe tadākāre bhūṣaṇe iti vyākhyeyam, anyathā karṇe puṣpaṁ kaṭau sūtraṁ veṇīṁ śirasi dhārayan | tāvadbhavati cāṇḍālo yāvadgaṅgāṁ na majjati | iti smṛtivirodhaḥ syāt ||23-24||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **śvāsair ejantyaś calantyo valayas tiryaṅ-nimna-rekhās tābhiḥ saha samvignaṁ cañcalaṁ nimna-nābhiḥ gabhīra-nābhiḥ | dalodaraṁ dalam aśvattha-patraṁ, tadvad udaraṁ yasya tam ||24||

 **...**

**|| 12.9.25 ||**

**cārv-aṅgulibhyāṁ pāṇibhyām unnīya caraṇāmbujam |**

**mukhe nidhāya viprendro dhayantaṁ vīkṣya vismitaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **cāravo’ṅgulayo yayos tābhyām unnīyākṛṣya dhayantaṁ pibantam ||25||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **cārv iti—


    karāravindena padāravindaṁ mukhāravinde viniveśayantam | 


    vaṭasya patrasya puṭe śayānaṁ bālaṁ mukundaṁ praṇato'smi nityam || 

iti granthāntaroktadhyānamatrāsūci | maccaraṇāravindaṁ kīdṛśaṁ—madhu yato bahavo madbhaktā etadāsvādāya yatante'to'hamapyetadāsvādayiṣyāmītīva pibantam ||25||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** mac-caraṇāmbuje kīdṛśaṁ madhu vartate yata etad āsvādanārthaṁ bahavo mad-bhaktā yatante tasmād idam aham apy āsvādya pariceṣye, itīva dhayantaṁ pibantam ||25||

 **...**

**|| 12.9.26 ||**

**tad-darśanād vīta-pariśramo mudā**

**protphulla-hṛt-padma-vilocanāmbujaḥ |**

**prahṛṣṭa-romādbhuta-bhāva-śaṅkitaḥ**

**praṣṭuṁ puras taṁ prasasāra bālakam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **hṛt-padmaṁ ca vilocanāmbuje ca protphullāni tāni yasya saḥ | adbhuta-bhāvo’ty-āścarya-rūpaṁ tena śaṅkitaḥ sann api taṁ praṣṭuṁ puraḥ prasasāra samīpaṁ gataḥ ||26||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **bhāvyate cintyate'neneti bhāvo rūpam ||26||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** adbhuta-bhāvena atyāścarya-svarūpeṇa śaṅkitaḥ nāyaṁ prākṛto bālaka iti prāptāśaṅko’pi praṣṭum ||26||

 **...**

**|| 12.9.27 ||**

**tāvac chiśor vai śvasitena bhārgavaḥ**

**so’ntaḥ śarīraṁ maśako yathāviśat |**

**tatrāpy ado nyastam acaṣṭa kṛtsnaśo**

**yathā purāmuhyad atīva-vismitaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ada idaṁ jagad yathā purā pralayāt pūrvaṁ nyastaṁ vinyastaṁ dṛṣṭvā cātīva vismitaḥ sann amuhyata ||27||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **yāvattatsamīpaṁ gatas tāvadeva | śvasitenocchvāsena | bhārgavo mārkaṇḍeyaḥ | maśako'tisūkṣmo raktapajīvaviśeṣaḥ | tatrāpyantaśśarīre'pi ||27||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **adaḥ jagat | yathā purā pralayāt pūrvam ||27||

 **...**

**|| 12.9.28 ||**

**khaṁ rodasī bhā-gaṇān adri-sāgarān**

**dvīpān sa-varṣān kakubhaḥ surāsurān |**

**vanāni deśān saritaḥ purākarān**

**kheṭān vrajān āśrama-varṇa-vṛttayaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kṛtsnaśo darśanaṁ prapañcayati, kham ity-ādinā | kakubho diśaḥ | purāṇyākarāṁś ca | kheṭān karṣaka-grāmān | vrajān gokulāni | āśramāṁś ca varṇāṁś ca teṣāṁ vṛttīś cety arthaḥ ||28||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **savarṣān sakhaṇḍān | ity artha iti—varṇāśramavṛttīrbhikṣākṛṣyādirūpā iti bhāvaḥ ||28||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** _na vyākhyātam._

 **...**

**|| 12.9.29 ||**

**mahānti bhūtāny atha bhautikāny asau**

**kālaṁ ca nānā-yuga-kalpa-kalpanam |**

**yat kiñcid anyad vyavahāra-kāraṇaṁ**

**dadarśa viśvaṁ sad ivāvabhāsitam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **nānā-yugāni kalpāṁś ca kalpayati tair vā kalpyata iti tathā taṁ kālaṁ ca | sad iva paramārtha ivāvabhāsitaṁ tenaiva ||29||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tenaiva bhagavataivāvabhāsitaṁ viśvaṁ sa mārkaṇḍeyo divā divasa ivāvabhāsitaṁ prakāśayuktaṁ dadarśoti vārthaḥ | divā tejasā vā yadbhāsā sarvam idaṁ vibhāti iti śruteḥ ||29||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **na mārkaṇḍeyaḥ divā divata eva avabhāsitaṁ prakāśa-yuktaṁ dadarśa ||28||

 **...**

**|| 12.9.30 ||**

**himālayaṁ puṣpavahāṁ ca tāṁ nadīṁ**

**nijāśramaṁ yatra ṛṣī apaśyata |**

**viśvaṁ vipaśyañ chvasitāc chiśor vai**

**bahir nirasto nyapatal layābdhau ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā), jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tatra nijāśrame | śiśormāyāśiśoḥ | śvasitācchavasitena bahirnirasto nunnaḥ layābdhau darśitapralayābdhau nyapatat ||30||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** puṣpavahāṁ puṣpabhadrām ||30||

 **...**

**|| 12.9.31 ||**

**tasmin pṛthivyāḥ kakudi prarūḍhaṁ**

**vaṭaṁ ca tat-parṇa-puṭe śayānam |**

**tokaṁ ca tat-prema-sudhā-smitena**

**nirīkṣito’pāṅga-nirīkṣaṇena ||**

**atha taṁ bālakaṁ vīkṣya netrābhyāṁ dhiṣṭhitaṁ hṛdi |**

**abhyayād ati-saṅkliṣṭaḥ pariṣvaktum adhokṣajam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : vaṭaṁ** ca **tokaṁ** ca vīkṣya **tasya premṇā sudhā**-tulya-**smita**-yuktena **apāṅga-nirīkṣaṇena** **nirīkṣitaḥ** san | **atha taṁ bālakam adhokṣajaṁ pariṣvaktum abhyayād** iti dvayor anvayaḥ | kathaṁ bhūtam ? **netrābhyāṁ hṛdi dhiṣṭhitam** adhiṣṭhitam ||31-32||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tasmin pūrvadarśita eva ||** **athāto'nantaram | dhiṣṭhitaṁ sthāpitam | adhyakāralopastvārṣaḥ | netrābhyāṁ netradvārā ||31-32||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** _na vyākhyātam._

 **...**

|| **12.9.33 ||**

**tāvat sa bhagavān sākṣād yogādhīśo guhāśayaḥ |**

**antardadha ṛṣeḥ sadyo yathehānīśa-nirmitā ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tāvat pariṣvaṅga-lābhāt pūrvam eva ṛṣes tasyāntarhito babhūva | tad-udyama-vaiphalye dṛṣṭāntaḥ, anīśo nirdaivas tena nirmitā īhā krīḍā yatheti ||33||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **sadyas tad-antardhāne dṛṣṭāntaḥ—yatheheti anīśa īhāyām asam arthaḥ, tena nirmitā īhā vāñchā yathā sadyo’ntardhatte, tathā tasmād ṛṣes tādṛśa-vāñchā-viṣayo’pi bhagavān antardadha ity arthaḥ ||32||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** layābdhau nipatya punar apy ayutāyuta-varṣa-paryantaṁ kaṣṭham anubhūya, pṛthivyāḥ kakudi baṭa-patra-śāyinaṁ bālaṁ dadarśa, tasya premṇā sudhā-tulya-smita-yuktenāpāṅga-nirīkṣaṇena nirīkṣitaḥ san punar api tadīya-śvāsena pūrvavat tat-praveśa-nirgamau | evam eva sapta-kṛtvaḥ praveśa-nirgama-vākya-dṛṣṭyā jñeyau | anīśo daridras tasya īhā dhanādi-vāñchā yathā sadya evotpadya sadya eva līyate tadvad ity arthaḥ ||33||

 **...**

**|| 12.9.34 ||**

**tam anv atha vaṭo brahman salilaṁ loka-samplavaḥ |**

**tirodhāyi kṣaṇād asya svāśrame pūrva-vat sthitaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **antarhitaṁ bhagavantam anu vaṭaḥ salilaṁ loka-saṁplavaś ca tiro-dhāyy antarhitaḥ | sa ca svāśrama eva yathā-pūrvaṁ sthita iti ||34||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **anīśo bhāgyarahite sarveśe durbale'pi ca iti niruktiḥ ||33-34||

iti śrīmad-bhāgavata-bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśe dvādaśa-skandhe navamo'dhyāyaḥ ||9||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **kṣaṇād asyeti | kṣaṇa-mātra-kāla-madhye eva spata-kalpa-saṅkhyaḥ kālaḥ praviṣṭo’bhūd atarkya-bhagavac-chaktyaiveti bhāvaḥ | tirodhāyīti karma-kartari ciṇ ||34||

iti sārārtha-darśinyāṁ harṣiṇyāṁ bhakta-cetasām |

dvādaśe navamo’dhyāyaḥ saṅgataḥ saṅgataḥ satām ||*||

 **...**


    iti śrīmad-bhāgavate mahā-purāṇe brahma-sūtra-bhāṣye pāramahaṁsyaṁ saṁhitāyāṁ vaiyāsikyāṁ daśama-skandhe 


    mārkaṇḍeyasya māyā-darśanaṁ nāma 


    navamo’dhyāyaḥ |

|| 12.9 ||

**...**

**(12.10)**


### atha daśamo’dhyāyaḥ


## mārkaṇḍeyasya vara-lābhaḥ 

**|| 12.10.1 ||**

**sūta uvāca—**

**sa evam anubhūyedaṁ nārāyaṇa-vinirmitam |**

**vaibhavaṁ yoga-māyāyās tam eva śaraṇaṁ yayau ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **

daśame śiva āgatya munes tuṣṭo varān adāt |

tena sākam ati-prītyā samābhāṣya sabhājayan ||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tena muninā | sabhājayansatkurvan | sa mārkaṇḍeyaḥ | vaibhavamutkarṣa prabhāvaṁ vā | tam eva nārāyaṇam eva | yasyaite rājamātaṅgāstasyaivāmī turaṅgamāḥ itivatsamāsāntargatasyāpi tyadādibhirāmarśa iti dhvananānnārāyaṇavinirmitamityatra samāsāntargatopi nārāyaṇaśavdastam eveti tacchabdena parāmṛśyata iti ||1||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :**

someśa-darśanaṁ tasya stutis tenābhinandanam |

muneḥ sveṣṭa-vara-prāptis tasmād daśama ucyate ||1||

 ...

**|| 12.10.2 ||**

**śrī-mārkaṇḍeya uvāca—**

**prapanno’smy aṅghri-mūlaṁ te prapannābhaya-daṁ hare |**

**yan-māyayāpi vibudhā muhyanti jñāna-kāśayā ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : jñāna-kāśayā** jñānavat prakāśamānayā | tvad-bhajanaṁ vinā vidvāṁso’pi yasya tava māyayā jñānino vayam ity ahaṅkāreṇa vimuhyantīty arthāh ||2||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **he hare iti—māyātatkāryahartā tvam eva mām eva ye prapadyante māyāmetāṁ taranti te iti gītokter iti sambuddhyābhiprāyaḥ | ity artha iti—puṁsāhaṅkāranivṛttye sarvatra bhagavad-dṛṣṭir eva kāryā—


    sarva-bhūteṣu madbhāvaṁ puṁso bhāvayato'cirāt | 


    spardhāsūyātiraskārāḥ sāhaṅkārāviyanti hi || 

iti śrīmukhokterayaṁ bhāvaḥ | jñānakāśayā jñāne vartamāne'pi kāśayā prakāśituṁ samarthayā, tatrāham eva pramāṇamabhūvam iti bhāvaḥ ||2||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** **jñāna-kāśayā** jñāne’vartamāne’pi kāśayā prakāśituṁ samartayety arthaḥ | tatrāham eva pramāṇam abhūvam iti bhāvaḥ ||4||

 ...

**|| 12.10.3 ||**

**sūta uvāca—**

**tam evaṁ nibhṛtātmānaṁ vṛṣeṇa divi paryaṭan |**

**rudrāṇyā bhagavān rudro dadarśa sva-gaṇair vṛtaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **śrī-nārāyaṇa eva sva-māyā-darśana-śrāntaṁ śiva-rūpeṇa sāntvayām āsa, tad āha—tam evam ity-ādinā | nibhṛtātmānaṁ samādita-cittam | rudrāṇyā bhavānyā ||3||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **taṁ munim ||3||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 ...

**|| 12.10.4 ||**

**athomā tam ṛṣiṁ vīkṣya giriśaṁ samabhāṣata |**

**paśyemaṁ bhagavan vipraṁ nibhṛtātmendriyāśayam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : nibhṛtā** niścalā **ātmendriyāśayā** dehendriya-manāṁsi yasya tam ||4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **atha rudrakartṛkadarśanānantarama | he bhagavann iti—sarvamanorathasampādanasamarthosīti bhāvaḥ ||4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** jñāna-kāśayā jñāne’vartamāne’pi kāśayā prakāśituṁ samartayety arthaḥ | tatrāham eva pramāṇam abhūvam iti bhāvaḥ ||4||

 ...

**|| 12.10.5 ||**

**nibhṛtoda-jhaṣa-vrāto vātāpāye yathārṇavaḥ |**

**kurv asya tapasaḥ sākṣāt saṁsiddhiṁ siddhi-do bhavān ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **nibhṛtaṁ niścala-bhaktim iti ||5||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **yadyapi prathamāntapāṭhaḥ prācuryeṇa dṛśyate bahu pustakeṣu tathāpi sa upamānopameyayorviruddhavibhaktikatvādviruddha iva bhāti paśyemam ityupameye dvitīyādarśanāt | kvacitta nibhṛtodajhaṣavrātam iti dvitīyānta eva pāṭho dṛśyate | saṁsiddhiḥ phalam saṁsiddhiḥ prakṛtau phale iti kośāt ||5||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** nibhṛtāni niścalī-bhūtāni udakāni jhaṣa-vrātāś ca yatra saḥ ||5||

 ...

**|| 12.10.6 ||**

**śrī-bhagavān uvāca—**

**naivecchaty āśiṣaḥ kvāpi brahmarṣir mokṣam apy uta |**

**bhaktiṁ parāṁ bhagavati labdhavān puruṣe’vyaye ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **āśiṣo ’bhyudaya-lakṣaṇāḥ | uta niścitam | atra hetuḥ, bhaktim iti ||6||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **atrā'nicchāyām | āśiṣo'ṇimādyāḥ siddhīḥ | tarhi mokṣaṁ dehīti tatrāha—mokṣamapīti | tarhi bhaktiṁ dehāti tatrāha—bhaktim iti viśvanāthaḥ ||6||

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** naivecchaty āśiṣa ity-ādi | kathaṁ necchati ? tatrāha—bhaktiṁ parāṁ bhagavati labdhavān | evaṁ-bhūto hi mokṣam api na vāñchatīti bhāvaḥ | tathāpi varam ekaṁ vṛṇe, tam āha—bhaktiṁ parāṁ bhagavati tat-pareṣu tathā tvayi iti ||6||

———————————————————————————————————————

**sanātana-gosvāmī : **[ha.bha.vi. 11.578] āśiṣo ’bhyudaya-lakṣaṇāḥ | uta smitau | tatra hetuḥ—bhaktim iti | avyaye paripūrṇe puruṣe śrī-kṛṣṇe ||6||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **āśiṣo’ṇimādyāḥ siddhīḥ | tarhi mokṣaṁ dehīti tatrāha—mokṣam apīti, tarhi bhaktiṁ dehītitatrāha—bhaktim iti ||6||

 ...

**|| 12.10.7 ||**

**athāpi saṁvadiṣyāmo bhavāny etena sādhunā |**

**ayaṁ hi paramo lābho nṛṇāṁ sādhu-samāgamaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **saṁvadiṣyāmaḥ saṁvadaṁ kariṣyāmaḥ ||7||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **yadyapyayaṁ na kiñcidicchati athāpi tathāpi ||7||

———————————————————————————————————————

**sanātana-gosvāmī : **[ha.bha.vi. 10.286] yadyapi,


    naivecchaty āśiṣaḥ kvāpi brahmarṣir mokṣam apy uta |


    bhaktiṁ parāṁ bhagavati labdhavān puruṣe’vyaye || [bhā.pu. 12.10.6].

tathāpi anena śrī-mārkaṇḍeyena saha saṁvādiṣyāmaḥ sambhāṣāṁ kariṣyāmaḥ, yataḥ sādhubhiḥ samāgamaḥ saṁyogaḥ, ayam eva paramo lābhaḥ phalam ||286||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ),** **viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 ...

**|| 12.10.8 ||**

**sūta uvāca—**

**ity uktvā tam upeyāya bhagavān sa satāṁ gatiḥ |**

**īśānaḥ sarva-vidyānām īśvaraḥ sarva-dehinām ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **satāṁ gatitve hetuḥ, īśān iti ||8||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** satām abhīpsita-bhakti-pradāyitvād gatiḥ | na kevalaṁ satām eva gatir, api tu sakāmānām apīty āha—īśāna iti | nātra citram ity āha—īśvara iti ||8||

 ...

**|| 12.10.9 ||**

**tayor āgamanaṁ sākṣād īśayor jagad-ātmanoḥ |**

**na veda ruddha-dhī-vṛttir ātmānaṁ viśvam eva ca ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ruddhā dhiyo’ntaḥ-karaṇasya vṛttayo yena saḥ ||9||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **sātvatāṁ vaiṣṇavānāṁ gatirgamyaḥ sarvavaiṣṇavamukhyatvāt vaiṣṇavānāṁ yathā śaṁbhuḥ ityagre vakṣyamāṇatvāt sa satāṁ gatiḥ iti pāṭhe tu satāmabhīpsitagatipradāyitvādbhaktirna kevalaṁ satām eva gatir api tu sakāmānapīty āha—īśāna iti | nātra citramityāha—īśvara iti ||8-9||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **samādhim āha—tayor iti | tayo rudra-tat-patnyoḥ | bhagavad-aṁśa-tac-chaktitvāj jagad-ātmanos tat-pravartakayor api | tatra hetuḥ—bhaktiṁ parāṁ [bhā.pu. 12.10.6] iti pūrvokteḥ | tasmād asamprajñāta-nāmno brahma-samādhito bhinna evāsau ||9||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** na kevalaṁ tayor āgamanaṁ veda, api tu ātmānam ahantāspadaṁ viśvam idaṅkārāspadaṁ ca ||9||

 ...

**|| 12.10.10 ||**

**bhagavāṁs tad abhijñāya giriśo yoga-māyayā |**

**āviśat tad-guhākāśaṁ vāyuś chidram iveśvaraḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **bhagavāṁs tad abhijñāyeti sva-niṣṭhābhivyakty-arthaḥ svayaṁ śrī-viṣṇāv antarhite satīti, giriśasya tad-vyudāsa-sāmarthyāyogāt | yad vā, śrī-bhagavān śivābhiprāyaṁ vijñāya yoga-māyayā giriśaḥ san tad-rūpam āviṣṭaḥ san punas tasya mārkaṇḍeyasya guhākāśaṁ hṛdayam āviśad ity arthaḥ | tatra hetuḥ—īśvara iti | evam evoktam ṭīkā-kṛdbhiḥ—śrī-nārāyaṇa eva sva-māyayā darśana-śrāntaṁ śiva-rūpeṇa sāntvayāmāsa [bhāvārtha-dīpikā 12.10.3] iti ||10||

 ...

**|| 12.10.11-13 ||**

**ātmany api śivaṁ prāptaṁ taḍit-piṅga-jaṭā-dharam |**

**try-akṣaṁ daśa-bhujaṁ prāṁśum udyantam iva bhāskaram ||**

**vyāghra-carmāmbara-dharaṁ śūla-dhanur-iṣv-asi-carmabhiḥ |**

**akṣa-mālā-ḍamaruka- kapālaṁ paraśuṁ saha ||**

**bibhrāṇaṁ sahasā bhātaṁ vicakṣya hṛdi vismitaḥ |**

**kim idaṁ kuta eveti samādher virato muniḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **na kevalaṁ bahir evātmany api prāptaṁ śivaṁ vicakṣya vismitaḥ | kathaṁ prāptam | sahasā kasmād eva hṛdi bhātam | kathaṁ bhūtam | taḍid-vat-piśaṅgā jaṭā dhārayatīti tathā tam | trīṇy akṣīṇi yasya tam | śūlādibhiḥ sahākṣa-mālādīn bibhrāṇam ity anvayaḥ | akṣa-mālādīnāṁ dvandvaikyam | vismaya-pūrvakaṁ bahir darśanam āha, kim idam iti ||11-13||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tat taddhīvṛttirodhanam | tasya guhākāśaṁ hṛdayākāśam | bhagavāṁstaditi—svaniṣṭhābhivyaktyarthaṁ svayaṁ śrīviṣṇāvantarhite satīti giriśasya tadvyudāsāyogāt | yad vā, śrī-bhagavāñśivābhiprāyaṁ vijñāya yogamāyayā giriśaḥ san mārkaṇḍeyahṛdākāśamāviśattatra hetuḥ—īśvara iti | idamevoktaṁ svāmicaraṇaḥ—śrīnārāyaṇa eva svamāyādarśanaśrāntaṁ śivarūpeṇa sāntvayāmāseti || atra dvandvaikye puṁstvamārṣam ||10-13||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 ...

**|| 12.10.14 ||**

**netre unmīlya dadṛśe sa-gaṇaṁ somayāgatam |**

**rudraṁ tri-lokaika-guruṁ nanāma śirasā muniḥ ||**

_na katamenāpi vyākhyātam_

 ...

**|| 12.10.15 ||**

**tasmai saparyāṁ vyadadhāt sa-gaṇāya sahomayā |**

**svāgatāsana-pādyārghya- gandha-srag-dhūpa-dīpakaiḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **somayā umayā sahāgataṁ rudraṁ dadṛśe | tato nanāma ||14||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **sa ubhayeti chedaḥ | so'ci lope cet iti salopaḥ ||14-15||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** somayā sa mārkaṇḍeyaḥ umayā saha, so’ci-lope cet pāda-pūraṇam iti so lopaḥ ||14||

 ...

**|| 12.10.16 ||**

**āha tv ātmānubhāvena pūrṇa-kāmasya te vibho |**

**karavāma kim īśāna yenedaṁ nirvṛtaṁ jagat ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **pūrṇa-kāmatvaṁ vyanakti, yena tvayā jagan-nirvṛtaṁ bhavatīti ||16||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **vibho iti—vibhutvādeva pūrṇakāmo'sīti bhāvaḥ | īśāneti—sarveśvarasya tava vayaṁ kim api kartuṁ na śaktā iti bhāvaḥ | nirvṛtaṁ prāptānandam ||16||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 ...

**|| 12.10.17 ||**

**namaḥ śivāya śāntāya sattvāya pramṛḍāya ca |**

**rajo-juṣo’pi ghorāya namas tubhyaṁ tamo-juṣe ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **nirguṇatvena tri-guṇatvena ca namas-karoti, namaḥ śivāya nirguṇāya | sattvāya sattvādhiṣṭhātre | ata eva pramṛḍayati sukhayatīti tathā tasmai ||17||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 ...

**|| 12.10.18 ||**

**sūta uvāca—**

**evaṁ stutaḥ sa bhagavān ādi-devaḥ satāṁ gatiḥ |**

**parituṣṭaḥ prasannātmā prahasaṁs tam abhāṣata ||**

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ata eva sattvādhiṣṭhātṛtvādeva | mṛḍayati sukhayati mṛḍa—sukhane iti dhātuḥ | apiśavdāttamojuṣe'pyamūḍhāyetyarthaḥ ||17-18||

 ...

**|| 12.10.19 ||**

**śrī-bhagavān uvāca—**

**varaṁ vṛṇīṣva naḥ kāmaṁ vara-deśā vayaṁ trayaḥ |**

**amoghaṁ darśanaṁ yeṣāṁ martyo yad vindate’mṛtam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **no’smattaḥ trayo brahma-viṣṇu-maheśvarāḥ | yad yebhyaḥ | te vayam ||19||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **varadānāmindrādidevānāmīśāḥ svāminaḥ | amoghaṁ phalavat ||19||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **no’smattaḥ yad yebhyaḥ ||19||

 ...

**|| 12.10.20 ||**

**brāhmaṇāḥ sādhavaḥ śāntā niḥsaṅgā bhūta-vatsalāḥ |**

**ekānta-bhaktā asmāsu nirvairāḥ sama-darśinaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **vara-dānādinā bhavat-sevaivāsmābhiḥ kriyate—na tv anugraho jagad-vandyatvād bhavatām iti brāhmaṇān stauti—brāhmaṇā ity-ādi | ye sādhavaḥ sad-ācārāḥ | śāntā matsarādi-rahitāḥ | niḥsaṅgā niṣkāmāḥ ||20||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **bhūtavatsalā dayālavaḥ, ata eva nirvairāḥ | asmāsu triṣu | samadarśinaḥ amedabuddhayaḥ| kramasandarbhastu—yatas te samadarśinastasmānmadādiṣu yā bhidā vartate tāmaṇvapi yathā syāttathā nācakṣata iti satyam, tattebhyopi haryyekāntabhaktānyuṣmānvayamīmahi priyatvena jānīma ity arthaḥ | tad-uktaṁ tenaiva caturthe—


    atha bhāgavatā yūyaṁ priyāḥ stha bhagavānyathā | 


    na madbhāgavatānāṁ ca preyānanyo'sti karhicit || iti | 

abhedaścettarhi mārkaṇḍeyasya samādhiviratirna syāttatrābhedadṛṣṭeruddṛṅkane'pi svayaṁ ca harīriśvaraḥ ityanena harer eva prādhānyamuktaṁ, tasyaiva svayamīśvaratvokteḥ| prathame'pi—pārthivāddāruṇo dhūmaḥ ity-ādinā | brāhme'pi śivena tathaivoktam—


    yo hi māṁ draṣṭumiccheta brahmāṇaṁ vā pitāmaham | 


    draṣṭavyastena bhagavānvāsadevaḥ pratāpavāna || 

parabrahmasvarūpasya tasya jñānena sarvajñānasambhavād iti ||20||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **brāhmaṇā iti | yatas te sama-darśanās tasmāt mad-ādiṣu yā bhidā vartate tām aṇv api yathā syāt tathā na cakṣata iti satyam eva, kintu tat tebhyo’pi yuṣmān hary-ekānta-bhaktān vayam īmahi priyatvena jānīma ity arthaḥ | tad uktaṁ tenaiva caturthe—


    atha bhāgavata yūyaṁ priyāḥ stha bhagavaṇ yathā | 


    na madbhāgavatānāṁ ca preyānanyosti karhicit || [bhā.pu. 4.24.26] iti |

abhedaś cet tarhi mārkaṇḍeyasya tad-anubhave samādhi-viratir na syāt | atrābheda-dṛṣṭer uṭṭaṅkane’pi svayaṁ ca harir īśvaraḥ [bhā.pu. 12.10.21] ity anena harer eva prādhānyam uktam | tasyaiva svayam īśvaratvaṁ coktaṁ prathama-skandhe pārthivād dāruṇaḥ [bhā.pu. 1.2.24] ity ādinā | brahma-purāṇe śrī-śiva-vākyam api tathaiva—


    yo hi māṁ draṣṭum iccheta brahmāṇaṁ vā pitāmaham |


    draṣṭavyas tena bhagavān vāsudevaḥ pratāpavān || [bra.pu. 226.46]

iti para-brahma-rūpasya tasya vijñānena sarva-vijñānād iti bhāvaḥ ||20|| [bhakti-sandarbha 106]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** he brāhmaṇā asmāsv ekānta-bhaktās tān loka-pālā vandante ||20|| 

 ...

**|| 12.10.21 ||**

**sa-lokā loka-pālās tān vandanty arcanty upāsate |**

**ahaṁ ca bhagavān brahmā svayaṁ ca harir īśvaraḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **na kevalaṁ ta eva, kintv ahaṁ cety-ādi ||21||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ta eva lokalokapālā eva | vandantītyārṣaṁ parasmaipadam ||21||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **na kevalaṁ loka-pālā eva vandante kintv ahaṁ cety ādi ||21||

 ...

**|| 12.10.22 ||**

**na te mayy acyute’je ca bhidām aṇv api cakṣate |**

**nātmanaś ca janasyāpi tad yuṣmān vayam īmahi ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **pūjyatamatve hetv-antaram āha—neti | aṇv apy aṇu-mātram api | na cakṣate na paśyanti | tat tasmād evaṁ-bhūtān yuṣmān īmahi bhajema ||22||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **evanbhūtān abhedadarśinaḥ ||22||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** aṇv apy aṇu-mātram api na cakṣate na paśyanti, yathaivāsmāsu bhedaṁ na paśyanti, tathaivātmanaḥ svasya janasyānyasyāpi sukha-duḥkhādiṣu bhedaṁ na paśyanti, tasmād evaṁ-bhūtān yuṣmān īmahi bhajema ||22||

 ...

**|| 12.10.23 ||**

**na hy am-mayāni tīrthāni na devāś cetanojjhitāḥ |**

**te punanty uru-kālena yūyaṁ darśana-mātrataḥ ||**[^59]

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** _na vyākhyātam._

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ammayāni jalasvarūpāṇi tīrthāni puṣkarādīni ki na punanti kintu punantyeva, cetanojjhitā mṛtpāṣāṇamayā devā na punanti kintu punantyeva, tadāha—te tīrthadevā urukālena bahusevanena | yūyaṁ brāhmaṇāḥ | kvacit darśanādeva sādhavaḥ iti pāṭho'pi sthānāntare paṭhyate, tatra sādhuśabdena bhagavanniṣṭhāvanto vedānuyāyina eva jñeyā na tu trivarṇetarā apīti ||23||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **na hīti | devā indādi-pratimā, na tu bhagavat-pratimā yuṣmābhir apy ārādhyatvād iti bhāvaḥ ||23||

 ...

**|| 12.10.24 ||**

**brāhmaṇebhyo namasyāmo ye’smad-rūpaṁ trayī-mayam |**

**bibhraty ātma-samādhāna- tapaḥ-svādhyāya-saṁyamaiḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **brāhmaṇebhyo brāhmaṇān | ātma-samādhānaṁ cittaikāgryam | tapa ālocanam | svādhyāyo’dhyayanam | saṁyamo vāg-ādi-niyamas taiḥ ||24||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **brāhmaṇaśabdena pāribhāṣikabrāhmaṇaśabdo—brahmādhīte veda vā brāhmaṇa ityevaṁrūpo na grāhya ityāha— ye'smadrūpaṁ mukhyamasmākaṁ rūpaṁ vedatrayīrūpamātmasamādhānādibhirbibhrati | saṁyama indriyajayaḥ| svādhyāyapadenādhyāpanam api gṛhyate | tathā ca kṣatriyavaiśyau na grāhyau kintu kevalaṁ vipra eva brāhmaṇa iti | brāhmaṇatāvivaraṇantu janmādyasya iti vyākhyāśatyāṁ viśeṣataḥ kṛtamastītyuparamyate ||24||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **namaskāre hetuḥ—yasmād iti | trayī-mayaṁ veda-lakṣaṇam upakārakatvād iti bhāvaḥ ||24||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** ātma-samādhānaṁ viṣṇu-dhyānam ||24||

 ...

**|| 12.10.25 ||**

**śravaṇād darśanād vāpi mahā-pātakino’pi vaḥ |**

**śudhyerann antyajāś cāpi kim u sambhāṣaṇādibhiḥ ||**[^60]

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kiṁ ca, śravaṇād ity-ādi ||25||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **anyadādhikyam āha—kiñceti | mahāpātakino brahmaghnādayaḥ pañca, kiṁ punaranya ityapiśabdārthaḥ | antyajāḥ kaivartādayaḥ, kiṁ punaḥ kṣatriyādayaḥ | sambhāṣaṇādeḥ kā vātatyāha—kimv iti | ādinā sparśanastavanādigrahaḥ | vā yuṣmākaṁ brāhmaṇānāmity arthaḥ | yatra 

kutracinmahattvaṁ tatra sarvatra brāhmaṇaprasādāvāptam eveti vipraprasādāddharaṇīdharo'haṁ vipraprasādātkamalākaroham ity-ādibhagavadukteḥ ||25||

———————————————————————————————————————

sanātanaḥ (ha.bha.vi. 10.217) : astu tāvad mahatāṁ saṅga-sevādikam, nāma-śravaṇādināpi mahā-duṣṭā api muktā bhavantīti śrī-mārkaṇḍeya-viṣayaka-śrī-śiva-vacanaṁ likhati—śravaṇād iti | vaḥ bhagavad-bhaktānāṁ yuṣmākam, mahā-pātakinaḥ mahā-pāpa-karma-ratāḥ, antyajāś ca mahā-pāpa-jātayaḥ, śudhyeran tat-tat-pāpataḥ saṁsāra-mahā-malādvā vimuktā bhavanti | ādi-śabdena praṇāmādiḥ ||25||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 ...

**|| 12.10.26 ||**

**sūta uvāca—**

**iti candra-lalāmasya dharma-guhyopabṛṁhitam |**

**vaco’mṛtāyanam ṛṣir nātṛpyat karṇayoḥ piban ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **candro lalāmo bhūṣaṇaṁ yasya tasya dharma-rahasya-yuktam amṛtāspadaṁ vacaḥ karṇābhyāṁ pibann ātṛpyad alam iti nāmanyata | karṇayor amṛtāyanam iti vānvayaḥ ||26||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **dharma-guhyaṁ bhagavad-bhakti-lakṣaṇaṁ tenopabṛṁhitam | ata evāmṛtāyanaṁ paramānandasyāpy āśraya-rūpam | ata eva nātṛpyat, na tu sva-stutyety arthaḥ ||26||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **dharma ekānta-bhaktā [bhā.pu. 12.10.20] iti, nātmanaś ca janasya [bhā.pu. 12.10.22] ity ādi, guhyaṁ tad yuṣmān vayam īmahi [bhā.pu. 12.10.22] ity-ādi | tābhyām upabṛṁhitaṁ nātṛpyad iti | nāyaṁ svas tavottha ānandaḥ, kintu stuti-miṣeṇāsmān dharmam evāśikṣayat tasmād etādṛśa-dharmavatā mayā bhavitavyam ity upadeśa-prāpty-uttha eva jñeyaḥ ||26||

 ...

**|| 12.10.27 ||**

**sa ciraṁ māyayā viṣṇor bhrāmitaḥ karśito bhṛśam |**

**śiva-vāg-amṛta-dhvasta- kleśa-puñjas tam abravīt ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **śivasya vāg evāmṛtaṁ tena dhvastaḥ kleśa-puñjo yasya saḥ ||27||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **viṣṇu-māyayeti svecchayaivāṅgīkriyetety[^61] arthaḥ | śivasyāpy atra viṣṇv-āviṣṭatvaṁ[^62] vyākhyātam iti na bhedo mantavyaḥ ||27||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** _na vyākhyātam._

 ...

**|| 12.10.28 ||**

**śrī-mārkaṇḍeya uvāca—**

**aho īśvara-līleyaṁ durvibhāvyā śarīriṇām |**

**yan namantīśitavyāni stuvanti jagad-īśvarāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **iyaṁ līlā durvibhāvyāvitarkyā | yad yayā īśitavyāni sva-niyamyāni yāni bhūtāni tāni jagad-īśvarāḥ | svayaṁ namanti stuvanti ceti ||28||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **durvibhāvya atarkyā | īśitavyāni sva-niyamyāny api bhūtāni ||28||

 ...

**|| 12.10.29 ||**

**dharmaṁ grāhayituṁ prāyaḥ pravaktāraś ca dehinām |**

**ācaranty anumodante kriyamāṇaṁ stuvanti ca ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **athavā loka-saṅgraha-mātram etad ity āha—dharmam iti | pravaktāro’pi yat svayaṁ dehināṁ dharmaṁ grāhayitum ācaranti ||29||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **itīttham | pibannādareṇa śṛṇvan | taṁ śivam | dharmasya pravaktāro'pi anumodante'nyāṁstatra pravartayanti—kriyamāṇaṁ stuvanti—dhanyo'yaṁ dharmo yaścaitādṛśairmahadbhir api kriyata iti dharmastutirdharmakartṛṣveva paryavasyati | dharmaḥ—ekāntabhaktaḥ ityārabhya nātmanaś ca janasya ity-ādi, guhyam—tadyuṣmānvayamīmahi ity-ādi, tābhyāmupabṛṁhitam | nātṛpyaditi—nāyaṁ svastutyottha ānandaḥ kintu stutimiṣeṇāsmāndharmamevāśikṣayattasmādetādṛśadharmavatā mayā bhavitavyamityupadeśaprāptyuttha eva jñeyaḥ ||26-29||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **dharmam ity atra prāya iti kadācit tatra nija-rucyā ca dehinām iti dehasya yat karma, tad evātmana iti manyamānānām ity arthaḥ | ata eva pravaktāras tad-vyatiriktāḥ ||29||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** athavā loka-saṅgraha-mātram etad ity āha—dharmam iti | kriyamāṇaṁ stuvantīti dhanyo’yaṁ dharmaḥ, yaḥ khalu etādṛśair mahadbhir kriyate | iti dharma-stutiḥ dharma-kartṛṣv eva paryāpnoti ||29||

 ...

**|| 12.10.30 ||**

**naitāvatā bhagavataḥ sva-māyā-maya-vṛttibhiḥ |**

**na duṣyetānubhāvas tair māyinaḥ kuhakaṁ yathā ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** nanv etat sva-prabhāva-tiraskārakaṁ kathaṁ mayā kriyate ? tatrāha—naitāvateti | etavatā loka-saṅgraha-mātreṇa | tair namanādibhiḥ kathaṁ-bhūtaiḥ ? sva-māyā-mayī vṛttir yeṣu, tair bhagavato māyinas tavānubhāvo na duṣyeta, yataḥ prasiddhasya māyinaḥ kuhakaṁ kapaṭaṁ yathā, tathā etāni namanādīni | atas tasya yathā kuhakair ātmānubhāvo na duṣyati tadvat | praduṣyetānubhāva iti pāṭhe na-kārasya dṛṣṭānte’py anuṣaṅgaḥ ||30||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **atrākṣipati—nanv iti | yata iti ata ityanenānveti | māyina aindrajālikādeḥ | anubhāvo niścayaḥ | anyebhyo dhanādigrahalakṣaṇaḥ | atra sandarbhaḥ—teṣu mukhyaṁ bhagavantamavalambya tatra doṣāntaraṁ nirasyati—nateti tribhiḥ | doṣā'bhāve hetuḥ—sveṣu bhakteṣu yā māyā kṛpā tanmayavṛttir iti mama bhaktaparamparāsveṣā rītiḥ pravartiteti kṛpayā prītivaśatayetyarthaḥ atra vyatirekeṇa dṛṣṭāntaḥ—māyinaḥ kuhakinaḥ kapaṭaṁ yathā praduṣyate tathā na duṣyata iti | viśvanāthastu—kenacidaindrajālikena svamukhātkaścidvānara udbhāvya sa stūyate namaskriyate ca tena tasyānabhāvo yathā na duṣyate tatheti na duṣyate iti pāṭhe dṛṣṭānte nakārasyānuṣaṅgaḥ | yadyapi śrīrudreṇa tadīyastutyādayo na māyayā kṛtāstadapi svastutyā lajjitena muninā prayukto'yaṁ dṛṣṭānto nānupapannaḥ ||30||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **teṣu mukhyaṁ bhagavantam avalaṁbya tatra doṣāntaraṁ nirasyati—naitāvateti tribhiḥ | adoṣe[^63] hetuḥ—sveṣu bhakteṣu yā māyā kṛpā, tan-maya-vṛttibhir iti mama bhakta-paramparāsv eṣā rītiḥ pravartiteti[^64] kṛpayā sva-prīti-vaśatayety arthaḥ | tatra vyatirekeṇa dṛṣṭāntaḥ—māyinaḥ kuhakaṁ yathā praduṣyeta, tatheti | na duṣyeteti pāṭhe’pi māyinaḥ kuhakaṁ yathā duṣyeta, tathā na, kintu na duṣyetaivety arthaḥ ||30||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** etāvatā loka-saṅgraha-mātreṇa tair namanādibhis tavānubhāvo na praduṣyati | kīdṛśaiḥ ? māyā-mayy eva vṛttiś ceṣṭā yeṣu taiḥ | māyinaḥ kuhakam iti dhana-prāpti-hetunā aindrajālikena kenacit sva-mukhād udbhāvitaḥ kaścid vā naraḥ stūyate namaskriyate tena tasyānubhavo na duṣyatīti | na duṣyeteti pāṭhe na-kārasya dṛṣṭenānuṣaṅgaḥ | yadyapi śrī-kṛṣṇeṇa tadīya-stuty-ādayo na māyayā kṛtās tad api sva-stutyā lajjitena muniā prayukto’yaṁ dṛṣṭānto nānupapannaḥ ||30||

 ...

**|| 12.10.31-32 ||**

**sṛṣṭvedaṁ manasā viśvam ātmanānupraviśya yaḥ |**

**guṇaiḥ kurvadbhir ābhāti karteva svapna-dṛg yathā ||**

**tasmai namo bhagavate tri-guṇāya guṇātmane |**

**kevalāyādvitīyāya gurave brahma-mūrtaye ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **māyā-ceṣṭitaṁ prapañcayati, sṛṣṭveti | svapna-dṛg yathety avidyā ceṣṭite dṛṣṭāntaḥ | tri-guṇatve’pi na jīva-vat tad-abhibhūtāya kintu guṇānām ātmane niyantre ||31-32||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **avidyayā svapnaṁ sṛjato jīvasyāpi vastutastatsambandho nāsti kimuteśvarasyeti tātparyavānāha—svapnadṛgyatheti | doṣāsparśamevāha yugmena | idaṁ viśvaṁ manasā saṅkalpenaiva nimittena guṇairupādānaiḥ sṛṣṭvāpi tataścātmanā svayaṁ tadanupraviśya praveśena sthāpayitvāpi tattadupalakṣaṇatvena saṁhṛtyāpi kartṛvadevābhāti na tu kartaiveti | tatra hetutvena guṇān viśiṣṭi—kurvadbhir iti | tatsānnidhyaprabhāveṇa cetanā iva guṇā eva sarvaṁ kurvanti na tu svayam iti saṅkalpasyābhāsāmātreṇa tadasambhavāt | tatrāvidyayā svapnaṁ sṛjatas tadīyataṭasthāṁśasya jīvasyāpi vastutastatsambandho nāsti kimuta tasyeti darśayandṛṣṭāntayati—svapnadṛgyatheti || gurave, kimbhūtāya—brahmamūrtaye brāhmaṇarūpāya | tvaṁ deveṣu brāhmaṇo'haṁ manuṣyeṣa iti jābālaśruteḥ | etena brāhmaṇasyaiva gurutvaṁ sūcitam | kevalāya mukhyāya | advitīyāya ekarūpāya | trayo'mṛtābhayakṣamarūpā guṇā yasya tasmai | guṇā aiśvaryādayo'pyātmānaḥ svarūpabhūtā yasya tasmai | kevalāya prakṛtisaṅgaśūnyāya | advitīyāyatulyāyāto gurave sarvopadeṣṭre'nto vedarūpāyeti sandarbhaḥ ||31-32||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **doṣāsparśam eva darśayati—sṛṣṭvedam iti yugmakena | idaṁ viśvaṁ manasā saṅkalpenaiva nimittena guṇair upādānaiḥ sṛṣṭvāpi, tataś cātmanā svayaṁ tad anupraviśya, praveśena sthāpayitvāpi, tat-tad-upalakṣaṇatvena saṁhṛtyāpi kartṛvad evābhāti, na tu kartaiveti | tatra hetutvāya guṇān viśinaṣṭi—kurvadbhir iti | tat-sānnidhya-prabhāveṇa cetanā iva guṇā eva sarvaṁ kurvanti, na tu svayam iti | saṅkalpasyābhāsa-mātratvena tad-asambandhād ity arthaḥ | tatrāvidyayā svapnaṁ sṛjatas tadīya-taṭasthāṁśasya jīvasyāpi vastutas tat-sambandho nāsti, kim uta tasyeti darśayan dṛṣṭāntayati—svapna-dṛg yatheti | 

trayaḥ amṛtābhaya-kṣema-rūpā guṇā yasya tasmai |[^65] guṇā aiśvaryādayo’pi ātmānaḥ svarūpa-bhūtā yasya tasmai | kevalāya prakṛti-saṅga-śūnyāya, advitīyāya sva-tulya-rahitāya, ata eva gurave sarvopadeṣṭre | brahmeti svopadeśyaṁ yad brahma vedaḥ, tad api mūrtiḥ svarūpaṁ yasya tasmai ||31-32||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** manasā saṅkalpa-mātreṇa kurvadbhir guṇaiḥ svīyaiḥ svayam akartāpi kartety ābhātīti na guṇair lepa iti bhāvaḥ | avidyayā svapnaṁ sṛjato jīvasyāpi vastutas tat-sambandho nāsti, kim uta tasyeti darśayan dṛṣṭāntayati—svapna-dṛg yatheti | guṇātmane guṇa-niyantre ||31-32||

 ...

**|| 12.10.33 ||**

**kaṁ vṛṇe nu paraṁ bhūman varaṁ tvad vara-darśanāt |**

**yad-darśanāt pūrṇa-kāmaḥ satya-kāmaḥ pumān bhavet ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **varaṁ vṛṇīṣva iti | yad uktaṁ, tatrāha—kam iti | varaṁ darśanaṁ yasya tasmāt tvattaḥ paraṁ kaṁ nu varaṁ vṛṇe | yasya tava darśanād avalokanāt pūrṇa-kāmaḥ sarvānanda-sandoha-rūpaḥ satya-kāmo yathecchaṁ prāpta-sarvānandaḥ ||33||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **he bhūmann iti—anantaphaladātuḥ sarveśvarāt—kaṁ varaṁ vṛṇomi na kamapīti bhāvaḥ | yad vā, varaḥ sarvotkṛṣṭavaro darśanaṁ yasya tasmāttvattaḥ kiṁ paramaparaṁ varaṁ vṛṇe | tatra hetuḥ—yaddarśanād iti ||33||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

...

**|| 12.10.34 ||**

**varam ekaṁ vṛṇe’thāpi pūrṇāt kāmābhivarṣaṇāt |**

**bhagavaty acyutāṁ bhaktiṁ tat-pareṣu tathā tvayi ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** _na vyākhyātam._

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tathā tvayīti | tvayi ca tat-para ity arthaḥ,


    kiṁ varṇaye tava vibho yad udīrito’suḥ


    saṁspandate tam anu vāṅ-mana-indriyāṇi |


    spandanti vai tanu-bhṛtām aja-śarvayoś ca 


    svasyāpy athāpi bhajatām asi bhāva-bandhuḥ || [bhā.pu. 12.8.40] 

ity anenaiva śrī-nārāyaṇa-rṣiṁ praty uktatvāt ||34||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** _na vyākhyātam._

 ...

**|| 12.10.35 ||**

**sūta uvāca—**

**ity arcito’bhiṣṭutaś ca muninā sūktayā girā |**

**tam āha bhagavāñ charvaḥ śarvayā cābhinanditaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **vara-dānāya svayam eva pravṛttaḥ śarvayomayā cābhinandito’numoditaḥ sann āha ||35||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **yadi varadāne'tīva haṭhastarhyekaṁ varam api vṛṇomīti yojyam | bhagavati śrīharau tvayi, tadrūpe hare ca | yad vā, madbhaktaśiromaṇau tvayi paramatatpare upadeśagurau bhaktiṁ ca vṛṇe, tatparatvaṁ ca svenaiva tena ṣaṣṭhe citraketūpākhyāna uktam—


    ayaṁ tasya mahābhāgaścitraketuḥ priyo'nugaḥ | 


    sarvatra samadṛk śānto hyahañcaivācyutapriyaḥ || iti | 

svayaṁ mārkaṇḍeyenāpyuktam—kiṁ varṇaye tava vibho yadudīrito'suḥ saṁspandate tamanu vāṅmana̮indriyāṇi | spandanti vai tanubhṛtāmajapūrvayośca—ityanena nārāyaṇarṣi prati | kiṁ ca—mukhyo'bhūdbrāhmaṇo guruḥ iti tṛtīyaskandhe maitrayeṇa viduraṁ pratyuktam | janmanā brāhmaṇo guruḥ iti śrīdaśame nandarājenāpi śrīgargaṁ pratyuktam iti ||34-35||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **varaṁ vṛṇuṣveti yad uktaṁ tatrāha kim iti—varo darśanaṁ yasya tasmāt | satyakāmaḥ satya-saṅkalpa eva, tat-pareṣu tad-bhakteṣu tathā tad-bhakta-śreṣṭhe tvayi bhakty-upadeṣṭari gurau tena tvayi me bhaktis tad-bhaktatvenaivāstu na tv īśvaratvena iti bhāvaḥ ||35||

 ...

**|| 12.10.36 ||**

**kāmo maharṣe sarvo’yaṁ bhaktimāṁs tvam adhokṣaje |**

**ā-kalpāntād yaśaḥ puṇyam ajarāmaratā tathā ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kāmo’yaṁ sarvo’py anyac ca yat puṇyaṁ yaśa ity-ādi-brahma-varcasvinas te bhūyād ity uttareṇānvayaḥ | yatas tvam adhokṣaje bhaktimān ||36||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ayaṁ hariharābhedabhaktitadbhaktabhaktirūpo manorathaḥ | he maharṣe iti—maharṣitvāttubhyaṁ varadānaṁ siddhasādhanameveti bhāvaḥ | yad vā, ahamadhokṣaje bhaktimānsyāmityayaṁ te kāmostv iti yojyam ||36||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** ayaṁ sarvo’pi kāmas te’stu yatas tvam adhokṣaje bhaktimān ||36||

 ...

**|| 12.10.37 ||**

**jñānaṁ traikālikaṁ brahman vijñānaṁ ca viraktimat |**

**brahma-varcasvino bhūyāt purāṇācāryatāstu te ||**

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **brahmann iti—vedavidbrahmaṇatvādbahuvaradānayogya eva tvam iti bhāvaḥ ||37||

 ...

**|| 12.10.38 ||**

**sūta uvāca—**

**evaṁ varān sa munaye dattvāgāt try-akṣa īśvaraḥ |**

**devyai tat-karma kathayann anubhūtaṁ purāmunā ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tasya karma tapa-ādi | amunā purānubhūtaṁ yad bhagavan-māyā-vaibhavaṁ tac ca kathayan ||38||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tryakṣastryambakaḥ ||38||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 ...

**|| 12.10.39 ||**

**so’py avāpta-mahā-yoga- mahimā bhārgavottamaḥ |**

**vicaraty adhunāpy addhā harāv ekāntatāṁ gataḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **avāpto mahā-yoga-mahimā yena saḥ ||39||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 ...

**|| 12.10.40 ||**

**anuvarṇitam etat te mārkaṇḍeyasya dhīmataḥ |**

**anubhūtaṁ bhagavato māyā-vaibhavam adbhutam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **etan mārkaṇḍeyasya caritaṁ tenānubhūtaṁ ca bhagavan-māyā-vaibhavaṁ te’nuvarṇitam ||40||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **mahāyogasya bhaktiyogasya mahimāṇimādisiddhipūrvakaṁ bhagavatsākṣātkāralakṣaṇaḥ | ekāntatāṁ nityabhaktitām ||39-40||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 ...

**|| 12.10.41 ||**

**etat kecid avidvāṁso māyā-saṁsṛtim ātmanaḥ |**

**anādy-āvartitaṁ nṝṇāṁ kādācitkaṁ pracakṣate ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **nanv evam apy asmat kulotpannasyāsya sapta-kalpāyuṣṭvaṁ vṛddhair ucyamānaṁ viruddham eva tatrāha—etan mārkaṇḍeyenānubhūtaṁ bhagavan-māyā-vaibhavaṁ nānā-kalpa-rūpaṁ kādācitkam īśvarecchayā tasyaivākasmikam, na tu sarva-sādhāraṇam | etat kecid anādi-bahu-kālam āvartitaṁ daiva-yuga-sahasra-dvayamānena punaḥ punaḥ parivartitaṁ pracakṣate | ke te ? nṝṇāṁ saṁsṛtiṁ sarga-pralayādi-lakṣaṇām ātmano bhagavato māyety evam avidvāṁsaḥ | vidvāṁsas tu māyā-śiśoḥ śvāsocchvāsābhyāṁ sapta-kṛtvas tad udara-praveśa-nirgamataḥ sapta-kalpatvaṁ tat-kṣaṇa-mātreṇeti vadanti, ato na virodha ity arthaḥ ||41||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **atrākṣipati—nanv iti ||41||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **etat mārkaṇḍeya-dṛṣṭam ātmano bhagavato māyā-saṁsṛtis tat-prārthanayā māyā-prasāra eva | tad etad api kecid avidvāṁso’nādita evāvartitaṁ bhagavatā punaḥ prāpitaṁ kādācitkaṁ pralayaṁ pracakṣate | anye tad-dṛṣṭāḥ kalpās tu manvantarāṇy eveti bhāvaḥ ||41||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **etan mārkaṇḍeyenānubhūtam ātmanaḥ parameśvarasya māyā-saṁsṛti-vaibhavam ity arthaḥ | bhagavataḥ śiśu-svarūpasya paramātarkya-śaktyā śvāsocchvāsābhyāṁ sapta-kṛtvas tad-udara-praveśa-nirgama-kālātmakaṁ kādācitkam eva kecid avidvāṁso nṝṇām ajñānādikaṁ bahu-kālata āvartitaṁ daiva-yuga-sahasra-mānena punaḥ punaḥ parāvartitaṁ sapta-kalpam eva pracakṣate ||41||

 ...

**|| 12.10.42 ||**

**ya evam etad bhṛgu-varya varṇitaṁ**

**rathāṅga-pāṇer anubhāva-bhāvitam |**

**saṁśrāvayet saṁśṛṇuyād u tāv ubhau**

**tayor na karmāśaya-saṁsṛtir bhavet ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **saṁśṛṇuyāt | u iti harṣe | saṁśrāvayed vā | yau tāv ubhau | tayoḥ karma-vāsanākṛtā saṁsṛtir na bhaved iti ||42||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tāvubhau śrotṛvaktārau tulyaphalabhāgināv iti śeṣaḥ | tad evāha—tayor iti | he bhṛguvaryeti—aho sa evaiko'smākaṁ kulaśreṣṭha āsīdahaṁ tu na tāddagaṁśabhāgapīti vimṛśaṁtaṁ śaunakaṁ sūtastam api protsāhayati—tvaṁ tu bahujanmasukṛtalabhyasarva-purāṇetihāsaśrotṛtvādbhṛguvaṁśe varya eveti bhāvaḥ ||42||

iti śrīmad-bhāgavata-bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśe dvādaśa-skandhe daśamo'dhyāyaḥ ||10||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **u iti pakṣāntare, saṁśrāvayed vā | tāv ubhau tulyāv ity arthaḥ | phalam āha—tayor iti ||42||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** he bhṛgu-varya anubhāvena prabhāvena bhāvitaṁ vāsitaṁ yaḥ śrāvayet, yaś ca śṛṇuyāt tāv ubhau tulyāv eveti śeṣaḥ | atas tayoḥ karma-vāsanā-mayī saṁsṛtir na bhavet ||42||

iti sārārtha-darśinyāṁ harṣiṇyāṁ bhakta-cetasām |

dvādaśe daśamo’dhyāyaḥ saṅgataḥ saṅgataḥ satām ||*||

 **...**


    iti śrīmad-bhāgavate mahā-purāṇe brahma-sūtra-bhāṣye pāramahaṁsyaṁ saṁhitāyāṁ vaiyāsikyāṁ dvādaśa-skandhe 

mārkaṇḍeyasya vara-lābho nāma 

daśamo’dhyāyaḥ |

|| 12.10 ||

**…**

**(12.11)**


### athaikādaśo’dhyāyaḥ


## āditya-vyūha-vivaraṇaṁ

**|| 12.11.1 ||**

**śrī-śaunaka uvāca—**

**athemam arthaṁ pṛcchāmo bhavantaṁ bahu-vittamam |**

**samasta-tantra-rāddhānte bhavān bhāgavata tattva-vit ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :**

ekādaśe tu pūjārthaṁ mahā-puruṣa-varṇanam |

raver vyūhasya cākhyānaṁ pratimāsaṁ pṛthak pṛthak ||

yenāmartyatvam āpanno martyo’sau bhārgavottamaḥ |

taṁ pṛcchati kriyā-yogaṁ sāṅgopāṅgādi-kalpitam ||

atheti | he bhāgavata, yato bhavān san samasta-tantra-rāddhānte tattva-vid rahasya-jñaḥ ||1||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **mahāpuruṣo virāṭ | vyūho racanāviśeṣaḥ | yena kriyāyogena | asau buddhisannihito mārkaṇḍeyaḥ | amṛtatvaṁ cirajīvitvam | ābhūtasaṁplavatvaṁ ca hyamṛtatvaṁ prabhāṣate iti smṛteḥ | atha sarvaśāstraśravaṇottaram | imaṁ buddhirathaṁ kriyāyogam | he bhāgavateti—bhāgavatā evaitattattvaṁ jānantīti bhāvaḥ ||1||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :**

mahā-puruṣajārtham aṅgopāga-vibhūtayaḥ |

ekādaśe ravi-vyūha-kathā api nirūpitāḥ ||

sa hy asmat-pūrva-puruṣā mārkaṇḍeyas tāntrike bhagavat-pūjā-vidhau viśārada āsīd atas tvāṁ pūjā-vivekaṁ jijñāse ity āha—atheti | yena pūrā-prakāreṇa sa munir bhagavantam aparokṣī-cakāra | imam arthaṁ pṛcchāmaḥ rāddhānte siddhānte ||1||

**...**

**|| 12.11.2-3 ||**

**tāntrikāḥ paricaryāyāṁ kevalasya śriyaḥ pateḥ |**

**aṅgopāṅgāyudhā-kalpaṁ kalpayanti yathā ca yaiḥ ||**

**tan no varṇaya bhadraṁ te kriyā-yogaṁ bubhutsatām |**

**yena kriyā-naipuṇena martyo yāyād amartyatām**[^66]** ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **praṣṭavyam āha—tāntrikā iti | **paricaryāyām** upāsanāyāṁ viṣaye | **kevalasya** caitanya-ghanasya | **aṅgāni** pādādīni, **upāṅgāni** garuḍādīni, **āyudhāni** sudarśanādīni, **ākalpāḥ** kaustubhādayaḥ, teṣāṁ dvandvaikyam | tad **yathā kalpayanti,** **yaiś ca** tattvaiḥ kalpayanti, **tan no varṇaya **iti ||2||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tāntrikāḥ pañcarātrādyāgamanipuṇāḥ | kevalasya pañcāyatanapūjāyāṁ mukhyasya || tadaṅgopāṅgādikalpanam | bubhutsatāṁ boddhumicchatām ||2-3||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : kevalasya** svarūpa-bhūtāṅgopāṅgādi-lakṣaṇasya **śriyaḥ pateḥ** svarūpa-bhūtatvena vakṣyamāṇāyā lakṣmyāḥ patyus tasyāṅgādikaṁ yaiḥ kalpayanti, māyika-vaibhavair abhinnatayopāsate, tat sarvaṁ no varṇaya | martyaḥ prapañcāviṣṭo’pi ||2-3||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **aṅgāni pāṇi-pādādīni, upāṅgāni garuḍādīni, āyudhāni sudarśanādīni, ākalpāḥ kaustubhādayaḥ, teṣāṁ dvandvaikyam | yad yathā kalpayanti yaiś ca tattvaiḥ kalpayanti, tan no varṇayeti | saccidānanda-vapuṣo bhagavato yeṣāṁ yeṣām aṅgānāṁ yā vibhūtayo māyika-prapañce’tra dṛśyante, tābhir eva punas tat-tad-aṅgāny upāsanārthaṁ kalpayanti ity arthaḥ ||2||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.4 ||**

**sūta uvāca—**

**namaskṛtya gurūn vakṣye vibhūtīr vaiṣṇavīr api |**

**yāḥ proktā veda-tantrābhyām ācāryaiḥ padmajādibhiḥ ||**

**śrīdharaḥ** gurūpadeśa-gamyatvād asyārthasya tan namaskāra-pūrvakam āha—namaskṛtyeti | vibhūtīr virāḍ-vigrahādyāḥ ||4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ādinā śaṅkaranāradādigrahaḥ ||4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **viṣṇor api vibhūtīḥ sādhāraṇīs tad-vibhūtīr vakṣye | tatra vaiṣṇavīs tat-svarūpa-bhūtā api vakṣya ity arthaḥ ||4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **gurūpadeśa-gamyatvād asyārthasya tan namaskāra-pūrvakam āha—namaskṛtyeti ||4||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.5 ||**

**māyādyair navabhis tattvaiḥ sa vikāra-mayo virāṭ |**

**nirmito dṛśyate yatra sa-citke bhuvana-trayam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **aṅgādi-kalpanāṁ bhūr-ādibhir darśayituṁ prathamaṁ tāvad yathā kalpayantīti praśnasya vairāja-rūpeṇety uttaraṁ vaktuṁ virāḍ-vigraham āha—māyādyaiḥ prakṛti-sūtra-mahad-ahaṅkāra-pañca-tan-mātrair navabhis tattvaiḥ | vikāra ekādaśendriyāṇi pañca mahā-bhūtānīti ṣoḍaśa | tan-mayo virāṭ sa prasiddho nirmitaḥ | yatra virāji sa-citke cetanādhiṣṭhite bhuvana-trayaṁ dṛśyate | anenāṅgādi-kalpanā-saulabhyaṁ darśitam ||5||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **anena virāḍvigrahatvakathanena ||5||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **māyādhyair iti catuṣṭayam eka-vākyam | yatra virāji sa-citke samaṣṭi-jīva-caitanyādhiṣṭhite ||5||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **bhagavato vibhūtibhiḥ kalpito vigraho virāḍ evāstīty āha—māyādyaiḥ prakṛti-sūtra-mahad-ahaṅkāra-pañca-tanmātrair navabhiḥ, vikārā ekādaśendriyāṇi pañca-mahā-bhūtāni ceti ṣoḍaśa | tan-mayo virāṭ sa prasiddho nirmitaḥ | yatra virāji sa-citke cetanādhiṣṭhite bhuvana-trayaṁ dṛśyate ||5||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.6 ||**

**etad vai pauruṣaṁ rūpaṁ bhūḥ pādau dyauḥ śiro nabhaḥ |**

**nābhiḥ sūryo’kṣiṇī nāse vāyuḥ karṇau diśaḥ prabhoḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **etad vai pauruṣaṁ rūpam | puruṣasya vairājasya rūpam eveśvareṇādhiṣṭhitatvāt tad-abheda-vivakṣayā tasya rūpam ucyate | aṅga-kalpanām āha—bhūḥ pādāv ity-ādi-tribhiḥ | bhūr ādy-anuvādena bhagavat-pādādi-bhāvanā vidhīyate ||6||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **etatpratyakṣasiddham | puruṣasya bhagavato māyikaṁ rūpaṁ na tu svarūpamity arthaḥ | kimaṅgaṁ kayā vibhūtyā kalpitam iti cettatrāha—bhūr iti | saccidānandarūpasya bhagavataḥ pādayoryā vibhūtirbhūstayāsya pādau kalpitāv iti tadabhedanirdeśādbhūr eva pādāvevaṁ sarvatra jñeyam | evaṁ ca virāṭpuruṣasya pādādibhāvanayā saccidānandapuruṣasya pādādīni smartavyāni | yathā matprabhuḥ svapādābhyāṁ pṛthivīṁ bibharti śirasā divaṁ tathānyāni bhagavadaṅgāni sarvavastūni, evaṁ sarvabhāvanāpi bhagavadbhāvanaiveti jñeyam ||6||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **bhūḥ pādāv ity ādau tat-pādādi-śaktyaiva bhūr-ādīnāṁ śaktir ity abhinnatayopāsyata ity arthaḥ ||6||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **pauruṣaṁ puruṣasya bhagavato māyikaṁ rūpaṁ, na tu svarūpam ity arthaḥ | kayā kayā vibhūtyā kiṁ kim aṅgaṁ kalpitam ? tad āha—bhūr iti | saccidānanda-vapuṣo bhagavataḥ pādayor yā vibhūtir bhūs tayāsya pādau kalpitāv iti | tad-abheda-nirdeśād bhūre eva pādau | evaṁ sarvatra jñeyam | evaṁ ca virāṭ-puruṣasya pādādi-bhāvanayā saccidānanda-puruṣasya pādādīni smartavyāni | yathā mat-prabhur bhagavān sva-pādābhyāṁ tad-vibhūtiṁ pṛthivīṁ bibharti, tad-vibhūtiṁ divaṁ bibhartīty evaṁ sarvāṇi eva vastūni nayana-mano-gatāni bhagavad-aṅgāny eva tad vibhūtitvād ity ataḥ sarva-bhāvanāpi bhagavad-bhāvanaiveti vivekaḥ ||6|| 

 **...**

**|| 12.11.7 ||**

**prajāpatiḥ prajananam apāno mṛtyur īśituḥ |**

**tad-bāhavo loka-pālā manaś candro bhruvau yamaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **prajananaṁ meḍhram | apānaḥ pāyuḥ ||7||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **prajanyate'neneti prajananam ||7||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.11.8 ||**

**lajjottaro’dharo lobho dantā jyotsnā smayo**[^67]** bhramaḥ |**

**romāṇi bhūruhā bhūmno meghāḥ puruṣa-mūrdhajāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā), jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **uttara uparitanaḥ | smayo hāsaḥ | bhramo bhramaheturmāyā ||8||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **uttara oṣṭho lajjā | adhara oṣṭho lobhaḥ | smayo hāsyam | bhramaḥ māyā ||8||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.9 ||**

**yāvān ayaṁ vai puruṣo yāvatyā saṁsthayā mitaḥ |**

**tāvān asāv api mahā-puruṣo loka-saṁsthayā ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **anuktam anyad apy evam ūhyam ity āha—yāvān ayaṁ vyaṣṭiḥ puruṣaḥ sva-mānataḥ sapta-vitastiḥ | saṁsthayāvayava-sanniveśena | mitaḥ parimitaḥ ||9||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **uttara uparitanaḥ | smayo hāsaḥ | bhramo bhramaheturmāyā ||9||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **samaṣṭi-vyaṣṭyoḥ prāyeṇaikyāt vyaṣṭi-puruṣasya prākṛtatvān malinasya darśanam eva nirmalaṁ sac-cid-ānanda-mayaṁ puruṣaṁ paricāyayati—yāvān ayam iti | mitaḥ parimitaḥ ||9||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.10-11 ||**

**kaustubha-vyapadeśena svātma-jyotir bibharty ajaḥ |**

**tat-prabhā vyāpinī sākṣāt śrīvatsam urasā vibhuḥ ||**

**sva-māyāṁ vana-mālākhyāṁ nānā-guṇa-mayīṁ dadhat |**

**vāsaś chando-mayaṁ pītaṁ brahma-sūtraṁ tri-vṛt svaram ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **bhūṣaṇādīny āha—kaustubhety-ādinā | svātma-jyotiḥ śuddhaṁ jīva-caitanyam | yā tasya kaustubhasya prabhā tām eva śrī-vatsaṁ bibharti ||10|| tri-vṛt svaraṁ tri-mātraṁ praṇavam ||11||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **vyapadeśo miṣaḥ vyapadeśomiṣe'sthane pakṣivarjite iti niruktiḥ | aṅgānyuktvā bhūṣaṇānyāha—kaustubhasvarūpeṇa śuddhajīvacaitamyaṁ kaustubhasyaiva vibhūti dhatte | tathā hi—


    akāraṇocyate viṣṇuḥ śrīrukāreṇa kathyate | 


    makāras tu tayordāsaḥ pañcaviṁśaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||
