iti bhaktivivekokteḥ | svadāsaṁ bhagavān hṛdi dhatte ityabhipretyaiva sādhavo hṛdayaṁ tvaham bhagavānbhaktabhaktimān ity-ādy-uktam | kaustubhasyaiva prabhā vyāpinī dakṣiṇastanorddhvaparyantagāminī yā tām eva śrīvatsaṁ dakṣiṇāvartamṛṇālatantusūkṣmaromāvalyākāraṁ bibharti, yasya vibhūtirdharmaḥ, tathaiva vāmastanorddhvalakṣmī rekhānikaṣāśmani kānako rekhevānuktāpi jñeyā, yasyā vibhūtiś ca rājādisampat || triguṇātmikā māyā vanamālāyā vibhūtiḥ, chandāṁsi pītāmbarasyopavītasya praṇavastrimātraś ca vibhūtir evam eva sarvatra svavibhūtyā sāmānādhikaraṇyam ||10-11||

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) : **kaustubha-vyapadeśenety-ādi | ātma-jyotir brahma-jyotis tat-prabheva śrīvatsam || brahma-sūtraṁ praṇavam ||10-11||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **kaustubheti | atra bhūr-ādīnām iva jīvākhya-svātma-jyotir-ādīnām api kaustubhādibhyo bahiraṅgatvaṁ darśitam | svātma-jyotiṣa evendriya-dvārā prakāśaḥ śrīvatsatayā kalpyata ity arthaḥ ||10||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** nānā-guṇa-mayīm iti tri-guṇātmikā māyā vana-mālāyā vibhāviḥ | vāsa iti pīta-vāsaso vibhāviś chandāṁsi | brahma-sūtram ity upavītasya vibhūtis trivṛt svaraḥ trimātraḥ praṇavaḥ | evam eva sarvatra sva-vibhūtyā samānādhikaraṇyam ||10-11||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.12 ||**

**bibharti sāṅkhyaṁ yogaṁ ca devo makara-kuṇḍale |**

**mauliṁ padaṁ pārameṣṭhyaṁ sarva-lokābhayaṅ-karam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **pārameṣṭhyaṁ padaṁ brahma-lokam ||12||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **sāṅkhyaṁ jñānam | yogaṁ karma ||12||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.11.13 ||**

**avyākṛtam anantākhyam āsanaṁ yad-adhiṣṭhitaḥ |**

**dharma-jñānādibhir yuktaṁ sattvaṁ padmam ihocyate ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **avyākṛtaṁ pradhānam | yad adhiṣṭhito’dhīṣṭhāya sthitaḥ, tad āsana-bhūtaṁ padmaṁ sattvaṁ sattva-guṇaḥ ||13||

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) : **avyākṛtaṁ pradhānam, grasate’vyākṛtaṁ rājan guṇān kālena coditam [bhā.pu. 12.4.18] ity-ādi, tan-mūla-bhūtaṁ padam āmananti yat [bhā.pu. 12.4.21] ity-antaṁ yat prāg uktaṁ, tad evāsanam adhiṣṭhānam | kaustubho’tropalakṣaṇaṁ, sarvam evābharaṇam | tathā… | evaṁ pīta-vāsaś copalakṣaṇaṁ, sarvam eva śayyādi-vāsaś ca | brahma-sūtram upalakṣaṇam, sarvāṇy eva hārādi-sūtrāṇi | āsanam upalakṣaṇam | sarvāṇy eva paryaṅkādīni | brahma-yonir veda-yonim | brahmaṇaḥ parama-jyotiṣo vā ||13||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **yad adhiṣṭhito’dhīṣṭhāya sthitaḥ, tad āsanam anantākhyam avyākṛtaṁ pradhānam ucyate iti anantasyaiva vibhūtiḥ | pradhānaṁ jagat-sṛṣṭy-ādi-kāraṇī-bhūtam | vana-mālā-vibhūtir māyā tu tato’pi mūrta-bhūtā jñeyā | tatra ca dharmādi-yuktam āsana-padmaṁ tu sattvaṁ sattva-guṇaḥ ||13||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.14 ||**

**ojaḥ-saho-bala-yutaṁ mukhya-tattvaṁ gadāṁ dadhat |**

**apāṁ tattvaṁ dara-varaṁ tejas-tattvaṁ sudarśanam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **mukhya-tattvaṁ prāṇa-tattvam | prāṇo vai mukhyaḥ iti śruteḥ | dara-varaṁ śaṅkham ||14||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **avyākṛtaṁ pradhānamanantasyaiva vibhūtistasyaiva viśvahetutvam yamāhurasya sthitisargasaṁyamaṁ tribhirvihīnaṁ yamanantamadvayam itiḥ utpattisthitilayahetavosya kalpāḥ sattvādyāḥ prakṛtiguṇā yadīkṣayāsan iti pañcamokteḥ | vanamālāvibhūtirmāyā tu tatopi mūlabhūtā jñeyā ||13||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.11.15 ||**

**nabho-nibhaṁ nabhas-tattvam asiṁ carma tamo-mayam |**

**kāla-rūpaṁ dhanuḥ śārṅgaṁ tathā karma-mayeṣudhim ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā), jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **nabhonibhaṁ nabhovannirmalam | asiṁ nandakam | tamomayaṁ tamoguṇavadācchādakam | puṇyakarmasvarūpe iṣudhī ||15||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** asiṁ nabhas tattvaṁ nabho-nibham ākāśa-tulyaṁ nirmalam | carma tamo-mayaṁ tamas-tattvam ||15||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.16 ||**

**indriyāṇi śarān āhur ākūtīr asya syandanam |**

**tan-mātrāṇy asyābhivyaktiṁ mudrayārtha-kriyātmatām ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ākūtīḥ kriyā-śakti-yuktaṁ manaḥ | asya rathasyābhivyaktiṁ bahir abhivyaktaṁ rūpam | mudrayā dhṛtayārtha-kriyātmatāṁ varadābhayadādi-rūpatvaṁ bibharti | tat-tan-mudrayā tathā tathā bhāvayed ity arthaḥ ||16||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ity artha iti—varadamudrayā varada tvamabhayamudrayābhayadatvaṁ ca bhāvayed iti bhāvaḥ | bāhuprasāraṇapūrvakaṁ dakṣahastasya vistṛtayottānīkaraṇenāśvāsanaṁ varamudrā bhavati, tasya tathaiva nyubjīkaraṇenāśvāsanamabhayadamudrā bhavatīti vivekaḥ | evamanyā 

api jñeyāḥ ||16||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **ākūtīr iti | lakṣaṇayā kriyā-śakti-yuktaṁ mano yasya bhagavataḥ syandanam āhuḥ tan-mātrāṇy asya bhagavato’bhivyaktim āhuḥ, tathā svasyārtha-kriyātmatāṁ varadābhayadādi-rūpatāṁ mudrām āhuḥ, mudrām evāhur ity arthaḥ | gotreṇa gārgya itivat tṛtīyā ||16||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** ākutiḥ kriyā-śakti-yutaṁ manaḥ | syandanaṁ rathasya vibhūtir manaḥ | tan-mātrāṇi śabdādayo viṣayā abhivyaktiḥ asya abhivyakter āvirbhāvasya vibhāvayaḥ | viṣaya-jighṛkṣā-rūpasya manorathasya bahir abhivyakti-rūpā eva śabdādayo viṣayī indriya-grāhyā ity arthaḥ | mudrayā varadābhayadā-rūpayā dhṛtayā artha-kriyātmatāṁ bibharti | artha-kriyā loka-vyavahāras tat-svarūpatāṁ dhatte vara-dat tasya abhayadatvasya vibhūtayas tās tā artha-kriyā ity arthaḥ ||16||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.17 ||**

**maṇḍalaṁ deva-yajanaṁ dīkṣā saṁskāra ātmanaḥ |**

**paricaryā bhagavata ātmano durita-kṣayaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **maṇḍalaṁ deva-yajanam | deva-pūjā-bhūmiṁ sūrya-maṇḍalatvena bhāvayed ity arthaḥ | antar-vahni-maṇḍalaṁ vā | dīkṣā-saṁskāra ātmano guru-kṛtāṁ mantra-dīkṣām evātmanas tat-pūjā-yogyatāṁ bhāvayed ity arthaḥ | paricaryeti | bhagavatas tāṁ paricaryāṁ svasya sakala-pāpa-kṣayāyety evaṁ bhāvayed ity arthaḥ ||17||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ity artha iti—sūryamaṇḍalaṁ yathā—dhyeyaḥ sadā savitṛmaṇḍalamadhyavartī nārāyaṇaḥ ity-ādy-ukter bhagavaddhyānādhiṣṭhānaṁ, tathedaṁ kṣetram api matpūjādhiṣṭhānam iti cintayed iti bhāvaḥ | yad vā, ekādaśaskandhoktarītyā hṛtkañjakarṇikā madhye somasūryāgnīnāmuttarottaracintayā vahnimadhye smaredrūpam ity uktes tad eva vahnimaṇḍalaṁ devapūjābhūmiṁ cintayed ity arthaḥ | ity artha iti—adīkṣitasya pūjānarhatvād iti bhāvaḥ| tad uktam—


    divyaṁ jñānaṁ yato dadyātkuryātmāpasya saṅkṣayam | 


    tasmāddīkṣeti sā proktā munibhistantravedibhiḥ || iti | 

kiṁ ca—sarvāśrameṣu dīkṣāyā āvaśyakatvamapi—


    dīkṣāmūlī japaḥ sarvo dīkṣāmūlaṁ paraṁ tapaḥ | 


    dīkṣāmāśritya nivasedyatra kutrāśrame vasan  | 


    adīkṣitā ye kurvanti japapūjādikāḥ kriyāḥ | 


    na bhavanti śriyasteṣāṁ śilāyāmuptabījavat | 


    devi dīkṣāvihīnasya na siddhirna ca sadgatiḥ | 


    tasmātsarvaprayatnena guruṇā dīkṣito bhavet | 


    gurorabhāve mantrāṇāṁ pustakaṁ gurumācaret | 


    na cāyogyādgurordīkṣā grahītavyā kadācana | 


    dakṣiṇāmūrtito yad vā,  dīkṣā grāhyā tathā ghaṭāt || iti | 

adīkṣito hi maraṇe rauravaṁ narakaṁ vrajet iti ca | yattūktam—


    kalpe dṛṣṭvā tu yo mantra gṛhṇāti hi narādhamaḥ | 


    manvantarasahasreṣu niṣkṛtirnaiva vidyate || 

iti tatsadgurusattve pustakāddīkṣā na grāhyetiparam iti tantrasāre | sadgurunirṇayas tu brahmavaivartīyakṛṣṇakhaṇḍatryaśītitamādhyāye—


    tejīyāṁsaṁ guru kuryātsarvato rakṣituṁ kṣamam | 


    kyoyukta ca vidvāṁsaṁ vipraṁ bhāryāsamanvitam | 


    vaiṣṇavaṁ ca kulīnaṁ ca svācāraṁ bodhane kṣamam || iti | 

vipakṣe doṣo'pi tatraivoktaḥ—


    vidyāhīnādbhavenmūḍho mantragrāhī hyapaṇḍitāt | 


    jātihīnākṣayaḥ prokto vyādhino vyādhiyuktathā | 


    vaṁśahīnādvaṁśahīno bhāryāhīnaḥ striyā rahāt | 


    tasmātsarvaprayatnena vicārya gurumācaret || iti | 

kiṁ ca—


    pramādādyadi jāyeta puṁso'yogyo gururmune | 


    taṁ tyaktvāpaciti kṛtvā kuryādyogyaṁ guruṁ punaḥ || 

prāyaścittaṁ tu—


    viprasya kṣatriyagurau gāyatryā lakṣamīritam | 


    vaiśye tu dviguṇaṁ śūdre daśalakṣa prakīrtitam | 


    kṣatrasya tu gurau veśya lakṣam eva prakīrtitam | 


    śūdre tu daśalakṣaṁ tadvaiṁśyasya śṛṇu bho mune | 


    śūdre gurau rudralakṣaṁ gāyatryāḥ parikīrtitam || iti vāratāntaviḥ | 

ity artha iti—haripūjayaiva sakalapāpakṣayo bhavatyataḥ saiva kāryeti bhāvaḥ | pāpaughānāṁ praśananaṁ pūjanaṁ sarvadā hareḥ ity-ādy-ukteḥ paricaryāyā duritakṣaya eva vibhūtir iti bhāvaḥ ||17||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **devasya yajanaṁ yatra kutracid bhagavataḥ pūjā-sthānam eva | maṇḍalaṁ bhagavato nija-sthāna-valayam | saṁskāro bhagavataḥ sākṣāt-prāpti-yogyatā ||17||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **sūryasyeva bhagavad-vigrahasya yan maṇḍalaṁ, tad deva-yajanam, deva-pūjā-bhūmim | dīkṣā tan-mantropadeśa eva ātmano jīvasya saṁskāraḥ | tan-mantra-prayogasya vibhūtir jīva-saṁskāra ity arthaḥ | paricaryeti tat-paricaryāyā jīva-dūrita-kṣaya eva vibhūtiḥ ||17||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.18 ||**

**bhagavān bhaga-śabdārthaṁ līlā-kamalam udvahan |**

**dharmaṁ yaśaś ca bhagavāṁś cāmara-vyajane’bhajat ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **pūrvam āsana-padmam uktam idānīṁ kara-sthaṁ padmam āha—bhagavān iti | bhaga-śabdārtham aiśvaryādi-ṣāḍ-guṇyam ||18||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **

aiśvaryasya samagrasya dharmasya yaśasaḥ śriyaḥ | 


    jñānavairāgyayoścaiva ṣaṇṇāṁ bhaga itīṅganā || 

iti smṛtyuktamaiśvaryādiṣāḍguṇyamity arthaḥ | udvahan bhavatīti śeṣaḥ | evaṁ sati bhinnavākyatvena bhagavacchabdapaunaruktyaṁ na bhavatīti bhagaśabdasyārthacatuṣkam | līlākamalaṁ dadhaditi—aiśvaryaśrījñānavairāgyāṇi prākṛtāni līlākamalasya vibhūtayaḥ, dharmaṁ yaśaca prākataṁ cāmaravyajanayorvibhūtī, parantu prākṛtāprākṛtayorabhedam eva bhāvayed iti tātparyam ||18||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **bhagaḥ prāpañcikas tad-atītaś ca | līlā-kamalaṁ tu tad-atīta-mayam | tathāpi dvayor abheda-mayaṁ bhāvayed ity arthaḥ ||18||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** bhaga-śabdasyārtham artha-catuṣkaṁ līlā-kamalaṁ dadhad iti līlā-kamalasya vibhūtayaḥ aiśvarya-śrī-jñāna-vairāgyāṇi prākṛtāni | dharmaḥ yaśaś ca prākṛtaṁ cāmara-vyajanayor vibhūtī ||18||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.19 ||**

**ātapatraṁ tu vaikuṇṭhaṁ dvijā dhāmākuto-bhayam |**

**tri-vṛd vedaḥ suparṇākhyo yajñaṁ vahati puruṣam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **he **dvijāḥ** ! eka-vacanānto vā pāṭhaḥ | **akuto-bhayaṁ** kaivalyaṁ **dhāma** gṛham abhajat | yad vā, **vaikuṇṭhasya** viśeṣaṇam akuto-bhayaṁ yad dhāmeti | **tri-vṛt** ṛg-yajuḥ-sāma-rūpo **vedaḥ**, suparṇo’si garutmāṁs tri-vṛtte śiraḥ ity-ādi mantra-liṅgāt | **yajñaṁ** yajña-rūpaṁ puruṣam, yajño vai viṣṇuḥ iti śruteḥ ||19||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **he dvijā iti—gaṇāpekṣaṁ bahutvaṁ pūjāyāṁ vā | ekavacanātapāṭhe tu gaṇamukhyaśaunakaviṣayaiva saṁbuddhir iti maduktapūjāyāṁ mukhyādhikāro dvijasyaivetyabhiprāyaḥ | brahmalokaḥ sanātanaḥ ity uktimāśrityāha—yadveti | yadyapi mantre trivṛttaṁ śiraḥ ity uktes trivṛto vedasya garutmacchirastvamuktaṁ tathāpi mukhamarddhaṁ śarīrasya sarvaṁ vā mukhamucyate iti nyāyena śiraso'pi sarvaśarīratvamāyātīti | etena vedoktayāgādirgaruḍasyaiva vibhūtirity arthaḥ | akutobhayaṁ vaikuṇṭhaṁ chatraṁ, loke yannirbhayatvaṁ pratīyate tatkhalu chatrasyaiva vibhūtir iti | chatravatsaṁsāratāpavārakatvādvaikuṇṭhasyetyarthaḥ ||19||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : vaikuṇṭhaṁ** brahma-lokopariṣṭād vikuṇṭhā-sutāvirbhāvitaṁ, tat-padam asya virāḍ-adhiṣṭhātuḥ śrī-nārāyaṇasya **ātapatraṁ** bhāvayed ity arthaḥ ||19||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** he **dvijāḥ** ! **akuto-bhayaṁ dhāma vaikuṇṭham** eva **ātapatraṁ** chatram abhajad iti loka-gataṁ yat kiñcin nirbhayatvaṁ pratīyate, tat khalu chatrasyaiva vibhūtir ity arthaḥ | **trivṛt** ṛg-yajuḥ-sāma-rūpo **vedaḥ**, vedokto yāgādir ity arthaḥ ||19||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.20 ||**

**anapāyinī bhagavatī śrīḥ sākṣād ātmano hareḥ |**

**viṣvaksenas tantra-mūrtir viditaḥ pārṣadādhipaḥ |**

**nandādayo’ṣṭau dvāḥ-sthāś ca te’ṇimādyā harer guṇāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **anapāyinī hareḥ śaktiḥ | tatra hetuḥ, sākṣād ātmanaḥ svarūpasya cid-rūpatvāt tasyās tad-abhedād ity arthaḥ | tantra-mūrtiḥ pañcarātrādy-āgama-rūpaḥ | ye’ṇimādayo’ṣṭau guṇās te harer dvāra-pālā nandādayaḥ ||20||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **viṣvaksena iti pacarātrādyāgamo viṣvaksenasya vibhūtiḥ | anapāyinī nityayoginī sākṣatsvarūpabhūtā śaktiḥ āhlādinī śaktarvibhūtirlaukikaḥ svargādyānanda ūhyaḥ| tatrānapāyinītve | ity artha iti—śaktiśaktimatorabhedopacārād iti bhāvaḥ ||20||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **anety ardhakam | evambhūtānanta-vṛttikā yā svarūpa-śaktiḥ, sā tv iha bhagavad-vāmāṁśa-vartinī mūrtimatī lakṣmīr evety āha—anapāyinīti | sākṣād ātmanaḥ parama-svarūpa-bhūtasya yā harer bhagavatī śrīḥ, saiva jagataḥ śrīr iti bhāvanayety[^68] arthaḥ |[^69] atra sākṣāc-chabdena vilajjamānayā yasya [bhā.pu. 2.5.13] ity-ādy uktā māyā neti dhvanitam | 

tatrānapāyitvaṁ, yathā śrī-hāyaśīrṣa-pañcarātre—


    paramātmā harir devas tac-chaktiḥ śrīr ihoditā |


    śrīr devī prakṛtiḥ proktā keśavaḥ puruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ |


    na viṣṇunā vinā devī na hariḥ padmajāṁ vinā || iti |

śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇe ca—


    nityaiva sā jagan-mātā viṣṇoḥ śrīr anapāyinī |


    yathā sarva-gato viṣṇus tathaiveyaṁ dvijottama || [vi.pu. 1.8.17] iti |

tatraivānyatra—


    evaṁ yathā jagat-svāmī deva-devo janārdanaḥ |


    avatāraṁ karoty eṣā tathā śrīs tat-sahāyinī || [vi.pu. 1.9.140] iti |

cid-rūpatvam api skānde—


    aparaṁ tv akṣaraṁ yā sā prakṛtir jaḍa-rūpikā |


    śrīḥ parā prakṛtiḥ proktā cetanā viṣṇu-saṁśrayā ||


    tām akṣaraṁ paraṁ prāhuḥ parataḥ param akṣaram | 


    harir evākhila-guṇa akṣara-trayam īritam || iti ||20|| [bhagavat-sandarbha 89]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **anapāyinī eka-rūpā sākṣāt svarūpa-bhūtā śaktiḥ | asyāhlādinī-śakter vibhūtir laukikaḥ svargādy-ānanda ūhyaḥ | tantra-mūrtiḥ pañcarātrādy-āgama-rūpaḥ pañcarātrādy-āgamā viṣvaksenasya vibhūtaya ity arthaḥ | harer dvāḥsthā ye nandādayaḥ, te’pi aṇimādyā guṇā anya-gatā vibhūtayaḥ ||20||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.21 ||**

**vāsudevaḥ saṅkarṣaṇaḥ pradyumnaḥ puruṣaḥ svayam |**

**aniruddha iti brahman mūrti-vyūho’bhidhīyate ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tasyaiva catur-vyūhopāsanām āha—vāsudevādi-śabdaiḥ puruṣaḥ śrī-nārāyaṇa eva svayaṁ mūrti-bhedair upāsya ity abhidhīyate ||21||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **yasyāṅgopāgānyuktāni tasyaivetyarthaḥ | vāsudeva ity-ādicatuṣṭayagataścaturvyūhaḥ | svayaṁ puruṣo bhagavānevetyarthaḥ ||21||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **vāsudevādayaḥ sākṣāc catur-vyūha-rūpā viśvāditvena kalpita-rūpā[^70] iti vāsudeva ity-ādi-padya-dvayārthaḥ ||22||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** dvāḥsthān uktvā dik-catuṣṭaya-gatāṁś caturo vyūhān āha—vāsudeva ity-ādi | mūrti-samūhaḥ | svayaṁ puruṣo bhagavān evety anvayaḥ ||21||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.22 ||**

**sa viśvas taijasaḥ prājñas turīya iti vṛttibhiḥ |**

**arthendriyāśaya-jñānair bhagavān paribhāvyate ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tasyaivādhyātmani caturdhopāsanām āha—sa eva bhagavān viśvādi-śabdair vṛttibhir jāgrad-ādy-avasthābhiḥ paribhāvyate | tad-vṛtty-upādhīn āha—arthā bāhyāḥ | indriyaṁ manaḥ | āśayas tad ubhaya-saṁskāra-yuktam ajñānam | jñānaṁ tritaya-sākṣi taiḥ ||22||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **adhyātmani cakṣurādikaraṇābhimānini jīve | paribhāvyate paricintyate | tadvṛttyupādhīn jāgradādivṛtyupādhīn | tathā cendriyairarthāvabhāsakajāgradavasthāyāṁ viśva iti, manomātrāvabhāsyasvapnāvasthāyāṁ taijasa iti ajñānopalakṣitasuṣuptyavasthāyāṁ prājña iti trayasya jāgradāditrayasya sākṣi yajjñānaṁ tac ca caitanyaṁ, sa eva turīya iti etairity arthaḥ | caturṇāṁ vyūhānāṁ vibhūtīrāha—ubhayasaṁskārayuktam | sukhamahamasvāpsam iti sukham na kiñcidavediṣam ityākārakaṁ jñānañcetyubhayaṁ tairviśva ity-ādyā vṛttayastābhirbhagavāneva paricintyante caturṇāṁ vyūhānām eva viśvādyāścatasro vṛttayo niyamyā vibhūtaya iti bhāvaḥ | tatra vāsudevasya viśvaḥ, saṅkarṣaṇasya taijasaḥ, pradyumnasya prājñaḥ, aniruddhasya turīyo jñānam iti bhedaḥ ||22||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _pūrva-ślokasya vyākhyā draṣṭavyā._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** caturṇāṁ vyūhānāṁ vibhūtīr āha—sa iti | arthādyā indriyaṁ manaḥ, āśayas tad-ubhaya-saṁskāra-yuktam | sukham aham asvāpsam iti sukhaṁ na kiñcid avediṣam ity ākārakam ajñānaṁ ca, tathā jñānaṁ ceti tair yā viśva ity ādyā vṛttayas tābhiḥ sa bhagavān eva paribhāvyate paricintyate, caturṇāṁ vyūhānām eva viśvādyāś catasro vṛttayo niyamyā vibhūtaya iti bhāvaḥ | atra vāsudevasya viśvaḥ | saṅkarṣaṇasya taijasaḥ | pradyumnasya prājñaḥ | aniruddhasya turīyo jñānam iti vibhūtayo vivecanīyāḥ ||22||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.23 ||**

**aṅgopāṅgāyudhākalpair bhagavāṁs tac catuṣṭayam |**

**bibharti sma catur-mūrtir bhagavān harir īśvaraḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ukta-catur-vyūha-dvayopāsane’pi pūrvokta-bhaṅgādy-upāsanam āha—aṅgeti | aṅgādibhir upālakṣito bhagavān harir vāsudevādi-catur-mūrtiḥ san viśvādi-catuṣṭayaṁ bibharti sma | viśvādi-bhāve’pi tan niyantus tasya na jīvatvam ity āha—viśvādi-catuṣṭayaṁ bibhrad api bhagavān īśvara eveti ||23||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tanniyaturviśvādiniyantuḥ | aṅgopāṅgādimāhitasya vāsudevasya viśva ityeva vibhūtiḥ | saṅkarṣaṇādīnāṁ taijasādyā vibhūtayaḥ | hari-bhaktāghahantā | iśvaro viśvādiniyatā ||23||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **teṣām arthādīnāṁ catuṣṭayam aṅgādi-rūpeṇa bibharttīti aṅgādy-abhedenārthādayo’py upāsyā ity arthaḥ ||23||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **vyañjitam evārthaṁ spaṣṭayati aṅgādibhiḥ sahita eva catur-mūrtir bhagavān catuṣṭayaṁ viśvādi-catuṣkaṁ niyāmakatayā bibharti | aṅgopāṅgāyudhākalpa-sahitasyaiva vāsudevasya vibhūtir viśvam ity evam eva saṅkarṣaṇādīnāṁ taijasādyā vibhūtayaḥ | harir ity upāsakānāṁ durita-hartā īśvaro viśvādīnāṁ niyantā ||23||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.24 ||**

**dvija-ṛṣabha sa eṣa brahma-yoniḥ svayaṁ-dṛk**

**sva-mahima-paripūrṇo māyayā ca svayaitat |**

**sṛjati harati pātīty ākhyayānāvṛtākṣo**

**vivṛta iva niruktas tat-parair ātma-labhyaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tasyaiva brahmādi-tri-mūrtitām āha—dvija-ṛṣabheti | sa eṣa eka eva bhagavān brahma-yonir vedasya kāraṇam ity-ādi-hetu-trayam | vastuto bhedābhāve’py etaj jagat sva-gata-māyayā sṛjati harati pātīti kṛtvākhyayā brahmādi-rūpayānāvṛtākṣo’nācchanna-jñāno’pi vivṛta iva bhinna iva niruktaḥ śāstreṣu na tu bhinnaḥ | atra vidvad anubhavaṁ pramāṇayati, yatas tat parair ātmatveneva labhyata iti ||24||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **he dvijaṛṣabheti—ṛtyakaḥ iti hrasve prakṛtibhāvaḥ | bhagavad-upāsakatvena tvaṁ brāhmaṇaśreṣṭho'si brāhmaṇo janmanā śreyānkimu matkalayā punaḥ itiḥ śrī-mukhokter iti saṁbuddherbhāvaḥ| svaśaktirūpeṇa svasminprāptayā māyayā | tvatprasādabladhajñānena tvatparāyaṇaiḥ bhaktyāham ekayā labhyaḥ ityāyukter ātma rūpeṇaiva tvaṁ prāpyasa ityāśayaḥ | caturvyūhamuktvā trimūrtitām āha—yoniḥ prakāśakaḥ| na cāsya ko'pi prakāśaka ityāha—svayaṁdṛk svayaṁprakāśakaḥ | na cāsya rājñaścaiśvaryārthaṁ prakṛtyapekṣetyāha—svamahimaparipūrṇaḥ, kintu krīḍārtham eva svayā śaktyā māyayā brahmādināmnā sṛjatītyādi, ityevamanāvṛtākṣo'pi aparicchinna jñānopi vivṛta iva kṛtavivaraṇa iva nirukta iva | vastutastu—nirvaktuṁ vivarituṁ brahmādibhiraśakya eva iti bhāvaḥ| tarhi kimarthametāvānāyāsaḥ kṛtastatrāha—tatparaistadbhaktairevātmanā manasā labhya etādṛśadhyāneneti bhāvaḥ | tatra tatpādānāṁ vibhūtibhiḥ pṛthivyādyairdṛṣṭasmṛtādibhir eva tatpādādismaraṇaṁ sukhena bhavet | tathā hi—sadādhyeyasya matprabhoścaraṇasyaiva vibhūtiriyaṁ pṛthvī sadā śrayate'taḥ pṛthvyāśritāḥ sthirajaṅgamā matprabhoścaraṇā śritā eva, te mayā saṁmānyā eva na tu dveṣyās tathā tadvakṣasthakaustubhasya sarve'pi jīvā vibhūtayo'tasteṣām eko'pi mayā dveṣṭuṁ na yujyata ityevaṁbhāvanaivātra phalaṁ dṛśyam iti viśvanāthaḥ ||24||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **yasmai te upāsana-bhedās tan-māhātmyaṁ darśayati—dvijeti | brahma-yonitvādi-trayeṇa svarūpa-śaktir darśitā | tatra māyā-doṣeṇa liptatvam āśaṅkyāha—māyayā cānāvṛtākṣa iti | tatra hetuḥ—svayā svādhīnayeti | māyāṁ viśinaṣṭi—etad viśvaṁ sṛjatīty ādyā khyātiḥ vikhyātir yayā evam-bhūtācintya-māhātmyo’pi tat-parair bhaktair vivṛta iva kara-kalita iva niruktaḥ pratipāditaḥ | yatas tair ātmani citte labhyaḥ anubhavituṁ śakya iti ||24||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** tasya catur-mūrtitām uktvā tri-mūrtitām āha—he dvijarṣabha ! eṣa bhagavān brahmaṇo vedasya yoniḥ prakāśakaḥ, na cāsya ko’pi prakāśaka ity āha—svayaṁ-dṛk sva-prakāśaḥ | na cāsya rājñaḥ ivaiśvaryārthaṁ prakṛty-apekṣety āha—sva-mahima-pūrṇaḥ | kintu krīḍārtham eva svayā sva-śaktyā māyayā māyākhyayā brahmādi-nāmnā sṛjati pātīty evam, anāvṛtākṣo’pi aparichinna-jñāno’pi māyayā vivṛta iva kṛta-vivaraṇa iva, nirukta iva | vastutas tu nirvaktuṁ vivarituṁ brahmādibhir apy ayam aśakya eveti bhāvaḥ | 

tarhi kim-artham etāvān āyāsaḥ kṛtaḥ ? tatrāha—tat-parais tad-bhakta-janair ātmanā manasā etādṛśa-dhyānena labhya iti | atra tat-pādādīnāṁ vibhūtibhiḥ pṛthivy-ādibhir dṛṣṭa-smṛtādibhir eva tat-pādādi-smaraṇaṁ sukhena bhavet | tathā hi sarvadā dhyeyasya mat-prabhoś caraṇasyaiva vibhūtir iyaṁ pṛthvī sarvadā dṛśyate, ataḥ pṛthvīm āśritāḥ sthāvara-jaṅgamā mat-prabhoś caraṇāśritā eva te mayā sammānanīyā eva, na tu dveṣṭavyāḥ | tathā mat-prabhor vakṣasi vṛtasya kaustubhasya vibhūtayaḥ sarve’pi jīvāḥ, atas teṣām eko’pi mayā dveṣṭuṁ nindituṁ vā na yujyata ity evaṁ bhāvanaivātra phalaṁ draṣṭavyam ||24||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.25 ||**

**śrī-kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇa-sakha vṛṣṇy-ṛṣabhāvani-dhrug**

**rājanya-vaṁśa-dahanānapavarga-vīrya |**

**govinda gopa-vanitā-vraja-bhṛtya-gīta-**

**tīrtha-śravaḥ śravaṇa-maṅgala pāhi bhṛtyān ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **yasyedam upāsanam uktaṁ taṁ śrī-kṛṣṇaṁ prārthayate—kṛṣṇa-sakha ! arjunasya sakhe ! vṛṣṇi-śreṣṭha ! avani-druho ye rājanyāḥ, teṣāṁ vaṁśasya dahana | anapavargam akṣīṇaṁ vīryaṁ yasya | gopa-vanitānāṁ vrajāḥ samūhā bhṛtyā nāradādayas tair gītaṁ tīrtha-bhūtaṁ śravaḥ kīrtir yasya | śravaṇam eva maṅgalaṁ yasya ||25||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **gopavanitāgītaṁ tu—jayati te'dhikaṁ janmanā vrajaḥ ity-ādinā, vāmabāhukṛtavāmakapolaḥ ity-ādinā, barhāpīḍaṁ naṭavaravapuḥ ity-ādinā | nāradagītaṁ saptamaskandhādiṣu prasiddham | ādinā sanakādigrahaḥ | saṁbuddhyabhiprāyāḥ kuntīstutau prathamaskandhe varṇitā api punar api kiñcidvarṇyante—kṛṣyate nijasamīpaṁ prāpyate bhaktajano'neneti kṛṣṇaḥ, śrīḥ rādhā tayā sahitaḥ śrī-kṛṣṇaḥ | aho svāsin śrīrādhayā saha tvayā vihāraḥ kevalaṁ mu (bhu) ktagopījanānāṁ nijasamīpākarṣaṇārtham eva yathā kṛtas tathādhunā mamāpyākarṣaṇaṁ kurv iti bhāvaḥ | antra hetutvena sambuddhyantaram āha—yatas tvaṁ kṛṣṇasakhosīti—kaṣyate viṣayair iti kṛṣṇo jīvastasya sakhā hitaiṣī ato māṁ jīvamapyuddhareti bhāvaḥ | tatraiva hetvantaram—vṛṣṇyṛṣabheti| varṣānti nijābhilaṣitam iti vṛṣṇayo vadānyā devāsteṣu śreṣṭhosīti viśvābhilaṣitapūrakasya tava mamābhilaṣitapūraṇaṁ na durghaṭam iti bhāvaḥ | atra hetutvena sambuddhyantaram āha—avanidhrugrājanyavaṁśaḥ | kaṁsanarakāsurādisamūhastasya dahane'kṣīṇaprabhāvo'sīti sarvalokahitārtaṁ yathā tvayā duṁṣṭā nāśitās tathā madajñānam api nāśayeti bhāvaḥ | śāstrapratipādyaṁ kamapyanyamāśrayāhaṁ tu vasudevanandano'smīti cettatrāha—govindeti | gobhirgībhirvedalakṣaṇābhirvidyate vicāryata iti govindaḥ | sarve vedā yatpadamāmananti iti śrutes tvam eva sarvaśāstrapratipādyo'sīti bhāvaḥ| yadyapyanye devā api hotāramindramavitāramindram iti, agnimītipurohitam ity-ādinā vedena pratipādyante tathāpi te na kintu smaraṇādi maṅgalāḥ śravaṇamaṅgalā santi tvantu śravaṇenaiva maṅgalaṁ karoṣīti bhāvaḥ | bhṛtyān bharituṁ yogyān | viśvambharasya te sarve eva bhṛtyāstadantargato'hamapyato mām api pāhīti bhāvaḥ | yadaṁśasya viṣṭabhyāham idaṁ kṛtsnam ekāṁśena sthito jagat iti gītokterupāsanamuktam | taṁ śrī-kṛṣṇaṁ sveṣṭadevaṁ paricāyayanprārthayate— śrī-kṛṣṇeti | kṛṣṇasyārjunasya sakheti pāṇveṣu snehaḥ svavaśīkārakaḥ, vṛṣṇyṛṣabheti yādaveṣu ca, tatra kiṁ dyotakaṁ tatrāha—avanidruho ye rājanyāsteṣāṁ vaṁśasya dahanam | yad vā, ta eva vaṁśāstatparasparasaṁmardotthavahne, tena pāṇḍavānāṁ yādavānāṁ ca vairiṇaḥ saṁhṛtya teṣāṁ pālaka iti | anapavargamakṣīṇaṁ vīryaṁ parākramo yasmād iti pāṇḍavānyādavāṁś ca yo bhavānsarvajayinaścakāreti bhāvaḥ | govindeti vrajasthalokeṣu tato'pyatisnehastatra kiṁ dyotakaṁ tatrāha—gopavanitānāṁ vrajasya samūhasya yo bhṛtyaḥ āsāmaho caraṇareṇujuṣāmahaṁ syām ity uktyaivābhipsitabhṛtyabhāva uddhavastena gītam | tā namasyannidaṁ jagau iti śrīśukokteryagītaṁ tīrthaṁ jagatpāvanaṁ śravo yaśastad eva śravaṇamaṅgalaṁ karṇasukhadaṁ yasya he tathābhūta ||25||

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) : **yasyedam upāsanam uktaṁ, sa tu śrī-kṛṣṇa eveti stauti—śrī-kṛṣṇety-ādi | gopa-vanitāś ca nāradādyāś ca tair gītaṁ tīrtha-bhūtam eva yaśo yasya ||25||

 

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tam eva nāmādi-grahaṇena spaṣṭayan prārthayate | yad vā, mama tv īdṛśa eva puruṣārtha iti vyañjayaṁs tādṛśam eva taṁ prārthayate—śrī-kṛṣṇeti | tatra śrī-kṛṣṇa-sakhety-ādinā pura-līlā, govindety-ādinā vraja-līlā | tatra vraja-līlāyā vyatyayenānte nirdeśāt tatraiva nija-sthitir darśitā tīrthety-ādinā tad vayam ime gopāś ca vanitās tad-aṅganāś ca vrajas tatra-sthā anye ca bhṛtyās tad-upāsakāś ca tair gīteti vigrahaḥ, vartamāne ktaḥ | bhṛtyān tan-mārge baddha-śraddhān asmān svayam eva tat siddhiṁ saṁpādayeti | evaṁ śrī-bhāgavata-śravaṇena kṛtaṁ sādhana-sādhya-naiyatyaṁ[^71] darśitam ||25||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** yad-ṁśasyedam upāsanam uktaṁ taṁ śrī-kṛṣṇaṁ sveṣṭa-devaṁ paricāyayan prārthayate—śrī-kṛṣṇeti | kṛṣṇasyārjunasya sakhe iti pāṇḍaveṣu snehaḥ sva-vaśīkārakaḥ, vṛṣṇy-ṛṣabheti yādaveṣu | tatra kiṁ dyotakam ? ity ata āha—avani-druho ye rājanyās teṣāṁ vaṁśasya dahana | yad vā, ta eva vaṁśās tat-paraspara-sammardottha-vahne | tena pāṇḍavānāṁ yādavānāṁ ca vairiṇaḥ saṁhṛtya teṣāṁ pālaka iti | anapavargam akṣīṇaṁ vīryaṁ parākramo yasmād iti pāṇḍavān yādavāṁś ca yo bhavān sarva-jayinaś cakāreti bhāvaḥ | govindeti vraja-stha-lokeṣu tato’py atisnehaḥ | tatra kiṁ dyotakam ity ata āha—gopa-vanitānāṁ vrajasya samūhasya yo bhṛtyaḥ—āsām aho caraṇa-reṇu-juṣām ahaṁ syāṁ [bhā.pu. 10.47.61] ity uktvaivābhīpsita-bhṛtya-bhāva uddhavas tena gītaṁ, tā manasyann idaṁ jagau [bhā.pu. 10.47.53] iti śrī-śukokter yad gītaṁ tīrthaṁ jagat-pāvanaṁ śravo yaśas tad eva śravaṇa-maṅgalaṁ karṇa-sukha-pradaṁ yasya he tathā-bhūta ! ||25||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.26 ||**

**ya idaṁ kalya utthāya mahā-puruṣa-lakṣaṇam |**

**tac-cittaḥ prayato japtvā brahma veda guhāśayam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **etaj japa-mātrasyāpi brahma-jñānaṁ phalam ity āha—ya iti | kalye uṣaḥ-kāle yas tac cittaḥ prayataḥ śuciś ca sa japtvā guhāśayaṁ hṛdi-sthaṁ brahma paśyati ||26||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **pratyūṣo'harmukhaṁ kalyam ity amaraḥ | antasthavadidaṁ padaṁ na pavargavad iti | mahāpuruṣo virāṭ tatra lakṣyatentaryāmitayeti tathā | guhāyāṁ hṛdaye śete tiṣṭhatīti guhāśayam yo veda nihitaṁ guhāyām iti śruteḥ | prayataḥ pavitraḥ san pavitraḥ prayataḥ pūtaḥ ity amaraḥ ||26||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **brahma śrī-bhagavat-tattvaṁ | guhāśayaṁ durūham api ||26||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** ya idaṁ mahā-puruṣa-lakṣaṇaṁ brahma-tattva-svarūpaṁ japtvā veda sa guhāśayaṁ paramātmanam eva vedety anvayaḥ ||26||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.27-28 ||**

**śrī-śaunaka uvāca—**

**śuko yad āha bhagavān viṣṇu-rātāya śṛṇvate |**

**sauro gaṇo māsi māsi nānā vasati saptakaḥ ||**

**teṣāṁ nāmāni karmāṇi saṁyuktānām adhīśvaraiḥ |**

**brūhi naḥ śraddadhānānāṁ vyūhaṁ sūryātmano hareḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **maṇḍalaṁ deva-yajanam ity uktyā buddhim āgato mūrti-vyūha-prasaṅgena ravi-vyūho’tra pṛcchyate, śuka iti | pañcame yad āha—


    tathānye ca ṛṣayo gandharvā apsaraso nāgā grāmaṇyo yātudhānā devā ity ekaikaśo gaṇaḥ sapta [bhā.pu. 5.21.18] ity-ādinā | 

sauraḥ sūrya-saṁbandhī | saptakaḥ saptānāṁ gaṇaḥ | teṣāṁ saptānām adhīśvarais tat tat patibhis tat tan māsādhikṛta-sūryair vā vyūhaṁ vibhāgam ||27-28||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **saptānāṁ sambandhī saptakaḥ | atra sambandhe kaḥ | hantānena śukaparīkṣitsaṁvādamayaṁ śrī-bhāgavataśāstramasmatpūrvapuruṣamārkaṇḍeyaṁ tadanuṣṭhitabhagavatpūjanatattvaṁ ca matpraśnānurodhāduktamidānīmasya śrī-bhāgavatasya tadviṣayasya bhagavataś ca dṛṣṭāntaḥ sūryaḥ kṛtaḥ—


    kṛṣṇe svadhāmopagate dharmajñānā dibhiḥ saha | 


    kalau naṣṭadṛśāmeṣaḥ purāṇārko'dhunoditaḥ || 

iti tad-uktyā kṛṣṇadyumaṇinimloce ityuddhavoktyā cāvagatas taṁ dvādaśātmakaṁ graharājamadhunā dvādaśa-skandhātmakaṁ purāṇarājasamāptyavasare prastāvayitumarhāmīti parāmṛśyāha śuka iti sarvamanyatsamam || adhīśvaraiḥ saṁyuktānāmityanena teṣāṁ pratyekaṁ svasvapatisāhityena dvandvaṁ jñeyam, | ata eva dvādaśaḥ sapta pṛthak caturdaśa iti pañcamaskandhoktiḥ saṁgacchate | sūryasyāpi svaniyantrantaryāmisāhityena dvandvaṁ jñeyam iti bālabodhinyām | yaśvāsau puruṣe yaścāditye ity-ādiśruteḥ | adhīśvarāprasiddhimālakṣyāha—tattanmāsādhikṛtasūryeveti | vyahassyādvalavinyāse nirmāṇe tarkavṛndayoḥ | vibhāge nirvitarke ca iti kośāt ||27-28||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **śuka iti yugmakam | nanu, śruta-bhāgavata-tattvasya tava sūrya-gaṇa-śravaṇe ko’yam āgrahaḥ ? tatrāha—sūryasyātmā antaryāmī hariḥ, tasyaiva vyūham | tatraiva paryavasānād iti bhāvaḥ | iti gāyatry-upāsanā-tātparyaṁ[^72] vyañjitam ||27-28||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** hantānena śuka-parīkṣit-saṁvādam ayaṁ śrī-bhāgavata-śāstram asmabhyaṁ kathitaṁ tad-anantaram asmat-pūrva-puruṣasya mārkaṇḍeyasya caritaṁ tad-anuṣṭhita-bhagavat-pūjana-tattvaṁ cāsmat-praśnānurodhād uktam | idānīṁ yasya śrī-bhāgavatasya tad-viṣayasya svayaṁ bhagavataś ca dṛṣṭāntaḥ śrī-sūryaḥ—


    kṛṣṇe sva-dhāmopagate dharma-jñānādibhiḥ saha |


    kalau naṣṭa-dṛśām eṣa purāṇārko’dhunoditaḥ || [bhā.pu. 1.3.44] 

ity etad uktvā, kṛṣṇa-dyumaṇi nimloce [bhā.pu. 3.2.7] ity uddhavoktyā cāvagatas taṁ dvādaśātmakaṁ sakala-graha-rājam adhunā dvādaśa-skandhātmaka-purāṇa-rāja-samāpti-samaye prastāvayitum aham arhāmīti manasi parāmṛśyāha—śuka iti | pañcame yadāha—


    tathānye ca ṛṣayo gandharvā apsaraso nāgā grāmaṇyo yātudhānā devā ity ekaikaśo gaṇaḥ sapta [bhā.pu. 5.21.18] ity-ādinā | 

sauraḥ sūrya-saṁbandhī | adhīśvarair adhīśvareṇa parameśvareṇa ity arthaḥ | nanv alaṁ sūrya-viṣayakeṇa praśnena, tatrāha—sūryātmanaḥ sūrya-svarūpasya harer eva vyūhaṁ brūhi ||27-28||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.29 ||**

**sūta uvāca—**

**anādy-avidyayā viṣṇor ātmanaḥ sarva-dehinām |**

**nirmito loka-tantro’yaṁ lokeṣu parivartate ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tatra tāvat vyūhaṁ nirūpayituṁ prathamaṁ sūrya-svarūpam āha—anādy-avidyayā māyayā | ayaṁ sūryaḥ | loka-yātrā-pravartakaḥ ||29||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **anādyavidyayā māyākāryatvādavidyāyā api māyātvam | vidyāvidye mama tanū ityāramya māyayā me vinirmite ity-ukteḥ | lokaṁ tantrayati dhārayatīti tathā | nirmitaḥ pṛthaktvena prakāśitaḥ ||29||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **anādir avidyā yā, tayā māyayā viṣṇor eva sakāśān nirgato’yaṁ sūryaḥ ||29||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** sac-cid-ānanda-svarūpasya svayaṁ bhagavataḥ kṛṣṇasya śrī-bhāgavatasya ca dṛṣṭāntī-bhūto’yaṁ sūryaḥ prākṛto bhavituṁ nārhatīti mā maṁsthā ity āha—anādy-avidyayeti sarva-dehinām ātmano viṣṇor evāyaṁ nirmitaḥ viṣṇur naivāyaṁ sva-tejo-mūrtiḥ sūryo’nādy-avidyayā māyayā nirmitaḥ loka-tantraḥ loka-yātrā-pravartakaḥ ||29||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.30 ||**

**eka eva hi lokānāṁ sūrya ātmādi-kṛd dhariḥ |**

**sarva-veda-kriyā-mūlam ṛṣibhir bahudhoditaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **atas tasya kriyā-bhedopādhikam eva nānātvaṁ, na svata ity āha—eka eveti | sūrya ātmā jagatas tasthuṣaś ca [ṛ.ve. 1.115.7] iti śruteḥ | jagad-ātmā ādi-kṛt sṛṣṭi-kartā harir eva sūryaḥ, sa ca sarvāsāṁ vedokta-kriyāṇāṁ mūlaṁ saṁs tenopādhinā bahudhoktaḥ ||30||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **yataḥ sūryo vastuta eko harirūpatvādato hetostasya sūryasya kriyābhedo nānāvaidikakriyābhedastadupādhikam eva nānātvam | jagato jaṅgamasya tasthuṣaḥ sthāvarasyātmeti śrutipadārthaḥ | ajahalliṅgatvānmūlaśabdasya tatpuruṣasya paravalliṅgatvātklībatvam ||30||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **atas tad-ananyatva-nyāyena harir eva sūryaḥ | harer viśeṣaṇaṁ lokānām eka evātmā ity-ādi | ata eva sūryo’pi teṣām ātmādir ity arthaḥ ||30||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** eka eva lokānām ātmā hariḥ sūryo bahudhā dvādaśadhā uktaḥ ||30||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.31 ||**

**kālo deśaḥ kriyā kartā karaṇaṁ kāryam āgamaḥ |**

**dravyaṁ phalam iti brahman navadhokto’jayā hariḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kāla-rūpa-dhāriṇo harer dvādaśāditya-rūpaṁ bhedaṁ kriyopādhikaṁ darśayituṁ prathamaṁ sarva-karma-pravṛttaye māyā-kṛtaṁ navadhā bhedam āha—kāla iti | kālaḥ prātarādiḥ | deśaḥ samādiḥ | kriyā anuṣṭhānam | kartā brāhmaṇādiḥ | karaṇaṁ srug-ādiḥ | kāryaṁ yāgādi | āgamo mantrādiḥ | dravyaṁ vrīhy-ādi | phalaṁ svargādi ||31||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ādipadagrāhyān kramata āha—madhyāhnādi 1, śucyādi 2, kriyā anuṣṭhānam 3, kṣatriyādi 4, struvapraṇotādi 5, iṣṭisatrādi 6, brāhmaṇādi-kramādi 7, godhūmādi 8, cittaśudvyādīti 9 ||31||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **na kevalaṁ sūrya-rūpeṇa bahudhā karma-pravartanārthaṁ kālādi-rūpeṇāpi bahudhety āha—kāla iti | kālaḥ prātar-ādiḥ | deśaḥ vedikādiḥ | kriyā anuṣṭhānam | kartā brāhmaṇādiḥ | karaṇaṁ srug-ādiḥ | kāryaṁ yāgādi | āgamo mantrādiḥ | dravyaṁ vrīhy-ādi | phalaṁ svargādi ||31||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.32 ||**

**madhv-ādiṣu dvādaśasu bhagavān kāla-rūpa-dhṛk |**

**loka-tantrāya carati pṛthag dvādaśabhir gaṇaiḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tatra ca kāla-svarūpa-dhārī bhagavān pṛthak carati | madhv-ādiṣu caitrādiṣu | loka-tantrāya loka-yātrā-nirvāhāya ||32||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tatra navasu | bhagavānsūryaḥ ||32||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** kāla-rūpa-dhārī bhagavān eva sūrya-rūpaḥ san | loka-tantrāya loka-yātrā-nirvāhaṇāya ||32||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.33 ||**

**dhātā kṛtasthalī hetir vāsukī rathakṛn mune |**

**pulastyas tumburur iti madhu-māsaṁ nayanty amī ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tān eva gaṇān āha—dhāteti dvādaśabhiḥ | dhātā sūryaḥ | kṛta-sthalī apsarāḥ | hetī rākṣasaḥ | vāsukir nāgaḥ | rathakṛd yakṣaḥ | pulastya ṛṣiḥ | tumburur gandharvaḥ | madhu-māsaṁ caitram | nayanty anuvartayanti ||33||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **syāc caitre caitriko madhuḥ ity amaraḥ ||33||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** sauro gaṇo māsimāsīti yat pṛṣṭaṁ, tatra prathamaṁ caitra-māsasya saptakam āha—dhātā sūryaḥ | kṛta-sthalī apsarāḥ, hetiḥ rākṣasaḥ, vāsukir nāgaḥ, rathakṛt yakṣaḥ, pulastyaḥ ṛṣiḥ, tumburur gandharvaḥ ||33||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.34 ||**

**aryamā pulaho’thaujāḥ prahetiḥ puñjikasthalī |**

**nāradaḥ kacchanīraś ca nayanty ete sma mādhavam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **athaujā yakṣaḥ | prahetī rākṣasaḥ | nārado gandharvaḥ | kacchanīro nāgaḥ | mādhavaṁ vaiśākham ||34||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **vaiśākhe mādhavo rādhaḥ ity amaraḥ ||34||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **aryamā** **sūryaḥ | pulaha ṛṣiḥ | athaujā yakṣaḥ | prahetī rākṣasaḥ | puñjika-sthalī apsarāḥ | nārado gandharvaḥ | kacchanīro nāgaḥ | mādhavaṁ vaiśākham ||34||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.35 ||**

**mitro’triḥ pauruṣeyo’tha takṣako menakā hahāḥ |**

**rathasvana iti hy ete śukra-māsaṁ nayanty amī ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **mitraḥ sūryaḥ | pauruṣeyo rākṣasaḥ | rathasvano yakṣaḥ | śukra-māsaṁ jyeṣṭham ||35||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **jyeṣṭhe śukraḥ ity amaraḥ ||35||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **mitraḥ sūryaḥ | atrir muniḥ | pauruṣeyo rākṣasaḥ | takṣako nāgaḥ | menakā apsarāḥ | hāhā gandharvaḥ | rathasvano yakṣaḥ | śukra-māsaṁ jyeṣṭham ||35||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.36 ||**

**vasiṣṭho varuṇo rambhā sahajanyas tathā huhūḥ |**

**śukraś citrasvanaś caiva śuci-māsaṁ nayanty amī ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **varuṇaḥ sūryaḥ | sahajanyo yakṣaḥ | śukro nāgaḥ | citrasvano rākṣasaḥ | śuci-māsam āṣāḍham ||36||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **śucistvayam | āṣāḍhe ity amaraḥ ||36||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** vaśiṣṭho muniḥ | varuṇaḥ sūryaḥ | sahajanyo rākṣasaḥ | huhūr gandharvaḥ | śukro nāgaḥ | citrasvano yakṣaḥ | śuci-māsam āṣāḍham ||36||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.37 ||**

**indro viśvāvasuḥ śrotā elā-patras tathāṅgirāḥ |**

**pramlocā rākṣaso varyo nabho-māsaṁ nayanty amī ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **indraḥ sūryaḥ | viśvāvasur gandharvaḥ | śrotā yakṣaḥ | elāpatro nāgaḥ | varyo rākṣasa iti svayam eva vyākhyātam | nabho-māsaṁ śrāvaṇam ||37||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **śravaṇe tu syānnabhāḥ ity amaraḥ ||37||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **indraḥ sūryaḥ | viśvāvasur gandharvaḥ | śrotā yakṣaḥ | elāpatro nāgaḥ | aṅgirā muniḥ | pramlocā apsarāḥ | varyo rākṣasaḥ | iti svayam eva vyākhyātam | nabho-māsaṁ śrāvaṇam ||37||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.38 ||**

**vivasvān ugrasenaś ca vyāghra āsāraṇo bhṛguḥ |**

**anumlocā śaṅkhapālo nabhasyākhyaṁ nayanty amī ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **vivasvān sūryaḥ | ugraseno gandharvaḥ | vyāghro rākṣasaḥ | āsāraṇo yakṣaḥ | śaṅkhapālo nāgaḥ | nabhasyākhyaṁ bhādra-padam ||38||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **syurnabhasye prauṣṭhapadabhādrabhādrapadāḥ ||38||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **vivasvān sūryaḥ | ugraseno gandharvaḥ | vyāghro rākṣasaḥ | āsāraṇo yakṣaḥ | bhṛgur muniḥ | anumlocā apsarāḥ | śaṅkhapālo nāgaḥ | nabhasyākhyaṁ bhādra-padam ||38||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.39 ||**

**pūṣā dhanañjayo vātaḥ suṣeṇaḥ surucis tathā |**

**ghṛtācī gautamaś ceti tapo-māsaṁ nayanty amī ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **dhanañjayo nāgaḥ | vāto rākṣasaḥ | suṣeṇo gandharvaḥ | surucir yakṣaḥ | tapo-māsaṁ māgham | māsa-kramāti-laṅghranaṁ kaurmoktādityānukramānusāreṇa | vaiṣṇave tu māsa-krameṇoktiḥ | kvacin nāmavyatyayas tu kalpa-bhedeneti jñeyam ||39||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tadā  māghe ity amaraḥ ||39||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **pūṣā sūryaḥ | dhanañjayo nāgaḥ | vāto rākṣasaḥ | suṣeṇo gandharvaḥ | surucir yakṣaḥ | ghṛtācī apsarā | gautamo muniḥ | tapo-māsaṁ māghaḥ ||39||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.40 ||**

**ṛtur varcā bharadvājaḥ parjanyaḥ senajit tathā |**

**viśva airāvataś caiva tapasyākhyaṁ nayanty amī ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ṛtur yakṣaḥ | varcā rākṣasaḥ | parjanyaḥ sūryaḥ | senajid apsarāḥ | viśvo gandharvaḥ | airāvato nāgaḥ | tapasyākhyaṁ phālgunam ||40||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **syāttapasyaḥ phālgunikaḥ ity amaraḥ ||40||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **ṛtur yakṣaḥ | varcā rākṣasaḥ | bharadvājo muniḥ | parjanyaḥ sūryaḥ | śyenajid apsarāḥ | viśvo gandharvaḥ | airāvato nāgaḥ | tapasyākhyaṁ phālgunam ||40||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.41 ||**

**athāṁśuḥ kaśyapas tārkṣya ṛtasenas tathorvaśī |**

**vidyucchatrur mahāśaṅkhaḥ saho-māsaṁ nayanty amī ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** aṁśuḥ sūryaḥ | aṁśa iti vā pāṭhaḥ | tārkṣyo yakṣaḥ | ṛtaseno gandharvaḥ | vidyucchatrū rākṣasaḥ | mahāśaṅkho nāgaḥ | saho-māsaṁ mārga-śīrṣam ||41||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **mārgaśīrṣa sahā mārgaḥ ity amaraḥ ||41||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **aṁśuḥ sūryaḥ | aṁśa iti ca pāṭhaḥ | kaśyapo muniḥ | tārkṣyo yakṣaḥ | ṛtaseno gandharvaḥ | urvaśī aparāḥ | vidyucchatrū rākṣasaḥ | mahāśaṅkho nāgaḥ | saho-māsaṁ mārga-śīrṣam ||41||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.42 ||**

**bhagaḥ sphūrjo’riṣṭanemir ūrṇa āyuś ca pañcamaḥ |**

**karkoṭakaḥ pūrvacittiḥ puṣya-māsaṁ nayanty amī ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **bhagaḥ sūryaḥ | sphūrjo rākṣasaḥ | ariṣṭanemir gandharvaḥ | ūrṇo yakṣaḥ āyur ṛṣiḥ | karkoṭako nāgaḥ ||42||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **puṣyamāsaṁ puṣyanakṣatropalakṣitapūrṇimāyutamāsaṁ, pauṣamity arthaḥ ||42||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **bhagaḥ sūryaḥ | sphūrjo rākṣasaḥ | ariṣṭanemir gandharvaḥ | ūrṇo yakṣaḥ | karkoṭako nāgaḥ | pūrvacittir apsarāḥ | puṣyaṁ pauṣam ||42||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.43 ||**

**tvaṣṭā ṛcīka-tanayaḥ kambalaś ca tilottamā |**

**brahmāpeto’tha śatajid dhṛtarāṣṭra iṣam-bharāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tvaṣṭā sūryaḥ | ṛcīka-tanayo jamadagniḥ | kambalo nāgaḥ | brahmāpeto rākṣasaḥ | śatajid yakṣaḥ | dhṛtarāṣṭro gandharvaḥ | iṣam-bharā āśvina-pālakāḥ ||43||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **syādāśvina iṣo'pyāśvayujo'pi ity amaraḥ ||43||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **tvaṣṭā sūryaḥ | ṛcīka-tanayo jamadagnir muniḥ | kambalāśvo nāgaḥ | tilottamā apsarāḥ | brahmāpeto rākṣasaḥ | śatajid yakṣaḥ | dhṛtarāṣṭro gandharvaḥ | iṣam-bharā ete āśvina-pālakāḥ ||43||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.44 ||**

**viṣṇur aśvataro rambhā sūryavarcāś ca satyajit |**

**viśvāmitro makhāpeta ūrja-māsaṁ nayanty amī ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **viṣṇur ādityaḥ | aśvataro nāgaḥ | sūryavarcā gandharvaḥ | satyajid yakṣaḥ | makhāpeto rākṣasaḥ | ūrja-māsaṁ kārtika-māsam | ete cādity-ādayaḥ kaurme vibhajyoktāḥ, 


    dhātāryamā ca mitraś ca varūṇaś cendra eva ca | 


    vivasvān atha pūṣā ca parjanyaś cāṁśur eva ca | 


    bhagas tvaṣṭā ca viṣṇuś ca ādityā dvādaśa smṛtāḥ | 


    pulastyaḥ pulahaś cātrir vasiṣṭho’thāṅgirā bhṛguḥ | 


    gautamo’tha bharadvājaḥ kaśyapaḥ kratur eva ca | 


    jamadagniḥ kauśikaś ca munayo brahma-vādinaḥ | 


    rathakūrco’riṣṭanemir grāmaṇīś ca rathasvanaḥ | 


    ratha-citrasvanaḥ śrotā aruṇaḥ senajit tathā | 


    tārkṣyaś cāriṣṭanemiś ca ṛtajit satyajit tathā || ete yakṣāḥ | 


    atha hetiḥ prahetiś ca pauruṣeyo vadhas tathā | 


    varyo vyāghras tathāyaś ca vāyur vidyud divākaraḥ | 


    brahmāpetaś ca viprendrā yajñāpetaś ca rākṣasaḥ | 


    vāsukiḥ kacchanīraś ca takṣakaḥ sarpa-puṅgavaḥ | 


    elāpatraḥ śaṅkhapālas tathairāvata-saṁjñitaḥ | 


    dhanañjayo mahāpadmas tathā karkoṭako dvijāḥ | 


    kambalo’śvataraś caiva vahanty enaṁ yathā-kramam | 


    tumburur nārado hāhā hūhūr viśvāvasus tathā | 


    ugraseno vasurucir viśvāvasur athāparaḥ | 


    citrasenas tathorṇāyur dhṛtarāṣṭro dvijottamāḥ | 


    sūryavarcā dvādaśeti gandharvā gāyatāṁ varāḥ | 


    kṛtasthaly apsaro-varyā tathānyā puñjikasthalī | 


    menakā sahajanyā ca pramlocā ca dvijottamāḥ | 


    anumlocā ghṛtācī ca viśvācī corvaśī tathā | 


    anyā ca pūrvacittiḥ syād anyā caiva tilottamā | 


    sambhā ceti dvija-śreṣṭhās tathaivāpsarasaḥ smṛtāḥ || iti ||44||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **bāhulorjau kārttikikaḥ ity amaraḥ | iha māsavyutkramo hi kaurmoktasūyarṣiyajñādikramāpekṣayaiva jñeyaḥ ||44||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **viṣṇuḥ sūryaḥ | aśvataro nāgaḥ | rambhā apsarāḥ | sūryavarcā gandharvaḥ | satyajid yakṣaḥ | makhāpeto rākṣasaḥ | ūrja-māsaṁ kārtikam ||44||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.45 ||**

**etā bhagavato viṣṇor ādityasya vibhūtayaḥ |**

**smaratāṁ sandhyayor nṝṇāṁ haranty aṁho dine dine ||**

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ādityasyādityarūpasya viṣṇoḥ | ahaṁ pāpam ||45||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.46 ||**

**dvādaśasv api māseṣu devo’sau ṣaḍbhir asya vai |**

**caran samantāt tanute paratreha ca san-matim ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **eteṣāṁ pṛthak karmāṇi nirūpayati—dvādaśasv apīti tribhiḥ | asau devaḥ sūryaḥ ṣaḍbhir gandharvādibhir asya janasya samantāc caran śubhāṁ matiṁ tanute | gāyatry-artho’nena sūcitaḥ ||46||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **asau devaḥ sūryaḥ | ṣaḍbhir gandharvādibhiḥ sva-vibhūtibhiḥ ||46||

 **...**

**|| 12.11.47 ||**

**sāmarg-yajurbhis tal-liṅgair ṛṣayaḥ saṁstuvanty amum |**

**gandharvās taṁ pragāyanti nṛtyanty apsaraso’grataḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tal-liṅgaiḥ sūrya-prakāśakaiḥ ||47||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **samantātsaptasu dvīpeṣu | iha sanmatitananaṁ tu sūryodaye caurajārādayo'pi svakarma tyajati sādhava iva tiṣṭhantīti prasiddham eva | paratra paralokanimittaṁ sanmatitananam api sūryādeva, sūryodaya eva śrautasmārtapāralaukikakarmapravṛtteḥ prāyo darśanāt | iha paratreti saptamyau nimitterthe evātra jñeye | tad uktam—yasyodayenehajagatprabudhyate pravartate cākhilakarmasiddhaye iti bhaviṣyottare paratreha ca sanmatitananoktyā dhiyaḥ prerakatārūpo gāyatryartho'tra dhvanitas tathā ca gāyatryā samāptirasūcīti jñeyam ||46-47||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **eteṣāṁ pṛthak karmāṇi nirūpayati sāmeti | tal-liṅgaiḥ sūrya-prakāśakaiḥ ||47|| 

 **...**

**|| 12.11.48 ||**

**unnahyanti rathaṁ nāgā grāmaṇyo ratha-yojakāḥ |**

**codayanti rathaṁ pṛṣṭhe nairṛtā bala-śālinaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **unnahyanti dṛḍhaṁ badhnanti | grāmaṇyo yakṣāḥ | nairṛtā rākṣasāḥ ||48||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **grāmaṇīḥ pradhāne'dhipatau yakṣanāpitayor api iti kośāt | nairṛto yāturakṣasī ity amaraḥ ||48||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **unnahyanti dṛḍhaṁ badhnanti | grāmaṇyo yakṣāḥ rathaṁ yojayanti | codayanti balena nodanaiś cālayanti nairṛtā rākṣasāḥ ||48||

 **...**

|| **12.11**.**49 ||**

**vālakhilyāḥ sahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭir brahmarṣayo’malāḥ |**

**purato’bhimukhaṁ yānti stuvanti stutibhir vibhum ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kiṁ ca, vālakhilyā iti | evaṁ pratimāsaṁ ta eva stuvanti vibhuṁ sūryam ||49||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **stāvakarṣiṣu punarādhikyam āha—kiñceti | stutibhiḥ stutiprakāśakaiḥ udutyaṁ jātavedasam ity-ādimantraiḥ | viśeṣeṇa bhāti bhāpayati veti vibhustam ||49||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.11.50 ||**

**evaṁ hy anādi-nidhano bhagavān harir īśvaraḥ |**

**kalpe kalpe svam ātmānaṁ vyūhya lokān avaty ajaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **vyūhya vibhajya ||50||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **kalpekalpe pratikalpaṁ harir eva svamātmānamādityarūpeṇa dvādaśadhā vibhajya lokānavati duḥkhajālādrakṣatīty arthaḥ ||50||

iti śrīmad-bhāgavata-bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśe dvādaśa-skandhe ekādaśo'dhyāyaḥ ||11||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

iti sārārtha-darśinyāṁ harṣiṇyāṁ bhakta-cetasām |

ekādaśo dvādaśe’tra saṅgataḥ saṅgataḥ satām ||*||

 **...**


    iti śrīmad-bhāgavate mahā-purāṇe brahma-sūtra-bhāṣye pāramahaṁsyaṁ saṁhitāyāṁ vaiyāsikyāṁ dvādaśa-skandhe 


    āditya-vyūha-vivaraṇaṁ nāma 


    ekādaśo’dhyāyaḥ |

|| 12.11 ||

…

(12.12)


### dvādaśo’dhyāyaḥ


## skandhārtha-nirūpaṇaṁ

**|| 12.12.1 ||**

**sūta uvāca—**

**namo dharmāya mahate namaḥ kṛṣṇāya vedhase |**

**brahmaṇebhyo namaskṛtya dharmān vakṣye sanātanān ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :**

dvādaśe tu purāṇokta-sarvārthānukramaḥ kṛtaḥ |

prathama-skandham ārabhya prādhānyena samāsataḥ ||

tad evam asmin purāṇe vistareṇoktān arthān saṅkṣepato varṇayiṣyan dharmādīn praṇamati, nama iti. mahate hari-bhakti-lakṣaṇāya. brāhmaṇebhyo brāhmaṇān. sanātanān anādīn. dharmān ity upalakṣaṇaṁ purāṇoktārthānām ||1||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** kṛṣṇāya tad-ākhyayātiprasiddhāya svayaṁ bhagavate | vedhase avatārādi-sarva-vidhātre | tatra sva-dainyena vinayaḥ brāhmaṇebhyo namaskṛtyeti | sanātanān, kālena naṣṭā pralaye vāṇīyaṁ [bhā.pu. 11.14.3] ity-ādi-pramāṇena prasiddhān, dharmān bhāgavatān vakṣya iti tat-tat-prasaṅgānukrameṇa tān eva sūcayiṣyāmi—patitaḥ skhalitaḥ [bhā.pu. 12.12.47] ity-ādinā ca sākṣād vakṣyāmīty arthaḥ ||1||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **anukramo gaṇanā | samāsataḥ saṅkṣepataḥ, saṅkṣepakathane'pi prādhānyena mukhyārthasyaiva kathanaṁ natu sarvata ity arthaḥ dharmasyava haripriyatvena saṁsāratārakatvādādau namati—nama iti | haripriyatvaṁ dharmasya yadāyadā hi dharmasya iti śrīgītāvākyādavasīyate | dharmāntaravyāvṛttaye—mahata iti | mahattvam api hari-bhaktilakṣaṇadharmasya duktyaivāvasīyate| tathā hi—sarvadharmānparityajya mām ekaṁ śaraṇaṁ vraja iti | brāhmaṇebhya iti dvitīyārthe caturthī | sanātanāñchrīmadvyāsakathanād api prāktanānnatu vyāsapraṇītāṁs tathā ca vedavatsanātanatvamasya purāṇasya śrīsūtena dhvanitam | vedhase'vatārādisarvavidhātre | svadainyaṁ jñāpayannamati—brāhmaṇebhyo vyāsādibhyastatprakāśakebhyaḥ | sanātanam kālena pralaye naṣṭā vāṇīyam ity-ādipramāṇena prasiddhān dharmān bhāgavatānvakṣye tattatprasaṅgānukrameṇa tāneva sūcayiṣyāmi patitaḥ skhalitaḥ ity-ādinā ca sākṣādvakṣyāmīty arthaḥ | śravaṇakīrtanādiviṣayatve sati tac caritānyeva paramasanātanadharmā bhavantīti bhāvaḥ | yad vā, bhagavato bhaktiyogasya tac caritānāṁ ca nirguṇatvātsanātanatvameva, saguṇasyaiva vastunaḥ sanātanatvābhāvād ity arthaḥ ||1||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :**

prathamāditaḥ ārabhyopākhyāna-vitateḥ punaḥ |

anukramaḥ prasiddhāyāṁ dvādaśe kriyate sphuṭam ||

mahate bhakti-lakṣaṇāya kṛṣṇāya tat-prāpyāya, vedhase sarva-kāraṇāya, brāhmaṇebhyo vyāsādibhyas tat-prakāśakebhyo dvitīyārthe caturthī | dharmān bhagavac-caritrāṇi śravaṇa-kīrtanādir viṣayatve sati bhagavac-caritāny eva parama-dharmā bhavantīti bhāvaḥ | sanātanān nityān | bhagavato bhakti-yogasya ca tac-caritānāṁ ca nirguṇatvād iti bhāvaḥ ||1||

 **...**

**|| 12.12.2 ||**

**etad vaḥ kathitaṁ viprā viṣṇoś caritam adbhutam |**

**bhavadbhir yad ahaṁ pṛṣṭo narāṇāṁ puruṣocitam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **puruṣatve ucitaṁ śravaṇādi-yogyam ||2||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **yadbhavadbhirnarāṇāṁ sambandhi puṁsām ekāntataḥ śreyastannaśśaṁsitumarhasi ityahaṁ pṛṣṭastadetadvo viṣṇoradbhūtacaritaṁ mayā kathitam iti sambandhaḥ | he viprā iti—vigataḥ prāpūrayitā svīyabodhena yeṣāṁ te viprāḥ sarvajñā iti | sarvajñānāmagre mayā yathāśrutam evoktam iti bhāvaḥ | tatra bhagavaccaritaśravaṇam eva mukhyamityabhipretyopasaṁharannanukramitumupakramate—narāṇāṁ madhye ye puruṣāsteṣāmevocitaṁ na tu tadvimukhānāṁ paśūnām iti teṣāṁ gālipradānam | tad uktam— 


    śvaviḍvarāhoṣṭrakharaiḥ saṁstutaḥ puruṣaḥ paśuḥ | 


    na yatkarṇapathopeto jātu nāma gadāgrajaḥ || iti | 

yad vā, narāṇāṁ puruṣe bhagavati yaducitam ||2||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) :** tatraiva bhagavac-carita-śravaṇam eva mukhyam ity abhiprāyeṇa tenaiva mahā-prasaṅgam upasaṁharan tān anukramitum upakramate—etad iti | narāṇāṁ madhye ye puruṣās teṣām evocitaṁ, na tu ye teṣāṁ madhye paśavas teṣām ity artha iti tad-bahir-mukhebhyo gāli-pradānaṁ, yathoktam, śva-viḍ-varāhoṣṭra-kharaiḥ [bhā.pu. 2.3.19] ity-ādi | yad vā, narāṇāṁ jīvānāṁ puruṣe śrī-bhagavati yad ucitam ||2||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** narāṇāṁ madhye ye puruṣās teṣām ucitaṁ, na tu narāṇāṁ madhye ye paśavas teṣām iti | yad uktaṁ, śva-viḍ-varāhoṣṭra-kharaiḥ saṁstutaḥ puruṣaḥ paśuḥ [bhā.pu. 2.3.19] iti ||2||

**...**

**|| 12.12.3 ||**

**atra saṅkīrtitaḥ sākṣāt sarva-pāpa-haro hariḥ |**

**nārāyaṇo hṛṣīkeśo bhagavān sātvatāṁ patiḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **etat prapañcayati—atreti | bhagavān aiśvaryādi-ṣaḍ-guṇaḥ | sākṣāt saṅkīrtita iti devatā-kāṇḍārthaḥ ||3||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **etatpuruṣasya śravaṇādiyogyametad ity arthaḥ | atra śrī-bhāgavate | sākṣāddhariḥ śrī-kṛṣṇaḥ ete cāṁśakalāḥ puṁsaḥ kṛṣṇas tu bhagavānsvayam ity-ukteḥ | sarvapāpahara ity-ādiviśeṣaṇānāṁ tatraiva sāmañjasyāt | atra dvādaśa-skandheṣu harirbhagavad-ādyākhyayānantāvirbhāvaḥ parameśvarastāvanmukhyatvena kīrtyate | tatrāpi guṇarūpalīlātvena mukhyatvena kortyate | tasya ca prādhānyena bhedadvayaṁ darśitamityāha—nārāyaṇaḥ sarvajīvāśrayaḥ | hṛṣīkeśastadīyasarvendriyapravartakaś ca paramātmetyartha ityeko bhedaḥ | dvitīyam āha—bhagavāniti | sa eva kaḥ—sātvatāmuddhavādīnāṁ patiḥ svayaṁ bhagavānity arthaḥ ||3||

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** atra śrī-bhāgavate sātvatāṁ patiḥ śrī-kṛṣṇaḥ saṅkīrtyate, sa eva bhagavān | hary-ādīny api tan-nāmāni ||3||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **atra śrī-bhāgavate harir bhagavad-ādy-ākhyayānantāvirbhāvaḥ parameśvaras tāvan-mukhyatvena kīrtyate, tatrāpi guṇa-rūpa-līlābhiḥ sākṣād eva kīrtyate | tasya ca prādhānyena bheda-dvayaṁ darśitam ity āha—nārāyaṇaḥ sarva-jīvāśrayaḥ hṛṣīkeśas tadīya sarvendriya-pravartakaś ca paramātmety arthaḥ | ity eko bhedaḥ | dvitīyam āha—bhagavān iti | sa ca sātvatāṁ patiḥ svayaṁ bhagavān śrī-yādavendra-rūpatvena kīrtyata ity arthaḥ ||3||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** yaḥ sarva-pāpa-hartṛtvena hari-śabdenocyate yaś ca nārasya jīva-samūhasya āśramatvena nārāyaṇa-śabdenocyate | yaś ca sarvendriyāṇāṁ pravartakatvena hṛṣīkeśa-śabdenocyate sa eva bhagavān atra dvādaśasv api skandheṣu kīrtyate | sa hi ka ity ata āha—sātvatām uddhavādīnāṁ patiḥ ||3||

 **...**

**|| 12.12.4 ||**

**atra brahma paraṁ guhyaṁ jagataḥ prabhavāpyayam |**

**jñānaṁ ca tad-upākhyānaṁ proktaṁ vijñāna-saṁyutam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :**brahma-kāṇḍārtham āha—atra brahmeti | guhyaṁ nirguṇam | prabhavāpyayam, prabhavaty asmād iti prabhavam, apyety asminn ity apyayam, tac ca tac ca | anenāśraya-śabdārtho darśitaḥ | vijñāna-saṁyutam aparokṣa-jñāna-paryantaṁ jñānam | tad-upākhyānaṁ taj-jñānam upākhyāyate prakāśyate yena taj-jñāna-sādhanam ity arthaḥ ||4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **saguṇamuktvā nirguṇam āha—brahmeti | ity artha iti—śravaṇādisādhanamantareṇa jñānānutpattes tadapyuktam iti bhāvaḥ | tadīyanirviśeṣaprakāśarūpaṁ yadbrahma tadapi proktaṁ vāgādyagrāhyatvādguhyam | tahi kathaṁ svayaṁ proktaṁ tatrāha—jagata utpattilayau yatas tadityevaṁrītyoktaṁ na tu sākṣād ity arthaḥ ||4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** atra brahmety-ādi | atra śrī-bhāgavate brahma-paraṁ guhyaṁ viśvasya prabhavāpyayaṁ jñānaṁ ca vijñāna-saṁyutaṁ yat proktaṁ, tat-tad-upākhyānaṁ śrī-kṛṣṇopākhyānam | upa ākhyāyate iti karmaṇi yuṭ, hīne upaś ca kathyate iti upa-śabdo’tra hīnārthaḥ | upārjunaṁ yoddhāraḥ itivat | tat tataḥ kṛṣṇākhyānād dhīnam ity arthaḥ | tad ity avyayaṁ tad upa taṁ śrī-kṛṣṇam upa, tato hīnam ity arthaḥ | ākhyānaṁ—ākhyāyate kathyate kathā-prasaṅgāt nirdiśyate ity ākhyānaṁ, tat sarvaṁ brahmādi kathanīyam iti kathitam | vastutaḥ śrī-kṛṣṇa eva pratipādyaḥ, vedyaṁ vāstavam atra vastu [bhā.pu. 1.1.2] ity upakrānteḥ, tasya sarveśvareśvaratvāt | yad vā, ākhyāyate yata ity ākhyānaḥ śrī-kṛṣṇaḥ, tad brahmādi sarvam upākhyānaṁ śrī-kṛṣṇaād dhīnam iti ||4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **atra brahmeti sārdhakam | atra bhagavat-tattva-kīrtana eva tadīya-nirviśeṣa-prakāśa-rūpaṁ yad brahma yad eva jagaj-janmādinā sāmānyato lakṣitaṁ tad api proktam ||4||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** tadīya-nirviśeṣa-prakāśa-rūpaṁ yad brahma, tad api proktaṁ, vāg-ādīndriya-grāhyatvābhāvād guhyaṁ tarhi kathaṁ proktaṁ, tatrāha jagataḥ prabhava utpattir apyayo layaś ca yatas tad ity etat-prakāreṇaiva proktaṁ, na tu sākṣāt proktam iti bhāvaḥ | tat-prāpti-sādhanaṁ jñānaṁ ca tad upākhyāyate prakāśyate yena taj jñāna-sādhanaṁ ca vijñānam aparokṣānubhavas tat-sahitaṁ ca ||4|| 

 **...**

**|| 12.12.5 ||**

**bhakti-yogaḥ samākhyāto vairāgyaṁ ca tad-āśrayam |**

**pārīkṣitam upākhyānaṁ nāradākhyānam eva ca ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **karma-kāṇḍārtham āha, bhakti-yogaś ca sādhya-sādhana-rūpaḥ | tad-āśrayaṁ bhakti-yogena niṣpāditam | evaṁ sāmānyato nirūpyedānīṁ dvādaśa-skandha-prakaraṇārthān anukrāmati | pārīkṣitam upākhyānaṁ parīkṣij-janmādi, tat-prastāvāya nāradākhyānaṁ ca ||5||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tatprastāvāya parīkṣijjanmādiprasaṅgāya prathamaskandhata upakramate—pārīkṣitam iti | ihānukramaṇikādhyāye | yatprasiddham api kiñcitkicidullaṅghayate tannāniṣṭam iti | anukramaṇikā hi noktasamastārthavyāpinī bhavet yatprathamata eva janmaguhyādhyāyakathātiprasiddhāpyullaṅghitā | tathā drauṇidaṇḍabhīṣmaniryāṇādikathācitraketutripuravadhāmbarīṣādikathāghāsurabrahmamohādikathā ca bahuśa ullaṅghya kvacitkrameṇātyukteti ||5||

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** atra bhakti-yoga eva mukhyatvenākhyāyate, tad-upāyatvena vairāgyaṁ ca | tad-āśrayaṁ bhakty-āśrayam ||5||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tad-artham eva jñāna-vijñāna-bhakti-yogāḥ yathottarotkarṣa-sopānavat krameṇa samākhyātās tad-āśrayaṁ tad-upayogi-vairāgyaṁ ceti padya-dvayena veda-tātparya-rūpo brahma-kāṇḍārtho darśitaḥ | tad evaṁ sārvatrikaṁ pratipādyam uktvā kramoktam āha—pārīkṣitam iti ||5||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **bhakti-yogaḥ sādhana-rūpaḥ sādhya-rūpaś ca samya-guṇa-kramopasaṁhārābhyāsair ākhyātaḥ | tad-āśrayaṁ tad-uttham | atha prathama-skandhata eva prākaraṇikānarthān anukrāmyati | pārīkṣitam iti atrānukramaṇikādhyāye yat prasiddham api kiñcit kiñcid upākhyānam ullaṅghitam | nātrāniṣṭam āśaṅkanīyam anukramaṇikā hi nokta-samastārtha-vyāpinī bhavet, yat prathamata eva janma-guhyādhyāya-kathā atiprasiddhāpy ullaṅghitā | evaṁ drauṇi-daṇḍa-bhīṣma-niryāṇādi-kathā citraketu-tripura-vadhādi-kathā ambarīṣādi-kathā aghāsura-vadha-brahma-mohanādi-kathā bahuśa evollaṅghitā | kvacid vyutkrameṇāpy ukta iti ||5-7||

 **...**

**|| 12.12.6 ||**

**prāyopaveśo rājarṣer vipra-śāpāt parīkṣitaḥ |**

**śukasya brahmarṣabhasya saṁvādaś ca parīkṣitaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **brahma-rṣabhasya brāhmaṇottamasya | iti prathama-skandhārthaḥ ||6||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **vipraśāpācchṛṅgiśāpāt | brahmasu brāhmaṇeṣu ṛṣiṣu uttamo brahmarṣistasya— vedāsye bṛhati vipre brahma vede parātmani | tapoyajñapradhāneṣu iti kośāt | ṛṣiḥ śreṣṭhe ca sarvajñe brāhmaṇe ca manau tathā iti ||6||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.12.7 ||**

**yoga-dhāraṇayotkrāntiḥ saṁvādo nāradājayoḥ |**

**avatārānugītaṁ ca sargaḥ prādhāniko’grataḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **utkrāntir arcir ādi-gatiḥ | prādhaṇikaḥ pradhāna-kārya-virāḍ-rūpaḥ sargaḥ | agrata ādito mahad-ādi-krameṇety arthaḥ | iti dvitīyārthaḥ ||7||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.12.8 ||**

**viduroddhava-saṁvādaḥ kṣattṛ-maitreyayos tataḥ |**

**purāṇa-saṁhitā-praśno mahā-puruṣa-saṁsthitiḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **mahā-puruṣasya saṁsthitiḥ pralaye tūṣṇīm avasthānam ||8||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **acirādigatiḥ te'rcirabhisambhavanti iti śrutyuktagatiḥ ||7-8||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** mahā-puruṣe padmanābhe saṁsthitiḥ pralaye brahmaṇas tad-udare śayanam ||8||

 **...**

**|| 12.12.9 ||**

**tataḥ prākṛtikaḥ sargaḥ sapta-vaikṛtikāś ca ye |**

**tato brahmāṇḍa-sambhūtir vairājaḥ puruṣo yataḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **prākṛtikaḥ prakṛti-bhavo guṇa-kṣobha-rūpaḥ | vaikṛtikā mahad-ādayaś ca-kārād vikārāś ca ye teṣāṁ sargaḥ ||9||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **yato yatra brahmāṇḍe vairājo virāḍantaryāmī puruṣo'stīti ||9||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.12.10 ||**

**kālasya sthūla-sūkṣmasya gatiḥ padma-samudbhavaḥ |**

**bhuva uddharaṇe’mbhodher hiraṇyākṣa-vadho yathā ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **gatiḥ svarūpam | uddharaṇe uddhāraṇe ||10||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **uddhāraṇe nimitte yathā hiraṇyākṣavadhaḥ kṛtas tathokta ity arthaḥ ||10||

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** bhuva uddharaṇam ambhodheḥ sakāśāt ma-kāra-lopaś chāndasaḥ ||10||

 **...**

**|| 12.12.11 ||**

**ūrdhva-tiryag-avāk-sargo rudra-sargas tathaiva ca |**

**ardha-nārīśvarasyātha yataḥ svāyambhuvo manuḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ardhābhyāṁ nārī ca naraś ca tasya sargaḥ ||11||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ūrdhvasargo devasargaḥ, tiryaksargaḥ paśvādisargaḥ, avāksargo'dhaḥsargā'surādilakṣaṇaḥ | yad vā, ūrdhvasarga ūrdhvasañcārasargaḥ vṛkṣādisargaḥ | tiryaksargo'ṣṭāviṁśatidhā | avāksargaḥ nṛsargaḥ avāksrotās tu navamaḥ kṣattarekavidho nṛṇām ity-ukteḥ | nārīnarayoḥ samāhāradvandve tasya tṛtoyādvivacanāntārddhaśabdena punassamāsaḥ | tathā hi—arddhābhyāṁ nārīnaraṁ yasya tasya brahmaṇaḥ sakāśādatha sargo'bhūt | yato yatra sarge svāyaṁbhuvo manuḥ śatarūpā cābhūt ||11||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.12.12 ||**

**śatarūpā ca yā strīṇām ādyā prakṛtir uttamā |**

**santāno dharma-patnīnāṁ kardamasya prajāpateḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **santāno dharma-patnīnām iti nava-brahma-samutpattir ity asyānantaraṁ draṣṭavyam ||12||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.12.13 ||**

**avatāro bhagavataḥ kapilasya mahātmanaḥ |**

**devahūtyāś ca saṁvādaḥ kapilena ca dhī-matā ||**

**śrīdharaḥ, jīva-gosvāmī (kṛṣṇa-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** ardhābhyāṁ nārī ca naraś ca tasya ||13||

 **...**

**|| 12.12.14 ||**

**nava-brahma-samutpattir dakṣa-yajña-vināśanam |**

**dhruvasya caritaṁ paścāt pṛthoḥ prācīnabarhiṣaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **iti tṛtīyārthaḥ | caturtha-skandhārtham āha—nava-brahmaṇāṁ marīcy-ādīnāṁ samutpattiḥ santānaḥ ||14||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **yā strīṇāmādyā prakṛtirmūlakāraṇaṁ, tata eva strīsargapravṛtteḥ| dharmapatnīnāṁ kīrtyādīnām, kardamasya ca yathā santānas tathā varṇitaḥ ||12-14||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._ **

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **nava-brahmabhyaḥ marīcy-ādibhyaḥ samutpattiḥ sudyumnasyety atra upākhyānam iti śeṣaḥ ||14||

 **...**

**|| 12.12.15 ||**

**nāradasya ca saṁvādas tataḥ praiyavrataṁ dvijāḥ |**

**nābhes tato’nucaritam ṛṣabhasya bharatasya ca ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **pañcama-skandhārtham āha—tataḥ praiyavrataṁ priyavratasya caritam ||15||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **he dvija iti—dvijatvātkathitam api punaḥ smārayāmīti bhāvaḥ ||15||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.12.16 ||**

**dvīpa-varṣa-samudrāṇāṁ giri-nady-upavarṇanam |**

**jyotiś-cakrasya saṁsthānaṁ pātāla-naraka-sthitiḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **dvīpādy-upavarṇanaṁ prathamaṁ saṅkṣepatas tato dvīpādīnāṁ ye girayo nadyaś ca teṣām upavarṇanam | pātālānāṁ narakāṇāṁ ca saṁsthitiḥ | anenaiva naraka-nivartakam ajāmilopākhyānaṁ gṛhītaṁ tataḥ parācīnam ||16||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **anena narakasthitivarṇanaprasaṅgena ||16||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.12.17 ||**

**dakṣa-janma pracetobhyas tat-putrīṇāṁ ca santatiḥ |**

**yato devāsura-narās tiryaṅ-naga-khagādayaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ṣaṣṭhārtham āha—dakṣa-janmeti ||7||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tatputrīṇāṁ dakṣaputrīṇām | yato yatra santanyāṁ devādayo jātāḥ ||17||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.12.18 ||**

**tvāṣṭrasya janma-nidhanaṁ putrayoś ca diter dvijāḥ |**

**daityeśvarasya caritaṁ prahrādasya mahātmanaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **saptamārtham āha—putrayoś ceti ||18||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tvāṣṭrasya vṛtrasya | diteḥ putrayoḥ | saṁbuddhis tu pūrvavat ||18||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.12.19 ||**

**manv-antarānukathanaṁ gajendrasya vimokṣaṇam |**

**manv-antarāvatārāś ca viṣṇor hayaśirādayaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **aṣṭamārtham āha—manvantarānukathanam iti | kvacit kasyācid anuktir vyutkramoktiś ca bhakti-rasākulatveneti draṣṭavyam ||19||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ādinājitādigrahaḥ | atrāvatārakramo na vivakṣito varṇitacaritakathane tātparyāt | ata eva svāmicaraṇair apy uktam—kvacitkasyacidanuktirity-ādi | bhakti samagnatvācchrīsūtasya yathākramakathanavismṛtirabhūd iti bhāvaḥ ||19||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.12.20 ||**

**kaurmaṁ mātsyaṁ nārasiṁhaṁ vāmanaṁ ca jagat-pateḥ |**

**kṣīroda-mathanaṁ tadvad amṛtārthe divaukasām ||**

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **divaukasāmamṛtārthe'mṛtanimittaṁ tadvatkathitamity arthaḥ ||20||

 **...**

**|| 12.12.21 ||**

**devāsura-mahā-yuddhaṁ rāja-vaṁśānukīrtanam |**

**ikṣvāku-janma tad-vaṁśaḥ sudyumnasya mahātmanaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **navamārtham āha—rāja-vaṁśeti ||21||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **sudyamnasya vaṁśaś ca kīrtitaḥ | atra tad iti padaṁ bhinnaṁ jñeyaṁ ṣaṣṭhyarthe, vaṁśa ityubhayatrānveti | maha utsavastaṁ karotīti mahakarastādṛśa ātmā deho yasya sa mahātmā, tasminpūrvaṁ putrīrūpeṇa jāte manormaho na jātāḥ, punargurukṛpayā tasyāḥ puruṣatve satyatīvotsavo'bhūdityata uktaṁ—mahātmana iti | atra madhyamapadalopī samāso jñeyaḥ ||21||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.12.22-24 ||**

**ilopākhyānam atroktaṁ tāropākhyānam eva ca |**

**sūrya-vaṁśānukathanaṁ śaśādādyā nṛgādayaḥ ||**

**saukanyaṁ cātha śaryāteḥ kakutsthasya ca dhīmataḥ |**

**khaṭvāṅgasya ca māndhātuḥ saubhareḥ sagarasya ca ||**

**rāmasya kośalendrasya caritaṁ kilbiṣāpaham |**

**nimer aṅga-parityāgo janakānāṁ ca sambhavaḥ ||**

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **atraiva sudyumnaprakṛte | sarvaṁ vākyaṁ sāvadhāraṇam iti nyāyenaivakāro'tra bodhyaḥ | ādinā yaiḥ kavyādibhī rājyaṁ na gṛhītaṁ te'pi kathitā iti kaviḥ kanīyānviṣayeṣu niḥspṛho visṛjya rājyam ity-ukteḥ || sukanyāyā idaṁ saukanyaṁ, caritam iti śeṣaḥ || kośalā'yodhyā deśo vā kośalaḥ ||22-24||

 **...**

**|| 12.12.25 ||**

**rāmasya bhārgavendrasya niḥkṣatrī-karaṇaṁ bhuvaḥ |**

**ailasya soma-vaṁśasya yayāter nahuṣasya ca ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **soma-vaṁśādi-bhūtasyailasya caritam ||25||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.12.26 ||**

**dauṣmanter bharatasyāpi śāntanos tat-sutasya ca |**

**yayāter jyeṣṭha-putrasya yador vaṁśo’nukīrtitaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tat-sutasya bhīṣmasya ||26||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **bhārgavaṁ bhṛguvaṁśamindayati samarddhayatīti bhārgavendrastasya sakāśādbhuyo niḥkṣatrakaraṇaṁ yathāsīttathā varṇitam ||25-26||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.12.27 ||**

**yatrāvatīrṇo bhagavān kṛṣṇākhyo jagad-īśvaraḥ |**

**vasudeva-gṛhe janma tato vṛddhiś ca gokule ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā),** **viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **yatra yaduvaṁśe | tato janmānantaram ||27||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tasya vṛddhiś ca gokula iti cakārāj janma cety arthaḥ | anyathā vṛddhis tv ity evoktaṁ syāt | asya sthāpanaṁ—nandas tv ātmaja utpannaḥ [bhā.pu. 10.5.1] ity ādau kṛṣṇa-sandarbhe (147-153) kṛtam eva ||27||

 **...**

**|| 12.12.28 ||**

**tasya karmāṇy apārāṇi kīrtitāny asura-dviṣaḥ |**

**pūtanāsu-payaḥ-pānaṁ śakaṭoccāṭanaṁ śiśoḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **daśamārtham āha—tasya karmāṇīti | pūtanāyā asu-sahitasya stanya-payasaḥ pānam ||28||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tasya kṛṣṇākhyasya | śiśoḥ śiśurūpāt | śakaṭasyoccāṭanaṁ bhedanam caṭa—bhedane ||28||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **pūtanāyā asu-sahitasya stanya-payasaḥ pānam | śiśoḥ śiśunā niṣpeṣaḥ sammardaḥ ||28||

 **...**

**|| 12.12.29 ||**

**tṛṇāvartasya niṣpeṣas tathaiva baka-vatsayoḥ |**

**aghāsura-vadho dhātrā vatsa-pālāvagūhanam] ||**

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **naṣpeṣaścūrṇanam, hananam iti yāvat | tathaiva niṣpeṣaḥ ||29||

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** tṛṇāvartasya niṣpeṣas tathaiva baka-vatsayor ity antam aghāsura-mokṣo na likhita iti kecit tatra vismayante | tad asat, yamalārjuna-bhaṅgasya purāṇāntareṣv api likhitasya kathaṁ na likhanam akarot ? 


    śṛṇuṣvāvahito rājann api guhyaṁ vadāmi te |


    brūyuḥ snigdhasya śiṣyasya guravo guhyam apy uta || [bhā.pu. 10.13.3] 

iti daśame śrī-śukokter yad yad vyākhyātaṁ, tad eva bījam idam iti ||29||

———————————————————————————————————————

_na katamenānyena vyākhyātam._

 **...**

**|| 12.12.30 ||**

**dhenukasya saha-bhrātuḥ pralambasya ca saṅkṣayaḥ |**

**gopānāṁ ca paritrāṇaṁ dāvāgneḥ parisarpataḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **saha-bhrātuḥ sa-sakhasya ||30||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **parisarpataḥ sarvataḥ pravṛt tasya ||30||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **saha-bhrātuḥ jñāti-sahitasya ||30||

**...**

**|| 12.12.31 ||**

**damanaṁ kāliyasyāher mahāher nanda-mokṣaṇam |**

**vrata-caryā tu kanyānāṁ yatra tuṣṭo’cyuto vrataiḥ ||**

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **yatra vratacaryāyām | yajñagānāṁ patnyo yajñapatnyaḥ ||31||

 **...**

**|| 12.12.32-33 ||**

**prasādo yajña-patnībhyo viprāṇāṁ cānutāpanam |**

**govardhanoddhāraṇaṁ ca śakrasya surabher atha ||**

**yajñābhiṣekaḥ kṛṣṇasya strībhiḥ krīḍā ca rātriṣu |**

**śaṅkhacūḍasya durbuddher vadho’riṣṭasya keśinaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **śekraṇa kṛtā pūjā, surabhyā kṛto'bhiṣeka iti vivekaḥ || strīharaṇapravṛtterdurbuddhitvam | ariṣṭo vṛṣāsuraḥ ||32-33||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **viprānutāpanaṁ sūkṣmam api | atrāvadhāpanārthāya smāritaṁ surabhi-kartṛkaṁ ca yajñābhiṣekam ||32||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** śakrasya śakreṇa surabheḥ surabhyā yajñaḥ pūjanam abhiṣekaś ca tat ||32||

 **...**

**|| 12.12.34-36 ||**

**akrūrāgamanaṁ paścāt prasthānaṁ rāma-kṛṣṇayoḥ |**

**vraja-strīṇāṁ vilāpaś ca mathurālokanaṁ tataḥ ||**

**gaja-muṣṭika-cāṇūra- kaṁsādīnāṁ tathā vadhaḥ |**

**mṛtasyānayanaṁ sūnoḥ punaḥ sāndīpaner guroḥ ||**

**mathurāyāṁ nivasatā yadu-cakrasya yat priyam |**

**kṛtam uddhava-rāmābhyāṁ yutena hariṇā dvijāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā),** **viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ādinā kaṁsabhrātrādigrahaḥ || ānayanaṁ, saṁyaminyā iti śeṣaḥ || he dvijā iti saṁbuddhibahutvamādarārtham | kuśasthalyā dvārakāyā niveśanaṁ racanā ||34-36||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **uddhava-rāmābhyām ity uddhavasyāpi tādṛśatvaṁ darśitam ||36||

 **...**

**|| 12.12.37-39 ||**

**jarāsandha-samānīta- sainyasya bahuśo vadhaḥ |**

**ghātanaṁ yavanendrasya kuśasthalyā niveśanam ||**

**ādānaṁ pārijātasya sudharmāyāḥ surālayāt |**

**rukmiṇyā haraṇaṁ yuddhe pramathya dviṣato hareḥ ||**

**harasya jṛmbhaṇaṁ yuddhe bāṇasya bhuja-kṛntanam |**

**prāgjyotiṣa-patiṁ hatvā kanyānāṁ haraṇaṁ ca yat ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ye ca śambarādayas teṣāṁ māhātmyaṁ prabhāvo vadhaś ca ||39||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **surālayādindralokāt | sudharmā devasabhā syātsudharmā devasabhā ity amaraḥ || prāgjyotiṣapatirnarakāsuraḥ ||37-38||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **caidyādīnāṁ māhātmyaṁ vadhaś ca ye ca śambarādayas teṣāṁ cety anvayaḥ ||39||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** _na vyākhyātam._

**...**

**|| 12.12.40 ||**

**caidya-pauṇḍraka-śālvānāṁ dantavakrasya durmateḥ |**

**śambaro dvividaḥ pīṭho muraḥ pañcajanādayaḥ ||**
