**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ekādaśārtham āha—vipra-śāpeti ||40||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **pīṭho hi narakāsuracamūpatiḥ | pīṭhaṁ puraskṛtya camūpati mṛdhe bhaumaprayuktā niragam ity-ukteḥ ādinā tatputrādayaḥ ||39-40||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** _na vyākhyātam._

 **...**

**|| 12.12.41 ||**

**māhātmyaṁ ca vadhas teṣāṁ vārāṇasyāś ca dāhanam |**

**bhārāvataraṇaṁ bhūmer nimittī-kṛtya pāṇḍavān ||**

**śrīdharaḥ, jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **apadeśo vyājaḥ ||41||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **māhātmyaṁ caidyādīnāṁ parākramaḥ ||40||

 **...**

**|| 12.12.42 ||**

**vipra-śāpāpadeśena saṁhāraḥ sva-kulasya ca |**

**uddhavasya ca saṁvādo vasudevasya cādbhutaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **dharma-vinirṇayo varṇāśrama-dharma-viniścayaḥ | martya-parityāgo manuṣyatvasyāntardhānam ||42||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **yatra bhagavad-uddhavasaṁvāde ||42||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **martyasya martya-lokasya parityāgaḥ ātmano yoga-māyā-prabhāvata iti lokair durvitarkatā dhvanitā ||42||

 **...**

**|| 12.12.43 ||**

**yatrātma-vidyā hy akhilā proktā dharma-vinirṇayaḥ |**

**tato martya-parityāga ātma-yogānubhāvataḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **dvādaśārtham āha—yugeti | yuga-lakṣaṇaṁ tad-anurūpā vṛttiś cety arthaḥ | tri-vidha prākṛtikī naimittikī nityā ceti ||43||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ity artha iti—yasmin yasminyuge yā yā vṛttiḥ sāpyukteti bhāvaḥ | upaplavo nāśaḥ, dharmāder iti śeṣaḥ | prākṛtikī prakṛtimadhikṛtya pravṛttā mahadādiprādurbhāveṇa sṛṣṭilakṣaṇā | naimittikī nimittaṁ śubhāśubhaṁ karma, tadadhikṛtya pravṛttāderamānuṣādilakṣaṇā | nityā hi pratikṣaṇaṁ śarīranāśotpattisvīkāreṇātīvasūkṣmā bālyanāśayauvanotpattyanumeyeti dhyeyaṁ sudhībhiḥ ||43||

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** tato martya-parityāgaḥ martya-loka-parityāgaḥ ||43||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.12.44 ||**

**yuga-lakṣaṇa-vṛttiś ca kalau nṝṇām upaplavaḥ |**

**catur-vidhaś ca pralaya utpattis tri-vidhā tathā ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ṛṣer vyāsasya | sūryasya ca vinyāsa ity arthaḥ ||44||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **dhīmataḥ śrīśukaprasādāvāptajñānasya | ity artha iti—samāsāntargatam api vinyāsapadamatra vipra kīrṇajaṭācchannaṁ rauraveṇājinena ca itivatsambadhyate iti bhāvaḥ ||44||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** yuga-lakṣaṇaṁ tad-anurūpā vṛttiś ca | utplavaḥ dharma-viplavaḥ | trividhā prākṛtī naimittikī nityā ca ||44||

 **...**

**|| 12.12.45 ||**

**deha-tyāgaś ca rājarṣer viṣṇu-rātasya dhīmataḥ |**

**śākhā-praṇayanam ṛṣer mārkaṇḍeyasya sat-kathā |**

**mahā-puruṣa-vinyāsaḥ sūryasya jagad-ātmanaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **iti coktam iti ca-kārād anyad api vo yuṣmābhir iha yat pṛṣṭo’smi, tad uktam iti | kim evaṁ nānārtha-kathanena ? tatrāha—līleti | sarvaśaḥ tat-tad-artha-kīrtana-dvāreṇety arthaḥ ||45||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **atrākṣipati—kimevam iti | ity artha iti—teṣāṁ teṣāṁ līlādīnāmarthaprayojanaṁ tatkīrtanadvāreṇeti bhāvaḥ | dvijaśreṣṭhatvādetatsarvaṁ bhavadbhyo mayodīritam iti saṁbuddhyabhiprāyaḥ ||45||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.12.46 ||**

**iti coktaṁ dvija-śreṣṭhā yat pṛṣṭo’ham ihāsmi vaḥ |**

**līlāvatāra-karmāṇi kīrtitānīha sarvaśaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tat-kīrtanenāpi kim ? ity apekṣāyāṁ tat-phalam āha dvābhyām ||46||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **sarvāṇi pātakāni yasmistatsarvapātakaṁ karmajālaṁ tasmāt ||46||

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** iti coktam ity-ādi | līlāvatāra-karmāṇi kīrtitānīha sarvaśa iti ||46||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.12.47 ||**

**patitaḥ skhalitaś cārtaḥ kṣuttvā vā vivaśo gṛṇan |**

**haraye nama ity uccair mucyate sarva-pātakāt ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : patitaḥ** kūpādiṣu | **skhalitaḥ** sopānādiṣu | **ārto** duḥkhitaḥ | **kṣuttvā** kṣutaṁ kṛtvā **vivaśo**’pi ||47||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **vyasanaṁ duḥkham ||47||

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** samyak kīrtanasya phalaṁ yathā kathaṁcit kīrtana-phala-darśana-sukhena vyatirekata āha—patita ity-ādi | haraye nama ity uccair mucyate, sarva-pātakāt vimukto bhavati | kūpādau patitādīnāṁ vivaśatvenoccaiḥ kīrtanābhāve’pi uccair mucyate ||47||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **patita iti kaimutyārtham uktiḥ ||47||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** etāvat kathā kīrtanasya phalaṁ brūhīti cet, tatra kaimutyenāha—patita uccapradeśād adhaḥ prāptaḥ, skhalitaḥ samāna-pradeśe’py ayathā pāda-vinyāsāt prāpta-vyathaḥ | kṣuttvā kṣutaṁ kṛtvā uccair atighora-pāpād api ||47||

 **...**

**|| 12.12.48 ||**

**saṅkīrtyamāno bhagavān anantaḥ**

**śrutānubhāvo vyasanaṁ hi puṁsām |**

**praviśya cittaṁ vidhunoty aśeṣaṁ**

**yathā tamo’rko’bhram ivātivātaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : saṅkīrtyamāno** yad vā **śruto’nubhāvo** yasya sa **puṁsāṁ** **cittaṁ praviśya** niḥśeṣaṁ duḥkhaṁ **vidhunoti** | hīti satām anubhavaṁ pramāṇayati | **arko** giri-guhādi-dhvāntaṁ na dhunotīty aparitoṣād dṛṣṭāntāntaram āha—**ativāto’bhram** **iva** iti ||48||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : vyasanaṁ** duḥkham ||48||

———————————————————————————————————————

**kaivalya-dīpikā : saṅkīrtyamāna** iti | **anubhāvo** mahimā | **vyasanaṁ** malam | tac ced dvedhā māyikaṁ kāryaṁ ca | tatrobhayor api nirvartya vivakṣayā kramāt tayo bhramayo rūpādānam ||48|| [mu.pha. 8.34]

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** yathā kathaṁcit kīrtita eva sarva-pātakaṁ nāśayati, kiṁ punaḥ samyak kīrtitaḥ ? ity āha—**saṅkīrtyamāna** iti | **hi** niścitaṁ | **vyasanaṁ** pāpādi-kṛtaṁ duḥkhaṁ **vidhunoti** viśeṣeṇa dūrīkaroti, vyasana-nāśānantaraṁ **cittaṁ** ca nirmalaṁ karotīti sūrya-dṛṣṭāntaḥ | samyaṅ nirasane **ativāta**-dṛṣṭāntaḥ | **ativātaḥ** vyātyā ||48||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **cittaṁ praviśya vyasanaṁ dhunoti | arkas tama iva | sa ca guhāgataṁ tamo na dhunotīty aparitoṣād āha ativāto’bhram iva ||48||

 **...**

**|| 12.12.49 ||**

**mṛṣā giras tā hy asatīr asat-kathā**

**na kathyate yad bhagavān adhokṣajaḥ |**

**tad eva satyaṁ tad u haiva maṅgalaṁ**

**tad eva puṇyaṁ bhagavad-guṇodayam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **hari-saṅkīrtanam eva mahā-phalaṁ tad-vyatiriktaṁ sarvaṁ mithyālāpa-mātram iti prapañcayati—mṛṣā-gira iti caturbhiḥ | mṛṣā-giro mithyā-vācaḥ | asatīr asatyaḥ | asatāṁ kathā yāsu tāḥ | yad yāsu uttama-ślokasya yaśo’nugīyata iti yat tad eva satyaṁ tad eva hi maṅgalam | u ha iti harṣe | bhagavad-guṇānām abhyudayo yasmāt tat ||49||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **asya śāstrasya kṛṣṇa-kīrtana eva tātpīttad anya-kīrtanam avigītam api na kuryāt, tat kīrtanaṁ yat paśubhir vigītatvenoktaṁ tad api kuryād ity āha—**mṛṣā** iti | tāḥ satyā api giro mithyā eva, priyā api giro'satīr asatyāḥ kaṭūktaya eva, tathā satāṁ viduṣām api kathā asat-kathā eva | kutaḥ ? yad yato bhagavān na kathyata iti | ataḥ sa satya-vādī api mithyā-vādī, priyaṁ-vado'pi kaṭu-vādī, sat-kathako'py asat-kathaka ucyata iti bhāvaḥ | sva-kalpitatvād asatyam api bhagavad-yaśaś cet tad eva satyaṁ saṁsṛti-dhvaṁsakatvāt, amaṅgalam api tad eva maṅgalaṁ nānyat, bhagavataḥ para-dāra-ramaṇādikam adhamair apuṇyatvenoktam api tad eva puṇyaṁ, yato bhagavato guṇasyaiva na tu doṣasyodayo yasmāt tat ||49||

———————————————————————————————————————

**kaivalya-dīpikā : mṛṣā** iti | **mṛṣā** asatyāḥ | vācyasya mithyā-bhūtatvāt | **asatīḥ** amaṅgalāḥ | **asat-kathā** apuṇya-rūpāḥ yad yābhiḥ | **u** aho | **ha** prasiddham | **bhagavatāṁ** śrīmatāṁ **guṇānām udayo** yasmāt tat tathā | kās tarhi samīkṣyāha—**tad eva** iti ||49|| [mu.pha. 8.35]

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** saṅkīrtanaṁ vinā sarvam eva vacanaṁ vedādi-pāṭho mṛṣety āha—**mṛṣā giras ta** ity-ādi | tā giro mṛṣā yad yāsu yābhir vā adhokṣajo bhagavān śrī-kṛṣṇo na kathyate | asat-kathāś ca asatīḥ asatya eva asatī strī yathā nāśayati, tathāpi, atas tad eva satyam ity-ādi | tad eva satyaṁ tad eva maṅgalaṁ sva-sukha-jananaṁ puṇyaṁ puṇya-janakam, na dānādi ||49||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **asya śāstrasya kṛṣṇa-kīrtana eva tātparyāt, tad anya-kīrtanam avigītam api na kuryāt | tat kīrtanaṁ yat paśubhir vigītatvenoktaṁ tad api kuryād ity āha—mṛṣeti | tāḥ satyā api giro mithyā eva | priyā api giro’satīr asatyaḥ kaṭūktaya eva | tathā satāṁ viduṣām api kathā asat-kathā eva | kutaḥ ? yad yato bhagavān na kathyate iti | ataḥ sa satyavādy api mithyā-vādī priyaṁvado’pi kaṭu-bhāṣī sat-kathako’py asat-kathaka ucyate iti bhāvaḥ | svakalpitatvād asatyam api bhagavad-yaśaś cet tad eva satyaṁ gṛhāśrama-vidhvaṁsakatvāt amaṅgalam api tad eva maṅgalaṁ nānyat bhagavataḥ para-dāra-haraṇādikam apuṇyatvenādhamair uktam api tad eva puṇyam | yato bhagavato guṇasyaiva na tu doṣasyodayo yasmāt tat ||49||

 **...**

**|| 12.12.50 ||**

**tad eva ramyaṁ ruciraṁ navaṁ navaṁ**

**tad eva śaśvan manaso mahotsavam |**

**tad eva śokārṇava-śoṣaṇaṁ nṛṇāṁ**

**yad uttamaḥśloka-yaśo’nugīyate ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** **navaṁ navaṁ** yathā bhavati, tathā **ruciraṁ** ruci-pradam | **mahān utsavo** yasmāt ||50||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **aramyam api prasena-mārgānugamana-bhalluka-bila-praveśādi, **ramyam** eva | **ruciram** iti—bhaktānām arocakam api śrī-jānakī-tyāgādi ruciram eveti | purātanam api bhagavac-caritaṁ **navaṁ navam** eva | mārīcānugamanottaraṁ śrī-jānakī-haraṇaṁ rāvaṇa-kṛtaṁ **manaso mahotsava**-nāśakam api mahotsava-karam eva | pati-putrādi-vairāgyotpādakatvena **śokārṇavam** api tac-chokārṇava-tārakam eva ||50||

———————————————————————————————————————

**kaivalya-dīpikā : tad eva** iti | **ruciraṁ** prīti-vardhanam | **tad eva ramyam** āyatī sundaram | ato **navaṁ navaṁ** **śaśvat** āpady anāpadi ca | **śoka-śoṣakaṁ** **mahotsavaṁ** ca yasmin ||50|| [mu.pha. 8.36]

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) : **tad eva ruciraṁ ruci-pradaṁ, tad vinā nānyatra kvāpi tādṛśī rucir bhavatīty arthaḥ | tad eva **navaṁ navam** ayāta-yāmaṁ, tad eva **manaso mahotsavaṁ**, tad eva **śaśvat** śāśvatam, śāśvato **mahotsava** iti vā | klībatvam ārṣam | athavā, tad eva mahasya utsaṁ prasravaṇaṁ vayate iti mahotsavas tad-ākulitam eva bhavati, tad eva **śokārṇava-śoṣaṇam** ||50||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **aramyam api prasena-mārgānugamana-bhalluka-bila-praveśādikaṁ yat tat ramyam eva | ruciram iti bhaktānām arocakam api śrī-jānakī-tyāgādikaṁ ruciram eva | purātanam api bhagavac-caritraṁ navaṁ navam eva | mārīcānugamanānantara-rāvaṇa-kṛta-sītā-haraṇādikaṁ manaso mahotsava-nāśakam api mahotsava-karam eva | pati-putrādi-vairāgyotpādakatvena śokārṇavam api tat **śokārṇava-śoṣaṇam** eva ||50||

 **...**

**|| 12.12.51 ||**

**na yad vacaś citra-padaṁ harer yaśo**

**jagat pavitraṁ pragṛṇīta karhicit |**

**tad dhvāṅkṣa-tīrthaṁ na tu haṁsa-sevitaṁ**

**yatrācyutas tatra hi sādhavo’malāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** citrāṇi padāni yasmin, tad api jagat pavitrayatīti tathā tad dharer yaśo na pragṛṇīta na varṇayet tad vaco dhvāṅkṣa-tīrthaṁ kāka-tulya-narāṇaṁ rati-sthānaṁ na tu haṁsair jñānibhiḥ sevitam | tatra hetuḥ—yatreti ||51||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tatra haṁsāsevane | padyānīmāni vyākhyātacarāṇyeva | na yadvaca ity-ādi padyatrayaṁ bhakterutkarṣākhyāpanārtham eva mahā-purāṇasyāsya prathame'pi śeṣe'pi sthāpitam | yathā mahāmantraḥ kaścidādyantavartinā bījadvayena trayeṇa ca puṭitaḥ syāt ||50-51||

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** vyatirekam āha—na tad ity-ādi | tat tasmāt citrapadam api citrair adbhutaiḥ padair grathitam api vaco harer yaśo na gṛṇīte yadi, tadā tad-vaco dhvāṅkṣa-tīrthaṁ kāka-tīrtham ucchiṣṭa-patrādi-nikṣepa-sthānam | tatra yathā kākā ramante, tathā tat-tulyāḥ kāmina eva tatra ramante | jagat pavitraṁ yaśo-viśeṣaṇaṁ jagati pavitram api śuddham api, tad-vacaḥ iti vaco-viśeṣaṇam ||51||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **na yad iti | yatrācyuto gīyata iti śeṣaḥ ||51||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **na yad vaca iti śloka-trayaṁ bhakter eva sarvotkarṣa-khyāpakam | mahā-purāṇasyāsya prathame’pi śeṣe’pi sthāpitam | yathā mahā-mantraḥ kaścid ādy-antar-vartinā bīja-dvayena trayeṇa puṭitaḥ syād iti ||52||

 **...**

**|| 12.12.52 ||**

**sa**[^73]** vāg-visargo janatāgha-samplavo**

**yasmin prati-ślokam abaddhavaty api |**

**nāmāny anantasya yaśo’ṅkitāni yat**

**śṛṇvanti gāyanti gṛṇanti sādhavaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : sa vāg-visargaḥ** sa eva vācaḥ prayogo **janatāgha-samplavo** jana-samūhāgha-nāśakaḥ | **yad** yasmāt | tāny evānyaiḥ kīrtyamānāni **śṛṇvanti,** śrotari sati **gāyanti**, no cet svayam eva **gṛṇanti** ||52||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ity artha iti—śreyaḥsruti bhaktimudasya ity-ādy-ukter ayaṁ bhāvaḥ ||52||

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** tad vāg-visarga ity-ādi | tad ity avyayam, sa ity arthaḥ | **sa** eva **vāg-visargo janatāgha-viplavaḥ, yasmin abaddhavaty api** apaśabdādi-yukto’pi grāmya-bhāṣā-maye’pīti yāvat | **anantasya nāmāni** kīdṛśāni ? **yaśo’ṅkitāni** govardhanoddharaṇa-kālīya-mardana-keśi-nāśādīni | **yad** yasmāt **śṛṇvanti gāyanti gṛṇanti** **prati ślokaṁ** ślokaṁ prati pratipādyam ity arthaḥ | athavā, prati-ślokaṁ prati-yaśaḥ, naikam eva yaśo geyam ||52||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tad-vāg-visarga iti prathame [1.5.11] vyākhyātam eva | uttama-gāyake sati śṛṇvanti, svasya tu tādṛśatve gāyanti | tad ubhayābhāve gṛṇanti | gīr-mātreṇābhyasyanti cety arthaḥ || [punaruktir ādarāt |] ||52||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** _na vyākhyātam._

 **...**

**|| 12.12.53 ||**

**naiṣkarmyam apy acyuta-bhāva-varjitaṁ**

**na śobhate jñānam alaṁ nirañjanam |**

**kutaḥ punaḥ śaśvad abhadram īśvare**

**na hy arpitaṁ karma yad apy anuttamam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **idānīṁ jñāna-karmādarād api bhagavat-kīrtanādiṣv evādaraḥ kartavya ity āha—**naiṣkarmyaṁ** brahma, tat-prakāśakaṁ **yaj jñānaṁ,** yato **nirañjanam** upādhi-nivartakaṁ, tad **api acyuta-bhakti-varjitaṁ** cen **na śobhate** nāparokṣa-paryantaṁ bhavatīty arthaḥ ||53|| ** **

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **nanu varṇāśramācārādinā niḥśreyasaṁ syādeva varṇāśramācārayuto gṛhasthopi vimucyate iti smṛterato'cyutabhāvena kimityata āha—kiñceti | ity artha iti—kīrtisampattyoḥ satyor api harismṛtiṁ vinātyantikaśreyo na siddhyatīti bhāvaḥ | sāpi kathaṁ syāttatrāha—harerguṇānuvādeti | ādinā smaraṇādigrahaḥ | varṇāśramadharmādiṣu yaḥ paramo mahānpariśramaḥ sa yaśoyuktāyāṁ śriyām eva paryāptaḥ prāyo bhavenna bhagavad-bhaktisādhakaḥ, harerguṇānuvādaśravaṇādibhis tu yaḥ pariśramaḥ sa tu na vismṛtiḥ śrīdharapādapadmayoryasmāttādṛśa ity arthaḥ ||53||

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) : **kiṁ bahunā, hari-kīrtanādi vinā kaivalya-pradam api jñānaṁ na kiñcid ity āha—naiṣkarmyam apīty-ādi | **alam** atyarthaṁ **nirañjanam** upādhi-nivartakam api **jñānaṁ na śobhate** | jñānam apy evam, kim uta karmety āha—**kutaḥ punar** ity-ādi | **anuttamam api śaśvat abhadram īśvare’narpitaṁ **sat ||53||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam. _**[bhakti-sandarbhaḥ 87, prīti-sandarbha 1]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** **anuttamaṁ** śreṣṭhaṁ niṣkāma-**karma** ||53||

 **...**

**|| 12.12.54 ||**

**yaśaḥ-śriyām eva pariśramaḥ paro**

**varṇāśramācāra-tapaḥ-śrutādiṣu |**

**avismṛtiḥ śrīdhara-pāda-padmayor**

**guṇānuvāda-śravaṇādarādibhiḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kiṁ ca, varṇaśramācārādiṣu yaḥ **paro** mahān **pariśramaḥ**, sa **yaśo**-yuktāyāṁ **śriyām** eva | kīrtiḥ saṁpattiś ca kevalaṁ paraḥ puruṣārtha ity arthaḥ | **guṇānuvādādibhis** tu **śrīdhara-pāda-padmayor** **avismṛtir** bhavati ||54||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tataḥ kṛṣṇa-padāravindāsmṛteḥ | sattvasyāntaḥ-karaṇasya sattvaṁ dravye guṇe jīve dhairyāntaḥkaraṇe tathā iti niruktiḥ | jñānam anubhavaḥ | jñānaṁ parokṣam ||54||

———————————————————————————————————————

**kaivalya-dīpikā : yaśa** iti | **yaśasāṁ śrīṇām** ca sambandhiṣu yaśo-nimitteṣu śrī-nimitteṣu ācārādiṣu yaḥ **paraḥ** kevalaḥ **pariśramaḥ** kleśa eva, na tu phalam | yad bhagavat-**pādayor avismṛtiḥ** | sā ca **guṇānuvādādibhiḥ** ||54|| [mu.pha. 9.3]

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** naiṣkarmyasyāpi vipūrvatvam anūdya varṇāśramācārādi niṣpūrvatvam āha—**yaśaḥ-śriyām** ity-ādi | varṇāśrama-tapaḥ-śāstrādiṣu kevalaṁ pariśramaḥ, **paraḥ** pariśiṣṭaḥ, niṣpūrvatvāt | sa kevalaṁ yaśaḥ-śriyāṁ yaśaḥ-sampattāv eva, **śrīdhara-pādayor** vismṛtir eva teṣu | tarhi sā kathaṁ bhavatīty āha—**avismṛtir** ity-ādi | harer guṇānuvāda-caraṇāravindādibhiḥ śrīdhare śrī-yukte ye pāda-padme tayor avismṛtir bhavati | dhriyate iti dharāh, śriyā dharaḥ śrīdhara iti pāda-padmasyaiva vā viśeṣaṇam ||54||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam. _**[bhakti-sandarbhaḥ 88]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** kiṁ ca, varṇāśramādiṣu yaḥ **paro** mahān **pariśramaḥ**, sa yaśo-yuktāyāṁ śriyām eva paryāptaḥ prāyo bhavet | yaśaḥ-saṁpatti-sādhaka eva, na tu bhagavat-prāpti-sādhaka ity arthaḥ | harer guṇānuvāda-śāstrādibhis tu yaḥ pariśramaḥ, sa tu śrīdhara-pāda-padmayor avismṛtir, na bhavati vismṛtir yasmāt saḥ ||54||

 **...**

**|| 12.12.55 ||**

**avismṛtiḥ kṛṣṇa-padāravindayoḥ**

**kṣiṇoty abhadrāṇi ca śaṁ tanoti |**

**sattvasya śuddhiṁ paramātma-bhaktiṁ**

**jñānaṁ ca vijñāna-virāga-yuktam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tataḥ kim ata āha—avismṛtir iti | kṣiṇoti nāśayati ||55||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **haribhajanam eva dvijāgryāpādakamityabhipretyāha—dvijāgryā iti | ata eva sarvāntaryāmitvādeva | adevatve hetuḥ—īśam iti | vidhyarthe'pi loṭo vidhānādāha—yadveti | avaśyabhāvāḥ iti pāṭhe tu na vaśyastato nivartayitumaśakyo bhāva ātmā buddhir iti yāvat, yeṣāṁ ta ity arthaḥ ||55||

———————————————————————————————————————

**kaivalya-dīpikā : **nanu kim avismṛtyā iti tatrāha—**avismṛtir** iti | **kṣiṇoti** hinasti | **abhadrāṇi** durvāsanāḥ | **śaṁ** sukham | **sattva-śuddhiṁ** nīrujakatā | tato bhagavati prema | tato’nyatra **virāgaḥ** | tataḥ parokṣa-bodhaḥ | tataḥ sākṣātkāra ity arthaḥ ||55|| [mu.pha. 9.4]

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** avismṛtiś ced bhavati, tadā kiṁ syād ity āha—avismṛtiḥ kṛṣṇa-pādāravindayor ity-ādi | abhadrāṇi kṣiṇoti | etāvan-mātram eva nety āha—śamaṁ ca tanoti | tena kim ? ity āha—sattvasya śuddhiṁ sattva-guṇasya śuddhim | tataḥ kim ? vijñāna-virāga-yuktaṁ jñānaṁ ca | tataḥ kim ? tatrāha—paramāṁ prema-lakṣaṇāṁ bhaktim ity upasaṁhāraḥ ||55||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam. _**[bhakti-sandarbhaḥ 89]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** tataḥ kim ? ata āha—avismṛtir iti | śamaṁ buddher bhagavan-niṣṭhāṁ śamo man-niṣṭhatā buddheḥ [bhā.pu. 11.19.36] iti bhagavad-ukteḥ ||55||

 **...**

**|| 12.12.56 ||**

**yūyaṁ dvijāgryā bata bhūri-bhāgā**

**yac chaśvad ātmany akhilātma-bhūtam |**

**nārāyaṇaṁ devam adevam īśam**

**ajasra-bhāvā bhajatāviveśya ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **athedānīṁ śrotṝnātmānaṁ cābhinandann āha—yūyam iti dvābhyām | he dvijāgryāḥ, yad yasmād ātmany antaḥ-karaṇe śrī-nārāyaṇam āviveśya śaśvad bhajata | saṁbhāvanāyāṁ loṭ | ato bhūri-bhāgā bahu-puṇyāḥ | kathaṁ-bhūtam ? akhilātma-bhūtaṁ sarvāntaryāmiṇam, ata eva devaṁ sarvopāsyam | adevaṁ na devo’nyo yasya tam | kutaḥ ? īśam | yad vā, yasmād yūyaṁ bhūri-bhāgās tapa-ādi-saṁpannās tato nārāyaṇaṁ bhajateti vidhiḥ ||56||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ātmanastattvaṁ svarūpam ||56||

———————————————————————————————————————

**kaivalya-dīpikā : vidyā** vairājopāsanā[^74] | **prāṇa-nirodhaḥ** prāṇāyāmaḥ | **japyaṁ** praṇavādi nānyat ||56||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (bhakti-sandarbhaḥ 90) **: atra tapa-ādi-sampatteḥ sārthakatvaṁ nārāyaṇa-bhajanenaiva bhavatīti svāmy-abhiprāyaḥ ||56||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** adevaṁ na vidyate devo yasya yasmād iti vā | bhajateti saṁbhāvanāyāṁ loṭ ||56||

 **...**

**|| 12.12.57 ||**

**ahaṁ ca saṁsmārita ātma-tattvaṁ**

**śrutaṁ purā me paramarṣi-vaktrāt |**

**prāyopaveśe nṛpateḥ parīkṣitaḥ**

**sadasy ṛṣīṇāṁ mahatāṁ ca śṛṇvatām ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **me mayā śrutam ||57||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **he viprā iti—yūyaṁ tu viprā matto'pyadhikataraṁ jānītheti bhāvaḥ| sarveṣāmaśubhānāṁ duṣkarmaphalānāṁ vināśanaṁ yena tattathā na vāsudevabhaktānāmaśubhaṁ vidyate kvacit ity-ukteḥ ||57||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ),** **viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (bhakti-sandarbhaḥ 91) :** etat-prasaṅgenāhaṁ cātma-tattvam akhilātma-bhūtaṁ nārāyaṇaṁ smāritaḥ | taṁ prati[^75] paramotkaṇṭhitīkṛto’smīty arthaḥ | yad **ātma-tattvaṁ me** mayā maharṣi-vaktrāc chrutam ||57||

**...**

**|| 12.12.58 ||**

**etad vaḥ kathitaṁ viprāḥ kathanīyoru-karmaṇaḥ |**

**māhātmyaṁ vāsudevasya sarvāśubha-vināśanam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **evam ity ātmānam eva punātīti kiṁ vaktavyam ? kākvā sarvam eva punātīty arthaḥ | etat-purāṇa-kīrtanādi-phalaṁ prapañcayitum āha—etad ity aṣṭabhiḥ ||58||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **etacchrīmadbhāgavatarūpaṁ vāsudevamāhātmyam | yāmaś ca kṣaṇaścānayoḥ samāhāro yāmakṣaṇam | kālādhvanoratyantasaṁyoge iti dvitīyā | bahvavakāśe yāmamātraṁ śṛṇuyādalpāvakāśe tu kṣaṇamātraṁ ca śṛṇuyāt | etenāsyāvaśyaśrotavyatā dhvaniyā'nyathā kāladvayavidhānānupapatteḥ| ata evāmbarīṣa prati śrīgautamenoktam—ambarīṣa śukaproktaṁ nityaṁ bhāgavataṁ śṛṇu | paṭhasva svamukhenāpi yadīcchasi bhavakṣayam | iti | ananyadhīḥ sthiracittaḥ | ātmapāvanaṁ jīvabhāvaparityāgapūrvakaṁ brahmabhāvena sthitiḥ, ajñānamalanivṛttyai tatsaṁgacchata eveti ||58||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ),** **viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.12.59 ||**

**ya etat śrāvayen nityaṁ yāma-kṣaṇam ananya-dhīḥ |**

**ślokam ekaṁ tad-ardhaṁ vā pādaṁ pādārdham eva vā |**

**śraddhāvān yo’nuśṛṇuyāt punāty ātmānam eva saḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **yāma-kṣaṇaṁ yāmaṁ kṣaṇaṁ cety arthaḥ | ātmānam eva sākṣāt punāti, na tu snānādi-vad deha-mātram ||59||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **sarvadā śravaṇānavakāśe tu dvādaśyāmavaśyaṁ śṛṇuyāt, vratavaiguṇyāpanuttaye tvekādaśyāmapyavaśyaṁ śṛṇuyādeveti vā śabda evārthe | āyurvarddhate'nenetyāyuṣyo dharmaḥ dharmeṇa varddhate cāyuḥ ity uktes tadvānbhavati sarvadharmaphalabhāgbhavatīti bhāvaḥ | akālamṛtyuhīno vā bhaved ity arthaḥ | grahādyariṣṭajanyāyurnāśo na bhavatīti bhāvaḥ| prayataḥ pūtaḥ upavāsaṁ kurvanyaḥ paṭhati sa tataḥ sopavāsapāṭhāt apātakī mahāpātakopapātakādibhyo hīno bhavatīty arthaḥ | mahāpātakānyāha manuḥ—


    brahmahatyā surāpānaṁ steyaṁ gurvaṅganāgamaḥ | 


    mahānti pātakānyāhuḥ saṁyogaṁ caiva taiḥ saha || 

upapātakāni tu yājñavalkyaḥ—


    govadho vrātyatā steyam ṛṇānāṁ cānapakriyā | 


    anāhitāgni-tāpaṇya-vikrayaḥ parivedanam ||1|| 


    bhṛtād adhyayanādānaṁ bhṛtakādhyāpanaṁ tathā | 


    pāradāryaṁ pārivittyaṁ vārdhuṣyaṁ lavaṇa-kriyā ||2|| 


    strī-śūdra-viṭ-kṣatra-vadho niditārthopajīvanam | 


    nāstikyaṁ vrata-lopaś ca sutānāṁ caiva vikrayaḥ ||3|| 


    dhānya-kupya-paśu-steyam ayājyānāṁ ca yājanam | 


    pitṛ-mātṛ-suta-tyāgas taḍāga-rāma-vikrayaḥ ||4|| 


    kanyā-sandūṣaṇaṁ caiva parivindaka-yājanam | 


    kanyā-pradānaṁ tasyaiva kauṭilyaṁ vrata-lopanam ||5|| 


    ātmano'rthe kriyārambho madyapa-strī-niṣevaṇam | 


    svādhyāyāgni-suta-tyāgo bāndhava-tyāga eva ca ||6|| 


    indhanārthaṇa dumacchedaḥ strī-hiṁsauṣadhi-jīvanam | 


    hiṁsra-yantra-vidhānaṁ ca vyasanāny ātma-vikrayaḥ ||7|| 


    śūdra-preṣyaṁ hīna-sakhyaṁ hīna-yoni-niṣevaṇam | 


    tathaivānāśrame vāsaḥ parānna-paripuṣṭatā ||8|| 


    asac-chāstrādhigamanam ākareṣv adhikāritā | 


    bhāryāyā vikrayaś caiṣām ekaikam upapātakam ||9|| iti | 

athaiṣām arthaḥ—go-vadho go-piṇḍa-vyāpādanam, kāle'nupanītatvaṁ vrātyatā, brāhmaṇa-suvarṇa-tat-sama-vyatirikta-para-dravyāpaharaṇaṁ steyam, gṛhītasya suvarṇāder apradānam ṛṇānām apākaraṇaṁ, tathā devarṣi-pitṛ-sambadhyaṇasyāpākaraṇaṁ ca, saty adhikāre'nāhitāgnitvam, tathāpaṇyasya lavaṇāder vikrayaḥ, sahodarasya jyeṣṭhasya tiṣṭhataḥ kanīyaso bhrātur dārāgni-saṁyogaḥ parivedanam ||1|| 

paṇa-pūrvam adhyāpakādhyayana-grahaṇam, paṇa-pūrvādhyāpanam, para-dāra-sevanam, pāritrāttyaṁ kanīyasi kṛta-vivāhe jyeṣṭhasya vivāha-rāhityam, vārdhuṣyaṁ pratiṣiddha-vṛddhy-upajīvanam, lavaṇasyotpādanam ūparāditaḥ ||2||

strīty-ādi spaṣṭam, ninditāpi jīvanam arāja-sthāpitārthor ajīvanam, nāsti para-loka ity-ādy-abhiniveśo nāstikyam, vrata-lopo brahmacāriṇaḥ strī-prasaṅgaḥ, sutānām apatyānāṁ vikrayaḥ ||3|| 

dhānyaṁ brīhy-ādi, kupyam asāraṁ trapusīsādi, paśavo gavādayasteṣāmapaharaṇam, go-vadho vrātyatā steyam ity anenaiva siddhe punar dhānyādi-grahaṇaṁ prāyaścitta-viśeṣārtham evam eva bāndhava-tyāga-grahaṇenaiva siddhe punaḥ pitrādi-tyāgo vijñeyaḥ, ayājyānāṁ jāti-karma-duṣṭānāṁ śūdra-vrātyādīnāṁ yājanam, pitṛ-mātṛ-sutānām apatitānāṁ parityāgo gṛhān niṣkāsanam, taḍāgādi-vikrayaḥ ||4|| 

kanyā-dūṣaṇam aṅgulyādinā yoni-vidāraṇaṁ na tu bhogaḥ, tasya sakhi-bhāryā-kumārīṣu iti guru-talpa-samatvokteḥ | pārivindakasya parivettur yājanam, tasyaiva kanyā-pradānaṁ ca, kauṭilyaṁ guror anyatra, guru-viṣayasya tu kauṭilyasya surāpāna-samatvokteḥ | punar vrata-lopa-grahaṇaṁ śiṣṭāprasiddheṣv api śrī-hari-caraṇekṣaṇaṁ vinā tāmbūlaṁ na bhakṣayāmīty evaṁ-rūpeṣu vrateṣu prāpty-artham ||5|| 

kriyārambhaḥ pākārambhaḥ adhaṁ sa kevalaṁ bhuṅkte yaḥ pacaty ātmakāraṇāt iti tasyaiva pratiṣiddhatvākriyāmāna-viṣaye tv atiprasaṅgaḥ syāt | madyapāyā jāyāyā bhogaḥ, svādhyāya-tyāgo vedābhyāsādi-rāhityam, agnīnāṁ śrauta-smārtānāṁ tyāgaḥ, suta-tyāgas tat-saṁskārākaraṇam, bāndhavānāṁ pitṛvya-mātulādīnāṁ tyāgaḥ sati vibhave'parirakṣaṇam ||6||

pākādi-dṛṣṭa-prayojana-siddhy-artham ārdra-druma-cchedo na tv āhavanīyādi-rakṣaṇārtham api, striyā, hiṁsayā, auṣadhena ca jīvanam | tatra strījīvanam—bhāryāṁ paṇyabhāvena puruṣāntarabhogārthaṁ prayojya tallabdhopajīvanaṁ, strīdhanenopajīvanaṁ vā, hiṁsayā prāṇivadhena jīvanan, auṣadhajīvanaṁ vaśīkaraṇādinā, hiṁsrayantrasya tilekṣvādipīḍanādirūpasya pravartanam, vyasanāni mṛgayādīni, ātmavikrayo dravyagrahaṇena paradāsyakaraṇam ||7|| 

śūdrasya preṣyaṁ sevanam, hīnajātiṣu maitrīkaraṇam, anūḍhasavarṇadārasya kevalaṁ hīnavarṇadāropasevanam, sādhāraṇastrīsabhogaśca, agṛhītāśramatvaṁ satyadhikāre, parapākaratitvam ||8|| 

cārvākādigranthāvāmaḥ, ākareṣu suvarṇādyutyattisthāneṣu rājājñayādhikāritvam, bhāryāyā vikrayaḥ cānmanvādyuktābhicāramatipūrvalaśunādibhakṣaṇāndagrahaṇam ||9|| 

mātṛgamanaduhitṛgamanasnuṣāgamanānyatipātakāni, svasṛsakhīsagotrottamavarṇārajasvalāśaraṇāgatāpravrajitānikṣiptanāṁ gamanamanupātakāni, anupātakānām eva viṣṇunā pātakasaṁjñoktā— 


    mahā-pāpaṁ cātipāpaṁ tathā pātakam eva ca | 


    prāsaṅgikaṁ copapāyam ity eṣāṁ pañcako gaṇaḥ || 

iti kṛtaṁ prasaktānuprasaktyā ||59||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.12.60 ||**

**dvādaśyām ekādaśyāṁ vā śṛṇvann āyuṣyavān bhavet ||**

**paṭhaty anaśnan prayataḥ pūto bhavati pātakāt |**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : dvādaśyām ekādaśyāṁ** **vā** iti yadā yasyāṁ vrataṁ prāpyate, tadā tasyām evety arthaḥ ||59||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **yataḥ saṁyataś cāsāv ātmā buddhiryatātmā so'syāstīti yatātmavān | oṣya sthitvā upavāsārthakatvaṁ tu nirannasya yattātmatvāsambhavātyāṭhasyāpi duṣkarataiveti pratīyate | bhayātsaṁsārāt  ||60||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.12.61-62 ||**

**puṣkare mathurāyāṁ ca dvāravatyāṁ yatātmavān |**

**upoṣya saṁhitām etāṁ paṭhitvā mucyate bhayāt ||**

**devatā munayaḥ siddhāḥ pitaro manavo nṛpāḥ |**

**yacchanti kāmān gṛṇataḥ śṛṇvato yasya kīrtanāt ||**

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **atra ye devādayaḥ kīrtitāste'pi kīrtanāt yatra yad bhāgavataṁ gṛṇataḥ śṛṇvataś ca nṛnkāmān yacchanti dadati yatreti dvitīyārthe tral || gṛhya-sūtroktaṁ phalam āha—ṛca iti | tathā hi—yahaco'dhīte payasaḥ kulyā asya pitṛn svadhā upakṣarānti yadyapi ghṛtasya kulyā ya tsāmāni madhvaḥ kulyā yo'tharvāṅgirasaḥ somasya kulyā yad brāhmaṇāni kalpān gāthā nārāśaṁsīr itihāsa-purāṇānīty amṛtasya kulyāḥ iti ||61-62||

 **...**

**|| 12.12.63 ||**

**ṛco yajūṁṣi sāmāni dvijo’dhītyānuvindate |**

**madhu-kulyā ghṛta-kulyāḥ payaḥ-kulyāś ca tat phalam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **ṛg-ādy adhītya dvijo madhu-kulyādi yad anuvindate, tat phalam etāṁ paṭhitvānuvindata iti ||63||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **jīvan-mukti-phalakatvam asyāha—kiṁ ceti | 


    manasā vacasā dṛṣṭyā gṛhyate'nyair apīndriyaiḥ | 


    aham eva na mattā'nyad iti buddhy-adhvam añjasā || 

iti rītyā yat sarvātmakatva-rūpaṁ bhagavataḥ padaṁ svarūpaṁ bhagavataivarṣibhyaḥ proktam arthād advaitānaṣṭhā-rūpaṁ tad vrajel labhed ity arthaḥ ||63||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.12.64 ||**

**purāṇa-saṁhitām etām adhītya prayato dvijaḥ |**

**proktaṁ bhagavatā yat tu tat padaṁ paramaṁ vrajet ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kiṁ ca, proktam iti ||64||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **prajñā prakṛṣṭa-jñānaṁ sarva-purāṇetihāsādhyayanādhyāpana-sāmarthya-lakṣaṇaṁ prāpnuyāt | udadhir mekhaleva parito vyāpto yasyāḥ sodadhi-mekhalā bhūmer nāmedam | samudra-mekhale devi parvata-stana-maṇḍale iti mantrāt | tathā ca bhūmiṁ prāpnuyān na tu samudrāntar-gatāṁ sarvām iti narendrādi-padavad yat kiñcin narāṇāṁ patyāv api yathā narendra-padaṁ prayujyate, tathā yat kiñcid bhūpatir apy udadhi-mekhalā-patir ucyata iti | atra sandhir ārṣaḥ | yad vā, udadhiḥ, āpa adhikotdhādhikā yasminn ity udadhiḥ | atrārṣatvād varṇa-vikāro mayūrādivat | avasthāntara-prāptir vikāras tasmāt yasya saḥ | evaṁ nidhipatir api jñeyaḥ | nidhiḥ padmādi-navake vasv-abdhi-sthāpaneṣu ca iti dharaṇiḥ | dhanapatiḥ syād ity arthaḥ | śūdraḥ śṛṇvann eva tasya pāṭhānadhikārāt | tad-uktaṁ purāṇādhikāra-prastāve bhaviṣye—


    adhyetavyaṁ brāhmaṇena vaiśyena kṣatriyeṇa ca | 


    śrotavyam eva śūdrāṇāṁ nādhyetavyaṁ kadācana || 


    śrītaṁ smārtaṁ ca vaidharmaṁ proktam asmin nṛpottama | 


    tasmāc chūdrair vinā vipraṁ na śrotavyaṁ kadācana || iti ||64||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ), viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : _na vyākhyātam._**

 **...**

**|| 12.12.65 ||**

**vipro’dhītyāpnuyāt prajñāṁ rājanyodadhi-mekhalām |**

**vaiśyo nidhi-patitvaṁ ca śūdraḥ śudhyeta pātakāt ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **rājanya udadhi-mekhalāṁ pṛthvīm | sandhir ārṣaḥ | vipro’dhītyety ādikaṁ tat-tat-kāmāgraha-parāṇāṁ pravartanārtham āpāta-phalam ||65||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **evaṁ prabhāvātireke pūrvoktarītyā prabhāvādhikye | iha śrī-bhāgavate | aśeṣamūrtiranantamūrtiḥ | anupadaṁ pratiślokam | padāni santyatranti padaḥ| ajatra matvarthīyaḥ| padyam | padaṁ padamanupadaṁ vīpsārthakānupadayoge dvitīyā | tattatkathāprasaṅgairbhagavānevātra kīrtita iti | atra karma brahmādipratipādakaśāstre'khileśo virāḍantaryāmī tatpālako viṣṇurvāpi na gīyate, kacidgīyate vā tatra tvabhīkṣṇa neva gīyate | turavadhāraṇe | iha bhāgavate bhagavānevābhīkṣṇaṁ gīyate nārāyaṇādayo ye'tra varṇitāstepyaśeṣā eva mūrtayo'vatārā yasya sa tathābhata eva gīyate na tviratreva tadvivekenetyarthaḥ | ata eva tattatkathāprasaṅgair api bhagavāneva paṭhito vyaktam evokta ity arthaḥ ||65||

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) : **vipro’dhītyety-ādi | śūdro’dhītya pātakāt śudhyeta | idaṁ bhāgavataṁ nāma purāṇaṁ brahma-sammitam [bhā.pu. 1.3.40] iti bhāgavatasya brahma-sammitatvāt kathaṁ tac-chūdro’dhyeta ? satyam | bhaktiś cec chūdra-yoṣitām ity uktatvād bhakta-śūdrasyaādhyaynādhikāro boddhavyaḥ | śūdro’dhītyeti pṛthag-dhyeteti-pada-prayogāt śrutveti nārthāntaraṁ kāryam | etenaivāsmin śrī-bhāgavate śūdra-kartṛkādhyayana-sambhāvanā ||65||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **vipro’dhītyety-ādikaṁ tat-tat-kāmāgraha-parāṇāṁ pravartanārtham āpāta-phalaṁ rājanya udadhi-mekhalāṁ sandhir ārṣaḥ ||65||

 **...**

**|| 12.12.66 ||**

**kali-mala-saṁhati-kālano’khileśo**

**harir itaratra na gīyate hy abhīkṣṇam |**

**iha tu punar bhagavān aśeṣa-mūrtiḥ**

**paripaṭhito’nu-padaṁ kathā-prasaṅgaiḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **asya purāṇasyaivaṁ prabhāvātir eke kāraṇam āha—**kali-malānāṁ saṁhatiṁ** samūhaṁ **kālayati** vināśayatīti tathā | **itaratra** śāstrāntare ||66||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ādinānantādigrahaḥ | sarvajñar api devairajñātaguṇagaṇatvād durjñeyaṁ taṁ nato'smīti | tamajaṁ nato'smi, kiṁ brahmāṇaṁ namasi? na, anantam | kiṁ pradhānaṁ? ātmatattvaṁ cetanasvarūpam | kiṁ śuddhajīvaṁ? na, jagadudayādaya ātmaśaktito yasya tam | kiṁ durgāpatiṁ śabhum? viśveśvarīṁ jagaddhātrīṁ sthitisaṁhārakāriṇīm iti mārkaṇḍeyokteḥ śivāddhāṅgaharā durgā iti purāṇāntarāc ca, na, dyapatibhirajādyair apy ajñātastutikamacyuta śrī-kṛṣṇam, ko vetti bhūmanbhagavanparātmanyogeśvaroktīrbhavatas trilokyām iti brahmokteḥ | nāha vedāpare'pi ca ity ukteḥ, yato yato vāco nivartante aprāpya manasā saha iti śruteś ca ||66||

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** anyebhyaḥ purāṇebhyo’sya śraiṣṭhyam upakrame’pi dharmaḥ projjhita-kaitavo’tra [bhā.pu. 1.1.2] iti yathoktaṁ, tathaivopasaṁhāre’pi darśayann āha—kali-mala-saṁhatīty-ādi | **itaratra** purāṇādau **abhīkṣṇaṁ na gīyate**, **iha tu** **anupadaṁ** padaṁ padam anu pari parito **bhagavān** śrī-kṛṣṇaḥ | kīdṛśaḥ ? **aśeṣa-mūrtiḥ**, śeṣaḥ pariṇāmas tad-rahitā mūrtiḥ śrī-vigraho yasya | **kathā-prasaṅgaiḥ** kathābhiḥ sākṣāt kathyamānābhiḥ prasaṅgaiś ca ||66||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : kālano** nāśanaḥ | **itaratra** karma-brahmādi-pratipādaka-śāstrāntare | **akhileśo** virāḍ-antaryāmī nārāyaṇo’pi tat-pālako viṣṇur vāpi **na gīyate** kvacid gīyate vā, tatra tv **abhīkṣṇaṁ** naiva gīyate | **tu**-śabdo’vadhāraṇe | sākṣāt śrī-**bhagavān** punar iha śrī-bhāgavata evābhīkṣṇaṁ gīyate | nārāyaṇādayo vā ye’tra varṇitāḥ, te’py **aśeṣā** eva **mūrtayo**’vatārā yasya saḥ | tathā-bhūta eva gīyate, na tv itaratreva tad-avivekenety arthaḥ | ata eva tat-tat-**kathā-prasaṅgair anupadaṁ** padaṁ padam api lakṣyīkṛtya bhagavān eva **pari** sarvato-bhāvena **paṭhito** vyaktam evokta iti[^76] ||66|| [paramātma-sandarbha 107]

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) : **kali-mala iti | **kālano** nāśanaḥ | **anupadaṁ** prati-prakaraṇam eva, **itaratra** karma-brahmādi-pratipādaka-śāstrāntare | **akhileśo** virāḍ antaryāmī nārāyaṇo’pi tat-pālako viṣṇur vāpi na gīyate | kvacid gīyate vā, tatra tv **abhīkṣṇaṁ** **naiva gīyate** | **tu**-śabdo’vadhāraṇe | sākṣāt śrī-**bhagavān punar iha** śrī-bhāgavata evābhīkṣṇaṁ gīyate | nārāyaṇādayo vā ye’tra varṇitāḥ, te’py **aśeṣā** eva **mūrtayo**’vatārā yasya saḥ | tathābhūta eva gīyate, na tv itaratraiva tad-avivekenety arthaḥ | ata eva tat-tat-**kathā-prasaṅgair anupadaṁ** padaṁ padam api lakṣyīkṛtya bhagavān eva **pari** sarvato-bhāvena **paṭhito **vyaktam evokta iti ||66|| 

**...**

**|| 12.12.67 ||**

**tam aham ajam anantam ātma-tattvam **

**jagad-udaya-sthiti-saṁyamātma-śaktim |**

**dyu-patibhir aja-śakra-śaṅkarādyair**

**duravasita-stavam acyutaṁ nato’smi ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **śāstra-pratipāditaṁ bhagavantaṁ namaskaroti—tam iti dvābhyam | jagad-udaya-sthiti-saṁyamātmāno raja-ādayaḥ śaktayo yasya tam | dyu-patibhir devair api duravasito’jñātaḥ stavaḥ stotraṁ yasya tam ||67||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **ādinānantādi-grahaḥ | sarvajñar api devairajñātaguṇagaṇatvād durjñeyaṁ taṁ nato'smīti | tam ajaṁ nato'smi, kiṁ brahmāṇaṁ namasi? na, anantam | kiṁ pradhānaṁ? ātmatattvaṁ cetanasvarūpam | kiṁ śuddhajīvaṁ? na, jagadudayādaya ātmaśaktito yasya tam | kiṁ durgāpatiṁ śabhum? viśveśvarīṁ jagaddhātrīṁ sthitisaṁhārakāriṇīm iti mārkaṇḍeyokteḥ śivād dhāṅgaharā durgā iti purāṇāntarāc ca, na, dyapatibhir ajādyair apy ajñāta-stutikam acyuta śrī-kṛṣṇam, ko vetti bhūman bhagavan parātman yogeśvaroktīr bhavatas trilokyām [bhā.pu. 10.14.21] iti brahmokteḥ | nāhaṁ vedāpare'pi ca ity ukteḥ, yato vāco nivartante aprāpya manasā saha [tai.u. 2.4.1] iti śruteś ca ||66||

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** tat tasmāt taṁ nato’smīty āha—**tam aham** ity-ādi | **taṁ** śrī-kṛṣṇam **ajam** anantam apariṇāmam **ātma-tattvam** | ātmā svayam eva tattvaṁ bhagavat-tattvaṁ yasya, **acyutaṁ** śāśvatam, ata eva **ajādibhir** **duravasito** yāthārthyena jñātaḥ **stavo** yasya ||67||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** śāstra-pratipāditaṁ devaṁ praṇamati—tam ajaṁ nato’smi | kiṁ brahmāṇaṁ namasi ? na | anantaṁ kiṁ pradhānam ? na | **ātma-tattvaṁ** cetana-svarūpam | kiṁ śuddha-jīvam ? na | **jagad-udayādaya ātma-śaktito** yasya tam | kiṁ durgā-patiṁ śambhum ? na | **dyupatibhir** devair **ajādyair** api **duravasita-stavam** ajñāta-stutikam | **acyutaṁ** śrī-kṛṣṇam ||67||

 **...**

**|| 12.12.68 ||**

**upacita-nava-śaktibhiḥ sva ātmany**

**uparacita-sthira-jaṅgamālayāya |**

**bhagavata upalabdhi-mātra-dhāmne**

**sura-ṛṣabhāya namaḥ sanātanāya ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : upacitābhir** udriktābhir **nava-śaktibhiḥ** prakṛti-puruṣa-mahad-ahaṅkāra-tan-mātra-rūpābhiḥ **sva ātmany** eva **uparacitaṁ sthiraṁ jaṅgamaṁ** ca **ālayo** yasya, tasmai **bhagavate** ||68||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **sve svīye | ātmani svarūpe | uparacitam āvirbhāvitaṁ yat sthiraṁ sthāvaraṁ jaṅgamaṁ ca tad evālayo nivāsa-sthānaṁ yasya, tasmai sva-prakāśita-jagati jīva-rūpeṇāntaryāmi-rūpeṇa ca sthitāya | upalabdhi-mātra-dhāmne sarva-jñāna-svarūpāya jñāna-mātrādhiṣṭhānāya vā | suraṛṣabhāya sarva-devottamāya śrī-kṛṣṇāya | sanātanāya sarvāvasthāsu vidyamānāya | etac ca śrī-kṛṣṇa evaṁ sampadyate | ahaṁ sarvasya prabhavo mattaḥ sarvaṁ pravartate [gītā 10.8] iti, mayā tatam idaṁ sarvaṁ jagat sthāvara-jaṅgamam [gītā 9.4] iti ca tad-ukteḥ | 

yad vā, **upalabdhi-mātraṁ **paraṁ brahma, tasya **dhāmne** sthānāya, jñāna-mātraṁ paraṁ brahma [bhā.pu. 3.32.21] ity ukteḥ, brahmaṇo hi pratiṣṭhāham [gītā 14.27] iti śrī-mukhokteḥ, sanātanas tvaṁ puruṣo mato me ity arjunokteś ca sanātanatvam api tatraiva saṁgacchate devānām acyuto yathā ity agre vakṣyamāṇatvāt tat sarva-deva-śreṣṭho'pi sa eveti ||68||

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** punar namaskaroti—upacitety ādi | sanātanāya bhagavat śrī-kṛṣṇāya namaḥ | upalabdhi-mātraṁ nirupahita-caitanyaṁ dhāma sthānaṁ yasya—kṣemaṁ vindanti mat-sthānaṁ yad brahma paramaṁ viduḥ [bhā.pu. 11.20.37] iti bhagavad-ukteḥ | surāṇāṁ brahmādīnām ṛṣabhāya śreṣṭhāya | upalabdhi-dhāmatvam āha—upacitety-ādi | upacitānudriktān vā, aprākṛtā nūyate stūyate iti nava, karmṇy an | tathā-bhūtā yā śaktayaḥ līlādyās tābhiḥ sve ātmani cit-svarūpe’dhiṣṭhāne uparacitāḥ sthirās tarv-ādaya ālayā gṛhā yena | etenopakrama-labdhasya, yatra tri-isargo mṛṣā [bhā.pu. 1.1.1] iti vyākhyātasya vastuna upasaṁhāre’pi prakaṭanam ||68||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** tam eva svāntaryāmitvena praṇam iti | nava-śaktiḥ | prakṛti-puruṣa-mahad-ahaṅkāra-tanmātra-rūpābhiḥ ||68||

 **...**

**|| 12.12.69 ||**

**sva-sukha-nibhṛta-cetās tad-vyudastānya-bhāvo'py **

**ajita-rucira-līlākṛṣṭa-sāras tadīyam |**

**vyatanuta kṛpayā yas tattva-dīpaṁ purāṇaṁ**

**tam akhila-vṛjina-ghnaṁ vyāsa-sūnuṁ nato’smi ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :** śrī-guruṁ namaskaroti | **sva-sukhenaiva nibhṛtaṁ** pūrṇaṁ **ceto** yasya | tenaiva **vyudasto’nyasmin bhāvo** yasya tathābhūto’py **ajitasya rucirābhir līlābhir ākṛṣṭaḥ sāraḥ** sva-sukha-gataṁ sthairyaṁ yasya saḥ | **tattva-dīpaṁ** paramārtha-prakāśakaṁ śrī-bhāgavataṁ yo **vyatanuta taṁ nato’smīti** ||69||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **sva-sukhena paramānandāvāptyā | tenaiva svasukhapūrṇacetastvenaiva | anyasminparamānandasvarūpāditaratra, bhāvaḥ sneho yasya | tathābhūtopi paramānandatṛptopi | ajitasya śrī-kṛṣṇasya | rucirābhirmanoharābhirbālyādicaritairākṛṣṭa ākarṣaṇaviṣayīkṛtaḥ | tad iti brahmaṇo nāma iti śrutes tad brahma tasya bhāvas tattvaṁ śrī-kṛṣṇaḥ—


    aho bhāgyam aho bhāgyaṁ nanda-gopa-vrajaukasām | 


    yan-mitraṁ paramānandaṁ pūrṇaṁ brahma sanātanam || [bhā.pu. 10.14.32]

iti brahmoktes tasya prakāśakam | akhilāni vṛjināni pāpāni hanti darśana-smaraṇādinety **akhila-vṛjinaghnaḥ,** kaluṣaṁ vṛjinainogham [bhā.pu. 12.13.21] ity amaraḥ | brahma-rūpatvāt tasya sarvāgha-nivartakatvam | śukāya brahma-rūpiṇe ity agrimādhyāyokteḥ sveṣṭa-devaṁ śāstra-pratipādyaṁ natvā sva-guruṁ praṇamati—sva-sukhena brahmānandena **nibhṛtaṁ** paripūrṇaṁ **ceto** yasya tam | tena tathātvena vyudasto dūrībhūto'nyasmin bhāvo mano-vyāpāro yasya tam | tathā-bhūto'py ajitasya śrī-kṛṣṇasya rucira-līlayā kartryātibalavatyākṛṣṭas tasmād brahmānanda-sakāśāt svasminn ānatiḥ sāro rasānubhava-sāmarthyaṁ yasya saḥ, brahma-rasāsvādād api līlā-rasāsvāde mādhuryādhikyam anubhūya tatraiva yaḥ prāpta-niṣṭho'bhūd iti bhāvaḥ | tena līlā-raso'yaṁ tasya na samādhi-bhañjakaḥ pratyūhas tathātve tena tatraiva punaḥ samādhyartham evāyatiṣyata na tu tathā-kṛtaṁ pratyuta kṛpayānyebhyo'pi līlā-rasāsvāda-ditsayā **tattva-dīpaṁ** līlā-rasa-tattva-prakāśakaṁ vyatanuta | ata evoktam—harer guṇākṣipta-matir bhagavān bādarāyaṇiḥ [bhā.pu. 1.7.11] iti, pariniṣṭhito'pi nairguṇye [bhā.pu. 2.1.9] ity-ādi purāṇaṁ śrī-bhāgavataṁ vyatanuta vistara-pūrvaṁ vyākhyātavān ||68||

iti śrīmad-bhāgavata-bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśe dvādaśa-skandhe dvādaśo'dhyāyaḥ ||12||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **namaskurvann eva vaktṛ-hṛdaya-niṣṭhā-paryālocanayā samasta-grantha-tātparyaṁ nirdhārayati—sva-sukheti | atra **akhila-vṛjinaṁ** tādṛśa-bhāvasya pratikūlam udāsīnaṁ ca sarvaṁ jñeyam | **ajita**-śabdenātra pūrṇatvena mukhyatayā śrī-kṛṣṇa-saṁjña eveti prathame śrī-bādarāyaṇa-samādhau vyaktīkṛto’sti ||69||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** sveṣṭa-devaṁ praṇamya śrī-guruṁ praṇamati | **sva-sukhena** brahmānandena **nibhṛtaṁ** paripūrṇaṁ **ceto** yasya saḥ | tena tathātvenaiva **vyudasto** dūrībhūto’**nyatra bhāvo** mano-vyāpāro yasya tathābhūto’py **ajitasya** kṛṣṇasya **rucira-līlayā** kartryā atibalavatyā **ākṛṣṭas** tasmād brahmānandāt sakāśād api svasminn ānītaḥ **sāro** rasānubhava-sāmarthyaṁ yasya saḥ | brahma-rasāsvādād api līlā-rasāsvāde mādhuryādhikyam anubhūya, tatraiva yaḥ prāpta-niṣṭho’bhūd iti bhāvaḥ | tena līlā-raso’yaṁ tasya na samādhi-bhañjakaḥ pratyūha iti vyākhyeyam | tathātve sati tena punar api tādṛśa-samādhy-artham evāyatiṣyata | na tu tathākṛtaṁ pratyuta **kṛpayā**nyebhyo’pi tādṛśa-līlā-rasāsvāda-ditsayā **tattva-dīpaṁ **līlā-rasa-tattva-prakāśakaṁ **vyatanuta** | ata evoktaṁ harer guṇākṣipta-matir bhagavān bādarāyaṇir [bhā.pu. 1.7.11] iti, pariṇiṣṭhito’pi nairguṇye [bhā.pu. 2.1.9] ity-ādi ca ||69||

iti sārārtha-darśinyāṁ harṣiṇyāṁ bhakta-cetasām |

dvādaśe dvādaśo’dhyāyaḥ saṅgataḥ saṅgataḥ satām ||*||

 **...**


    iti śrīmad-bhāgavate mahā-purāṇe brahma-sūtra-bhāṣye pāramahaṁsyaṁ saṁhitāyāṁ vaiyāsikyāṁ dvādaśa-skandhe 


    skandhārtha-nirūpaṇaṁ nāma 


    dvādaśo’dhyāyaḥ

|| 12.12 ||

**...**

**(12.13)**


### trayodaśo’dhyāyaḥ


## skandhārtha-nirūpaṇaṁ

**|| 12.13.1 ||**

**sūta uvāca—**

**yaṁ brahma-varuṇendra-rudra-marutaḥ stunvanti divyaiḥ stavair**

**vedaiḥ sāṅga-pada-kramopaniṣadair gāyanti yaṁ sāma-gāḥ |**

**dhyānāvasthita-tad-gatena manasā paśyanti yaṁ yogino**

**yasyāntaṁ na viduḥ surāsura-gaṇā devāya tasmai namaḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) :**

trayodaśe purāṇānāṁ saṅkhyām āha yathā-kramam |

dānaṁ dānasya māhātmyaṁ śrīmad-bhāgavatasya ca ||*||

sarva-purāṇa-saṅkhyādīn upavarṇayiṣyaṁs tat pratipādyaṁ devaṁ praṇamati—yam iti | **stavair vedaiś** ca **stunvanti** stuvanti | **upaniṣac**-chabdasyākārāntatvaṁ chando'nurodhena | **dhyānena** **avasthitaṁ** niścalaṁ **tad-gataṁ** ca yan **manaḥ**, tena **yasyāntaṁ na viduḥ surāsura-gaṇāḥ** ||1||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : _yathā-kramaṁ_** saptamādhyāyokta-purāṇa-gaṇanā-kramam anatikramya | tatra hi—brāhmaṁ pādmaṁ vaiṣṇavaṁ hi [varāha-pu.] ity-ādinā purāṇāṣṭādaśakam uktam iti ||*|| 

_tat-pratipādyam_ aṣṭādaśa-purāṇa-pratipādyam | **divyair** alaukikaiḥ | aṅgādi-pāṭha-catuṣkeṇa **aṅga**-pāṭha-**pada**-pāṭha-**krama**-pāṭh**opaniṣat**-pāṭhair **gāyanti** | aṅgādi-pāṭha-jñānaṁ ca vedādhyayana-sādhyam iti | yad vā, antime'dhyāye punar api maṅgalaṁ natyātmakam ācarati | upaniṣac-chabdo'd-anta ārṣaḥ, tenaitat-purāṇa-pāṭhena bhagavatas tasya stuti-saṁkīrtanam eva mama yathākathañcid abhūt, na tu samyag avagama iti bhāvaḥ ||1||

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** yaṁ brahma-varuṇendrety-ādi | **devāya** śrī-kṛṣṇāya **nama** ity avatāriṇaṁ śrī-kṛṣṇaṁ natvā śrī-kṛṣṇasya durjñeyatvaṁ kiṁ vācyam | tad-aṁśāṁśasya kūrmādeś caritam apy atidurjñeyam iti śrī-kṛṣṇasyaivāvatārāntaraṁ stauti—**pṛṣṭhe bhrāmyad** ity-ādi ||1-2||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (paramātma-sandarbhaḥ 109) :** artha-vādena [anena liṅgena śrīmad-bhāgavata-śāstre śrī-bhagavata eva mukhyatvaṁ pratipāditam, yathā] yam iti | **stavair** **vedaiś** ca **stunvanti** stuvanti | **dhyānenāvasthitaṁ** niścalaṁ **tad-gataṁ** yan manaḥ, tena ||1||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** 

trayodaśe punar natyā maṅgalācaraṇaṁ prabhoḥ |

ādy-antayoḥ purāṇasya saṅkhyā-dānādi cocyate ||

antime’trādhyāye punar api bhagavantaṁ praṇaman maṅgalam ācarati—yam iti | **stunvanti** stuvanti | **upaniṣac**-chabdasyākārāntam ārṣam | tenaitat-purāṇa-pāṭhena bhagavatas tasya stuti-saṅkīrtana-dhyānam eva mama yathā-kathañcid abhūt, na tu samyag avagama iti bhāvaḥ ||1||

**...**

**|| 12.13.2 ||**

**pṛṣṭhe bhrāmyad amanda-mandara-giri-grāvāgra-kaṇḍūyanān**

**nidrāloḥ kamaṭhākṛter bhagavataḥ śvāsānilāḥ pāntu vaḥ |**

**yat-saṁskāra-kalānuvartana-vaśād velā-nibhenāmbhasāṁ**

**yātāyātam atandritaṁ jala-nidher nādyāpi viśrāmyati ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **kṣīroda-mathanādau durjñeyatvam eva pradarśayituṁ kūrmāvatāram anusmārayann āśiṣaḥ prārthayate, pṛṣṭhe bhrāmyann amando mandara-girir gariṣṭho mandarācalas tasya grāvāṇas teṣām agrāṇi taiḥ kaṇḍūyanāt tena sukhena nidrālor nidrā-śīlasya | yeṣāṁ śvāsānilānāṁ saṁskārās teṣāṁ kalāś ca leśās tad anuvartana-vaśāj jala-nidher ambhasāṁ yātāyātaṁ na viśrāmyati | nanu samudra-kṣobhād eva tan na saṁskāra-vaśāt tatrāha, velākṣobhas tasya nibhena miṣeṇa |

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **surāsura-gaṇa-durjñeyānantatā bhagavatā kūrmāvatāra eva darśitātastat-smaraṇa-pūrvakaṁ śrī-bhāgavataṁ samāpayan śrī-bhāgavatasyāpi durjñeyārthatāṁ dhvanayati | śvāsānilāḥ prāṇa-vāyavaḥ vo yusmān adhyetr-adhyāpaka-vaktṛ-śrotèn pāntu balauja-ādi-dānena rakṣantu | śrī-bhagavata eva śvasanataḥ sarveṣāṁ balādyuttatti-śravaṇāt | tad uktam ekādaśe—yasyedriyaistanubhṛtāmubhayendriyāṇi jñānaṁ svataḥ śvasanato balamoja īhā ity-ādīti | atrākṣipati—nanv iti | kiṁ ca—samudramathanaṁ bhagavataiva kūrmarūpeṇa kṛtaṁ devānāṁ tu tatra nāmamātreṇaiva nimittatā tathedamapyapāravedamahāsamudramathanaṁ mannāmnā śrī-bhagavataiva katamity arthavyañjakaṁ vyāsoktamanuvadati—pṛṣṭa iti | yenaiva samudro mathitastenaiva bhagavatā mohinīrūpeṇāsurānvañcayitvā tadutthamamṛtaṁ svabhaktebhyo devebhyo dattaṁ, tathaiva vedasamudramathanottham idaṁ bhaktyanṛtaṁ śrī-bhāgavatarūpeṇābhaktānasurānvañcayitvā yuṣmamyaṁ dadāv iti bhaktānpratyāśīrvādaḥ ||2||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** kiṁ ca, yathā samudra-mathanaṁ bhagavataiva kūrmādi-rūpeṇa kṛtaṁ divaukasāṁ tu tatra nāma-mātreṇaiva nimittatā | tathaivedam apāra-veda-mahā-samudra-mathanaṁ yan-nāmnā bhagavataiva kṛtam ity artha-vyañjakaṁ śrī-vyāsoktam anuvadati pṛṣṭha iti | pṛṣṭhe bhrāmyann amando mahā-gurur mandara-giris tasya grāvāṇas teṣām agrāṇi taiḥ kaṇḍūyanāt nidrāloḥ kaṇḍūyanottha-sukhena nidrāśīlasya śvāsānilāḥ pāntu vaḥ | iti yenaiva samudro mathitas tenaiva bhagavatā mohinī-rūpeṇa asurān vañcayitvā samudra-mathanottham amṛtaṁ sva-bhaktebhyo devebhyo yathā dattaṁ tathaiva veda-samudra-mathanotthaṁ bhakty-amṛtam idaṁ śrī-bhāgavata-rūpeṇa abhaktān asurān vañcayitvā yuṣmabhyaṁ dadātv iti bhaktān pratyāśīrvādaḥ | yeṣāṁ śvāsānilānāṁ saṁskārās teṣāṁ kalā leśās tad-anuvartana-vaśāt jana-nidher ambhasāṁ yātāyātaṁ na viśrāmyati | nanu, tat-samudra-kṣobhād eva na tat-saṁskāra-vaśāt tatrāha—velā-kṣobhasya nibhena miṣeṇa ||2||

**...**

**|| 12.13.3 ||**

**purāṇa-saṅkhyā-sambhūtim asya vācya-prayojane |**

**dānaṁ dānasya māhātmyaṁ pāṭhādeś ca nibodhata ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **purāṇa-saṁhitānāṁ sañkhyās tāsāṁ saṁbhūtiṁ samāhāram | asya tu śrī-bhāgavatasya vācyaṁ viṣayaḥ prayojanaṁ ca dānaṁ ca tasya pāṭhādeś ca māhātmyaṁ nibodhata |

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **yathākhaṇḍa-maṇḍalapates tava maṇḍaleśā etāvanta iti gaṇyate tathaiva mahā-purāṇacakravartinaḥ śrī-bhāgavatasya sannidhau purāṇānyavaśyaṁ gaṇayāmītyataḥ purāṇānāṁ saṅkhyāyāssambhūti sambhavam ||3||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** yathā pṛthvī-pater agratas tava maṇḍaleśvarā etāvanta iti gaṇyante tathaiva mahā-purāṇa-cakravartinaḥ śrī-bhāgavatasya sannidhau purāṇāny avaśya-gamyānīty ataḥ purāṇānāṁ saṅkhyāyāḥ sambhūtiṁ sambhavam | tathāsya śrī-bhāgavatasya vācyaṁ ca prayojanaṁ ceti ||3||

**...**

**|| 12.13.4-9 ||**

**brāhmaṁ daśa sahasrāṇi pādmaṁ pañcona-ṣaṣṭi ca |**

**śrī-vaiṣṇavaṁ trayo-viṁśac catur-viṁśati śaivakam ||**

**daśāṣṭau śrī-bhāgavataṁ nāradaṁ pañca-viṁśati |**

**mārkaṇḍaṁ nava vāhnaṁ ca daśa-pañca catuḥ-śatam ||**

**catur-daśa bhaviṣyaṁ syāt tathā pañca-śatāni ca |**

**daśāṣṭau brahma-vaivartaṁ laiṅgam ekādaśaiva tu ||**

**catur-viṁśati vārāham ekāśīti-sahasrakam |**

**skāndaṁ śataṁ tathā caikaṁ vāmanaṁ daśa kīrtitam ||**

**kaurmaṁ sapta-daśākhyātaṁ mātsyaṁ tat tu catur-daśa |**

**ekona-viṁśat sauparṇaṁ brahmāṇḍaṁ dvādaśaiva tu ||**

**evaṁ purāṇa-sandohaś catur-lakṣa udāhṛtaḥ |**

**tatrāṣṭādaśa-sāhasraṁ śrī-bhāgavatam iṣyate ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **trayo-viṁśat trayo-viṁśatiḥ sahasrāṇi | catur-viṁśati catur-viṁśatiḥ | śaivakaṁ śiva-purāṇam | vāhnam agni-purāṇam | daśa-pañca-sahasrāṇi catvāri śatāni ca | skāndaṁ śatādhikaikāśīti-sahasram | sauparṇaṁ garuḍa-purāṇam ekona-viṁśad ekona-viṁśatiḥ | mahābhārataṁ tv itihāsaḥ | rāmāyaṇaṁ ca ṛṣi-proktaṁ kāvyam | ataḥ purāṇānāṁ sandohaḥ samūhaś catur-lakṣa-saṅkhyāka eva | idānīm asya vācya-prayojanādīn darśayitum āha, tatrety ādinā ||4-9||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **brāhmaṁ brahmapurāṇam | daśasahasrāṇi ayutaślokaparimitamity arthaḥ | pādmaṁ padmapurāṇam | pañcabhirūnā ṣaṣṭiḥ ślokasahasrāṇāṁ yatra tattathā | uttarapadalopī samāsaḥ | evamagre'pi jñeyam | tribhiradhikā viśatistrayoviṁśatiḥ, chāndasatvāviṁśate viṁśadādeśaḥ || daśasahasrāṇyaṣṭau sahasrāṇi ca yatra ślokāstacchrobhāgavatamity arthaḥ | mārkaṇḍaṁ mārkaṇḍeyam, pṛṣodarādiḥ | vahneridaṁ vāhnam, catuḥśatamity ukter daśapañcasahasrāṇīti labhyate, caturṇāṁ śatānāṁ samāhāraścatu śatam | yad vā, daśabhiḥ sahitāḥ pañca yatra tattathā | punaścatvāri 

śatāni yatra tattathā | evamagre'pi || tattu purāṇaṁ tu || mahābhāratādīnāṁ purāṇatvaśaṅkā nirasyati svāmī—mahābhārataṁ v iti | ṛṣiproktaṁ vālmīkiproktam | ato mahābhāratarāmāyaṇayoḥ purāṇatvābhāvāt | tatrāṣṭādaśasu purāṇeṣu | tatreti—athaivāvatāratvādavatāramadhye kṛṣṇaṁ gaṇayitvā punaḥ ete cāṁśakalāḥ puṁsaḥ kṛṣṇas tu bhagavānsvayam iti kṛṣṇasya pṛthaggaṇanā, tathaiva purāṇatvātpurāṇamadhye śrī-bhāgavataṁ gaṇayitvā tatrāṣṭādaśasāhasraṁ śrī-bhāgavatamipyate iti punargaṇanā purāṇacakravatitvavyañjikā | yathā ca tatra padaṁ sarvotkarṣavyañjakaṁ, tathā trāpi śrīmad iti padam iti prakrāntaṁ sampūrṇam eva ||4-9||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : _na vyākhyātam._**

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** trayoviṁśat trayoviṁśati | śaivakaṁ śiva-purāṇaṁ vāhnaṁ vahni-purāṇam | daśa-pañca-sahasrāṇi catvāri śatāni ca skāndaṁ śatādhikikāśīti-sahasraṁ tatrāṣṭādaśeti yathaivāvatāratvād avatāra-madhye kṛṣṇaṁ gaṇayitvā punar ete cāṁśa-kalāḥ puṁsaḥ kṛṣṇas tu bhagavān svayaṁ [bhā.pu. 1.3.28] iti kṛṣṇasya pṛthag gaṇanā | tatraiva purāṇatvāt purāṇa-madhye śrī-bhāgavataṁ gaṇayitvā tatrāṣṭādaśa-sāhasraṁ śrī-bhāgavatam iṣyate iti punar gaṇanā purāṇa-cakravartitva-vyañjikā yathā ca tatra svayaṁ padaṁ sarvotkarṣa-vyañjakaṁ tathaivātrāpi śrīmad iti padam idaṁ prakrāntaṁ sampūrṇam eva ||4-9||

**...**

**|| 12.13.10-12 ||**

**idaṁ bhagavatā pūrvaṁ brahmaṇe nābhi-paṅkaje |**

**sthitāya bhava-bhītāya kāruṇyāt samprakāśitam ||**

**ādi-madhyāvasāneṣu vairāgyākhyāna-saṁyutam |**

**hari-līlā-kathā-vrātāmṛtānandita-sat-suram ||**

**sarva-vedānta-sāraṁ yad brahmātmaikatva-lakṣaṇam |**

**vastv advitīyaṁ tan-niṣṭhaṁ kaivalyaika-prayojanam ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : hari-līlā-kathānāṁ vrātaḥ** samūhaḥ sa eva **amṛtam**, tena **ānanditāḥ** **santaḥ surāś** ca yena tat | **tan-niṣṭhaṁ** tad-viṣayam ||11-12||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tad eva vyanakti—kāruṇyātkṛpāpāravaśyāt | bhagavatā śrī-kṛṣṇena | garbhodaśāyine nābhipaṅkaje sthitāya brahmaṇe || yat sarveṣāṁ vedāntānāmupaniṣadāṁ sāraṁ brahmātmanorbrahmajīvayorekatvalakṣaṇamabhedarūpamadvitīyaṁ vastu tad eva niṣṭhāviṣayo vācyaṁ yasya tattanniṣṭhaṁ brahaukajñānamasya viṣaya ity arthaḥ | kaivalyaṁ svarūpāvāptir evaikaṁ mukhyaṁ prayojanaṁ yasya tattathā prasaṅgādasya sambandhas tu vācyavācakabhāvarūpo jñeyaḥ | adhikārī tvetajjijñāsurevetyetadanubandhacatuṣṭayam—dharmaḥ projjitakaitavaḥ ityatroktamapyatra smṛtilābhāya dhvanitam iti | vācyaṁ prayojanañcāha—harerlīlākathānāṁ brātaḥ samūha evāmṛtaṁ tenānanditāḥ santo bhaktā eva surā yena tad iti līlākathāvrātaśabdena bhaktirūpaṁ vācya vyañjitaṁ tad evāmṛtam iti premarūpaṁ prayojanaṁ ca premṇaiva bhakteramṛtavadāsvādyatvaprasiddheḥ, tena satāmānanda iti premṇo'nubhāvaḥ | tatra kathāyāmamūtatvāropeṇa tatsampradānānāṁ satāṁ suratvāropeṇa ca tatsampradātuḥ śāstrasyāsya mohinītvāropo labhyate, mohinyaiva surebhyo'mṛtadānatvaprasiddheḥ | tataś ca surānsvabhaktānsvaṁ viduṣaḥ prati bhrūvibhaṅgenaivānyajanājñātaṁ yathā brūte sma madanubhāvasyāsya yuṣmadānukūlyam eva kartavyaṁ prayojanaṁ cāsurānvañcayitvā yuṣmabhyamamṛtadānam | yathā cāsurānsvatattvamaviduṣaḥ prati api bhrūcālanenaitatspaṣṭam eva brūte sma tadāvirbhāvasya yuṣmākaṁ vijayaprāpaṇam eva kartavyaṁ, prayojanaṁ ca yuṣmabhyamamṛtadānāmatīdaṁ gauṇam eva | mukhyaprayojanaṁ tu yadyuṣmānnityamānandacamatkāraṁ prāpayāmi yuṣmadgṛhasthityaivāto'tidīnānetāndevānprathamaṁ kiñcitpariveṣayāmīti tathaivedaṁ bhāgavataśāstram api svatattvajñānsvabhaktān harilīlā ityardhapadyena svavācyam parokṣavādā ṛṣayaḥ parokṣaṁ mama ca priyam iti bhagavad-ukter vyañjanāvṛttyaiva sarvalokālakṣitamuktvā svatattvamaviduṣaḥ śāstrajñamāninaḥ prakaṭam eva svavācyaprayojane anye evāha—sarvavedāntānāṁ sāraṁ yadbrahmaṇā sahātmaikyamadvitīyaṁ vastu tasminvācakatvena niṣṭhā yasya tat | kaivalyam ekaṁ mukhyaṁ prayojanaṁ yasya tat | kecitpunar evaṁ vyācakṣate—śāstre'smindvayor eva bhaktijñānayoruktatvādbhaktipremaṇī vācyaprayojane uktvā jñānakaivalye api vācyaprayojane āha—sarveti | apare tvevamāhuḥ—śāstre'sminprakrame eva dharmaḥ projjhitakaitavo'tra paramaḥ ityanena paramadharmasya bhakter eva vācyatvāvagamāt īśvaraḥ | sadyo hṛdyavarudhyate'tra kṛtibhiḥ ityanena premṇa eva prayojanatvāvagamāc ca | tathā sarvaskandheṣu jñānāttatsādhyamukteś ca sakāśādbhakter eva prādhānyadarśanāt prādhānyena vyapadeśā bhavanti iti nyāyādbhaktipremṇor eva vācyatvaprayojanatve vyajyete, tasmānmohinīsādharmyaprāpakaprakaṭārthametatpadyamābhyantareṇāpyarthāntareṇa yojanīyam | tadyathā—brahmātmaikyalakṣaṇaṁ yadvastu tānniṣṭhaṁ tato'pi niḥsṛtya tiṣṭhatīti tanniṣṭhaṁ jñānakarmādyabhilāṣarahitā kevalā ananyabhaktāsteṣāṁ bhāvaḥ kaivalyaṁ tad eva prayojanaṁ yasya tad iti ||10-12||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **idam iti trikam | garbhodaka-śāyino nābhi-paṅkaje sthitāya brahmaṇe bhagavatā śrī-kṛṣṇena prakāśitam ||10||

**santa** ātmārāmā eva **surāḥ** | itthaṁ satāṁ brahma-sukhānubhūtyā [bhā.pu. 10.12.11] ity atra sac-chabdāt | 

nanu nīla-pītādy-ākāraṁ kṣaṇikam eva jñānaṁ dṛṣṭam, tat punar advayaṁ nityaṁ jñānaṁ kathaṁ lakṣyate, yan-niṣṭham idaṁ śāstram ?—sarveti | **brahmātmano** yad **ekatvam**, tad eva **lakṣaṇaṁ** yasya, tad **advitīyaṁ** **sarva-vedānta-sāraṁ vastu** **tan-niṣṭham** ity anvayaḥ | 

ayam arthaḥ—satyaṁ jñānam anantaṁ brahma [tai.u. 2.1.2] iti yasya svarūpam uktam, yenāśrutaṁ śrutaṁ bhavati [chā.u. 6.1.3] ity anayā, yad vijñānena [chā.u. 6.2.1] ity anayā sarva-vijñānaṁ pratijñātam, yasminn anantā nitya-siddhā eva nānā-dharmā abhyupagatāḥ, sad eva saumyedam agra āsīt [chā.u. 6.2.1] ity-ādinā nikhila-jagad-eka-kāraṇatā, sa aikṣata bahu syāṁ [chā.u. 6.2.3] ity anena satya-saṅkalpatā ca pratipāditā, tena brahmaṇā svarūpa-śaktibhyāṁ sarva-bṛhattamena, atha kasmād ucyate brahma bṛṁhati bṛṁhayati ca [atharva-śirā 3.5] iti śrutibhiḥ | bṛhattvāt bṛṁhaṇatvāc ca yad brahma paramaṁ viduḥ [vi.pu. 3.3.21] iti śrī-viṣṇu-purāṇādibhiś ca pratipāditena sārdham, anena jīvenātmanā [chā.u. 6.3.2] ity-ādi tadīya-vacana-rūpāyāṁ śrutāv idaṁtā-nirdeśena tato’bhinnatve’py ātmatā-nirdeśeṇa tad-ātmāṁśa-viśeṣatvena labdhasya—mamaivāṁśo jīva-loke jīva-bhūtaḥ sanātanaḥ [gītā 15.7] ity-ādi-pratipāditasya—aṁśo nānā-vyapadeśāt [ve.sū. 2.3.41] ity-ādi-nyāya-siddhasya, bādarāyaṇa-samādhi-dṛṣṭa-yukter atyabhinnatā-rahitasya jīvātmano yad ekatvam, tat tvam asi [chā.u. 6.8.7] ity ādau jñātṛtayā tad-aṁśa-bhūta-cid-rūpatvena samānākāratā, tad eva lakṣaṇaṁ prathamato jñāne sādhakatamaṁ yasya, tathābhūtaṁ—


    vadanti tattva-vidas tattvaṁ yaj jñānam advayam |


    brahmeti paramātmeti bhagavān iti śabdyate || [bhā.pu. 1.2.11] 

iti tridhāvirbhūtaṁ yat **sarve-vedānta-sāram** advitīyaṁ vastu, **tan-niṣṭhaṁ** tad-eka-viṣayam idaṁ śrīmad-bhāgavataṁ mahā-purāṇam iti prāktana-padyasthenānuṣāṅgaḥ | [tattva-sandarbha 52]

tathā **kaivalyaika-prayojanam** | kevalaḥ śuddhaḥ | sa ca projjhita-kaitavo yo bhaktaḥ, sa eva dharmaḥ projjhita-kaitavo’tra paramaḥ [bhā.pu. 1.1.2] ity uktatvāt | tasya bhāvaḥ kaivalyam, mokṣādi-kāma-rahitā bhaktiḥ | kaivalya-sammata-panthas tv atha bhakti-yogaḥ [bhā.pu. 2.3.12] ity atra kaivalyam ity eva sammataḥ panthā yo bhakti-yogaḥ iti ṭīkā-kṛdbhir vyākhyātatvāt | tatra panthā iti bhagavat-prāpty-upāya ity arthaḥ | sā bhaktiḥ prema-lakṣaṇaiva, tasyaiva tatra mukhyatvāt | tasmāt kaivalyaṁ bhagavat-premaiva puruṣārthatvena pratipādyaṁ yasya tat | sālokya-ṣarṣṭi-sāmīpyam ity-ādi-vacana-vṛndebhya iti ||11-12|| 

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (prīṭi-sandarbha 1) : **mukti-sāmānyasya śāstra-prayojanatvam āha—sarva-vedāntety ādau kaivalyaika-prayojanam iti | kevalaḥ śuddhaḥ, tasya bhāvaḥ kaivalyam | tad ekam eva prayojanaṁ parama-puruṣārthatvena pratipādyaṁ yasya tad idaṁ śrī-bhāgavatam iti pūrva-śloka-sthenānvayaḥ | doṣa-mūlaṁ hi jīvasya parama-tattva-jñānābhāva evety uktam—bhayaṁ dvitīyābhiniveśataḥ syād ity ādau, īśād apetasya [bhā.pu. 12.2.37] ity ādibhiḥ | atas taj-jñānam eva śuddhatvam iti kaivalya-śabdasyātra pūrvavat tad-anubhava eva tātparyam | 

athavā kaivalya-śabdena paramasya svabhāva evocyate | yathā skānde—


    brahmeśānādibhir devair yat prāptuṁ naiva śakyate |


    sa yat-svabhāvaḥ kaivalyaṁ sa bhavān kevalo hare || iti |

kvacit svārthika-tad-dhitāntena kaivalya-śabdenāpi parama ucyate | yathā śrī-dattātreya-śikṣāyāṁ—


    parāvarāṇāṁ parama āste kaivalya-saṁjñitaḥ |


    kevalānubhavānanda-sandoho nirupādhikaḥ || [bhā.pu. 11.9.18] iti |

tathāpy ubhayathaiva tad-anubhava eva tāt-paryam | tat-svabhāvam eva vā | tam evānubhāvayitum idaṁ śāstraṁ pravṛttam ity arthaḥ ||11-12|| 

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** vācya-prayojane cāha—harer līlā-kathānāṁ vrātaḥ samūha eva amṛtaṁ tena ānanditāḥ santo bhaktā eva surā yena tad iti līlā-kathā-vrāta-śabdena bhakti-rūpaṁ vācyaṁ vyañjitam | sa eva amṛtam iti prema-rūpaṁ prayojanaṁ ca | premnaiva bhakter amṛtavad āsvādyatva-siddheḥ | tena satām ānanda iti premno’nubhāvaḥ | tatra kathāyā amṛtatvāropeṇa tat-sampradānānāṁ satāṁ suratāropeṇa ca tat-sampradātuḥ śāstrasyāsya mohinītvāropo labhyate | mohinyā surebhyo’mṛta-dāna-prasiddheḥ | tataś ca surān sva-bhaktān svaṁ viduṣaḥ prati bhrū-riṅgaṇenaiva anya-janālakṣitaṁ yathā brūte sma mad-āvirbhāvasyāsya yuṣmad-ānukūlyam eva kartavyaṁ prayojanaṁ cāsurān vañcayitvā yuṣmabhyam evāmṛta-dānam | yathā cāsurān sva-tattvam aviduṣaḥ praty api bhrū-cālanenaivaṁ spaṣṭam eva brūte sma mad-āvirbhāvasya yuṣmākaṁ vijaya-prāpaṇam eva kartavyam | 

prayojanaṁ ca yuṣmabhyam amṛta-pradānam itīdaṁ gauṇam eva, mukhya-prayojanaṁ tv etad eva yad ānanda-camatkāraṁ yuṣmān nityaṁ prāpayāmi yuṣmad-gṛhasthitaiveti | tat-prathamam etān atidīnān nikṛṣṭān devān kiṁcit pariveṣayāmīti | tathaivedaṁ śrī-bhāgavata-śāstram api sva-tattva-jñān sva-bhaktān hari-līlety ardha-padyena sva-vācyaṁ parokṣa-vādā ṛṣayaḥ parokṣaṁ ca mama priyaṁ [bhā.pu. 11.21.35] iti bhagavad-ukter vyañjanayaiva vṛttyā sarva-lokālakṣitam uktvā sva-tattvam aviduṣaḥ śāstra-jña-māninaḥ prakaṭam eva sva-vācya-prayojane anye evāha sarva-vedāntānāṁ sāraṁ yat brahmaṇā saha ātmaikyam advitīyaṁ vastu tan-niṣṭhaṁ tasmin vācakatvena niṣṭhā yasya tat | kaivalyam ekaṁ mukhyaṁ prayojanaṁ yasya tat | 

kecit punar evaṁ vyācakṣate—śāstre’smin bhakti-jñānayor dvayor api mārgayor uktatvāt bhakti-premaṇī vācya-prayojane uktvā jñāna-kaivalye api vācya-prayojane āha sarva-vedānteti | kaivalyam apekṣaṁ prayojanaṁ yasya tat | apare tv evam āhuḥ | śāstre’sminn upakrama eva dharmaḥ projjhita-kaitavo’tra parama [bhā.pu. 1.1.2] ity anena parama-dharmasya bhakter eva vācyatvāvagamāt īśvaraḥ sadyo hṛdy avaruddhyate’tra kṛtibhiḥ ity anena premna eva prayojanatvāvagamāc ca tathā sarveṣv api skandheṣu jñānāt tat-sādhyāyān mukter api śakāśāt bhakter eva prādhānya-darśanāt prādhānyena vyapadeśā bhavantīti nyāyāt bhakti-premnor evābhidheyatva-prayojanatve vājyete | tasmān mohinī sārdharmya-prāpaka-prakaṭārtham etat padyam ābhyantareṇārthāntareṇa prayojanīyaṁ tad yathā brahmātmaikatva-lakṣaṇaṁ yad vastu tan-niṣṭhaṁ tato’pi niḥsṛtya tiṣṭhatīti tat tathā | jñāna-karma-svargādyābhilāṣa-rahitāḥ kevalā ananya-bhaktās teṣāṁ bhāvaḥ kaivalyaṁ tad eva prayojanaṁ yasya tad iti ||11-12||

**...**

**|| 12.13.13-14 ||**

**prauṣṭhapadyāṁ paurṇamāsyāṁ hema-siṁha-samanvitam |**

**dadāti yo bhāgavataṁ sa yāti paramāṁ gatim ||**

**rājante tāvad anyāni purāṇāni satāṁ gaṇe |**

**yāvad bhāgavataṁ naiva śrūyate’mṛta-sāgaram ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **prauṣṭha-padyāṁ bhādrapadyām | hema-siṁha-samanvitaṁ suvarṇa-siṁhāsanārūḍham ||13-14||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **nāmaikadeśoccāraṇanyāyena siṁhapadaṁ siṁhāsanaṁ vaktotyāha—suvarṇasiṁhāsaneti | dānapātraṁ tu janmādyasya iti vyākhyāśatake proktam api prasaṅgātpunaratrocyate—


    suvṛttāya gṛhasthāya kṛṣṇabhaktāya santatam | sarvaśāstravide'dhyāpane niratāya ca viprāya deyametattu śrīmadbhāgavataṁ mune | yasya pāṭhādinirato virakto'pi yadā dvijaḥ | tasmā api deyametanna baddhvā sthāpine kvācit | iti saṁhitokteḥ | 

prauṣṭhapadyāṁ bhādrasambandhinyām | tasminn eva dine śrīmunīndraiṇaitatpurāṇaṁ samāptīkṛtam iti pādmottarakhaṇḍamāhātmye dṛṣṭam | hemasiṁheti—


    sarvaśāstramahārājasyāsya purāṇasūryasya sāmrājyārthaṁ siṁhāsanaucityāt | sarvagraharājasya sūryasyā'pi siṁharāśigasya siṁhāsanārūḍhatā dṛṣṭaiva | paramāṁ paramasya bhagavataḥ sannidhirūpām | jñānena vaiyāsakiśabditena bheje khagendradhvajapādamūlam || ity-ukteḥ ||

śrūyata ityatra dṛśyate iti pāṭhaścakravartyādisammato'sti | asya sarvaśāstrarājatvamevāha—rājanta iti | anyāni purāṇāni tāvacchāstrarājatvavanti, yāvanneti bhāgavataṁ tu samrāḍevātaḥ śāstramahārājatvamatraiveti bhāvaḥ| yad vā, asya purāṇasūryatvam āha—rājante dīpyante rātrau nakṣatrāṇi veti bhāvaḥ yāvadrāntryante, yāvanneti sati sūrye na dṛśyete iti bhāvaḥ ||13-14||

———————————————————————————————————————

**sanātana-gosvāmī :** [ha.bha.vi. 10.404] amṛtaṁ bhagavad-bhakti-rasaḥ | tasya sāgaraḥ ||14||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **tad-dānasyāpi tādṛg eva phalam āha—prauṣṭhapadyām iti | paramāṁ paramasya bhagavataḥ sannidhi-rūpāṁ, jñānena vaiyāsaki-śabditena [bhā.pu. 1.18.16] ity-ādeḥ ||13|| rājanta iti | svarṇa-siṁhāsanārūḍhatve hetutayā rājatvam eva darśitam ||14||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** prauṣṭhapadyāṁ bhādra-sambandhinyām iti tad-dina eva śrīman-mīndreṇa śāstram etat samāpta-kṛtam iti pādmottara-khaṇḍa-gata-bhāgavata-māhātmye dṛṣṭam | hema-siṁha-samanvitam iti sarva-śāstra-mahārājasya purāṇa-sūryasyāsya sāmrājyārthaṁ siṁhāsanaucityāt sarva-graha-rājasyetad upamānasya sūryasyāpi tadānīṁ siṁha-rāśi-gatatvena siṁhāsanādhirūḍhatā dṛṣṭaiva | asya sarva-śāstra-mahārājatvam evāha—rājnta iti | anyāni purāṇāny api prāyas tāvat śāstra-rājāni yāvan neti śrī-bhāgavataṁ tu samrāḍ evātaḥ śāstra-mahārājam iti bhāvaḥ | yad vā, asya purāṇa-sūryatam āha—rājante dīpyante rātrau nakṣatrāṇīveti bhāvaḥ | yāvad rātryante yāvan neti sati sūryo na dṛśyate ||13-14||

**...**

**|| 12.13.15-17 ||**

**sarva-vedānta-sāraṁ hi śrī-bhāgavatam iṣyate |**

**tad-rasāmṛta-tṛptasya nānyatra syād ratiḥ kvacit ||**

**nimna-gānāṁ yathā gaṅgā devānām acyuto yathā |**

**vaiṣṇavānāṁ yathā śambhuḥ purāṇānām idaṁ tathā ||**

**kṣetrāṇāṁ caiva sarveṣāṁ yathā kāśī hy anuttamā |**

**tathā purāṇa-vrātānāṁ śrīmad-bhāgavataṁ dvijāḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **tad-rasa evaṁ-ṛtaṁ tena tṛptasya nirvṛtasya ||15||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **tadrasaḥ śrī-bhāgavatarasaḥ pibata bhāgavataṁ rasamālayam ity-ukteḥ | sa ca śrī-kṛṣṇalīlāmādhuryādilakṣaṇa eva amṛtaṁ pīyūṣam || nimnaṁ gacchantīti nimnagāḥ nadyastāsāṁ gaṅgā bhāgīrathī, agrimaśloke yathā—kāśī hyanuttamā ity ukter acyutādipadair api talliṅgavyatyāsenottamapadaṁ yojyam | na uttama utkṛṣṭo yasmādyasyā veti yathocitaṁ samasanīyam | kiṁ ca, —sarvavaiṣṇavaśiromaṇeḥ śrīśivasya tripuṇḍrabhasmarudrākṣadhṛtidarśanādetatkālikaistatkathaṁ na dhāryata iti na śaṅkanīyam na devacaritaṁ caret iti smṛteḥ | yaccaitaddhāraṇe vaiṣṇavaḥ, tulasyādidhāraṇe śaivaiś ca nindocyate, tatparamārthā'jñānavijambhitaiva | yāni tu tattannindāvākyānyudāhniyante, tāni nirmūlānyeveti | na hi rudrākṣādidhṛtyā vaiṣṇavatvaṁ naśyati kintu varddhata eva, tathaiva tulasyādidhṛtyā śaivatvaṁ na naśyati kintu varddhata eva, tathāpi mahājano yena gataḥ sa panthā iti iti nyāyamāśritya vartitavyam iti tattvam | idaṁ śrī-bhāgavatam || kāśyā mahattvaṁ hi śatapathabrāhmaṇe varṇitam | tathā hi—


    avimuktaṁ ha vai kurukṣetraṁ devānāṁ devayajanaṁ sarveṣāṁ bhūtānāṁ brahmasadanamatra hi jantoḥ prāṇeṣu kramamāṇeṣu rudrastārakaṁ caṣṭe yenāsāvabhṛtī bhūtvā mokṣī bhavati || iti śruteḥ | 

yad vā, kaṁ sarvapurovilakṣaṇaṁ mokṣasukhaṁ yatra sā kāśī mathurā | yaduktaṁ vārāhe—


    kāśyādayo yadyapi santi puryastāsāṁ tu madhye mathuraiva dhanyā | 


    yā janmamauñjīvratamṛtyudauharnṛṇāṁ caturddhā vidadhāti muktim || iti | 

yad vā, kaṁ brahmāśnute sarvadā tiṣṭhatyeti kāśī puṇyaṁ madhuvanaṁ yatra sānnidhyaṁ nityadā hareḥ iti nāradokteḥ, mathurā bhagavānyatra nityaṁ sannihito hariḥ iti śrīdaśamokteś ca | 


    mathureti trivarṇīyaṁ trayīto'pi garīyasī | 


    trayī tu dhāvati brahma tadenāmanudhāvati || 

ityabhiyuktokteś ca | kaṁ brahmaṇi sukhe'mbuni iti viśvaḥ | kṣetrāṇāṁ puṇyakṣetrāṇām | kṣīyante yatra pāpāni trāyate yanmahābhayāt | tatkṣetramucyate prājñaḥ iti skāndokteḥ ||15-17||

———————————————————————————————————————

**sanātana-gosvāmī : **[ha.bha.vi. 10.405] tad-rasaḥ, tasyāsvādanaṁ tat-prītir vā, sa evāmṛtaṁ tena tṛptasya, anyatra vedāntādau ||15||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **śrī-mahan-mukharitasya mahat-kīrtyamānasya śrī-bhagavad-guṇa-śravaṇasya mahā-māhātmyaṁ mahā-sukha-pradatvaṁ coktam | tatrāpi śravaṇe śrī-bhāgavata-śravaṇaṁ tu parama-śreṣṭhaṁ—(ka) tasya tādṛśa-prabhāvamaya-śabdātmakatvāt, (kha) parama-rasamayatvāc ca | tatra (ka) pūrvasmād yathāha—śrīmad-bhāgavate mahā-muni-kṛte [bhā.pu. 1.1.2] iti, (kha) uttarasmād vyanakti—sarveti | tad-rasaḥ śrī-bhagavad-bhakti-rasāmṛtaṁ, tena tṛptasya, pibata bhāgavataṁ rasam ālayaṁ [bhā.pu. 1.1.3] ity-ādy-ukteḥ | nātyantikaṁ vigaṇayanty api [bhā.pu. 3.15.48] ity-ādeś ca ||15||

ata evāha—nimnagānām iti ||17||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** sarva-vedāntebhyo’pi sāraṁ śreṣṭham | gaṅgeti sarva-pāpa-nāśanatvena | acyuta iti sarvotkarṣeṇa śambhur iti sarva-bhagavad-dharmopadeṣṭṛtvenopamā ||15-17||

**...**

**|| 12.13.18 ||**

**śrīmad-bhāgavataṁ purāṇam amalaṁ yad vaiṣṇavānāṁ priyaṁ**

**yasmin pāramahaṁsyam ekam amalaṁ jñānaṁ paraṁ gīyate |**

**tatra jñāna-virāga-bhakti-sahitaṁ naiṣkarmyam āviṣkṛtaṁ**

**tac chṛṇvan su-paṭhan vicāraṇa-paro bhaktyā vimucyen naraḥ ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **pārama-haṁsyaṁ parama-haṁsaiḥ prāpyam | naiṣkarmyaṁ sarva-karmoparamaḥ | bhaktyā tac-chravaṇādi-paro vimucyate ||18||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **amalaṁ sarvaśuddhikaram | amalaṁ śuddhādvaitaviṣayam | vipaṭhan viśeṣeṇa paṭhan | vicāraṇaparaḥ sātatyenaitaccintanaparaḥ sarvotkarṣamevāha—bhāgavata purāṇam eva śrīmat śobhāyuktam | na bhavanti malāstriguṇotthā yasmāttat | yadyato vaiṣṇavānāṁ priyaṁ bhaktyutkarṣapratipādakatvād iti bhaktyutthajñānaprāptilobhibhirjñānisiddhair apy etadāśrayaṇīyamevetyāha—yasminn iti | paramahaṁsebhyo hitaṁ pāramahaṁsyam | paraṁ bhaktyutthatvācchraiṣṭham | jñānasādhakair apy etatsevyamityāha—yatreti | naiṣkarmyaṁ sarvakarmoparamam ||18||

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** śrīmad-bhāgavatam ity-ādi | vaiṣṇavānāṁ priyam iti svarūpa-nirdeśaḥ | tatra hetuḥ—yasmin pāramahaṁsyam ity-ādi | paramahaṁsā bhāgavata-paramahaṁsās teṣām idaṁ pāramahaṁsyaṁ kevalaṁ prema-bhakty-ānando yasmin | naiṣkarmyaṁ ca āviṣkṛtaṁ naiṣkarmyaṁ bhagavad-bhakti-yoga-viruddhaṁ karma, tad-abhāvaḥ | atas tat tat śṛṇvan paṭhan vicāraṇa-paras tu bhaktyaiva vimucyate, na tv anyenety arthaḥ | ato bhaktir evātra puruṣārtha ity upasaṁhāraḥ ||18||

———————————————————————————————————————

**sanātana-gosvāmī : **[ha.bha.vi. 10.407] vaiṣṇavatve priyatve hetum āha—yasminn ity ādinā | pāramahaṁsyaṁ paramahaṁsānām api hitaṁ paraṁ jñānaṁ bhagavad-bhakti-māhātmyādi-viṣayam | ato’malaṁ sarva-mala-nivartakam | ata eva śrī-bhāgavate vyākhyātaṁ—ādau jñānam, tatas tattva-vedanam, tato virāgaḥ viṣayādi-vairāgyam, tato bhaktiś ca śravaṇādi-lakṣaṇā, tat-sahitaṁ naiṣkarmyaṁ niṣkarmāṇo bhagavad-bhaktās taiḥ prāpyaṁ bhagavat-prema āviṣkṛtaṁ sākṣād iva darśitam | eat śravaṇādi-pravṛttyā evasvatas tat-tat-siddheḥ | tat śrīmad-bhāgavataṁ bhaktyā śṛṇvan vipaṭhan saṅkīrtayan vicāraṇa-paraś ca, tad-arthaṁ vicārayaṁś ca san naraḥ sarvo janaḥ viśeṣeṇa mucyate, śrī-vaikuṇṭha-lokaṁ prāpnotīty arthaḥ ||18||

———————————————————————————————————————

**jīva-gosvāmī (krama-sandarbhaḥ) : **kiṁ ca, śrīmad-bhāgavatam iti, vaiṣṇavānāṁ priyam ity anenaiva tathā vivakṣitam | atrānuṣaṅgikaṁ guṇam āha—yasminn iti | vimucyet—sarva-bhakty-antarāyebhyo’pi nistaret ||18||

———————————————————————————————————————

**viśvanātha-cakravartī (sārārtha-darśiṇī) :** sarvotkarṣam evopapādayati bhāgavataṁ purāṇam eva śrīmat sarva-śobhā-yuktaṁ na bhavanti malās triguṇotthā yasmāt tat | yat yato vaiṣṇavānāṁ priyaṁ bhakty-utkarṣa-pratipādakatvād iti bhāvaḥ bhakty-uttha-jñāna-prāpti-lobhibhir jñāna-siddhair ātmārāmair apy etad-āśrayaṇīyam evety āha yasminn iti paramahaṁsebhyo hitaṁ pāramahaṁsyaṁ hitārthe ṣaṇ pāramahaṁsyaṁ paraṁ bhakty-utthatvāt śreṣṭham | jñāna-sādhakair apy etad avaśya-sevyam ity āha | yatreti naiṣkarmyaṁ sarva-karmoparamaḥ ||18||

**...**

**|| 12.13.19 ||**

**kasmai yena vibhāsito’yam atulo jñāna-pradīpaḥ purā**

**tad-rūpeṇa ca nāradāya munaye kṛṣṇāya tad-rūpiṇā |**

**yogīndrāya tad-ātmanātha bhagavad-rātāya kāruṇyatas**

**tac chuddhaṁ vimalaṁ viśokam amṛtaṁ satyaṁ paraṁ dhīmahi ||**

**śrīdhara-svāmī (bhāvārtha-dīpikā) : **śrī-bhāgavata-sampradāya-pravartaka-rūpeṇa bhagavad-dhyāna-lakṣaṇaṁ maṅgalam ācarati—kasmai brahmaṇe atulo’samaḥ | ayaṁ śrī-bhāgavata-rūpaḥ | purā kalpādau | tad-rūpeṇa brahma-rūpena nāradāya tad-rūpiṇā nārada-rūpiṇā kṛṣṇāya vyāsāya | tad-rūpiṇā yogīndrāya śukāya tad-ātmanā śuka-rūpeṇa | tat paraṁ satyaṁ śrī-nārāyaṇākhyaṁ tattvaṁ dhīmahi | iti gāyatryaiva yathopakramam upasaṁharan gāyatry-ākhya-brahma-vid yeyam iti darśayati ||19||

———————————————————————————————————————

**vaṁśīdharaḥ (bhāvārtha-dīpikā-prakāśaḥ) : **granthādau granthamadhye granthānte maṅgalamācaraṇīyam iti śiṣṭācārāt maṅgalādīni maṅgalamadhyāni maṅgalāntāni ca śāstrāṇi prathante ity-ādi bhāṣyāc ca śāstrasamāptau tadācaratīty āha—śrī-bhāgavatasampradāyetyādi | kasmai—asarvanāmnopi sarvanāmakāryamārṣatvāt | yena parabrahmaṇā | jñānaṁ parokṣāparokṣarūpaṁ prakarṣeṇa dīpayatīti tathā | ayaṁ śrīmadbhāgavatalakṣaṇā| kṛṣṇāya vyāsāya | atheti—tadātmanetyasya dviyojanāyoktam | śuddhaṁ sarvopādhivinirmuktam | vimalamajñānatatkāryanivartakam | tarati śokamātmavit iti śruteḥ | śokopalakṣitassaṁsāraḥ, vigataḥ śoko yena tadviśākaṁ saṁsārataraṇasādhanam | amṛtaṁ mṛtinivartakam | vimalaviśokāmṛtapadānāṁ tātparyaṁta ekārthatve'pi punaruktiḥ sarvathā saṁsārabhayanāśakamity artheti 

jñeyam | satyaṁ traikālikābādhyam | jñānāntareṇa viṣayāsatyapratītirbādhastadayogyamata eva paraṁ sarvataḥ paraṁ sarvāvadhībhūtam | puruṣānna paraṁ kiñcitsā kāṣṭhā sā parā gatiḥ iti śruteḥ | dhīmahīti sākṣādgāyatrīpadayogena gāyatryeveti pūrvam vastvadvitīyaṁ tanniṣṭham iti sāmānyatas tātparyaṁ darśayitvā janmādyasya ity-ādy-upakramapoṣakaṁ śrī-bhagavatyeva tasya paryavasānaṁ darśayannupasaṁharati—kasmād iti | mahāvaikuṇṭhaṁ darśayatā yena bhagavatā brahmaṇe vibhāsitaṁ prakāśitam, na tu viracitam idaṁ bhāgavatam | purā pūrvaparārddhādau | tadātmanetyasyottarottareṇāpyanvayaḥ | tatra tadātmanā śrīśukarūpeṇeti na kevalaṁ catuḥślokyeva tena prakāśitā, api tu tatratatrāviṣṭenākhaṇḍamevedaṁ purāṇam iti dyotitam | śrīsaṅkarṣaṇasampradāyapravṛttis tu śrīdvaipāyanakartṛkaprakāśāntargatatvāt pṛthagnoktā | tatparaṁ satyaṁ bhagavad-ākhyaṁ tattvaṁ dhīmahi yattatpadamanuttamam iti sahasranāmasu tacchabdasya tannāmatvena gaṇitatvāt | paraśabdena śrī-bhagavānevocyate ādyo'vatāraḥ puruṣaḥ parasya iti dvitīyokteḥ | brahmādīnāṁ buddhivṛttipravartakatvenābhidhānāt | gāyatryarthopalakṣitena dhīmahīti gāyatrīpadenopasaṁhārādgāyatryākhyabrahmavidyaiveyaṁ śrī-bhāgavatapurāṇam ||19||

———————————————————————————————————————

**śrīnātha-cakravartī (caitanya-mata-mañjuṣā) :** kasmai yenety-ādi | yena śrī-kṛṣṇena kasmai brahmaṇe’yaṁ śrī-bhāgavatkhyo jñāna-pradīpaḥ vibhāsitaḥ | purā prathamaṁ tad-rūpeṇa nāradāya ca, tad-rūpiṇā nārada-rūpiṇā kṛṣṇāya veda-vyāsāya | tad-rūpiṇā vyāsa-rūpiṇā yogīndrāya śukāya | tad-ātmanā śuka-rūpeṇa bhagavad-rātāya parīkṣite tat śrī-kṛṣṇākhyam amṛtaṁ, satyaṁ paraṁ dhīmahi | tad ity avyayam uttamam ity arthaḥ | upakrame copasaṁhāre gāyatryaiva nibaddham iti bhāgavatsyāsādhāraṇo dharmaḥ ||19||
